Matthew1:1 Mazita amadzitateguru aJesu Kristu, mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, mwanakomana waAbhurahamu." 
Matthew1:2 Abhurahamu akabereka Isaka; Isaka akabereka Jakobho; Jakobho akabereka Judha navanun'una vake; 
Matthew1:3 Judha akabereka Faresi naZara nomukadzi wake Tamari; Faresi akabereka Esiromi; Esiromi akabereka Arami; 
Matthew1:4 Arami akabereka Aminadhabhu; Aminadhabhu akabereka Nasoni; Nasoni akabereka Saremoni. 
Matthew1:5 Saremoni akabereka Bhoazi kumukadzi wake Rahabhi; Bhoazi akabereka Obhedhi nomukadzi wake Rute; Obhedhi akabereka Jesi; 
Matthew1:6 Jesi akabereka mambo Dhavhidhi. Dhavhidhi akabereka Soromoni nomukadzi waUriya; 
Matthew1:7 Soromoni akabereka Robhoami; Robhoami akabereka Abhia; Abhia akabereka Asafa; 
Matthew1:8 Asafa akabereka Josafati; Josafati akabereka Joramu; Joramu akabereka Uziya. 
Matthew1:9 Uziya akabereka Jotamu; Jotamu akabereka Ahazi; Ahazi akabereka Hezekiya; 
Matthew1:10 Hezekiya akabereka Manase; Manase akabereka Amoni; Amoni akabereka Josiya; 
Matthew1:11 Josiya akabereka Jekonia navanun'una vake nenguva yokutapwa kwavo Bhabhironi. 
Matthew1:12 Shure kwokutapwa kwavo Bhabhironi Jekonia akabereka Saratieri; Saratieri akabereka Zerubhabheri; 
Matthew1:13 Zerubhabheri akabereka Abhiudhi; Abhiudhi akabereka Eriyakimi; Eriyakimi akabereka Azori; 
Matthew1:14 Azori akabereka Sadhoki; Sadhoki akabereka Akimi; Akimi akabereka Eriudhi; 
Matthew1:15 Eriudhi akabereka Eriazari; Eriazari akabereka Matani; Matani akabereka Jakobho; 
Matthew1:16 Jakobho akabereka Josefa, murume waMaria, iye akabereka Jesu, anonzi Kristu." 
Matthew1:17 Naizvozvo zvizvarwa zvose kubva kuna Abhurahamu kusvikira kuna Dhavhidhi zvaiva zvizvarwa gumi nezvina; kubva kuna Dhavhidhi kusvikira pakutapwa Bhabhironi zvizvarwa zvine gumi nezvina; kubva pakutapwa Bhabhironi kusvikira kuna Jesu Kristu zvizvarwa zvine gumi nezvina. 
Matthew1:18 Kuberekwa kwaJesu Kristu kwaiva kudai: Maria, mai vake, akati aroorwa naJosefa, vasati vasangana, akaonekwa ava napamuviri naMweya Mutsvene." 
Matthew1:19 Zvino Josefa, murume wake, zvaakanga ari munhu akarurama, asingadi kumunyadzisa, akafunga kumuramba chinyararire." 
Matthew1:20 Zvino akati acharangarira izvozvo, tarira mutumwa waIshe akazviratidza kwaari pakurota akati, “Josefa, mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, usatya kutora Maria, mukadzi wako; nokuti chakaumbwa mukati make ndechaMweya Mutsvene." 
Matthew1:21 Iye achazvara mwanakomana, agomutumidza zita rinonzi Jesu; nokuti ndiye achaponesa vanhu vake pazvivi zvavo.”" 
Matthew1:22 Izvozvo zvose zvakaitwa kuti zviitike zvakarehwa naIshe, nomuromo womuporofita achiti," 
Matthew1:23 “Tarira, mhandara ichava nepamuviri, ichazvara mwanakomana, vachamutumidza zita rinonzi Emanueri;” ndokuti, “Kana zvichishandurwa, Mwari anesu.”" 
Matthew1:24 Zvino Josefa akamuka pahope dzake akaita sezvaakarairwa nomutumwa waIshe, akatora mukadzi wake;" 
Matthew1:25 akasamuziva kusvikira azvara mwanakomana wake wedangwe, ndokumutumidza zita rinonzi Jesu." 
Matthew2:1 Jesu akati aberekwa muBhetirehemu reJudhiya, pamazuva amambo Herodhi, tarira, vachenjeri vakasvika Jerusaremu vachibva mabvazuva," 
Matthew2:2 vakati, “Aripiko Mambo wavaJudha akazvarwa? Nokuti takaona nyenyedzi yake kumabvazuva, tauya kuzomupfugamira.”" 
Matthew2:3 Mambo Herodhi akati achizvinzwa, akatambudzika kwazvo, neJerusaremu rose naye." 
Matthew2:4 Akakokera vapristi vakuru vose navanyori pakati pevanhu, akavabvunza kuti, “Kristu uchaberekerwepi.”" 
Matthew2:5 Vakati kwaari, “MuBhetirehemu reJudhiya; nokuti ndizvo zvakanyorwa nomuporofita, zvichinzi;" 
Matthew2:6 ‘Newe Bhetirehemu, nyika yeJudhiya, Hausi muduku kwazvo kuvabati vaJudha; Nokuti mauri muchabuda Mutungamiriri, Achafudza vanhu vangu VaIsiraeri.’ ”" 
Matthew2:7 Zvino Herodhi akadana vachenjeri, vari voga, akavabvunzisisa nguva yakaonekwa nyenyedzi navo," 
Matthew2:8 akavatuma Bhetirehemu, akati, “Endai munatsobvunzisisa zvomwana; kana mamuwana, mundiudze, kuti neniwo ndiuye kuzomupfugamirawo.”" 
Matthew2:9 Vakati vanzwa mambo, vakaenda; zvino, tarira, nyenyedzi yavakanga vaona kumabvazuva, yakavatungamirira, kusvikira yandomira pamusoro peimba makanga muno mwana." 
Matthew2:10 Vakati vaona nyenyedzi, vakafara nomufaro mukuru–kuru." 
Matthew2:11 Vakapinda mumba, vakawana mwana naMaria mai vake; vakawira pasi, vakamupfugamira; vakasunungura mabutwa avo, vakamupa zvipo zvendarama, nezvinonhuwira, nemura." 
Matthew2:12 Vakati vanyeverwa pakurota naMwari, kuti varege kudzokera kuna Herodhi, vakaenda kunyika yavo neimwe nzira." 
Matthew2:13 Vakati vaenda, tarira, mutumwa waIshe akaonekwa naJosefa pakurota, achiti, “Simuka, utore mwana namai vake, utizire Ijipiti, ugareko kusvikira ndichikuudza; nokuti Herodhi achatsvaka mwana kuti amuuraye.”" 
Matthew2:14 Akasimuka, akatora mwana namai vake usiku, akaenda Ijipiti," 
Matthew2:15 akagarako kusvikira Herodhi afa, kuti zviitike zvakarehwa naIshe nomuromo womuporofita, achiti, “Ndakadana mwanakomana wangu abve Ijipiti.”" 
Matthew2:16 Zvino Herodhi, akati aona kuti anyengerwa navachenjeri, akatsamwa kwazvo–kwazvo; akatuma vanhu kundouraya vana vakomana vose vaiva muBhetirehemu munyika yose yakapoteredza, vaiva namakore maviri navaduku kwavari, iri nguva yaakanzwisisa kuvachenjeri." 
Matthew2:17 Zvikaitika zvakarehwa nomuporofita Jeremiya achiti," 
Matthew2:18 “Izwi rakanzwika muRama, Rokuchema nokurira kukuru; Racheri achichema vana vake, Asingadi kunyaradzwa, nokuti havachipo.”" 
Matthew2:19 Herodhi akati afa, tarira, mutumwa waIshe akaonekwa naJosefa pakurota muIjipiti," 
Matthew2:20 akati, “Simuka, utore mwana namai vake, uende kunyika yaIsiraeri, nokuti vaitsvaka kuuraya mwana vakafa.”" 
Matthew2:21 Akasimuka, ndokutora mwana namai vake, akasvika kunyika yaIsiraeri." 
Matthew2:22 Asi, akati achinzwa kuti Akerasi wava mambo panzvimbo yababa vake Herodhi, akatya kuendako; akanyeverwa mukurota, akaenda kumativi enyika yeGareriya;" 
Matthew2:23 akandogara muguta rinonzi Nazareta, kuti zvakarehwa navaporofita zviitike, kuti achanzi muNazareta." 
Matthew3:1 Namazuva iwayo Johani Mubhabhatidzi akauya achiparidza murenje reJudhiya, achiti," 
Matthew3:2 “Tendeukai, nokuti ushe hwokudenga hwaswedera pedyo.”" 
Matthew3:3 Nokuti uyu ndiye wakarehwa nomuporofita Isaya, achiti, “Izwi raanodana murenje: ‘Gadzirai nzira yaIshe, Ruramisai migwagwa yake.’ ”" 
Matthew3:4 Iye Johani aiva nenguo yamakushe engamera, nebhanhire reganda pachiuno chake; zvokudya zvake zvaiva mhashu nouchi hwemusango" 
Matthew3:5 Zvino veJerusaremu rose neJudhiya nenyika yose yakapoteredza Jodhani vakabudira kwaari," 
Matthew3:6 vakabhabhatidzwa naye murwizi Jodhani vachireurura zvivi zvavo. 
Matthew3:7 Asi akati achiona vazhinji vaVaFarisi navaSadhusi vachiuya kuzobhabhatidzwa, akati kwavari, “Vana venyoka, ndianiko akakunyeverai kuti mutize kutsamwa kunouya?" 
Matthew3:8 Naizvozvo berekai zvibereko zvakafanira kutendeuka. 
Matthew3:9 Musafunga kutaura mumwoyo menyu, muchiti, ‘Abhurahamu ndibaba vedu;’ nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Mwari angamutsira Abhurahamu vana pamabwe awa.’" 
Matthew3:10 Zvino sanhu ratoiswa pamudzi wemiti; saka muti mumwe nomumwe usingabereki michero yakanaka, unotemwa, ukakandirwa mumoto." 
Matthew3:11 Ini ndinokubhabhatidzai nemvura, kuti mutendeuke; asi anouya shure kwangu, anesimba, kupfuureni, wandisakafanira kutakura shangu dzake; iye achakubhabhatidzai naMweya Mutsvene nomoto." 
Matthew3:12 Rusero rwake ruri muruoko rwake; achanatsa buriro rake kwazvo; achaunganidzira koroni mudura, asi hundi achaipisa mumoto usingadzimwi.”" 
Matthew3:13 Zvino Jesu akabva Gareriya, akasvika kuna Jodhani kuzobhabhatidzwa naJohani." 
Matthew3:14 Asi Johani akaedza kumudzivisa, akati, “Ndini ndinofanira kubhabhatidzwa nemi, ko mouya kwandiri sei?”" 
Matthew3:15 Asi Jesu akapindura akati, “Chirega hako zvino, nokuti saizvozvo zvakafanira kuti tizadzise kururama kwose.” Johani ndokubva atenda hake." 
Matthew3:16 Jesu, akati abhabhatidzwa, pakarepo akabuda mumvura; zvino, tarira, denga rakamuzarukira, akaona Mweya waMwari achiburuka senjiva, akauya pamusoro pake." 
Matthew3:17 Zvino tarira, izwi rakabva kudenga, richiti, “Uyu ndiye Mwanakomana wangu anodikanwa, ndinofadzwa naye!”" 
Matthew4:1 Zvino Jesu akatungamirirwa naMweya kurenje, kuzoedzwa naDhiabhori." 
Matthew4:2 Akati azvinyima zvokudya mazuva ana makumi mana, nousiku hunamakumi mana, akabva oziya." 
Matthew4:3 Zvino muedzi akauya akati kwaari, “Kana uri Mwanakomana waMwari, taura kuti mabwe awa zvive zvingwa.”" 
Matthew4:4 Asi akapindura, akati, “Kwakanyorwa kuchinzi, ‘Munhu haararami nechingwa bedzi, asi namashoko ose anobuda mumuromo waMwari.’ ”" 
Matthew4:5 Zvino Dhiabhori akaenda naye kuguta dzvene, akamumisa pachiruvi chetemberi," 
Matthew4:6 akati kwaari, “Kana uri Mwanakomana waMwari, uzviwisire pasi; nokuti kwakanyorwa kuchinzi, ‘Iye acharaira vatumwa vake pamusoro pako, Pamaoko avo vachakusimudza, Kuti urege kugumburisa rutsoka rwako nebwe.’ ”" 
Matthew4:7 Jesu akati kwaari, “Kwakanyorwawo, ‘Usaedza Ishe, Mwari wako.’ ”" 
Matthew4:8 Dhiabhori akamuisazve pagomo refu–refu, akamuratidza ushe hwose hwenyika, nokubwinya kwahwo;" 
Matthew4:9 akati kwaari, “Izvi zvose ndichakupa, kana ukawira pasi ukandipfugamira.”" 
Matthew4:10 Ipapo Jesu akati kwaari, “Ibva, Satani, nokuti kwakanyorwa kuchinzi, ‘Pfugamira Ishe, Mwari wako, umushumire iye oga.’ ”" 
Matthew4:11 Zvino Dhiabhori akamusiya, vatumwa vakauya vakamushandira." 
Matthew4:12 Jesu akati anzwa kuti Johani asungwa, akaenda Gareriya." 
Matthew4:13 Zvino, akabva Nazareta, akandogara Kapenaume pagungwa, munyika yeZabhuroni neNafitari;" 
Matthew4:14 kuti zviitike zvakarehwa nomuporofita Isaya, achiti," 
Matthew4:15 “Nyika yeZabhuroni, nenyika yeNafitari, Panzira yegungwa, mhiri kwaJodhani, Gareriya ravahedheni;" 
Matthew4:16 Vanhu vakanga vagere murima Vakaona chiedza chikuru; Navakanga vagere panyika yorufu nomumumvuri worufu, Chiedza chakavabudira.”" 
Matthew4:17 Kubva panguva iyeyo Jesu akatanga kuparidza, achiti, “Tendeukai, nokuti ushe hwokudenga hwaswedera pedyo.”" 
Matthew4:18 Akati achifamba paGungwa reGareriya, akaona varume vaviri, vana vomunhu mumwe, Simoni anonzi Petirosi, naAndireya munun'una wake, vachikandira usvasvi mugungwa, nokuti vakanga vari vabati vehove." 
Matthew4:19 Akati kwavari, “Nditeverei, ndigokuitai vabati vavanhu.”" 
Matthew4:20 Pakarepo vakasiya usvasvi hwavo, vakamutevera." 
Matthew4:21 Zvino akati apfuura mberi, akaona vamwe varume vaviri muigwa, vana vomunhu mumwe, Jakobho mwanakomana waZebhedhi, naJohani munun'una wake, vaina Zebhedhia, baba vavo, vachigadzira usvasvi hwavo, akavadana." 
Matthew4:22 Pakarepo vakasiya igwa nababa vavo, vakamutevera." 
Matthew4:23 Jesu akapota neGareriya rose, akadzidzisa mumasinagoge avo, achiparidza Vhangeri youshe, achiporesa zvirwere zvose zvavanhu." 
Matthew4:24 Mukurumbira wake wakanzwika kunyika yose yeSiria; vakauya kwaari navairwara vose, navakabatwa nezvirwere zvamarudzi mazhinji namarwadzo, navakanga vane mweya yakaipa, navakanga vane zvipusha, navakanga vakafa mitezo, akavaporesa." 
Matthew4:25 Vanhu vazhinji zhinji vaibva Gareriya, neDhekaporisi, neJerusaremu, neJudhiya, nemhiri kwaJodhani vakamutevera." 
Matthew5:1 Akati achiona vanhu vazhinji, akakwira mugomo; akagara pasi, vadzidzi vake vakaswedera kwaari." 
Matthew5:2 Akashama muromo wake, akavadzidzisa achiti." 
Matthew5:3 “Vakaropafadzwa varombo mumweya; nokuti ushe hwedenga ndohwavo. 
Matthew5:4 “Vakaropafadzwa vanochema; nokuti vachanyaradzwa. 
Matthew5:5 “Vakaropafadzwa vakapfava; nokuti vachagara nhaka yenyika. 
Matthew5:6 “Vakaropafadzwa vane nzara nenyota yoururami; nokuti vachagutiswa. 
Matthew5:7 “Vakaropafadzwa vane ngoni; nokuti vachaitirwa ngoni. 
Matthew5:8 “Vakaropafadzwa vane mwoyo yakachena; nokuti vachaona Mwari. 
Matthew5:9 “Vakaropafadzwa vanoyananisa; nokuti vachanzi vana vaMwari. 
Matthew5:10 “Vakaropafadzwa vanotambudzwa nokuda kwokururama; nokuti ushe hwedenga ndohwavo. 
Matthew5:11 “Makaropafadzwa imi, kana vachikuzvidzai, vachikutambudzai, vachikupomerai zvakaipa zvose nenhema, nokuda kwangu." 
Matthew5:12 Farai, mufarise kwazvo; nokuti mubairo wenyu mukuru kudenga; nokuti vakatambudza saizvozvo vaporofita vakakutangirai." 
Matthew5:13 “Imi muri munyu wenyika; asi kana munyu washapa, ucharungwa neiko? Hauchabatsiri chinhu, asi kurasirwa kunze, utsikwe navanhu." 
Matthew5:14 “Imi muri chiedza chenyika. Guta rakavakwa pagomo haringavanziki. 
Matthew5:15 Nomwenje havangautungidzi, vakauisa pasi pedengu, asi pachigadziko, uvhenekere vose vari mumba." 
Matthew5:16 Naizvozvo chiedza chenyu ngachivhenekere pamberi pavanhu, kuti vaone mabasa enyu akanaka, vakudze Baba venyu vari kudenga." 
Matthew5:17 “Musafunga kuti ndakauya kuparadza murairo kana vaporofita, handina kuuya kuzoparadza, asi kuzadzisa." 
Matthew5:18 “Nokuti zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, kusvikira denga napasi zvichipfuura, yota imwe kana tsanga imwe yoMurairo hazvingatongopfuuri, zvisati zvaitika zvose." 
Matthew5:19 “Naizvozvo ani naani anotyora mumwe wemirairo miduku iyi, akadzidzisa vanhu kuita saizvozvo, achanzi muduku muushe hwedenga; asi anoiita, akaidzidzisa, achanzi mukuru muushe hwedenga." 
Matthew5:20 “Nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Kana kururama kwenyu kusingapfuuri kwavanyori nokwaVaFarisi, hamungatongopindi muushe hwedenga.’" 
Matthew5:21 “Makanzwa kuti zvakanzi kuna vakare, ‘Usauraya; ani naani anouraya achapara mhosva ingatongwa;’" 
Matthew5:22 asi ini ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Anotsamwira hama yake achapara mhosva ingatongwa;’ anoti kuhama yake, ‘Raka’ achapara mhosva kumakurukota; anoti, ‘Benzi,’ achapara mhosva kuti atongwerwe Gehena romoto." 
Matthew5:23 “Naizvozvo kana iwe uchiuya nechipo chako paatari, ukarangarira ipapo kuti hama yako ine mhosva newe," 
Matthew5:24 usiye chipo chako ipapo pamberi peatari, uende, umbondoyanana nehama yako, ugozouya woisa chipo chako." 
Matthew5:25 “Kurumidza kutenderana nomudzivisi wako, uchiri munzira naye; kuti mudzivisi arege kukukwirira kumutongi, mutongi kumutariri, ukaiswa mujeri." 
Matthew5:26 “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwauri, haungatongobudimo, usati waripa kamari kwokupedzisira." 
Matthew5:27 “Makanzwa kuti zvakanzi, ‘Usaita upombwe.’" 
Matthew5:28 Asi ini ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Mumwe nomumwe anotarira mukadzi achimuchiva, atoita upombwe naye mumwoyo make." 
Matthew5:29 Kana ziso rako rorudyi richikugumbusa, uribvise, urirasire kure kwauri; nokuti zviri nani kwauri kuti mutezo wako mumwe ufe, muviri wako wose urege kukandirwa muGehena." 
Matthew5:30 Kana ruoko rwako rworudyi ruchikugumbusa, urugure ururasire kure kwauri, nokuti zviri nani kwauri kuti mutezo wako mumwe ufe, muviri wako wose urege kukandirwa muGehena.’" 
Matthew5:31 Zvakanziwo, ‘Ani naani anoramba mukadzi wake, ngaamupe rugwaro rwokumuramba.’" 
Matthew5:32 Asi ini ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Mumwe nomumwe unoramba mukadzi wake, kunze kwemhosva youpombwe, anomuitisa upombwe; ani naani anowana arambwa, anoita upombwe.’" 
Matthew5:33 “Makanzwawo kuti zvakanzi kuna vakare, ‘Usapika nhema, asi uripire Ishe pawakapika napo.’" 
Matthew5:34 Asi ini ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Musatongopika, kana nokudenga, nokuti ndicho chigaro choushe chaMwari;" 
Matthew5:35 kana nenyika, nokuti ndicho chitsiko chetsoka dzake; kana neJerusaremu, nokuti ndiro guta raMambo mukuru." 
Matthew5:36 Usapika kana nomusoro wako, nokuti haugoni kushandura ruvhudzi rumwe kuti ruve ruchena kana rutema.’" 
Matthew5:37 Asi shoko renyu rizoti, ‘Hongu,’ ave ‘hongu;’ ‘Kwete,’ ave ‘kwete;’ zvinopfuura izvozvo zvinobva kumuipi." 
Matthew5:38 “Makanzwa kuti zvakanzi, ‘Ziso rinotsihwa neziso, zino nezino.’" 
Matthew5:39 Asi ini ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Musadzivisa akaipa, asi anokurova padama rorudyi, umurinzire rimwewo.’" 
Matthew5:40 Kana munhu achida kukukwirira, kuti akutorere nguo yako yomukati, umutendere nenguo yokunzewo." 
Matthew5:41 Ani naani anokumanikidza kuenda maira imwe, uende naye mbiri." 
Matthew5:42 “Anokumbira kwauri mupe, usafuratira anoda kukwereta kwauri." 
Matthew5:43 “Makanzwa kuti zvakanzi, ‘Ida wokwako, venga muvengi wako.’" 
Matthew5:44 Asi ini ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Ida vavengi venyu, munyengeterere vanokutambudzai;" 
Matthew5:45 kuti muve vana vaBaba venyu vari kudenga; nokuti vanobudisira zuva ravo vakanaka nevakaipa vanonisira mvura vakarurama navasakarurama.’ 
Matthew5:46 Nokuti kana muchida avo vanokudai, muno mubairo weiko? Ko vateresi havaiti saizvozvowo here?" 
Matthew5:47 “Kana muchikwazisa hama dzenyu bedzi, munopfuura vamwe neiko? Ko vahedheni havaiti saizvozvowo here?" 
Matthew5:48 “Naizvozvo muve vakakwana, saBaba venyu vari kudenga vakakwana." 
Matthew6:1 “Chenjerai, kuti murege kuita kururama kwenyu pamberi pavanhu, kuti muonekwe navo; kana madaro hamuna mubairo kuna baba venyu vari kudenga." 
Matthew6:2 “Zvino kana uchipa varombo zvipo, rega kuridza hwamanda pamberi pako, sezvinoita vanyengeri mumasinagoge nomumigwagwa kuti vakudzwe navanhu. Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, vapiwa mubairo wavo." 
Matthew6:3 Asi iwe, kana uchipa zvipo, ruoko rwako rworuboshwe ngarurege kuziva chinoitwa norudyi rwako," 
Matthew6:4 kuti kupa kwako kuve pakavanda; ipapo Baba vako vanoona pakavanda vachakupa mubairo. 
Matthew6:5 “Kana muchinyengetera, musava savanyengeri, nokuti vanofarira kunyengetera vamire mumasinagoge napamharadzano dzemigwagwa dzomusha, kuti vaonekwe navanhu. Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, vapiwa mubairo wavo." 
Matthew6:6 “Asi iwe, kana uchinyengetera, pinda mumba mako, kana wazarira mukova wako, unyengetere kuna baba vako vari pakavanda; zvino Baba vako vanoona pakavanda, vachakupa mubairo." 
Matthew6:7 “Pakunyengetera kwenyu, musapamhidza zvisina maturo savahedheni; nokuti ivo vanofunga kuti vachanzwika nokutaura kwavo kuzhinji." 
Matthew6:8 Naizvozvo musafanana navo; nokuti Baba venyu vanoziva zvamunoshayiwa, musati makumbira kwavari." 
Matthew6:9 Zvino imi nyengeterai kudai: ‘Baba vedu muri kudenga, zita renyu ngarikudzwe." 
Matthew6:10 Ushe hwenyu ngahuuye, kuda kwenyu ngakuitwe pasi sokudenga." 
Matthew6:11 Mutipei nhasi zvokudya zvedu zvinotiringana. 
Matthew6:12 Mutiregerere mhosva dzedu sezvatinoregererawo vane mhosva nesu. 
Matthew6:13 Musatirege tichiedzwa, asi mutinunure pane zvakaipa. (Nokuti ushe ndohwenyu, nesimba nokubwinya, nokusingaperi. Ameni)’" 
Matthew6:14 Nokuti kana muchiregerera vanhu kutadza kwavo, Baba venyu vari kudenga vachakuregereraiwo." 
Matthew6:15 Asi kana musingaregerera vanhu kutadza kwavo, Baba venyu havangakuregerereiwo kutadza kwenyu." 
Matthew6:16 “Kana muchizvinyima zvokudya, regai kuva nechiso chinopunyaira, savanyengeri; nokuti vanoipisa zviso zvavo, vaonekwe navanhu kuti vanozvinyima zvokudya. Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Vapiwa mubairo wavo.’" 
Matthew6:17 Asi iwe, kana uchizvinyima zvokudya, zodza musoro wako, ugeze chiso chako;" 
Matthew6:18 kuti urege kuonekwa navanhu kuti unozvinyima zvokudya, asi kuonekwa naBaba vako vari pakavanda; zvino baba vako vanoona pakavanda, vachakupa mubairo." 
Matthew6:19 “Regai kuzviunganidzira pfuma pasi pano, pane zvipfunho nengura zvinopedza, napane mbava dzinopaza dzichiba." 
Matthew6:20 “Asi muzviunganidzire pfuma kudenga, pasina zvipfukuto nengura zvinopedza, pasina mbavha dzinopaza dzichiba." 
Matthew6:21 “Nokuti pane pfuma yako, nomwoyo wako uchavapowo." 
Matthew6:22 Mwenje womuviri iziso; zvino kana ziso rako rakanaka, muviri wako wose uchavhenekerwa." 
Matthew6:23 “Asi kana ziso rako rakaipa, muviri wako wose uchava rima. Zvino kana chiedza chiri mauri riri rima, rima iro iguru sei!" 
Matthew6:24 “Hapana munhu angashandire vatenzi vaviri; nokuti achavenga mumwe, akada mumwe; kana achafarira mumwe, akazvidza mumwe. Hamungashandire Mwari nemari." 
Matthew6:25 “Saka ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Regai kufunganya pamusoro peupenyu hwenyu, muchiti ndichadyei, kana ndichanwei; kana pamusoro pomuviri wenyu, muchiti, ndichapfekeiko?’ Upenyu hahupfuuri zvokudya here, kana muviri haupfuuri zvokupfeka here?" 
Matthew6:26 Tarirai shiri dzokudenga, hadzidyari, hadzikohwi, hadzitutiri mumatura; asi Baba venyu vari kudenga vanodzipa zvokudya. Imi hamudzipfuuri zvikuru here?" 
Matthew6:27 Ndianiko kwamuri angawedzera kubhiti rimwe paurefu hwake nokufunganya? 
Matthew6:28 “Munofunganyireiko pamusoro pezvokupfeka? Fungai maruva ebundo, kumera kwawo; haabati basa, haaruki;" 
Matthew6:29 asi ndinoti kwamuri, kuti kunyangwe naSoromoni pakubwinya kwake kwose, haana kushongedzwa serimwe rawo." 
Matthew6:30 “Zvino kana Mwari achifukidza saizvozvo uswa hwebundo, huripo nhasi, huchikandirwa muchoto mangwana, haangakufukidziyi nokupfuurisa imi vokutenda kuduku here?" 
Matthew6:31 “Naizvozvo musafunganya muchiti, ‘Tichadyei?’ Kana, ‘Tichanweyi?’ Kana, ‘Tichapfekeiko?’" 
Matthew6:32 Nokuti vahedheni vanotsvaka izvozvi zvose, nokuti Baba venyu vokudenga vanoziva kuti munoshayiwa izvozvi zvose." 
Matthew6:33 Asi tangai kutsvaka ushe hwaMwari, nokururama kwake; izvozvi zvose zvichawedzerwa kwamuri." 
Matthew6:34 Naizvozvo musafunganya pamusoro pezvamangwana; nokuti mangwana achazvifunganyira zvawo; zuva rimwe nerimwe rinokwanirwa nenhamo dzaro. 
Matthew7:1 “Musatonga, kuti murege kutongwa;" 
Matthew7:2 nokuti kutonga kwamunotonga nako, muchatongwa nako, nechiero chamunoera nacho, muchaerwa nacho." 
Matthew7:3 Unotarireiko kabanzu kari muziso rehama yako, asi hauoni danda riri muziso rako?" 
Matthew7:4 Kana ungataura seiko kuhama yako, uchiti, ‘Rega, ndibvise kabanzu muziso rako,’ izvo danda riri muziso rako?" 
Matthew7:5 Iwe munyengeri, tanga kubvisa danda muziso rako; ugoona kwazvo kubvisa kabanzu muziso rehama yako." 
Matthew7:6 “Musapa imbwa zvinhu zvitsvene, uye, musakanda mapera enyu pamberi penguruve, kuti dzirege kuatsika netsoka dzadzo, dzikatendeuka dzikakubvamburai." 
Matthew7:7 “Kumbira, muchapiwa; tsvakai muchawana; gogodzai, muchazarurirwa." 
Matthew7:8 “Nokuti mumwe nomumwe anokumbira anopiwa; anotsvaka anowana; anogogodza anozarurirwa. 
Matthew7:9 Munhu ndoupiko kwamuri, kana mwanakomana wake akakumbira chingwa, angamupa ibwe?" 
Matthew7:10 Kana akakumbira hove, angamupa nyoka?" 
Matthew7:11 Zvino kana imi makaipa muchiziva kupa vana venyu zvipo zvakanaka, Baba venyu vari kudenga vachapfuurisa seiko kupa zvinhu zvakanaka ivo vanokumbira kwaari!" 
Matthew7:12 “Saka zvinhu zvose zvamunoda kuti vanhu vakuitirei, muvaitire nemiwo saizvozvo, nokuti ndiwo murairo navaporofita." 
Matthew7:13 “Pindai nesuwo rakamanikana; nokuti suwo rakafara, nzira yakapamhamha, inoenda mukuparadzwa; vanopinda napo vazhinji." 
Matthew7:14 Nokuti suwo rakamanikana, nenzira inhete, inoenda kuupenyu, uye vanoiwana vashoma." 
Matthew7:15 “Chenjerai vaporofita venhema, vanouya kwamuri vane nguo dzamakwai, asi mukati ari mapere anoparadza." 
Matthew7:16 “Muchavaziva nezvibereko zvavo. Mazambiringa anombotanhwa paminzwa here, kana maonde parukato?" 
Matthew7:17 Saka izvozvo muti mumwe nomumwe wakanaka unobereka michero yakanaka, asi muti wakaipa unobereka michero yakaipa." 
Matthew7:18 “Muti wakanaka haungabereki michero yakaipa, nomuti wakaipa haungabereki michero yakanaka." 
Matthew7:19 Muti mumwe nomumwe usingabereki michero yakanaka, unotemwa, ukakandirwa mumoto." 
Matthew7:20 Saka muchavaziva nemichero yavo. 
Matthew7:21 “Havasi vose vanoti kwandiri, ‘Ishe, Ishe,’ vachapinda muushe hwokudenga; asi anoita kuda kwaBaba vangu vari kudenga." 
Matthew7:22 Vazhinji vachati kwandiri nezuva iro, ‘Ishe, Ishe, hatina kuporofita muzita renyu here?’ Nokudzinga mweya yakaipa muzita renyu here? Nokuita zvishamiso zvizhinji muzita renyu here?" 
Matthew7:23 Zvino ndichavaudza pachena, handina kutongokuzivai; ibvai kwandiri, imi vaiti vezvisakarurama." 
Matthew7:24 “Naizvozvo mumwe nomumwe anonzwa mashoko angu awa, akaaita, angafananidzwa nomurume akachenjera, akavaka imba yake paruware." 
Matthew7:25 “Mvura ikanaya, mvura zhinji ikauya, madutu akavhuvhuta, zvikarova imba iyo; ikasawa, nokuti yakanga yakavakirwa paruware." 
Matthew7:26 Mumwe nomumwe anonzwa mashoko angu awa, akasaaita, angafananidzwa nomurume benzi, akavaka imba yake pajecha." 
Matthew7:27 Mvura ikanaya, mvura zhinji ikauya, madutu akavhuvhuta, zvikarova imba iyo, ikawa, kuwa kwayo kukava kukuru.”" 
Matthew7:28 Jesu akati apedza mashoko iwaya, vanhu vazhinji vakashamiswa nokudzidzisa kwake;" 
Matthew7:29 nokuti akanga achivadzidzisa somunhu ane chiremera, asingaiti savanyori vavo." 
Matthew8:1 Akati aburuka pagomo, vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakamutevera." 
Matthew8:2 Tarira, munhu ana maperembudzi akauya kwaari, akamupfugamira, akati, “Ishe, kana muchida, munogona kundinatsa.”" 
Matthew8:3 Akatambanudza ruoko rwake, akamubata, akati, “Ndinoda; chinatswa!” Pakarepo maperembudzi ake akanatswa." 
Matthew8:4 Jesu akati kwaari, “Tarira, usaudza munhu; asi enda, uzviratidze kumupristi, ubayire chipo chakarairwa naMosesi, chive chapupu kwavari.”" 
Matthew8:5 Akati apinda Kapenaume, mumwe mukuru wezana akauya kwaari, akakumbira zvikuru kwaari," 
Matthew8:6 achiti, “Ishe, muranda wangu avete kumba, akafa mitezo, asi anotambudzika kwazvo.”" 
Matthew8:7 Akati kwaari, “Ndichauya kuzomuporesa.”" 
Matthew8:8 Mukuru wezana akapindura, akati, “Ishe, handina kufanirwa kuti mupinde mumba mangu; asi taurai henyu shoko rimwechete, muranda wangu achapora." 
Matthew8:9 Nokuti neniwo ndiri munhu anorairwa, ndina varwi pasi pangu; ndinoti kuno mumwe, ‘Enda!’ Anoenda; kuno mumwe, ‘Uya!’ Anouya; nokumuranda wangu, ‘Ita chichi!’ Anochiita.”" 
Matthew8:10 Jesu, akati achinzwa izvozvo, akashamiswa, akati kuna vakanga vachitevera, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, “Handina kumboona kutenda kwakadai, kunyangwe napakati paVaIsiraeri." 
Matthew8:11 Ndinoti kwamuri, vazhinji vachauya vachibva kumabvazuva, nokumavirira, vachagara naAbhurahamu, naIsaka, naJakobho, muushe hwedenga," 
Matthew8:12 asi vanakomana voushe vachabudiswa kurima rokunze; apo pachava nokuchema nokugeda–geda kwameno.” 
Matthew8:13 Zvino Jesu akati kumukuru wezana, “Enda uitirwe sokutenda kwako.” Muranda wake akapora nenguva iyo." 
Matthew8:14 Jesu, akati achipinda mumba maPetirosi, akaona vambuya vaPetirosi vavete, vachinzwa fivha." 
Matthew8:15 Akabata ruoko rwavo, fivha ikabva kwavari, vakasimuka, vakamushumira." 
Matthew8:16 Ava madekwana, vakauya kwaari navazhinji vaiva nemweya yakaipa; akabudisa mweya neshoko, akaporesa vose vairwara." 
Matthew8:17 Kuti zviitike zvakarehwa nomuporofita Isaya, achiti, “Iye akatora utera hwedu, akatakura zvirwere zvedu.”" 
Matthew8:18 Jesu, akati achiona vanhu vazhinji vakamukomba, akaraira kuti vayambukire mhiri." 
Matthew8:19 Zvino mumwe munyori akauya akati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, ndichakuteverai kwose kwamunoenda.”" 
Matthew8:20 Jesu akati kwaari, “Makava ana mwena, neshiri dzokudenga dzina matendere; asi Mwanakomana womunhu haana paangatsamidza musoro wake.”" 
Matthew8:21 Mumwe wavadzidzi akati kwaari, “Ishe, nditenderei henyu, ndimbondoviga baba vangu.”" 
Matthew8:22 Asi Jesu wakati kwaari, “Nditevere; rega vakafa vavige vakafa vavo.”" 
Matthew8:23 Akati apinda muigwa, vadzidzi vake vakamutevera." 
Matthew8:24 Ipapo dutu guru rikamuka mugungwa, nokudaro igwa rakafukidzwa namafungu; asi iye akanga avete." 
Matthew8:25 Zvino vadzidzi vake vakauya, vakamumutsa, vakati, “Ishe, tiponesei, tofa!”" 
Matthew8:26 Akati kwavari, “Munotyireiko, imi vokutenda kushoma?” Zvino akamuka, akaraira dutu negungwa; kudzikama kukuru kukavapo." 
Matthew8:27 Vanhu vakashamiswa, vakati, “Uyu munhu kunyi, zvaanotererwa nedutu negungwa?”" 
Matthew8:28 Akati asvika mhiri kunyika yavaGadhara, vanhu vaviri vaiva nemweya yakaipa vakasangana naye, vachibva kumakuva; vakanga vane hasha kwazvo kwazvo, naizvozvo kwakanga kusina munhu aigona kupfuura nenzira iyoyo." 
Matthew8:29 Zvino vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Tinemhaka yeiko nemi, Mwanakomana waMwari? Mauya pano kuzotitambudza, nguva isati yasvika here?”" 
Matthew8:30 Kwakanga kune boka guru renguruve dzakanga dzichifura kure navo. 
Matthew8:31 Mweya yakaipa ikakumbira zvikuru kwaari, ichiti, “Kana muchitibudisa, mutitumire kuboka renguruve.”" 
Matthew8:32 Akati kwairi, “Endai.” Ikabuda, ikapinda munguruve; boka rose rikamhanyira kumawere kugungwa, dzikafira mumvura." 
Matthew8:33 Ipapo vaidzifudza vakatiza, vakaenda kuguta, vakataura zvose, nezvakaitirwa vakanga vane mweya yakaipa." 
Matthew8:34 Zvino guta rose rikabuda kundosangana naJesu; vakati vachimuona, vakakumbira zvikuru kwaari kuti abve munyika yavo." 
Matthew9:1 Akapinda muigwa, akayambuka, ndokusvika kuguta rake." 
Matthew9:2 Zvino vakauya kwaari nomunhu akanga akafa mitezo achiona kutenda kwavo, akati kumunhu akanga akafa mitezo, “Mwana, tsunga mwoyo, waregererwa zvivi zvako.”" 
Matthew9:3 Zvino vamwe vavanyori vakati mumwoyo yavo, “Munhu uyu anoshonha Mwari.”" 
Matthew9:4 Asi Jesu achiziva mifungo yavo, akati, “Munofungireiko zvakaipa mumwoyo yenyu?" 
Matthew9:5 Nokuti Chiiko chakareruka, kuti, ‘Waregererwa zvivi zvako,’ kana kuti, ‘Simuka, ufambe?’" 
Matthew9:6 Asi kuti muzive kuti Mwanakomana womunhu ane simba panyika rokuregerera zvivi,” (akati kumunhu akanga akafa mitezo,) “Simuka, tora nhoo dzako, uende kumba kwako!”" 
Matthew9:7 Akasimuka, akaenda kumba kwake." 
Matthew9:8 Vanhu vazhinji vakati vachizviona, vakatya, vakarumbidza Mwari, akapa vanhu simba rakadai." 
Matthew9:9 Jesu akati achibvapo, akaona munhu, ainzi Mateu, agere panotereswa, akati kwaari, “Nditevere!” Ipapo akasimuka, akamutevera." 
Matthew9:10 Zvino akati agere pakudya mumba, tarira, vateresi vazhinji navatadzi vakauya vakagara pakudya naJesu navadzidzi vake." 
Matthew9:11 Zvino VaFarisi vachizviona, vakati kuvadzidzi vake, “Mudzidzisi wenyu anodyireiko navateresi navatadzi?”" 
Matthew9:12 Iye, achizvinzwa, akati, “Vasingarwari havatsvaki n'anga, asi vanorwara." 
Matthew9:13 Asi endai, mudzidze kuti ndokudiniko kuti, ‘Ndinoda ngoni, handidi chibayiro;’ nokuti handina kuuya kuzodana vakarurama, asi vatadzi.”" 
Matthew9:14 Zvino vadzidzi vaJohani vakauya kwaari, vakati, “Isu, naVaFarisi, tinozvinyimireiko zvokudya kazhinji, asi vadzidzi venyu havazvinyimi neiko?”" 
Matthew9:15 Jesu akati kwavari, “Shamwari dzemuwani dzingachema seiko muwani dzichinaye? Asi mazuva achasvika, achabviswa muwani kwavari; nenguva iyo vachazvinyima zvokudya." 
Matthew9:16 “Hakuna munhu anoisa chiremo chitsva panguo yakasakara; nokuti chakasonerwa chinobvarura nguo, buri rikanyanya." 
Matthew9:17 Havadiriwo waini itsva muhombodo tsaru, nokuti hombodo dzingaparuka, waini ikateuka, nehombodo dzikapararawo; asi vanodira waini itsva muhombodo itsva, zviviri zvose zvichengeteke.”" 
Matthew9:18 Akati achavaudza izvozvo, mumwe mukuru akasvikapo, akamupfugamira, akati, “Mukunda wangu afa ikozvino, asi uyai muise ruoko rwenyu pamusoro pake, ararame.”" 
Matthew9:19 Ipapo Jesu akasimuka, akamutevera navadzidzi vake." 
Matthew9:20 Zvino mumwe mukadzi, aiva nokurwara kwokubuda ropa makore ane gumi namaviri, akauya shure kwake, akabata mupendero wenguo yake;" 
Matthew9:21 nokuti akati nechomumwoyo, “Kana ndikabata nguo yake bedzi, ndichaponeswa.”" 
Matthew9:22 Asi Jesu akatendeuka, akamuona, akati, “Mukunda, tsunga mwoyo, kutenda kwako kwakuponesa.” Mukadzi akaponeswa kubva panguva iyo." 
Matthew9:23 Zvino Jesu akati asvika mumba momukuru, akaona varidzi venyere navanhu vazhinji vachiita mhere–mhere," 
Matthew9:24 akati kwavari, “Ibvai, nokuti musikana haana kufa, asi avete.” Vakamuseka." 
Matthew9:25 Asi vanhu vazhinji vakati vabudiswa, akapinda, akabata ruoko rwake, musikana ndokumuka." 
Matthew9:26 Mukurumbira wazvo ukapararira kunyika iyo yose. 
Matthew9:27 Zvino Jesu akati achibvapo, mapofu maviri akamutevera, akadanidzira, achiti, “Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, tinzwirei ngoni!”" 
Matthew9:28 Akati apinda mumba, mapofu akauya kwaari; Jesu akati kwaari, “Munotenda kuti ndinogona kuita izvozvo here?” Akati kwaari, “Hongu, Ishe!”" 
Matthew9:29 Zvino akabata meso avo, akati, “Muitirwe sokutenda kwenyu.”" 
Matthew9:30 Meso avo akasvinudzwa. Jesu akavaraira zvikuru, akati, “Chenjerai kuti zvirege kuzikanwa nomunhu.”" 
Matthew9:31 Asi vakabuda, vakamurumbidza munyika iyo yose." 
Matthew9:32 Vakati vachibuda, tarira, vakauya kwaari nomunhu akanga ari mbeveve aiva nomweya wakaipa." 
Matthew9:33 Mweya wakaipa ukati wabudiswa, mbeveve ikataura; vanhu vazhinji vakashamiswa, vakati, “Hakuna kumboonekwa zvakadai pakati paVaIsiraeri.”" 
Matthew9:34 Asi VaFarisi vakati, “Anobudisa mweya yakaipa nomukuru wemweya yakaipa.”" 
Matthew9:35 Zvino Jesu wakapota namaguta ose nemisha, achidzidzisa mumasinagoge avo, achiparidza vhangeri youshe, nokuporesa kurwara kwose noukosha hwose." 
Matthew9:36 Asi akati achiona vanhu vazhinji, akavanzwira tsitsi, nokuti vakanga vaneta, vakaraswa, samakwai asina mufudzi." 
Matthew9:37 Zvino akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Zvirokwazvo kukohwa kukuru, asi vakohwi vashoma." 
Matthew9:38 Naizvozvo kumbirai kuna Ishe wokukohwa kuti abudise vakohwi mukukohwa kwake.” 
Matthew10:1 Zvino akadanira kwaari vadzidzi vake vane gumi navaviri, akavapa simba pamusoro pemweya yetsvina kuti vaibudise, nokuporesa kurwara kwose noukosha hwose." 
Matthew10:2 Mazita avapostori vane gumi navaviri ndiwaya: Wokutanga Simoni, ainzi Petirosi, naAndireya, munun'una wake; Jakobho, mwanakomana waZebhedhi, naJohani munun'una wake;" 
Matthew10:3 Firipi naBhatoromiyo; Tomasi naMateu, muteresi; Jakobho, mwanakomana waArifeusi, naTadhiasi;" 
Matthew10:4 Simoni muKenani, naJudhasi Isikarioti, uya wakamupandukira." 
Matthew10:5 Ava vane gumi navaviri Jesu akavatuma, akavaraira achiti, “Musaenda munzira yavahedheni, musapinda muguta ravaSamaria;" 
Matthew10:6 asi zviri nani muende kumakwai akarasika eimba yaVaIsiraeri. 
Matthew10:7 Mufambe, muparidze, muchiti, ‘Ushe hwekudenga hwaswedera.’" 
Matthew10:8 Poresai vanorwara, mutsai vakafa, natsai vanamaperembudzi, budisai mweya yakaipa. Makangopiwa henyu, chingopai henyu." 
Matthew10:9 Musatora ndarama kana sirivha, kana ndarira muzvikwama zvenyu;" 
Matthew10:10 kana hombodo yorwendo, kana nguo mbiri, kana shangu, kana tsvimbo; nokuti mushandi akafanira kuti apiwe zvokudya zvake." 
Matthew10:11 “Muguta kana mumusha mamunopinda, bvunzai kuti ndiani arimo akafanira; mugarepo kusvikira muchibva." 
Matthew10:12 “Kana muchipinda mumba muikwazise. 
Matthew10:13 Kana imba yakafanira, rugare rwenyu ngaruuye pamusoro payo, asi kana isina kufanira, rugare rwenyu ngarudzokere kwamuri." 
Matthew10:14 Ani naani asingakugamuchirii, kana kunzwa mashoko enyu, kana muchibva paimba iyo kana paguta iro, muzunze guruva riri patsoka dzenyu." 
Matthew10:15 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, nyika dzeSodhoma neGomora dzicharerukirwa nezuva rokutongwa, kupfuura guta iro." 
Matthew10:16 “Tarirai, ndinokutumai samakwai pakati pamapere; saka chenjerai senyoka, mururame senjiva." 
Matthew10:17 Asi chenjerai vanhu, nokuti vachakuisai kumatare amakurukota, nokukurovai zvikuru mumasinagoge avo." 
Matthew10:18 Muchaiswawo pamberi pavabati namadzimambo nokuda kwangu, muve zvapupu kwavari nokuvahedheni." 
Matthew10:19 Asi kana vachikuisai, musafunganya muchiti, muchataura sei, kana tichataurei, nokuti muchapiwa nenguva iyo zvamunofanira kutaura." 
Matthew10:20 “Nokuti hamusimi munotaura, asi Mweya waBaba venyu anotaura mukati menyu." 
Matthew10:21 “Mukoma achaisa munun'una parufu, nababa mwana wavo; vana vachamukira vabereki vavo nokuvaurayisa." 
Matthew10:22 Muchavengwa navose nokuda kwezita rangu; asi anotsungirira kusvikira pakuguma, achaponeswa." 
Matthew10:23 Asi kana vachikutambudzai muguta rimwe, tizirai kune rimwe; nokuti zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Hamungapedzi maguta aVaIsiraeri, Mwanakomana womunhu asati asvika.’" 
Matthew10:24 “Mudzidzi haakundi mudzidzisi wake, kana muranda ishe wake." 
Matthew10:25 Zvakaringanira mudzidzi kuti ave somudzidzisi wake, nomuranda ave sashe wake. Zvavakaidza mwene weimba Bheerizebhuri, vachadaro zvikuru sei veimba yake!" 
Matthew10:26 “Naizvozvo musavatya; nokuti hakuna chinhu chakafukidzwa, chisingazozarurwi; kana chakavanzika, chisingazobudi pachena." 
Matthew10:27 Zvandinokuudzai murima, taurai pachena; zvamunonzwa munzeve, paridzirai pamusoro pedzimba." 
Matthew10:28 Musatya vanouraya muviri, asi vasingagoni kuuraya mweya; zvikuru mutye uyo anogona kuuraya mweya nomuviri zvose muGehena." 
Matthew10:29 Ko shiri duku mbiri hadzitengeswi nehafu yepeni here? Asi imwe yazvo haingawiri pasi kunze kwababa venyu. 
Matthew10:30 Kana murimi, nevhudzi romusoro wenyu rakaverengwa rose." 
Matthew10:31 Naizvozvo musatya; munopfuura shiri zhinji. 
Matthew10:32 “Mumwe nomumwe achandipupura pamberi pavanhu, neni ndichamupupurawo pamberi paBaba vangu vari kudenga." 
Matthew10:33 “Asi mumwe nomumwe anondiramba pamberi pavanhu, neni ndichamurambawo pamberi paBaba vangu vari kudenga." 
Matthew10:34 “Musafunga kuti ndakauya kuisa rugare panyika; handina kuuya kuisa rugare, asi kurwa." 
Matthew10:35 Nokuti ndakauya kupesanisa munhu nababa vake, nomwanasikana namai vake, nomukadzi womwana navamwene vake;" 
Matthew10:36 navavengi vomunhu vachava veimba yake. 
Matthew10:37 “Anoda baba kana mai kupfuureni, haana kufanireni; nounoda mwanakomana nomwanasikana kupfuureni, haana kufanireni." 
Matthew10:38 Asingatakuri muchinjikwa wake, akanditevera, haana kufanireni." 
Matthew10:39 Anowana upenyu hwake, acharasikirwa nahwo; asi anorasikirwa noupenyu hwake nokuda kwangu, achahuwana." 
Matthew10:40 “Anokugamuchirai imi, anondigamuchireni; noanogamuchireni, anogamuchira akandituma." 
Matthew10:41 Anogamuchira muporofita muzita romuporofita achapiwa mubairo womuporofita; noanogamuchira akarurama muzita roakarurama, achapiwa mubairo woakarurama." 
Matthew10:42 Ani naani unopa muzita romudzidzi mumwe wavaduku ava mukombe bedzi wemvura inotonhora anwe, zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, haangatongorasikirwi nomubairo wake.”" 
Matthew11:1 Jesu akati apedza kuraira vadzidzi vake vane gumi navaviri, akapfuura kundodzidzisa nokuparidza pamaguta avo." 
Matthew11:2 Zvino Johani, ari mutorongo, akanga anzwa mabasa aKristu, akatuma shoko navadzidzi vake," 
Matthew11:3 achiti kwaari, “Ko ndimi iye akanga achinzi anouya here, kana tichakatarira mumwe?”" 
Matthew11:4 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Endai, mundoudza Johani zvamunonzwa nezvamunoona;" 
Matthew11:5 zvokuti, mapofu anosvinudzwa, vanokamhina vanofamba, vana maperembudzi vanonatswa, vamatsi vanonzwa, vakafa navarombo vanoparidzirwa vhangeri." 
Matthew11:6 Akaropafadzwa iye asingagumburwi neni.” 
Matthew11:7 Ava vakati vachienda, Jesu akatanga kuudza vanhu vazhinji pamusoro paJohani, akati, “Makanga mabuda kundooneiko kurenje? Rutsanga runozununguswa nemhepo here?" 
Matthew11:8 Ko makanga mabuda kundooneiko? Munhu akapfeka nguo nyoro here? Tarirai, vanopfeka nguo nyoro vari mudzimba dzamadzimambo." 
Matthew11:9 Asi makanga mabudireiko? Kuzoona muporofita here? Hongu, ndinoti kwamuri, anopfuura kwazvo muporofita." 
Matthew11:10 Nokuti ndiye akanyorwa pamusoro pake, zvichinzi, ‘Tarira, ndinotuma munyai wangu pamberi pako, Achakugadzirira nzira yako pamberi pako.’" 
Matthew11:11 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, kuna vakaberekwa navakadzi, hakuna kumuka mukuru kuna Johani Mubhabhatidzi; asi muduku muushe hwedenga mukuru kwaari." 
Matthew11:12 Kubva pamazuva aJohani Mubhabhatidzi kusvikira zvino, ushe hwedenga hunopambwa, vapambi vanohutora nesimba." 
Matthew11:13 Nokuti vaporofita vose nomutemo zvakaporofita kusvikira kuna Johani. 
Matthew11:14 Kana muchida kuzvigamuchira, ndiye Eriya akanga achinzi anouya." 
Matthew11:15 Ane nzeve dzokunzwa, ngaanzwe." 
Matthew11:16 “Asi ndichafananidza rudzi urwu neiko? Rwakafanana navana vagere padare, vanodanidzira kushamwari dzavo, vachiti," 
Matthew11:17 ‘Takakuridzirai nyere, mukasatamba; takaungudza, mukasachema.’" 
Matthew11:18 Nokuti Johani akauya, asingadyi, asinganwi, zvino vanoti, ‘Ane mweya wakaipa.’" 
Matthew11:19 “Mwanakomana womunhu akauya, achidya, achinwa, zvino voti, ‘Tarirai munhu anokara, nomunwi, shamwari yavateresi navatadzi!’ Kuchenjera kwakaruramiswa namabasa ako.”" 
Matthew11:20 Zvino akatanga kutuka maguta makanga maitwa mabasa ake esimba mazhinji, nokuti haana kutendeuka, akati," 
Matthew11:21 “Une nhamo iwe, Korazini! Une nhamo iwe, Bhetisaidha! Nokuti mabasa akaitwa mukati menyu, dai aiitwa muTaya neSidhoni, vangadai vatendeuka kare vakaisa masaga nedota." 
Matthew11:22 “Asi ndinoti kwamuri, Taya neSidhoni acharerukirwa nezuva rokutongwa kupfuuremi." 
Matthew11:23 Iwe Kapenaume, uchasimudzirwa kudenga here? Uchaburukira kuHadhesi, nokuti dai iwo mabasa esimba akaitwa mukati mako, akaitwa muSodhoma, ringadai richipo nanhasi." 
Matthew11:24 “Asi ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Nyika yeSodhoma icharerukirwa nezuva rokutongwa kupfuura iwe.’ ”" 
Matthew11:25 Nenguva iyo Jesu akapindura, akati, “Ndinokutendai, Baba, Ishe wekudenga napasi, kuti makavanzira vakachenjera navakangwara zvinhu izvozvi, mukazvizivisa vacheche." 
Matthew11:26 Hongu, Baba, nokuti ndizvo zvakakufadzai." 
Matthew11:27 “Zvinhu zvose ndakazvipiwa naBaba vangu, hakuna anoziva Mwanakomana, asi Baba; hakuna anoziva Baba, asi Mwanakomana, naiye waanenge Mwanakomana achida kumuzivisa iye." 
Matthew11:28 “Uyai kwandiri, imi mose makaneta, makaremerwa, ini ndichakuzorodzai." 
Matthew11:29 Takurai joko rangu, mudzidze kwandiri; nokuti ndiri munyoro, ndinomwoyo unozvininipisa, kuti muwane zororo pamweya yenyu." 
Matthew11:30 Nokuti joko rangu rakanaka, nomutoro wangu unorerukira.”" 
Matthew12:1 Nenguva iyo Jesu akafamba napakati peminda yezviyo nomusi weSabata; vadzidzi vake vakanga vane nzara, vakapurura hura, vachidya." 
Matthew12:2 VaFarisi vakati vachizviona, vakati kwaari, “Tarira, vadzidzi vako vanoita zvisina kutenderwa nomusi weSabata.”" 
Matthew12:3 Asi akati kwavari, “Ko hamuna kurava here zvakaitwa naDhavhidhi, musi waakanga aziya, iye navakanga vanaye;" 
Matthew12:4 kuti akapinda mumba maMwari, akadya zvingwa zvokuratidza, zvakanga zvisina kutenderwa kudyiwa naye, navaiva naye, asi navapristi bedzi?" 
Matthew12:5 Ko hamuna kurava muMutemo, kuti neSabata vapristi vanotyora murairo weSabata mutemberi, vasina mhosva?" 
Matthew12:6 Asi ndinoti kwamuri, anokurira temberi ari pano." 
Matthew12:7 Asi dai maiziva kuti zvinoti kudini kuti, ‘Ndinoda ngoni, handidi chibayiro,’ mungadai musina kutonga vasina mhosva." 
Matthew12:8 Nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu ndiye Ishe weSabata.” 
Matthew12:9 Akabvapo, akapinda musinagoge ravo." 
Matthew12:10 Zvino tarira, kwakanga kuno munhu akanga anoruoko rwakakokonyara. Vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Zvakatenderwa kuporesa neSabata here?” Kuti vamupomere mhosva." 
Matthew12:11 Akati kwavari, “Ndiani kwamuri angava negwai rimwe, kana rikawira mugomba neSabata, angarega kuribata akaribudisa here?" 
Matthew12:12 Munhu anopfuura hwai zvikuru sei! Saka zvakatenderwa kuita zvakanaka neSabata.” 
Matthew12:13 Zvino akati kumunhu, “Tambanudza ruoko rwako!” Akarutambanudza, rukapora, rukava sorumwe." 
Matthew12:14 Zvino VaFarisi vakabuda, vakarangana pamusoro pake, kuti vangamuuraya sei." 
Matthew12:15 Jesu akati achizviziva, akabvapo; vanhu vazhinji vakamutevera, akavaporesa vose," 
Matthew12:16 akavaraira kuti varege kumuzivisa pachena," 
Matthew12:17 kuti zviitike zvakarehwa nomuporofita Isaya, achiti," 
Matthew12:18 “Tarira, muranda wangu wandakasanangura; Mudikanwi wangu, anofarirwa nomweya wangu, Ndichaisa Mweya wangu pamusoro pake, Iye achazivisa vahedheni kutonga." 
Matthew12:19 Haangarwi, haangaiti mhere–mhere; Hakuna munhu achanzwa izwi rake mumigwagwa." 
Matthew12:20 Rutsanga rwakapwanyika haangaruvhuni, Nomwenje unopwititika haangaudzimi, Kusvikira achiita kutonga kuti kukunde." 
Matthew12:21 Vahedheni vachaita zita rake tariro yavo.” 
Matthew12:22 Zvino vakaisa kwaari munhu aiva nomweya wakaipa, raiva bofu nembeveve; akamuporesa, naizvozvo mbeveve yakataura nokuonawo." 
Matthew12:23 Vanhu vazhinji vose vakashamiswa, vakati, “Ko uyu haasi mwanakomana waDhavhidhi here?”" 
Matthew12:24 Zvino VaFarisi vakati vachizvinzwa, vakati, “Munhu uyu haabudisi mweya yakaipa, asi naBheerizebhuri, muchinda wemweya yakaipa.”" 
Matthew12:25 Zvino Jesu achiziva kufunga kwavo, akati kwavari, “Ushe humwe nohumwe hunozvipesanisa, hunoparadzwa; neguta kana imba inozvipesanisa, haingamiri." 
Matthew12:26 NaSatani kana achibudisa Satani, anozvipesanisa; ushe hwake huchamira seiko?" 
Matthew12:27 “Neni, kana ndichibudisa mweya yakaipa naBheerizebhuri, ko vanakomana venyu vanoibudisa nani? Saka ivo vachava vatongi venyu." 
Matthew12:28 Asi kana ndichibudisa mweya yakaipa noMweya waMwari, ipapo hushe hwaMwari hwasvika kwamuri." 
Matthew12:29 “Munhu angapinda seiko paimba yaanesimba, akatora nhumbi dzake, kana asati ambosunga uya ane simba? Ipapo achaparadza imba yake." 
Matthew12:30 Asi neni, anopesana neni, noasingaunganidzi neni, anoparadza." 
Matthew12:31 “Naizvozvo ndinoti kwamuri, vanhu vacharegererwa zvivi zvose nokushonha, asi kushonha Mweya, havangaregererwi." 
Matthew12:32 Ani naani anotaura shoko rakaipa pamusoro poMwanakomana womunhu, acharegererwa asi anotaura shoko rakaipa pamusoro peMweya Mutsvene, haaregererwi, kana panguva ino, kana pane inouya." 
Matthew12:33 “Itai muti uve wakanaka, nemichero yawo yakanakawo; kana itai muti uve wakaipa, nemichero yawo yakaipawo; nokuti muti unozikanwa nemichero yawo." 
Matthew12:34 Imi, vana venyoka, mungagona seiko kutaura zvinhu zvakanaka, zvamuri vakaipa? Nokuti muromo unotaura zvizere mumwoyo." 
Matthew12:35 “Munhu akanaka anobudisa zvinhu zvakanaka papfuma yake yakanaka; nomunhu akaipa anobudisa zvinhu zvakaipa papfuma yake yakaipa. 
Matthew12:36 Ndinoti kwamuri, shoko rimwe nerimwe risina maturo rakarehwa navanhu, vachazvidavirira pamusoro paro nezuva rokutonga." 
Matthew12:37 Nokuti namashoko ako ucharuramiswa, uye namashoko ako uchapiwa mhosva.”" 
Matthew12:38 Zvino vamwe vanyori naVaFarisi vakapindura, vakati, “Mudzidzisi, tinoda kuona chiratidzo kwamuri.”" 
Matthew12:39 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Rudzi rwakaipa rwoupombwe runotsvaka chiratidzo, asi harungapiwi chiratidzo, asi chiratidzo chomuporofita Jona." 
Matthew12:40 Nokuti Jona sezvaakava mudumbu rehove huru mazuva matatu nousiku utatu, saizvozvo Mwanakomana womunhu achava mumwoyo wenyika mazuva matatu nousiku utatu." 
Matthew12:41 Varume veNinivha vachasimuka pakutongwa norudzi urwu, vacharupa mhosva, nokuti vakatendeuka nokuparidza kwaJona; asi tarirai, mukuru kuna Jona ari pano." 
Matthew12:42 Mambokadzi weZasi achasimuka pakutongwa norudzi urwu, acharupa mhosva, nokuti akabva pamagumisiro enyika kuzonzwa kuchenjera kwaSoromoni; asi tarirai, mukuru kuna Soromoni ari pano." 
Matthew12:43 “Zvino kana mweya wetsvina wabuda kumunhu unopota panzvimbo dzisina mvura, uchitsvaka zororo, uchirishayiwa." 
Matthew12:44 “Zvino unoti, ‘Ndichadzokera kumba kwangu kwandakabuda;’ asi uchisvika, unoiwana isina chiro, yakatsvairwa, yanatswa." 
Matthew12:45 Zvino unoenda, ndokutora mimwe mweya minomwe inoupfuura nokuipa, ndokupinda, ndokugaramo. Kupedzisira kwomunhu uyu kwakaipa kupfuura kutanga kwake. Zvichaita saizvozvowo norudzi urwu rwakaipa.”" 
Matthew12:46 Akati achataura navanhu vazhinji, tarira, mai vake navanun'una vake vakamira kunze, vachitsvaka kutaura naye." 
Matthew12:47 Mumwe akati kwaari, “Havo mai venyu navanun'una venyu vamire kunze, vachitsvaka kutaura nemi.”" 
Matthew12:48 Akapindura, akati kuna iye amuudza, “Mai vangu ndianiko, navanun'una vangu ndivanaaniko?”" 
Matthew12:49 Ndokutambanudza ruoko rwake kuvadzidzi vake, akati, “Tarirai, mai vangu navanun'una vangu!" 
Matthew12:50 “Nokuti ani naani anoita kuda kwaBaba vangu vari kudenga, ndiye mukoma nomunun'una, nehanzvadzi, namai kwandiri.”" 
Matthew13:1 Nezuva iro Jesu akabuda mumba, akandogara pagungwa." 
Matthew13:2 Zvino vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakaungana kwaari, nokudaro akapinda muigwa, akagaramo vazhinji vose vakamira pamhenderekedzo." 
Matthew13:3 Ipapo akavaudza zvinhu zvizhinji nemifananidzo, akati, “Tarirai, mukushi akabuda kundokusha." 
Matthew13:4 Zvino pakukusha kwake dzimwe mbeu dzakawira panzira, shiri dzikasvika dzikadzidya." 
Matthew13:5 Dzimwe dzakawira parukangarabwe, padzakanga dzisina ivhu zhinji, dzikamera pakarepo, nokuti dzakanga dzisina ivhu rakadzika." 
Matthew13:6 “Asi zuva rakati rabuda, dzikapiswa; dzikaoma, nokuti dzakanga dzisina mudzi." 
Matthew13:7 Dzimwe dzakawira muminzwa; minzwa ikamera, ikadzivhunga." 
Matthew13:8 “Asi dzimwe dzakawira muvhu rakanaka, dzikabereka vana; dzimwe zana, dzimwe makumi matanhatu, dzimwe makumi matatu.”" 
Matthew13:9 “Ane nzeve dzokunzwa, ngaanzwe.”" 
Matthew13:10 Zvino vadzidzi vakauya, vakati kwaari, “Munotaurireiko kwavari nemifananidzo?”" 
Matthew13:11 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Nokuti imi makapiwa kuziva zvakavanzika zvoushe hwedenga, asi ava havana kupiwa." 
Matthew13:12 Nokuti ani naani anazvo achapiwa, ave nezvakawanda; asi ani naani asina, achatorerwa kunyangwe nezvaanazvo." 
Matthew13:13 Naizvozvo ndinotaura kwavari nemifananidzo, nokuti vanoona, asi havaoni; vanonzwa, asi havanzwi, kana kunzwisisa." 
Matthew13:14 Kuporofita kwaIsaya kwakaitika kwavari, kunoti, ‘Kunzwa, muchanzwa, musingatongonzwisisi; Kuona, muchaona, musingatongoonesesi;" 
Matthew13:15 Nokuti mwoyo yavanhu ava yava mikukutu, Nzeve dzavo hadzinzwi zvakanaka; Nameso avo vakaatsinzina. Kuti zvimwe varege kuona nameso, Nokunzwa nenzeve, Nokunzwisisa nomwoyo, Kuti varege kupinduka Ini ndichivaporesa.’" 
Matthew13:16 “Asi meso enyu akaropafadzwa, nokuti anoona; nenzeve dzenyu, nokuti dzinonzwa." 
Matthew13:17 Nokuti zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, kuti vaporofita navakarurama vazhinji vakanga vachida kuona zvinhu zvamunoona, asi havana kuzviona; nokunzwa zvamunonzwa, asi havana kuzvinzwa." 
Matthew13:18 “Naizvozvo imi inzwai mufananidzo womukushi. 
Matthew13:19 Kana munhu akanzwa shoko roushe, asingarinzwisisi, muipi anosvika, ndokubvuta chakakushwa mumwoyo make. Ndiye akakushwa munzira." 
Matthew13:20 “Asi akakushwa parukangarabwe, ndiye anonzwa shoko, ndokurigamuchira pakarepo nomufaro." 
Matthew13:21 Asi haana mudzi mukati make, ndiye wechinguva chiduku; kana kutambudzika nokuvengwa zvichiuya nokuda kweshoko, pakarepo anogumburwa." 
Matthew13:22 Akakushwa pakati peminzwa, ndiye anonzwa shoko; zvino kufunganya kwenyika nokunyengera kwepfuma zvinounga shoko, rikashaiwa zvibereko." 
Matthew13:23 Akakushwa muvhu rakanaka, ndiye anonzwa shoko, akarinzwisisa; ndiye anobereka zvibereko, mumwe achiita zana, mumwe makumi matanhatu, mumwe makumi matatu.”" 
Matthew13:24 Akaisa pamberi pavo mumwe mufananidzo, achiti, “Ushe hwedenga hunofananidzwa nomunhu akakusha mbeu yakanaka mumunda make." 
Matthew13:25 Asi vanhu vavete, muvengi wake akauya, akakusha masawi pakati pezviyo, akaenda." 
Matthew13:26 Asi chipande chakati chamera nokubereka, zvino masawi akaonekwawo." 
Matthew13:27 Zvino varanda vomuridzi weimba vakauya, vakati kwaari, ‘Ishe, hamuna kukusha mbeu yakanaka mumunda menyu here? Munda wawanepiko masawi?’" 
Matthew13:28 Akati kwavari, ‘Munhu anondivenga aita izvozvo.’ Varanda vakati kwaari, ‘Ko munoda kuti tindoaunganidza here?’" 
Matthew13:29 Akati, ‘Kwete, zvimwe kana muchiunganidza masawi, mungadzura nezviyowo.’" 
Matthew13:30 “Regai zvikure zvose zviri zviviri kusvikira pakucheka; nenguva yokucheka ndichati kuvacheki, ‘Tangai kuunganidza masawi, muasunge zvimwanda kuti apiswe, asi mututire zviyo mudura rangu.’ ”" 
Matthew13:31 Akaisa pamberi pavo mumwe mufananidzo, achiti, “Ushe hwedenga hwakafanana netsanga yembeu yemasitadhi, yakatorwa nomunhu, akaidyara mumunda make;" 
Matthew13:32 iyo iduku kumbeu dzose, asi kana yakura, ihuru pamiriwo yose, inoita muti wakakura ukadaro kuti shiri dzedenga dzinouya, dzichigara mumatavi awo.”" 
Matthew13:33 Akavaudza mumwe mufananidzo, akati, “Ushe hwedenga hwakafanana nembiriso yakatorwa nomukadzi, akaiisa muzviero zvitatu zvoupfu, kusvikira hwose hwaviriswa.”" 
Matthew13:34 Zvinhu zvose Jesu wakaudza vanhu vazhinji nemifananidzo; haana kutaura chinhu kwavari asingafananidzi; 
Matthew13:35 kuti zviitike zvakarehwa nomuporofita, achiti, “Ndichataura nemifananidzo, Ndichataura zvakavanzika kubva pakuvambwa kwenyika.”" 
Matthew13:36 Zvino Jesu akati aendesa vanhu vazhinji, akapinda mumba, vadzidzi vake vakauya kwaari, vakati, “Tidudzirei mufananidzo wamasawi omumunda.”" 
Matthew13:37 Akapindura, akati, “Anokusha mbeu yakanaka ndiye Mwanakomana womunhu." 
Matthew13:38 Munda inyika; mbeu yakanaka ndivo vanakomana voushe, masawi ndiwo vanakomana vomuipi." 
Matthew13:39 Muvengi akakusha ndiye Dhiabhori; kucheka ndiko kuguma kwenyika; vacheki ndivo vatumwa vaMwari. 
Matthew13:40 “Zvino masawi sezvaanounganidzwa achipiswa mumoto, ndizvo zvichaitwa pakuguma kwenyika." 
Matthew13:41 Mwanakomana womunhu achatuma vatumwa vake, vagounganidza muushe hwake zvose zvinogumbusa, navanoita zvisakarurama," 
Matthew13:42 vachavakandira muvira romoto; ipapo pachava nokuchema nokugeda–geda kwameno. 
Matthew13:43 Ipapo vakarurama vachapenya sezuva muushe hwaBaba vavo. Ane nzeve dzokunzwa, ngaanzwe." 
Matthew13:44 “Ushe hwedenga hwakafanana nepfuma yakavanzwa mumunda, iyo yakawanikwa nomunhu, akaivanzazve; zvino nokufara kwake anoenda, akatengesa zvose zvaanazvo, akatenga munda uyo." 
Matthew13:45 “Ushe hwedenga hwakafananazve nomushambadzi anotsvaka mapera akanaka; 
Matthew13:46 akati awana pera rimwe rinomutengo mukuru, akaenda, akandotengesa zvose zvaakanga anazvo, akaritenga iro." 
Matthew13:47 “Ushe hwedenga hwakafananazve nousvasvi hunokandirwa mugungwa, hunounganidza marudzi ose ehove;" 
Matthew13:48 kana hwazara vanohukwevera pamhenderekedzo, vakagara pasi, vakaunganidzira dzakanaka mumidziyo, asi dzakaipa vanodzirasa." 
Matthew13:49 Ndizvo zvichaitwa pakuguma kwenyika; vatumwa vachabuda, vachabudisa vakaipa pakati pavakarurama," 
Matthew13:50 vachavakandira muvira romoto; ipapo pachava nokuchema nokugeda–geda kwameno.” 
Matthew13:51 (Jesu akati kwavari), “Manzwisisa izvozvo zvose here?” Vakati kwaari, “Hongu, Ishe.”" 
Matthew13:52 Akati kwavari, “Naizvozvo munyori mumwe nomumwe wakadzidziswa zvoushe hwekudenga, akafanana, mwene weimba, anobudisa zvinhu zvitsva nezvekare papfuma yake.”" 
Matthew13:53 Jesu akati apedza mifananidzo iyo, akabvapo." 
Matthew13:54 Akasvika kunyika yake, akavadzidzisa musinagoge ravo, nokudaro vakakatyamara, vakati, “Munhu uyu awanepiko kuchenjera uku namabasa esimba?" 
Matthew13:55 Ko haasi mwanakomana womuvezi here? Ko mai vake havazi Maria here, vakoma navanun'una vake havanzi Jakobho, naJosefa, naSimoni, naJudhasi here." 
Matthew13:56 Nehanzvadzi dzake hadzisi pakati patiri dzose here? Ko iye akagowanepi zvinhu izvozvo zvose?” 
Matthew13:57 Vakagumburwa naye. Asi Jesu akati kwavari, “Muporofita haangashayiwi kukudzwa, asi munyika yake, nomumba make.”" 
Matthew13:58 Akasaita mabasa esimba mazhinji ipapo nokusatenda kwavo. 
Matthew14:1 Nenguva iyo ishe Herodhi, akanzwa mukurumbira waJesu," 
Matthew14:2 akati kuvaranda vake, “Uyu ndiJohani Mubhabhatidzi; akamuka kuvakafa, saka masimba aya anobata maari.”" 
Matthew14:3 Nokuti Herodhi akanga abata Johani, akamusunga, akamuisa mutorongo, nokuda kwaHerodhiasi, mukadzi waFiripi, munun'una wake." 
Matthew14:4 Nokuti Johani akati kwaari, “Hauna kutenderwa kuti uve naye.”" 
Matthew14:5 Zvino akanga achida kumuuraya, asi akatya vanhu vazhinji, nokuti vaimuti muporofita." 
Matthew14:6 Asi zuva rokupemberera kuberekwa kwaHerodhi rakati rasvika, mukunda waHerodhiasi akatamba pamberi pavo, akafadza Herodhi." 
Matthew14:7 Naizvozvo wakamupikira nemhiko kuti, “Ndichamupa chipi nechipi chaanenge akumbira.”" 
Matthew14:8 Zvino iye, akati arayirwa namai vake, akati, “Ndipei pano mundiro musoro waJohani Mubhabhatidzi.”" 
Matthew14:9 Mambo akazvidya mwoyo, asi nokuda kwokupika kwake, uye nokuda kwavakanga vagere pakudya, akaraira kuti apiwe." 
Matthew14:10 Akatuma vanhu kundogura musoro waJohani mutorongo. 
Matthew14:11 Vakauya nomusoro wake uri mundiro, musikana akaupiwa; iye akaenda nawo kunamai vake." 
Matthew14:12 Vadzidzi vake vakauya vakatora chitunha chake, vakachiviga; ndokuenda kundoudza Jesu." 
Matthew14:13 Jesu akati azvinzwa, akabvapo negwa, akaenda kurenje ari oga. Zvino vanhu vachizvinzwa, vakabva kumaguta, vakamutevera netsoka." 
Matthew14:14 Zvino akati achibuda muigwa, akaona vanhu vazhinji zhinji, akavanzwira tsitsi, akaporesa varwere vavo." 
Matthew14:15 Zvino ava madekwana, vadzidzi vakauya kwaari, vakati, “Pano irenje, zuva roda kuvira, endesai vanhu vazhinji, vaende kumisha, vandozvitengera zvokudya.”" 
Matthew14:16 Asi Jesu akati kwavari, “Havafaniri havo kuenda; imi muvape zvavangadya.”" 
Matthew14:17 Vakati kwaari, “Hatina chinhu pano, asi zvingwa zvishanu bedzi nehove mbiri.”" 
Matthew14:18 Iye akati, “Uyai nazvo kuno kwandiri.”" 
Matthew14:19 Akaraira vanhu vazhinji kuti vagare pasi pauswa, akatora zvingwa zvishanu nehove mbiri, ndokutarira kudenga, akavonga, akamedura zvingwa, ndokupa vadzidzi vake, vadzidzi vakapa vanhu vazhinji." 
Matthew14:20 Vakadya vose, vakaguta; vakaunganidza zvimedu zvakasara, matengu ane gumi namaviri azere." 
Matthew14:21 Vakanga vadya vaiva varume vane zviuru zvishanu, vakadzi navana vasingaverengwi." 
Matthew14:22 Pakarepo wakagombedzera vadzidzi vake kuti vapinde muigwa, vamutungamirire mhiri, iye ndokusara kuendesa vanhu vazhinji." 
Matthew14:23 Zvino akati aendesa vanhu vazhinji, akakwira mugomo ari oga kundonyengetera; ava madekwana akanga aripo ari oga." 
Matthew14:24 Asi igwa zvino rakanga rava pakati pegungwa, richitambudzika namafungu, nokuti mhepo yakanga ichivadzivisa." 
Matthew14:25 Nenguva yechina yousiku akauya kwavari, achifamba pamusoro pegungwa." 
Matthew14:26 Zvino vadzidzi vakati vachimuona achifamba pamusoro pegungwa, vakavhunduka, vachiti, “Madzimudzangara,” vakaridza mhere nokutya." 
Matthew14:27 Pakarepo Jesu akataura navo, akati, “Tsungai mwoyo ndini, musatya.”" 
Matthew14:28 Zvino Petirosi akamupindura, akati, “Ishe, kana murimi, ndiraire kuti ndiuye kwamuri pamusoro pemvura.”" 
Matthew14:29 Iye akati, “Uya!” Petirosi akaburuka muigwa, akafamba pamusoro pemvura, akaenda kuna Jesu." 
Matthew14:30 Asi akati achiona mhepo ine simba, akatya; zvino akati otanga kunyura, akadanidzira achiti, “Ishe, ndiponesei!”" 
Matthew14:31 Pakarepo Jesu akatambanudza ruoko rwake, akamubata, akati kwaari, “Iwe unokutenda kuduku, wakona kutenda neiko?”" 
Matthew14:32 Vakati vapinda muigwa, mhepo ikanyarara." 
Matthew14:33 Ipapo vakanga vari muigwa vakamupfugamira, vachiti, “Zvirokwazvo, ndimi Mwanakomana waMwari!”" 
Matthew14:34 Vakati vayambukira mhiri, vakasvika panyika yeGenesareti." 
Matthew14:35 Varume venzvimbo iyo vakamuziva, vakatuma shoko panyika yose iyo yakapoteredza; vakauya kwaari navose vairwara;" 
Matthew14:36 vakakumbira zvikuru kwaari kuti vabate chete mupendero wenguo yake; vose vakabata vakaporeswa. 
Matthew15:1 Zvino VaFarisi navanyori vakauya kuna Jesu vachibva Jerusaremu, vakati," 
Matthew15:2 “Vadzidzi venyu vanodarikireiko tsika dzavakuru, nokuti havashambe maoko kana vachidya zvokudya?”" 
Matthew15:3 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Nemiwo munodarikireiko murairo waMwari nokuda kwetsika dzenyu?" 
Matthew15:4 “Nokuti Mwari wakati, ‘Kudza baba vako namai vako;’ uye, ‘Anotuka baba kana mai, ngaafe norufu.’" 
Matthew15:5 Asi imi munoti, ani naani anoti kuna baba vake kana mai vake, ‘Chinhu chipi nechipi chamaiti munobatsirwa nacho kwandiri, chava chipo kuna Mwari,’" 
Matthew15:6 haachakudzi baba vake kana mai vake, asi haane mhosva. Makatorera murairo waMwari simba netsika dzenyu." 
Matthew15:7 Imi vanyengeri, Isaya akaporofita kwazvo pamusoro penyu, achiti," 
Matthew15:8 ‘Vanhu ava vanondikudza nemiromo yavo, Asi mwoyo yavo iri kure neni." 
Matthew15:9 Asi vanondinamata pasina, Vachidzidzisa dzidziso nemirairo yavanhu.’ ”" 
Matthew15:10 Zvino akadana vanhu vazhinji kwaari, akati kwavari, “Teererai, munzwisise." 
Matthew15:11 Izvo zvinopinda mumuromo, hazvisvibisi munhu, asi zvinobuda mumuromo, ndizvo zvinosvibisa munhu.”" 
Matthew15:12 Zvino vadzidzi vakauya kwaari, vakati, “Munoziva kuti VaFarisi vakagumburwa vachinzwa shoko iri here?”" 
Matthew15:13 Akapindura, akati, “Muti mumwe nomumwe usina kusimwa naBaba vangu vari kudenga uchadzurwa.”" 
Matthew15:14 “Varegei; mapofu anotungamirira mapofu. Zvino kana bofu richitungamirira bofu, achawira mugomba ose ari maviri.”" 
Matthew15:15 Petirosi akapindura, akati kwaari, “Tidudzireiwo mufananidzo uyu.”" 
Matthew15:16 Iye akati, “Nazvino nemiwo muchigere kunzwisisa here?" 
Matthew15:17 Hamunzwisisi here kuti zvose zvinopinda mumuromo, zvinoenda mudumbu, zvikazoraswa kunze?" 
Matthew15:18 Asi zvinobuda mumuromo, zvinobva mumwoyo; ndizvo zvinosvibisa munhu." 
Matthew15:19 Nokuti mumwoyo munobuda mifungo yakaipa, nokuuraya, noupfeve, noupombwe, nokuba, nokupupura nhema, nokushonha Mwari;" 
Matthew15:20 ndizvo zvinosvibisa munhu; asi kudya namaoko asati ashamba, hazvisvibisi munhu.”" 
Matthew15:21 Zvino Jesu akabvapo, akaenda kumativi enyika yeTiya neSidhoni." 
Matthew15:22 Zvino, tarira, mukadzi muKenani akabva kunyika iyo, akadana, achiti, “Ndinzwirei ngoni, Ishe, Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi; mwanasikana wangu akabatwa kwazvo nomweya wakaipa.”" 
Matthew15:23 Asi haana kumupindura neshoko rimwe. Ipapo vadzidzi vake vakauya vakakumbira kwaari, vachiti, “Mumuendesei, nokuti anodanidzira shure kwedu.”" 
Matthew15:24 Asi akapindura, akati, “Ndakangotumirwa kumakwai akarashika eimba yaVaIsiraeri.”" 
Matthew15:25 Zvino akauya, akamupfugamira, akati, “Ishe, dondibatsirai henyu.”" 
Matthew15:26 Akapindura, akati, “Hazvina kunaka kutora chingwa chavana, ndokuchikandira mbwanana.”" 
Matthew15:27 Akati, “Hongu, Ishe, kunyangwe nembwananawo dzinodya zvimedu zvinodonha patafura ravatenzi vadzo.”" 
Matthew15:28 Zvino Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Haiwa, mai, kutenda kwako kukuru, zvaunoda ngazviitwe.” Mwanasikana wake akapora kubva panguva iyo." 
Matthew15:29 Jesu akati achibva ipapo, akaenda achitevedza gungwa reGareriya, akakwira mugomo, akagarapo pasi." 
Matthew15:30 Zvino vanhu vazhinji vakauya kwaari navanokamhina, nezvirema, namapofu, nembeveve, navamwe vazhinji, vakavaisa pamberi paJesu; akavaporesa." 
Matthew15:31 Naizvozvo vanhu vazhinji vakashamiswa vachiona mbeveve dzichitaura, nezvirema zvapora, navanokamhina vachifamba, namapofu achiona; vakarumbidza Mwari waVaIsiraeri." 
Matthew15:32 Zvino Jesu akadanira vadzidzi vake kwaari, akati, “Ndine tsitsi navanhu vazhinji ava, nokuti atova mazuva matatu avakagara neni vasina zvavangadya; handidi kuvaendesa vane nzara, zvimwe vangaziya panzira.”" 
Matthew15:33 Vadzidzi vakati kwaari, “Tichawanepiko murenje zvingwa zvakawanda zvakadaro, kuti tigutise vanhu vazhinji vakadai?”" 
Matthew15:34 Jesu akati kwavari, “Mune zvingwa zvinganiko?” Vakati, “Zvinomwe, nehove duku shomanana.”" 
Matthew15:35 Zvino akaraira vanhu vazhinji kuti vagare pasi; 
Matthew15:36 akatora zvingwa zvinomwe nehove, akavonga, akazvimedura, ndokupa vadzidzi vake, vadzidzi vakapa vanhu vazhinji." 
Matthew15:37 Vakadya vose, vakaguta; vakanonga zvimedu zvakasara, vakawana matengu manomwe azere." 
Matthew15:38 Vakadya vakanga vari varume vane zviuru zvina, vakadzi navana vasingaverengwi." 
Matthew15:39 Zvino akati aendesa vanhu vazhinji, akapinda muigwa, akasvika munyika yeMagadhani." 
Matthew16:1 VaFarisi navaSadhusi vakauya kuzomuedza, vakakumbira kwaari kuti avaratidze chiratidzo chinobva kudenga." 
Matthew16:2 Asi akapindura, akati kwavari, “Panguva yamadekwana munoti, ‘Kuchachena, nokuti denga rakatsvuka.’" 
Matthew16:3 Mangwanani munoti, ‘Nhasi kuchasviba, nokuti denga rakatsvuka, richifiduka. Munoziva kududzira zvinoonekwa mudenga, asi hamugoni kududzira zviratidzo zvenguva." 
Matthew16:4 Rudzi rwakaipa rwoupombwe runotsvaka chiratidzo, asi harungapiwi chiratidzo, asi chiratidzo chaJona.’ ” Ipapo akavasiya, akabva." 
Matthew16:5 Zvino vadzidzi vakaenda mhiri, vakakanganwa kutora zvingwa." 
Matthew16:6 Jesu akati kwavari, “Tarirai, muchenjere mbiriso yaVaFarisi navaSadhusi.”" 
Matthew16:7 Vakarangana pakati pavo, vachiti, “Anodaro, nokuti hatina kutora chingwa.”" 
Matthew16:8 Zvino Jesu, achizviziva, akati kwavari, “Imi vokutenda kuduku, munorangana pakati penyu nemhaka yeiko, kuti hamuna zvingwa?" 
Matthew16:9 Hamunzwisisi nazvino here, kana kurangarira zvingwa zvishanu zvavanhu vane zviuru zvishanu, namatengu amakawana kuti aiva mangani?" 
Matthew16:10 Kana zvingwa zvinomwe zvavanhu vane zviuru zvina, namatengu amakawana kuti aiva mangani?" 
Matthew16:11 Hamunzwisisi neiko, kuti handina kutaura kwamuri pamusoro pezvingwa? Asi muchenjere mbiriso yaVaFarisi navaSadhusi.”" 
Matthew16:12 Zvino vakanzwisisa kuti haana kutaura kuti vachenjere mbiriso yezvingwa, asi dzidziso yaVaFarisi navaSadhusi." 
Matthew16:13 Jesu akati asvika kumativi enyika yeKesaria Firipi, akabvunza vadzidzi vake, akati, “Vanhu vanoti Mwanakomana womunhu ndianiko?”" 
Matthew16:14 Vakati, “Vamwe vanoti, Johani Mubhabhatidzi; vamwe Eriya; vamwe Jeremiya, kana mumwe wavaporofita.”" 
Matthew16:15 Akati kwavari, “Ko imi munoti ndini ani?”" 
Matthew16:16 Ipapo Simoni Petirosi akapindura, akati, “Ndimi Kristu, Mwanakomana waMwari mupenyu.”" 
Matthew16:17 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Wakaropafadzwa iwe, Simoni Bhari–Jona, nokuti nyama neropa hazvina kukuzivisa izvozvo, asi Baba vangu vari kudenga." 
Matthew16:18 Neni ndinoti kwauri, ndiwe Petirosi, pamusoro poruware urwu ndichavaka Chechi yangu, masuwo eHadhesi haangaikundi." 
Matthew16:19 Ndichakupa kiyi dzoushe hwedenga; chinhu chipi nechipi chauchasunga panyika, chichasungwa kudenga, nechinhu chipi nechipi chauchasunungura panyika, chichasunungurwa kudenga.”" 
Matthew16:20 Ipapo akaraira vadzidzi vake kuti varege kuudza munhu kuti ndiye Kristu. 
Matthew16:21 Kubva panguva iyo Jesu akatanga kuzivisa vadzidzi vake, kuti anofanira kuenda Jerusaremu, kundotambudzwa zvizhinji navakuru navapristi vakuru navanyori, nokuurayiwa, nokumutswazve nezuva retatu." 
Matthew16:22 Petirosi akaenda naye vari voga, akatanga kumuraira, akati, “Mwari ngaakunzwirei ngoni, Ishe! Hamungaitirwi izvozvo.”" 
Matthew16:23 Asi wakatendeuka, akati kuna Petirosi, “Ndibvirepo Satani! Uri chigumburiso kwandiri, nokuti haurangariri zvinhu zvaMwari, asi zvinhu zvavanhu.”" 
Matthew16:24 Zvino Jesu akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Kana munhu achida kuuya shure kwangu, ngaazvirambe, atakure muchinjikwa wake, anditevere." 
Matthew16:25 Nokuti ani naani anoda kuponesa upenyu hwake, acharasikirwa nahwo; asi ani naani anorasikirwa noupenyu hwake nokuda kwangu, achahuwana." 
Matthew16:26 Nokuti munhu achabatsirwa neiko kana awana nyika yose, akarasikirwa noupenyu hwake? Kana munhu acharipeiko kuti adzikinure upenyu hwake?" 
Matthew16:27 Nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu achauya navatumwa vake nokubwinya kwaBaba vake; ipapo acharipira mumwe nomumwe paakashanda napo. 
Matthew16:28 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwauri, kuna vamwe vamire pano, vasingazonzwi rufu, vasati vaona Mwanakomana womunhu achiuya muushe hwake.”" 
Matthew17:1 Mazuva matanhatu akati apfuura, Jesu akatora Petirosi, naJakobho, naJohani munun'una wake, akaenda navo mugomo refu vari voga." 
Matthew17:2 Akasanduka pamberi pavo; chiso chake chikapenya sezuva, nguo dzake dzikachena sechiedza." 
Matthew17:3 Pakarepo Mosesi naEriya vakaonekwa navo, vachitaurirana naye." 
Matthew17:4 Zvino Petirosi akapindura, akati kuna Jesu, “Ishe, zvakanaka zvatiri pano; kana muchida, ndichavaka matumba matatu pano, rimwe renyu, rimwe raMosesi, rimwe raEriya.”" 
Matthew17:5 Akati achataura navo, tarira, gore rinobwinya rikavafukidza; izwi rikabva mugore, richiti, “Uyu Mwanakomana wangu unodikanwa, wandinofarira, mumunzwei.”" 
Matthew17:6 Vadzidzi vakati vachizvinzwa, vakawira pasi nezviso zvavo, vakatya zvikuru." 
Matthew17:7 Jesu akaswedera, akavabata, akati, “Simukai, musatya.”" 
Matthew17:8 Vakati vachitarira, havana kuzoona munhu, asi Jesu bedzi." 
Matthew17:9 Zvino vakati vachiburuka mugomo, Jesu akavaraira, akati, “Musaudza munhu zvamaratidzwa, kusvikira Mwanakomana womunhu amuka kuvakafa.”" 
Matthew17:10 Vadzidzi vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Vanyori vanotaurireiko, vachiti, Eriya anofanira kutanga kuuya?”" 
Matthew17:11 Akapindura, akati, “Eriya achauya hake, avandudze zvinhu zvose.”" 
Matthew17:12 Asi ndinoti kwamuri, “Eriya akatosvika, asi havana kumuziva; asi vakamuitira pavakada napo. Saizvozvowo Mwanakomana womunhu achabva otambudzwa navo.”" 
Matthew17:13 Zvino vadzidzi vakanzwisisa kuti akavaudza zvaJohani Mubhabhatidzi. 
Matthew17:14 Vakati vasvika kuvanhu vazhinji, mumwe munhu akauya kwaari, akamupfugamira, akati," 
Matthew17:15 “Ishe, donzwirai mwanakomana wangu ngoni, nokuti ane tsviyo, anotambudzika kwazvo. Nokuti kazhinji anowira mumoto, kazhinji mumvura." 
Matthew17:16 Ndakauya naye kuvadzidzi venyu, vakasagona kumuporesa.”" 
Matthew17:17 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Haiwa! Rudzi rusingatendi, rwakatsauka, ndichagara nemi kusvikira rinhiko? Ndichakuitirai mwoyo murefu kusvikira rinhiko? Uyai naye pano kwandiri.”" 
Matthew17:18 Zvino Jesu akamuraira, mweya wakaipa ukabuda kwaari, mukomana akapora kubva panguva iyo." 
Matthew17:19 Zvino vadzidzi vakauya kuna Jesu vari voga, vakati, “Ko isu takanga tisingagoni neiko kuubudisa?”" 
Matthew17:20 Akati kwavari, “Nemhaka yokutenda kwenyu kuduku, nokuti zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, kana muno kutenda kwakaita setsanga yemasitadhi, mungati kugomo iri, ‘Ibva pano, enda koko!’ Ringaenda hakuna chinhu chingakukundai.” [" 
Matthew17:21 Asi rudzi urwu runongobva chete nokunyengetera, nokuzvinyima zvokudya.]" 
Matthew17:22 Zvino vachafamba muGareriya, Jesu akati kwavari, “Mwanakomana womunhu achabva oiswa mumaoko avanhu;" 
Matthew17:23 vachamuuraya, asi nezuva retatu achamutswazve.” Vakafa neshungu kwazvo." 
Matthew17:24 Vakati vachisvika Kapenaume, vanhu vaigamuchira muripo wetemberi vakauya kuna Petirosi, vakati, “Mudzidzisi wenyu haateri mutero wetemberi here?”" 
Matthew17:25 Akati, “Hongu.” Zvino akati achipinda mumba, Jesu akatanga kutaura kwaari, achiti, “Simoni, unofungeiko? Madzimambo enyika anotora muripo nomutero kuna vanaaniko? Kuvana vavo kana kuvatorwa?”" 
Matthew17:26 Akati, “Kuvatorwa.” Jesu akati kwavari, “Saka vana vakasununguka." 
Matthew17:27 “Asi, kuti tirege kuvagumbusa, enda kugungwa, ukande chiredzo, ubate hove inotanga kudyira; kana washamisa muromo wayo, uchawana sitaterimo; uritore, uvape kuripira ini newe.”" 
Matthew18:1 Nenguva iyo vadzidzi vakauya kuna Jesu, vakati, “Ndianiko mukuru muushe hwedenga?”" 
Matthew18:2 Akadanira kwaari mwana muduku, akamuisa pakati pavo," 
Matthew18:3 akati, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, kana musingasanduki, mukava savana vaduku, hamungatongopindi muushe hwedenga." 
Matthew18:4 Naizvozvo ani naani anozvininipisa somwana uyu muduku, ndiye mukuru muushe hwedenga." 
Matthew18:5 Ani naani anogamuchira mwana muduku mumwe wakadai nezita rangu, anogamuchira ini." 
Matthew18:6 “Asi ani naani anogumbusa mumwe wavaduku ava, vanotenda kwandiri, zviri nani kwaari kuti guyo guru risungirirwe mumutsipa wake, anyudzwe mugungwa rakadzika." 
Matthew18:7 “Nyika ine nhamo nemhaka yezvigumbuso! Nokuti zvigumbuso zvinofanira kuuya hazvo; asi anenhamo munhu uyo anogumbusa vamwe. 
Matthew18:8 “Kana ruoko rwako kana rutsoka ruchikugumbusa, urugure, ururasire kure newe; zviri nani kwauri kuti upinde muupenyu uri chirema, kana uchikamhina, pakukandwa mumoto usingagumi, unamaoko maviri kana tsoka mbiri." 
Matthew18:9 Kana ziso rako richikugumbusa, uribvise, urirasire kure newe. Zviri nani kwauri kuti upinde muupenyu, uneziso rimwe, pakukandwa muGehena romoto, unameso maviri." 
Matthew18:10 “Chenjerai kuti murege kuzvidza mumwe wavaduku ava; nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, kudenga vatumwa vavo vanosiona misi yose chiso chaBaba vangu vari kudenga. [" 
Matthew18:11 Nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu akauya kuzoponesa charasika.] 
Matthew18:12 “Munofungeiko? Kana munhu anamakwai ane zana, rimwe rawo rikarasika, haangasiyi makumi mapfumbamwe namapfumbamwe, akaenda kumakomo kundotsvaka yarasika here?" 
Matthew18:13 “Kana aiwana, zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, anofarira kupfuura makumi mapfumbamwe namapfumbamwe dzisina kurasika." 
Matthew18:14 Nokudaro hakusi kuda kwaBaba venyu vari kudenga kuti mumwe wavaduku ava aparare. 
Matthew18:15 “Kana hama yako yakutadzira, enda umuudze mhosva yake, iwe naiye muri moga; kana akakunzwa, wadzora hama yako." 
Matthew18:16 Asi kana asinganzwi, tora mumwe kana vaviri newe, kuti mashoko ose asimbiswe nemiromo yezvapupu zviviri kana zvitatu." 
Matthew18:17 Kana asingavanzwi, uudze ungano; kana asinganzwiwo ungano, ngaave kwauri somuhedheni nomuFarisi." 
Matthew18:18 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, zvose zvamunosunga panyika, zvichasungwa kudenga; nezvose zvamunosunungura panyika, zvichasunungurwa kudenga." 
Matthew18:19 Ndinoti kwamurizve, kana vaviri venyu vakatenderana panyika pamusoro pechimwe chinhu chavanokumbira, vachachiitirwa naBaba vangu vari kudenga." 
Matthew18:20 Nokuti apo pakaungana vaviri kana vatatu muzita rangu, ndiripo pakati pavo.”" 
Matthew18:21 Zvino Petirosi akauya akati kwaari, “Ishe, hama yangu ichanditadzira kanganiko, ndakairegerera? Kusvikira kanomwe here?”" 
Matthew18:22 Jesu akati kwaari, “Handiti kwauri, kusvikira kanomwe; asi kusvikira makumi manomwe anoverengwa kanomwe." 
Matthew18:23 Saka ushe hwedenga hungafanana nomumwe mambo, akanga achida kugadzira mangava navaranda vake." 
Matthew18:24 Zvino akati achitanga kugadzira, mumwe akanga ane chikwereti chamatarenda ane zviuru zvamazana zvine gumi akaiswa kwaari." 
Matthew18:25 Asi akati achishayiwa chaangaripa nacho, ishe wake akarayira kuti atengeswe, iye nomukadzi navana, nezvose zvaakanga anazvo, kuti chikwereti chigoripwa" 
Matthew18:26 Zvino muranda akawira pasi, akakumbira, akati, ‘Ishe, ivai nomwoyo murefu neni, ndichazokuripirai zvose.’" 
Matthew18:27 Ishe womuranda uyo akamunzwira tsitsi, akamusunungura, akamuregerera chikwereti." 
Matthew18:28 “Asi muranda uyo akati achibuda, akawana mumwe muranda waishanda pamwechete naye, akanga ane chikwereti kwaari chamadhinari ane zana; akamubata, akamudzipa, akati, ‘Ripa chikwereti changu!’" 
Matthew18:29 Zvino muranda uyo aishanda pamwechete naye, akawira pasi, akakumbira zvikuru kwaari, akati, ‘Uve nomwoyo murefu neni, ndichazokuripira.’" 
Matthew18:30 “Asi iye akaramba, akaenda, akamuisa mutorongo, kusvikira achizoripa chikwereti." 
Matthew18:31 Zvino vamwe varanda vaishanda pamwechete naye vakati vachiona zvaitwa, vakafa neshungu kwazvo, vakaenda kundoudza ishe wavo zvose zvakaitwa." 
Matthew18:32 Zvino ishe wake akamudana, akati kwaari, ‘Iwe muranda wakaipa, ndakakuregerera chikwereti icho chose, nokuti iwe wakakumbira zvikuru kwandiri." 
Matthew18:33 Ko iwe hausi waifanira kunzwira tsitsi mumwe muranda unoshanda pamwechete newe, seni ndakakunzwira tsitsi here?’" 
Matthew18:34 Zvino ishe wake akatsamwa, akamuisa kuvarwadzi, kusvikira achizoripa chikwereti chake chose.”" 
Matthew18:35 Saizvozvo Baba vangu vari kudenga vachakuitiraiwo, kana asingaregerere mumwe nomumwe hama yake nomwoyo wose." 
Matthew19:1 Jesu akati apedza mashoko iwayo, akabva Gareriya, akaenda kunyika yeJudhiya mhiri kweJodhani." 
Matthew19:2 Vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakamutevera, akavaporesapo." 
Matthew19:3 VaFarisi vakauya kwaari, vakamuedza, vachiti, “Ko munhu anotenderwa kuramba mukadzi wake nemhaka ipi neipi here?”" 
Matthew19:4 Akapindura, akati, “Hamuna kurava here, kuti uyo akavasika pakutanga, akavaita munhurume nomunhukadzi?”" 
Matthew19:5 Akati, “Nokuda kwaizvozvo murume achasiya baba vake namai vake, akanamatira mukadzi wake; ava vaviri vachava nyama imwe." 
Matthew19:6 Nokudaro havachiri vaviri, asi vava nyama imwe. Zvino, izvo Mwari zvaakasanganisa, munhu ngaarege kuzviparadzanisa.”" 
Matthew19:7 Vakati kwaari, “Mosesi wakagorayireiko kuti murume amupe rugwaro rwokumuramba, agomuramba?”" 
Matthew19:8 Akati kwavari, “Nokuda kwoukukutu hwemwoyo yenyu Mosesi akakutenderai kuramba vakadzi venyu, asi kubva pakutanga zvakanga zvisina kudaro." 
Matthew19:9 Ndinoti kwamuri, ani naani anoramba mukadzi wake, asi nemhaka youpombwe, akawana mumwe, anoita upombwe; noanowana wakarambwa, anoita upombwe.”" 
Matthew19:10 Vadzidzi vakati kwaari, “Kana zvakadaro pakati pomurume nomukadzi, hazvina kunaka kuwana.”" 
Matthew19:11 Asi iye akati kwavari, “Vose havagamuchiri shoko iri, asi avo vakazvipiwa." 
Matthew19:12 Nokuti ngomwa dziripo, dzakaberekwa dzakadaro kubva mudumbu ramai; ngomwa dziripo, dzakaitwa ngomwa navanhu; ngomwa dziripo dzakazviita ngomwa nokuda kwoushe hwedenga. Angagamuchira shoko iri, ngaarigamuchire.”" 
Matthew19:13 Zvino vakauya navana vaduku kwaari, kuti aise maoko pamusoro pavo, avanyengeterere; vadzidzi vakavadzivisa." 
Matthew19:14 Asi Jesu akati kwavari, “Regai vana vaduku, musavadzivisa kuuya kwandiri; nokuti ushe hwekudenga ndohwavakadai.”" 
Matthew19:15 Akaisa maoko pamusoro pavo, akabvapo." 
Matthew19:16 Tarira, mumwe akauya kwaari, akati, “Mudzidzisi Wakanaka, ndingaita chinhu chakanaka chipi, kuti ndive noupenyu husingaperi?”" 
Matthew19:17 Akati kwaari, “Unondibvunzireiko pamusoro pezvakanaka? Aripo mumwechete akanaka. Asi kana uchida kupinda muupenyu, chengeta mirairo.”" 
Matthew19:18 Akati kwaari, “Ipiko?” Jesu akati, “Usauraya, usaita upombwe, usaba, usapupura nhema;" 
Matthew19:19 kudza baba vako namai vako, ude wokwako sezvaunozvida iwe.”" 
Matthew19:20 Jaya rikati kwaari, “Izvozvo zvose ndakazvichengeta; ko chipi chandinoshayiwa?”" 
Matthew19:21 Jesu akati kwaari, “Kana uchida kukwana, enda utengese zvose zvaunazvo, upe varombo, ugova nepfuma kudenga; ugouya unditevere.”" 
Matthew19:22 Asi jaya rakati richinzwa shoko iri, rikaenda rasuwa kwazvo; nokuti rakanga rine pfuma zhinji." 
Matthew19:23 Jesu akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, zvinoremera mupfumi kupinda muushe hwedenga." 
Matthew19:24 “Ndinoti kwamurizve, ngamera ingarerukirwa kupinda paburi petsono, kumupfumi kupinda muushe hwaMwari.”" 
Matthew19:25 Vadzidzi vakati vachizvinzwa, vakakahadzika kwazvo, vakati, “Ndianiko angagoponeswa?”" 
Matthew19:26 Jesu ndokuvatarira, akati kwavari, “Kuvanhu izvi hazvibviri, asi kuna Mwari zvose zvinobvira.”" 
Matthew19:27 Zvino Petirosi akapindura, akati kwaari, “Tarirai, isu takasiya zvose, tikakuteverai; tichagopiweiko?”" 
Matthew19:28 Jesu akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, imi makanditevera pakuberekwa kutsva, kana Mwanakomana womunhu achizogara pachigaro choushe chokubwinya kwake, imiwo muchagara pazvigaro zvine gumi nezviviri, muchitonga marudzi ane gumi namaviri aVaIsiraeri." 
Matthew19:29 Mumwe nomumwe akasiya dzimba, kana vakoma kana vanun'una, kana hanzvadzi, kana baba, kana mai, kana mukadzi, kana vana, kana minda, nokuda kwezita rangu, uchapiwa zvine zana, akagara nhaka youpenyu husingaperi." 
Matthew19:30 Asi vazhinji vokutanga vachava vokupedzisira, novokupedzisira vachava vokutanga." 
Matthew20:1 “Nokuti ushe hwokudenga hwakafanana nasaimba, akabuda mangwanani kundotsvakira munda wake wemizambiringa vashandi." 
Matthew20:2 Akati atenderana navashandi kuvapa dhinari pazuva, akavatuma kumunda wake wemizambiringa." 
Matthew20:3 “Akabuda nenguva inenge yechitatu, akaona vamwe vamire padare, vasina basa," 
Matthew20:4 akati kwavari, ‘Endai imiwo mumunda wemizambiringa, ndigokupai zvakafanira.’ Vakaenda." 
Matthew20:5 Akabudazve nenguva inenge yechitanhatu neyepfumbamwe, akadarozve." 
Matthew20:6 Akabuda nenguva inenge yegumi neimwe, akawana vamwe vamire; akati kwavari, ‘Makamirireiko pano zuva rose musina basa.’" 
Matthew20:7 Vakati kwaari, ‘Nokuti hapana nomunhu akatipa basa.’ Akati kwavari, ‘Endai nemiwo mumunda wangu wemizambiringa.’" 
Matthew20:8 Ava madekwana, mwene womunda wemizambiringa akati kumutariri wake, ‘Dana vashandi, uvape mubairo wavo, uchitanga kuno wokupedzisira, ugumire kune wokutanga.’" 
Matthew20:9 “Zvino venguva inenge yegumi neimwe vakati vachiuya, mumwe nomumwe akapiwa dhinari." 
Matthew20:10 Vokutanga vakati vachiuya, vakafunga kuti tichapiwa kupfuura; ivo vakapiwawo mumwe nomumwe dhinari." 
Matthew20:11 Vakati vachipiwa, vakapopotera saimba," 
Matthew20:12 vakati, ‘Ava vokupedzisira, vakashanda awa imwechete, mavaenzanisa nesu, takatambudzika zuva rose, tichipiswa nezuva.’" 
Matthew20:13 Akapindura, akati kuno mumwe wavo, ‘Shamwari, handikuitiri zvisakarurama; hauna kutenderana neni kuti upiwe dhinari here?" 
Matthew20:14 Tora zvako, uende, ndinoda kupa vokupedzisira sewe." 
Matthew20:15 Ko handina kutenderwa kuita pandinoda napo here? Ziso rako rakaipa, nokuti ini ndakanaka here?’ ”" 
Matthew20:16 “Saizvozvo vokupedzisira vachava vokutanga, novokutanga vachava vokupedzisira.”" 
Matthew20:17 Jesu akati okwira Jerusaremu, akatora vadzidzi vake vane gumi navaviri vari voga. Akati kwavari panzira,"
