Matthew20:18 “Tarirai, tinokwira Jerusaremu, Mwanakomana womunhu achaiswa kuvapristi vakuru navanyori, vachamutongera rufu." 
Matthew20:19 “Vachamuisa kuvahedheni, kuti asekwe, arohwe, aroverwe pamuchinjikwa, asi nezuva retatu achamutswazve.”" 
Matthew20:20 Zvino mai vevanakomana vaZebhedhi vakauya kwaari navanakomana vavo, vachimupfugamira, kuzokumbira chinhu kwaari." 
Matthew20:21 Akati kwavari, “Munotsvakeiko?” Vakati kwaari, “Rayirai, kuti vanakomana vangu ava vaviri vagare, mumwe kurudyi rwenyu, mumwe kuruboshwe, muushe hwenyu.”" 
Matthew20:22 Asi Jesu akapindura, akati, “Hamuzivi zvamunokumbira. Mungagona kunwira mukombe pandinozonwira ini, here?” Vakati kwaari, “Tingagona.”" 
Matthew20:23 Akati kwavari, “Muchanwira henyu mukombe wangu, asi kugara kurudyi, nokuruboshwe, handisini ndinopa, asi ndezvavakazvigadzirirwa izvo naBaba vangu.”" 
Matthew20:24 Vane gumi vakati vachizvinzwa, vakatsamwira avo vaviri vana vomunhu mumwe." 
Matthew20:25 Asi Jesu akavadanira kwaari, akati, “Munoziva kuti machinda avahedheni anovarayira, navakuru vavo vanoita simba navo." 
Matthew20:26 Pakati penyu ngazvirege kuva kudaro; asi ani naani anoda kuva mukuru pakati penyu, ngaave mushandiri wenyu." 
Matthew20:27 Ani naani anoda kuva wokutanga pakati penyu, ngaave muranda wenyu." 
Matthew20:28 Zvakaita soMwanakomana womunhu asina kuuya kuzoshandirwa, asi kushandira, nokupa upenyu hwake ruve rudzikinuro rwavazhinji.”" 
Matthew20:29 Vakati vachibva Jeriko, vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakamutevera." 
Matthew20:30 Zvino tarira, mapofu maviri akanga agere panzira, akati achinzwa kuti Jesu opfuura, akadanidzira, achiti, “Ishe, Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, tinzwirei ngoni!”" 
Matthew20:31 Vanhu vazhinji vakaarayira kuti anyarare; asi akanyanya kudanidzira, achiti, “Ishe, Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, tinzwirei ngoni!”" 
Matthew20:32 Ipapo Jesu akamira, akaadana, akati, “Munoda kuti ndikuitireiko?”" 
Matthew20:33 Akati kwaari, “Ishe, kuti meso edu asvinudzwe.”" 
Matthew20:34 Jesu akaanzwira tsitsi, akabata meso awo; pakarepo akasvinudzwa, akamutevera." 
Matthew21:1 Vakati vachisvika Bhetifage, pagomo reMiorivhi, Jesu akatuma vadzidzi vaviri," 
Matthew21:2 akati kwavari, “Endai kumusha wakatarisana nemi, pakarepo muchawana dhongi nemwana waro akasungirirwa, murisunungure, muuye naro kwandiri." 
Matthew21:3 Kana ani naani achitaura chinhu kwamuri, muti, ‘Ishe anorida;’ pakarepo acharidzosa.”" 
Matthew21:4 Izvozvo zvakaitwa, kuti zvakataurwa nomuporofita zviitike, paakati," 
Matthew21:5 “Udzai mwanasikana weZioni, Tarira Mambo wako anouya kwauri, Ari munyoro, akatasva dhongi, Nemhuru yechipfuwo chinokweva.”" 
Matthew21:6 Vadzidzi vakaenda, vakaita sezvavakarairwa naJesu," 
Matthew21:7 vakauya nedhongi nemwana waro, vakaisa nguo dzavo pamusoro paro; Jesu ndokuritasva." 
Matthew21:8 Vazhinji pakati pavanhu vakawarira nguo dzavo munzira; vamwe vakatema matavi emiti vakaawarira munzira. 
Matthew21:9 Vanhu vazhinji vakanga vakamutungamirira, navakanga vachitevera, vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Hosana kuMwanakomana waDhavhidhi! Ngaakudzwe iye anouya muzita raIshe! Hosana kumusoro–soro!”" 
Matthew21:10 Akati apinda Jerusaremu, guta rose rikapesaniswa, vanhu vakati, “Uyu ndianiko?”" 
Matthew21:11 Vanhu vazhinji vakati, “NdiJesu muporofita weNazareta reGareriya.”" 
Matthew21:12 Zvino Jesu akapinda mutemberi, akabudisa vose vaitengesa navaitenga mutemberi; akawisa matafura avaitsinhanhisa mari, nezvigaro zvavaitengesa njiva," 
Matthew21:13 akati kwavari, “Kwakanyorwa kuchinzi, ‘Imba yangu ichanzi imba yokunyengetera,’ asi imi munoiita bako ramakororo.”" 
Matthew21:14 Zvino mapofu navaikamhinha vakauya kwaari mutemberi akavaporesa. 
Matthew21:15 Asi vapristi vakuru navanyori vakati vachiona zvinoshamisa zvaakanga achiita, navana vachidanidzira mutemberi, vachiti, “Hosana Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi!” Vakafa neshungu," 
Matthew21:16 vakati kwaari, “Unonzwa zvavanotaura ivavo here?” Jesu akati kwavari, “Hongu,” hamuna kutongorava here, panoti, “Mumiromo yavacheche navanomwa makakwanisa kukudza?”" 
Matthew21:17 Akavasiya, akabva muguta, akaenda Bhetania, kwaakandovata." 
Matthew21:18 Mangwanani akati achidzokera kuguta, akanzwa nzara." 
Matthew21:19 Zvino, akati achiona muonde mumwe panzira, akaenda kwauri, akasawana chinhu kwauri, asi mashizha bedzi; akati kwauri, “Ngakurege kuva nemichero kwauri nokusingaperi.” Muonde ukaoma pakarepo." 
Matthew21:20 Vadzidzi vakati vachizviona, vakashamiswa, vakati, “Muonde waoma pakarepo seiko?”" 
Matthew21:21 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, dai maiva nokutenda, musinganyunyuti, hamungaiti izvi zvomuonde bedzi, asi kana mukati kugomo iri, ‘Simudzwa, ukandirwe mugungwa,’ zvichaitwa." 
Matthew21:22 Nezvose zvamunokumbira muchinyengetera, kana muchitenda, muchazvipiwa.”" 
Matthew21:23 Akati achipinda mutemberi, vapristi vakuru navakuru vavanhu vakauya kwaari achidzidzisa, vakati, “Munoita zvinhu izvozvi nesimba ripiko? Ndiani akakupai simba iri?”" 
Matthew21:24 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Neni ndichakubvunzaiwo shoko rimwe; kana mukandiudza iro, neni ndichakuudzaiwo simba randinoita naro zvinhu izvi." 
Matthew21:25 “Rubhabhatidzo rwaJohani rwakabvepiko? Kudenga kana kuvanhu here?” Vakataurirana vachiti, “Kana tikati, ‘Kudenga,’ uchati kwatiri, ‘Makagoregerei kumutenda?’" 
Matthew21:26 Asi kana tikati, ‘Kuvanhu,’ tinotya vanhu vazhinji; nokuti vose vanoti, Johani muporofita.”" 
Matthew21:27 Vakapindura, vakati kuna Jesu, “Hatizivi.” Akati kwavari, “Neni handingakuudziyiwo simba randinoita naro zvinhu izvi." 
Matthew21:28 “Zvino munofungeiko? Mumwe munhu akanga ana vana vaviri; akaenda kuno wokutanga, akati, ‘Mwana, enda nhasi undoshanda mumunda wangu wemizambiringa.’" 
Matthew21:29 Iye akapindura, akati, ‘Handidi;’ asi pashure akazvidya mwoyo, akaenda." 
Matthew21:30 Akaenda kuno wechipiri, akataura saizvozvo. Iye akapindura, akati, ‘Ndinoenda, ishe;’ akasaenda." 
Matthew21:31 “Ndoupiko kuna ivavo vaviri akaita kuda kwababa vake?” Vakati, “Wokutanga.” Jesu akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, vateresi nezvipfeve vanokutangirai kupinda muushe hwaMwari." 
Matthew21:32 Nokuti Johani akauya kwamuri nenzira yokururama, mukasamutenda, asi vateresi nezvipfeve vakamutenda. Imi makati muchiona izvozvo, hamuna kuzopinduka mukamutenda." 
Matthew21:33 “Inzwai mumwe mufananidzo, kwaiva nomunhu aivapo, saimba, akasima munda wake wemizambiringa; akaukomberedza noruzhowa, akachera guvi rokusvinira mauri, akavaka chirindo chirefu, akaupa varimi, ndokufamba rwendo." 
Matthew21:34 “Nguva yemichero yakati yosvika, akatuma varanda vake kuvarimi, kundopiwa michero yake." 
Matthew21:35 Asi varimi vakabata varanda vake, vakarova mumwe, vakauraya mumwe, vakataka mumwe namabwe." 
Matthew21:36 Akatumazve vamwe varanda, vazhinji kukunda wokutanga; vakavaitira saizvozvo." 
Matthew21:37 Zvino pashure akatuma mwanakomana wake kwavari, achiti, ‘Mwanakomana wangu vachava nehanya naye.’" 
Matthew21:38 Asi varimi vakati vachiona mwanakomana, vakataurirana, vachiti, ‘Uyu ndiye mugari wenhaka; uyai timuuraye, titore nhaka yake.’" 
Matthew21:39 Zvino vakamubata vakamubudisa kunze kwomunda wemizambiringa, vakamuuraya." 
Matthew21:40 “Zvino kana tenzi womunda wemizambiringa achizouya, achaiteiko navarimi ivavo?”" 
Matthew21:41 Vakati kwaari, “Achaparadza kwazvo vanhu avo vakaipa, akaisa vamwe varimi mumunda wemizambiringa, vachazomupa michero nenguva yavo.”" 
Matthew21:42 Jesu akati kwavari, “Hamuna kutongorava here muMagwaro paye panoti: Ibwe rakaraswa navavaki, Ndiro rakazova musoro wekona; Izvozvo zvakaitwa naIshe, Zvinoshamisa pameso edu?”" 
Matthew21:43 Naizvozvo ndinoti kwamuri, muchatorerwa imi ushe hwaMwari, hukapiwa vanhu vanobereka michero yahwo. [" 
Matthew21:44 “Anowira pamusoro pebwe iri, achapwanyika asi richaparadza warinowira.”]" 
Matthew21:45 Vapristi vakuru naVaFarisi vakati vachinzwa mifananidzo yake, vakaziva kuti anovareva ivo." 
Matthew21:46 Zvino vakatsvaka kumubata, asi vakatya vanhu vazhinji, nokuti vakanga vachiti muporofita." 
Matthew22:1 Zvino Jesu akapindura, akataurazve navo nemifananidzo, akati,"

Matthew22:3 akatuma varanda vake kundodana avo vakanga vakokerwa kumutambo wokuchata; vakaramba kuuya. 
Matthew22:4 Akatumazve vamwe varanda, akati, ‘Udzai vakakokwa, muti, tarirai, ndagadzira mabiko angu; nzombe dzangu nezvakakora zvangu zvabayiwa, zvinhu zvose zvagadzirwa; uyai kumutambo wokuchata.’" 
Matthew22:5 Asi havana kurangarira, vakaenda, mumwe kumunda wake, mumwe kukutengesa kwake;" 
Matthew22:6 vamwe vakabata varanda vake, vakavaitira zvakaipa, vakavauraya." 
Matthew22:7 Zvino mambo akatsamwa, akatuma hondo dzake, akaparadza vaya vakauraya, varanda vake akapisa guta ravo." 
Matthew22:8 “Zvino akati kuvaranda vake, ‘Mutambo wokuchata wakagadzirwa, asi vakanga vakokerwa vakanga vasina kufanirwa." 
Matthew22:9 Naizvozvo, endai kumharadzano dzenzira, mukokere kumutambo vose vamunowana.’" 
Matthew22:10 Varanda ivavo vakaenda kunzira, vakaunganidza vose vavakawana, vakaipa navakanaka; imba yomuchato ikazara navagere pakudya." 
Matthew22:11 “Zvino mambo akati achipinda kuzoona vagere pakudya, akaona munhu asina kupfeka nguo yomuchato;" 
Matthew22:12 akati kwaari, ‘Shamwari, wapinda pano seiko, usina nguo yomuchato?’ ” Akanyarara." 
Matthew22:13 Zvino mambo akati kuvaranda, “Musungei makumbo namaoko, mumukandirei kunze murima; apo pachava nokuchema nokugeda–geda kwameno.”" 
Matthew22:14 “Nokuti vazhinji vakadanwa, asi vakasanangurwa vashoma.”" 
Matthew22:15 Zvino VaFarisi vakaenda kundorangana kuti vangamubata sei pakutaura kwake. 
Matthew22:16 Vakatuma kwaari vadzidzi vavo navaHerodhi, vachiti, “Mudzidzisi, tinoziva kuti ndimi wechokwadi, munodzidzisa nzira yaMwari nechokwadi, musingarangariri zvinoonekwa zvomunhu; nokuti hamutariri zviri kunze kwomunhu." 
Matthew22:17 Zvino tiudzei, munofungeiko? Munhu anotenderwa kutera mutero waKesari here, kana kwete?”" 
Matthew22:18 Asi Jesu akaziva kuipa kwavo, akati, “Munondiedzereiko, imi vanyengeri?" 
Matthew22:19 Ndiratidzei mari yomutero.” Vakauya kwaari nedhinari. 
Matthew22:20 Zvino akati kwavari, “Mufananidzo uyu norunyoro urwu ndezvaani?”" 
Matthew22:21 Vakati kwaari, “ZvaKesari.” Akati kwavari, “Naizvozvo, ipai Kesari zvaKesari, naMwari zvaMwari.”" 
Matthew22:22 Vakati vachinzwa izvozvo, vakashamiswa, vakamusiya, vakaenda." 
Matthew22:23 Nezuva iro vaSadhusi vakasvika kwaari, ivo vanoti hakuna kumuka kwavakafa, vakamubvunza," 
Matthew22:24 vachiti, “Mudzidzisi, Mosesi akati, kana munhu akafa asina vana, munun'una wake ngaawane mukadzi wake, agomutsira mukoma wake vana." 
Matthew22:25 Kwatiri kwakanga kuna vanakomana vomunhu mumwe vanomwe; wedangwe akawana mukadzi, akafa asina vana, akasiyira munun'una wake mukadzi wake;" 
Matthew22:26 nokudarowo wechipiri, nowechitatu, kusvikira kuno wechinomwe." 
Matthew22:27 Shure kwavose mukadzi akafawo. 
Matthew22:28 Zvino pakumuka kwavakafa, achava mukadzi waaniko wavanomwe ava, nokuti vose vaiva naye.”" 
Matthew22:29 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Marasika, nokusaziva Magwaro, kana simba raMwari." 
Matthew22:30 Nokuti pakumuka kwavakafa havawani, kana kuwaniswa; asi vakaita savatumwa kudenga." 
Matthew22:31 Asi kana kuri kumuka kwavakafa, hamuna kurava here zvamakaudzwa naMwari, paakati," 
Matthew22:32 ‘Ini ndiri Mwari waAbhurahamu, naMwari waIsaka, naMwari waJakobho?’ Haasi Mwari wavakafa, asi wavapenyu.”" 
Matthew22:33 Vanhu vazhinji vachinzwa izvozvo, vakashamiswa nokudzidzisa kwake." 
Matthew22:34 VaFarisi vakati vachinzwa kuti wapwisa vaSadhusi, vakaungana pamwechete." 
Matthew22:35 Mumwe wavo, mududziri womurairo, akamubvunza, achimuedza, akati," 
Matthew22:36 “Mudzidzisi, murairo mukuru pamirairo ndoupiko?”" 
Matthew22:37 Akati kwaari, “Ida Ishe, Mwari wako, nomwoyo wako wose, nomweya wako wose, nokufunga kwako kwose." 
Matthew22:38 Ndiwo murairo mukuru nowokutanga. 
Matthew22:39 Wechipiri unofanana nawo, ndiwoyu, ‘Ida wokwako, sezvaunozvida iwe.’" 
Matthew22:40 Murairo wose navaporofita zvakabatanidzwa pamirairo iyi miviri.” 
Matthew22:41 Zvino VaFarisi vachakaungana, Jesu akavabvunza," 
Matthew22:42 akati, “Munofungeiko pamusoro paKristu? Mwanakomana waaniko?” Vakati kwaari, “WaDhavhidhi.”" 
Matthew22:43 Akati kwavari, “Dhavhidhi akagomutumidza seiko noMweya, Ishe wake, achiti," 
Matthew22:44 ‘Ishe akati kuna Ishe wangu, Gara kurudyi rwangu, Kusvikira ndaisa vavengi vako pasi petsoka dzako?’" 
Matthew22:45 Zvino, kana Dhavhidhi achimutumidza Ishe, angagova mwanakomana wake seiko?”" 
Matthew22:46 Kwakanga kusina munhu akagona kumupindura shoko, uye kwakanga kusina munhu akatsunga kumubvunza chinhu pazuva iro." 
Matthew23:1 Zvino Jesu akataura kuvanhu vazhinji navadzidzi vake," 
Matthew23:2 akati, “Vanyori naVaFarisi vagere pachigaro chaMosesi;" 
Matthew23:3 saka zvose zvavanokuudzai, muzviite nokuzvichengeta, asi musatevera mabasa avo; nokuti vanotaura, asi havaiti." 
Matthew23:4 Vanosunga mitoro inorema, inotambudza kutakura, vachiisa pamafudzi avanhu, asi ivo vamene havadi kuibata nomunwe wavo." 
Matthew23:5 Asi mabasa avo ose vanoaita kuti vaonekwe navanhu; nokuti vanofarisa mafirakitera avo, vanokurisa mipeto yenguo dzavo," 
Matthew23:6 vanofarira zvigaro zvapamberi pamitambo, nezvigaro zvapamberi mumasinagoge," 
Matthew23:7 nokukwaziswa padare, nokunzi, ‘Rabhi’ navanhu." 
Matthew23:8 Asi imi musanzi, ‘Rabhi;’ nokuti mudzidzisi wenyu ndomumwe, imi mose muri hama." 
Matthew23:9 Musati munhu ari panyika baba venyu, nokuti mumwechete ndiBaba venyu, ivo vari kudenga." 
Matthew23:10 Musati ‘Vatenzi,’ nokuti mumwechete, nditenzi wenyu, iye Kristu." 
Matthew23:11 Asi mukuru pakati penyu ngaave muranda wenyu. 
Matthew23:12 Ani naani anozvikudza achaninipiswa, naani naani anozvininipisa, achakudzwa." 
Matthew23:13 “Mune nhamo, imi vanyori naVaFarisi, vanyengeri! Nokuti munopfigira vanhu ushe hwedenga; nokuti imi hamupindi mumene, naivo, vopinda, hamuvatenderi kupinda. [" 
Matthew23:14 Mune nhamo, imi vanyori naVaFarisi, vanyengeri! Nokuti munoparadza dzimba dzechirikadzi muchiita minyengetero mirefu yemanomano; naizvozvo muchatongerwa zvakaipa nokupfuurisa.]" 
Matthew23:15 “Mune nhamo, imi vanyori naVaFarisi, vanyengeri! Nokuti munofamba pagungwa napanyika kuzotapa mudzidzi mumwe; kana awanikwa, munomuita mwanakomana weGehena kukunda imi kaviri." 
Matthew23:16 “Mune nhamo, imi vatungamiriri vakapofumara, munoti, ‘Ani naani anopika netemberi, hazvina hazvo; asi ani naani anopika nendarama yetemberi, ndiye ane mhosva.’" 
Matthew23:17 Imi mapenzi namapofu! Chikuru ndechipiko, ndarama kana temberi, inoita ndarama ive tsvene?" 
Matthew23:18 Munotizve, ‘Ani naani anopika neatari, hazvina hazvo mhosva; asi ani naani anopika nechipo chiri pamusoro payo, ndiye ane mhosva.’" 
Matthew23:19 Imi mapenzi namapofu! Chikuru ndechipiko, chipo kana atari, inoita chipo chive chitsvene?" 
Matthew23:20 “Naizvozvo, anopika neatari, anopika nayo, nezvose zviri pamusoro payo." 
Matthew23:21 “Neanopika netemberi, anopika nayoo, neanogara mairi." 
Matthew23:22 Neanopika nedenga, anopika nechigaro choushe chaMwari, neanogara pamusoro pacho." 
Matthew23:23 “Mune nhamo, imi vanyori naVaFarisi, vanyengeri! Nokuti munopa chegumi chemindi, neanisi, nekumini, muchirega zvinhu zvikuru zvomurairo, zvinoti kururamisira mhaka, nengoni, nokutendeka; maifanira kuzviita izvi, nokusarega kuita izvozvo." 
Matthew23:24 Imi vatungamiri vakapofumara, munomimina runyunyu, muchimedza ngamera." 
Matthew23:25 “Mune nhamo, imi vanyori naVaFarisi, vanyengeri! Nokuti munonatsa kunze kwomukombe nendiro, asi mukati muzere nekukara nokusazvidzora." 
Matthew23:26 “Iwe muFarisi wakapofumara, tanga kunatsa mukati momukombe, nendiro, kuti kunze kwazvo kugochenawo." 
Matthew23:27 “Mune nhamo, imi vanyori naVaFarisi, vanyengeri! Nokuti makafanana namarinda akacheneswa, anoonekwa saakanaka kunze kwawo, asi mukati muzere namapfupa avakafa netsvina yose." 
Matthew23:28 Saizvozvo nemiwo munoonekwa navanhu kunze kwenyu makaita samakarurama, asi mukati muzere nokunyengera nokuipa." 
Matthew23:29 “Mune nhamo, imi vanyori naVaFarisi vanyengeri! Nokuti munovaka marinda avaporofita, nokushongedza marinda avakarurama," 
Matthew23:30 muchiti, dai taivapo pamazuva amateteguru edu, tingadai tisina kuvabatsira kuuraya vaporofita." 
Matthew23:31 Saka munozvipupurira kuti muri vanakomana vavakauraya vaporofita. 
Matthew23:32 Zvino chizadzisai gamha rakasiyiwa namateteguru enyu. 
Matthew23:33 Imi nyoka, imi vana venyoka! Muchatiza seiko kutonga kweGehena?" 
Matthew23:34 Saka, tarirai, ndinotumira kwamuri vaporofita, navakachenjera, navanyori; muchauraya vamwe vavo, nokuvarovera pamuchinjikwa; mucharovesa vamwe vavo mumasinagoge enyu, nokuvadzingirira mumaguta ose." 
Matthew23:35 Kuti ropa rose ravakarurama, rakateurirwa panyika, riuye pamusoro penyu, kubva paropa raAbheri akanga akarurama, kusvikira paropa raZekariya, mwanakomana waBharakia, wamakauraya pakati petemberi neatari." 
Matthew23:36 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, izvi zvose zvichauya pamusoro porudzi urwu." 
Matthew23:37 “Jerusaremu! Jerusaremu! Iwe unouraya vaporofita, nokutaka namabwe avo vakatumwa kwauri! Ndakanga ndichida kazhinji sei kuunganidza vana vako, sembambo inounganidza hukwana dzayo, munyasi mamapapiro ayo, mukaramba!" 
Matthew23:38 Tarirai, masiyirwa imba yenyu rava dongo." 
Matthew23:39 Nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, kubva zvino hamuchazondioni, kusvikira muchiti, ‘Ngaarumbidzwe iye anouya nezita raIshe.’ ”" 
Matthew24:1 Zvino Jesu akabuda mutemberi, akati oenda, vadzidzi vake vakauya kwaari kuzomuratidza dzimba dzetemberi." 
Matthew24:2 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Munoona zvinhu izvi zvose here? Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, hakungaregwi dombo pamusoro pedombo, risingazowisirwi pasi.”" 
Matthew24:3 Akati agara pagomo reMiorivhi, vadzidzi vake vakauya kwaari, vari voga, vakati, “Tiudzei, kuti izvozvi zvichagova rinhiko? Nechiratidzo chokuuya kwenyu nechokuguma kwenyika chichava chipiko?”" 
Matthew24:4 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Chenjerai kuti murege kutsauswa nomunhu." 
Matthew24:5 Nokuti vazhinji vachauya nezita rangu, vachiti, ‘Ndini Kristu;’ vachitsausa vazhinji." 
Matthew24:6 Muchanzwa zvokurwa nenyaya yokurwa; chenjerai, musavhunduka, nokuti izvozvi zvose zvinofanira kumboitwa, asi kuguma kuchigere kusvika." 
Matthew24:7 Nokuti rudzi ruchamukira rudzi, noushe huchamukira ushe; nenzara dzichavapo, nehosha, nokudengenyeka kwenyika kunzvimbo zhinji." 
Matthew24:8 “Asi zvinhu izvozvi zvichava kutanga kwenhamo. 
Matthew24:9 “Zvino vachakuisai kumatambudziko, vachakuurayai, muchavengwa namarudzi ose nokuda kwezita rangu." 
Matthew24:10 Vazhinji vachadonha, uye vachapandukirana nokuvengana." 
Matthew24:11 “Vaporofita vazhinji venhema vachamuka, vachitsausa vazhinji." 
Matthew24:12 Rudo rwavazhinji ruchatonhora, nokuti kusarurama kuchawanda." 
Matthew24:13 Asi anotsungirira kusvikira pakuguma, achaponeswa." 
Matthew24:14 Vhangeri iyi youshe ichaparidzirwa munyika dzose, chive chapupu kumarudzi ose; ipapo kuguma kuchasvika." 
Matthew24:15 “Naizvozvo kana muchiona nyangadzi yokuparadza, yakarehwa nomuporofita Dhaniere, imire panzvimbo tsvene (anorava ngaacherekedze);" 
Matthew24:16 zvino vari muJudhiya ngavatizire kumakomo; 
Matthew24:17 ari pamusoro pedenga reimba, ngaarege kuburuka kuzotora zviri mumba make;" 
Matthew24:18 naari mumunda, ngaarege kudzokera shure kuzotora nguo yake." 
Matthew24:19 “Vachava nenhamo vane pamuviri navanoyamwisa namazuva iwayo; 
Matthew24:20 Nyengeterai kuti kutiza kwenyu kurege kuva panguva yechando kana neSabata. 
Matthew24:21 Nokuti nenguva iyo kuchavapo kutambudzika kukuru, kusati kwakambovapo kwakadaro, kubva pakutanga kwenyika kusvikira zvino, uye hakuchazovipo." 
Matthew24:22 “Dai mazuva iwayo asaitapudzwa, hakuna munhu airarama; asi nokuda kwavakasanangurwa mazuva iwayo achatapudzwa." 
Matthew24:23 “Zvino kana munhu akati kwamuri, ‘Tarirai, Kristu ari pano,’ kana, ‘Apo’ regai kutenda." 
Matthew24:24 Nokuti vachamuka vanaKristu venhema, navaporofita venhema, vacharatidza zviratidzo zvikuru nezvinoshamisa, kuti kana zvichibvira, vatsause navakasanangurwawo." 
Matthew24:25 “Tarirai, ndagara ndakuudzai." 
Matthew24:26 Zvino, kana vakati kwamuri, ‘Tarirai, ari kurenje,’ regai kubuda; ‘Tarirai, ari mudzimba dzomukati,’ regai kutenda." 
Matthew24:27 “Nokuti semheni inobva mabvazuva, ichipenyeresa kumavirira, ndizvo zvichaita kuuya kwoMwanakomana womunhu." 
Matthew24:28 Apo pane chitunha, ndipo pachaunganira magora." 
Matthew24:29 “Pakarepo, shure kwokutambudzika kwamazuva iwayo, zuva richasviba, mwedzi hauchazobwinyi, nyenyedzi dzichawa kudenga, namasimba okudenga achazununguswa." 
Matthew24:30 Ipapo chiratidzo choMwanakomana womunhu chichaonekwa kudenga; zvino marudzi ose enyika achachema, achiona Mwanakomana womunhu achiuya pamusoro pamakore okudenga nesimba nokubwinya kukuru." 
Matthew24:31 “Achatuma vatumwa vake nehwamanda huru, vachaunganidza vasanangurwa vake kunobva mhepo ina, kubva kurutivi rumwe rwedenga kusvikira kuno rumwe rutivi." 
Matthew24:32 “Dzidzai pamuonde mufananidzo uyu, kana davi rawo rava nyoro, mashizha achitunga, munoziva kuti zhizha rava pedyo." 
Matthew24:33 Saizvozvowo, nemiwo, kana moona izvozvo zvose, zivai kuti ava pedyo asvika pamukova." 
Matthew24:34 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, rudzi urwu harungatongopfuuri kusvikira izvozvi zvose zvaitika." 
Matthew24:35 Denga nenyika zvichapfuura, asi mashoko angu haangatongopfuuri." 
Matthew24:36 “Asi kana riri zuva iro nenguva iyo, hakuna anozviziva, kunyangwe vatumwa vokudenga, kunyangwe Mwanakomana, asi Baba voga." 
Matthew24:37 Sapamazuva aNowa, ndizvo zvichaita kuuya kwoMwanakomana womunhu." 
Matthew24:38 Nokuti sapamazuva iwayo, mvura zhinji isati yasvika, vaidya nokunwa, nokuwana, nokuwaniswa, kusvikira zuva Nowa raakapinda naro muareka," 
Matthew24:39 vasingazivi zvichavawira kusvikira mvura zhinji yauya, ikavaparadza vose; ndizvo zvichaita kuuya kwoMwanakomana womunhu." 
Matthew24:40 Nenguva iyo vaviri vachava mumunda, mumwe achatorwa, mumwe akasiyiwa." 
Matthew24:41 Vakadzi vaviri vachakuya paguyo rimwe, mumwe uchatorwa, mumwe akasiyiwa." 
Matthew24:42 Rindai naizvozvo, nokuti hamuzivi zuva, Ishe wenyu raanouya naro." 
Matthew24:43 Asi zivai izvi, kuti dai saimba, aiziva nguva yokusvika kwembavha, angadai airinda, akasatendera kuti imba yake ipazwe." 
Matthew24:44 Naizvozvo nemiwo, garai makazvigadzirira; nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu achauya nenguva yomusingamutariri." 
Matthew24:45 Ndianiko muranda akatendeka, akangwara, akagadzwa nashe wake kuti ave mutariri weimba yake, kuti avape zvokudya nenguva yakafanira?" 
Matthew24:46 “Akaropafadzwa muranda uyo, anoti kana ishe wake achisvika, akamuwana achiita saizvozvo." 
Matthew24:47 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, achamugadza kuti ave mutariri wezvose zvaanazvo." 
Matthew24:48 Asi kana muranda uyo akaipa akataura mumwoyo make, achiti, ‘Ishe wangu anonoka;’" 
Matthew24:49 akatanga kurova vamwe varanda vanoshanda pamwechete naye, akadya, akanwa pamwechete navanoraradza," 
Matthew24:50 ishe womuranda uyo achasvika nezuva raasingamutariri, nenguva yaasingazivi;" 
Matthew24:51 akamurovesa kwazvo, akamupa mugove wake pamwechete navanyengeri; apo pachava nokuchema nokugeda–geda kwameno." 
Matthew25:1 “Zvino ushe hwedenga hungafananidzwa navasikana vane gumi, vakatora mwenje yavo, vakabuda kundochingamidza muwani." 
Matthew25:2 Vashanu vavo vakanga mapenzi, vashanu vakanga vakachenjera." 
Matthew25:3 “Nokuti mapenzi akatora mwenje yawo, akasatora mafuta." 
Matthew25:4 Asi vakachenjera vakatora mafuta mumidziyo yavo nemwenje yavo. 
Matthew25:5 Zvino, muwani akati anonoka, vakakotsira vose, vakavata." 
Matthew25:6 “Pakati pousiku vakanzwa mhere–mhere, ‘Muwani auya! Budai mumuchingamidze!’" 
Matthew25:7 Zvino vasikana vose vakamuka, vakagadzira mwenje yavo." 
Matthew25:8 Mapenzi akati kuna vakachenjera, ‘Tipeiwo mamwe mafuta enyu, nokuti mwenje yedu yodzima.’" 
Matthew25:9 Asi vakachenjera vakapindura, vakati, ‘Kwete, zvimwe haangakwaniri isu nemi tose; endai henyu kuna vanotengesa, muzvitengere.’" 
Matthew25:10 Vakati vachienda kundotenga, muwani ndokusvika; zvino, vakanga vakazvigadzira vakapinda naye pamutambo wemuchato, mukova ukapfigwa." 
Matthew25:11 “Pashure vaya vamwe vasikana vakasvika, vakati, ‘Ishe, Ishe, tizarurireiwo!’" 
Matthew25:12 “Akapindura, akati, ‘Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, handikuzivii imi.’ ”" 
Matthew25:13 “Naizvozvo rindai, nokuti hamuzivi zuva kana nguva." 
Matthew25:14 “Nokuti zvakafanana nomunhu akaenda kuneimwe nyika, akadana varanda vake, akavaronzera pfuma yake." 
Matthew25:15 Akapa mumwe matarenda mashanu, mumwe maviri, mumwe rimwe, mumwe nomumwe zvakakwanira simba rake; akaenda kune imwe nyika." 
Matthew25:16 Pakarepo iye, akapiwa matarenda mashanu, akaenda akaita mhindu nawo, akawana mamwe mashanu." 
Matthew25:17 Saizvozvowo, akapiwa maviri, akawana mamwe maviri." 
Matthew25:18 Asi akapiwa rimwe, akenda, akachera pasi, akaviga mari yaishe wake." 
Matthew25:19 “Nguva huru yakati yapfuura, ishe wavaranda ivavo akasvika, akagadzira mashoko navo." 
Matthew25:20 Akanga apiwa matarenda mashanu, akati, ‘Ishe, makandipa matarenda mashanu, tarirai, ndawana mamwe matarenda mashanu.’" 
Matthew25:21 Ishe wake akati kwaari, ‘Zvakanaka, muranda wakanaka, wakatendeka; wakanga wakatendeka pazvinhu zvishoma, ndichakuisa pamusoro pezvinhu zvizhinji; pinda mumufaro washe wako.’" 
Matthew25:22 Akanga apiwa matarenda maviri akauyawo, akati, ‘Ishe, makandipa matarenda maviri; tarirai, ndawana mamwe matarenda maviri.’" 
Matthew25:23 Ishe wake akati kwaari, ‘Zvakanaka, muranda akanaka, akatendeka; wakanga wakatendeka pazvinhu zvishoma, ndichakuisa pamusoro pezvinhu zvizhinji; pinda mumufaro washe wako.’" 
Matthew25:24 “Akanga apiwa tarenda rimwe, naiye akauyawo, akati, ‘Ishe, ndakanga ndichikuzivai imi, kuti muri munhu ane hasha, munokohwa pamusati makadyara, munounganidza pamusati makakusha;" 
Matthew25:25 zvino ndakatya, ndikandoviga tarenda renyu pasi; hecho, chinhu chenyu!’" 
Matthew25:26 Ishe wake akapindura, akati kwaari, ‘Iwe, muranda akaipa, uno usimbe, wakanga uchiziva kuti ndinokohwa pandisina kudyara, ndichiunganidza pandisina kukusha;" 
Matthew25:27 saka waifanira kuisa mari yangu kune vane bhangi, kuti pakusvika kwangu ndingadai ndapiwa zvangu zvawanda." 
Matthew25:28 Naizvozvo mutorerei tarenda rake, mupe ana matarenda ane gumi." 
Matthew25:29 Nokuti mumwe nomumwe unazvo, achapiwa, ave nezvizhinji; asi asina, achatorerwa nezvaanazvo." 
Matthew25:30 Budisirai muranda pasina, murima nokunze; ipapo pachava nokuchema nokugeda–geda kwameno.’" 
Matthew25:31 “Zvino kana Mwanakomana womunhu achiuya nokubwinya kwake, navatumwa vose vanaye, achagara pachigaro chake choushe chinobwinya;" 
Matthew25:32 namarudzi ose achaunganidzwa pamberi pake; achavaraura somufudzi anoraura makwai nembudzi. 
Matthew25:33 Achaisa makwai kurudyi rwake, mbudzi kuruboshwe." 
Matthew25:34 “Zvino Ishe achati kuna vari kurudyi, ‘Uyai imi, makaropafadzwa naBaba, mugare nhaka youshe hwakagadzirirwemi kubva pakuvamba kwenyika." 
Matthew25:35 Nokuti ndakanga ndine nzara, mukandipa chokudya; ndakanga ndine nyota, mukandipa chokunwa; ndakanga ndiri mweni, mukandigamuchira;" 
Matthew25:36 ndakanga ndisina nguo, mukandipfekedza; ndakanga ndichirwara, mukandifambira; ndakanga ndiri mujeri, mukauya kwandiri.’" 
Matthew25:37 “Zvino vakarurama vachamupindura, vachiti, ‘Ishe, takakuonai rinhiko mune nzara, tikakupai chokudya? Kana mune nyota, tikakupai chokunwa?" 
Matthew25:38 Takakuonai rinhiko muri mweni, tikakugamuchirai? Kana musina nguo, tikakupfekedzai?" 
Matthew25:39 Takakuonai rinhiko muchirwara, kana muri mujeri, tikauya kwamuri?’" 
Matthew25:40 “Ishe achapindura, achiti, kwavari, ‘Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, pamakazviitira mumwe wavaduku vehama dzangu idzi, makazviitireni.’" 
Matthew25:41 Zvino achati kuna vari kuruboshwe, ‘Ibvai kwandiri, imi manyombwa, muende kumoto usingaperi, wakagadzirirwa Dhiabhori navatumwa vake." 
Matthew25:42 Nokuti ndakanga ndine nzara, mukasandipa chokudya; ndakanga ndine nyota, mukasandipa chokunwa;" 
Matthew25:43 ndakanga ndiri mweni, mukasandigamuchira; ndisina nguo, mukasandipfekedza; ndichirwara, nomujeri, mukasandifambira.’" 
Matthew25:44 Zvino naivava vachapindura, vachiti, ‘Ishe, takakuonai rinhiko mune nzara, kana mune nyota, kana muri mweni, kana musina nguo, kana muchirwara, kana muri mutorongo, tikasakushumirai?’" 
Matthew25:45 Zvino achavapindura, achiti, ‘Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, pamusati makazviitira mumwe wavaduku ava, hamusakazviitireni.’" 
Matthew25:46 Ava vachaenda kunorohwa kusingaperi; asi vakarurama kuupenyu husingaperi.” 
Matthew26:1 Jesu akati apedza mashoko iwayo ose, akati kuvadzidzi vake," 
Matthew26:2 “Munoziva kuti kana mazuva maviri apfuura Pasika inosvika, Mwanakomana womunhu achaiswa kuvatongi, kuti aroverwe pamuchinjikwa.”" 
Matthew26:3 Zvino vapristi vakuru, navakuru vavanhu vakaungana pamuzinda woMupristi Mukuru, ainzi Kaifasi." 
Matthew26:4 Vakarangana kuti vabate Jesu namano, vagomuuraya." 
Matthew26:5 Asi vakati, “Zvirege kuitwa pamutambo, kuti kurege kuva nebope pakati pavanhu.”" 
Matthew26:6 Zvino Jesu akati ari paBhetania, mumba maSimoni wamaperembudzi," 
Matthew26:7 mumwe mukadzi akauya kwaari ane chinu chearibhasitera chaiva namafuta chino mutengo mukuru, akachidururira mumusoro wake, agere pakudya." 
Matthew26:8 Asi vadzidzi vake vachizviona, vakafa neshungu, vakati, “Kuparadzwa kwakadaro kwaitirweiko?”" 
Matthew26:9 “Nokuti mafuta awa angadai atengeswa nemari zhinji, ikapiwa varombo.”" 
Matthew26:10 Asi Jesu, achizvinzwa, akati kwavari, “Munotambudzireiko mukadzi uyu? Nokuti andiitira basa rakanaka." 
Matthew26:11 Nokuti varombo munavo nguva dzose, asi ini hamuneni nguva dzose." 
Matthew26:12 Nokuti zvaakadira mafuta awa pamuviri wangu, akazviitira kuvigwa kwangu." 
Matthew26:13 Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, kwose kunozoparidzirwa Vhangeri iyi panyika dzose, izvi zvakaitwa naye zvicharehwawo, kuti vamurangarire nazvo.”" 
Matthew26:14 Zvino mumwe wavane gumi navaviri, wainzi Judhasi Isikarioti, akaenda kuvapristi vakuru," 
Matthew26:15 akati, “Muchandipeiko, kana ndikamuisa kwamuri?” Vakamutemera makumi matatu emari yesirivha." 
Matthew26:16 Zvino kubva ipapo akatsvaka nguva yakafanira yokumuisa kwavari nayo. 
Matthew26:17 Nezuva rokutanga rezvingwa zvisina mbiriso, vadzidzi vakauya kuna Jesu vakati, “Munoda kuti tikugadzirirei kupiko pamungadya Pasika?”" 
Matthew26:18 Akati, “Endai muguta kuna nyakuti, muti kwaari, ‘Zvanzi noMudzidzisi, nguva yangu yava pedyo; ndichadya Pasika paimba yako, navadzidzi vangu.’ ”" 
Matthew26:19 Vadzidzi vakaita pavakarayirwa napo naJesu, vakagadzira Pasika." 
Matthew26:20 Ava madekwana, akagara pakudya navadzidzi vane gumi navaviri." 
Matthew26:21 Vakati vachidya, akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, mumwe wenyu achandipandukira.”" 
Matthew26:22 Zvino vakava neshungu kwazvo, vakatanga mumwe nomumwe kutaura kwaari, achiti, “Ishe, ndini here?”" 
Matthew26:23 Akapindura, akati, “Waisa ruoko neni mundiro, ndiye achandipandukira." 
Matthew26:24 Mwanakomana womunhu achaenda hake, sezvazvakanyorwa pamusoro pake; asi ane nhamo munhu uyo, anouyisa Mwanakomana womunhu kuvavengi vake, zvaiva nani kumunhu uyu dai asina kuberekwa.”" 
Matthew26:25 Zvino Judhasi, uyo akamupandukira, akapindura, akati, “Rabhi, ndini here?” Akati kwaari, “Ndizvo zvawataura.”" 
Matthew26:26 Vakati vodya, Jesu akatora chingwa, akavonga, akachimedura, ndokupa vadzidzi vake, achiti kwavari, “Gamuchirai, mudye; uyu muviri wangu.”" 
Matthew26:27 Akatora mukombe, akavonga, akavapa, achiti, “Inwai mose pauri.”" 
Matthew26:28 “Nokuti iri iropa rangu rechitenderano chitsva, rakadururirwa vazhinji kuti varegererwe zvivi.”" 
Matthew26:29 Asi ndinoti kwamuri, “Handichatongonwizve zvibereko zvomuzambiringa, kusvikira zuva iro randachizonwa naro nemi, zvava zvitsva, muushe hwaBaba vangu.”" 
Matthew26:30 Zvino vakati vaimba rwiyo, vakabuda vakaenda kugomo reMiorivhi." 
Matthew26:31 Zvino Jesu akati kwavari, “Imi mose muchagumburwa neni usiku huno; nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, ‘Ndicharova mufudzi, namakwai eboka achaparadzwa.’" 
Matthew26:32 Asi kana ndamutswa, ndichakutungamirirai Gareriya.”" 
Matthew26:33 Zvino Petirosi akapindura, akati kwaari, “Kana vose vakagumburwa nemi, ini handingatongogumburwi.”" 
Matthew26:34 Jesu akati kwaari, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwauri, kuti usiku huno, jongwe risati rakukuridza, uchandiramba katatu.”" 
Matthew26:35 Petirosi akati kwaari, “Kunyangwe ndikafanira kufa nemi, handingatongokurambii ini.” Vadzidzi vose vakadarowo." 
Matthew26:36 Zvino Jesu akasvika navo panzvimbo inonzi Getsemani, akati kuvadzidzi, “Garai pano, ini ndichaenda kundonyengetera uko.”" 
Matthew26:37 Akatora Petirosi navanakomana vaZebhedhi vaviri, akatanga kuva neshungu nokudumbirwa." 
Matthew26:38 Akati kwavari, “Mweya wangu une shungu kwazvo, kusvikira pakufa; garai pano murinde neni.”" 
Matthew26:39 Akapfuura mberi zvishomanene, akawira pasi nechiso chake, akanyengetera, achiti, “Baba vangu, kana zvichibvira, mukombe uyu ngaupfuure kwandiri; kunyangwe zvakadaro kurege kuva kuda kwangu, asi kuda kwenyu.”" 
Matthew26:40 Akaenda kuvadzidzi, akavawana vavata; akati kuna Petirosi, “Makanga musingagoni seiko kurinda neni awa imwechete?" 
Matthew26:41 Rindai, munyengetere, kuti murege kupinda mukuedzwa; mweya unoda hawo, asi nyama haina simba.”" 
Matthew26:42 Akaendazve rwechipiri, akanyengetera, achiti, “Baba vangu, kana mukombe uyu usingagoni kupfuura ndisingaunwi, kuda kwenyu ngakuitwe.”" 
Matthew26:43 Akaendazve, akavawana vavata; nokuti meso avo akanga abatwa nehope." 
Matthew26:44 Akavasiyazve, akandonyengetera rwechitatu, achitaurazve mashoko iwayo." 
Matthew26:45 Zvino akaenda kuvadzidzi, akati kwavari, “Chivatai henyu, muzorore; tarirai, nguva yasvika, Mwanakomana womunhu achaiswa mumaoko avatadzi." 
Matthew26:46 Simukai, tiende; tarirai, wondiisa kwavari wava pedyo.”" 
Matthew26:47 Achataura, tarira Judhasi, mumwe wavane gumi navaviri, akasvika, ana vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakabata minondo, netsvimbo, vachibva kuvapristi vakuru navakuru vavanhu." 
Matthew26:48 Zvino iye, akamupandukira, akanga avapa chiratidzo, achiti, “Uyo wandichatsvoda, ndiye; mumubate.”" 
Matthew26:49 Pakarepo akasvika kuna Jesu, akati, “Kwaziwai, Rabhi!” Akamutsvoda zvikuru." 
Matthew26:50 Jesu akati kwaari, “Shamwari, ita zvawavinga.” Ipapo vakauya, vakaisa maoko kuna Jesu, vakamubata." 
Matthew26:51 Zvino tarira, mumwe wavaiva naJesu, akatambanudza ruoko rwake, akavhomora munondo wake, akatema muranda woMupristi Mukuru, akagura nzeve yake." 
Matthew26:52 Zvino Jesu akati kwaari, “Dzosera munondo wako muhara ravo, nokuti vose vanobata munondo, vachafa nomunondo." 
Matthew26:53 Unofunga here kuti handigoni kukumbira kuna Baba vangu, vakandipa iko zvino vatumwa vanopfuura mapoka makuru–kuru ane gumi namaviri?" 
Matthew26:54 “Magwaro angagoitika seiko, anoti zvinofanira kuitwa kudaro?”" 
Matthew26:55 Nenguva iyo Jesu akati kuvanhu vazhinji, “Mabuda neminondo netsvimbo kuzondibata sendiri gororo here? Ndaigara mutemberi mazuva ose, ndichidzidzisa, mukasandibata." 
Matthew26:56 Asi izvi zvose zvaitwa kuti magwaro avaporofita azadziswe.” Zvino vadzidzi vose vakamusiya, vakatiza." 
Matthew26:57 Avo, vakanga vabata Jesu, vakamuisa kuna Kaifasi, Mupristi Mukuru, apo pakanga paungana vanyori navakuru vavanhu." 
Matthew26:58 Asi Petirosi akamutevera ari kure, kusvikira paruvazhe rwomupristi mukuru, akapinda mukati, akagara navatariri kuzoona kupera kwazvo." 
Matthew26:59 Zvino vapristi vakuru namakurukota ose vakatsvaka uchapupu hwenhema kuti vapomere Jesu, vamuuraye;" 
Matthew26:60 asi havana kuwana, kunyangwe zvapupu zvizhinji zvenhema zvakauya. Pashure zviviri zvakasvika, zvikati," 
Matthew26:61 “Munhu uyu akati, ‘Ndinogona kuputsa temberi yaMwari, ndikaivakazve namazuva matatu.’ ”" 
Matthew26:62 Zvino Mupristi Mukuru akasimuka, akati kwaari, “Haupinduri chinhu here? Chiiko ichi chavanokupomedzera?”" 
Matthew26:63 Asi Jesu akaramba anyerere. Mupristi Mukuru akati kwaari, “Ndinokupikisa naMwari mupenyu, kuti utiudze kana uri Kristu, Mwanakomana waMwari.”" 
Matthew26:64 Jesu akati kwaari, “Ndizvo zvawataura; asi ndinoti kwamuri, kubva zvino muchaona Mwanakomana womunhu agere kurudyi rwaSamasimba achiuya ari mumakore edenga.”" 
Matthew26:65 Ipapo Mupristi Mukuru akabvarura nguo dzake, akati, “Ashonha Mwari! Tichatsvakireiko zvapupu? Tarirai, manzwa zvino kushonha kwake." 
Matthew26:66 Munoti kudiniko?” Vakapindura, vakati, “Anofanira kufa.”" 
Matthew26:67 Zvino vakamupfira mate kumeso, vakamurova netsiva, vamwe nembama," 
Matthew26:68 vachiti, “Fembera iwe Kristu, kuti ndiani akurova.”" 
Matthew26:69 Petirosi akanga agere panze paruvazhe. Zvino mushandiri akauya kwaari, akati, “Newewo wakanga unaJesu weGareriya.”" 
Matthew26:70 Asi iye akaramba pamberi pavose, achiti, “Handizivi zvaunoreva.”" 
Matthew26:71 Zvino akati asvika kusuwo, mumwe mushandirikadzi akamuona, akati kuna vaivapo, “Uyu munhu akanga ana Jesu weNazareta.”" 
Matthew26:72 Akarambazve nokupika, achiti, “Handimuzivi munhu uyu.”" 
Matthew26:73 Chava chinguva vaya vakanga vamirepo vakauya, vachiti kuna Petirosi, “Zvirokwazvo, newewo uri mumwe wavo, nokuti kutaura kwako kunoita kuti uzikanwe.”" 
Matthew26:74 Zvino akatanga kutuka nokupika, nemhiko achiti, “Handimuzivi munhu uyu.” Pakarepo jongwe rikakukuridza." 
Matthew26:75 Ipapo Petirosi akarangarira shoko rakanga rarehwa naJesu, rokuti, “Jongwe risati rakukuridza, uchandiramba katatu.” Ipapo akabuda panze, akandochema zvikuru." 
Matthew27:1 Ava mangwana, vapristi vakuru vose navakuru vavanhu vakarangana pamusoro paJesu kuti vamuuraye;" 
Matthew27:2 vakamusunga, vakaenda naye, vakamuisa kuna Pirato, aiva gavhuna." 
Matthew27:3 Zvino Judhasi, uyo akamupandukira, akati achiona kuti atongerwa kufa, ndokuzvidya mwoyo, akadzosera mari iya makumi matatu esirivha kuvapristi vakuru navakuru vavanhu," 
Matthew27:4 achiti, “Ndatadza, ndapandukira ropa risina chipomerwa.” Vakati, “Tine mhaka yeiko nazvo? Imhaka yako.”" 
Matthew27:5 Akakandira pasi mari iya mutemberi; akabva, akaenda ndokuzvisungirira." 
Matthew27:6 Vapristi vakuru vakatora mari yesirivha, vakati, “Hazvina kufanira kuti ichengetwe munovigwa mari, zvauri mutengo weropa.”" 
Matthew27:7 Vakarangana, vakatenga nawo munda womuumbi wehari kuzovigapo vatorwa." 
Matthew27:8 Naizvozvo munda uyo wakanzi, “Munda weropa” kusvikira zuva ranhasi." 
Matthew27:9 Zvino zvakarehwa nomuporofita Jeremiya zvakaitika, zvinoti: “Vakatora mari yesirivha makumi matatu, Mutengo womunhu aitengeswa, Wakatarwa navana VaIsiraeri;" 
Matthew27:10 Vakatenga nawo munda womuumbi wehari, Sezvandakarairwa naIshe.”" 
Matthew27:11 Zvino Jesu akamira pamberi pagavhuna, gavhuna akamubvunza, akati, “Ndiwe mambo wavaJudha here?” Jesu akati kwaari, “Ndizvo zvamataura.”" 
Matthew27:12 Asi akati achipomerwa mhosva navapristi vakuru navakuru, haana kupindura chinhu." 
Matthew27:13 Zvino Pirato akati kwaari, “Haunzwi zvinhu zvizhinji zvavanokupomedzera here?”" 
Matthew27:14 Asi haana kuvapindura, kunyangwe neshoko rimwechete, gavhuna akashamiswa kwazvo–kwazvo nazvo." 
Matthew27:15 Zvino, pamutambo mubati aisisunungurira vanhu vazhinji musungwa mumwe, wavanenge vaida." 
Matthew27:16 Nenguva iyo vaiva nomusungwa akakurumbira, ainzi Bharabhasi." 
Matthew27:17 Naizvozvo vakati vaungana, Pirato akati kwavari, “Munoda kuti ndikusunungurirei aniko? Bharabhasi, kana Jesu, anonzi Kristu?”" 
Matthew27:18 Nokuti akanga achiziva kuti vakanga vamuisa kwaari negodo. 
Matthew27:19 Zvino akati agere pachigaro chokutonga, mukadzi wake akatumira izwi kwaari, achiti, “Usava nemhaka nomunhu uyo akarurama; nokuti ndakatambudzika zvikuru nhasi pakurota nokuda kwake.”" 
Matthew27:20 Vapristi vakuru navakuru vakagombedzera vanhu vazhinji kuti vakumbire Bharabhasi, Jesu aurawe." 
Matthew27:21 Gavhuna akapindura, akati kwavari, “Munoda kuti ndikusunungurirei aniko kuna ivavo vaviri?” Vakati, “Bharabhasi.”" 
Matthew27:22 Pirato akati kwavari, “Ndichagoiteiko naJesu, anonzi Kristu?” Vose vakati kwaari, “Ngaaroverwe pamuchinjikwa.”" 
Matthew27:23 Iye akati, “Chakaipa chaakagoita ndecheiko?” Vakanyanyisa kudanidzira, vachiti, “Ngaaroverwe pamuchinjikwa!”" 
Matthew27:24 Zvino Pirato, achiona kuti hazvibatsiri, asi kuti potomuka bope, akatora mvura, akageza maoko ake pamberi pavanhu vazhinji, achiti, “Handine mhaka neropa romunhu uyu akarurama; imhaka yenyu!”" 
Matthew27:25 Vanhu vose vakapindura, vakati, “Ropa rake ngarive pamusoro pedu napamusoro pavana vedu.”" 
Matthew27:26 Zvino akavasunungurira Bharabhasi, asi Jesu akamurovesa kwazvo, akamuisa kwavari, kuti aroverwe pamuchinjikwa." 
Matthew27:27 Zvino varwi vaPirato vakaenda naJesu mumuzinda wagavhuna hondo yose ikaunganira kwaari. 
Matthew27:28 Vakamubvisa nguo dzake, vakamufukidza nguo tsvuku;" 
Matthew27:29 vakaruka korona yeminzwa, ndokuiisa pamusoro wake; norutsanga muruoko rwake rworudyi; vakapfugama pamberi pake, vakamuseka, vachiti, “Kwaziwai, Mambo wavaJudha!”" 
Matthew27:30 Vakamupfira mate, vakatora rutsanga, vakaramba vachimurova musoro." 
Matthew27:31 Vakati vamuseka, vakamubvisa nguo tsvuku, vakamupfekedza nguo dzake, vakaenda naye kundomurovera pamuchinjikwa." 
Matthew27:32 Vakati vachibuda, vakawana munhu weKurini, ainzi Simoni; vakamumanikidza iye kuti atakure muchinjikwa wake." 
Matthew27:33 Vakati vasvika panzvimbo inonzi, Gorogota, ndokuti, “Nzvimbo yedehenya,”" 
Matthew27:34 vakamupa waini yakavhenganiswa nenduru, kuti anwe; asi akati aravira, akaramba kunwa." 
Matthew27:35 Vakati vamurovera pamuchinjikwa, vakagovana nguo dzake pakati pavo, vachikanda mijenya, (kuti zvakarehwa nomuporofita zviitike, zvinoti: Vakagovana nguo dzangu pakati pavo, vakakanda mijenya pamusoro pezvokufuka zvangu)" 
Matthew27:36 Vakagara, vakamurindapo." 
Matthew27:37 Vakaisa pamusoro wake rugwaro rwemhosva yake, rwokuti, “UYU NDI JESU MAMBO WAVAJUDHA.”" 
Matthew27:38 Vakarovera pamwechete naye makororo maviri, mumwe kurudyi, mumwe kuruboshwe." 
Matthew27:39 Vakanga vachipfuura, vakamunyomba, vachidzungudza misoro yavo," 
Matthew27:40 vachiti, “Iwe wokuputsa temberi, nokuivakazve namazuva matatu, chizviponesa. Kana uri Mwanakomana waMwari, buruka pamuchinjikwa.”" 
Matthew27:41 Saizvozvo vapristi vakuru, navanyori navakuru, vakamuseka, vachiti," 
Matthew27:42 “Akaponesa vamwe; haagoni kuzviponesa! Ndiye Mambo waVaIsiraeri! Ngaaburuke zvino pamuchinjikwa, titende kwaari." 
Matthew27:43 Aivimba naMwari; ngaachimusunungura zvino pamuchinjikwa, kana achimuda; nokuti akati, ‘Ndiri Mwanakomana waMwari.’ ”" 
Matthew27:44 Namakororo akanga aroverwa pamuchinjikwa pamwechete naye, akamuzvidza saizvozvo." 
Matthew27:45 Zvino kubva panguva yechitanhatu kusvikira panguva yepfumbamwe, rima rakavapo panyika yose." 
Matthew27:46 Nenguva inenge yepfumbamwe, Jesu akadana nezwi guru, achiti, “Eri, Eri, rama sabakitani?” Ndokuti, “Mwari wangu, Mwari wangu, mandisiyireiko?”" 
Matthew27:47 Vamwe vakanga vamirepo, vachinzwa, vakati, “Uyo anodana Eriya.”" 
Matthew27:48 Pakarepo mumwe wavo wakamhanya, akatora chifovefove, akachizadza nevhiniga, ndokuchiisa parutsanga, akamunwisa." 
Matthew27:49 Vamwe vakati, “Regai, timboona kana Eriya achizouya kumuponesa.”" 
Matthew27:50 Zvino Jesu akadanidzirazve nezwi guru, ndokubva afa." 
Matthew27:51 Ipapo tarira, chidzitiro chetemberi chakabvaruka napakati, kubva kumusoro kusvikira pasi; nyika ikadengenyeka, mabwe akatsemuka;" 
Matthew27:52 mahwiro akazaruka, zvitunha zvizhinji zvavarurami, vakanga vavete, zvakamutswa;" 
Matthew27:53 zvikabuda pamahwiro, iye akati amuka, vakapinda muguta dzvene, vakaonekwa navazhinji." 
Matthew27:54 Zvino mukuru wezana, navagariri vaJesu naye, vakati vachiona kudengenyeka kwenyika, nezvakaitwa, vakatya zvikuru, vakati, “Zvirokwazvo uyu akanga ari Mwanakomana waMwari.”" 
Matthew27:55 Vakadzi vazhinji vakanga varipo, vakatarira vari kure, vakanga vatevera Jesu, vachibva Gareriya vachimushandira." 
Matthew27:56 Pakati pavo kwakanga kuna Maria Magadharene, naMaria mai vaJakobho naJose, namai vavanakomana vaZebhedhi." 
Matthew27:57 Zvino ava madeko kukasvika mumwe mupfumi weArimatia, ainzi Josefa, akanga ari mudzidzi waJesu," 
Matthew27:58 akaenda kuna Pirato, akakumbira chitunha chaJesu. Pirato akarayira kuti apiwe." 
Matthew27:59 Josefa akatora chitunha, akachiputira nomucheka muchena," 
Matthew27:60 akauviga muhwiro hwake hutsva, hwaakanga azvigadzirira iye; akakungurusira ibwe guru pamuromo wehwiro, akabva oenda." 
Matthew27:61 Maria Magadharene, nomumwe Maria, vakanga varipo vagere vakatarisana nohwiro." 
Matthew27:62 Fume mangwana ndiro zuva raitevera zuva roKugadzirira vapristi vakuru naVaFarisi vakaungana kuna Pirato," 
Matthew27:63 vakati, “Ishe, tinorangarira kuti munyengeri uyu, achiri mupenyu, akati, ‘Mazuva matatu apfuura, ndichamuka.’" 
Matthew27:64 “Saka rairai kuti hwiro huchengetwe kusvikira pazuva retatu, kuti vadzidzi varege kuuya kumuba, vagoti kuvanhu, akamutswa kuvakafa; kurasika kwokupedzisira kukazopfuura kwokutanga.”" 
Matthew27:65 Pirato akati kwavari, “Imi muna vagariri; endai muhuchengete sezvamunoziva.”" 
Matthew27:66 Vakaenda, vakandochengeta hwiro, vakaisa chinamatidzo chokusimbisa pabwe." 
Matthew28:1 Nokupera kweSabata, kwoedza, nomusi wokutanga wevhiki, Maria Magadharene, nomumwe Maria, vakauya kuzoona hwiro." 
Matthew28:2 Zvino kukavapo kudengenyeka kukuru kwenyika, nokuti mutumwa waIshe akaburuka kudenga, akauya, akakungurusa ibwe, ndokugara pamusoro paro." 
Matthew28:3 Kuonekwa kwake kwakanga kwakaita semheni, nezvokufuka zvake zvaiva zvichena sechando." 
Matthew28:4 Zvino vanyakugaririra vakadedera vachimutya, vakaita savakafa." 
Matthew28:5 Zvino mutumwa akapindura, akati kuvakadzi, “Musatya imi, nokuti ndinoziva kuti munotsvaka Jesu, akanga akaroverwa pamuchinjikwa." 
Matthew28:6 Haapo pano, nokuti akamuka, sezvaakareva. Uyai, muone paakanga akaradzikwa." 
Matthew28:7 “Kurumidzai muende mundoudza vadzidzi vake, ‘Kuti akamuka kuvakafa;’ tarirai anokutungamirirai Gareriya, muchandomuonapo. Tarirai, ndakuudzai.”" 
Matthew28:8 Zvino vakakurumidza kubva pahwiro, vachitya nokufara zvikuru, vakamhanyira kundoudza vadzidzi vake." 
Matthew28:9 Zvino tarira, Jesu akasangana navo, akati, “Kwaziwai!” Vakauya, vakabata tsoka dzake, vakamupfugamira." 
Matthew28:10 Zvino Jesu akati kwavari, “Musatya, endai mundoudza hama dzangu, kuti vaende Gareriya, vagondionako.”" 
Matthew28:11 Zvino vachiri munzira, vamwe vagariri vakasvika muguta, vakaudza vapristi vakuru zvose zvakaitwa." 
Matthew28:12 Vakati vaungana navakuru, vakarangana, vakapa varwi mari zhinji," 
Matthew28:13 vachiti, “Taurai muchiti, ‘Vadzidzi vake vakauya usiku vakamuba, isu tivete.’" 
Matthew28:14 Kana zvikanzwika nagavhuna, tichamugutsa, imi murege kusundirwa mhosva.”" 
Matthew28:15 Zvino vakatora mari, vakaita sezvavakadzidziswa, shoko iri rikaparidzirwa pakati pavaJudha, kusvikira zuva ranhasi." 
Matthew28:16 Zvino vadzidzi vane gumi nomumwe vakaenda Gareriya, kugomo ravakarayirwa naJesu." 
Matthew28:17 Vakati vachimuona, vakamupfugamira, asi vamwe vakanyunyuta." 
Matthew28:18 Ipapo Jesu akasvika, akataura kwavari, akati, “Ndakapiwa simba rose kudenga napanyika." 
Matthew28:19 Endai naizvozvo, mudzidzise marudzi ose, muvabhabhatidze muzita raBaba, neroMwanakomana, neroMweya Mutsvene;" 
Matthew28:20 muvadzidzise kuchengeta zvose zvandakakurairai tarirai, ndinemi mazuva ose, kusvikira pakuguma kwenyika.”" 
Mark1:1 Kutanga kweVhangeri yaJesu Kristu, Mwanakomana waMwari." 
Mark1:2 Sezvazvakanyorwa mumuporofita Isaya zvichinzi, “Tarira, ‘Ndinotuma munyai wangu pamberi pako,’ Achakunatsira nzira yako;" 
Mark1:3 Izwi raanodana murenje, ‘Gadzirai nzira yaIshe, Ruramisai migwagwa yake.’ ”" 
Mark1:4 Johani akauya achibhabhatidza murenje, achiparidza rubhabhatidzo rwokutendeuka kuti vanhu varegererwe zvivi zvavo." 
Mark1:5 Nyika yose yeJudhiya, navanhu veJerusaremu vose vakaenda kwaari, vakabhabhatidzwa naye muna Jodhani, vachireurura zvivi zvavo." 
Mark1:6 Johani akanga akapfeka nguo yamakushe engamera, nebhandi reganda muchiuno chake; aidya mhashu nouchi hwesango." 
Mark1:7 Akaparidza, achiti, “Shure kwangu kunouya mumwe ane simba kupfuureni, wandisino kufanira kukotama kuti ndisunungure rukanda rweshangu dzake." 
Mark1:8 Ini ndakakubhabhatidzai nemvura, asi iye achakubhabhatidzai naMweya Mutsvene.”" 
Mark1:9 Namazuva iwayo Jesu akabva Nazareta muGareriya, akabhabhatidzwa naJohani muna Jodhani." 
Mark1:10 Pakarepo achibuda mumvura, akaona denga richizarurwa, naMweya achiburukira pamusoro pake senjiva;" 
Mark1:11 izwi rikabva kudenga, richiti, “Ndiwe Mwanakomana wangu mudiwa, ndinokufarira.”" 
Mark1:12 Pakarepo Mweya akamubudisira kurenje; 
Mark1:13 akava murenje mazuva makumi mana, achiedzwa naSatani; akagara nezvikara, vatumwa vakamushumira." 
Mark1:14 Johani akati asungwa, Jesu akasvika Gareriya, achiparidza Vhangeri yaMwari," 
Mark1:15 achiti, “Nguva yazadziswa, ushe hwaMwari hwaswedera pedyo; tendeukai, mutende Vhangeri.”" 
Mark1:16 Akati achifamba pagungwa reGareriya, akaona Simoni, naAndireya, munun'una waSimoni, vachikandira usvasvi mugungwa, nokuti vakanga vari vabati vehove." 
Mark1:17 Jesu akati kwavari, “Nditeverei, kuti ndikuitei vabati vavanhu.”" 
Mark1:18 Vakasiya usvasvi hwavo pakarepo, vakamutevera." 
Mark1:19 Akati apfuura zvishoma, akaona Jakobho, mwanakomana waZebhedhi, naJohani munun'una wake, vachigadzira usvasvi muigwa." 
Mark1:20 Akavadana pakarepo, vakasiya baba vavo Zebhedhi muigwa navaranda, vakamutevera." 
Mark1:21 Vakapinda Kapenaume; pakarepo nomusi weSabata akapinda musinagoge, akadzidzisa." 
Mark1:22 Vakashamiswa nokudzidzisa kwake, nokuti akavadzidzisa somunhu ane chiremera, asingaiti savanyori." 
Mark1:23 Zvino musinagoge ravo makanga muno munhu akanga anomweya wakaipa, akadanidzira," 
Mark1:24 achiti, “Tine mhaka yeiko nemi, Jesu weNazareta? Mauya kuzotiparadza kanhi? Ndinokuzivai kuti ndimi ani; muri Mutsvene waMwari.”" 
Mark1:25 Zvino Jesu akamuraira; akati, “Nyarara, ubude kwaari!”" 
Mark1:26 Mweya wakaipa akamubvundisa, ndokudanidzira nezwi guru, ndokubuda kwaari." 
Mark1:27 Vakatya zvikuru vose, nokudaro vakaita nyaya, vachiti, “Chiiko ichi? Kudzidzisa kutsva kune simba! Anoraira kunyangwe nemweya yakaipa ikamuterera.”" 
Mark1:28 Pakarepo mukurumbira wake ukanzwika panyika yose yakapoteredza yeGareriya. 
Mark1:29 Pakarepo vakati vachibva musinagoge, vakapinda mumba maSimoni naAndireya, Jakobho naJohani vanavo." 
Mark1:30 Vambuya vaSimoni vakanga vavete vachirwara nefivha; pakarepo vakamuudza izvozvo. 
Mark1:31 Akaenda, akavabata noruoko, akavamutsa; fivha ikavarega, vakavashandira." 
Mark1:32 Madekwana, zuva ravira, vakaisa kwaari vose vakanga vachirwadziwa, navakanga vakabatwa nemweya yakaipa." 
Mark1:33 Guta rose rakanga raungana pamusuwo. 
Mark1:34 Akaporesa vazhinji vakanga vachirwadziwa namarudzi ehosha, akabudisa mweya yakaipa mizhinji; asi akanga asingatenderi mweya yakaipa kutaura, nokuti yakanga ichimuziva." 
Mark1:35 Mangwanani kuchine rima, akamuka akabuda, akaenda kunzvimbo murenje, akandonyengeterapo." 
Mark1:36 Simoni, navakanga vanaye, vakamutevera." 
Mark1:37 Vakamuwana, vakati kwaari, “Vose vanokutsvakai.”" 
Mark1:38 Akati kwavari, “Ngatiende kumwe, kumisha iri pedyo, kuti ndinoparidza ikokowo, nokuti ndizvo zvandakauyira.”" 
Mark1:39 Akaenda, akaparidza mumasinagoge avo muGareriya rose achibudisa mweya yakaipa." 
Mark1:40 Zvino munhu aiva namaperembudzi akauya kwaari, akakumbira zvikuru kwaari, ndokupfugama pamberi pake, akati kwaari, “Kana muchida henyu, munogona kundinatsa.”" 
Mark1:41 Akamunzwira ngoni, akatambanudza ruoko rwake, akamubata, akati kwaari, “Ndinoda, chinatswa.”" 
Mark1:42 Pakarepo maperembudzi akabva kwaari, akanatswa." 
Mark1:43 Zvino akamurayira kwazvo, akamuendesa pakarepo." 
Mark1:44 Akati kwaari, “Chenjera kuti urege kuudza munhu chinhu; asi enda uzviratidze kumupristi, ubayire pamusoro pokunatswa kwako zvakarairwa naMosesi, chive chapupu kwavari.”" 
Mark1:45 Asi iye akabuda, akatanga kuzviudza vanhu vazhinji, nokuparidzira shoko iro, nokudaro Jesu akanga asingagoni kupinda muguta pachena, asi akanga ari kunze panzvimbo murenje; vakauya kwaari vachibva kumativi ose." 
Mark2:1 Kwakati mazuva apfuura, akapindazve Kapenaume; vanhu vakanzwa kuti ari mumba." 
Mark2:2 Vazhinji vakaungana nokudaro vakashaiwa nzvimbo, kunyangwe pamusuwo; akavataurira shoko." 
Mark2:3 Vakauya vakaisa kwaari munhu akanga akafa mitezo, akatakurwa navanhu vana." 
Mark2:4 Zvino vakati vasingagoni kuswedera kwaari nokuda kwavazhinji, vakazarura denga paakanga ari; vakati variputsa, vakaburusa nhoo, pakanga pavete munhu akanga akafa mitezo;" 
Mark2:5 Jesu akati achiona kutenda kwavo, akati kuno akanga akafa mitezo, “Mwana, waregererwa zvivi zvako.”" 
Mark2:6 Zvino vamwe vanyori vakanga vegeremo, vakafunga mumwoyo yavo, vachiti," 
Mark2:7 “Uyu anorevereiko kudaro? Anoshonha Mwari; ndianiko anogona kuregerera zvivi, asi mumwechete, ndiye Mwari?”" 
Mark2:8 Pakarepo Jesu achiziva mumweya make kuti vanofunga kudaro mumwoyo yavo, akati kwavari, “Munofungireiko zvinhu izvi mumwoyo yenyu?" 
Mark2:9 Chakareruka ndechipiko, kuti kunowakafa mitezo, ‘Waregererwa zvivi zvako,’ kana kuti, ‘Simuka, tora nhoo dzako, ufambe?’" 
Mark2:10 “Asi kuti muzive kuti Mwanakomana womunhu ane simba panyika rokuregerera zvivi,” (akati kumunhu akanga akafa mitezo)," 
Mark2:11 “Ndinoti kwauri, simuka, tora nhoo dzako, uende kumba kwako!”" 
Mark2:12 Pakarepo akasimuka, akatora nhoo, ndokubuda pamberi pavo vose; naizvozvo vose vakashamiswa, vakarumbidza Mwari, vachiti, “Hatina kumboona zvakadai.”" 
Mark2:13 Akabudazve akaenda kugungwa; vazhinji vose vakauya kwaari, akavadzidzisa." 
Mark2:14 Akati achipfuura, akaona Revhi, mwanakomana waArifeusi, agere panotereswa, akati kwaari, “Nditevere.” Akasimuka, akamutevera." 
Mark2:15 Zvino akati agere pakudya mumba make, vateresi vazhinji navatadzi vakagara naJesu navadzidzi vake; nokuti vakanga vari vazhinji vaimutevera." 
Mark2:16 Zvino vanyori naVaFarisi vakati vachimuona achidya navatadzi navateresi, vakati kuvadzidzi vake, “Mudzidzisi anodyireiko navateresi navatadzi?”" 
Mark2:17 Jesu akati achizvinzwa, akati kwavari, “Vasingarwari havatsvaki murapi, asi vanorwara; handina kuuya kuzodana vakarurama, asi vatadzi.”" 
Mark2:18 Vadzidzi vaJohani naVaFarisi vakanga vachizvinyima zvokudya; vakauya vakati kwaari, “Vadzidzi vaJohani navadzidzi vaVaFarisi vanozvinyimireiko zvokudya, asi vadzidzi venyu havazvinyimi neiko?”" 
Mark2:19 Jesu akati kwavari, “Shamwari dzemuwani dzingazvinyima zvokudya seiko achiri kwavari? Havangazvinyimi zvokudya muwani achiri kwavari." 
Mark2:20 “Asi mazuva achasvika, achazobviswa muwani kwavari; zvino nenguva iyo vachazvinyima zvokudya." 
Mark2:21 “Hakuna munhu anosonera chiremo chitsva panguo yakasakara, nokuti chiremo chitsva chinobvarura nguo yakasakara, buri rikanyanya." 
Mark2:22 “Hakuna munhu anodira waini itsva muhombodo tsaru; nokuti waini inoparusa hombodo, waini nehombodo zvikafa; asi waini itsva inodirwa muhombodo itsva.”" 
Mark2:23 Kwakati nomusi weSabata, achifamba napakati peminda, vadzidzi vake vakatanga kupurura hura vachifamba." 
Mark2:24 VaFarisi vakati kwaari, “Tarirai, vanoitireiko zvisina kutenderwa nomusi weSabata?”" 
Mark2:25 Akati kwavari, “Hamuna kurava here zvakaitwa naDhavhidhi, musi waakanga ashaiwa zvokudya, aziya, iye navakanga vanaye?" 
Mark2:26 Kuti akapinda mumba maMwari, Abhiatari ari Mupristi Mukuru, akadya zvingwa zvokuratidza Mwari zvakanga zvisina kutenderwa kudyiwa, asi navapristi voga, akapawo vaiva naye?”" 
Mark2:27 Akati kwavari, “Sabata rakaitirwa munhu, munhu haana kuitirwa Sabata;" 
Mark2:28 naizvozvo Mwanakomana womunhu ndiye Ishe weSabatawo.” 
Mark3:1 Akapindazve musinagoge; zvino kwakanga kune munhu akanga ane ruoko rwakakokonyara. 
Mark3:2 Vakamutarisisa kuona kana angamuporesa nomusi weSabata; kuti vamupomere mhosva. 
Mark3:3 Zvino akati kumunhu akanga ano ruoko rwakakokonyara, “Simuka pakati pavo!”" 
Mark3:4 Akati kwavari, “Zvakatenderwa here neSabata kuita zvakanaka kana zvakaipa, kuponesa munhu kana kuuraya?” Vakanyarara." 
Mark3:5 Zvino akati aringa–ringa achivatarira nokutsamwa, ane shungu nokuda kwokuoma kwemwoyo yavo, akati kumunhu, “Tambanudza ruoko rwako.” Akarutambanudza, ruoko rwake rukapora." 
Mark3:6 Zvino VaFarisi vakati vabuda, vakandorangana pakarepo navaHerodhi pamusoro pake kuti vangamuuraya sei." 
Mark3:7 Zvino Jesu akaenda navadzidzi vake kugungwa; vanhu vazhinji–zhinji vakamutevera vachibva Gareriya; nokuJudhiya," 
Mark3:8 neJerusaremu, neIdhumia, nemhiri kwaJodhani, nokunyika yeTaya neSidhoni, vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakati vanzwa zvaanoita, vakauya kwaari." 
Mark3:9 Akaudza vadzidzi vake kuti igwa rigare nokuda kwavazhinji, kuti varege kumutsikirira." 
Mark3:10 Nokuti akanga aporesa vazhinji; naizvozvo vose vakanga vaine zvirwere vaitsikinyidzana, kuti vachida kumubata panguva imwechete." 
Mark3:11 Nemweya yakaipa yakati kana yamuona, yaiwira pasi pamberi pake, ikadanidzira ichiti, “Ndiwe Mwanakomana waMwari!”" 
Mark3:12 Akairayira zvikuru kuti irege kumuzivisa pachena. 
Mark3:13 Zvino akakwira mugomo akadana vaakanga achida, vakauya kwaari." 
Mark3:14 Akagadza vane gumi navaviri kuti vagare naye, avatume kuti vaparidze," 
Mark3:15 uye vave nesimba rokubudisa mweya yakaipa. 
Mark3:16 Akatumidza Simoni zita rinonzi Petirosi," 
Mark3:17 naJakobho, mwanakomana waZebhedhi, naJohani, munun'una waJakobho; akavatumidza ivo mazita anonzi Bhoanerigesi, ndokuti “Vanakomana vokutinhira;”" 
Mark3:18 naAndireya, naFiripi, naBhatoromiyo, naTomasi, naJakobho mwanakomana waArifeusi, naTadhiasi, naSimoni muKenani," 
Mark3:19 naJudhasi Isikarioti akazomupandukirawo. Zvino akapinda mumba," 
Mark3:20 vazhinji vakaunganazve, nokudaro vakanga vasingagoni kunyangwe kudya chingwa." 
Mark3:21 Vanhu vokwake vakati vachizvinzwa, vakabuda kuzomubata, nokuti vakati, “Anopenga.”" 
Mark3:22 Navanyori vakanga vaburuka vachibva Jerusaremu, vakati, “Ana Bheerizebhuri, anobudisa mweya yakaipa nomuchinda wemweya yakaipa.”" 
Mark3:23 Zvino akavadanira kwaari, akati kwavari nemifananidzo. “Satani angabudisa Satani seiko?" 
Mark3:24 Kana ushe huchizvipesanisa, ushe uhwo hahungagoni kumira." 
Mark3:25 Kana imba ichizvipesanisa, imba iyo haingagoni kumira." 
Mark3:26 Kana Satani achizvimukira, akazvipesanisa, haangagoni kumira, asi anopera." 
Mark3:27 “Hakuna munhu angapinda mumba moane simba, akatora nhumbi dzake, asati ambosunga ane simba; zvino angaparadza imba yake." 
Mark3:28 “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, vanakomana vavanhu vacharegererwa zvivi zvose, nokushonha kwose kwavanoshonha Mwari nako;" 
Mark3:29 asi ani naani ashonha Mweya Mutsvene, haangaregerwi nokusingaperi, asi ane mhosva yechivi chisingaperi.”" 
Mark3:30 Nokuti vakati, “Ano mweya wakaipa.”" 
Mark3:31 Zvino mai vake navanun'una vake vakauya, vakamira kunze, vakatumira nhume kwaari, kumudana." 
Mark3:32 Vazhinji vakanga vagere, vakamukomba, vakati kwaari, “Tarirai, mai venyu navanun'una venyu navakoma nehanzvadzi dzenyu vari kunze vachikutsvakai.”" 
Mark3:33 Akavapindura, akati, “Mai vangu, vakoma navanun'una vangu ndivanaaniko?”" 
Mark3:34 Zvino akaringa–ringa vanhu vakanga vagere, vakamukomba, akati, “Tarirai mai vanhu navakoma navanun'una vangu!" 
Mark3:35 “Nokuti ani naani anoita kuda kwaMwari, ndiye mukoma nomunun'una wangu, nehanzvadzi, naamai.”" 
Mark4:1 Zvino akatangazve kudzidzisa pagungwa; vanhu vazhinji–zhinji vakaunganira kwaari, nokudaro akapinda muigwa, akagaramo; vazhinji vose vakanga vari pedyo negungwa pamhenderekedzo." 
Mark4:2 Akavadzidzisa zvizhinji nemifananidzo, akati kwavari pakudzidzisa kwake," 
Mark4:3 “Teererai, Mukushi akabuda kundokusha." 
Mark4:4 Akati achikusha, dzimwe mbeu dzakawira panzira; shiri dzikauya dzikadzidya." 
Mark4:5 Dzimwe dzakawira parukangarabwe, padzakanga dzisina ivhu zhinji; dzikamera pakarepo, nokuti dzakanga dzisina ivhu rakadzika;" 
Mark4:6 asi zuva rakati rabuda, dzikapiswa; dzikaoma, nokuti dzakanga dzisina mudzi." 
Mark4:7 “Dzimwe dzakawira muminzwa; minzwa ikamera, ikadzivhunga, dzikasaita vana." 
Mark4:8 Dzimwe dzakawira muvhu rakanaka, dzikaita vana, nokuti dzakakura, dzikawanza; dzikabereka makumi matatu, namakumi matanhatu, nezana.”" 
Mark4:9 Akati, “Ane nzeve dzokunzwa, ngaanzwe.”" 
Mark4:10 Akati ari oga, vakanga vanaye vane gumi navaviri vakamubvunza zvemifananidzo." 
Mark4:11 Akati kwavari, “Imi makapiwa kuziva zvakavanzika zvoushe hwaMwari, asi kuna ava, vari kunze, zvose zvinoitwa nemifananidzo," 
Mark4:12 kuti, kuona vaone, asi varege kuonesesa, nokunzwa vanzwe, asi varege kunzwisisa, kuti zvimwe varege kutendeuka, vakaregererwa zvivi zvavo.”" 
Mark4:13 Zvino akati kwavari, “Hamuzivi here mufananidzo uyu? Muchaziva seiko mifananidzo yose?" 
Mark4:14 Mukushi ndiye anokusha shoko. 
Mark4:15 Vari munzira panokushwa shoko ndivo vanoti kana vanzwa, pakarepo Satani anouya, ndokubvisa shoko rakakushwa mavari." 
Mark4:16 Navakakushwa parukangarabwe vakaita saizvozvo, ndivo vanoti kana vanzwa shoko rakakushwa, vanorigamuchira pakarepo nomufaro," 
Mark4:17 asi havana mudzi mavari, asi ndivo vechinguva chiduku; pashure kana kutambudzika nokuvengwa zvichiuya nokuda kweshoko, pakarepo vanogumburwa." 
Mark4:18 “Vamwe vanokushwa muminzwa, ndivo vanonzwa shoko," 
Mark4:19 asi kufunganya kwenyika nokunyengera kwepfuma, nokuchiva zvimwe, kunopinda, kuchivhunga shoko, rikashaiwa zvibereko." 
Mark4:20 “Vakakushwa muvhu rakanaka, ndivo vanonzwa shoko, vakarigamuchira, vakabereka, mumwe makumi matatu, mumwe makumi matanhatu, mumwe zana.”" 
Mark4:21 Zvino akati kwavari, “Mwenje uripo kuti uiswe pasi pedengu, kana pasi pomubhedha here? Hausipo kuti uiswe pachigadziko here?" 
Mark4:22 Nokuti hapana chinhu chakavanzika chisingazooneswi, hapana chavigwa chisingazobudi pachena." 
Mark4:23 Kana munhu ane nzeve dzokunzwa, ngaanzwe.”" 
Mark4:24 Zvino akati kwavari, “Chenjerai zvamunonzwa. Chiero chamunoera nacho, nemi muchaerwa nacho; mukawedzerwa." 
Mark4:25 Nokuti uya ane chaanacho achapiwa, asi uya asina, achatorerwa kunyangwe nechaanacho.”" 
Mark4:26 Zvino akati, “Ushe hwaMwari hwakafanana nomunhu anodyara mbeu muvhu," 
Mark4:27 akavata, akamuka, usiku namasikati; mbeu inomera, ichikura, iye asingazivi kuti zvinoitika sei;" 
Mark4:28 ivhu rinongobereka haro, pakutanga chipande, pashure hura, pashure zviyo zvakakora pahura." 
Mark4:29 Kana yaibva, pakarepo anocheka nejeko, nokuti kukohwa kwasvika.”" 
Mark4:30 Zvino akati, “Ushe hwaMwari tichahufananidza neiko? Tichahuenzanisira nomufananidzo upiko?" 
Mark4:31 Hwakafanana netsanga yemasitadhi, iyo kana ichidyarwa muvhu iduku kumbeu dzose dzapanyika;" 
Mark4:32 asi kana yadyarwa, inomera, ichiva huru kumiriwo yose ichiita matavi makuru, akadaro kuti shiri dzedenga dzinovakira matendere adzo imomo.”" 
Mark4:33 Akasireva shoko kwavari nemifananidzo mizhinji yakadaro, pavaigona kunzwa napo." 
Mark4:34 Haana kutaura navo kunze kwemifananidzo, asi waizodudzira vadzidzi vake zvose vari voga." 
Mark4:35 Zvino nezuva iro, ava madekwana, akati kwavari, “Ngatiyambukire mhiri.”" 
Mark4:36 Vakasiya vanhu vazhinji, vakaenda naye muigwa akangodaro; mamwe magwa akanga akamutevera." 
Mark4:37 Zvino dutu guru remhepo rakamuka, mafungu emvura akarova achipinda muigwa, rikanga roda kuzara." 
Mark4:38 Asi iye akanga ari mushure megwa avete pamutsago; vakamumutsa, vakati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, hamune hanya kuti tofa here?”" 
Mark4:39 Akamuka, akarayira mhepo, akati kugungwa, “Nyarara, ugadzikane!” Mhepo ikanyarara, kudzikama kukuru kukavapo." 
Mark4:40 Zvino akati kwavari, “Munotyireiko kudaro? Hamuna kutenda here?”" 
Mark4:41 Vakatya nokutya kukuru, vakataurirana vachiti, “Ndianiko uyu, nokuti mhepo kunyangwe negungwa zvinomuteerera?”" 
Mark5:1 Vakasvika mhiri kwegungwa kunyika yavaGerasa. 
Mark5:2 Zvino akati abuda muigwa, pakarepo akasangana nomunhu aiva nomweya wakaipa, achibva kumarinda." 
Mark5:3 Uyo aigara mumarinda; kwakanga kusino munhu akanga achagona kumusunga kunyangwe nengetani. 
Mark5:4 Nokuti kazhinji aisungwa nezvisungo zvamakumbo nengetani, asi aidambura ngetani, nokudashura zvisungo; kwakanga kusino munhu aigona kumudzikamisa." 
Mark5:5 Nguva dzose, usiku namasikati, aigara mumarinda nomumakomo, achiridza mhere, achizvicheka namabwe." 
Mark5:6 Zvino akati achiona Jesu ari kure, akamhanya, ndokumupfugamira;" 
Mark5:7 akadanidzira nezwi guru, akati, “Ndine mhaka yeiko nemi Jesu, Mwanakomana waMwari Wokumusoro–soro? Ndinokupikirai naMwari kuti murege kunditambudza.”" 
Mark5:8 Nokuti akati kwaari, “Buda pamunhu, iwe mweya wakaipa!”" 
Mark5:9 Akamubvunza, akati, “Zita rako ndianiko?” Akati kwaari, “Ndinonzi Regioni, nokuti tiri vazhinji.”" 
Mark5:10 Akakumbira zvikuru kwaari kuti arege kuidzinga panyika iyo. 
Mark5:11 Zvino kwakanga kuine pagomo boka guru renguruve dzakanga dzichifura. 
Mark5:12 Ikakumbira zvikuru kwaari, ichiti, “Titumirei kunguruve, kuti tindopinda madziri.”" 
Mark5:13 Akaitendera. Mweya yakaipa ikabuda, ikapinda munguruve; boka rikamhanyira kumawere kugungwa, dzinenge dzaiva zviuru zviviri, dzikafira mugungwa." 
Mark5:14 Vaidzifudza vakatiza, vakandoudza izvozvo muguta nomumaruwa. Vanhu vakauya kuzoona zvaitwa." 
Mark5:15 Vakauya kuna Jesu, vakaona akanga ane mweya yakaipa agere, apfeka, ari munhu kwaye iye aiva neRegioni; vakatya." 
Mark5:16 Vaya vakanga vazviona, vakarondedzera zvaakaitirwa iye akanga ane mweya yakaipa, nenguruvewo." 
Mark5:17 Vakatanga kukumbira zvikuru kwaari kuti abve munyika yavo. 
Mark5:18 Zvino akati achipinda muigwa, iye aiva nemweya yakaipa akakumbira zvikuru kwaari kuti agare naye." 
Mark5:19 Asi haana kumutendera, asi akati kwaari, “Enda kumba kwako, kuhama dzako, uvaudze zvinhu zvikuru zvawakaitirwa naIshe, napawakaitirwa ngoni napo.”" 
Mark5:20 Akaenda, akatanga kuparidza munyika yeDhekaporisi zvinhu zvikuru zvaakaitirwa naJesu; vakashamiswa vose." 
Mark5:21 Jesu akati ayambukirazve mhiri negwa, vanhu vazhinji vakaunganira kwaari; akanga ari pagungwa." 
Mark5:22 Mumwe wavakuru vesinagoge, wainzi Jairosi, akasvika; akati achimuona, akazviwisira pasi petsoka dzake," 
Mark5:23 akakumbira zvikuru kwaari, achiti, “Mukunda wangu muduku wotandadza, uyai, muise maoko enyu pamusoro pake aporeswe, ararame.”" 
Mark5:24 Akaenda naye; vanhu vazhinji vakamutevera, vachimutsikirira." 
Mark5:25 Zvino mumwe mukadzi aiva nokurwara kwokubuda ropa makore ane gumi namaviri," 
Mark5:26 akanga aoneswa nhamo nevarapi vazhinji, akapedza zvose zvaakanga anazvo asina kutongobatsirwa, asi kungonyanyiswa," 
Mark5:27 akati anzwa zvaJesu, akauya pakati pavanhu vazhinji vaiva mashure, akabata nguo yake." 
Mark5:28 Nokuti akati, “Kana ndikabata nguo yake bedzi, ndichaponeswa.”" 
Mark5:29 Pakarepo tsime rake reropa rikapwa, akanzwa pamuviri wake kuti aporeswa pakurwara kwake." 
Mark5:30 Pakarepo Jesu akati achiziva mukati make kuti simba rakabuda kwaari, akatendeuka pakati pavanhu vazhinji, akati, “Ndianiko abata nguo dzangu?”" 
Mark5:31 Vadzidzi vake vakati kwaari, “Munoona vanhu vazhinji vanokutsikirirai, zvino mungati seiko, ndiani andibata?”" 
Mark5:32 Zvino akaringa–ringa kuti aone akaita izvozvo. 
Mark5:33 Mukadzi akatya, akadedera, achiziva zvaaitirwa, akauya, ndokuzviwisira pamberi pake, ndokumuudza zvirokwazvo zvose." 
Mark5:34 Akati kwaari, “Mukunda, kutenda kwako kwakuponesa; enda norugare, upore pakurwara kwako.”" 
Mark5:35 Akati achataura, vamwe veimba yomukuru wesinagoge vakasvika, vakati, “Mukunda wenyu afa; muchatambudzireiko Mudzidzisi?”" 
Mark5:36 Jesu akati achinzwa shoko rataurwa, akati kumukuru wesinagoge, “Usatya, tenda bedzi.”" 
Mark5:37 Akasatendera munhu kumutevera, asi Petirosi, naJakobho, naJohani munun'una waJakobho." 
Mark5:38 Vakasvika mumba momukuru wesinagoge; akawana iri mhere–mhere, navanochema zvikuru, navanorira." 
Mark5:39 Akapinda, akati kwavari, “Munoitireiko mhere–mhere, muchichema? Mwana haana kufa, asi avete.”" 
Mark5:40 Vakamuseka. Akavabudisa vose, akatora baba vomwana namai, navaakanga anavo, akapinda kwakanga kuno mwana." 
Mark5:41 Akabata ruoko rwomwana, akati kwaari, “Tarita kumi!” Ndokuti, “Kana zvichishandurwa, Musikana, ndinoti kwauri, muka!”" 
Mark5:42 Pakarepo musikana akasimuka, akafamba; nokuti waiva namakore ane gumi namaviri; vakashamiswa nokushama kukuru." 
Mark5:43 Akavaraira zvikuru kuti zvirege kuziikanwa nomunhu; akati musikana ungapiwe zvokudya. 
Mark6:1 Akabvapo, akasvika kunyika yake, vadzidzi vake vakamutevera." 
Mark6:2 Musi weSabata wakati wasvika, akatanga kudzidzisa musinagoge; vanhu vazhinji vakati vachimunzwa, vakashamiswa, vachiti, “Munhu uyu awanepiko izvozvi? Kuchenjera kwakapiwa munhu uyu ndokweiko? Namabasa esimba akadai anoitwa namaoko ake?" 
Mark6:3 Ko uyu haasi muvezi here, mwanakomana waMaria, nomukoma waJakobho, naJose, naJudha, naSimoni? Nehanzvadzi dzake hadzisi pano pakati patiri here?” Vakagumburwa naye." 
Mark6:4 Jesu akati kwavari, “Muporofita haangashayiwi kukudzwa, asi munyika yake, nokuhama dzake, nomumba make.”" 
Mark6:5 Akasagona kubata basa resimba ipapo, asi akaisa maoko ake pamusoro pavairwara vashoma, akavaporesa." 
Mark6:6 Akashamiswa nokusatenda kwavo. Ipapo akapota nemisha, achidzidzisa." 
Mark6:7 Zvino akadanira kwaari vane gumi navaviri, akatanga kuvatuma vaviri vaviri, akavapa simba pamusoro pemweya yakaipa;" 
Mark6:8 akavaraira kuti “Varege kutongotora zvomunzira, asi mudonzvo bedzi; varege kutora chingwa, nehombodo, nemari muchikwama." 
Mark6:9 Asi vapfeke shangu, varege kupfeka nguo mbiri.”" 
Mark6:10 Akati kwavari; “Pose pamunopinda mumba, mugaremo, kusvikira muchibvapo." 
Mark6:11 Pose pavasingakugamuchirii nokukunzwai, kana muchibvapo, muzunze guruva riri patsoka dzenyu, chive chapupu kwavari.”" 
Mark6:12 Vakabuda, vakaparidza kuti vanhu vatendeuke." 
Mark6:13 Vakabudisa mweya yakaipa mizhinji, vakazodza vazhinji vairwara mafuta, vachivaporesa." 
Mark6:14 Zvino mambo Herodhi akazvinzwa, nokuti zita rake rakanga rakurumbira, akati, “Johani Mubhabhatidzi akamuka kuvakafa, saka masimba aya anobata maari.”" 
Mark6:15 Vamwe vakati, “NdiEriya;” vamwe vakati, “Muporofita, akafanana nomumwe wavaporofita.”" 
Mark6:16 Asi Herodhi akati achizvinzwa, akati, “NdiJohani akamuka, uya wandakagura musoro.”" 
Mark6:17 Nokuti Herodhi akanga atuma vanhu, akabata Johani, akamusunga mujeri nokuda kwaHerodhiasi, mukadzi waFiripi, munun'una wake, nokuti akanga amuwana." 
Mark6:18 Nokuti Johani akanga ati kuna Herodhi, “Hauna kutenderwa kuti uve nomukadzi womunun'una wako.”" 
Mark6:19 Herodhiasi akamuvenga, akada kumuuraya, akasagona;" 
Mark6:20 nokuti Herodhi akanga achitya Johani, achiziva kuti munhu akarurama, mutsvene, akamuchengeta zvakanaka. Akati amunzwa, akatambudzika kwazvo kunyangwe zvakadaro, aisafanira kumunzwa." 
Mark6:21 Asi zuva rakafanira rakati rasvika, Herodhi nezuva rokupemberera kuberekwa kwake akaitira madzishe ake navakuru vezviuru zvamazana navakuru veGareriya mutambo mukuru;" 
Mark6:22 zvino mwanasikana waHerodhiasi amene akapinda, akatamba, akafadza Herodhi navakanga vagere pakudya naye; mambo akati kumwanasikana, “Kumbira kwandiri chaunoda, ndikupe.”" 
Mark6:23 Akamupikira, achiti, “Chaunokumbira kwandiri ndichakupa, kusvikira pahafu youshe hwangu.”" 
Mark6:24 Akabuda, akati kuna amai vake, “Ndichakumbireiko?” Vakati, “Musoro waJohani Mubhabhatidzi.”" 
Mark6:25 Pakarepo akakurumidza kupinda kuna mambo, akakumbira achiti, “Ndinoda kuti mundipe mundiro ikozvino musoro waJohani Mubhabhatidzi.”" 
Mark6:26 Ipapo mambo akazvidya mwoyo kwazvo, asi akanga asingadi kumurambira nokuda kwokupika kwake, uye nokuda kwavakanga vagere naye pakudya." 
Mark6:27 Pakarepo mambo akatuma musoja, akaraira kuti auye nomusoro wake." 
Mark6:28 Akaenda, akamugura musoro mujeri, akauya nomusoro wake mundiro, akaupa musikana, musikana ndokuupa mai vake." 
Mark6:29 Vadzidzi vake vakati vachizvinzwa, vakauya vakatora chitunha chake, vakachiviga muhwiro." 
Mark6:30 Zvino vapostori vakaunganira kuna Jesu, vakamuudza zvose zvavakanga vaita, nezvavakanga vadzidzisa." 
Mark6:31 Akati kwavari, “Uyai imi muri moga tiende kunzvimbo yerenje, muzorore zvishoma;” nokuti kwakanga kuna vazhinji vaiuya navaienda, vakasava nenguva kunyangwe yokudya." 
Mark6:32 Vakaenda negwa kunzvimbo isina vanhu vari voga. 
Mark6:33 Vanhu vakavaona vachienda, vazhinji vakamuziva, vakamhanyira vose ikoko, vachibva pamaguta ose, vakavatangira kusvika." 
Mark6:34 Zvino akati achibuda muigwa, akaona vazhinji zhinji, akavanzwira tsitsi, nokuti vakanga vakafanana namakwai asina mufudzi; akatanga kuvadzidzisa zvizhinji." 
Mark6:35 Zvino zuva roda kuvira, vadzidzi vake vakauya kwaari, vakati, “Ino inzvimbo yerenje, zuva roda kuvira;" 
Mark6:36 vaendisei; kuti vaende kuruwa nemisha yakapoteredza, vandozvitengera zvokudya.”" 
Mark6:37 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Imi vapei zvavangadya.” Vakati kwaari, “Tingaenda kundotenga zvingwa nemadhinari ana mazana maviri, tivape vadye here?”" 
Mark6:38 Akati kwavari, “Mune zvingwa zvinganiko? Endai mutarire.” Vakati vaziva, vakati, “Zvishanu, nehove mbiri.”" 
Mark6:39 Zvino akavaraira kuti vagarise vose pasi pauswa hunyoro vakaita mapoka–mapoka. 
Mark6:40 Vakagara pasi vakaita mapoka–mapoka ane zana naana makumi mashanu. 
Mark6:41 Zvino akatora zvingwa zvishanu nehove mbiri, akatarira kudenga, akavonga, akamedura zvingwa, akapa vadzidzi vake, kuti vazviise pamberi pavo; nehove mbiri akadzigovera vose." 
Mark6:42 Vakadya vose, vakaguta." 
Mark6:43 Vakaunganidza zvimedu nezvehovewo, matengu ane gumi namaviri akazadzwa." 
Mark6:44 Vakanga vadya zvingwa vaiva varume vane zviuru zvishanu. 
Mark6:45 Pakarepo akagombedzera vadzidzi vake kuti vapinde muigwa, vamutungamirire kuyambukira mhiri Bhetisaidha, iye achiendesa vanhu vazhinji." 
Mark6:46 Akati aonekana navo, akaenda mugomo kundonyengetera." 
Mark6:47 Ava madekwana igwa rakanga riri pakati pegungwa, iye ari oga panyika." 
Mark6:48 Zvino akati achiona kuti vanotambudzika nokukwasva, nokuti mhepo yakanga ichivadzivisa, nenguva inenge seyechina yousiku, akauya kwavari achifamba pamusoro pegungwa; akada kupfuura." 
Mark6:49 Zvino vakati vachimuona achifamba pamusoro pegungwa, vakati “Mudzimudzangara,” vakaridza mhere." 
Mark6:50 Nokuti vose vakamuona, vakakundiswa; akataura navo, akati kwavari, “Tsungai mwoyo, ndini, musatya.”" 
Mark6:51 Akakwira kwavari muigwa, mhepo ikanyarara; vakashamiswa kwazvo–kwazvo mumwoyo yavo." 
Mark6:52 Nokuti vakanga vasati vanzwisisa shoko rezvingwa, nokuti mwoyo yavo yakanga iri mikukutu." 
Mark6:53 Vakati vayambukira mhiri, vakasvika kunyika yeGenesareti, vakasungira igwa pamhenderekedzo." 
Mark6:54 Vakati vabuda muigwa, pakarepo vanhu vakamuziva," 
Mark6:55 vakamhanyira munyika yose iyo, vakatanga kutakura vairwara panhoo dzavo, vakavaisa pavainzwa kuti ndiko kwaari." 
Mark6:56 Pose paakapinda pamisha napamaguta, naparuwa vakaradzika vairwara padare, vakakumbira zvikuru kwaari kuti vabate kunyangwe mupendero wenguo dzake chete; vose vakamubata vakaporeswa." 
Mark7:1 Zvino VaFarisi navamwe vavanyori vaibva Jerusaremu, vakaunganira kwaari;" 
Mark7:2 vakaona vamwe vadzidzi vake vachidya namaoko ane tsvina, ndokuti asina kushambwa." 
Mark7:3 Nokuti VaFarisi, navaJudha vose havadyi vasina kumboshamba maoko kwazvo, vachichengeta tsika dzavakuru." 
Mark7:4 Kana vachibva kumusika havangadyi vasina kumboshamba; nezvimwe zvizhinji zviripo zvavakanga vagamuchira, kuti vazvichengete, zvinoti: Kusuka mikombe, nehari, nemidziyo yendarira." 
Mark7:5 Ipapo VaFarisi navanyori vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Vadzidzi venyu vanoregereiko kufamba netsika dzavakuru, zvavanodya chingwa namaoko ane tsvina?”" 
Mark7:6 Akati kwavari, “Isaya akaporofita kwazvo pamusoro penyu, imi vanyengeri, sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, ‘Vanhu ava vanondikudza nemiromo yavo, Asi mwoyo yavo iri kure neni." 
Mark7:7 Asi vanondinamata pasina, Vachidzidzisa zvakatemwa navanhu, sokunge zvidzidziso zvechokwadi.’" 
Mark7:8 “Munosiya mirairo yaMwari, muchichengeta tsika dzavanhu.”" 
Mark7:9 Akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo, munoramba murairo waMwari, kuti muchengete tsika dzenyu;" 
Mark7:10 nokuti Mosesi akati, ‘Kudza baba vako namai vako, uye anotuka baba namai, ngaafe norufu.’" 
Mark7:11 “Asi imi munoti, kana munhu achiti kuna baba vake kana mai vake, ‘Chinhu chipi nechipi chamaiti munobatsirwa nacho kwandiri chava Koribhani,’ ndokuti chava chipo chaMwari," 
Mark7:12 hamuchamutenderi kuitira baba vake namai vake chinhu," 
Mark7:13 muchitorera shoko raMwari simba netsika dzenyu dzamakachengeta, nezvinhu zvizhinji zvakadaro munozviita.”" 
Mark7:14 Akadanirazve kwaari vanhu vazhinji akati kwavari, “Nditererei mose, munzwisise!" 
Mark7:15 “Hapana chinhu kunze kwomunhu chingamusvibisa, kana chichipinda maari; asi zvinobuda maari, ndizvo zvinosvibisa munhu.” [" 
Mark7:16 Kana munhu ane nzeve dzokunzwa, ngaanzwe.]" 
Mark7:17 Zvino akati abva kuvanhu vazhinji, apinda mumba, vadzidzi vake vakamubvunza zvomufananidzo uyo." 
Mark7:18 Akati kwavari, “Nemiwo hamunzwisisi saizvozvo here? Hamunzwisisi here kuti zvose zviri kunze, kana zvichipinda mumunhu, hazvigoni kumusvibisa?" 
Mark7:19 “Nokuti hazvipindi mumwoyo make asi mudumbu, zvichiraswa kunze. Nokutaura kwakadaro akanatsa zvokudya zvose.”" 
Mark7:20 Ipapo akati, “Zvinobuda mumunhu ndizvo zvinosvibisa munhu." 
Mark7:21 Nokuti mukati, mumwoyo yavanhu munobuda mifungo yakaipa, noupombwe, nokuba, nokuuraya," 
Mark7:22 noupfeve, noruchiva, nokuipa, nokunyengera, noutere, neziso rine godo, nokutuka, namanyawi, noupenzi;" 
Mark7:23 zvakaipa izvozvo zvose zvinobva mukati, zvinosvibisa munhu.”" 
Mark7:24 Akasimuka ipapo, akaenda kunyika yeTaya neSidhoni; akapinda mumba, asingadi kuzikanwa nomunhu; akakoniwa kuzvivanza." 
Mark7:25 Nokuti mumwe mukadzi, aiva nomwanasikana muduku, akanga ane mweya wakaipa, akati achimunzwa, akauya akazviwisira pasi petsoka dzake." 
Mark7:26 Zvino iye mukadzi aiva muGiriki, worudzi rwaveSairofonishia; akaramba achikumbira kwaari kuti abudise mweya wakaipa pamwanasikana wake." 
Mark7:27 Akati kwaari, “Vana ngavatange kuguta, nokuti hazvina kunaka kutora chingwa chavana, ndokuchikandira mbwanana.”" 
Mark7:28 Akapindura, akati kwaari, “Hongu, Ishe, kunyangwe nembwananawo dzinodya pasi petafura zvimedu zvavana.”" 
Mark7:29 Akati kwaari, “Nokuda kweshoko iro, enda; mweya wakaipa wabva pamwanasikana wako.”" 
Mark7:30 Akaenda kumba kwake, akawana mwana avete pamubhedha, mweya wakaipa wabva." 
Mark7:31 Zvino akati achibvazve munyika yeTaya, akaenda napakati peSidhoni kuGungwa reGareriya, napakati penyika yeDhekaporisi." 
Mark7:32 Vakaisa kwaari munhu wematsi, aiva mbeveve, vakakumbira zvikuru kuti aise ruoko rwake pamusoro pake." 
Mark7:33 Akamubvisa pakati pavanhu vazhinji, ndokuenda naye parutivi, akapinza munwe munzeve dzake, akapfira mate, ndokubata rurimi rwake." 
Mark7:34 Ipapo akatarira kudenga, akagomera, akati kwaari, “Efata,” ndokuti, “Dziuka.”" 
Mark7:35 Pakarepo nzeve dzake dzakavhurika, chisungo chorurimi rwake chikasununguka, akataura zvakanaka." 
Mark7:36 Zvino akavaraira, kuti varege kuudza vanhu; asi iye achinyanya kuvarayira, ivo vakanyanyisa kuparidza izvozvo." 
Mark7:37 Vakashamiswa zvikuru–kuru, vachiti, “Akaita zvose zvakanaka; akaita matsi kuti dzinzwe, nembeveve kuti dzitaure.”" 
Mark8:1 Namazuva iwayozve kwakanga kuna vazhinji zhinji, vakanga vasina zvavangadya, akadanira vadzidzi vake kwaari, akati kwavari," 
Mark8:2 “Ndine tsitsi navanhu vazhinji, nokuti atova mazuva matatu avakagara neni vasina zvavangadya." 
Mark8:3 Kana ndikavaendesa kumusha kwavo vane nzara, vachaziya panzira; vamwe vavo vanobva kure.”" 
Mark8:4 Vadzidzi vake vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Munhu angawanepiko murenje muno, zvingwa zvingagutisa vanhu ava?”" 
Mark8:5 Akavabvunza, akati, “Mune zvingwa zvinganiko?” Vakati, “Zvinomwe.”" 
Mark8:6 Zvino akarayira vanhu vazhinji kuti vagare pasi, akatora zvingwa zvinomwe, akavonga, akazvimedura, ndokupa vadzidzi vake, kuti vaise pamberi pavo; vakazviisa pamberi pavazhinji." 
Mark8:7 Uye vakanga vane hove duku shomanene; zvino akatenda, Mwari akati zviiswewo pamberi pavo." 
Mark8:8 Vakadya, vakaguta, ndokuunganidza zvimedu zvakasara, matengu manomwe." 
Mark8:9 Vanenge vaiva zviuru zvina; akavaendesa. 
Mark8:10 Pakarepo akapinda muigwa navadzidzi vake, akasvika kumativi enyika yeDharimanuta." 
Mark8:11 Zvino VaFarisi vakabuda, vakatanga kuita nyaya naye, vachitsvaka kwaari chiratidzo chinobva kudenga, vachimuedza." 
Mark8:12 Akagomera zvikuru mumweya make, akati “Rudzi urwu runotsvakireiko chiratidzo? Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, rudzi urwu harungapiwi chiratidzo.”"
