Mark8:13 Ipapo akavasiya, akapindazve muigwa, akayambukira mhiri." 
Mark8:14 Vakanga vakanganwa kutora zvingwa muigwa; vakanga vasina zvingwa muigwa, asi chimwe bedzi." 
Mark8:15 Zvino akavaraira, akati, “Chenjerai, mutye mbiriso yaVaFarisi nembiriso yaHerodhi.”" 
Mark8:16 Vakarangana vakati, “Anodaro nokuti hatine zvingwa.”" 
Mark8:17 Zvino Jesu akati achizviziva, akati kwavari, “Munorangana nemhaka yeiko kuti hamune zvingwa? Hamuzivi, nokunzwisisa here? Mwoyo yenyu ichiri mikukutu here?" 
Mark8:18 Zvamuna meso, hamuoni here? Zvamune nzeve, hamunzwi here? Hamurangariri here?" 
Mark8:19 Musi wandakamedurira vane zviuru zvishanu zvingwa zvishanu, makanonga matengu manganiko azere nezvimedu?” Vakati kwaari, “Gumi namaviri.”" 
Mark8:20 “Nomusi wandakamedurira vane zviuru zvina zvingwa zvinomwe, makanonga matengu manganiko akazadzwa nezvimedu?” Vakati, “Manomwe.”" 
Mark8:21 Akati kwavari, “Ko hamunzwisisi nazvino here?”" 
Mark8:22 Zvino vakasvika Bhetisaidha; vakauya nebofu, vakakumbira zvikuru kwaari, kuti amunyangate." 
Mark8:23 Akabata ruoko rwebofu, akariisa kunze kwomusha, ndokupfira mate pamaziso aro, akaisa maoko pamusoro pake, akamubvunza achiti, “Unoona chinhu here?”" 
Mark8:24 Iye akatarira, akati, “Ndinoona vanhu, ndinovaona vachifamba vakafanana nemiti.”" 
Mark8:25 Zvino akaisazve maoko pamusoro pamaziso aro, iye akatarisisa, akaporeswa, akaona zvose zvakanaka." 
Mark8:26 Akamuendesa kumba kwake akati, “Usatongopinda mumusha.”" 
Mark8:27 Zvino Jesu navadzidzi vake vakaenda kumisha yeSizaria Firipi; munzira akabvunza vadzidzi vake akati kwavari, “Vanhu vanoti ndini aniko?”" 
Mark8:28 Vakapindura vachiti kwaari, “Vamwe vanoti, ‘Johani Mubhabhatidzi; vamwe Eriya, vamwezve mumwe wavaporofita.’ ”" 
Mark8:29 Zvino akavabvunza, akati, “Ko imi munoti ndini ani?” Petirosi akapindura, akati kwaari, “Ndimi Kristu.”" 
Mark8:30 Akavaraira zvikuru kuti varege kuzivisa munhu izvozvo nezvake. 
Mark8:31 Zvino akatanga kuvadzidzisa kuti Mwanakomana womunhu anofanira kutambudzika zvizhinji nokuraswa navakuru, navapristi vakuru, navanyori, auraiwe, amukezve mazuva matatu apfuura." 
Mark8:32 Akataura shoko iro pachena. Zvino Petirosi akaenda naye vari voga, akatanga kumutsiudza." 
Mark8:33 Asi iye akatendeuka, ndokutarira vadzidzi vake, akaraira Petirosi, akati, “Ibva shure kwangu, Satani, nokuti haurangariri zvinhu zvaMwari, asi zvinhu zvavanhu.”" 
Mark8:34 Zvino akadanira kwaari vanhu vazhinji navadzidzi vake, akati kwavari, “Kana munhu achida kuuya shure kwangu, ngaazvirambe, atakure muchinjikwa wake, anditevere." 
Mark8:35 Nokuti ani naani anoda kuponesa upenyu hwake, acharasikirwa nahwo; asi ani naani anorasikirwa noupenyu hwake nokuda kwangu nokweVhangeri, achahuponesa." 
Mark8:36 “Nokuti munhu achagobatsirweiko, kana awana nyika yose, akarasikirwa noupenyu hwake?" 
Mark8:37 Nokuti munhu acharipeiko kuti adzikinure upenyu hwake? 
Mark8:38 Nokuti ani naani anonyara pamusoro pamashoko angu parudzi urwu rwohupombwe norwokutadza, Mwanakomana womunhu achanyarawo pamusoro pake, musi waanouya navatumwa vatsvene nokubwinya kwaBaba vake.”" 
Mark9:1 Zvino akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, vamwe varipo kuna vamire pano, vasingazooni rufu, vasati vaona ushe hwaMwari huchiuya nesimba.”" 
Mark9:2 Mazuva matanhatu akati apfuura, Jesu akatora Petirosi, naJakobho, naJohani, akaenda navo mugomo refu kurutivi vari voga; akasanduka pamberi pavo." 
Mark9:3 Nguo dzake dzikapenya, dzikachena zvikuru; hakuna musuki pano panyika, angagona kudzichenesa kudaro." 
Mark9:4 Ipapo Eriya naMosesi vakaonekwa navo, vachitaurirana naJesu." 
Mark9:5 Petirosi akati kuna Jesu, “Rabhi, zvakanaka zvatiri pano; ngativake matumba matatu, rimwe renyu, rimwe raMosesi, rimwe raEriya.”" 
Mark9:6 Nokuti akanga asingazivi chaanotaura, nokuti vakatya zvikuru." 
Mark9:7 Zvino gore rikauya rikavafukidza, izwi rikabuda mugore, richiti, “Uyu Mwanakomana wangu mudiwa, mumunzwei!”" 
Mark9:8 Kamwe, vakati vachiringaringa, havana kuzoona munhu, asi Jesu bedzi anavo." 
Mark9:9 Zvino vakati vachiburuka mugomo, akavaraira kuti, varege kuudza munhu zvavakanga vaona kusvikira Mwanakomana womunhu amuka kuvakafa." 
Mark9:10 Vakarichengeta shoko iro, vachiita nyaya pakati pavo, kuti, “Kumuka kwavakafa chiiko?”" 
Mark9:11 Vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Vanyori vanotaurireiko vachiti, ‘Eriya anofanira kutanga kuuya?’ ”" 
Mark9:12 Akati kwavari, “Eriya achatanga kuuya hake, avandudze zvinhu zvose, asi kwakagonyorwa seiko zvoMwanakomana womunhu, kuti achatambudzika zvikuru nokuzvidzwa?" 
Mark9:13 Asi ndinoti kwamuri, Eriya akatosvika, vakamuitira zvose pavakanga vachida napo, sezvazvakanyorwa pamusoro pake.”" 
Mark9:14 Vakati vasvika kuvadzidzi, vakaona vanhu vazhinji zhinji, vakavakomba, navanyori vachiita nyaya navo." 
Mark9:15 Pakarepo vazhinji vose vakati vachimuona, vakashamiswa kwazvo, vakamhanyira kwaari, vakamukwazisa." 
Mark9:16 Akavabvunza, akati, “Munoita nyaya neiko navo?”" 
Mark9:17 Mumwe wavazhinji akamupindura, akati, “Mudzidzisi, ndauya kwamuri nomwanakomana wangu, anomweya wembeveve." 
Mark9:18 Kwose kwaanomubata, anomuwisira pasi, achipupuma furo, achigeda–geda meno, uye anoonda kwazvo. Ndakataura navadzidzi venyu kuti vaubudise, vakasagona.”" 
Mark9:19 Akavapindura, akati, “Haiwa, rudzi rusingatendi, ndichagara nemi kusvikira rinhiko? Ndichakuitirai mwoyo murefu kusvikira rinhiko? Uyai naye kwandiri.”" 
Mark9:20 Vakauya naye kwaari; akati achimuona, pakarepo mweya ukamubvundisa, akawira pasi, akakunguruka, achipupuma furo." 
Mark9:21 Zvino akabvunza baba vake, akati, “Yava nguva yakadiniko kubvira izvozvi zvichimuwira?” Akati, “Kubva pauduku hwake.”" 
Mark9:22 “Kazhinji wakamuwisira mumoto kana mumvura kuti umuparadze; asi kana muchigona kuita chinhu, mutinzwire tsitsi, mutibatsire.”" 
Mark9:23 Jesu akati kwaari, “Kana iwe uchigona kutenda, zvose zvingaitika kuna anotenda.”" 
Mark9:24 Pakarepo baba vomwana vakachema, vachiti, “Ndinotenda, ndibatsirei pakusatenda kwangu.”" 
Mark9:25 Zvino Jesu akati achiona vanhu vazhinji vachimhanyirana pamwechete, akarayira mweya wakaipa, akati kwauri, “Iwe, mweya wembeveve nematsi, ndinokurayira kuti ubve maari, urege kupindazve maari!”" 
Mark9:26 Ukadanidzira, ukamubvundisa zvikuru, ukabuda; akafanana nomunhu akafa, nokudaro vazhinji vakati, “Afa.”" 
Mark9:27 Asi Jesu akabata ruoko rwake, akamusimudza, iye akasimuka." 
Mark9:28 Zvino akati apinda mumba, vadzidzi vake vakamubvunza vari voga vachiti, “Isu takanga tisingagoni neiko kuubudisa?”" 
Mark9:29 Akati kwavari, “Rudzi urwu harungatongobudi, asi nokunyengetera.”" 
Mark9:30 Vakabva ipapo, vakagura neGareriya, akaramba kuti zvizikanwe nomunhu." 
Mark9:31 Nokuti akadzidzisa vadzidzi vake, akati kwavari, “Mwanakomana womunhu achaiswa mumaoko avanhu, vachamuuraya; kana aurayiwa, achamukazve mazuva matatu apfuura.”" 
Mark9:32 Asi havana kunzwisisa shoko iro, vakatya kumubvunza." 
Mark9:33 Vakasvika Kapenaume; zvino akati ava mumba, akavabvunza, achiti, “Makanga muchiita nyaya yeiko munzira?”" 
Mark9:34 Vakaramba vanyerere, nokuti vakanga vaita nharo pakati pavo munzira, kuti mukuru ndiani." 
Mark9:35 Ipapo akagara pasi, akadana vane gumi navaviri, akati kwavari, “Kana munhu achida kuva wokutanga, achazova weshure kuna vose nomuranda wavose.”" 
Mark9:36 Akatora mwana muduku, akamuisa pakati pavo; akamupfumbatira mumaoko akati kwavari," 
Mark9:37 “Ani naani anogamuchira mumwe wavaduku vakadai nezita rangu, anondigamuchireni; ani naani anondigamuchira ini, haagamuchiri ini, asi uya akandituma.”" 
Mark9:38 Johani akati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, taona munhu achibudisa mweya yakaipa muzita renyu, tikamudzivisa, nokuti haana kutitevera.”" 
Mark9:39 Jesu akati, “Musamudzivisa, nokuti hakuna munhu angaita basa resimba nezita rangu, angakurumidza kutaura zvakaipa pamusoro pangu." 
Mark9:40 Nokuti asingapesani nesu, anesu." 
Mark9:41 Nokuti ani naani anokunwisai mukombe wemvura muzita rangu, nemhaka yokuti muri vaKristu, zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, haana kurasikirwa nomubairo wake." 
Mark9:42 “Ani naani anogumbusa mumwe wavaduku ava vanotenda kwandiri, zviri nani kwaari kuti guyo guru risungirirwe mumutsipa wake, akandirwe mugungwa." 
Mark9:43 Kana ruoko rwako ruchikugumbusa, urugure; zviri nani kwauri kuti upinde muupenyu uri chirema, pakuenda muGehena, mumoto usingadzimwi, una maoko maviri. [" 
Mark9:44 Apo pasingafi honye yavo, napasingadzimwi moto.]" 
Mark9:45 Kana rutsoka rwako ruchikugumbusa, urugure; zviri nani kwauri kuti upinde muupenyu uchikamhina, pakukandirwa muGehena, unetsoka mbiri. [" 
Mark9:46 Apo pasingafi honye yavo, napasingadzimwi moto.]" 
Mark9:47 Kana ziso rako richikugumbusa, urirase; zviri nani kwauri kuti upinde muushe hwedenga une ziso rimwe, pakukandirwa muGehena, una meso maviri." 
Mark9:48 Apo pasingafi honye yavo, napasingadzimwi moto." 
Mark9:49 “Nokuti mumwe nomumwe acharangwa nomoto. 
Mark9:50 “Munyu wakanaka; asi kana munyu usichavavi, mungaurunga neiko? Ivai nomunyu mukati menyu, mugare norugare pakati penyu.”" 
Mark10:1 Zvino akasimukapo, akasvika munyika yeJudhiya, nemhiri kwaJodhani, vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakaunganirazve kwaari; akavadzidzisazve sezvaakanga achisiita." 
Mark10:2 VaFarisi vakauya kwaari, vakamubvunza, vachimuedza, vachiti, “Murume akatenderwa kuramba mukadzi wake here?”" 
Mark10:3 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Mosesi akakuraireiko?”" 
Mark10:4 Vakati, “Mosesi akatendera murume kunyora rugwaro rwokumuramba, agorambwa.”" 
Mark10:5 Jesu akati kwavari, “Akakunyorerai murairo iwoyo nokuda kwoukukutu hwemwoyo yenyu." 
Mark10:6 Asi kubva pakutanga kwokusikwa akavaita, ‘Munhurume nomunhukadzi.’" 
Mark10:7 ‘Nokuda kwaizvozvo murume achasiya baba vake namai vake, akanamatira mukadzi wake;" 
Mark10:8 ava vaviri vachava nyama imwe; nokudaro havachiri vaviri; asi nyama imwe.’ 
Mark10:9 Zvino izvo Mwari zvaakasanganisa, munhu ngaarege kuzviparadzanisa.”" 
Mark10:10 Zvino mumba vadzidzi vakamubvunzazve pamusoro paizvozvo. 
Mark10:11 Akati kwavari, “Ani naani anoramba mukadzi wake, akawana mumwe, anoita upombwe kwaari." 
Mark10:12 Uye kana iye mukadzi akaramba murume wake, akawanikwa nomumwe, anoita upombwe.”" 
Mark10:13 Zvino vakauya navana vaduku kwaari, kuti avanyangate; asi vadzidzi vakavaraira." 
Mark10:14 Zvino Jesu akati achizviona, akatsamwa, akati kwavari, “Regai vana vaduku vauye kwandiri, musavadzivisa, nokuti ushe hwaMwari ndohwavakadai." 
Mark10:15 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, ani naani usingagamuchiri ushe hwaMwari somwana muduku, haangatongopindi mahuri.”" 
Mark10:16 Ipapo akavafungatira mumaoko, akavaropafadza, ndokuisa maoko pamusoro pavo." 
Mark10:17 Zvino akati achibuda kunzira, mumwe akamhanyira kwaari, akapfugama pamberi pake akamubvunza, achiti, “Mudzidzisi Wakanaka, ndingaiteiko kuti ndigare nhaka youpenyu husingaperi?”" 
Mark10:18 Jesu akati kwaari, “Anondiidzireiko wakanaka? Hakuna akanaka, asi mumwechete, iye Mwari." 
Mark10:19 Mirairo unoiziva, inoti, usauraya, usaita upombwe, usaba, usapupura nhema, usanyengera, kudza baba vako namai vako.”" 
Mark10:20 Akati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, izvi zvose ndakazvichengeta kubva pauduku hwangu.”" 
Mark10:21 Jesu akamutarira akamuda, akati kwaari, “Unoshaiwa chinhu chimwechete; enda, utengese zvose zvaunazvo, upe varombo, uve nepfuma kudenga; ugouya, unditevere.”" 
Mark10:22 Asi akasuwa kwazvo neshoko iro, ati hurududu nokuti akanga ane pfuma zhinji." 
Mark10:23 Ipapo Jesu akaringa–ringa, akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Vane pfuma vacharemerwa sei kupinda muushe hwaMwari!”" 
Mark10:24 Vadzidzi vakashamiswa namashoko ake. Asi Jesu akapindurazve, akati kwavari, “Vana, zvinorema sei kuna vanovimba nepfuma kupinda muushe hwaMwari!" 
Mark10:25 Ngamera ingarerukirwa kupinda paburi retsono, kumupfumi kupinda muushe hwaMwari.”" 
Mark10:26 Ipapo vakakahadzika zvikuru, vakati kwaari, “Ndianiko angagoponeswa?”" 
Mark10:27 Zvino Jesu akati achivatarira, akati, “Kuvanhu izvi hazvibviri, asi kuna Mwari zvinobvira.”" 
Mark10:28 Petirosi akatanga kutaura kwaari, achiti, “Tarirai isu takasiya zvose tikakuteverai.”" 
Mark10:29 Jesu akati, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, hakuna munhu akasiya imba, kana vakoma kana vanun'una, kana hanzvadzi, kana mai, kana baba, vana, kana minda, nokuda kwangu nokweVhangeri," 
Mark10:30 asingazopiwi zvine zana nenguva ino, zvedzimba vakoma navanun'una, nehanzvadzi, namadzimai, navana, neminda, pamwechete nokuvengwa, noupenyu husingaperi nenguva inouya." 
Mark10:31 Asi vazhinji vokutanga vachava vokupedzisira, novokupedzisira vachava vokutanga.”" 
Mark10:32 Zvino vakanga vari munzira, vachikwira Jerusaremu; Jesu akanga achivatungamirira; vakashamiswa; navakanga vachitevera, vakatya. Ipapo akatorazve vane gumi navaviri, akatanga kuvaudza izvo zvaakanga oda kuitirwa, achiti," 
Mark10:33 “Tarirai tinokwira Jerusaremu, Mwanakomana womunhu achaiswa kuvapristi vakuru navanyori; vachamutongera rufu, nokumuisa kuvahedheni." 
Mark10:34 Vachamuseka, nokumupfira mate, nokumurova kwazvo, nokumuuraya; kana mazuva matatu apfuura, achamukazve.”" 
Mark10:35 Zvino Jakobho naJohani, vanakomana vaZebhedhi, vakauya, kwaari, vakati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, tinoda kuti mutiitire sezvatinokumbira kwamuri.”" 
Mark10:36 Akati kwavari, “Munoda kuti ndikuitireiko?”" 
Mark10:37 Vakati kwaari, “Tigarisei mukubwinya kwenyu, mumwe kuruoko rwenyu rworudyi, mumwe kuruboshwe.”" 
Mark10:38 Asi Jesu akati kwavari, “Hamuzivi zvamunokumbira. Mungagona kunwira mumukombe wandinonwira ini, nokubhabhatidzwa norubhabhatidzo rwandinobhabhatidzwa narwo here?”" 
Mark10:39 Vakati kwaari, “Tingagona.” Jesu akati kwavari, “Muchanwira henyu mumukombe wandinonwira ini, nokubhabhatidzwa norubhabhatidzo rwandinobhabhatidzwa narwo ini;" 
Mark10:40 asi kugara kuruoko rwangu rworudyi, kana kuruboshwe, handisini ndinopa, asi ndezvavakazvigadzirirwa izvo.”" 
Mark10:41 Vane gumi vakati vachizvinzwa, vakatanga kutsamwira Jakobho naJohani." 
Mark10:42 Ipapo Jesu akavadanira kwaari, akati kwavari, “Munoziva kuti avo vanonzi machinda avahedheni vanovaita mukundo navakuru vakuru vano vanovaitira zvesimba." 
Mark10:43 “Zvino pakati penyu ngazvirege kuva kudaro; asi ani naani anoda kuva mukuru pakati penyu, ngaave mushandiri wenyu;" 
Mark10:44 ani naani anoda kuva wokutanga pakati penyu, ngaave muranda wavose." 
Mark10:45 “Nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu naiye haana kuuya kuzoshandirwa, asi kuzoshandira, nokupa upenyu hwake ruve rudzikinuro rwavazhinji.”" 
Mark10:46 Vakasvika Jeriko; zvino akati achibuda Jeriko navadzidzi vake navazhinji zhinji, Bhatimeo, mwanakomana waTimeo, raiva bofu riri rombe, wakanga agere panzira." 
Mark10:47 Iye akati anzwa, kuti ndiJesu weNazareta, akatanga kudanidzira, achiti, “Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, ndinzwirei ngoni!”" 
Mark10:48 Vazhinji vakamuraira kuti anyarare, asi iye akanyanya kudanidzira kwazvo, achiti, “Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, ndinzwirei ngoni!”" 
Mark10:49 Ipapo Jesu akamira, akati, “Mudanei.” Vakadana bofu, vachiti kwariri, “Tsunga mwoyo, simuka, anokudana.”" 
Mark10:50 Ipapo akarasira nguo yake, akasimuka, akaenda kuna Jesu." 
Mark10:51 Jesu akamupindura, akati kwaari, “Unoda kuti ndikuitireiko?” Bofu rikati kwaari, “Rabhoni, kuti ndione.”" 
Mark10:52 Jesu akati kwaari, “Enda hako, kutenda kwako kwakuponesa.” Pakarepo akaona, akatevera Jesu munzira." 
Mark11:1 Vakati vachiswedera Jerusaremu, paBhetifage neBhetania, pagomo reMiorivhi, akatuma vaviri vavadzidzi vake," 
Mark11:2 akati kwavari, “Endai kumusha wakatarisana nemi; pakarepo kana muchipinda mauri, muchawana mhuru yembongoro yakasungirwa, isina kumbotasva nomunhu; muisunungure, mugouya nayo." 
Mark11:3 Kana munhu akati kwamuri, munoitireiko kudaro? Muti, Ishe anoida. Pakarepo achaidzora pano.”" 
Mark11:4 Vakaenda, vakandowana mhuru yembongoro yakasungirwa kunze pamusuwo, pamharadzano dzenzira, vakaisunungura." 
Mark11:5 Vamwe vakanga vamirepo, vakati kwavari, “Munoiteiko zvamunosunungura mhuru yembongoro?”" 
Mark11:6 Vakavaudza sezvavakarairwa naJesu; vakavarega. 
Mark11:7 Zvino vakauya nemhuru yembongoro kuna Jesu, vakawarira nguo dzavo pamusoro payo; iye ndokuitasva." 
Mark11:8 Vazhinji vakawarira nguo dzavo panzira, navamwe mashizha avakanga vatema mubundo." 
Mark11:9 Avo vakanga vachitungamira, navakanga vachitevera vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Hosana, ngaakudzwe iye anouya muzita raIshe." 
Mark11:10 Ngahukudzwe ushe hwababa vedu Dhavhidhi, hunouya! Hosana kumusoro–soro!”" 
Mark11:11 Ipapo Jesu akapinda Jerusaremu mutemberi; akati aringa–ringa zvinhu zvose, zuva zvarakanga ravira, akabuda, akaenda Bhetania ana vane gumi navaviri." 
Mark11:12 Fume mangwana vakati vachibva Bhetania, akaziya;" 
Mark11:13 zvino akati achiona muonde uri kure unamashizha, akaendako, achiti, zvimwe angawana chinhu pauri; zvino achisvika pauri, haana kuwana chinhu, asi mashizha bedzi; nokuti yakanga isi nguva yamaonde." 
Mark11:14 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Kusava nomunhu, anozodya michero pauri nokusingaperi.” Vadzidzi vake vakazvinzwa." 
Mark11:15 Vakasvika Jerusaremu; akapinda mutemberi, akatanga kubudisa vaitengesa, navaitenga mutemberi; akawisa matafura avaitsinhanhisa mari, nezvigaro zvavaitengesa njiva." 
Mark11:16 Akasatendera munhu kuti atakure nhumbi mutemberi. 
Mark11:17 Akadzidzisa, achiti kwavari, “Hakuna kunyorwa here kuchinzi, ‘Imba yangu ichanzi imba yokunyengetera yamarudzi ose?’ Asi imi makaiita bako ramakororo.”" 
Mark11:18 Vapristi vakuru navanyori vakati vachizvinzwa, vakatsvaka pavangamuuraya napo; nokuti vakanga vachimutya, nokuti vazhinji vose vakashamiswa nokudzidzisa kwake." 
Mark11:19 Zvino, nguva dzose kana ava madekwana, waienda kunze kweguta." 
Mark11:20 Vakati vachipfuura napo mangwanani, vakaona muonde waoma kubva pamidzi." 
Mark11:21 Petirosi akarangarira, akati kwaari, “Rabhi, tarirai muonde wamakatuka waoma.”" 
Mark11:22 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Ivai nokutendeka kuna Mwari." 
Mark11:23 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, mumwe nomumwe anoti kugomo iri, simudzwa, ukandwe mugungwa, asinganyunyuti mumwoyo make, asi achitenda kuti zvaanoreva zvichaiitika, achava nazvo." 
Mark11:24 Saka ndinoti kwamuri, zvinhu zvose–zvose zvamunokumbira nokunyengetera, tendai kuti mazvigamuchira, mugova nazvo." 
Mark11:25 Kana mukamira muchinyengetera, regererai kana mune mhaka nomumwe, kuti naBaba venyu vari kudenga, vazokuregereiwo imi kudarika kwenyu; [" 
Mark11:26 asi kana musingakanganwiriyi imi, nababa venyu vari kudenga havangakukanganwiriyi imi kudarika kwenyu.]”" 
Mark11:27 Vakasvikazve Jerusaremu. Zvino akati achifamba mutemberi, vapristi vakuru navanyori navakuru vakauya kwaari;" 
Mark11:28 vakati kwaari, “Munoita zvinhu izvozvi nesimba ripiko? Ndianiko akakupai simba iri, kuti muite izvi?”" 
Mark11:29 Jesu akati kwavari, “Neni ndichakubvunzaiwo shoko rimwe, mundipindure, neni ndichakuudzaiwo simba randinoita naro zvinhu izvozvi." 
Mark11:30 Rubhabhatidzo rwaJohani rwakabva kudenga here kana kuvanhu? Ndipindurei.” 
Mark11:31 Vakataurirana, vachiti, “Kana tikati, ‘Kudenga,’ achati, ‘Makagoregerei kumutenda?’" 
Mark11:32 Asi tingati, ‘Kuvanhu, here?’ ” Vakanga vachitya vanhu vazhinji, nokuti vose vakanga vachiti Johani muporofita zvirokwazvo." 
Mark11:33 Vakapindura vachiti kuna Jesu, “Hatizivi.” Jesu akati kwavari, “Neni handingakuudziyiwo simba randinoita naro zvinhu izvi.”" 
Mark12:1 Zvino akatanga kutaura navo nemifananidzo, achiti, “Mumwe munhu akanga asima munda wemizambiringa, akaukomba norusvingo, akachera guvi rokusvinira, akavaka chirindo, chirefu akaurongera varimi, ndokufamba rwendo." 
Mark12:2 “Nenguva yemichero akatuma muranda kuvarimi, kuti apiwe navarimi michero yomunda wemizambiringa." 
Mark12:3 “Vakamubata, vakamurova, vakamudzosa asina." 
Mark12:4 Akatumazve mumwe muranda kwavari; vakamutaka namabwe, vakamutema musoro, vakamunyadza." 
Mark12:5 Akatumazve mumwe, vakamuuraya; navamwe vazhinji, vakarova vamwe, nokuuraya vamwe." 
Mark12:6 “Zvino akanga achine mwanakomana mumwe, mudikanwi; akamutuma kwavari pakupedzisira, achiti, ‘Vachakudza mwanakomana wangu.’" 
Mark12:7 Asi varimi ivavo vakataurirana, vachiti, ‘Uyu ndiye mugari wenhaka; uyai timuuraye, nhaka igova yedu.’" 
Mark12:8 Vakamubata, vakamuuraya, vakamubudisa kunze kwomunda wemizambiringa." 
Mark12:9 Zvino muridzi womunda wemizambiringa achaiteiko? Achauya, akaparadza varimi ivavo, akarongera vamwe varimi munda wemizambiringa." 
Mark12:10 Ko hamuna kutongorava here rugwaro urwu, runoti, ‘Ibwe rakaraswa navavaki, Ndiro rakazova musoro wekona;" 
Mark12:11 Izvozvo zvakaitwa naIshe, Zvinoshamisa pameso edu?’ ”" 
Mark12:12 Ipapo vakatsvaka kumubata, asi vakatya vanhu vazhinji; nokuti vakanga vachiziva kuti akavareva ivo nomufananidzo iwoyo; vakamusiya, vakabvapo." 
Mark12:13 Zvino vakatuma kwaari vamwe vaVaFarisi navaHerodhi, kuti vamubate pakutaura kwake." 
Mark12:14 Vakauya, vakati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, tinoziva kuti ndimi wazvokwadi, musingarangariri zvinoonekwa zvomunhu; hamutariri zviri kunze kwomunhu, asi munodzidzisa nzira yaMwari nezvokwadi, munhu anotenderwa kutera mutero waKesari here, kana kwete?" 
Mark12:15 “Tichatera here, kana tirege kutera?” Asi iye achiziva kunyengera kwavo, akati kwavari, “Munondiedzereiko? Uyai nedhinari kwandiri, ndirione.”" 
Mark12:16 Vakauya naro. Ipapo akati kwavari, “Mufananidzo uyu norunyoro urwu ndezvaani?” Vakati kwaari, “ZvaKesari.”" 
Mark12:17 Jesu akati kwavari, “Ipai Kesari zvaKesari, naMwari zvaMwari.” Vakashamiswa zvikuru naye." 
Mark12:18 Zvino vaSadhusi vakauya kwaari, ivo vanoti hakuna kumuka kwavakafa, vakamubvunza vachiti," 
Mark12:19 “Mudzidzisi, Mosesi akatinyorera kuti, ‘Kana mukoma womunhu akafa, akasiya mukadzi asina mwana, munun'una wake atore mukadzi wake, amutsire mukoma wake vana.’" 
Mark12:20 Zvino kwakanga kuna vanakomana vomunhu mumwe vanomwe; wedangwe akatora mukadzi, akafa asina vana." 
Mark12:21 Wechipiri akamutora, akafa asingasiyi vana; nowechitatu akadarowo." 
Mark12:22 “Navanomwe vose havana kuva nomwana; shure kwavose mukadzi akafawo. 
Mark12:23 Zvino pakumuka kwavakafa, kana vachimuka, achava mukadzi waaniko? Nokuti akanga ari mukadzi wavose vanomwe.”" 
Mark12:24 Jesu akati kwavari, “Hamuti makarasika here, nemhaka yokusaziva magwaro nesimba raMwari?" 
Mark12:25 “Nokuti kana vachimuka kuvakafa, havawani kana kuwanikwa; asi vakaita savatumwa kudenga." 
Mark12:26 Kana kuri kumutswa kwavakafa, hamuna kurava here mubhuku raMosesi pashoko regwenzi, kuti Mwari akataura naye, akati, ‘Ndini Mwari waAbhurahamu, naMwari waIsaka, naMwari waJakobho?’" 
Mark12:27 Haasi Mwari wavakafa, asi wavapenyu; marasika kwazvo.”" 
Mark12:28 Zvino mumwe wavanyori akanga anzwa kutaurirana kwavo, achiziva kuti akanga avapindura zvakanaka, akauya, akamubvunza, achiti, “Murairo wokutanga pana yose ndoupiko?”" 
Mark12:29 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Wokutanga ndiwoyu, ‘Inzwai VaIsiraeri, Ishe Mwari wedu, ndiye Ishe mumwechete!" 
Mark12:30 Ida Ishe Mwari wako, nomwoyo wako wose, nomweya wako wose, nokufunga kwako kwose, nesimba rako rose.’" 
Mark12:31 Wechipiri ndiwoyu, ‘Ida wokwako sezvaunozvida pachako.’ Hakuna murairo mukuru kuna iyoyi.”" 
Mark12:32 Zvino munyori akati kwaari, “Zvakanaka Mudzidzisi, mareva zvirokwazvo, kuti ndiye mumwechete, hakuna mumwe kunze kwake;" 
Mark12:33 nokumuda iye nomwoyo wose, nokufunga kwose, nesimba rose, nokuda wokwake sezvaanozvida pachake, zvinopfuura zvikuru zvipiriso zvose zvinopiswa chose, nezvibairo.”" 
Mark12:34 Zvino Jesu akati achiona kuti apindura nokufunga, akati kwaari, “Hausi kure noushe hwaMwari.” Kukasava nomunhu akazotsunga kumubvunza chinhu." 
Mark12:35 Zvino Jesu akati achidzidzisa mutemberi, akapindura, akati, “Vanyori vanoreva seiko kuti Kristu ndiye mwanakomana waDhavhidhi?" 
Mark12:36 Dhavhidhi amene akati noMweya Mutsvene, ‘Ishe akati kuna Ishe wangu, Gara kurudyi rwangu, Kusvikira ndaisa vavengi vako pasi petsoka dzako.’" 
Mark12:37 “Dhavhidhi amene anoti, ‘Ishe,’ angagova mwanakomana wake seiko?” Vazhinji zhinji vakanga vachifara kumunzwa." 
Mark12:38 Zvino pakudzidzisa kwake akati, “Chenjerai vanyori, vanoda kufamba nenguo refu, nokukwaziswa padare," 
Mark12:39 nezvigaro zvapamberi mumasinagoge, nenzvimbo dzapamberi pamitambo;" 
Mark12:40 vachiparadza dzimba dzechirikadzi, vachinyengetera neminyengetero mirefu. Ivava vachatongerwa mhosva huru inodarika yavamwe.”" 
Mark12:41 Zvino akanga agere akatarisana neimba yaichengeterwa upfumi hwetemberi akatarira vanhu vazhinji vachikanda mari muzibhokisi, vapfumi vazhinji vakanga vachikanda zvizhinji." 
Mark12:42 Kukasvika chirikadzi, yaiva murombo, ikakanda tumari tuviri tuduku." 
Mark12:43 Akadanira vadzidzi vake kwaari, akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, chirikadzi iyi, iri murombo, yakaisa zvizhinji kunaavo vose vakaisa muchivigiro," 
Mark12:44 nokuti avo vose vakaisa vachitora pazvizhinji zvavo; asi iye wakaisa achitora pakushaiwa kwake, zvose zvaakanga anazvo, zvose zvaaifanira kurarama nazvo.”" 
Mark13:1 Akati achibuda mutemberi, mumwe wavadzidzi vake akati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, tarirai mabwe, kunaka! Nedzimba kunaka!”" 
Mark13:2 Jesu akati kwaari, “Unoona dzimba idzi huru? Hakungaregwi ibwe pamusoro pebwe, risingazowisirwi pasi.”" 
Mark13:3 Zvino akati agere pagomo reMiorivhi, pakatarisana netemberi, Petirosi, naJakobho, naJohani, naAndireya vakamubvunza vari voga, vachiti," 
Mark13:4 “Tiudzei kuti izvozvi zvichagova rinhiko? Nechiratidzo chichava chipiko, kana izvozvi zvose zvoda kuitwa?”" 
Mark13:5 Zvino Jesu akatanga kuvaudza, akati, “Chenjerai kuti murege kutsauswa nomunhu." 
Mark13:6 Vazhinji vachauya nezita rangu, vachiti, ‘Ndini Kristu, vachitsausa vazhinji.’" 
Mark13:7 Kana muchinzwa zvokurwa, nenyaya yokurwa, musavhunduka; izvozvo zvinofanira kumboitika; asi kuguma kuchigere kusvika." 
Mark13:8 Nokuti rudzi ruchamukira rudzi, ushe huchamukira ushe; kudengenyeka kwenyika kuchavapo kune dzimwe nzvimbo; nenzara dzichavapo. Ndiko kutanga kwenhamo." 
Mark13:9 “Zvichenjerei imi, nokuti vachakuisai kumakurukota, uye mucharohwa mumasinagoge, muchaiswa pamberi pamadzishe namadzimambo nokuda kwangu, chive chapupu kwavari." 
Mark13:10 Vhangeri inofanira kutanga kumboparidzirwa marudzi ose. 
Mark13:11 Kana vachienda nemi kunotongwa, vachikuisai kumakurukota, musambofunganya zvamuchataura, asi taurai chamunenge mapiwa nenguva iyo. Nokuti hamusirimi munotaura, asi ndiMweya Mutsvene." 
Mark13:12 Mukoma achaisa munun'una kurufu, nababa mwana wavo; navana vachamukira vabereki vavo nokuvaurayisa." 
Mark13:13 Muchavengwa navose nokuda kwezita rangu; asi anotsunga kusvikira pakuguma achaponeswa. 
Mark13:14 “Zvino kana muchiona nyangadzi yokuparadza imire paisina kufanira kumira anorava ngaacherekedze, vari muJudhiya ngavatizire kumakomo;" 
Mark13:15 ari pamusoro pedenga reimba ngaarege kuburuka, kana kupinda kuzotora chinhu mumba make." 
Mark13:16 Nowari mumunda ngaarege kudzokera shure kuzotora nguo yake. 
Mark13:17 Vachava nenhamo vane pamuviri navanoyamwisa namazuva iwayo! 
Mark13:18 Nyengeterai kuti zvirege kuva panguva yechando. 
Mark13:19 Nokuti namazuva iwayo kuchavapo kutambudzika, kusati kwakambovapo kwakadaro, kubva pakutanga kwokusikwa kwakasikwa naMwari, kusvikira zvino, uye hakuchazovipo." 
Mark13:20 “Dai Ishe asaitapudza mazuva iwayo, hakuna munhu airarama; asi nokuda kwavakasanangurwa vaakasanangura, akatapudza mazuva iwayo." 
Mark13:21 “Zvino kana munhu achiti kwamuri, ‘Tarirai Kristu ari pano, tarirai, ari apo,’ regai kutenda." 
Mark13:22 Nokuti vanaKristu venhema vachamuka, navaporofita venhema, vachaita zviratidzo nezvinoshamisa, kuti vatsause vakasanangurwa, kana zvichibvira." 
Mark13:23 Asi chenjerai imi; tarirai, ndagara ndakuudzai zvose!" 
Mark13:24 “Asi namazuva iwayo, shure kwokutambudzika ikoko, zuva richasviba, nomwedzi hauchazobwinyi," 
Mark13:25 nenyenyedzi dzichawa kudenga, namasimba ari kudenga achazununguswa." 
Mark13:26 Ipapo vachaona Mwanakomana womunhu achiuya mumakore nesimba guru nokubwinya. 
Mark13:27 “Ipapo achatuma vatumwa, akaunganidza vakasanangurwa vake kunobva mhepo ina, kubva kurutivi rumwe rwenyika kusvikira kuno rumwe rutivi rwedenga." 
Mark13:28 “Dzidzai pamuonde mufananidzo uyu; kana davi rawo rava nyoro, mashizha achitunga, munoziva kuti zhizha rava pedyo." 
Mark13:29 Saizvozvo imiwo, kana moona izvozvo zvichiitwa, zivai kuti ava pedyo atosvika pamusuwo." 
Mark13:30 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, rudzi urwu harungatongopfuuri, kusvikira izvozvo zvose zvaitika." 
Mark13:31 Denga nenyika zvichapfuura, asi mashoko angu haangatongopfuuri." 
Mark13:32 “Asi kana riri zuva iro nenguva iyo, hakuna anozviziva, kunyangwe vatumwa vokudenga, kunyangwe Mwanakomana, asi Baba." 
Mark13:33 Chenjerai, murinde, nokunyengetera; nokuti hamuzivi kuti nguva ichasvika rinhi." 
Mark13:34 Zvakaita somunhu akaenda kune imwe nyika, akasiya imba yake, akapa varanda vake simba, mumwe nomumwe basa rake, akarayira murindi womusuwo kuti arindire." 
Mark13:35 Naizvozvo rindai, nokuti hamuzivi musi muridzi weimba anouya nawo, kana madeko, kana pakati pousiku, kana pakurira kwehuku, kana mangwanani;" 
Mark13:36 kuti arege kuuya kamwe–kamwe, akakuwanai muvete." 
Mark13:37 Zvandinokuudzai imi, ndinoudza vose, ndichiti, ‘Rindai!’ ”" 
Mark14:1 Zvino mazuva maviri akanga asara pakusvika kwePasika nomutambo wezvingwa zvisina mbiriso. Vapristi vakuru navanyori vakanga vachitsvaka mutoo wavangamubata nawo namano, kuti vamuuraye." 
Mark14:2 Nokuti vakati, “Zvirege kuitwa pamutambo, kuti kurege kuva nebope pakati pavanhu.”" 
Mark14:3 Zvino akati ari paBhetania, mumba maSimoni wamaperembudzi, agere pakudya, mumwe mukadzi akauya ane chinu chearibhasitera chaiva namafuta chenaridho chakanakisa, chinomutengo mukuru; akaputsa chinu chearibhasitera, akachidurura mumusoro wake." 
Mark14:4 Asi vamwe vakanga varipo vakatsamwa pamwoyo yavo, vakati, “Kuparadza ikoko kwemafuta kwakaitirweiko?" 
Mark14:5 Nokuti mafuta oga angadai atengeswa namadhinari anopfuura mazana matatu, akapiwa varombo. Vakatsamwira mukadzi.”" 
Mark14:6 Asi Jesu akati, “Muregei. Muno mutambudzireiko? Akandiitira basa rakanaka." 
Mark14:7 “Nokuti varombo munavo nguva dzose, nguva ipi neipi yamunoda, mungavaitira zvakanaka; asi ini hamuneni nguva dzose." 
Mark14:8 Akaita paakagona napo; akagara azora muviri wangu ndisati ndavigwa. 
Mark14:9 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, kwose kunozoparidzirwa Vhangeri panyika dzose, zvakaitwa naye zvicharehwawo, kuti vamurangarire nazvo.”" 
Mark14:10 Judhasi Isikarioti, mumwe wavane gumi navaviri, akaenda kuvapristi vakuru, kuti amuise kwavari." 
Mark14:11 Ivo vakati vachizvinzwa, vakafara, vakamupikira kuti vachamupa mari. Ipapo akatsvaka nzira yaangamuisa kwavari nayo panguva yakafanira." 
Mark14:12 Nezuva rokutanga rezvingwa zvisina mbiriso, musi wavaibayira Pasika nawo, vadzidzi vakati kwaari, “Munoda kuti tikugadzirirepiko pamungadya Pasika?”" 
Mark14:13 Akatuma vadzidzi vake vaviri, akati kwavari, “Endai muguta, ipapo muchasangana nomunhu akatakura chirongo chemvura; mumutevere iye." 
Mark14:14 “Paanenge achipinda, muti kumuridzi weimba, ‘Zvanzi nomudzidzisi, imba yangu yavaeni iripiko, mandingadyire Pasika navadzidzi vangu?’" 
Mark14:15 Ipapo iye achakutaridzai imba huru yokumusoro, yakarongedzwa, yakagadzirwa; mutigadzirirepo.”" 
Mark14:16 Vadzidzi vake vakabuda, vakasvika muguta, vakandowana sezvavakanga vaudzwa naye; vakagadzira Pasika." 
Mark14:17 Ava madekwana, akauya navane gumi navaviri." 
Mark14:18 Zvino vakati vagere pakudya, Jesu akati, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, mumwe wenyu achandipandukira, iye anodya neni.”" 
Mark14:19 Ipapo vakatanga kuva neshungu, mumwe nomumwe akati kwaari, “Ndini here?”" 
Mark14:20 Akati kwavari, “Ndomumwe wavane gumi navaviri, anoisa ruoko neni mundiro." 
Mark14:21 Nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu anoenda hake, sezvazvakanyorwa pamusoro pake; asi ane nhamo munhu uyo, Mwanakomana womunhu waanopandukirwa naye; kwaiva nani kumunhu uyu dai asina kuberekwa.”" 
Mark14:22 Zvino vakati vachidya, Jesu akatora chingwa, akavonga, akachimedura, ndokuvapa, achiti, “Gamuchirai, ichi uyu muviri wangu.”" 
Mark14:23 Akatora mukombe, akavonga, akavapa, vakanwa vose pauri." 
Mark14:24 Akati kwavari, “Iri iropa rangu rechitenderano chitsva, rinodururirwa vazhinji." 
Mark14:25 “Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, handichazonwizve muchero womuzambiringa, kusvikira zuva iro randichazonwa naro, zvava zvitsva, muushe hwaMwari.”" 
Mark14:26 Zvino vakati vaimba rwiyo, vakabuda, vakaenda kugomo reMiorivhi." 
Mark14:27 Zvino Jesu akati kwavari, “Imi mose muchagumburwa kwandiri, nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, ‘Ndicharova mufudzi, namakwai achapararira.’" 
Mark14:28 Asi kana ndamutswa, ndichakutungamirirai Gareriya.”" 
Mark14:29 Zvino Petirosi akati kwaari, “Kunyangwe vose vakagumburwa, ini kwete.”" 
Mark14:30 Jesu akati kwaari, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwauri, kuti nhasi, usiku huno, jongwe risati rarira kaviri, uchandiramba katatu.”" 
Mark14:31 Asi iye akareva nokusimbisa, achiti, “Kunyangwe ndikafanira kufa nemi, handingatongokurambii.” Navose vakadarowo." 
Mark14:32 Zvino vakasvika panzvimbo inonzi Getsemani, akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Garai pano, ini ndichindonyengetera.”" 
Mark14:33 Akatora Petirosi naJakobho naJohani, akatanga kuvhunduka kwazvo nokudumbirwa." 
Mark14:34 Akati kwavari, “Mweya wangu une shungu kwazvo, kusvikira pakufa; garai pano murinde.”" 
Mark14:35 Akapfuura mberi zvishoma, akawira pasi akanyengetera kuti, kana zvichibvira, nguva ipfuure kwaari." 
Mark14:36 Akati, “Baba, Baba, zvose zvinobvira kwamuri, bvisai mukombe uyu kwandiri, asi kuda kwangu ngakurege kuitwa, asi kuda kwenyu.”" 
Mark14:37 Zvino akasvika, akavawana vavata; akati kuna Petirosi, “Simoni, uvete here? Wakanga usingagoni kurinda nguva imwechete here?" 
Mark14:38 Rindai, munyengetere, kuti murege kupinda mukuedzwa; mweya unoda hawo, asi nyama haine simba.”" 
Mark14:39 Akaendazve, akanyengetera achireva mashoko iwayo." 
Mark14:40 Akaendazve, akavawana vavata, nokuti meso avo akanga abatwa nehope kwazvo; vakasaziva zvavangamupindura." 
Mark14:41 Akaendazve rwechitatu, akati kwavari, “Chivatai henyu, muzorore; zvaringana, nguva yasvika, tarirai, Mwanakomana womunhu woiswa mumaoko avatadzi." 
Mark14:42 Simukai, tiende; tarirai, wondiisa kwavari wava pedyo.”" 
Mark14:43 Pakarepo, achataura, Judhasi, mumwe wavane gumi navaviri, akasvika, ana vanhu vazhinji vakabata minondo netsvimbo, vachibva kuvapristi vakuru navanyori navakuru vakuru." 
Mark14:44 Zvino iye, akamupandukira, akanga avapa chiratidzo, achiti, “Uyo wandinotsvoda ndiye, mumubate muende naye makamusunga zvakasimba.”" 
Mark14:45 Zvino akati asvika, pakarepo akaswedera kwaari, akati, “Rabhi!” Akamutsvoda kwazvo." 
Mark14:46 Ipapo vakaisa maoko kwaari, vakamubata." 
Mark14:47 Zvino mumwe wavakanga vamirepo, akavhomora munondo wake, akatema muranda woMupristi Mukuru, akagura nzeve yake." 
Mark14:48 Ipapo Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Mabuda kuzondibata neminondo netsvimbo, sendiri gororo here?" 
Mark14:49 Ndakanga ndinemi mazuva ose, ndichikudzidzisai mutemberi, mukarega kundibata, asi izvi zvaitwa, kuti Magwaro aitike.”" 
Mark14:50 Ipapo vakamusiya vose, vakatiza." 
Mark14:51 Zvino rimwe jaya rakamutevera, rakapfeka mucheka bedzi pamuviri, vakaribata;" 
Mark14:52 asi rakasiya mucheka, rikatiza risina nguo." 
Mark14:53 Zvino vakaisa Jesu kumupristi mukuru; vapristi vakuru vose navakuru vakuru navanyori vakaunganira kwaari. 
Mark14:54 Petirosi akanga amutevera ari kure kusvikira paruvazhe rwomupristi mukuru; akanga agere navatariri, achidziya moto." 
Mark14:55 Zvino vapristi vakuru namakurukota ose vakatsvaka uchapupu pamusoro paJesu kuti vamuuraye, asi havana kuuwana." 
Mark14:56 Nokuti vazhinji vaimupupurira nhema, asi kupupura kwavo kwakapesana." 
Mark14:57 Vamwe vakasimuka, vakamupupurira nhema vachiti," 
Mark14:58 “Takamunzwa isu achiti, ‘Ndichaputsa temberi iyi yakavakwa namaoko, ndikavaka imwe namazuva matatu, isina kuvakwa namaoko.’ ”" 
Mark14:59 Asi kupupura kwavo kwakapesana. 
Mark14:60 Zvino mupristi mukuru akasimuka pakati pavo, akabvunza Jesu, achiti, “Haupinduri chinhu here? Chinyi ichi chavanokupomedzera?”" 
Mark14:61 Asi iye akaramba anyerere, asingapinduri chinhu. Mupristi Mukuru akamubvunzazve, akati kwaari, “Ndiwe Kristu, Mwanakomana woAnokudzwa here?”" 
Mark14:62 Jesu akati, “Ndini. Nemi muchaona Mwanakomana womunhu agere kurudyi rwesimba, achiuya namakore okudenga.”" 
Mark14:63 Ipapo Mupristi Mukuru akabvarura nguo dzake, akati, “Tichatsvakireiko zvapupu?" 
Mark14:64 “Manzwa kushonha kwake Mwari; munofungeiko?” Ipapo vose vakamutongera kuti anofanira kufa. 
Mark14:65 Vamwe vakatanga kumupfira mate, vakafukidza meso ake, vakamurova netsiva, vachiti kwaari, “Porofita; navatariri vakamurova namaoko.”" 
Mark14:66 Zvino Petirosi achiri panze paruvazhe, mumwe murandasikana woMupristi Mukuru akasvika," 
Mark14:67 akaona Petirosi achidziya moto, akamutarira, akati, “Newewo wakanga una Jesu weNazareta!”" 
Mark14:68 Asi iye akaramba, achiti, “Handizivi kana kunzwisisa zvaunoreva; akabuda panze kuruvazhe rwapamberi, jongwe rikarira.”" 
Mark14:69 Zvino murandasikana akamuona, akatangazve kureva kuna vakanga varipo, achiti, “Uyu ndomumwe wavo!”" 
Mark14:70 Asi iye akarambazve. Nguva duku yakati yapfuura, vakanga vamirepo vakatizve kuna Petirosi, “Zvirokwazvo, uri mumwe wavo, nokuti newewo uri muGareriya.”" 
Mark14:71 Ipapo akatanga kutuka nokupika, achiti, “Handimuzivi munhu uyu wamunoreva.”" 
Mark14:72 Pakarepo jongwe rikarira rwechipiri; ipapo Petirosi akarangarira shoko rakanga rarehwa kwaari naJesu rokuti, “Jongwe risati rarira kaviri, uchandiramba katatu.” Zvino akati achifunga izvozvo, akachema." 
Mark15:1 Pakarepo mangwanani vapristi vakuru vakarangana navakuru navanyori namakurukota ose, vakasunga Jesu, vakaenda naye, vakamuisa kuna Pirato." 
Mark15:2 Pirato akamubvunza, akati, “Ndiwe Mambo wavaJudha here?” Akapindura, akati kwaari, “Ndizvo zvamataura.”" 
Mark15:3 Vapristi vakuru vakaramba vachimupomera zvizhinji. 
Mark15:4 Pirato akamubvunzazve akati, “Haupinduri chinhu here? Chinzwa, vanokupomera zvizhinji seiko!”" 
Mark15:5 Asi Jesu haana kuzopindura chinhu, Pirato akashamiswa nazvo." 
Mark15:6 Zvino pamutambo waisivasunungurira musungwa mumwe, wavanenge vaikumbira." 
Mark15:7 Zvino kwakanga kuno mumwe wainzi Bharabhasi, akanga asungwa pamwechete navamwe vakanga vamutsa bope, vakauraya vanhu pabope iroro." 
Mark15:8 Vanhu vazhinji vakakwira, vakatanga kukumbira kuna Pirato kuti avaitire saizvozvo." 
Mark15:9 Pirato akavapindura, akati, “Munoda kuti ndikusunungurirei Mambo wavaJudha here.”" 
Mark15:10 Nokuti akanga achiziva kuti vapristi vakuru vakanga vamuisa kwaari negodo. 
Mark15:11 Zvino vapristi vakuru vakakurudzira vanhu vazhinji, kuti vati zviri nani avasunungurire Bharabhasi." 
Mark15:12 Pirato akapindurazve, akati kwavari, “Ndichagoiteiko naiye, wamunoti ndiye Mambo wavaJudha?”" 
Mark15:13 Vakadanidzirazve, vachiti, “Murovere pamuchinjikwa!”" 
Mark15:14 Pirato akati kwavari, “Akagotadzeiko?” Vakanyanyisa kudanidzira, vachiti, “Muroverei pamuchinjikwa!”" 
Mark15:15 Zvino Pirato, nokuti akanga achida kufadza vanhu vazhinji, akavasunungurira Bharabhasi, asi Jesu akamurovesa, akamuisa kwavari kuti aroverwe pamuchinjikwa." 
Mark15:16 Zvino varwi vakamuisa mukati moruvazhe, imo mumba yomubati, vakaunganidza hondo yose;" 
Mark15:17 vakamupfekedza nguo tsvuku, vakaruka korona yeminzwa, vakamudzika iyo." 
Mark15:18 Vakatanga kumukwazisa, vachiti, “Kwaziwai, Mambo wavaJudha!”" 
Mark15:19 Vakamurova musoro norutsanga, vakamupfira mate, vakapfugama namabvi, vakamunamata." 
Mark15:20 Vakati vamuseka, vakamubvisa nguo tsvuku, ndokumupfekedza nguo dzake, vakaenda naye kunomurovera pamuchinjikwa." 
Mark15:21 Zvino vakamanikidza mumwe, akanga achipfuura achibva kuruwa, ainzi Simoni weKurini, baba vaArekizanda naRufosi, kuti atakure muchinjikwa wake." 
Mark15:22 Vakamuisa kunzvimbo inonzi, Gorogota, ndokuti, “Nzvimbo yeDehenya,” kana zvichishandurwa." 
Mark15:23 Vakamupa waini, yakavhenganiswa nemura, asi iye akazviramba." 
Mark15:24 Vakati vamurovera pamuchinjikwa, vakagovana nguo dzake, vachikanda mijenya pamusoro padzo, kuti mumwe nomumwe apiwe chake." 
Mark15:25 Yakanga iri nguva yechitatu, vakamurovera pamuchinjikwa." 
Mark15:26 Norugwaro rwemhosva yake rwakanga rwakanyorwa pamusoro pake, ruchiti, “MAMBO WAVAJUDHA.”" 
Mark15:27 Vakarovera pamuchinjikwa pamwechete naye makororo maviri, mumwe kurudyi rwake, mumwe kuruboshwe. [" 
Mark15:28 Rugwaro rukaitika, runoti, “Akarovererwa navadariki vomurairo.”]" 
Mark15:29 Navaipfuura vakamutuka, vachidzungudza misoro yavo, vachiti, “Iwe, wokuputsa temberi, nokuivakazve namazuva matatu," 
Mark15:30 chizviponesa iwe, uburuke pamuchinjikwa!”" 
Mark15:31 Saizvozvo vapristi vakuru navanyori vakamuseka pakati pavo, vachiti, “Akaponesa vamwe, zvino haagoni kuzviponesa." 
Mark15:32 Kristu, Mambo waVaIsiraeri, ngaaburuke zvino pamuchinjikwa, kuti tione titende.” Navakanga varoverwa pamwechete naye vakamuzvidza." 
Mark15:33 Zvino yakati yava nguva yechitanhatu, rima rikavapo panyika yose kusvikira panguva yepfumbamwe." 
Mark15:34 Nenguva yepfumbamwe Jesu akadana nezwi guru, achiti, “Eroi, Eroi, rama Sabhakitani!” Ndokuti kana zvichishandurwa, “Mwari wangu, Mwari wangu, mandisiyireiko?”" 
Mark15:35 Vamwe vakanga vamirepo vakati vachizvinzwa, vakati, “Chinzwai, anodana Eriya.”" 
Mark15:36 Ipapo mumwe akamhanya, akazadza chipanje nevhiniga, achiisa parutsanga, ndokumunwisa, achiti, “Regai timboona kana Eriya achizouya kumuburusa.”" 
Mark15:37 Ipapo Jesu akadana nezwi guru, ndokubva afa." 
Mark15:38 Keteni retemberi rikabvaruka napakati, kubva kumusoro kusvikira pasi." 
Mark15:39 Zvino mukuru wezana akanga amirepo, akatarisana naye, akati achiona mutowo wokufa kwake, akati, “Zvirokwazvo, munhu uyu akanga ari Mwanakomana waMwari.”" 
Mark15:40 Navakadzi vakanga varipo, vakatarira vari kure; pakati pavo kwakanga kuna Maria Magadharina, naMaria mai vaJakobho muduku naJose, naSarome;" 
Mark15:41 ndivo vaimutevera achiri muGareriya vachimushandira, navamwe vakadzi vazhinji vakanga vakwira Jerusaremu naye." 
Mark15:42 Zvino hwava usiku, zvarakanga riri zuva rokugadzirira, ndokuti rinotangira Sabata," 
Mark15:43 Josefa weArimatia, mumwe wamakurukota, munhu akakudzwa iye amene akanga achigarirawo ushe hwaMwari akauya akapinda nokutsunga kuna Pirato, akakumbira chitunha chaJesu." 
Mark15:44 Pirato akashamiswa achinzwa kuti akanga atofa; akadana mukuru wezana, akamubvunza kana anguva afa." 
Mark15:45 Zvino akati achinzwa kumukuru wezana, akapa Josefa chitunha." 
Mark15:46 Iye akatenga mucheka, akamuburusa, akamuputira nomucheka, ndokumuviga muhwiro hwakanga hwakacherwa pabwe, ndokukungurusira ibwe pamuromo wohwiro." 
Mark15:47 Maria Magadharina, naMaria mai vaJose, vakaona paakavigwa." 
Mark16:1 Sabata yakati yapfuura, Maria Magadharina, naMaria mai vaJakobho, naSarome, vakatenga zvinonhuwira, kuti vaende kuzomuzodza." 
Mark16:2 Mangwanani nomusi wokutanga wevhiki, vakaenda kuhwiro, zuva robuda." 
Mark16:3 Vakataurirana, vachiti, “Ndianiko achatikungurusira ibwe pamusuwo wehwiro?”" 
Mark16:4 Zvino vakati vachitarira, vakaona kuti ibwe rakanga ratokunguruswa, nokuti raiva guru–guru." 
Mark16:5 Vakapinda muhwiro, vakaona jaya, rakanga rigere kurudyi, rakapfeka nguo chena yakarehwa, vakavhunduka." 
Mark16:6 Rikati kwavari, “Musavhunduka, munotsvaka Jesu weNazareta, akanga aroverwa pamuchinjikwa; amuka, haapo pano; tarirai pavakanga vamuisa." 
Mark16:7 “Asi endai, mundoudza vadzidzi vake naPetirosi, kuti anokutungamirirai Gareriya, muchandomuonako, sezvaakakuudzai.”" 
Mark16:8 Vakabuda, vakatiza vachibva pahwiro, nokuti vakanga vabatwa nokudedera nokushamiswa; vakasaudza munhu chinhu, nokuti vakanga vachitya. [" 
Mark16:9 Zvino akati amuka mangwanani nomusi wokutanga wevhiki, akazviratidza pakutanga kuna Maria Magadharina, waakanga abudisa mweya yakaipa minomwe kwaari." 
Mark16:10 Iye akaenda kundoudza avo vaiva naye, vakanga vachichema nokusuwa." 
Mark16:11 Ivo vakati vachinzwa kuti ari mupenyu, uye kuti akaonekwa naye, vakasatenda." 
Mark16:12 Shure kwaizvozvo wakazviratidza nomumwe mutowo kuna vaviri vavo, vakanga vachifamba muruwa." 
Mark16:13 Naivowo vakaenda, vakandoudza vamwe; naivo vakasavatendawo." 
Mark16:14 Pashure wakazviratidza kuna vane gumi nomumwe, vagere pakudya; akavapa mhaka pamusoro pokusatenda kwavo noukukutu hwemwoyo yavo, nokuti havana kutenda vaya vakanga vamuona amuka." 
Mark16:15 Akati kwavari, “Endai munyika yose, muparidzire zvisikwa zvose Vhangeri." 
Mark16:16 Anotenda, akabhabhatidzwa, achaponeswa; asi asingatendi achatongwa." 
Mark16:17 Zviratidzo izvi zvichava navanotenda, vachabudisa mweya yakaipa nezita rangu, vachataura nendimi itsva;" 
Mark16:18 vachabata nyoka; kunyangwe vakanwa chinhu chinouraya, hachingavarwadzi; vachaisa maoko pamusoro pavarwere, vakapora.”" 
Mark16:19 Zvino Ishe Jesu akati ataura navo, akagamuchirwa kudenga, akagara kuruoko rworudyi rwaMwari." 
Mark16:20 Ivo vakaenda, vakaparidza kwose–kwose, Ishe achibatsirana navo, achisimbisa shoko nezviratidzo zvaiteverana navo.]" 
Luke1:1 Vazhinji zvavakaedza kurondedzera mashoko ezvinhu izvo zvakaitika pakati pedu," 
Luke1:2 sezvavakatipa ivo vakazviona nameso avo kubva pakutanga, navaiva vanyai veshoko," 
Luke1:3 neniwo, ndakati ndanatsofeya zvose kubva pakutanga, ndakati zvakanaka kuti ndikunyorereiwo nokutevedzanisa, imi Tiofiro, makakurumbira;" 
Luke1:4 kuti muzive kuti mashoko amakadzidziswa ndeezvokwadi. 
Luke1:5 Namazuva aHerodhi, mambo weJudhiya, mumwe mupristi aivapo, ainzi Zekariya, wegovero raAbhia; mukadzi wake aiva wavanasikana vaAroni, zita rake rainzi Erizabheti." 
Luke1:6 Vakanga vakarurama vose, vari vaviri, pamberi paMwari, vachifamba nemirairo nezvakarurama zvose zvaIshe, vasina chavangapomerwa." 
Luke1:7 Vakanga vasina mwana, nokuti Erizabheti akanga asingabereki, uye vakanga vachembera vose vari vaviri." 
Luke1:8 Zvino, akati achibata basa roupristi pamberi paMwari, padzoro regovero rake," 
Luke1:9 akagoverwa netsika dzoupristi, kuti apinde mutemberi yaIshe, kuzopisa zvinonhuwira." 
Luke1:10 Vanhu vazhinji vose vakanga vachinyengetera kunze nenguva yokupisa zvinonhuwira. 
Luke1:11 Ipapo mutumwa waIshe akaonekwa naye, amire kurudyi rweatari yezvinonhuwira." 
Luke1:12 Zekariya akatambudzika achimuona; kutya kukamuwira. 
Luke1:13 Mutumwa akati kwaari, “Usatya Zekariya, nokuti kukumbira kwako kwanzwika. Mukadzi wako Erizabheti achakuberekera mwanakomana, ugomutumidza zita rinonzi Johani." 
Luke1:14 Iwe uchava nomufaro nokufarisisa, navazhinji vachafarira kuberekwa kwake." 
Luke1:15 Nokuti iye achava mukuru pamberi paIshe; haangatongonwi waini nezvinodhaka; achazadzwa noMweya Mutsvene kubva mudumbu ramai vake. 
Luke1:16 Achadzorera vazhinji vevana VaIsiraeri kuna Ishe, Mwari wavo." 
Luke1:17 “Achafamba pamberi pake noMweya nesimba raEriya, kuti adzorere mwoyo yamadzibaba kuvana, navasingateereri kuuchenjeri hwavakarurama, agadzirire Ishe vanhu vakamugadzirirwa kwazvo.”" 
Luke1:18 Zekariya akati kumutumwa, “Izvozvi ndichazviziva seiko? Nokuti ini ndava harahwa, nomukadzi wangu achembera.”" 
Luke1:19 Mutumwa akapindura, akati kwaari, “Ndini Gabhurieri, ndinomira pamberi paMwari; ndatumwa kuti nditaure newe, ndikuparidzire mashoko awa akanaka." 
Luke1:20 “Tarira, uchanyarara, usingagoni kutaura, kusvikira zuva rinoitwa zvinhu izvi, nokuti hauna kutenda mashoko angu, achaitika nenguva yawo.”" 
Luke1:21 Vanhu vakanga vakamirira Zekariya vakashamiswa nokunonoka kwake mutemberi. 
Luke1:22 Zvino akati achibuda, akasagona kutaura navo; vakaziva kuti akanga aona chiratidzo mutemberi; iye akaramba achininira namaoko, akaramba ari mbeveve." 
Luke1:23 Zvino mazuva okushumira kwake akati apera, akaenda kumba kwake." 
Luke1:24 Mazuva iwayo akati apfuura, Erizabheti mukadzi wake akava napamuviri, akazvivanza mwedzi mishanu achiti," 
Luke1:25 “Ndizvo zvandakaitirwa naIshe namazuva aakanditarira, kuti abvise kunyadzwa kwangu pakati pavanhu.”" 
Luke1:26 Nomwedzi wechitanhatu mutumwa Gabhurieri akatumwa naMwari kuguta reGareriya, rinonzi Nazareta," 
Luke1:27 kumhandara yakanga yakaroorwa nomurume, ainzi Josefa, weimba yaDhavhidhi; zita remhandara rainzi Maria." 
Luke1:28 Mutumwa akapinda kwaari, akati, “Kwaziwa, iwe wakaropafadzwa, Ishe anewe!”" 
Luke1:29 Iye akavhunduswa kwazvo neshoko iro, akafunga kuti kukwazisa kwakadaro ndokweiko." 
Luke1:30 Ipapo mutumwa akati kwaari, “Usatya Maria, nokuti wanzwirwa nyasha naMwari." 
Luke1:31 Tarira, uchava napamuviri, uchazvara mwanakomana, ugomutumidza zita rinonzi Jesu." 
Luke1:32 Iye achava mukuru, achanzi Mwanakomana woWokumusoro–soro; Ishe Mwari achamupa chigaro choushe chababa vake Dhavhidhi." 
Luke1:33 Achatonga imba yaJakobho nokusingaperi, noushe hwake hahungavi nomugumo.”" 
Luke1:34 Ipapo Maria akati kumutumwa, “Izvozvi zvingava seiko, zvandisingazivi murume?”" 
Luke1:35 Mutumwa akapindura, akati kwaari, “Mweya Mutsvene achauya pamusoro pako, nesimba roWokumusoro–soro richakufukidza; saka icho chitsvene chichaberekwa chichanzi, Mwanakomana waMwari." 
Luke1:36 Uye tarira, Erizabheti, hama yako, naiye wava napamuviri pomwanakomana pakuchembera kwake; mwedzi uno wava wechitanhatu kuna iye ainzi haabereki." 
Luke1:37 “Nokuti hakuna shoko raMwari richashaiwa simba.” 
Luke1:38 Ipapo Maria akati, “Tarirai, ndiri mushandiri waIshe; ndiitirwe hangu sezvamataura.” Mutumwa akabva kwaari." 
Luke1:39 Namazuva iwayo Maria akasimuka, akakurumidza kuenda kunyika yamakomo, kuguta reJudhiya;" 
Luke1:40 akapinda mumba maZekariya, akakwazisa Erizabheti." 
Luke1:41 Zvino Erizabheti akati achinzwa kukwazisa kwaMaria, mwana akakwakuka mudumbu rake; ipapo Erizabheti akazadzwa noMweya Mutsvene," 
Luke1:42 akadana nezwi guru, akati, “Wakaropafadzwa iwe pakati pavakadzi, nomwana wemimba yako akakomborerwazve!" 
Luke1:43 Zvaita seiko kwandiri, kuti ndamutswa namai vaIshe wangu?" 
Luke1:44 Nokuti, tarira, izwi rokukwazisa kwako rakati richisvika munzeve dzangu, mwana akakwakuka nomufaro mudumbu rangu." 
Luke1:45 Wakaropafadzwa iwe nokuti wakatenda, kuti zvakataurwa naIshe kwauri zvichaitika.”" 
Luke1:46 Maria akati, “Mwoyo wangu unokudza Ishe," 
Luke1:47 Mweya wangu wakafara naMwari, Muponesi wangu;" 
Luke1:48 Zvaakaona urombo hwomushandiri wake; Nokuti, tarira, kubva zvino marudzi ose achanditi, ndakaropafadzwa;" 
Luke1:49 Nokuti uyo anamasimba akandiitira zvinhu zvikuru; Zita rake idzvene. 
Luke1:50 Ngoni dzake dziri kumarudzi namarudzi Avanhu vanomutya. 
Luke1:51 Wakaratidza simba rake noruoko rwake; Akaparadza vaizvikudza mundangariro dzemwoyo yavo; 
Luke1:52 Wakabvisa madzimambo pazvigaro zvavo zvoushe, Akasimudza vakaninipiswa;" 
Luke1:53 Vane nzara akavagutsa nezvakanaka, Akadzosera vapfumi vasina;" 
Luke1:54 Akabatsira Isiraeri, muranda wake, Kuti arangarire ngoni dzake," 
Luke1:55 Sezvaakareva kumadzibaba edu, Kuna Abhurahamu nokurudzi rwake nokusingaperi.”" 
Luke1:56 Maria akagara naye mwedzi inenge mitatu, akadzokera kumusha kwake." 
Luke1:57 Zvino nguva yaErizabheti yokusunguka kwake yakasvika; akabereka mwanakomana. 
Luke1:58 Zvino vakavakidzana navo nehama dzavo vakati vanzwa kuti Ishe akanga amuitira ngoni huru, vakafara naye." 
Luke1:59 Zvino nezuva rorusere vakauya kuzodzingisa mwana, vakada kumutumidza zita rababa vake, Zekariya." 
Luke1:60 I papo mai vakapindura, vakati, “Kwete, achatumidzwa Johani.”" 
Luke1:61 Vakati kwaari, “Hakuna munhu kuhama dzenyu akatumidzwa zita iro.”" 
Luke1:62 Vakabvunza baba vake, vachidudzira namaoko, kuti anzi aniko?" 
Luke1:63 Vakakumbira chinyorero vakanyora kuti, “Johani, ndiro zita rake.” Vakashamiswa vose." 
Luke1:64 Kamwe–kamwe muromo wake ukashamiswa, norurimi rwake rukasununguka, akataura, akarumbidza Mwari." 
Luke1:65 Kutya kukawira vose vakanga vagere navo; namashoko iwayo ose akanzwika kunyika yose yamakomo eJudhiya. 
Luke1:66 Vose vakaanzwa, vakaachengeta mumwoyo mavo, vachiti, “Achazova mwana wakadiniko?” Nokuti ruoko rwaIshe rwakava naye." 
Luke1:67 Baba vake, Zekariya, vakazadzwa noMweya Mutsvene, vakaporofita, vachiti," 
Luke1:68 “Ishe, Mwari waVaIsiraeri, ngaakudzwe; Nokuti aakamutsa vanhu vake, nokuvadzikinura," 
Luke1:69 Akatisimudzira runyanga rwokuponeswa Mumba momuranda wake, Dhavhidhi;" 
Luke1:70 Sezvaakataura nomuromo wavaporofita vake vatsvene, vakanga varipo kubva pakuvamba kwenyika," 
Luke1:71 Kutiponesa pavavengi vedu, napamaoko avose vanotivenga;" 
Luke1:72 Kunzwira madzibaba edu ngoni, Nokurangarira sungano yake tsvene;" 
Luke1:73 Kupika kwaakapika nako kuna baba vedu Abhurahamu," 
Luke1:74 Kutipa simba isu, tasunungurwa mumaoko avavengi vedu, Kuti timushumire tisingatyi," 
Luke1:75 Nohutsvene nokururama pamberi pake mazuva edu ose. 
Luke1:76 Iwe, Mwana, uchanzi muporofita woWokumusorosoro, Nokuti iwe uchatungamira pamberi paIshe, kumugadzirira nzira dzake;" 
Luke1:77 Kuzivisa vanhu vake nzira yokuponeswa nayo, Vachiregererwa zvivi zvavo," 
Luke1:78 Nomwoyo munyoro waMwari wedu, Achatishanyira namambakwedza okudenga," 
Luke1:79 Kuvhenekera vagere murima nomumumvuri worufu; Nokuraramisa tsoka dzedu munzira yorugare.” 
Luke1:80 Mwana akakura, akasimba mumweya, akagara mumarenje, kusvikira zuva rokuratidzwa kwake kuVaIsiraeri." 
Luke2:1 Zvino namazuva iwayo chirevo chakaitwa naKesari Augusto, kuti nyika yose inyorwe mazita." 
Luke2:2 Uku ndokwaiva kunyorwa kwokutanga, kwakaitwa Kuriniosi ari mubati weSiria." 
Luke2:3 Vanhu vose vakaenda kundonyorwa, mumwe nomumwe kuguta rake." 
Luke2:4 NaJosefawo akabva Gareriya, muguta reNazareta, akaenda Judhiya, kuguta raDhavhidhi, rinonzi Bhetirehemu, nokuti aiva weimba yaDhavhidhi, noworudzi rwake;" 
Luke2:5 kuti anyorwe naMaria, wakanga arooorwa, ava napamuviri." 
Luke2:6 Zvino vakati varipo, mazuva okusununguka kwake akasvika;" 
Luke2:7 akasununguka dangwe rake mwanakomana, akamuputira nemicheka, akamuvanzarika muchidyiro chezvipfuwo, nokuti vakashaiwa nzvimbo mumba mavaeni." 
Luke2:8 Zvino kwakanga kuna vafudzi munyika iyo, vaigara kuhuragu vachirinda mapoka avo usiku." 
Luke2:9 Mutumwa waIshe akamira navo, nokubwinya kwaIshe kukavakomba, vakatya nokutya kukuru." 
Luke2:10 Ipapo mutumwa akati kwavari, “Musatya; nokuti tarirai, ndinokuparidzirai mashoko omufaro mukuru, uchava wavanhu vose;" 
Luke2:11 nokuti nhasi mazvarirwa muguta raDhavhidhi Muponesi, ndiye Kristu Ishe." 
Luke2:12 Ichi ndicho chiratidzo kwamuri, muchandowana mwana mucheche, akaputirwa nemicheka, avete muchidyiro chezvipfuwo.”" 
Luke2:13 Ipapo kamwe–kamwe kukavapo pamwechete nomutumwa, vazhinji vehondo yokudenga, vachirumbidza Mwari, vachiti," 
Luke2:14 “Mwari ngaarumbidzwe kumusoro, Norugare ngaruve navanhu vaanofarira.”" 
Luke2:15 Zvino vatumwa vakati vabva kwavari, vaenda kudenga, vafudzi vakataurirana, vachiti, “Ngatiende hedu Bhetirehemu, tindoona chinhu ichi chakaitwa; chatakaziviswa naIshe.”" 
Luke2:16 Ipapo vakakurumidza kuenda, vakawana Maria naJosefa, nomwana mucheche avete muchidyiro chezvipfuwo." 
Luke2:17 Vakati vaona, vakazivisa kwose shoko ravakanga vaudzwa rezvomwana uyo." 
Luke2:18 Vose vakanzwa vakashamiswa nezvavakaudzwa navafudzi. 
Luke2:19 Asi Maria akachengeta mashoko iwayo ose, achifungisisa mumwoyo make." 
Luke2:20 Zvino vafudzi vakadzokera kwakare, vachikudza nokurumbidza Mwari pamusoro pezvose zvavakanzwa nezvavakaona, sezvavakanga vaudzwa." 
Luke2:21 Mazuva masere akati apfuura, musi wokudzingiswa wasvika, vakatumidza zita rake Jesu, iro raakanga atumidzwa nomutumwa, asati agamuchirwa mudumbu ramai." 
Luke2:22 Zvino mazuva okuzvinatsa kwavo nomurairo waMosesi akati apera, vakaenda naye Jerusaremu, kuti vamuise pamberi paIshe;" 
Luke2:23 sezvazvakanyorwa pamurairo waIshe, zvichinzi, “Mwanarume mumwe nomumwe anotanga kuzarura chizvaro, achanzi mutsvene waIshe,”" 
Luke2:24 uye kubayira chibayiro; sezvazvakarehwa pamurairo waIshe, zvinoti, njiva mbiri, kana hangaiwa mbiri duku." 
Luke2:25 Zvino, kwakanga kune munhu paJerusaremu, ainzi Simioni; aiva munhu akarurama aida Mwari, aitarira kunyaradzwa kwaVaIsiraeri; noMweya Mutsvene wakanga anaye." 
Luke2:26 Iye akanga aratidzwa noMweya Mutsvene, kuti haangaoni rufu, asati aona Kristu waIshe." 
Luke2:27 Iye akauya mutemberi achifambirwa noMweya; zvino vabereki vakati vachiuya nomwana Jesu, kuti vaite naye nomutoo womurairo," 
Luke2:28 akamubata mumaoko ake akarumbidza Mwari, achiti," 
Luke2:29 “Zvino, Tenzi, muranda wenyu ngaaende hake Norugare sezvamakareva;" 
Luke2:30 Nokuti meso angu aona ruponeso rwenyu," 
Luke2:31 Rwamakagadzira pamberi pavanhu vose; 
Luke2:32 Chiedza chokuvhenekera vahedheni, Nokurumbidzwa kwavanhu venyu VaIsiraeri.”" 
Luke2:33 Baba vake namai vake vakashamiswa nezvakarehwa pamusoro pake. 
Luke2:34 Ipapo Simioni akavaropafadzwa, akati kuna Maria, mai vake, “Tarira, mwana uyu akaisirwa kuwa nokumuka kwavazhinji pakati paVaIsiraeri, chichava chiratidzo chicharambwa;" 
Luke2:35 uye munondo uchabaya mweya wakowo; kuti ndangariro dzemwoyo mizhinji dzizikanwe.” 
Luke2:36 Zvino kwakanga kuna Anawo, muporofitakadzi, mukunda waFanueri, worudzi rwaAshuru; iye wakanga achembera kwazvo, akanga ano murume makore manomwe kubvira pahumhandara hwake," 
Luke2:37 akanga ari chirikadzi yaiva namakore makumi masere namana, akanga asingabvi mutemberi, achishumira Mwari nokuzvinyima zvokudya nokukumbira usiku namasikati." 
Luke2:38 Naiye akati achisvika nenguva iyo, akatenda Mwari, akataura pamusoro pake kuna vose vakanga vachitarira kusunungurwa kweJerusaremu." 
Luke2:39 Zvino vakati vapedza zvose zvomurairo waIshe, vakadzokera Gareriya, kuguta ravo Nazareta." 
Luke2:40 Mwana akakura, akasimba, akazara nenjere; nenyasha dzaMwari dzikava pamusoro pake." 
Luke2:41 Zvino vabereki vake vaisienda Jerusaremu makore ose kumutambo wePasika. 
Luke2:42 Zvino iye akati ava namakore ane gumi namaviri, akakwirako netsika yomutambo." 
Luke2:43 Vakati vapedza mazuva, pakudzoka kwavo mwana Jesu akasara Jerusaremu, vabereki vake vasingazivi." 
Luke2:44 Asi zvavaiti zvimwe ari kuna vamwe vakanga vari panzira navo, vakafamba zuva rimwe, vakazomutsvaka kuhama dzavo nokushamwari dzavo." 
Luke2:45 Vakati vamushaiwa, vakadzokera Jerusaremu vachimutsvaka." 
Luke2:46 Mazuva matatu akati apfuura, vakamuwana ari mutemberi, agere pakati pavadzidzisi achiteerera nokuvabvunza." 
Luke2:47 Vose vakanga vachimunzwa, vakashamiswa nokuziva kwake uye nokupindura kwake." 
Luke2:48 Zvino vakati vamuona, vakakatyamara; mai vake vakati kwaari, “Mwana, watiitireiko zvakadai? Tarira, Baba vako neni takakutsvaka tichichema.”" 
Luke2:49 Akati kwavari, “Makanga muchinditsvakireiko? Makanga musingazivi kuti ndinofanira kuva pazvinhu zvaBaba vangu here?”" 
Luke2:50 Vakasanzwisisa shoko raakavaudza. 
Luke2:51 Ipapo akaburuka navo, akasvika Nazareta, akavateerera. Mai vake vakachengeta mashoko iwayo ose mumwoyo mavo." 
Luke2:52 Jesu akaramba achienda mberi pakuchenjera, napakukura, napakufadza Mwari navanhu." 
Luke3:1 Negore regumi namashanu rokutonga kwaTibherio Kesari, Pontio Pirato ari ishe weJudhiya, Herodhi ari ishe weGareriya, Firipi munun'una wake, ari ishe weIturea neTirakoniti, Raisaniani ari ishe weAbhirene," 
Luke3:2 Anasi naKayafasi vari vapristi vakuru, shoko raMwari rakauya kuna Johani, mwanakomana waZekariya, murenje." 
Luke3:3 Iye akaenda munyika yose yakapoteredza Jodhani, akaparidza rubhabhatidzo rwokutendeuka kuzokanganwirwa zvivi;" 
Luke3:4 sezvazvakanyorwa mubhuku yamashoko aIsaya muporofita, zvichinzi, “Izwi roanodana murenje, ‘Gadzirai nzira yaIshe, Ruramisai migwagwa yake." 
Luke3:5 Mipata yose ichafusirwa, Makomo ose nezvikomo zvose zvichaderedzwa; Zvakakombama zvicharuramiswa, Pasakaenzana pachaitwa nzira dzakaenzaniswa;" 
Luke3:6 Munhu wose achaona ruponeso rwaMwari.’ ” 
Luke3:7 Naizvozvo akati kuvazhinji vaiuya kuzobhabhatidzwa naye, “Imi vana venyoka, ndianiko akakunyeverai kuti mutize kutsamwa kunouya?" 
Luke3:8 Naizvozvo berekai zvibereko zvakafanira kutendeuka; musatanga kureva mumwoyo menyu, muchiti, Abhurahamu ndibaba vedu; nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, Mwari angamutsira Abhurahamu vana pamabwe awa." 
Luke3:9 Zvino sanhu ratoiswa pamudzi wemiti; naizvozvo muti mumwe nomumwe usingabereki michero yakanaka, unotemwa, ukakandirwa mumoto.”" 
Luke3:10 Vanhu vazhinji vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Zvino todiniko?”" 
Luke3:11 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Ane nguo mbiri ngaagovane noasina; noane zvokudya ngaaite saizvozvo.”" 
Luke3:12 Navateresi vakauyawo kuzobhabhatidzwa, vakati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, todiniko?”" 
Luke3:13 Akati kwavari, “Musareva mari kupfuura pamakarayirwa napo.”" 
Luke3:14 Navarwiwo vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Nesuwo todiniko?” Akati kwavari, “Musatorera munhu chinhu nesimba, kana kupomera munhu nhema; mutende nomubairo wenyu.”" 
Luke3:15 Zvino vanhu vakati vagere vachatarisira, vose vachirangarira mumwoyo mavo pamusoro paJohani kuti zvimwe ndiKristu," 
Luke3:16 Johani akapindura, akati kuna vose, “Ini ndinokubhabhatidzai nemvura, asi uyo anouya, ane simba kupfuureni, wandisina kufanira kusunungura rukanda rweshangu dzake; iye achakubhabhatidzai noMweya Mutsvene nomoto." 
Luke3:17 Rusero rwake ruri muruoko rwake; achanatsa buriro rake kwazvo; achaunganidzira zviyo mudura rake; asi hundi achaipisa nomoto usingadzimwi.” 
Luke3:18 Akaparidzira vanhu Vhangeri, achivaraira namamwe mashoko mazhinji;" 
Luke3:19 asi ishe Herodhi, akati arairwa naye pamusoro paHerodhiasi, mukadzi womunun'una wake, nezvakaipa zvose zvaakanga aita iye Herodhi," 
Luke3:20 akawedzera pamusoro pezvose chinhu ichi, kuti akapfigira Johani mutorongo." 
Luke3:21 Vanhu vose vakati vabhabhatidzwa, naiye Jesu abhabhatidzwawo, achinyengetera, denga rikazarurwa," 
Luke3:22 Mweya Mutsvene akaburukira pamusoro pake nomufananidzo wakaita sowenjiva, izwi rikabva kudenga, richiti, “Ndiwe Mwanakomana wangu, unodikanwa; ndinokufarira.”" 
Luke3:23 Zvino iye Jesu akanga ana makore anenge makumi matatu, nguva yaakatanga kudzidzisa, ari, pakufunga kwavanhu, mwanakomana waJosefa, mwanakomana waHeri," 
Luke3:24 mwanakomana waMatati, mwanakomana waRevhi, mwanakomana waMereki, mwanakomana waJanai, mwanakomana waJosefa," 
Luke3:25 mwanakomana waMatatiasi, mwanakomana waAmosi, mwanakomana waNaumi, mwanakomana waEsiri, mwanakomana waNagai," 
Luke3:26 mwanakomana waMaati, mwanakomana waMatatiasi, mwanakomana waSimioni, mwanakomana waJoseki, mwanakomana waJodha," 
Luke3:27 mwanakomana waJoanani, mwanakomana waResa, mwanakomana waZerubhabheri, mwanakomana waSaratieri, mwanakomana waNeri," 
Luke3:28 mwanakomana waMereki, mwanakomana waAdhi, mwanakomana waKosamu, mwanakomana waErimadhamu, mwanakomana waEri," 
Luke3:29 mwanakomana waJese, mwanakomana waEriezeri, mwanakomana waJorimu, mwanakomana waMatati, mwanakomana waRevhi," 
Luke3:30 mwanakomana waSimioni, mwanakomana waJudha, mwanakomana waJosefa, mwanakomana waJonamu, mwanakomana waEriakimu," 
Luke3:31 mwanakomana waMerea, mwanakomana waMena, mwanakomana waMatata, mwanakomana waNatamu, mwanakomana waDhavhidhi," 
Luke3:32 mwanakomana waJese, mwanakomana waJobhedhi, mwanakomana waBhoasi, mwanakomana waSara, mwanakomana waNasoni," 
Luke3:33 mwanakomana waAminadhabhi, mwanakomana waAdhimini, mwanakomana waArini, mwanakomana waEsiromi, mwanakomana waFaresi, mwanakomana waJudha," 
Luke3:34 mwanakomana waJakobho, mwanakomana waIsaka, mwanakomana waAbhurahamu, mwanakomana waTara, mwanakomana waNahori," 
Luke3:35 mwanakomana waSeruki, mwanakomana waRagau, mwanakomana waFareki, mwanakomana waEbheri, mwanakomana waSara," 
Luke3:36 mwanakomana waKainami, mwanakomana waArifakisadhi, mwanakomana waSemu, mwanakomana waNowa, mwanakomana waRameki," 
Luke3:37 mwanakomana waMatusara mwanakomana waInoki, mwanakomana waJareti, mwanakomana waMahareeri, mwanakomana waKainami," 
Luke3:38 mwanakomana waEnosi, mwanakomana waSeti, mwanakomana waAdhamu, mwanakomana waMwari." 
Luke4:1 Zvino Jesu azere noMweya Mutsvene, akadzokazve achibva kuJodhani, akatungamirirwa noMweya murenje" 
Luke4:2 achiedzwa naDhiabhori mazuva ana makumi mana. Akanga asingadyi chinhu namazuva iwayo; zvino akati apera, akaziya." 
Luke4:3 Zvino Dhiabhori akati kwaari, “Kana uri Mwanakomana waMwari, udza ibwe iri kuti rive chingwa.”" 
Luke4:4 Jesu akamupindura, akati, “Kwakanyorwa kuti munhu haangararami nechingwa bedzi.”" 
Luke4:5 Zvino akamutungamirira kugomo refurefu, akamuratidza ushe hwose hwenyika nenguva duku–duku." 
Luke4:6 Dhiabhori akati kwaari, “Ndichakupa simba iri rose nokubwinya kwazvo, nokuti ndakahupiwa ini, kuti ndihupe wandinoda." 
Luke4:7 Zvino, iwe, kana ukandinamata, zvose zvichava zvako.”" 
Luke4:8 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Kwakanyorwa kuchinzi, ‘Namata Ishe, Mwari wako, umushumire iye oga.’ ”" 
Luke4:9 Akaenda naye Jerusaremu, akamuisa pachiruvi chetemberi, akati kwaari, “Kana uri Mwanakomana waMwari, uzviwisire pasi pano;" 
Luke4:10 Nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, ‘Acharayira vatumwa vake pamusoro pako, kuti vakuchengete;’" 
Luke4:11 ‘Pamaoko avo vachakusimudza, Kuti urege kugumbusa rutsoka rwako pabwe.’ ”" 
Luke4:12 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Kwakanzi, ‘Usaedza Ishe, Mwari wako.’ ”" 
Luke4:13 Dhiabhori akati apedza kuedza kwose, akamusiya kusvikira imwe nguva." 
Luke4:14 Zvino Jesu akadzokera Gareriya nesimba roMweya; mukurumbira wake ukanzwika nenyika yose yakapoteredza. 
Luke4:15 Aidzidzisa mumasinagoge avo, achikudzwa navanhu vose." 
Luke4:16 Akasvika kuNazareta, kwaakanga arerwa, akapinda musinagoge nomusi weSabata sezvaaisiita, akasimuka kuti arave." 
Luke4:17 Akapiwa Bhuku yoMuporofita Isaya; zvino akati aripetenura, akawana pakanyorwa panoti," 
Luke4:18 “Mweya waIshe uri pamusoro pangu, Nokuti akandizodza, kuti ndiparidzire varombo Vhangeri; Akandituma kuti ndizivise vakatapwa kusunungurwa kwavo; Namapofu kuti vaonezve; Ndiregedze vakatsikirirwa;" 
Luke4:19 Nokuzivisa gore raIshe rakanaka.” 
Luke4:20 Akapeta bhuku, akaridzosera kumutariri, akagara pasi; meso avose vaiva musinagoge akamutarisisa." 
Luke4:21 Zvino akatanga kuvaudza, achiti, “Nhasi rugwaro urwu rwaitika munzeve dzenyu.”" 
Luke4:22 Vose vakamupupurira zvakanaka, vakashamiswa namashoko akanaka akabuda mumuromo make, vakati, “Ko uyu haazi mwanakomana waJosefa here?”" 
Luke4:23 Akati kwavari, “Ndinoziva, muchareva tsumo iyi kwandiri, ‘N'anga uzviporese; zvose izvo zvatakanzwa zvakaitwa paKapenaume, uzviitewo nomuno munyika yako.’ ”" 
Luke4:24 Akati, “Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, hakuna muporofita anogamuchirwa munyika yake." 
Luke4:25 Ndinokuudzai shoko iri razvokwadi. Kwakanga kune chirikadzi zhinji pakati paVaIsiraeri pamazuva aEriya, panguva yakazarirwa denga makore matatu nemwedzi mitanhatu, nzara huru ikavapo panyika yose;" 
Luke4:26 asi Eriya haana kutumwa kune mumwe wavo, asi akatumwa Sarepita bedzi, munyika yeSidhoni, kumukadzi aiva chirikadzi." 
Luke4:27 Kwakanga kuna vaiva namaperembudzi vazhinji pakati paVaIsiraeri pamazuva omuporofita Erisha; hakuna mumwe wavo akanatswa, asi Naamani bedzi, muSiria.”" 
Luke4:28 Ipapo vose vakanga vari musinagoge, vakatsamwa zvikuru, vachinzwa izvozvo," 
Luke4:29 vakasimuka, vakamudzingira kunze kweguta, vakaenda naye kumawere egomo, pakanga pakavakwa guta ravo, kuti vamuwisire pasi." 
Luke4:30 Asi iye akapinda napakati pavo, akaenda." 
Luke4:31 Zvino akaburukira Kapenaume, raiva guta reGareriya; akasivadzidzisa nemisi yeSabata;" 
Luke4:32 vakashamiswa nokudzidzisa kwake; nokuti shoko rake rakanga rine simba. 
Luke4:33 Zvino musinagoge makanga muno munhu akanga anomweya wakaipa wakan'ora; iye akadanidzira nezwi guru, achiti," 
Luke4:34 “Haiwa, tine mhaka yeiko nemi, Jesu weNazareta? Mauya kuzotiparadza kanhi? Ndinokuzivai kuti ndimi ani; muri Mutsvene waMwari.”" 
Luke4:35 Ipapo Jesu akaurayira, achiti, “Nyarara, ubude kwaari!” Mweya wakaipa ukamuwisira pasi pakati pavo, ukabuda kwaari, usina kutongomukuvadza." 
Luke4:36 Kutya kukavawira vose, vakataurirana, vachiti, “Shoko iri ndereiko? Nokuti anoraira mweya yakan'ora nechikuriri nesimba, ikabuda.”" 
Luke4:37 Mukurumbira wake ukanzwika kumativi ose enyika yakapoteredza. 
Luke4:38 Zvino akasimuka musinagoge, akapinda mumba maSimoni. Mai vomukadzi waSimoni vakanga vakabatwa nefivhiri zvikuru; vakavakumbirira kwaari." 
Luke4:39 Ipapo akakotamira pamusoro pavo, akarayira fivha, ikavarega; vakasimuka pakarepo, vakavashandira." 
Luke4:40 Zvino zuva rakati rovira, vose vaiva navanorwara nezvirwere zvizhinji vakauya navo kwaari; akaisa maoko ake pamusoro pomumwe nomumwe wavo, akavaporesa." 
Luke4:41 Nemweya yakaipa yakabuda kuvazhinji, ichidanidzira, ichiti, “Ndimi Mwanakomana waMwari!” Asi akayiraira, akasaitendera kutaura, nokuti yakanga ichiziva kuti ndiye Kristu." 
Luke4:42 Zvino kwakati kwaedza, akabuda, akaenda kwakanga kusina vanhu; vazhinji vakamutsvaka, vakasvika kwaari, vakaedza kumudzivisa, kuti arege kubva kwavari." 
Luke4:43 Asi akati kwavari, “Ndinofanira kuparidzira mamwe magutawo Vhangeri youshe hwaMwari; nokuti ndizvo zvandakatumirwa.”" 
Luke4:44 Akasiparidza mumasinagoge eGareriya. 
Luke5:1 Zvino, vanhu vazhinji vakati vachimumanikidza kuti vanzwe shoko raMwari, iye amire paGungwa reGenesareti," 
Luke5:2 akaona magwa maviri ari pagungwa, asi vabati vehove vakanga vabuda maari, vachisuka husvasvi hwavo." 
Luke5:3 Akapinda mune rimwe igwa, raiva raSimoni, akakumbira kwaari kuti abve pamhenderekedzo zvishoma apinde mumvura. Zvino akagara, akadzidzisa vanhu vazhinji, ari muigwa." 
Luke5:4 Akati apedza kutaura, akati kuna Simoni, “Endai kwakadzika, mukande husvasvi hwenyu, kuti mubate.”" 
Luke5:5 Simoni akapindura, akati, “Tenzi, takatambura usiku hwose, tisingabati chinhu; asi zvamadaro imi, ndichakanda husvasvi.”" 
Luke5:6 Vakati vaita izvozvo, vakakuva hove zhinji, husvasvi hwavo hukabvaruka." 
Luke5:7 Vakaninira shamwari dzavo mune rimwe igwa, kuti vauye kuzovabatsira. Vakauya, vakazadza magwa ose ari maviri, akanga onyura." 
Luke5:8 Zvino, Simoni Pita wakati achizviona, akazviwisira pasi pamabvi aJesu, akati, “Ishe, ibvai kwandiri, nokuti ndiri mutadzi.”" 
Luke5:9 Nokuti akanga ashamiswa iye, navose vaakanga anavo nokuwanda kwehove dzavakanga vabata." 
Luke5:10 Ndizvo zvanga zvaitawo Jakobho, naJohani, vanakomana vaZebhedhi, vaiva shamwari dzaSimoni. Ipapo Jesu akati kuna Simoni, “Usatya, kubva zvino uchabata vanhu.”" 
Luke5:11 Zvino, vakati vaisa magwa kunyika, vakasiya zvose vakamutevera." 
Luke5:12 Akati ari kune rimwe guta, tarira, kwakanga kune murume akanga ana maperembudzi muviri wose; iye akati achiona Jesu, akazviwisira pasi nechiso, ndokukumbira kwaari, achiti, “Ishe, kana muchida, munogona kundinatsa.”" 
Luke5:13 Ipapo akatambanudza ruoko, akamubata, achiti, “Ndinoda, chinatswa!” Pakarepo maperembudzi akabva kwaari." 
Luke5:14 Akamurayira kuti asaudza munhu, akati, “Enda unozviratidza kumupristi, ubayire pamusoro pokunatswa kwako zvakarairwa naMosesi, chive chapupu kwavari.”" 
Luke5:15 Asi mukurumbira wake wakapararira nokupfuurisa; vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakaungana kuzomunzwa, nokuporeswa matenda avo." 
Luke5:16 Asi iye akaenda mumarenje, akandonyengetera." 
Luke5:17 Nerimwe ramazuva iwayo akanga achidzidzisa; VaFarisi navadzidzisi vomurairo vakanga vagerepo, vaibva kumisha yose yeGareriya neJudhiya neJerusaremu; simba raIshe rokuporesa rakanga rinaye." 
Luke5:18 Zvino, tarira, vamwe varume vakanga vakatakura munhu akanga akafa mitezo, ari panhoo, vakatsvaka kupinda naye, nokumuisa pamberi pake." 
Luke5:19 Zvino, vakati vachishayiwa pavangamupinza napo, nokuda kwavazhinji, vakakwira pamusoro peimba, vakamuburusira mukati nenhoo yake, napakati pamapfuriro, pamberi paJesu." 
Luke5:20 Iye akati achiona kutenda kwavo, akati, “Murume, wakanganwirwa zvivi zvako.”" 
Luke5:21 Vanyori navaFarisi vakatanga kufunga, vachiti, “Ndianiko uyu anotaura achishonha Mwari? Ndianiko angakanganwira zvivi, asi Mwari oga?”" 
Luke5:22 Zvino Jesu, zvaaiziva mifungo yavo, akapindura, akati kwavari, “Munofungeiko mumwoyo yenyu?" 
Luke5:23 Chiiko chakareruka, kuti, ‘Wakanganwirwa zvivi zvako,’ kana kuti, ‘Simuka, ufambe?’" 
Luke5:24 “Asi kuti muzive kuti Mwanakomana womunhu ane simba panyika rokukanganwira zvivi, akati kune akafa mitezo, ‘Ndinoti kwauri, simuka, utore nhoo yako, uende kumba kwako.’ ”" 
Luke5:25 Akasimuka pakarepo pamberi pavo, akatora chaakanga avete pamusoro pacho, akaenda kumba kwake, achirumbidza Mwari." 
Luke5:26 Vakashamiswa vose, vakarumbidza Mwari, vakatya kwazvo, vachiti, “Taona madambi nhasi!”" 
Luke5:27 Shure kwaizvozvo, akabuda, akaona muteresi, ainzi Revhi, agere panotereswa, akati kwaari, “Nditevere!”" 
Luke5:28 Iye akasiya zvose, akasimuka, akamutevera." 
Luke5:29 Revhi akamuitira mabiko makuru mumba make; kukavapo vazhinji zhinji vavateresi navamwe, vakanga vagere navo pakudya." 
Luke5:30 VaFarisi navanyori vavo vakanyunyutira vadzidzi vake, vachiti, “Munodyireiko navateresi navatadzi, nokunwa navo?”" 
Luke5:31 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Vasingarwari havatsvaki chiremba, asi vanorwara." 
Luke5:32 Handina kuuya kuzodana vakarurama, asi vatadzi, kuti vatendeuke.”" 
Luke5:33 Zvino vakati kwaari, “Vadzidzi vaJohani vanozvinyima zvokudya kazhinji, vachikumbira; navaVaFarisi vanodarowo, asi venyu vanodya nokunwa.”" 
Luke5:34 Jesu akati kwavari, “Mungadzivisa shamwari dzemuwani kudya, muwani achiri kwavari here?" 
Luke5:35 Asi mazuva achasvika; zvino kana muwani azobviswa kwavari, vachazvinyima zvokudya namazuva iwayo.”" 
Luke5:36 Akataura navo nomufananidzo, akati, “Hakuna munhu achabvarura chiremo panguo itsva, akachiisa panguo yakasakara; nokuti chichabvarura nguo itsva, uye chiremo chenguo itsva hachinganzwani neyakasakara." 
Luke5:37 Hakuna munhu achadira waini itsva muhombodo tsaru kana akadaro waini itsva ichaparusa hombodo, ikateuka, nehombodo dzikafawo;" 
Luke5:38 asi waini itsva inofanira kudirwa muhombodo itsva. 
Luke5:39 Hakuna munhu anoti kana anwa waini tsaru, angazoda itsva; nokuti anoti, ‘Tsaru ndiyo yakaisvonaka.’ ”" 
Luke6:1 Zvino nomusi weSabata akafamba napakati peminda yezviyo; vadzidzi vake vakatanha hura, vakadya, vachidzipukuta namaoko." 
Luke6:2 Zvino vamwe vavaFarisi vakati kwavari, “Munoitireiko zvisina kutenderwa kuitwa nomusi weSabata?”" 
Luke6:3 Jesu akavapindura, akati, “Ko hamuna kurava here zvakaitwa naDhavhidhi, musi waakanga aziya, iye navakanga vanaye;" 
Luke6:4 kuti akapinda mumba maMwari, akatora zvingwa zvokuratidza, akazvidya, akapawo vakanga vanaye, izvo zvakanga zvisina kutenderwa kudyiwa, asi navapristi voga?”" 
Luke6:5 Akati kwavari, “Mwanakomana womunhu ndiye Ishe weSabata.”" 
Luke6:6 Zvino neimwe Sabata akapinda musinagoge, akadzidzisa; zvino kwakanga kune munhu ipapo akanga ano ruoko rworudyi rwakakokonyara." 
Luke6:7 Vanyori navaFarisi vakamutarisisa, kuona kana angamuporesa nomusi weSabata, kuti vawane pavangamupomera mhosva napo." 
Luke6:8 Asi iye akaziva mifungo yavo, akati kumunhu akanga ano ruoko rwakakokonyara, “Simuka, umire pakati pavanhu.” Akasimuka, akamira." 
Luke6:9 Zvino Jesu akati kwavari, “Ndinokubvunzai shoko iri, zvakatenderwa here kuita zvakanaka kana zvakaipa neSabata, kuponesa munhu, kana kumuuraya?”" 
Luke6:10 Ipapo akaringa–ringa achivatarira vose, akati kwaari, “Tambanudza ruoko rwako.” Akadaro, ruoko rwake rwukavandudzwa." 
Luke6:11 Zvino vakatsamwa kwazvo, vakarangana vose kuti Jesu vangamuitei." 
Luke6:12 Namazuva iwayo akabudira kugomo kundonyengetera, akapedza usiku hwose achinyengetera kuna Mwari." 
Luke6:13 Zvino kwakati kwaedza, akadana vadzidzi vake; akasarudza kwavari vane gumi navaviri vaakatumidza zita rokuti vapostori;" 
Luke6:14 Simoni, waakatumidzao Petirosi, naAndireya, munun'una wake, naJakobho, naJohani, naFiripi, naBhatoromiyo," 
Luke6:15 naMateu, naTomasi, naJakobho mwanakomana waArifeusi, naSimoni, ainzi Zerote;" 
Luke6:16 naJudhasi mwanakomana waJakobho; naJudhasi Isikarioti, akazomupandukira." 
Luke6:17 Akaburuka navo, akamira pakati chechetere, navadzidzi vake vazhinji, navanhu vazhinji zhinji, vaibva Judhiya yose neJerusaremu, napamhenderekedzo yegungwa reTaya neSidhoni," 
Luke6:18 vakanga vauya kuzomunzwa, nokuporeswa zvirwere zvavo. Navakanga vachitambudzika nemweya yakan'ora vakaporeswa." 
Luke6:19 Vanhu vazhinji vose vakatsvaka kumunyangata, nokuti simba rakabuda kwaari rikavaporesa vose." 
Luke6:20 Zvino akatarisisa vadzidzi vake, akati, “Makaropafadzwa imi varombo, nokuti ushe hwaMwari ndohwenyu." 
Luke6:21 “Makaropafadzwa imi mune nzara zvino, nokuti muchagutiswa. Makaropafadzwa imi munochema zvino, nokuti muchaseka." 
Luke6:22 “Makaropafadzwa, kana vanhu vachikuvengai, vachikudzingai, vachikuzvidzai, vachirasa zita renyu sechinhu chakashata, nokuda kwoMwanakomana womunhu." 
Luke6:23 Farai nezuva iro, mupembere, nokuti tarirai, mubairo wenyu kudenga mukuru; nokuti madzibaba avo akaitira vaporofita zvakadaro." 
Luke6:24 Asi mune nhamo imi vapfumi, nokuti mapiwa kunyaradzwa kwenyu." 
Luke6:25 Mune nhamo imi makaguta zvino, nokuti muchava nenzara. Mune nhamo imi munoseka zvino, nokuti muchachema nokuungudza." 
Luke6:26 “Mune nhamo kana vanhu vose vachitaura zvakanaka pamusoro penyu, nokuti madzibaba avo akaitira vaporofita venhema zvakadaro." 
Luke6:27 “Asi ndinoti kwamuri imi munonzwa, idai vavengi venyu; muitire zvakanaka vanokuvengai." 
Luke6:28 Ropafadzai vanokutukai, munyengeterere vanokushonhai." 
Luke6:29 Anokurova padama, umurinzire rimwewo; anokutorera nguo yokunze, usaramba nenguo yomukatiwo." 
Luke6:30 Mumwe nomumwe anokumbira kwauri, umupe; noanokutorera zvako, usazvikumbirazve kwaari." 
Luke6:31 “Sezvamunoda kuti vanhu vakuitirei, muvaitirewo saizvozvo." 
Luke6:32 Kana muchingoda avo vanokudai, munokuvongwa kwakadiniko? Nokuti navatadziwo vanoda vanovada." 
Luke6:33 Kana muchingoitira zvakanaka avo vanokuitirai zvakanaka, munokuvongwa kwakadiniko? Nokuti navatadzi vanodarowo." 
Luke6:34 Kana muchingopa ivo chikwereti, vamunoti muchadzoserwazve navo, munokuvongwa kwakadiniko? Nokuti navatadzi vanopawo vatadzi chikwereti, kuti vapiwezve zvakaenzana nazvo." 
Luke6:35 Asi idai vavengi venyu, muvaitire zvakanaka. Mupe chikwereti musingaori mwoyo; mubairo wenyu uchava mukuru, mugova vanakomana voWokumusoro–soro; nokuti iye ano mwoyo munyoro kuna vasingavongi navakaipa." 
Luke6:36 Ivai netsitsi, saBaba venyu vane tsitsiwo." 
Luke6:37 “Musatonga, nemi hamungazotongwi; musapa mhaka, nemi hamungazopiwi mhaka; sunungurai, nemi muchasunungurwawo." 
Luke6:38 Ipai, nemi muchapiwa; vachakupai pamaoko enyu chiyero chakanaka, chakatsikirirwa, chakazunguzirwa, chakaita mupfunga; nokuti nechiyero chamunoyera nacho, muchayerwawo nacho.”" 
Luke6:39 Akavaudzawo mufananidzo, akati, “Bofu ringatungamirira rimwe bofu here? Haangawiri mugomba ose ari maviri here?" 
Luke6:40 Mudzidzi haapfuuri mudzidzisi wake. Asi mumwe nomumwe, kana akwaniswa, achava somudzidzisi wake." 
Luke6:41 “Unotarireiko rubanzu ruri muziso rehama yako, izvo, danda riri muziso rako haurioni?" 
Luke6:42 “Kana ungareva seiko kuhama yako, uchiti, ‘Hama, rega ndibvise rubanzu ruri muziso rako, usingaoni danda riri muziso rako?’ Iwe munyengeri, tanga kubvisa danda muziso rako, ipapo uchaonesesa kubvisa rubanzu ruri muziso rehama yako." 
Luke6:43 “Nokuti hakuna muti wakanaka unobereka zvibereko zvakaipa, kana muti wakaipa unobereka michero yakanaka;" 
Luke6:44 nokuti muti mumwe nomumwe unozikanwa nemichero yawo. Nokuti vanhu havatanhi maonde paminzwa, kana mazambiringa haatanwi parukato." 
Luke6:45 Munhu akanaka anobudisa zvakanaka papfuma yakanaka yomwoyo wake; akaipa anobudisa zvakaipa papfuma yakaipa yomwoyo wake; nokuti muromo unoreva zvizere pamwoyo. 
Luke6:46 “Munondiedzireiko, ‘Ishe! Ishe!’ Musingaiti zvandinoreva?" 
Luke6:47 Mumwe nomumwe anouya kwandiri, akanzwa mashoko angu, akaaita, ndichakuratidzai waakafanana naye." 
Luke6:48 Akafanana nomunhu akavaka imba, akachera, akadzikisa, akaiteya paruware; mvura zhinji ikauya, mvura ikarova imba iyo, ikasagona kuizunungusa, nokuti yakanga yakavakwa kwazvo." 
Luke6:49 Asi anonzwa, asingaiti, akafanana nomunhu akavaka imba pavhu, isina nheyo; mvura yakati ichiirova, ikawa pakarepo, kuputsika kweimba iyo kukava kukuru.”" 
Luke7:1 Zvino akati apedzisa mashoko ake ose, vanhu vachianzwa, akapinda Kapenaume." 
Luke7:2 Muranda womumwe mukuru wezana aidikanwa naye, akanga achirwara, achitandadza." 
Luke7:3 Zvino akati anzwa zvaJesu, akatuma vakuru vavaJudha kwaari achikumbira kuti auye kuzoporesa muranda wake." 
Luke7:4 Ivo vakati vachisvika kuna Jesu, vakakumbira zvikuru kwaari, vachiti, “Iye akafanira kuti mumuitire izvozvo;" 
Luke7:5 nokuti anoda rudzi rwedu, ndiye akativakira sinagoge redu.”" 
Luke7:6 Jesu akaenda navo. Zvino ava pedyo neimba, mukuru wezana akatuma shamwari dzake, kuzoti kwaari, “Ishe, musazvitambudza; nokuti handina kufanirwa kuti mupinde mumba mangu;" 
Luke7:7 naizvozvo ndakati handifaniri kuuya kwamuri; asi taurai henyu shoko, muranda wangu achapora."
