Luke7:8 Nokuti neniwo ndiri munhu akaiswa pasi pavamwe, ndinavarwi pasi pangu; kana ndikati kune mumwe, ‘Enda!’ Anoenda; kune mumwe, ‘Uya!’ Anouya; nokumuranda wangu, ‘Ita ichi,’ anoita.”" 
Luke7:9 Jesu akati achinzwa izvozvo, akashamiswa naye, akatendeuka, akati kuvazhinji vakanga vachimutevera, “Ndinoti kwamuri, handina kumboona kutenda kwakadai, kunyangwe napakati paVaIsiraeri.”" 
Luke7:10 Vakanga vatumwa vachidzokera kumba, vakandowana muranda apora." 
Luke7:11 Zvino nezuva rinotevera, akaenda kuguta rainzi Naini; vadzidzi vake navanhu vazhinji zhinji vakaenda naye." 
Luke7:12 Zvino, akati achiswedera pedyo nesuwo reguta, akaona vanhu vakanga vakatakura munhu akafa, mwanakomana mumwe oga wamai vake, yaiva chirikadzi; navanhu vazhinji veguta vakanga vanaye." 
Luke7:13 Zvino Ishe akati achimuona, akamunzwira tsitsi, akati kwaari, “Usachema.”" 
Luke7:14 Ipapo akaswedera, akabata hwanyanza; vakanga vachitakura vakamira. Akati, “Jaya, ndinoti kwauri, muka.”" 
Luke7:15 Iye akanga afa akagara, akatanga kutaura; akamupa mai vake." 
Luke7:16 Vose vakabatwa nokutya; vakarumbidza Mwari, vachiti, “Muporofita mukuru akamuka pakati pedu; uyezve Mwari akashanyira vanhu vake.”" 
Luke7:17 Shoko iri pamusoro pake rikazwika muJudhiya rose nenyika yose yakapoteredza. 
Luke7:18 Vadzidzi vaJohani vakamuudza izvozvo zvose. 
Luke7:19 Johani akadana vadzidzi vake vaviri, akavatuma kuna Ishe neshoko rokuti, “Ko ndimi iye akanga achinzi anouya here, kana tichakatarira mumwe?”" 
Luke7:20 Zvino varume vachisvika kwaari, vakati, “Johani Mubhabhatidzi akatitumira kwamuri neshoko rokuti, ko ndimi iye akanga achinzi anouya here, kana tichakatarira mumwe?”" 
Luke7:21 Nenguva iyo akaporesa vazhinji zvirwere zvavo, nohurwere, nemweya yakaipa; namapofu mazhinji akavasvinudza meso avo." 
Luke7:22 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Endai, mundoudza Johani zvamakaona nezvamakanzwa; zvokuti, mapofu anoona, vanokamhina vanofamba, vanamaperembudzi vanonatswa, vamatsi vanonzwa, vakafa vanomutswa, navarombo vanoparidzirwa Vhangeri." 
Luke7:23 Akaropafadzwa asingagumburwi neni.” 
Luke7:24 Nhume dzaJohani dzakati dzabva, akatanga kuudza vanhu vazhinji pamusoro paJohani, achiti, “Makanga mabuda kundooneiko kurenje? Rutsanga runozununguswa nemhepo here?" 
Luke7:25 Asi makanga mabuda kundooneiko? Munhu akapfeka nguo nyoro here? Tarirai, vane nguo dzinobwinya, navanogara zvakanaka, vari mudzimba dzamadzimambo." 
Luke7:26 Asi makanga mabuda kundooneiko? Muporofita here? Hongu, ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Anopfuura zvikuru muporofita.’" 
Luke7:27 Uyu ndiye akanyorwa pamusoro pake, zvichinzi, ‘Tarira, ndinotuma munyai wangu pamberi pako, Achakugadzirira nzira yako pamberi pako.’ ”" 
Luke7:28 Ndinoti kwamuri, “Kuna vakaberekwa navakadzi, hakuna mukuru kuna Johani Mubhabhatidzi; asi muduku muushe hwaMwari mukuru kwaari.”" 
Luke7:29 Zvino vanhu vose navateresi vakati vachizvinzwa vakati Mwari akarurama, zvavakanga vabhabhatidzwa norubhabhatidzo rwaJohani." 
Luke7:30 Asi VaFarisi navadudziri vomurairo vakaramba kufunga kwaMwari pamusoro pavo, vakasabhabhatidzwa naye." 
Luke7:31 “Naizvozvo vanhu vorudzi urwu ndichavafananidza neiko? Vakafanana nei? 
Luke7:32 Vakafanana navana vagere padare, vanodanidzira, vachiti, ‘Takakuridzirai nyere, mukasatamba; takakuririrai, mukasachema.’" 
Luke7:33 Nokuti Johani Mubhabhatidzi akauya, asingadyi chingwa, asinganwi waini, zvino moti, ‘Ane mweya wakaipa.’" 
Luke7:34 Mwanakomana womunhu akauya achidya, achinwa, zvino moti, ‘Tarirai, munhu anokara, nomunwi, neshamwari yavateresi navatadzi.’" 
Luke7:35 Asi uchenjeri hunoruramiswa navana vahwo vose.” 
Luke7:36 Zvino mumwe wavaFarisi akamukumbira kuti adye naye. Akapinda mumba momuFarisi uyu, akagara pakudya." 
Luke7:37 Zvino tarira, muguta iro makanga muno mukadzi aiva mutadzi; iye akati anzwa kuti agere pakudya mumba momuFarisi, akauya nechinu chearibhasitera chaiva namafuta okuzora," 
Luke7:38 akamira patsoka dzake mumashure make, achingochema, akatanga kunyorovesa tsoka dzake nemisodzi, akadzipukuta nevhudzi romusoro wake, ndokutsvoda tsoka dzake ndokudzizodza namafuta." 
Luke7:39 Zvino muFarisi akanga amudana, akati achizviona, akareva mumwoyo make, achiti, “Munhu uyu, dai aiva muporofita, angadai aiziva mukadzi uyu anomubata kuti ndiani, uye kuti akadini, nokuti mutadzi.”" 
Luke7:40 Ipapo Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Simoni ndine shoko newe.” Akati, “Taurai henyu, mudzidzisi.”" 
Luke7:41 Jesu akati, “Vanhu vaviri vakanga vane chikwereti kumunhu mumwe; mumwe akanga ane chikwereti chamadhinari ana mazana mashanu, mumwe chamakumi mashanu." 
Luke7:42 Vakati vashayiwa chokuripa nacho, akangovakanganwira vose vari vaviri. Zvino ndoupiko kwavari achanyanya kumuda?”" 
Luke7:43 Simoni akapindura, akati, “Handiti ndiye wakakanganwirwa zvizhinji here?” Akati kwaari, “Wareva kwazvo.”" 
Luke7:44 Zvino akatendeukira kumukadzi, akati kuna Simoni, “Unoona mukadzi uyu here? Ndakapinda mumba mako, ukasandipa mvura yetsoka dzangu; asi uyu akanyorovesa tsoka dzangu nemisodzi yake, akadzipukuta nevhudzi rake." 
Luke7:45 Hauna kunditsvoda, asi uyu chinguri chandapinda, haana kurega kutsvoda tsoka dzangu." 
Luke7:46 “Hauna kundizodza musoro wangu namafuta, asi uyu akazodza tsoka dzangu namafuta okuzora." 
Luke7:47 Naizvozvo ndinoti kwauri, ‘Zvivi zvake, zviya zvizhinji, wazvikanganwirwa, nokuti akada zvikuru; asi anokanganwirwa zvishoma, anoda zvishoma.’ ”" 
Luke7:48 Zvino akati kwaari, “Wakanganwirwa zvivi zvako.”" 
Luke7:49 Vakanga vagere naye pakudya vakatanga kureva mumwoyo yavo, vachiti, “Uyu ndianiko anokanganwira zviviwo?”" 
Luke7:50 Akati kumukadzi, “Kutenda kwako kwakuraramisa; enda hako norugare.”" 
Luke8:1 Zvino shure kwaizvozvo, akapota nokumaguta nemisha, achiparidza nokureva zveVhangeri youshe hwaMwari, vane gumi navaviri vanaye." 
Luke8:2 Navamwe vakadzi vakanga vaporeswa pamweya yakaipa napazvirwere, vaiti, Maria anonzi Magadharina, iye akanga abuda mweya yakaipa minomwe kwaari," 
Luke8:3 naJohana, mukadzi waKuza, mutariri waHerodhi, naSusana, navamwe vazhinji, vaimushumira nezvavo." 
Luke8:4 Zvino vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakati vaungana, navakanga vabva kumaguta ose vakasvika kwaari, akataura nomufananidzo, akati," 
Luke8:5 “Mukushi akabuda kundokusha mbeu dzake; akati achikusha, dzimwe mbeu dzakawira panzira, dzikatsikwa, shiri dzokudenga dzikadzidya." 
Luke8:6 Dzimwe dzakawira paruware; dzikamera, dzikaoma, nokushayiwa mwando." 
Luke8:7 Dzimwe dzakawira pakati peminzwa; minzwa ikakura pamwechete nadzo, ikadzivhunga." 
Luke8:8 Dzimwe dzakawira muvhu rakanaka, dzikamera, dzikabereka zvibereko zvine zana. Akati ataura izvozvo, akadanidzira, achiti, ‘Ane nzeve dzokunzwa, ngaanzwe.’ ”" 
Luke8:9 Zvino vadzidzi vake vakamubvunza, kuti mufananidzo uyo wairevei." 
Luke8:10 Akati, “Imi makapiwa kuziva zvakavanzika zvoushe hwaMwari; asi vamwe vanozvipiwa nemifananidzo, kuti vachiona, varege kuona; vachinzwa, varege kunzwisisa." 
Luke8:11 Zvino mufananidzo ndiwo: mbeu ishoko raMwari. 
Luke8:12 Avo vapanzira ndivo vakanzwa; zvino Dhiabhori wouya, achibvisa shoko pamwoyo yavo, kuti varege kutenda, vakaponeswa." 
Luke8:13 Avo vaparuware ndivo vanoti kana vanzwa shoko, vanorigamuchira nomufaro; havano mudzi, vanongotenda nguva duku; nenguva yokuedzwa vanotsauka." 
Luke8:14 Dzakawira pakati peminzwa ndivo vakanzwa; zvino vanoenda, vakavhungiwa nokufunganya nepfuma, nezvinofadza zvoupenyu huno, vakasasvitsa zvibereko." 
Luke8:15 Asi dzomuvhu rakanaka, ndivo vakanzwa shoko mumwoyo wakarurama nowakanaka, vanorichengeta, vachibereka zvibereko nokutsungirira." 
Luke8:16 “Hakuna munhu, anoti kana atungidza mwenje, anozoufukidzira nomudziyo, kana kuuisa pasi pomubhedha; asi anouisa pachigadzikiro, kuti vanopinda vaone chiedza." 
Luke8:17 “Nokuti hakuna chakavanzika, chisingazooneswi, hakuna chakavigwa, chisingazozikanwi, nokubuda pachena." 
Luke8:18 “Naizvozvo, chenjerai mutoo wamunonzwa nawo; nokuti anazvo, achapiwa; asina, achatorerwa naichochowo chaanoti ndinacho." 
Luke8:19 “Zvino mai vake navakoma navanun'una vake vakauya kwaari, vakasagona kusvika kwaari nemhaka yavanhu vazhinji." 
Luke8:20 “Akaudzwa, zvichinzi, ‘Mai venyu navakoma navanun'una venyu vamire kunze, vanoda kukuonai.’ ”" 
Luke8:21 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Mai vangu navakoma navanun'una vangu ndivo vaya vanonzwa shoko raMwari vachiriita.”" 
Luke8:22 Zvino nerimwe ramazuva iwayo akapinda muigwa navadzidzi vake, akati kwavari, “Ngatiyambukire mhiri kwegungwa.” Vakaenda." 
Luke8:23 Zvino vakati vachienda, iye akavata; dutu guru remhepo rikauya pagungwa; vakatanga kuzarirwa nemvura, vakava munjodzi." 
Luke8:24 Vakauya kwaari, vakamumutsa, vachiti, “Tenzi! Tenzi! Tofa!” Ipapo akamuka, akarayira mhepo namafungu emvura; zvikaguma, kukadzikama." 
Luke8:25 Zvino akati kwavari, “Kutenda kwenyu kuripiko?” Vakatya nokushamiswa, vakataurirana, vachiti, “Ndianiko uyu, zvaanoraira kunyangwe nemhepo nemvura, zvichimuteerera?”" 
Luke8:26 Zvino vakasvika kunyika yavaGerasa, yakatarisana neGareriya." 
Luke8:27 Akati achibuda muigwa panyika, mumwe murume weguta akasangana naye, akanga ane mweya yakaipa; nguva huru akanga asina kupfeka nguo, asingagari mumba, asi mumarinda." 
Luke8:28 Zvino iye akati achiona Jesu, akadanidzira, ndokuzviwisira pamberi pake, akati nezwi guru, “Ndine mhaka yeiko nemi Jesu, Mwanakomana woWokumusoro–soro? Ndinokumbira kwamuri kuti musanditambudza.”" 
Luke8:29 Nokuti akarayira mweya wakan'ora kuti ubude kumunhu. Nokuti kazhinji akanga abatwa nawo; akasungwa nezvisungo nengetani akarindiwa; akadambura zvisungo, akadzingirwa kumarenje nomweya wakaipa." 
Luke8:30 Jesu akamubvunza, achiti, “Zita rako ndianiko?” Akati, “Regioni.” Nokuti mweya yakaipa mizhinji yakanga yapinda maari." 
Luke8:31 Ikakumbira zvikuru kwaari, kuti arege kuyiraira kuti iende kwakadzika–dzika." 
Luke8:32 Zvino kwakanga kuripo boka guru renguruve zhinji, raifura mugomo; ikakumbira zvikuru kwaari, kuti aitendere kupinda madziri; akaitendera." 
Luke8:33 Mweya yakaipa ikabuda kumunhu, ikapinda munguruve; ipapo boka rakamhanyira kumawere kugungwa, rikanyura." 
Luke8:34 Vaidzifudza vakati vaona zvaitwa, vakatiza, vakandoudza izvozvo muguta naparuwa." 
Luke8:35 Vakabuda kundoona zvaitwa; vakasvika kuna Jesu, vakandoona munhu, makanga mabuda mweya yakaipa maari, agere patsoka dzaJesu, apfeka, ava munhu kwaye; vakatya." 
Luke8:36 Vakanga vazviona vakavaudza mutoo waakaporeswa nawo, iye waiva nemweya yakaipa." 
Luke8:37 Vanhu vose venyika yakapoteredza yavaGerasa vakakumbira kwaari kuti abve kwavari, nokuti vakanga vabatwa nokutya kukuru. Akapinda muigwa, akadzoka." 
Luke8:38 Asi munhu uyo, makanga mabuda mweya yakaipa maari, akakumbira kwaari kuti agare naye. Asi akamudzosa, achiti," 
Luke8:39 “Dzokera kumba kwako, undotaura zvinhu zvikuru zvawaitirwa naMwari.” Akaenda, akandoparidza muguta rose zvinhu zvikuru zvaakaitirwa naJesu." 
Luke8:40 Zvino Jesu akati achidzoka, vazhinji vakamugamuchira; nokuti vose vakanga vakamumirira." 
Luke8:41 Ipapo mumwe murume, ainzi Jairosi, akanga ari mukuru wesinagoge, akauya akazviwisira patsoka dzaJesu, akakumbira zvikuru kwaari kuti apinde mumba make." 
Luke8:42 Nokuti akanga anomukunda mumwechete, waiva namakore anenge gumi namaviri, akanga atotandadza. Zvino akati achienda, vanhu vazhinji vakamumanikidza." 
Luke8:43 Ipapo mumwe mukadzi, aiva nokurwara kwokubuda ropa makore ane gumi namaviri, akanga apedzera pan'anga zvose zvaairarama nazvo, asingaporeswi neimwe," 
Luke8:44 akauya mumashure make, akabata mupendero wenguo yake, pakarepo kubuda kwake kweropa kukaguma." 
Luke8:45 Jesu akati, “Ndianiko andibata?” Zvino vose vakati vachiramba, Petirosi akati, “Tenzi, vanhu vazhinji vanokumanikidzai nokukutsikirirai.”" 
Luke8:46 Asi Jesu akati, “Mumwe andibata, nokuti ndanzwa kuti simba rabuda kwandiri.”" 
Luke8:47 Zvino mukadzi akati achiona kuti haana kuvanzika, akauya, achidedera, akazviwisira pasi pamberi pake, akamuudza pamberi pavose kuti akanga amubata nemhaka yei, uye kuti akaporeswa pakarepo." 
Luke8:48 Akati kwaari, “Mukunda, kutenda kwako kwakuporesa, enda hako norugare.”" 
Luke8:49 Akati achataura, mumwe akasvika, achibva kumba kwomukuru wesinagoge, akati kwaari, “Mukunda wenyu afa; regai henyu kutambudza Mudzidzisi.”" 
Luke8:50 Zvino Jesu akati achizvinzwa, akapindura, akati, “Usatya, tenda bedzi, iye achaponeswa.”" 
Luke8:51 Zvino akati asvika kumba, akasatendera munhu kupinda naye, asi Petirosi, naJohani, naJakobho, nababa vomusikana, namai." 
Luke8:52 Vose vakanga vachichema, vachimuungudza. Iye akati, “Musachema, haana kufa, asi avete.”" 
Luke8:53 Vakamuseka, vachiziva kuti wafa." 
Luke8:54 Zvino iye akabata ruoko rwake, akadana, achiti, “Musikana, muka!”" 
Luke8:55 Ipapo mweya wake wakadzoka, akamuka pakarepo. Akarayira kuti apiwe zvokudya." 
Luke8:56 Vabereki vake vakashamiswa, asi akavaraira kuti varege kuudza munhu zvakaitwa." 
Luke9:1 Zvino akaunganidza vane gumi navaviri, akavapa simba nechiremera pamusoro pemweya yakaipa yose, nokuporesa kurwara." 
Luke9:2 Akavatuma kuparidza ushe hwaMwari nokuporesa. 
Luke9:3 Akati kwavari, “Musatongotora zvomunzira, kana mudonzvo, kana hombodo, kana chingwa, kana mari; musava nenguo mbiri." 
Luke9:4 Imba ipi neipi yamunopinda mairi, garaimo, mugozobvapo." 
Luke9:5 Uye vose vasingakugamuchirii, kana mobva paguta iro, muzunze guruva riri patsoka dzenyu, chive chapupu kwavari.”" 
Luke9:6 Ipapo vakabva, vakapota nemisha, vakaparidza Vhangeri, nokuporesa panzvimbo dzose." 
Luke9:7 Zvino ishe Herodhi, akanzwa zvose zvakanga zvichiitwa; akakanganiswa, nokuti vamwe vakanga vachiti, Johani akamuka kuvakafa;" 
Luke9:8 Vamwe kuti Eriya aonekwa; navamwezve, kuti mumwe wavaporofita vekare amuka." 
Luke9:9 Herodhi akati, “Johani ndakamugura musoro; zvino ndianiko uyu, wandinonzwa zvinhu zvakadai pamusoro pake?” Akatsvaka kumuona." 
Luke9:10 Vapostori vakati vadzoka, vakamurondedzera zvose zvavakanga vaita; akavatora, akaenda navo vari voga kuguta rainzi Bhetisaidha." 
Luke9:11 Zvino vanhu vazhinji vachizviziva, vakamutevera; akavagamuchira, akavaudza zvoushe hwaMwari, akaporesa vakanga vachida kuporeswa." 
Luke9:12 Zuva rakati rovira, vane gumi navaviri vakauya, vakati kwaari, “Endesai vanhu vazhinji, vaende kumisha nokuruwa rwakapoteredza, vagareko, vawane zvokudya; nokuti pano tiri murenje.”" 
Luke9:13 Asi iye akati kwavari, “Muvape imi, vadye.” Vakati, “Isu hatine nezvingwa zvingapfuura zvishanu, nehove mbiri, asi kana tikaenda kundotengera vanhu vose zvokudya.”" 
Luke9:14 Nokuti vaiva varume vanenge zviuru zvishanu. Akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Vagarisei pasi vaite mapoka, ana vanhu vanenge makumi mashanu.”" 
Luke9:15 Vakaita kudaro, vakavagarisa vose." 
Luke9:16 Ipapo akatora zvingwa zvishanu nehove mbiri, akatarira kudenga, akavonga, akazvimedura, ndokupa vadzidzi kuti vaise pamberi pavanhu vazhinji." 
Luke9:17 Vakadya, vakaguta vose; vakaunganidza zvimedu zvavakanga vasarirwa nazvo, matengu ane gumi namaviri." 
Luke9:18 Zvino akati achinyengetera ari oga, vadzidzi vake vakanga vanaye; akavabvunza, achiti, “Vanhu vazhinji vanoti ndini aniko?”" 
Luke9:19 Vakapindura, vakati, “Vamwe vanoti, Johani Mubhabhatidzi;” vamwe, “Eriya; vamwezve, kuti mumwe wavaporofita vekare amuka.”" 
Luke9:20 Akati kwavari, “Ko imi munoti ndini ani?” Ipapo Petirosi akapindura, akati, “Ndimi Kristu waMwari.”" 
Luke9:21 Akavaudza zvikuru, nokuvarayira kuti varege kuzivisa munhu izvozvo;" 
Luke9:22 achiti, “Mwanakomana womunhu anofanira kutambudzika zvizhinji, nokuraswa navakuru navapristi vakuru navanyori, nokuurayiwa, nokumutswa nezuva retatu.”" 
Luke9:23 Zvino akati kuna vose, “Kana munhu achida kuuya shure kwangu, ngaazvirambe, atakure muchinjikwa wake zuva rimwe nerimwe, anditevere." 
Luke9:24 “Nokuti ani naani anoda kuponesa upenyu hwake, acharasikirwa nahwo; asi anorasikirwa noupenyu hwake nokuda kwangu, achahuponesa." 
Luke9:25 Nokuti munhu achabatsirwa neiko, kana awana nyika yose, akazvirasa nokuzvitadzira?" 
Luke9:26 “Nokuti ani naani anonyara pamusoro pangu namashoko angu, Mwanakomana womunhu achanyarawo pamusoro pake musi waanouya nokubwinya kwake nokwaBaba, nokwavatumwa vatsvene." 
Luke9:27 “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, vamwe varipo kuna vamire pano vasingazofi, vasati vaona ushe hwaMwari.”" 
Luke9:28 Mashoko iwayo akati apera kutaurwa mazuva anenge masere, akatora Petirosi naJohani naJakobho, akakwira mugomo kundonyengetera." 
Luke9:29 Zvino akati achinyengetera, uso hwake hwakashanduka, nguo dzake dzikachena dzikapenya." 
Luke9:30 Zvino tarira, varume vaviri, vanaMosesi naEriya, vakaonekwa vachitaurirana naye." 
Luke9:31 Vakaonekwa vachibwinya, vakataura zvokuenda kwake, kwaakanga ondopedzisa muJerusaremu." 
Luke9:32 Zvino Petirosi, navaiva naye, vakanga vabatwa nehope; asi vakati vachipepuka, vakaona kubwinya kwake, navarume vaviri vamire naye." 
Luke9:33 Zvino vakati voparadzana naye, Petirosi akati kuna Jesu, “Tenzi, zvakanaka, zvatiri pano; ngativake matumba matatu, rimwe renyu, rimwe raMosesi, rimwe raEriya, asingazivi zvaanoreva.”" 
Luke9:34 Akati achataura izvozvo, gore rikauya, rikavafukidza; vakatya vachipinda mugore." 
Luke9:35 Ipapo izwi rakabva mugore, richiti, “Uyu Mwanakomana wangu, musanangurwa wangu, mumunzwei!”" 
Luke9:36 Izwi rakati raenda, Jesu akaonekwa ari oga. Vakanyarara, vakasaudza munhu namazuva iwayo chinhu chimwe chavakanga vaona." 
Luke9:37 Nezuva rinotevera vakati vaburuka mugomo, vazhinji zhinji vakamugamuchira." 
Luke9:38 Zvino mumwe murume pakati pavazhinji akadana, akati, “Mudzidzisi, ndinokumbira kwamuri kuti mutarire mwanakomana wangu, nokuti ndiye mwana wangu mumwe woga." 
Luke9:39 Tarirai, mweya unomubata, zvino woridza mhere pakarepo; unomubvundisa, achipupuma furo; haudi kumurega, asi unomurwadzisa zvikuru." 
Luke9:40 Ndakakumbira vadzidzi venyu kuti vaubudise, vakasagona.”" 
Luke9:41 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Haiwa! Rudzi rusingatendi, rwakatsauka; ndichagara nemi kusvikira rinhiko, nokukuitirai mwoyo murefu? Uya pano nomwanakomana wako.”" 
Luke9:42 Akati achauya, mweya wakaipa ukamuwisira pasi, ukamubvundisa zvikuru. Asi Jesu wakarayira mweya wakaipa, akaporesa mwana, akamudzosera kuna baba vake." 
Luke9:43 Vose vakashamiswa noukuru hwaMwari. Zvino vose vachashamiswa nezvose zvaakaita, akati kuvadzidzi vake," 
Luke9:44 “Mashoko awa ngaapinde munzeve dzenyu; nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu achaiswa mumaoko avanhu.” 
Luke9:45 Asi ivo havana kunzwisisa kutaura uku; vakanga vakuvanzirwa, kuti varege kukunzwisisa; vakatya kumubvunza pamusoro pokutaura uku." 
Luke9:46 Zvino nharo dzikamuka pakati pavo, kuti ndiani mukuru kwavari." 
Luke9:47 Asi Jesu, zvaakanga achiziva kufunga kwemwoyo yavo, akatora mwana muduku, akamuisa parutivi rwake," 
Luke9:48 akati kwavari, “Ani naani anogamuchira mwana uyu muduku muzita rangu, anondigamuchira ini, uye ani naani anondigamuchira ini, anogamuchira akandituma; nokuti muduku kwamuri mose, ndiye mukuru.”" 
Luke9:49 Johani akapindura, akati, “Tenzi, taona munhu achibudisa mweya yakaipa muzita renyu, tikamudzivisa, nokuti haateveri nesu.”" 
Luke9:50 Asi Jesu akati kwaari, “Musamudzivisa; nokuti asingapesani nemi, anemi.”" 
Luke9:51 Mazuva okukwidzwa kwake akati oswedera, akaramba akaratidza chiso chake kuenda Jerusaremu," 
Luke9:52 akatuma nhume pamberi pake. Idzo dzikaenda, dzikapinda mumusha wavaSamaria kundomugadzirira." 
Luke9:53 Asi havana kumugamuchira, nokuti chiso chake chakanga chakaringira Jerusaremu." 
Luke9:54 Vadzidzi vake, Jakobho naJohani, vakati vachizviona, vakati, “Ishe, munoda kuti titi moto uburuke kudenga, uvaparadze here?”" 
Luke9:55 Asi iye akatendeuka, akavaraira." 
Luke9:56 Ipapo vakaenda kune mumwe musha. 
Luke9:57 Zvino vakati vachifamba munzira, mumwe munhu akati kwaari, “Ndichakuteverai pose pamunoenda.”" 
Luke9:58 Jesu akati kwaari, “Mhungubwe dzine mwena, neshiri dzokudenga dzina matendere, asi Mwanakomana womunhu haana paangatsamidza musoro wake.”" 
Luke9:59 Akati kune mumwe, “Nditevere.” Iye akati, “Nditenderei henyu ndimbondoviga baba vangu.”" 
Luke9:60 Asi iye akati kwaari, “Rega, vakafa ngavavige vakafa vavo; asi iwe, enda undoparidza ushe hwaMwari.”" 
Luke9:61 Mumwezve akati, “Ndichakuteverai Ishe, asi munditendere henyu ndimbondoonekana navari mumba mangu.”" 
Luke9:62 Asi Jesu akati kwaari, “Hakuna munhu angati kana aisa ruoko rwake pabadza, akacheukira shure, angafanirwa noushe hwaMwari.”" 
Luke10:1 Shure kwaizvozvo Ishe akagadzazve vamwe vana makumi manomwe, akavatuma vaviri vaviri pamberi pake mumaguta ose, uye kwose kwaakanga achida kuenda." 
Luke10:2 Akati kwavari, “Kukohwa kukuru, asi vakohwi vashoma; naizvozvo kumbirai kuna Ishe wokukohwa kuti abudise vakohwi mukukohwa kwake." 
Luke10:3 Fambai henyu; tarirai, ndinokutumai samakwayana pakati pamapere." 
Luke10:4 Musatora chikwama, kana hombodo, kana shangu; musakwazisa munhu panzira." 
Luke10:5 Paimba ipi neipi yamunopinda, mutange kuti, ‘Rugare ngaruve neimba ino.’" 
Luke10:6 Kana munhu worugare anenge aripo, rugare rwenyu ruchazorora pamusoro pake; kana kusina, ruchadzokera kwamuri." 
Luke10:7 Garai muimba iyo, muchidya nokunwa zvavainazvo; nokuti mubati akafanirwa nomubairo wake; musapota–pota nedzimba." 
Luke10:8 “Paguta ripi neripi, pamunopinda, kana vakakugamuchirai, idyai zvamunopakurirwa." 
Luke10:9 Poresai varwere varimo, muchiti kwavari, ‘Ushe hwaMwari hwaswedera kwamuri.’" 
Luke10:10 Asi guta ripi neripi pamunopinda, kana vasingakugamuchiriyi, budirai munzira dzaro, muti," 
Luke10:11 ‘Kunyangwe neguruva reguta renyu rakanamatira tsoka dzedu, tinorikuhumurira kwamuri; asi muzive chinhu ichi kuti ushe hwaMwari hwaswedera.’" 
Luke10:12 “Ndinoti kwamuri, Sodhoma richarerukirwa nezuva iro kupfuura guta iro." 
Luke10:13 Une nhamo, iwe Korazini! Une nhamo, iwe Bhetisaidha! Nokuti mabasa esimba akaitwa mukati menyu dai akaitwa muTaya neSidhoni, vangadai vatendeuka kare, vakagara vana masaga nedota." 
Luke10:14 Asi Taya neSidhoni acharerukirwa pakutongwa kupfuuremi. 
Luke10:15 Newe Kapenaume, uchasimudzirwa kudenga here? Uchadzika kuHadhesi.”" 
Luke10:16 “Anokunzwai imi, anondinzwa ini; anokurambai imi, anondiramba ini; anoramba ini, anoramba iye akandituma.”" 
Luke10:17 Vana makumi manomwe vakadzoka nomufaro, vachiti, “Ishe, kunyangwe nemweya yakaipa inozviisa pasi pedu muzita renyu.”" 
Luke10:18 Akati kwavari, “Ndakaona Satani achiwa kudenga semheni." 
Luke10:19 “Tarirai, ndakakupai simba rokutsika pamusoro penyoka nezvinyavada, napamusoro pesimba rose romuvengi; hakuna chinhu chingatongokukuvadzai." 
Luke10:20 Asi, musafara bedzi nechinhu ichi, kuti mweya inozviisa pasi penyu; asi mufare kuti mazita enyu akanyorwa kudenga.”" 
Luke10:21 Nenguva iyo akafara noMweya Mutsvene, akati, “Ndinokuvongai baba, Ishe wokudenga napasi, kuti makavanzira vakachenjera navakangwara zvinhu izvi, mukazvizarurira vacheche. Hongu Baba, nokuti ndizvo zvakakufadzai." 
Luke10:22 “Zvinhu zvose ndakazvipiwa naBaba vangu; hakuna anoziva kuti Mwanakomana ndiani, asi Baba, uye kuti Baba ndiani, asi Mwanakomana, naiye Mwanakomana waanenge achida kumuzarurira iye.”" 
Luke10:23 Ipapo akatendeukira kuvadzidzi vake, akati kwavari, vari voga, “Meso, anoona zvamunoona, akaropafadzwa." 
Luke10:24 “Nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, vaporofita vazhinji namadzimambo vaida kuona zvamunoona, vakasazviona, nokunzwa zvamunonzwa, vakasazvinzwa.”" 
Luke10:25 Zvino mumwe mududziri womurairo akasimuka, akamuedza, achiti, “Mudzidzisi, ndingaiteiko kuti ndigare nhaka youpenyu husingaperi?”" 
Luke10:26 Akati kwaari, “Pamurairo pakanyorweiko? Unorava sei?”" 
Luke10:27 Iye akapindura, akati, “Ida Ishe, Mwari wako, nomwoyo wako wose, nomweya wako wose, nesimba rako rose, nokufunga kwako kwose, nowokwako sezvaunozvida iwe.”" 
Luke10:28 Akati kwaari, “Wapindura zvakanaka; ita izvozvo, ugorarama.”" 
Luke10:29 Asi iye, achida kuzviruramisa, akati kuna Jesu, “Wokwangu ndianiko?”" 
Luke10:30 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Mumwe munhu akabva Jerusaremu, akaburukira Jeriko, akawirwa namakororo, akamupamba nguo, akamurova, akaenda, ndokumusiya oda kufa." 
Luke10:31 Zvino mumwe mupristi akanga achingoburuka hake nenzira iyo; akati achimuona, akamunyenyeredza." 
Luke10:32 Noku daro muRevhiwo akasvikapo, akamuona, akamunyenyeredza." 
Luke10:33 Zvino mumwe muSamaria, akanga ari parwendo, akasvika kwaari; akati achimuona, akamunzwira tsitsi," 
Luke10:34 akaenda kwaari, ndokupombera mavanga ake, akaadira mafuta newaini; akamukwidza pachipfuwo chake, ndokumuisa kuimba yavaeni, ndokumuchengeta." 
Luke10:35 “Zvino, ava mangwana, akabudisa madhinari maviri, akaapa muridzi wemba, akati, ‘Muchengete, zvose zvaunomupa kupfuura izvi, ndichakupazve, kana ndichidzoka.’ ”" 
Luke10:36 “Unofungei, ndoupiko kuna vatatu ava akanga ari wokwake waiye akawirwa namakororo?”" 
Luke10:37 Akati, “Ndiye akamuitira ngoni.” Jesu akati kwaari, “Enda, unoita saizvozvo.”" 
Luke10:38 Zvino vakati vachifamba, akapinda muno mumwe musha; mumwe mukadzi ainzi Marita, akamugamuchira mumba make." 
Luke10:39 Iye akanga anomunun'una ainzi Maria, akagarawo pamakumbo aJesu, akanzwa shoko rake." 
Luke10:40 Asi Marita akanga achitambudzika nokushanda zvikuru, akauya, akati, “Ishe, hamuna hanya muchiona munun'una wangu achindirega ndichishanda ndoga here? Muudzei andibatsire.”" 
Luke10:41 Ishe akapindura, akati kwaari, “Marita! Marita! Unofunganya, nokuzvitambudza nezvinhu zvizhinji," 
Luke10:42 asi chinhu chimwe chinodikanwa; nokuti Maria akasanangura mugove wakanaka, waasingazotorerwi.”" 
Luke11:1 Zvino akati achinyengetera pane imwe nzvimbo, apedza, mumwe wavadzidzi vake akati kwaari, “Ishe, tidzidzisei kunyengeterawo Johani sezvaakadzidzisa vadzidzi vakewo.”" 
Luke11:2 Akati kwavari, “Kana muchinyengetera, muti, ‘Baba, zita renyu ngarikudzwe nohutsvene; ushe hwenyu ngahuuye;" 
Luke11:3 mutipe zuva rimwe nerimwe zvokudya zvedu zvinotiringana; 
Luke11:4 mutikanganwire zvivi zvedu, nokuti nesu tinokanganwira vose vane mhosva nesu; musatiisa mukuedzwa.’ ”" 
Luke11:5 Akati kwavari, “Ndianiko kwamuri angava neshamwari; akaenda kwaari pakati pousiku, akati kwaari, ‘Shamwari ndiposewo zvingwa zvitatu;" 
Luke11:6 nokuti shamwari yangu iri parwendo yakasvika kwandiri, zvino handina chandingamupakurira.’" 
Luke11:7 Ari mukati akapindura, akati, ‘Usandinetsa; musuwo watopfigwa, navana vangu vava neni panhoo; handingamuki ndikakupa.’" 
Luke11:8 “Ndinoti kwamuri, kunyangwe asingamuki akamupa, nokuda kwokuti ishamwari yake, achamuka, akamupa zvose zvaanoshaiwa nokuda kwokutsungirira kwake." 
Luke11:9 Ndinoti kwamuri, kumbirai, muchapiwa; tsvakai, muchawana; gogodzai, muchazarurirwa." 
Luke11:10 “Nokuti mumwe nomumwe anokumbira, anopiwa; anotsvaka, anowana; neanogogodza, anozarurirwa." 
Luke11:11 Ndavapiko baba pakati penyu, kana mwanakomana achikumbira chingwa, vangamupa ibwe here? Kana hove, vangamupa nyoka panzvimbo yehove here?" 
Luke11:12 Kana akakumbira zai, vangamupa chinyavada here?" 
Luke11:13 Naizvozvo kana imi makaipa muchiziva kupa vana venyu zvipo zvakanaka, Baba venyu vari kudenga vachapa zvikuru sei Mweya Mutsvene vanokumbira kwaari.”" 
Luke11:14 Zvino akanga achibudisa mweya wakaipa, waiva mbeveve; mweya wakaipa ukati wabva, mbeveve ikataura, vanhu vazhinji vakashamiswa." 
Luke11:15 Asi vamwe vavo vakati, “Anobudisa mweya yakaipa naBheerizebhuri, mukuru wemweya yakaipa.”" 
Luke11:16 Asi vamwe vakamuedza, vakakumbira chiratidzo kwaari chinobva kudenga." 
Luke11:17 Zvino iye akati achiziva kufunga kwavo, akati kwavari, “Ushe humwe nohumwe hunozvipesanisa, hunoparadzwa; neimba inopesana neimba, inowa." 
Luke11:18 NaSatani, kana achizvipesanisa, ushe hwake hungamiri seiko, zvamunoti, ndinobudisa mweya yakaipa naBheerizebhuri?" 
Luke11:19 Kana ini ndichibudisa mweya yakaipa naBheerizebhuri, ko vanakomana venyu vanoibudisa nani? Naizvozvo ivo vachava vatongi venyu." 
Luke11:20 “Asi kana ndichibudisa mweya yakaipa nomunwe waMwari, ipapo ushe hwaMwari hwasvika kwamuri." 
Luke11:21 “Kana munhu ane simba, akashonga nhumbi dzokurwa, achirinda imba yake, nhumbi dzake dzinochengeteka." 
Luke11:22 Asi kana mumwe anomupfuura nesimba akamuvamba, akamukunda, ipapo achamutorera nhumbi dzose dzokurwa, dzaakanga achivimba nadzo, ndokugovera izvo zvaapamba." 
Luke11:23 “Asi neni, anopesana neni, noasingaunganidzi neni, anoparadza." 
Luke11:24 “Mweya wakaipa kana wabuda kumunhu, anopota nenzvimbo dzakaoma, achitsvaka zororo; kana ukashaiwa, unoti, ‘Ndichadzokera kumba kwangu kwandabuda.’" 
Luke11:25 Kana wasvika, unoiwana yatsvairwa, yanatswa." 
Luke11:26 Ipapo unoenda, ndokundotora mimwe mweya minomwe inoukunda nokuipa, ndokupinda, ndokugaramo; kuguma kwomunhu uyo kwakaipa kupfuura kutanga kwake.”" 
Luke11:27 Akati areva izvozvo, mumwe mukadzi pakati pavanhu vazhinji akadanidzira, akati kwaari, “Rakaropafadzwa dumbu rakakutakurai, namazamu amakayamwa.”" 
Luke11:28 Asi iye akati, “Hongu, zvikuru vakaropafadzwa vanonzwa shoko raMwari, vachirichengeta.”" 
Luke11:29 Zvino vazhinji vakati vachiunganira kwaari, akatanga kuti, “Rudzi urwu, rudzi rwakaipa; runotsvaka chiratidzo, asi harungapiwi chiratidzo, asi chiratidzo chaJona." 
Luke11:30 Nokuti Jona sezvaakanga ari chiratidzo kuna vaNinivha, ndizvo zvichaitawo Mwanakomana womunhu kurudzi urwu." 
Luke11:31 Mambokadzi weZasi achasimuka pakutongwa navarume vorudzi urwu, akavapa mhosva, nokuti akabva pamigumo yenyika, kuzonzwa kuchenjera kwaSoromoni; tarirai, mukuru kuna Soromoni ari pano." 
Luke11:32 Varume veNinivha vachasimuka pakutongwa norudzi urwu, vakarupa mhosva, nokuti vakatendeuka nokuparidza kwaJona; tarirai, mukuru kuna Jona ari pano." 
Luke11:33 “Hakuna munhu anoti kana atungidza mwenje angauisa pakavanda, kana pasi pedengu, asi pachigadziko, kuti vanopinda vaone chiedza." 
Luke11:34 Mwenje womuviri iziso rako; kana ziso rako rakanaka, muviri wako wose uchavhenekerwa; asi kana rakaipa, muviri wako wose uchava nerima." 
Luke11:35 Naizvozvo chenjera kuti chiedza chiri mukati mako chirege kuva rima. 
Luke11:36 Zvino kana muviri wako wose wakavhenekerwa, pasina rutivi rune rima, uchavhenekerwa wose, somwenje unokuvhenekera nokupenya kwawo.”" 
Luke11:37 Akati achataura, mumwe muFarisi akakumbira kwaari kuti adye naye; akapinda, akagara pakudya." 
Luke11:38 Zvino muFarisi akashamiswa, achiona kuti haana kumboshamba asati adya." 
Luke11:39 Ishe akati kwaari, “Zvino imi VaFarisi, munosuka kunze kwomukombe nendiro, asi mukati menyu muzere nokukara nokuipa." 
Luke11:40 Imi mapenzi! Ko uyo akaita zviri kunze, haazi iye akaita zviri mukatiwo here?" 
Luke11:41 Asi ipai izvo zviri mukati zvive zvipo; ipapo tarirai zvose zvichava zvakanaka kwamuri. 
Luke11:42 “Asi mune nhamo, imi VaFarisi, nokuti munopa chegumi chemindi neruyi nemiriwo yose, muchirega kururamisira mhaka norudo kuna Mwari; maifanira kuzviita izvi, nokusarega kuita izvozvo." 
Luke11:43 “Mune nhamo, imi VaFarisi, nokuti munoda zvigaro zvapamberi mumasinagoge, nokukwaziswa padare." 
Luke11:44 Mune nhamo, imi, nokuti makaita samakuva asingaonekwi; vanhu vanofamba pamusoro pawo, vasingazivi.”" 
Luke11:45 Zvino mumwe wavadudziri vomurairo akapindura, akati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, kana muchitaura izvozvo, munotituka nesuwo.”" 
Luke11:46 Iye akati, “Mune nhamo nemiwo, vadudziri vomurairo; nokuti munotakudza vanhu mitoro inorema, inotambudza kutakura, asi imi mumene hamubati mitoro iyo kunyangwe nomunwe wenyu mumwechete." 
Luke11:47 “Mune nhamo, imi, nokuti munovaka marinda avaporofita vakaurayiwa namadzibaba enyu." 
Luke11:48 Naizvozvo muri zvapupu, muchitenderanawo namabasa amadzibaba enyu; nokuti ivo vakavauraya, nemi munovaka marinda avo." 
Luke11:49 Saka nokuchenjera kwaMwariwo kwakati, ‘Ndichatumira kwavari vaporofita navapostori, vachauraya vamwe vavo, nokuvatambudza;’" 
Luke11:50 kuti mhosva yeropa ravaporofita vose, rakateurwa kubva pakuvambwa kwenyika, itsvakwe parudzi urwu;" 
Luke11:51 kubva paropa raAbheri, kusvikira paropa raZekariya, akaurayiwa pakati peatari neImba yaMwari; hongu, ndinoti kwamuri, mhosva ichatsvakwa parudzi urwu." 
Luke11:52 “Mune nhamo, imi vadudziri vomurairo; nokuti makabvisa kiyi yokuziva; hamuna kupinda pachenyu, uye makadzivisa avo vakanga vachipinda.”" 
Luke11:53 Akati achibvapo, vanyori navaFarisi vakatanga kumumanikidza kwazvo, nokumubvunzisisa pamusoro pezvimwe zvizhinji," 
Luke11:54 vachimurindira, kuti vamubate pashoko rinobuda mumuromo make." 
Luke12:1 Zvino vanhu vane zviuru zvizhinji vakati vaunganira pamwechete kusvikira votsikirirana, akavamba kutaura kuvadzidzi vake pakutanga, achiti, “Chenjerai mbiriso yavaFarisi, ndiko kunyengera." 
Luke12:2 Hakuna chinhu chakafukidzwa, chisingazozarurwi; kana chakavanzika, chisingazozikanwi." 
Luke12:3 “Saka zvose zvamakataura murima, zvichanzwika muchiedza; nezvamakataura munzeve mudzimba dzomukati, zvichaparidzwa pamusoro pedzimba." 
Luke12:4 “Ndinoti kwamuri, hama dzangu, musatya vanouraya muviri, vasingazogoni kuita chimwe chinhu shure kwaizvozvo." 
Luke12:5 Asi ndichakuratidzai wamunofanira kutya; mumutye iye, anoti kana auraya, ane simbawo rokukandira muGehena. Hongu, ndinoti kwamuri, mutyei iye." 
Luke12:6 Ko shiri duku shanu hadzitengeswi nepeni here? Hakuna imwe yadzo inokanganikwa pamberi paMwari. 
Luke12:7 “Asi nevhudzi romusoro wenyu rakaverengwa rose. Musatya, munopfuura shiri duku zhinji." 
Luke12:8 “Ndinoti kwamuri, mumwe nomumwe anondipupura pamberi pavanhu, Mwanakomana womunhu achamupupurawo pamberi pavatumwa vaMwari." 
Luke12:9 Asi anondiramba pamberi pavanhu, acharambwawo pamberi pavatumwa vaMwari." 
Luke12:10 “Mumwe nomumwe anoreva shoko rakaipa pamusoro poMwanakomana womunhu, achakanganwirwa, asi anoshonha Mweya Mutsvene haangakanganwirwi." 
Luke12:11 “Kana vachikuisai pamberi pamasinagoge navatongi navakuru vakuru, musafunganya kuti tichapindura sei, kana tichapindurei, kana tichataurei." 
Luke12:12 Nokuti Mweya Mutsvene achakudzidzisai nenguva iyo zvamunofanira kutaura.” 
Luke12:13 Zvino mumwe pakati pavazhinji akati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, udzai munun'una wangu kuti agovane nhaka neni.”" 
Luke12:14 Iye akati kwaari, “Iwe munhu, ndianiko akandiita mutongi kana mugoveri pakati penyu?”" 
Luke12:15 Akati kwavari, “Chenjerai, muzvichengete pakuchiva kwose, nokuti upenyu hwomunhu hahuzi pazvinhu zvakawanda zvaanazvo.”" 
Luke12:16 Akavataurira mufananidzo, akati, “Munda womumwe mupfumi wakanga wabereka kwazvo;" 
Luke12:17 akafunga mumwoyo make, akati, ‘Ndichaita seiko? Nokuti handina pandingaunganidzira mbesanwa dzangu.’" 
Luke12:18 Akati, ‘Ndichaita kudai, ndichaputsa matura angu, ndikavaka makuru; ndichaunganidzirapo zviyo zvangu, nezvose zvangu zvakanaka zvandinazvo," 
Luke12:19 ndigoti kumweya wangu, Mweya, une zvakawanda zvakanaka, zvakavigirwa makore mazhinji, zorora, udye, unwe, ufare.’" 
Luke12:20 Asi Mwari akati kwaari, ‘Iwe benzi, nousiku uhwu vachakutorera mweya wako; izvo zvawagadzira, zvichagova zvaani?’" 
Luke12:21 “Ndizvo zvakaita munhu anozviunganidzira pfuma, asingapfumi kuna Mwari.”" 
Luke12:22 Zvino akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Naizvozvo ndinoti kwamuri, musafunganya pamusoro poupenyu hwenyu, kuti muchadyei, kana pamusoro pomuviri wenyu, kuti muchapfekei?" 
Luke12:23 Nokuti upenyu hunopfuura zvokudya, nomuviri unopfuwura zvokupfeka." 
Luke12:24 Fungai makunguo, kuti haadyari, haacheki, haane tsapi kana dura; asi Mwari anoapa zvokudya. Imi munokunda shiri zvikuru sei!" 
Luke12:25 Ndianiko kwamuri angawedzera kubhiti rimwe paurefu hwake nokufunganya? 
Luke12:26 Zvino kana imi musingagoni kuita chinhu chiduku, munofunganyireiko pamusoro pezvimwe?" 
Luke12:27 “Fungai maruva, kumera kwawo; haabati, haaruki; asi ndinoti kwamuri, kunyangwe naSoromoni pakubwinya kwake kwose, haana kushongedzwa serimwe rawo." 
Luke12:28 Zvino kana Mwari achipfekedza saizvozvo uswa hwenyika, huripo nhasi, mangwana hwokandirwa muchoto, haangakupfekedzi nokupfuurisa, imi vokutenda kuduku here?" 
Luke12:29 “Imi musatsvaka zvamuchadya, nezvamuchanwa; musazvidya mwoyo." 
Luke12:30 Nokuti zvinhu izvozvi zvose zvinotsvakwa navahedheni; asi Baba venyu vanoziva kuti munoshayiwa izvozvi. 
Luke12:31 Asi tsvakai ushe hwavo, naizvozvo zvose muchazviwedzerwa." 
Luke12:32 “Musatya henyu, imi veboka duku, nokuti Baba venyu vanofara kukupai ushe." 
Luke12:33 Tengesai zvamunazvo, mupe zvipo; muzviitire zvikwama zvisingasakari, pfuma isingaperi kudenga, pasingasviki mbavha, pasingaparadzi zvipfunho." 
Luke12:34 “Nokuti pane pfuma yenyu, nomwoyo wenyu uchavapowo." 
Luke12:35 “Zviuno zvenyu ngazvigare zvakasungwa, nemwenje yenyu ipfute." 
Luke12:36 Nemi muve savanhu vakarindira ishe wavo pakudzoka kwake kumutambo womuchato; kuti kana akasvika, akagogodza, vamuzarurire pakarepo." 
Luke12:37 Vakaropafadzwa varanda avo, vanoti, kana ishe achisvika, anovawana vakarindira. Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, achazvisunga chiuno iye, akavagarisa pakudya, akauya akavashandira." 
Luke12:38 “Kana akasvika nenguva yokurindira yechipiri, kana yechitatu yousiku, akavawana vakadaro, vakaropafadzwa varanda ivavo." 
Luke12:39 Asi muzive izvi, kuti dai muridzi weimba aiziva nguva inouya nayo mbavha, haazaitendera kuti imba yake ipazwe." 
Luke12:40 Nemiwo mugare makazvigadzira, nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu achauya nenguva yamusingafungi.”" 
Luke12:41 Zvino Petirosi akati kwaari, “Ishe, mufananidzo uyu munoutaura kwatiri, kana kuna vose here?”" 
Luke12:42 Ishe akati, “Ndianiko mutariri akatendeka, akachenjera, achaiswa nashe wake pamusoro pavaranda vake, kuti avape mugove wezvokudya zvavo nenguva yakafanira?" 
Luke12:43 “Akaropafadzwa muranda uyo anoti, kana ishe wake achisvika, akamuwana achiita saizvozvo." 
Luke12:44 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, kuti achamugadza ave mutariri wezvose zvaanazvo." 
Luke12:45 Asi kana muranda uyo akareva mumwoyo make, achiti, ishe wangu anonoka kuuya; akatanga kurova varanda, varume navakadzi, akadya, akanwa, akadhakwa," 
Luke12:46 ishe womuranda uyo achasvika nezuva raasingatariri, nenguva yaasingazivi, akamurovesa zvikuru, akamupa mugove wake pamwechete navasakatendeka." 
Luke12:47 Muranda uyo akaziva kuda kwashe wake, akasagadzira, kana kuita kuda kwake, acharohwa zvakanyanya." 
Luke12:48 “Asi asina kuziva, akaita zvakafanira kurohwa, acharohwa zvishoma. Akapiwa zvizhinji, zvizhinji zvichatsvakwa kwaari; anotendwa nezvizhinji, vachareva zvinopfuurisa kwaari." 
Luke12:49 “Ndakauya kuzokanda moto panyika; zvino ndinoti, dai watobatidzwa hawo!" 
Luke12:50 Ndino rubhabhatidzo rwandichabhabhatidzwa narwo; ndinomanikidzwa sei kusvikira zvichiitika. 
Luke12:51 Munofunga kuti ndakauya kuzopa rugare panyika here? Ndinoti kwamuri, kwete, asi kupesanisa." 
Luke12:52 Nokuti kubva zvino vashanu veimba imwe vachapesana, vatatu vachipesana navaviri, vaviri navatatu." 
Luke12:53 Baba vachapesana nomwanakomana wavo, nomwanakomana nababa vake; mai nomwanasikana wavo, nomwanasikana namai vake; vamwene nomukadzi womwanakomana wavo, nomukadzi womwanakomana navamwene vake.”" 
Luke12:54 Akati kuvanhu vazhinji, “Kana muchiona gore richikwira kumavirira, pakarepo munoti, mvura ichanaya; zvoitika saizvozvo." 
Luke12:55 Kana muchiona mhepo ichivhuvhuta ichibva zasi munoti, kuchapisa kwazvo; zvoitika." 
Luke12:56 Imi vanyengeri; munoziva kududzira zvamunoona zvenyika nezvokudenga, asi hamuzivi sei kududzira nguva ino?" 
Luke12:57 “Munoregereiko kuzvitongera mumene zvakarurama? 
Luke12:58 Nokuti kana uchienda kuna she nomudzivisi wako, edza kuti uregedzwe naye muchiri munzira; kuti arege kukukwirira kumutongi, mutongi akuise kumupurisa, mupurisa akuise mutorongo." 
Luke12:59 Ndinoti kwauri, haungatongobudimo, usati waripa kamari kokupedzisira.”" 
Luke13:1 Nenguva iyo vamwe vakanga varipo vakamuudza shoko ravaGareriya vakanga vavhenganisirwa ropa ravo nezvibairo zvavo naPirato. 
Luke13:2 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Munoti vaGareriya avo vakanga vari vatadzi here kupfuura vaGareriya vose, zvavakatambudzika saizvozvo?" 
Luke13:3 Ndinokuudzai, kwete; asi kana musingatendeuki, imi mose muchaurayiwa saizvozvo." 
Luke13:4 Kana vaya vane gumi navasere, vakawirwa nesvingo yeSiroami, ikavauraya, munoti vakanga vane mhosva kukunda vanhu vose vaigara Jerusaremu here?" 
Luke13:5 Ndinokuudzai, kwete; asi kana musingatendeuki, imi mose muchaurayiwa saizvozvo.”" 
Luke13:6 Zvino akataura mufananidzo uyu, “Mumwe munhu akanga ano muonde, wakanga wakasimwa mumunda wake wemizambiringa; akauya achitsvaka muchero kwauri, akaushayiwa." 
Luke13:7 Ipapo akati kumurimi womunda wemizambiringa, ‘Tarira, ndauya makore matatu ndichitsvaka michero pamuonde uyu, ndikaushayiwa; uuteme, unotadzireiko pasi?’" 
Luke13:8 Akapindura, akati kwaari, ‘Ishe, muuregei henyu nhaka, kusvikira ndichiurimira, nokuuisa mupfudze;" 
Luke13:9 kana ukazobereka michero, zvakanaka; asi kana usingabereki, mungazoutema henyu.’ ”" 
Luke13:10 Zvino akanga achidzidzisa mune rimwe sinagoge nomusi weSabata. 
Luke13:11 Zvino tarira, kwaivapo mukadzi aiva nomweya wourwere makore ane gumi namasere; akanga akafunyana, asingatongogoni kusimuka." 
Luke13:12 Jesu akati achimuona, akamudana, akati kwaari, “Mai, masunungurwa paurwere hwenyu.”" 
Luke13:13 Akaisa maoko ake pamusoro pake; akatasanuka pakarepo, akarumbidza Mwari." 
Luke13:14 Zvino mukuru wesinagoge akatsamwa, nokuti Jesu akaporesa nomusi weSabata, akapindura, akati kuvanhu vazhinji, “Mazuva matanhatu aripo, anofanira kushandwa nawo; uyai naiwayo, muporeswe; asi musauya nomusi weSabata.”" 
Luke13:15 Asi Ishe akamupindura, akati, “Imi, vanyengeri! Ko mumwe nomumwe wenyu haangasununguri mombe yake kana mbongoro yake pachidyiro nomusi weSabata, akaenda nayo kundoinwisa here?" 
Luke13:16 Zvino mukadzi uyu, mwanasikana waAbhurahamu, akanga akasungwa naSatani makore ane gumi namasere, haaizafanira kusunungurwa nomusi weSabata pachisungo ichi here?”" 
Luke13:17 Zvino akati areva izvozvo, vadzivisi vake vose vakanyadziswa; asi vanhu vazhinji vose vakafara nezvinhu zvose zvakaisvonaka, zvakaitwa naye." 
Luke13:18 Zvino akati, “Ushe hwaMwari hwakafanana neiko? Ndichahufananidza nei?" 
Luke13:19 Hwakafanana netsanga yembeu yemasitadhi, yakatorwa nomunhu, akadyara mumunda make, ikamera, ikaita muti, shiri dzokudenga dzikagara pamatavi awo.”" 
Luke13:20 Akatizve, “Ushe hwaMwari ndichahufananidza neiko?" 
Luke13:21 Hwakafanana nembiriso yakatorwa nomukadzi akaiisa muzviyero zvitatu zvoupfu, kusvikira hwose hwaviriswa.”" 
Luke13:22 Zvino akafamba namaguta nemisha, achidzidzisa, achingoenda Jerusaremu." 
Luke13:23 Mumwe akati kwaari, “Ishe, vachazoponeswa vashoma here?”" 
Luke13:24 Akati kwavari, “Irwai kupinda nesuwo rakamanikana; nokuti vazhinji, ndinoti kwamuri, vachatsvaka kupinda, asi havangagoni." 
Luke13:25 Panguva iyo kana muridzi weimba asimuka, azarira suwo, imi mukatanga kumira kunze, mukagogodza pasuwo, muchiti, ‘Ishe! Tizarurirei!’ Iye akapindura, achiti, kwamuri, ‘Handikuzivi kwamakabva.’" 
Luke13:26 Zvino muchatanga kuti, ‘Taidya, tainwa pamberi penyu, uye maidzidzisa panzira dzomumisha yedu.’" 
Luke13:27 Asi iye achati, ‘Ndinokuudzai, handizivi kwamakabva; ibvai kwandiri, imi mose, vaiti vezvisakarurama!’" 
Luke13:28 Apo pachava nokuchema nokugeda–geda kwameno, kana muchiona Abhurahamu naIsaka naJakobho navaporofita vose vari muushe hwaMwari, asi imi mabudiswa kunze." 
Luke13:29 “Vanhu vachabva kumabvazuva, nokumavirira, nokumusoro, nezasi, vakagara muushe hwaMwari." 
Luke13:30 Tarirai, varipo vokupedzisira vachava vokutanga, novokutanga vachava vokupedzisira.”" 
Luke13:31 Nenguva iyo vamwe VaFarisi vakasvika, vakati kwaari, “Budai, mubve pano, nokuti Herodhi anoda kukuurayai.”" 
Luke13:32 Akati kwavari, “Endai, mundoudza mhungubwe iyo, muti, ‘Tarira, ndinobudisa mweya yakaipa, ndinoporesa nhasi namangwana, nezuva retatu ndinopedzisa.’" 
Luke13:33 Asi ndinofanira kufamba nhasi namangwana, nerinotevera, nokuti hazvingaitiki kuti muporofita auraiwe kunze kweJerusaremu." 
Luke13:34 “Jerusaremu, Jerusaremu, unouraya vaporofita, nokutaka namabwe avo vakatumwa kwauri; ndakanga ndichida kazhinji sei kuunganidza vana vako semhambo inounganidza hukwana dzayo munyasi mamapapiro ayo, mukaramba." 
Luke13:35 Tarirai, masiyirwa imba yenyu rava dongo; asi ndinoti kwamuri, hamuchazondioni, kusvikira muchiti, ‘Ngaarumbidzwe iye anouya nezita raIshe!’ ”" 
Luke14:1 Zvino akati apinda mumba momumwe wavakuru vavaFarisi nomusi weSabata kuzodya zvokudya, vakamucherechedza." 
Luke14:2 Zvino kwakanga kune mumwe munhu pamberi pake aiva norukandwe. 
Luke14:3 Ipapo Jesu akapindura, akataura kuvadudziri vomurairo nokuvaFarisi, achiti, “Kwakatenderwa kuporesa nomusi weSabata here, kana kwete?”" 
Luke14:4 Vakaramba vanyerere. Zvino akamutora, akamuporesa, ndokumuendesa." 
Luke14:5 Akati kwavari, “Ndianiko pakati penyu, angati, kana mwanakomana wake, kana mombe yake yawira mugomba, angarega kuibudisa pakarepo nomusi weSabata?”" 
Luke14:6 Vakasagona kupindurazve pamusoro paizvozvi. 
Luke14:7 Zvino akataura mufananidzo kuna vakakokerwa, nokuti akaona vachizvisanangurira zvigaro zvapamberi, akati kwavari," 
Luke14:8 “Kana iwe uchinge wakokerwa nomunhu kumuchato, usagara pachigaro chepamberi; zvimwe mumwe, anokudzwa kupinda iwe, akokerwawo naye;" 
Luke14:9 zvino akakukokera iwe naye, angasvika, akati kwauri, ‘Ibvapo, munhu uyu agare; ipapo uchatanga kugara kuchigaro cheshure uchinyarara.’" 
Luke14:10 Asi kana wakokerwa, enda ugare pachigaro cheshure, kuti uyo akakukokera, kana achisvika, agoti kwauri, ‘Shamwari, pinda mberi!’ Zvino uchakudzwa iwe pamberi pavose vagere pakudya, newe." 
Luke14:11 Nokuti mumwe nomumwe anozvikudza, achaninipiswa; uye mumwe nomumwe anozvininipisa, achakudzwa.”" 
Luke14:12 Akatiwo kune akamukokera, “Kana wagadzira chisvusvuro kana chirariro, usadana shamwari dzako, kana vanun'una vako, kana hama dzako, kana vavakidzani vako, kuti varege kukukokerazve, ugoripirwa." 
Luke14:13 Asi kana wagadzira mutambo wokudya, ukokere varombo, nezvirema, navanokamhina, namapofu." 
Luke14:14 “Ipapo ucharopafadzwa, zvavasina zvavangakuripira nazvo, nokuti ucharipirwa pakumuka kwavakarurama.”" 
Luke14:15 Mumwe wavakanga vagere naye pakudya akati achizvinzwa, akati kwavari, “Akaropafadzwa uyo achadya zvokudya muushe hwaMwari!”" 
Luke14:16 Iye akati kwaari, “Mumwe munhu akagadzira chirariro chikuru, akakokera vazhinji." 
Luke14:17 “Akatuma muranda wake nenguva yokurarira kuti audze vakanga vakakokerwa, kuti, ‘Uyai, nokuti zvose zvagadzirwa zvino.’" 
Luke14:18 Ipapo vose vakatanga nomwoyo mumwe kuzvirevera. Wokutanga akati kwaari, ‘Ndatenga munda, ndinofanira kumbondouona; ndinokumbira kuti undirevere.’" 
Luke14:19 Mumwe akati, ‘Ndatenga nzombe dzamajoko mashanu, ndinoenda kundodziedza; ndinokumbira kuti undirevere.’" 
Luke14:20 Mumwe akati, ‘Ndawana mukadzi, naizvozvo handingauyi.’" 
Luke14:21 Muranda akauya, akaudza ishe wake izvozvo. Ipapo muridzi weimba akatsamwa, akati kumuranda wake, ‘Kurumidza, ubude kunzira huru neduku dzomumusha, uuye pano navarombo, nezvirema, namapofu, navanokamhina.’" 
Luke14:22 Muranda akati, ‘Ishe, izvo zvamarayira, zvaitwa, asi nzvimbo ichipo.’" 
Luke14:23 “Ishe akati kumuranda, ‘Buda kunzira nokuruzhowa, uvagombedzere vapinde, imba yangu izare." 
Luke14:24 Nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, hakuna mumwe kuna varume avo vandakokera, acharavira chirariro changu.’ ”" 
Luke14:25 Zvino vazhinji zhinji vakafamba naye; akatendeuka, akati kwavari," 
Luke14:26 “Kana munhu achiuya kwandiri, asingavengi baba vake namai, nomukadzi, navana, navanun'una, nehanzvadzi, kunyangwe noupenyu hwakewo, haangavi mudzidzi wangu." 
Luke14:27 Ani naani asingatakuri muchinjikwa wake, akauya shure kwangu, haangavi mudzidzi wangu." 
Luke14:28 Nokuti ndiani kwamuri, kana achida kuvaka svingo, asingatangi kugara pasi, akaverenga kukosha kwayo, kuona kana ane mari yokuipedzisa nayo?" 
Luke14:29 Kuti zvimwe kana atanga nheyo, akakoniwa kupedzisa, vose vanozviona, vasatanga kumuseka," 
Luke14:30 vachiti, ‘Uyu munhu akatanga kuvaka, akakoniwa kupedzisa.’" 
Luke14:31 Kana ndoupiko mambo, kana achienda kundorwa nomumwe mambo, asingatangi kugara pasi, akarangarira kana iye, ana vanhu vane zviuru zvamazana zvine gumi, angagona kundosangana noanouya kuzorwa naye, ana vanhu vane zviuru zvamazana zvina makumi maviri?" 
Luke14:32 Kana asingagoni, anotuma nhume, iye achiri kure, kundokumbira mashoko orugare." 
Luke14:33 Saizvozvowo, ani naani kwamuri asingasiyi zvose zvaanazvo, haangavi mudzidzi wangu.”" 
Luke14:34 “Munyu wakanaka; asi kana munyu wakashapa, acharungwa neiko?" 
Luke14:35 Hauchine basa pamunda, kana padutu romupfudze; vanourasira kunze. Ane nzeve dzokunzwa, ngaanzwe.”" 
Luke15:1 Zvino vateresi vose navatadzi vakaswedera kwaari, kuzomunzwa." 
Luke15:2 VaFarisi navanyori vose vakagun'un'una, vachiti, “Uyu munhu anogamuchira vatadzi, achidya navo.”" 
Luke15:3 Zvino akavaudza mufananidzo uyu, achiti," 
Luke15:4 “Ndianiko kwamuri anamakwai ane zana, kana akarasikirwa neimwe yadzo, angasasiya makumi mapfumbamwe namapfumbamwe murenje, akatevera rakarasika kusvikira ayiwana?" 
Luke15:5 “Kana ayiwana, anoriisa pamafudzi ake, achifara." 
Luke15:6 Kana asvika kumusha, anokokera shamwari dzake navavakidzani naye, achiti kwavari, ‘Farai neni, nokuti ndawana hwai yangu yakanga yakarasika.’" 
Luke15:7 “Ndinoti kwamuri, saizvozvo mufaro uchava kudenga pamusoro pomutadzi mumwe anotendeuka, kupfuura pavakarurama vana makumi mapfumbamwe navapfumbamwe, vasingatsvaki kutendeuka." 
Luke15:8 “Ndoupiko mukadzi ana madhirakema ane gumi, kana arasikirwa nerimwe, angarega kutungidza mwenje, akatsvaira imba, akatsvakisisa, kusvikira ariwana?" 
Luke15:9 “Kana ariwana, anokokera hama dzake navavakidzani vake, akati kwavari, ‘Farai neni, nokuti ndawana dhirakema randakanga ndarasikirwa naro.’" 
Luke15:10 Ndinoti kwamuri, saizvozvo mufaro uripo pamberi pavatumwa vaMwari pamusoro pomutadzi mumwe anotendeuka.”" 
Luke15:11 Zvino akati, “Mumwe munhu aiva navanakomana vaviri." 
Luke15:12 Muduku wavo akati kuna baba vake, ‘Baba, ndipei mugove wenhaka uchazova wangu.’ Akavagovera pfuma yake." 
Luke15:13 Mazuva mashoma akati apfuura, mwanakomana muduku akaunganidza zvose, akaenda kunyika iri kure; akaparadzako nhaka yake achifamba nemitoo yakaipa." 
Luke15:14 “Zvino akati apedza zvose, nzara huru ikasvika panyika iyo, akatanga kushayiwa." 
Luke15:15 Ipapo akaenda, akandozviisa kune mumwe wavanhu venyika iyo; iye akamutumira kuminda yake, kundofudza nguruve." 
Luke15:16 Akanga achida kuzvigutsa namateko aidyiwa nenguruve; asi kwakanga kusina munhu waimupa. 
Luke15:17 Zvino akati achizvifunga, akati, ‘Varanda vazhinji sei vababa vangu vane zvokudya zvakawandisa, asi ini ndofa nenzara." 
Luke15:18 Ndichasimuka, ndiende kuna Baba vangu, nditi kwavari, Baba, ndatadzira wedenga, nemi," 
Luke15:19 handichafaniri kunzi mwanakomana wenyu; mundiite somumwe wavaranda venyu.’ 
Luke15:20 Akasimuka, akaenda kuna baba vake. Akati achiri kure, baba vake vakamuona, vakamunzwira tsitsi, vakamhanya, ndokumufungatira, nokumusvoda." 
Luke15:21 “Mwanakomana akati kwavari, ‘Baba, ndatadzira wedenga nemi, handichafaniri kunzi mwanakomana wenyu.’" 
Luke15:22 Asi baba vakati kuvaranda vavo, ‘Kurumidzai, muuye nenguo yakaisvonaka, mumupfekedze iyo; muise mhete pamunwe wake, neshangu patsoka dzake;" 
Luke15:23 muuye nemhuru yakakodzwa, muibaye, tidye, tifare;" 
Luke15:24 nokuti mwanakomana wangu uyu akanga afa, araramazve; akanga arasika, awanikazve.’ Zvino vakatanga kufara." 
Luke15:25 Mwanakomana wake wedangwe akanga ari kumunda; zvino akati achisvika, achiswedera paimba, ndokunzwa kuimba nokutamba." 
Luke15:26 “Ipapo akadanira kwaari mumwe wavaranda, akamubvunza kuti, ‘Izvi zviiko.’" 
Luke15:27 Akati kwaari, ‘Munun'una wako asvika, zvino baba vako vabaya mhuru yakakodzwa, nokuti vamuwanazve ari mupenyu.’ ”" 
Luke15:28 “Asi iye akatsamwa, akaramba kupinda. Zvino Baba vake vakabuda, vakakumbira zvikuru kwaari." 
Luke15:29 Asi iye akapindura, akati kuna baba vake, ‘Tarirai, ndakakushandirai makore awa mazhinji, ndisingatongodariki murairo wenyu, asi hamuna kutongondipa mbudzana, kuti ndifare neshamwari dzangu." 
Luke15:30 Asi mwanakomana wenyu uyu, akaparadza pfuma yenyu nezvipfeve, akati achisvika, momubayira mhuru yakakodzwa.’" 
Luke15:31 Ivo vakati kwaari, ‘Mwana wangu, iwe uneni nguva dzose, zvose zvangu ndezvako." 
Luke15:32 Kwaifanira kuti tifare nokufarisisa, nokuti munun'una wako uyu wakanga afa, wararama; akanga arasika, akawanika.’ ”" 
Luke16:1 Zvino wakatiwo kuvadzidzi vake, “Kwakanga kuno mupfumi, aiva nomutariri; iye akacherwa kwaari, zvichinzi anoparadza pfuma yake." 
Luke16:2 Ipapo akamudana, akati kwaari, ‘Izvi zvandinonzwa pamusoro pako ndezveiko? Chizvidavirira pamusoro pohutariri hwako; nokuti haungazovi mutariri.’" 
Luke16:3 Zvino mutariri akati mumwoyo make, ‘Ndichaiteiko, ishe wangu zvaanditorera hutariri hwangu? Handina simba rokurima naro; kukumbira ndinonyara." 
Luke16:4 Ndinoziva zvandichaita, kuti kana ndabudiswa pahutariri, vandigamuchire mudzimba dzavo.’" 
Luke16:5 Zvino akadana mumwe nomumwe akanga ane chikwereti nashe wake, akati kune wokutanga, ‘Une chikwereti chakadiniko kuna ishe wangu?’" 
Luke16:6 Iye akati, ‘Makate ane zana amafuta.’ Akati kwaari, ‘Tora runyoro rwako, gara pasi pakarepo, unyore makumi mashanu.’" 
Luke16:7 Akati kuno mumwe, ‘Ko iwe, une chikwereti chakadiniko?’ Iye akati, ‘Matengu ane zana ezviyo.’ Akati kwaari, ‘Tora runyoro rwako, unyore makumi masere.’" 
Luke16:8 Ishe wake akarumbidza mutariri asakarurama, nokuti akanga aita nokuchenjera; nokuti vana venyika ino vakachenjera parudzi rwavo kukunda vana vechiedza.”" 
Luke16:9 Ndinoti kwamuri, “Muzviitire shamwari nepfuma isakarurama, kuti, kana yapera, vakugamuchirei mudzimba dzisingaperi." 
Luke16:10 Akatendeka pazvinhu zviduku–duku, akatendekawo pazvikuru; asi asakarurama pazvinhu zviduku–duku, haangaruramiwo pazvikuru." 
Luke16:11 Naizvozvo kana musina kuva vakatendeka papfuma isakarurama, ndianiko achakutendai nepfuma yechokwadi?" 
Luke16:12 Kana musina kuva vakatendeka pazvinhu zvomumwe, ndianiko achakupai zvenyu?" 
Luke16:13 “Hakuna muranda angagona kushandira vatenzi vaviri, nokuti achavenga mumwe, akada mumwe; kana achinamatira mumwe, akazvidza mumwe; hamungashandirii Mwari nepfuma.”" 
Luke16:14 Zvino VaFarisi, vakanga vachida mari, vakanzwa izvozvo zvose, vakamuseka." 
Luke16:15 Akati kwavari, “Imi munozviruramisa pamberi pavanhu, asi Mwari anoziva mwoyo yenyu; nokuti izvo zvinokudzwa pakati pavanhu, zvinonyangadza pamberi paMwari." 
Luke16:16 “Murairo navaporofita zvakanga zviripo kusvikira kuna Johani; kubva panguva iyo ushe hwaMwari hunoparidzwa, mumwe nomumwe anopinda mahuri nesimba." 
Luke16:17 Asi zvakareruka kuti denga nenyika zvipfuure, pakuti tsanga imwe yomurairo ikoneswe." 
Luke16:18 “Mumwe nomumwe anoramba mukadzi wake, akawana mumwe, anoita upombwe; uye mumwe nomumwe anowana wakarambwa nomurume, anoita upombwe." 
Luke16:19 “Mumwe mupfumi akanga aripo, aipfeka nguo tsvuku nemicheka yakanaka, nokufarira zvakaisvonaka misi yose." 
Luke16:20 “Zvino mumwe murombo, ainzi Razaro, akanga anamaronda mazhinji, akaiswa pasuwo rake," 
Luke16:21 achida kuzvigutisa nezvaidonhera patafura romupfumi; kunyangwe nembwa dzaiuya dzichinanzva maronda ake. 
Luke16:22 “Zvino murombo akati afa, vatumwa vakamuisa pachipfuva chaAbhurahamu. Mupfumi akafawo, akavigwa." 
Luke16:23 Zvino ari muHadhesi, ari pakurwadziwa, akatarira kumusoro, akaona Abhurahamu ari kure, naRazaro ari pachipfuva chake." 
Luke16:24 Akadanidzira, akati, ‘Baba Abhurahamu, ndinzwirei ngoni; tumai Razaro, kuti anyike muromo womunwe wake mumvura, atonhodze rurimi rwangu, nokuti ndinorwadziwa nomurazvo uyu womoto.’" 
Luke16:25 Abhurahamu akati, ‘Mwana, funga kuti wakapiwa zvakanaka zvako muupenyu hwako; naRazaro, saizvozvo akapiwa zvakaipa; asi zvino iye anonyaradzwa pano, iwe unorwadziwa." 
Luke16:26 Uye pazvinhu izvi zvose, mukaha mukuru wakaiswa pakati pedu nemi, kuti vokuno vanoda kuenda mhiri kwamuri, vakoniwe, novoko varege kuyambukira kwatiri.’" 
Luke16:27 Ipapo akati, ‘Ndinokumbira kwamuri baba, kuti mumutumire kumba kwababa vangu;" 
Luke16:28 nokuti ndina vanun'una vashanu; kuti andonatsovapupurira, kuti varege kuuyawo panzvimbo ino yokurwadziwa.’" 
Luke16:29 Abhurahamu akati, ‘Mosesi navaporofita vanavo, ngavavanzwe ivo.’" 
Luke16:30 Iye akati, ‘Kwete, baba Abhurahamu, asi kana mumwe akabva kuvakafa, akaenda kwavari, vangatendeuka.’" 
Luke16:31 “Akati kwaari, ‘Kana vasinganzwi Mosesi navaporofita, havangatendi, kunyangwe mumwe akamuka kuvakafa.’ ”" 
Luke17:1 Zvino akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Hazvingaitiki kuti zvigumbuso zvisauya. Asi ane nhamo iye wazvinouya naye." 
Luke17:2 Zvaiva nani kwaari, kuti guyo risungirirwe mumutsipa wake, awisirwe mugungwa, pakuti agumbuse mumwe wavaduku ava." 
Luke17:3 “Chenjerai; kana hama yako ikatadza, umurayire; kana akatendeuka, umukanganwire." 
Luke17:4 Kunyangwe akutadzira kanomwe nezuva rimwe, akadzokera kwauri kanomwe, achiti, ‘Ndatendeuka;’ umukanganwire.”" 
Luke17:5 Zvino vapostori vakati kuna Ishe, “Tiwedzerei kutenda kwedu.”" 
Luke17:6 Ishe akati, “Kana maiva nokutenda kwakaita setsanga yemasitadhi, maiti kumuonde uyu, ‘Dzurwa, usimwe mugungwa!’ Uchakuteererai." 
Luke17:7 “Ndiani kwamuri angava nomuranda anorima, kana anofudza makwai, akati kwaari, achibva kumunda, Uya, ugare pakudya?" 
Luke17:8 “Handiti angati kwaari, ‘Ndigadzirire zvokudya, uzvisunge chiuno, undishandire, kusvikira ini ndadya, ndikanwa; iwe ugozodya, nokunwa?’" 
Luke17:9 Ko angatenda muranda, zvaaita zvakanga zvarayirwa here?" 
Luke17:10 “Saizvozvo nemiwo, kana maita zvose zvamarayirwa, muti, ‘Tiri varanda pasina, takaita sezvataifanira kuita.’ ”" 
Luke17:11 Zvino vakati vachienda Jerusaremu, akapfuura napaSamaria neGareriya." 
Luke17:12 Zvino achipinda munomumwe musha, akasangana navarume vane gumi vaiva namaperembudzi, vamire kure." 
Luke17:13 Vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Jesu, Tenzi, tinzwirei ngoni!”" 
Luke17:14 Zvino akati achivaona, akati kwavari, “Endai mundozviratidza kuvapristi.” Vakati vachienda, vakapora." 
Luke17:15 Zvino mumwe wavo, akati achiona kuti ndaporeswa, akadzoka, achikudza Mwari nezwi guru;" 
Luke17:16 akawira pasi nechiso patsoka dzake, akamuvonga. Zvino iye akanga ari muSamaria." 
Luke17:17 Ipapo Jesu akapindura, akati, “Havana kuporeswa vane gumi here? Vapfumbamwe varipiko?" 
Luke17:18 Hapana akawanikwa adzokera kuzokudza Mwari, asi uyu mutorwa here?”" 
Luke17:19 Ipapo akati kwaari, “Simuka, uende; kutenda kwako kwakuponesa.”" 
Luke17:20 Zvino akati achibvunzwa navaFarisi kuti ushe hwaMwari hunosvika rini, akapindura akati, “Ushe hwaMwari hahuuyi huchionekwa." 
Luke17:21 Havangati, ‘Tarirai pano!’ Kana, ‘Uko!’ Nokuti tarirai, ushe hwaMwari huri mukati menyu.”" 
Luke17:22 Akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Mazuva achasvika amuchatsvaka kuona zuva rimwe ramazuva oMwanakomana womunhu, asi hamungarioni." 
Luke17:23 Vachati kwamuri, ‘Tarirai uko! Tarirai pano!’ Regai kuenda, kana kuvatevera;" 
Luke17:24 nokuti semheni inopenya, ichibva kune rumwe rutivi pasi pedenga, ichivhenekera kusvikira kune rumwe rutivi pasi pedenga; ndizvo zvichaita Mwanakomana womunhuo nezuva rake." 
Luke17:25 Asi anofanira kumbotambudzika zvizhinji, nokurambwa norudzi urwu." 
Luke17:26 Sezvazvakanga zvakaita namazuva aNowa, ndizvo zvazvichaitawo namazuva oMwanakomana womunhu;" 
Luke17:27 vaidya, nokunwa, nokuwana, nokuwaniswa, kusvikira zuva rakapinda Nowa muareka, mvura zhinji ikasvika, ikaparadza vose." 
Luke17:28 Sezvazvakanga zvakaitawo namazuva aRoti; vaidya, nokunwa, nokutenga, nokutengesa, nokusima, nokuvaka;" 
Luke17:29 asi nomusi wakabuda Roti muSodhoma, moto nesurufa zvakanaya, zvichibva kudenga, zvikavaparadza vose." 
Luke17:30 Ndizvo zvazvichaitawo nezuva iro, Mwanakomana womunhu raachaonekwa naro." 
Luke17:31 “Nezuva iro, ari pamusoro peimba, nhumbi dzake dziri mumba, ngaarege kuburuka kundodzitora; saizvozvowo, ari kumunda ngaarege kudzokera kune zviri shure." 
Luke17:32 “Rangarirai mukadzi waRoti. 
Luke17:33 Ani naani anotsvaka kungwarira upenyu hwake, acharasikirwa nahwo, uye ani naani anorasikirwa nahwo, acharuramiswa." 
Luke17:34 Ndinoti kwamuri, usiku uhwo varume vaviri vachava panhoo imwe, mumwe achatorwa, mumwe achasiyiwa." 
Luke17:35 Vakadzi vaviri vachakuya pamwechete, mumwe achatorwa, mumwe achasiyiwa. [" 
Luke17:36 Vaviri vachava kumunda, mumwe achatorwa, mumwe achasiyiwa.]”" 
Luke17:37 Ipapo vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Ipiko, Ishe?” Akati kwavari, “Apo pano mutumbi, ndipo panounganirawo magora.”" 
Luke18:1 Zvino akavaudza mufananidzo wokuti vanofanira kunyengetera nguva dzose, vasingarasi mwoyo;" 
Luke18:2 akati, “Mune rimwe guta makanga munomumwe mutongi, akanga asingatyi Mwari, kana kuva nehanya nomunhu." 
Luke18:3 Zvino kwakanga kune chirikadzi muguta iro, yairamba ichiuya kwaari, ichiti, ‘Ndiruramisire kumuvengi wangu.’" 
Luke18:4 Iye akamboramba nguva; asi pashure akati mumwoyo make, ‘Kunyangwe ndisingatyi Mwari, kana kuva nehanya nomunhu;" 
Luke18:5 iyi chirikadzi zvainonditambudza, ndichairuramisira, kuti irege kuzouya pashure indirove kumeso.’ ”" 
Luke18:6 Ishe akati, “Inzwai zvinorehwa nomutongi asakarurama." 
Luke18:7 Ko zvino Mwari haangaruramisiri vakasanangurwa vake, vanodanidzira kwaari masikati nousiku, kunyangwe achinonoka pamusoro pavo here?" 
Luke18:8 Ndinoti kwamuri, achakurumidza kuvaruramisira. Asi Mwanakomana womunhu kana achisvika, achawana kutenda panyika here?”" 
Luke18:9 Akarevawo mufananidzo uyu kuna vamwe, vakanga vachifunga, vachiti takarurama, vachizvidza vamwe akati," 
Luke18:10 “Vanhu vaviri vakakwira kutemberi kundonyengetera, mumwe ari muFarisi, mumwe ari muteresi." 
Luke18:11 MuFarisi akandomira, akanyengetera kudai, achizvireva, akati, ‘Ndinokutendai Mwari, kuti handina kufanana navamwe vanhu, makororo, vasakarurama, mhombwe, kana nomuteresi uyo." 
Luke18:12 Ndinozvinyima zvokudya kaviri pavhiki, ndinopa chegumi chezvose zvandinowana.’" 
Luke18:13 Asi muteresi akamira kure, asingadi kunyangwe nokutarira kudenga, akazvirova chipfuva, akati, ‘Mwari, ndinzwirei tsitsi, ini mutadzi!’ ”" 
Luke18:14 Ndinoti kwamuri, “Uyu akaburukira kumba kwake aruramiswa kupfuura uya. Nokuti mumwe nomumwe, anozvikudza, achaninipiswa, nomumwe nomumwe, anozvininipisa achakudzwa.”" 
Luke18:15 Zvino vakauya navachechewo kwaari, kuti avanyangate; asi vadzidzi vakati vachizviona, vakavarayira." 
Luke18:16 Ipapo Jesu akavadanira kwaari, akati, “Regai vana vaduku, vauye kwandiri, musavadzivisa, nokuti ushe hwaMwari ndohwavakadai." 
Luke18:17 Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, ani naani asingagamuchiri ushe hwaMwari somwana muduku, haangatongopindi mahuri.”" 
Luke18:18 Zvimo mumwe mukuru wakamubvunza, akati, “Mudzidzisi akanaka, ndingaiteiko kuti ndigare nhaka youpenyu husingaperi?”" 
Luke18:19 Jesu akati kwaari, “Unondiidzireiko wakanaka? Hakuna akanaka, asi mumwechete, iye Mwari." 
Luke18:20 Mirairo unoiziva, inoti, ‘Usaita upombwe, usauraya, usaba, usapupura nhema, kudza baba vako namai vako.’ ”" 
Luke18:21 Iye akati, “Izvi zvose ndakazvichengeta kubva pauduku hwangu.”" 
Luke18:22 Zvino Jesu achizvinzwa, akati kwaari, “Unoshayiwa chinhu chimwechete; tengesa zvose zvaunazvo, upe varombo, uve nepfuma kudenga; ugouya, unditevere.”" 
Luke18:23 Zvino akati achinzwa izvozvo, akabatwa neshungu kwazvo; nokuti akanga ane pfuma zhinji." 
Luke18:24 Zvino Jesu, achimuona, akati, “Vane pfuma vacharemerwa sei kupinda muushe hwaMwari." 
Luke18:25 “Nokuti ngamera ingarerukirwa kupinda paburi retsono, kumupfumi kupinda muushe hwaMwari.”" 
Luke18:26 Zvino vakanga vazvinzwa, vakati, “Ndianiko angagoponeswa?”" 
Luke18:27 Iye akati, “Izvo zvisingabviri kuvanhu, zvinobvira kuna Mwari.”" 
Luke18:28 Ipapo Petirosi akati, “Tarirai, isu takasiya zvose, tikakuteverai.”" 
Luke18:29 Akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Hakuna munhu akasiya imba, kana mukadzi, kana vanun'una kana vabereki, kana vana, nokuda kwoushe hwaMwari," 
Luke18:30 asingazopiwi zvizhinji kuna izvozvo nenguva ino, uye upenyu husingaperi nenguva inouya.’ ”" 
Luke18:31 Zvino akatora vane gumi navaviri, akati kwavari, “Tarirai, tinokwira Jerusaremu, Mwanakomana womunhu achaitirwa zvose zvakanyorwa navaporofita." 
Luke18:32 “Nokuti achaiswa kuvahedheni, nokusekwa, nokuitirwa zvakaipa, nokupfirwa mate," 
Luke18:33 vachamurova, nokumuuraya, asi nezuva retatu achamukazve.”" 
Luke18:34 Asi havana kunzwisisa chinhu chimwe chaizvozvo; shoko iri rakanga rakavanzika kwavari, uye havana kunzwisisa izvo zvakarehwa." 
Luke18:35 Zvino akati aswedera Jeriko, rimwe bofu raigara panzira richikumbira," 
Luke18:36 rakanzwa vanhu vazhinji vachipfuura, rikabvunza, richiti, “Chiiko?”" 
Luke18:37 Vakariudza, vachiti, “NdiJesu weNazareta anopfuura.”" 
Luke18:38 Ipapo rakadanidzira, richiti, “Jesu, Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, ndinzwirei ngoni!”" 
Luke18:39 Zvino vakanga vakatungamira vakariraira, kuti rinyarare; asi rakanyanya kudanidzira, richiti, “Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi, ndinzwirei ngoni!”" 
Luke18:40 Zvino Jesu akamira, akarayira kuti vauye naro kwaari; rikati raswedera, akaribvunza," 
Luke18:41 achiti, “Unoda kuti ndikuitireiko?” Rikati, “Ishe, kuti ndione.”" 
Luke18:42 Jesu akati kwariri, “Chiona, kutenda kwako kwakuponesa.”" 
Luke18:43 Pakarepo rikaona, rikamutevera, richirumbidza Mwari. Vanhu vose vakati vachizviona, vakakudza Mwari." 
Luke19:1 Akapinda Jeriko, akapfuura napakati." 
Luke19:2 Zvino murume aivapo, ainzi Zakeo; iye akanga ari mukuru wavateresi, uye aiva mupfumi;" 
Luke19:3 akatsvaka kuona Jesu, kuti ndiye ani; asi akanga asingagoni, nokuti akanga akapfupika." 
Luke19:4 Ipapo akamhanyira mberi, akakwira mumuonde kuti amuone, nokuti akanga opfuura napo." 
Luke19:5 Zvino Jesu akati achisvikapo, akatarira kumusoro, akati kwaari, “Zakeo, kurumidza uburuke; nokuti nhasi ndinofanira kugara mumba mako.”" 
Luke19:6 Iye akakurumidza kuburuka, akamugamuchira nomufaro." 
Luke19:7 Vose vakazviona, vakagunun'una, vachiti, “Wapinda kundogara nomurume uri mutadzi.”" 
Luke19:8 Ipapo Zakeo akamira, akati kuna Ishe, “Tarirai, Ishe, ndichapa varombo hafu yepfuma yangu, uye kana ndakatorera mumwe chinhu chake nokunyengera, ndichamudzosera zvava zvina.”" 
Luke19:9 Jesu akati kwaari, “Nhasi ruponeso rwasvika paimba ino; nokuti naiyewo mwanakomana waAbhurahamu." 
Luke19:10 “Nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu akauya kuzotsvaka nokuponesa chakarasika.” 
Luke19:11 Vakati vachinzwa izvozvo, akawedzera akataura mumwe mufananidzo, nokuti akanga ava pedyo neJerusaremu, ivo vakati ushe hwaMwari hwobva hwoonekwa pakarepo." 
Luke19:12 Naizvozvo akati, “Mumwe munhu mukuru akaenda kunyika yakanga iri kure, kuti andopiwa ushe, agodzokazve." 
Luke19:13 Akadana varanda vake vane gumi, akavapa gumi repondo, akati kwavari, ‘Shambadzirai, kusvikira ndichiuyazve.’" 
Luke19:14 Asi vanhu venyika yake vakanga vachimuvenga, vakatuma nhume kumutevera, kundoti, ‘Hatidi kuti uyu munhu ave ishe wedu.’" 
Luke19:15 “Zvino akati adzoka kuya kwaakanga andopiwa ushe, akarayira kuti vaya varanda vaakanga apa mari, vadanirwe kwaari, anzwe kuti mumwe nomumwe akawanei nokushambadzira kwake." 
Luke19:16 Wokutanga akasvika, akati, ‘Ishe, pondo yenyu yakawana dzimwe pondo dzine gumizve.’" 
Luke19:17 “Akati kwaari, ‘Zvakanaka, muranda wakanaka; zvawakanga wakatendeka pazviduku–duku, ubate maguta ane gumi.’" 
Luke19:18 “Wechipiri akasvika, akati, ‘Ishe, pondo yenyu yakawedzerazve pondo shanu.’" 
Luke19:19 “Akati kwaariwo, ‘Newe, ubate maguta mashanu.’" 
Luke19:20 Zvino mumwe akasvika, akati, ‘Ishe, tarirai pondo yenyu heyi, yandakanga ndachengeta mumucheka." 
Luke19:21 Nokuti ndakanga ndichikutyai, zvamuri munhu ane hasha, munotora zvamusakaisapo, munocheka zvamusakakusha.’" 
Luke19:22 Akati kwaari, ‘Ndichakutonga namashoko ako amene, iwe muranda wakaipa! Wakanga uchiziva kuti ndiri munhu ane hasha, ndichitora zvandisakaisa, ndichicheka zvandisakakusha;" 
Luke19:23 zvino wakaregereiko kuisa mari yangu mubangi, ndikazoitora pakudzoka kwangu yawanda.’" 
Luke19:24 Ipapo akati kuna vakanga vamirepo, ‘Mutorerei pondo iyo, muipe ane pondo dzine gumi.’" 
Luke19:25 Vakati kwaari, ‘Ishe, atova nepondo dzine gumi.’" 
Luke19:26 Ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Mumwe nomumwe ane chinhu, achapiwa; asi asina, achatorerwa nezvaanazvo." 
Luke19:27 Asi vavengi vangu avo, vakanga vasingadi kuti ndive ishe wavo, uyai navo pano, muvauraye pamberi pangu.’ ”" 
Luke19:28 Akati areva izvozvo, akatungamirira mberi achikwira Jerusaremu." 
Luke19:29 Akati oswedera Bhetifage neBhetania, kugomo rinonzi reMiorivhi, akatuma vadzidzi vake vaviri," 
Luke19:30 achiti, “Endai kumusha wakatarisana nemi; kana muchipinda mauri, muchawana mhuru yembongoro yakasungirwa, isina kumbotasvwa nomunhu; muisunungure, mugouya nayo." 
Luke19:31 Kana mumwe akakubvunzai, achiti, ‘Munoisunungurireiko?’ Muti kwaari, ‘Kudai ishe anoida.’ ”" 
Luke19:32 Avo vakatumwa vakaenda, vakandowana sezvaakanga avaudza." 
Luke19:33 Zvino vakati vachisunungura mhuru, varidzi vayo vakati kwavari, “Munosunungurireiko mhuru?”" 
Luke19:34 Vakati, “Ishe anoida.”" 
Luke19:35 Vakauya nayo kuna Jesu, vakaisa nguo dzavo pamusoro pemhuru, vakatasvisa Jesu pamusoro payo." 
Luke19:36 Zvino achifamba, vakawarira nguo dzavo munzira." 
Luke19:37 Akati oswedera pamaburusiro egomo reMiorivhi, vadzidzi vake vazhinji vose vakatanga kufara nokurumbidza Mwari nezwi guru pamusoro pamabasa ose esimba avakanga vaona," 
Luke19:38 vachiti, “Mambo ngaakudzwe, iye anouya muzita raIshe! Rugare ngaruve kudenga, nokubwinya kumusoro–soro!”" 
Luke19:39 Vamwe VaFarisi pakati pavazhinji vakati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, rairai vadzidzi venyu!”" 
Luke19:40 Akapindura, akati, “Ndinokuudzai, kana ava vakanyarara, mabwe angadanidzira.”" 
Luke19:41 Zvino akati aswedera pedyo, akaona guta, akachema pamusoro paro," 
Luke19:42 achiti, “Dai waiziva iwe zuva rino zvinhu zvingakupa rugare, asi zvino zvakavanzirwa meso ako!" 
Luke19:43 Nokuti uchasvikirwa namazuva, auchavakirwa nawo muchinjiziri navavengi vako, vachakukomba, nokukumanikidza pamativi ose;" 
Luke19:44 vachakuparadzira pasi, iwe navana vako mukati mako; havangaregi mukati mako ibwe rimwe riri pamusoro perimwe; nokuti hauna kuziva nguva yokushanyirwa kwako.”" 
Luke19:45 Zvino akapinda mutemberi, akatanga kubudisira kunze vakanga vachitengesamo," 
Luke19:46 achiti kwavari, “Kwakanyorwa kuti imba yangu ichava imba yokunyengetera; asi imi makaiita bako ramakororo.”" 
Luke19:47 Aidzidzisa zuva rimwe nerimwe mutemberi; asi vapristi vakuru navanyori navakuru vavanhu vakanga vachitsvaka kumuuraya. 
Luke19:48 Asi vakanga vasingawani zvavangaita, nokuti vanhu vose vakamunamatira, vachimunzwa." 
Luke20:1 Zvino pane rimwe ramazuva iwayo, achidzidzisa vanhu mutemberi, achivaparidzira Vhangeri, vapristi vakuru navanyori navakuru vakasvika," 
Luke20:2 vakataura, vakati kwaari, “Tiudzei, kuti munoita zvinhu izvi nesimba ripi, kana ndianiko akakupai simba iri?”" 
Luke20:3 Akapindura, akati kwavari, “Neni ndichakubvunzaiwo shoko; ndiudzei." 
Luke20:4 Rubhabhatidzo rwaJohani rwakabva kudenga kana kuvanhu here?” 
Luke20:5 Vakataurirana pakati pavo, vachiti, “Kana tikati, ‘Kudenga,’ achati, ‘Makagoregerei kumutenda?’" 
Luke20:6 Asi kana tikati, ‘Kuvanhu,’ vanhu vose vachatitaka namabwe; nokuti ivo vanotenda kuti Johani aiva muporofita.”" 
Luke20:7 Vakapindura, vachiti, “Hatizivi kwarwakabva.”" 
Luke20:8 Zvino Jesu akati kwavari, “Neniwo handingakuudziyi simba randinoita naro zvinhu izvi.”" 
Luke20:9 Zvino akatanga kuudza vanhu mufananidzo uyu, “Mumwe munhu akanga asima munda wemizambiringa; akaupa varimi; akandogara kumwe nguva refu." 
Luke20:10 Nenguva yezvibereko akatuma muranda kuvarimi, kuti vamupe zvibereko zvomunda wemizambiringa; asi varimi vakamurova, vakamudzosa asina." 
Luke20:11 “Akatumazve mumwe muranda; naiyewo vakamurova, vakamunyadzisa, vakamudzosa asina." 
Luke20:12 Akatumazve wechitatu; naiye vakamukuvadza, vakamubudisa kunze." 
Luke20:13 Zvino muridzi womunda wemizambiringa akati, ‘Ndichaiteiko? Ndichatuma mwanakomana wangu anodikanwa, zvimwe vachamukudza iye.’" 
Luke20:14 Asi varimi vakati vachimuona, vakarangana, vakati, ‘Uyu ndiye mugari wenhaka; ngatimuuraye, nhaka igova yedu.’" 
Luke20:15 Vakamubudisa kunze kwomunda wemizambiringa, vakamuuraya. Zvino, muridzi womunda wemizambiringa achavaiteiko?" 
Luke20:16 Achauya, akaparadza varimi ivava; munda wemizambiringa akaupa vamwe.” Zvino vachinzwa izvozvo, vakati, “Haisva!”" 
Luke20:17 Wakati avatarisisa, akati, “Zvino Chiiko icho chakanyorwa, chinoti, ‘Ibwe rakaraswa navavaki, Ndiro rakazova musoro wekona?’" 
Luke20:18 “Mumwe nomumwe anowira pamusoro pebwe iro, achavhunikanya; asi richaparadza warinowira.”" 
Luke20:19 Zvino vanyori navapristi vakuru vakatsvaka nenguva iyo kumubata, asi vakatya vanhu; nokuti vakaziva kuti akareva ivo nomufananidzo uyo." 
Luke20:20 Vakamucherechedza, vakatuma vashori, vakazviita savanhu vakarurama, kuti vamubate pakutaura kwake, vamuise kuushe nesimba romutongi." 
Luke20:21 Vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Mudzidzisi, tinoziva kuti munotaura nokudzidzisa zvakarurama, musingatendi zvinoonekwa zvomunhu, asi munodzidzisa nzira yaMwari nezvokwadi." 
Luke20:22 Ko zvino takatenderwa kuterera Kesari mutero here, kana kwete.”" 
Luke20:23 Asi iye achiziva kunyengera kwavo, akati kwavari," 
Luke20:24 “Ndiratidzei dhinari. Rinomufananidzo norunyoro rwaaniko?” Vakati, “ZvaKesari.”" 
Luke20:25 Ipapo akati kwavari, “Naizvozvo ipai Kesari zvaKesari, naMwari zvaMwari.”" 
Luke20:26 Vakakoniwa kumubata pakutaura kwake pamberi pavanhu; vakashamiswa nokupindura kwake, ndokunyarara." 
Luke20:27 Zvino vamwe vaSadhusi, ivo vanoramba kumuka kwavakafa vachiti hakuna, vakauya kwaari, vakamubvunza," 
Luke20:28 vachiti, “Mudzidzisi, Mosesi akatinyorera kuti, ‘Kana mukoma womunhu akafa, ano mukadzi, asi iye asina vana, munun'una wake atore mukadzi wake, amutsire mukoma wake vana.’" 
Luke20:29 Zvino, kwakanga kuna vanakomana vomunhu mumwe vanomwe; wedangwe akatora mukadzi, akafa asina vana;" 
Luke20:30 nowechipiri; 
Luke20:31 nowechitatu akamutorawo; nokudaro navanomwe vose, vakasasiya vana, vakafa." 
Luke20:32 Pashure mukadzi akafawo. 
Luke20:33 Zvino pakumuka achava mukadzi waaniko kwavari? Nokuti akanga ari mukadzi wavose vanomwe.” 
Luke20:34 Jesu akati kwavari, “Vanakomana venyika ino vanowana, uye vanowaniswa;" 
Luke20:35 asi avo vachanzi naMwari vakafanira kuwana nyika iyo nokumuka kwavakafa, havawani, uye havawaniswi." 
Luke20:36 Nokuti havazofizve; nokuti vachaenzana navatumwa; vava vana vaMwari zvavari vana vokumuka. 
Luke20:37 Naiye Mosesiwo akaratidza pashoko reGwenzi kuti vakafa vanomutswazve, paakati, ‘Ishe ndiye Mwari waAbhurahamu, naMwari waIsaka, naMwari waJakobho.’" 
Luke20:38 “Zvino Mwari haazi Mwari wavakafa, asi wavapenyu; nokuti vose vapenyu kwaari.”" 
Luke20:39 Ipapo vamwe vanyori vakamupindura, vakati, “Mudzidzisi, mataura zvakanaka.”" 
Luke20:40 Nokuti vakanga vachitya kuzomubvunza chinhu. 
Luke20:41 Zvino akati kwavari, “Vanoreva seiko kuti Kristu ndiye Mwanakomana waDhavhidhi?" 
Luke20:42 Nokuti Dhavhidhi akareva amene muBhuku yaMapisarema, achiti, ‘Ishe akati kuna Ishe wangu: Gara kurudyi rwangu," 
Luke20:43 Kusvikira ndaisa vavengi vako vave chitsiko chetsoka dzako.’ 
Luke20:44 “Naizvozvo, Dhavhidhi anomuti, ‘Ishe,’ zvino angagova Mwanakomana wake seiko?”" 
Luke20:45 Zvino akati kuvadzidzi vake, vanhu vose vachizvinzwa," 
Luke20:46 “Chenjerai vanyori, vanoda kufamba nenguo refu, vachifarira kukwaziswa padare, nezvigaro zvapamberi mumasinagoge, nougaro hwapamberi pamitambo;" 
Luke20:47 vanoparadza dzimba dzechirikadzi, vachiita mano–mano eminyengetero mirefu; ivavo vachatongerwa zvakaipa zvinopfuurisa.”" 
Luke21:1 Zvino akati achitarira, akaona vapfumi vachiisa zvipo zvavo muchivigiro chemari." 
Luke21:2 Akaona imwe chirikadzi, yaiva murombo, achiisamo tumari tuviri tuduku." 
Luke21:3 Akati, “Zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, chirikadzi iyi, iri murombo, yakaisa kupfuura vamwe vose;" 
Luke21:4 nokuti avo vose vakaisa zvipo, vachitora pazvizhinji zvavainazvo, asi uyu akaisa, achitora pakushayiwa kwake, zvaaifanira kurarama nazvo, zvose zvaakanga anazvo.”" 
Luke21:5 Zvino vamwe vakati vachitaura pamusoro petemberi, kuti yakanga yakashongedzwa namabwe akanaka nezvipo, iye akati," 
Luke21:6 “Kana zviri izvi zvamunoona, mazuva achasvika, asingazoregwi ibwe pamusoro pebwe, risingazowisirwi pasi.”" 
Luke21:7 Zvino vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Mudzidzisi, izvozvi zvichagova rinhiko? Nechiratidzo chichava chipi, kana izvozvi zvoda kuitwa?”" 
Luke21:8 Akati, “Chenjerai, kuti murege kutsauswa; nokuti vazhinji vachauya nezita rangu, vachiti, ‘Ndini Kristu’; ‘Nguva yaswedera.’ Musavatevera." 
Luke21:9 “Kana muchinzwa zvokurwa, nenyonganiso, musavhunduka henyu, nokuti izvozvi zvinofanira kumboitwa; asi kuguma hakusi pakarepo.”" 
Luke21:10 Akati kwavari, “Rudzi rumwe ruchamukira rumwe rudzi, noushe humwe huchamukira humwe ushe." 
Luke21:11 Kudengenyeka kukuru kwenyika kuchavapo, nokune dzimwe nzvimbo nzara nehosha, nezvinotyisa, uye zviratidzo zvikuru, zvichabva kudenga, zvichavapo." 
Luke21:12 Asi izvozvi zvose zvisati zvasvika, vachakubatai, nokukutambudzai, vachikuisai kumasinagoge nomumatorongo, nokukuisai pamberi pamadzimambo namadzishe, nokuda kwezita rangu." 
Luke21:13 Ichi chichava chapupu kwamuri. 
Luke21:14 Naizvozvo simbai mumwoyo menyu, kuti murege kumbofungisisa pamuchapindura napo." 
Luke21:15 Nokuti ndichakupai muromo nokuchenjera, kuchakonesa vavengi venyu vose kukukundai nokuramba zvamunoreva." 
Luke21:16 Muchaiswa kuvatongi kunyangwe navabereki, navanun'una, nehama, neshamwari; vamwe venyu vachaurayiwa." 
Luke21:17 Muchavengwa navanhu vose nokuda kwezita rangu. 
Luke21:18 “Asi ruvhudzi rumwe rwomusoro wenyu harungarasiki. 
Luke21:19 Nokutsungirira kwenyu muchawana upenyu hwenyu. 
Luke21:20 “Zvino kana muchiona Jerusaremu rakombwa nehondo, zivai kuti roda kuparadzwa." 
Luke21:21 Musi uyo vari muJudhiya ngavatizire kumakomo; navari mukati maro ngavabude; navari kuruwa ngavarege kupindamo. 
Luke21:22 Nokuti iwayo ndiwo mazuva okutsiva, kuti zvose zvakanyorwa zviitike." 
Luke21:23 Asi vachava nenhamo vane pamuviri navanoyamwisa namazuva iwayo, nokuti kutambudzika kukuru kuchavapo panyika, nokutsamwa pamusoro pavanhu ivavo." 
Luke21:24 Vachaparadzwa nomunondo, nokutapwa kumarudzi ose; Jerusaremu richatsikwa navahedheni, kusvikira nguva dzavahedheni dzazadzika." 
Luke21:25 “Zviratidzo zvichavapo pazuva napamwedzi, napanyenyedzi; napanyika hurombo hwavanhu, vachikanganiswa nokutinhira kwegungwa namafungu;" 
Luke21:26 vanhu vachapera nokutya nokutarira zvinowira nyika; nokuti masimba okudenga achadengenyeka. 
Luke21:27 Ipapo vachaona Mwanakomana womunhu achiuya negore, nesimba nokubwinya kukuru." 
Luke21:28 Asi kana izvozvi zvichitanga kuitika, tarirai kumusoro, musimudze misoro yenyu, nokuti kusunungurwa kwenyu kwaswedera.”" 
Luke21:29 Zvino akavataurira mufananidzo, achiti, “Tarirai muonde nemiti yose." 
Luke21:30 Kana yotunga, mukazviona, munoziva kuti zvino zhizha rava padyo." 
Luke21:31 “Saizvozvo, nemiwo, kana moona izvozvo zvoitwa, zivai kuti ushe hwaMwari hwava padyo." 
Luke21:32 “Zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, rudzi urwu harungatongopfuuri, kusvikira zvose zvaitika." 
Luke21:33 Denga nenyika zvichapfuura, asi mashoko angu haangatongopfuuri." 
Luke21:34 “Chenjerai, kuti mwoyo yenyu irege kuremedzwa nokudyisa nokuraradza, nokufunganya pamusoro pezvinhu zvoupenyu huno, kuti zuva iro rirege kukuwirai seriva." 
Luke21:35 Nokuti richawira vose vagere panyika yose. 
Luke21:36 Asi rindai nenguva dzose, mukumbire, kuti mugone kupukunyuka pazvinhu izvi zvose zvinozoitwa, mugomira pamberi poMwanakomana womunhu.”" 
Luke21:37 Zvino aidzidzisa masikati mutemberi, asi usiku aibuda, akandovata mugomo rinonzi reMiorivhi." 
Luke21:38 Vanhu vose vakauya kwaari mutemberi mangwanani, kuzomunzwa." 
Luke22:1 Zvino mutambo wezvingwa zvisina mbiriso, unonzi Pasika, wakaswedera." 
Luke22:2 Vapristi vakuru navanyori vakatsvaka kuti vangamuuraya sei; nokuti vakanga vachitya vanhu. 
Luke22:3 Zvino Satani akapinda kuna Judhasi ainzi Isikarioti, mumwe wavane gumi navaviri." 
Luke22:4 Akaenda, akandorangana navapristi vakuru navakuru vetemberi, kuti angamuisa kwavari sei." 
Luke22:5 Vakafara, vakatenderana naye vose kuti vamupe mari." 
Luke22:6 Akatenda, akatsvaka nguva yokumuisa nayo kwavari pasina vanhu vazhinji." 
Luke22:7 Zvino zuva rezvingwa zvisina mbiriso rakati rasvika, rakafanira kubayirwa Pasika naro," 
Luke22:8 akatuma Petirosi naJohani, achiti, “Endai, mundotigadzirira Pasika, kuti tidye.”" 
Luke22:9 Vakati kwaari, “Munoda kuti tigadzirirepiko?”" 
Luke22:10 Akati kwavari, “Tarirai, kana mapinda muguta, muchasangana nomunhu akatakura chirongo chemvura; mumutevere iye kumba kwaanoenda;" 
Luke22:11 muti kumuridzi weimba, ‘Mudzidzisi anoti kwauri, imba yavaeni iripiko, mandingadyira Pasika navadzidzi vangu?"
