Luke22:12 Achakuratidzai imba huru iri kumusoro, yakarongedzwa; gadzirai ipapo.’ ”" 
Luke22:13 Vakaenda, vakandowana sezvaakanga avaudza; vakagadzira Pasika." 
Luke22:14 Zvino nguva yakati yasvika, akagara pakudya navapostori." 
Luke22:15 Akati kwavari, “Ndakanga ndichida zvikuru kudya Pasika iyi nemi ndisati ndatambudzika." 
Luke22:16 Nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, handichazoidyi, kusvikira yaitika muushe hwaMwari.”" 
Luke22:17 Zvino akatora mukombe; akavonga, akati, “Torai ichi, mugovane pakati penyu." 
Luke22:18 Nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, kubva zvino handichatongonwizve michero yomuzambiringa, kusvikira ushe hwaMwari hwasvika.”" 
Luke22:19 Akatora chingwa, akavonga, akamedura, akavapa, achiti, “Ichi muviri wangu, unopirwemi; itai izvi, mugondirangarira.”" 
Luke22:20 Nokudarowo, vapedza kurayira, akatora mukombe, akati, “Mukombe uyu isungano itsva muropa rangu, rinoteurirwemi." 
Luke22:21 “Asi tarirai, ruoko rwaiye, anondipandukira, runeni patafura." 
Luke22:22 “Nokuti Mwanakomana womunhu anoenda hake, sezvazvakatemwa; asi ane nhamo munhu uyo waanopandukirwa naye.”" 
Luke22:23 Ipapo vakatanga kubvunzana kuti ndianiko kwavari angaita chinhu icho. 
Luke22:24 Zvino nharo dzakamuka pakati pavo kuti ndiani kwavari achanzi mukuru. 
Luke22:25 Akati kwavari, “Madzimambo avahedheni ane simba pamusoro pavo, navabati vavo vanonzi, ‘Vabatsiri.’" 
Luke22:26 Zvino imi musadaro, asi mukuru kwamuri ngaave somuduku, nomutungamiri seanoshandira." 
Luke22:27 Nokuti ndianiko mukuru, agere pakudya, kana anoshandira? Haazi iye ugere pakudya here? Asi ini ndiri pakati penyu sounoshumira." 
Luke22:28 “Zvino imi ndimi mavakugara neni pamiedzo yangu. 
Luke22:29 Ndinokugarisai nhaka youshe saBaba vangu vakandigarisa nhaka," 
Luke22:30 kuti mugodya nokunwa patafura rangu muushe hwangu; muchagara pazvigaro zvoushe, muchitonga marudzi ane gumi namaviri aVaIsiraeri.”" 
Luke22:31 “Simoni! Simoni! Tarira Satani akakumbira kuti akuzungurei imi sezviyo; 
Luke22:32 asi ini ndakakukumbirira iwe, kuti kutenda kwako kurege kupera; iwe kana watendeuka, usimbise hama dzako.”" 
Luke22:33 Akati kwaari, “Ishe, ndakazvigadzirira kuenda nemi mutorongo, kunyangwe kurufu.”" 
Luke22:34 Akati, “Petirosi, ndinoti kwauri, nhasi, jongwe risati rarira, uchandiramba katatu uchiti haundizivi.”" 
Luke22:35 Zvino akati kwavari, “Musi wandakakutumai, musina chikwama nehombodo neshangu, makashayiwa chinhu here?” Vakati, “Hakuna.”" 
Luke22:36 Akati kwavari, “Asi zvino, ane chikwama, ngaachitore, nokudarowo ane hombodo; asina munondo, ngaatengese nguo yake, autenge." 
Luke22:37 “Nokuti ndinoti kwamuri, kuti izvi zvakanyorwa zvinofanira kuitika kwandiri, zvinoti, ‘Akaverengwa pamwechete navadariki vomurairo;’ nokuti izvo zvakanyorwa pamusoro pangu zvoitika.”" 
Luke22:38 Ipapo vakati, “Ishe, tarirai, heyi minondo miviri.” Akati kwavari, “Zvaringana.”" 
Luke22:39 Zvino akabuda, akaenda kugomo reMiorivhi, sezvaaisiita; navadzidzi vake vakamutevera." 
Luke22:40 Akati asvika panzvimbo iyo, akati kwavari, “Nyengeterai kuti murege kupinda pakuedzwa.”" 
Luke22:41 Akaparadzana navo, chinhambo chingasvika ibwe, kana rikaposherwa; akapfugama, akanyengetera," 
Luke22:42 achiti, “Baba, kana muchida, bvisai mukombe uyu kwandiri! Asi kuda kwangu kurege kuitwa, asi kwenyu.”" 
Luke22:43 Ipapo mutumwa akaonekwa naye, akabva kudenga, akamusimbisa." 
Luke22:44 Zvino, ari pakutambudzika kukuru, akanyanya kunyengetera; ziya rake rikaita samadonhwe eropa, akadonhera pasi." 
Luke22:45 Akasimuka pakunyengetera, akaenda kuvadzidzi, akavawana vavata neshungu dzomwoyo." 
Luke22:46 Akati kwavari, “Mavatireiko? Mukai, munyengetere, kuti murege kupinda pakuedzwa.”" 
Luke22:47 Akati achataura, tarira, vanhu vazhinji, naiye ainzi Judhasi, mumwe wavane gumi navaviri, akavatungamirira; akaswedera kuna Jesu, kuti amutsvode." 
Luke22:48 Jesu akati kwaari, “Judhasi, unopandukira Mwanakomana womunhu nokumutsvoda here?”" 
Luke22:49 Zvino vaiva naye vakati vachiona zvichaitika, vakati, “Ishe, totema neminondo here?”" 
Luke22:50 Ipapo mumwe wavo akatema muranda woMupristi Mukuru, akamugura nzeve yorudyi." 
Luke22:51 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Regai, zvaringana.” Akabata nzeve yake, akamuporesa." 
Luke22:52 Zvino Jesu akati kuvapristi vakuru navakuru vetemberi, navakuru vakanga vauya kwaari kumubata, “Mabuda neminondo netsvimbo sokugororo here?" 
Luke22:53 Ndaiva nemi mutemberi mazuva ose mukasandibata; asi zvino inguva yenyu nesimba rerima.” 
Luke22:54 Zvino vakamubata, vakaenda naye, vakandomuisa kumba kwomupristi mukuru. Petirosi akatevera ari kure." 
Luke22:55 Vakati vavesa moto pakati poruvazhe, vakagara pasi pamwechete, naPetirosi akagara pakati pavo." 
Luke22:56 Zvino mumwe mushandiri akati achimuona agere muchiedza chomoto, akamutarisisa, akati, “Nouyuwo akanga anaye.”" 
Luke22:57 Asi iye akaramba achiti, “Iwe mukadzi handimuzivi.”" 
Luke22:58 Garegare, mumwezve akamuona, akati, “Iwe uri mumwe wavo.” Petirosi akati, “Iwe munhu, handizati.”" 
Luke22:59 Nguva inenge seimwe yakati yapfuura, mumwezve akasimbisa, achiti, “Zvirokwazvo, uyu akanga anayewo; nokuti muGareriya.”" 
Luke22:60 Petirosi akati, “Iwe munhu, handizivi zvaunoreva!” Pakarepo, achataura, jongwe rikarira." 
Luke22:61 Ipapo Ishe akatendeuka, akatarira Petirosi. Petirosi akarangarira shoko raIshe, raakanga amuudza, achiti, “Jongwe risati rarira nhasi, uchandiramba katatu.”" 
Luke22:62 Akabuda, akachema zvikuru." 
Luke22:63 Varumewo vakanga vabata Jesu, vakamuseka, nokumurova." 
Luke22:64 Vakafukidzira meso ake, vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Porofita kuti ndiani akurova.”" 
Luke22:65 Nezvimwe zvizhinji vakareva kwaari, vachimutuka." 
Luke22:66 Zvino kwakati kwaedza, vakuru vavanhu navapristi vakuru navanyori vakaungana, vakamuisa kumakurukota avo," 
Luke22:67 vachiti, “Kana uri Kristu, utiudze.” Iye akati kwavari, “Kana ndikakuudzai, hamungatendi." 
Luke22:68 Kana ndikakubvunzai, hamungandipinduri." 
Luke22:69 “Asi kubva zvino Mwanakomana womunhu achagara kurudyi rwesimba raMwari.” 
Luke22:70 Ipapo vose vakati, “Uri Mwanakomana waMwari kanhi?” Akati kwavari, “Mareva kuti ndini iye.”" 
Luke22:71 Ivo vakati, “Tichatsvakireiko chapupu? Nokuti tazvinzwira pachedu pamuromo wake.”" 
Luke23:1 Zvino vose vakanga vakaungana, vakasimuka, vakaenda naye kuna Pirato." 
Luke23:2 Vakatanga kumupomera mhosva, vachiti, “Takawana munhu uyu achitsausa rudzi rwedu, achivadzivisa kuti varege kuvigira Kesari kuterera; uye achizviti ndini Kristu Mambo.”" 
Luke23:3 Ipapo Pirato akamubvunza, akati, “Ko uri Mambo wavaJudha here?” Akamupindura, akati, “Ndizvo zvamareva.”" 
Luke23:4 Pirato akati kuvapristi vakuru nokuvazhinji, “Handiwani mhosva kumunhu uyu.”" 
Luke23:5 Ivo vakanyanya, vachiti, “Anomutsa vanhu, achidzidzisa muJudhiya rose, achitanga paGareriya kusvikira pano.”" 
Luke23:6 Pirato wakati achinzwa izvozvo, akabvunza kana munhu uyu ari muGareriya." 
Luke23:7 Akati anzwa kuti anobva kunyika yakatongwa naHerodhi, akamutumira kuna Herodhi, nokuti akanga ari muJerusaremu pamazuva iwayo." 
Luke23:8 Zvino Herodhi akafara kwazvo–kwazvo achiona Jesu; nokuti aida kumuona kare, zvaakanga anzwa zvake; akafunga kuti achaona chimwe chiratidzo chingaitwa naye." 
Luke23:9 Akamubvunza mashoko mazhinji; asi iye haana kumupindura chinhu. 
Luke23:10 Vapristi vakuru navanyori vakamira vakamupomera mhosva zvikuru. 
Luke23:11 NaHerodhi navarwi vake vakamuzvidza, nokumuseka; vakazomupfekedza nguo dzinobwinya, vakamudzosera kuna Pirato." 
Luke23:12 Nomusi uyo Pirato naHerodhi vakayanana; nokuti vaivengana. 
Luke23:13 Zvino Pirato akaunganidza vapristi vakuru namakurukota navanhu," 
Luke23:14 akati kwavari, “Mauya kwandiri nomunhu uyu, muchiti, anotsausa vanhu; tarirai ini ndamubvunzisisa pamberi penyu, ndikasawana kumunhu uyu mhosva yezvinhu zvamunomupomera nazvo;" 
Luke23:15 kunyangwe naHerodhiwo; nokuti wamudzosera kwatiri; tarirai, hakuna chinhu chakaitwa naye, chakafanira rufu." 
Luke23:16 “Naizvozvo ndichamurova, ndigomusunungura. [" 
Luke23:17 Nokuti aifanira kuvasunungurira mumwe pamutambo.]” 
Luke23:18 Asi vose vakadanidzira pamwechete, vachiti, “Bvisai munhu uyu, mutisunungurire Bharabhasi!”" 
Luke23:19 Iye akanga asungwa mutorongo nemhaka yebope rakanga ramutswa muguta, neyokuuraya." 
Luke23:20 Zvino Pirato akataurazve navo, achida kusunungura Jesu." 
Luke23:21 Asi ivo vakaramba vachidanidzira, vachiti, “Roverai pamuchinjikwa, mumurovere pamuchinjikwa!”" 
Luke23:22 Akati kwavari rwechitatu, “Uyu akagotadzeiko? Handina kuwana mhosva yorufu kwaari.”" 
Luke23:23 Asi ivo vakasimbisa namazwi makuru, vachikumbira kuti aroverwe pamuchinjikwa. Mazwi avo akakunda." 
Luke23:24 Zvino Pirato akatonga kuti zvavakakumbira zviitwe; 
Luke23:25 akavasunungurira uyo wavakakumbira, akanga asungwa mutorongo nemhaka yebope neyokuuraya; akavapa Jesu vaite nokuda kwavo." 
Luke23:26 Vakati vachienda naye, vakabata mumwe, ainzi Simoni weKurini, achibva kuruwa, vakamutakudza muchinjikwa, kuti autakure shure kwaJesu." 
Luke23:27 Akateverwa navanhu vazhinji zhinji, navakadzi vaimuririra nokumuchema." 
Luke23:28 Asi Jesu akatendeukira kwavari, akati, “Vakunda veJerusaremu, musandichema ini, asi muzvicheme imi navana venyu;" 
Luke23:29 nokuti tarirai, mazuva anouya, avachati, ‘Vakaropafadzwa vasingaponi, nezvizvaro zvisina kutongobereka, namazamu asina kuyamwisa.’" 
Luke23:30 Musi uyo muchatanga kureva kumakomo, muchiti, ‘Wirai pamusoro pedu,’ nokuzvikomo, ‘Tifukidzei.’" 
Luke23:31 Nokuti kana vachiita izvi kumuti munyoro, wakaoma uchaitirweiko?”" 
Luke23:32 Kwakanga kuna vamwe vatadzi vaviri, vavakaenda navo pamwechete naye kundourayiwa." 
Luke23:33 Zvino vakati vasvika panzvimbo inonzi, “Dehenya,” vakamuroverapo navatadzi, mumwe kurudyi mumwe kuruboshwe." 
Luke23:34 Ipapo Jesu akati, “Baba, muvakanganwire, nokuti havazivi chavanoita.” Vakagovana nguo dzake, vachikanda mijenya pamusoro padzo." 
Luke23:35 Vanhu vakamira, vachitarira; namakurukota vakamusekawo, vachiti, “Wakaponesa vamwe; ngaazviponese, kana ari Kristu waMwari, Mutsanangurwa wake.”" 
Luke23:36 Navarwiwo vakamuseka, vakauya kwaari, vakamupa vhiniga," 
Luke23:37 vachiti, “Kana uri Mambo wavaJudha, uzviponese.”" 
Luke23:38 Zvino kwakanga kune runyoro pamusoro pake rwaiti, “UYU NDIMAMBO WAVAJUDHA.”" 
Luke23:39 Mumwe wavatadzi vakanga vakaturikwa, akamutuka, achiti, “Hauzi Kristu here? Uzviponese, nesuwo.”" 
Luke23:40 Mumwe akapindura, akamurayira, achiti, “Hautyi kunyangwe naMwari kanhi, zvauri pakutongwa kamwe naye?" 
Luke23:41 Kana tirisu, takaitirwa patakafanirwa napo; nokuti isu tinopiwa zvakafanira mabasa edu; asi uyu haana kuita chinhu chisakafanira.”" 
Luke23:42 Ipapo akati, “Jesu mundirangarire, kana masvika muushe hwenyu!”" 
Luke23:43 Iye akati kwaari, “Zvirokwazvo, nhasi uchava neni muParadhiso.”" 
Luke23:44 Zvino yakanga yava nguva inenge yechitanhatu; rima rikavapo panyika yose, kusvikira panguva yepfumbamwe." 
Luke23:45 Zuva rikasviba; keteni retemberi rikabvaruka napakati. 
Luke23:46 Zvino Jesu akadana nezwi guru, achiti, “Baba, ndinoisa mweya wangu pamaoko enyu!” Akati areva izvozvo, akabudisa mweya wake." 
Luke23:47 Ipapo mukuru wezana akati aona zvaitwa, akarumbidza Mwari achiti, “Zvirokwazvo, munhu uyu akanga akarurama.”" 
Luke23:48 Vazhinji vose vakanga vakaungana kuzoona izvozvo, vakati vaona zvaitwa, vakadzoka vachirova zvipfuva zvavo." 
Luke23:49 Navazikanwi vake vose, navakadzi, vaimutevera vachibva Gareriya, vakamira kure, vachiona izvozvo." 
Luke23:50 Zvino kwakanga kuno mumwe munhu, ainzi Josefa, mumwe wamakurukota, murume akanaka akarurama," 
Luke23:51 iye akanga asina kutenderana navo pakurangana, nokuita kwavo, aiva weArimatia, guta ravaJudha, akanga achimirira ushe hwaMwari;" 
Luke23:52 iye akaenda kuna Pirato, akandokumbira chitunha chaJesu," 
Luke23:53 akachiburusa, akachiputira nomucheka, akachiuisa muhwiro hwakanga hwakacherwa pabwe, makanga musina kumbovigwa munhu." 
Luke23:54 Waiva musi woKugadzirira, Sabata roda kutanga." 
Luke23:55 Navakadzi vakanga vauya naye, vachibva Gareriya, vakavatevera, vakaona hwiro, nomuisirwo womutumbi wake." 
Luke23:56 Vakadzoka, vakagadzira zvinonhuwira namafuta. Vakazorora nomusi weSabata vachiterera murairo." 
Luke24:1 Nomusi wokutanga wevhiki, mambakwedza, vakauya kuhwiro, vakabata zvinonhuwira, zvavakanga vagadzira." 
Luke24:2 Vakawana ibwe rakunguruswa, rabviswa pahwiro," 
Luke24:3 vakapinda, vakashayiwa chitunha chashe Jesu." 
Luke24:4 Zvino vakati vachakanganiswa nazvo, tarira, varume vaviri vakamira navo vane nguo dzinopenya;" 
Luke24:5 zvino nokutya kwavo vakakotamira pasi nezviso zvavo, ivo vakati kwavari, “Munotsvakireiko mupenyu pakati pavakafa?" 
Luke24:6 “Haapo pano, amuka. Fungai zvaakakuudzai achiri Gareriya," 
Luke24:7 kuti, ‘Mwanakomana womunhu anofanira kuiswa mumaoko avanhu vakaipa aroverwe pamuchinjikwa, agomuka nezuva retatu.’ ”" 
Luke24:8 Ipapo vakarangarira mashoko ake," 
Luke24:9 vakadzoka vachibva kuhwiro, vakaudza vane gumi nomumwe navamwe vose zvinhu izvozvo zvose." 
Luke24:10 Vaiva Maria Magadharina naJohana naMaria, mai vaJakobho, navamwe vakadzi vaiva navo, vakandoudza vapostori izvozvo." 
Luke24:11 Mashoko awa akaita soupenzi kwavari; vakasaatenda. 
Luke24:12 Zvino Petirosi akasimuka, akamhanyira kuhwiro; akakotama, akaona micheka iri yoga; ndokudzoka kumba, ashamiswa nezvakanga zvaitwa." 
Luke24:13 Pazuva iroro vamwe vaviri vavo vakanga vachienda kumusha wainzi Emausi, wakanga uri kure neJerusaremu masitadhi ana makumi matanhatu;" 
Luke24:14 vakanga vachitaurirana pamusoro pezvinhu zvose zvakanga zvaitika. 
Luke24:15 Zvino vakati vachataurirana nokubvunzana, Jesu amene akaswedera, akafamba navo." 
Luke24:16 Asi meso avo akanga abatwa, vakasamuziva." 
Luke24:17 Akati kwavari, “Mashoko amunotaurirana pamusoro pawo muchifamba, ndeeiko?” Vakamira vane shungu pamwoyo." 
Luke24:18 Mumwe wavo, wainzi Kiropasi, akapindura, akati kwaari, “Ko ndiwe woga ugere muJerusaremu somutorwa, asingazivi zvakaitwamo mazuva ano here?”" 
Luke24:19 Akati kwavari, “Zvinyiko?” Vakati kwaari, “ZvaJesu weNazareta, aiva muporofita ane simba pabasa napashoko pamberi paMwari napavanhu vose;" 
Luke24:20 uye kuti vapristi vakuru navashandi vedu vakamuisa kuvatongi kuti atongerwe rufu, vakamurovera pamuchinjikwa." 
Luke24:21 Takanga tichiti ndiye aizodzikinura VaIsiraeri; uye pamusoro paizvozvo zvose, nhasi rava zuva retatu kubva pakuitwa kwazvo." 
Luke24:22 “Uyezve, vamwe vakadzi vokwedu, vakanga vafumira kuhwiro, vakatishamisa;" 
Luke24:23 nokuti vakati vachishayiwa chitunha chake, vakauya vachiti, vaona chiratidzo chavatumwa vaiti mupenyu." 
Luke24:24 “Zvino vamwe vaiva nesu, vakaenda kuhwiro, vakandozviwana sezvavakareva vakadzi; asi iye havana kumuona.”" 
Luke24:25 Zvino iye akati kwavari, “Imi vokusafunga, mune mwoyo inononoka kutenda zvose zvakarehwa navaporofita!" 
Luke24:26 “Kristu akanga asingafaniri kutambudzika saizvozvo, agopinda mukubwinya kwake here?”" 
Luke24:27 Ipapo akatanga kuna Mosesi navaporofita vose, akavadudzira zvakanyorwa pamusoro pake muMagwaro ose." 
Luke24:28 Zvino vakaswedera kumusha kwavakanga vachienda; iye akaita sooda kupfuura. 
Luke24:29 Vakamugombedzera, vachiti, “Garai nesu, nokuti ava madekwana, zuva ravira.” Ipapo akapinda kundogara navo." 
Luke24:30 Zvino akati agara navo pakudya, akatora chingwa, akachiropafadza, akachimedura, ndokuvapa." 
Luke24:31 Ipapo meso avo akasvinudzwa, vakamuziva; akanyangarika kwavari." 
Luke24:32 Vakataurirana, vachiti, “Ko mwoyo yedu yakanga isingapisi mukati medu, achitaura nesu munzira, nokutizarurira Magwaro here?”" 
Luke24:33 Vakasimuka nenguva iyo, vakadzokera Jerusaremu, vakawana vane gumi nomumwe navaiva navo vakaungana." 
Luke24:34 Ivo vakati, “Ishe amuka zvirokwazvo; aonekwa naSimoni.”" 
Luke24:35 Vakarondedzera zvakaitika munzira, uye kuti akazikanwa navo sei pakumedura chingwa." 
Luke24:36 Vakati vachataura izvozvo, akamira pakati pavo amene, akati kwavari, “Rugare ngaruve nemi!”" 
Luke24:37 Asi vakavhunduka, vakatya kwazvo, vakati zvimwe vaona mweya." 
Luke24:38 Akati kwavari, “Munotambudzika neiko? Mifungo inomukireiko mumwoyo yenyu?" 
Luke24:39 Tarirai zvanza zvangu netsoka dzangu, kuti ndini ndimene. Ndibatei, muone, nokuti mweya hauna nyama namapfupa, sezvamunondiona ndinazvo ini.”" 
Luke24:40 Akati areva izvozvo, akavaratidza zvanza zvake netsoka dzake." 
Luke24:41 Zvino vakati vachigere kutenda nokufara kwavo, vachashamiswa, akati kwavari, “Mune zvokudya pano here?”" 
Luke24:42 Vakamupa nhindi yehove yakagochwa. 
Luke24:43 Akatora, akadya vachizviona." 
Luke24:44 Akati kwavari, “Ndiwo mashoko angu, andakakuudzai ndichiri nemi, kuti zvose zvakanyorwa pamusoro pangu pamurairo waMosesi, napavaporofita, napaMapisarema, zvinofanira kuitika.”" 
Luke24:45 Ipapo akadziura kuziva kwavo, kuti vanzwisise Magwaro." 
Luke24:46 Akati kwavari, “Ndizvo zvakanyorwa, kuti Kristu achatambudzika, agomuka kuvakafa nezuva retatu;" 
Luke24:47 kuti marudzi ose aparidzirwe nezita rake kutendeuka nokukanganwirwa zvivi, vachitanga muJerusaremu." 
Luke24:48 Imi muri zvapupu zvezvinhu izvi. 
Luke24:49 Tarirai, ndinotuma pamusoro penyu chipikirwa chaBaba vangu; asi imi garai muguta, kusvikira mapiwa simba rinobva kumusoro.”" 
Luke24:50 Zvino akavatungamirira kunze kweguta kusvikira pakatarisana neBhetania, ndokutambanudza maoko ake, akavaropafadza." 
Luke24:51 Akati achavaropafadza, akaparadzana navo, akakwidzwa kudenga." 
Luke24:52 Ipapo vakamunamata, vakadzokera Jerusaremu vanomufaro mukuru." 
Luke24:53 Vakarambira mutemberi, vachirumbidza Mwari." 
John1:1 Pakutanga Shoko rakanga riripo, Shoko rakanga riri kuna Mwari, Shoko rakanga riri Mwari." 
John1:2 Irori pakutanga rakanga riri kuna Mwari. 
John1:3 Zvinhu zvose zvakaitwa naye; kunze kwake hakuna kuitwa kunyangwe chinhu chimwe chakaitwa. 
John1:4 Upenyu hwaiva maari; upenyu hwaiva chiedza chavanhu. 
John1:5 Chiedza chinovhenekera murima; asi rima harina kugona kuchikunda. 
John1:6 Kwakanga kune munhu akatumwa naMwari, zita rake rainzi Johani." 
John1:7 Iye akauya kuzopupura, kuti apupurire chiedza, kuti vose vatende naye." 
John1:8 Uyu akanga asati ari icho chiedza, asi akatumwa kuti apupurire chiedza." 
John1:9 Ichi chaiva chiedza chechokwadi, chinovhenekera munhu mumwe nomumwe, pakusvika kwake panyika." 
John1:10 Akanga ari panyika, asi nyika haina kumuziva." 
John1:11 Akauya kune zvake, asi vanhu vake havana kumugamuchira." 
John1:12 Asi vose vakamugamuchira, akavapa simba kuti vave vana vaMwari, ivavo vanotenda kuzita rake;" 
John1:13 avo vasina kuberekwa neropa, kana nokuda kwenyama, kana nokuda kwomurume, asi naMwari." 
John1:14 Izwi rakazova munhu, rikagara pakati pedu, tikaona kubwinya kwake, kubwinya sokwowakaberekwa mumwechete waBaba, azere nenyasha nechokwadi." 
John1:15 Johani akamupupurira, akadanidzira, achiti, “Ndiye wandaireva, ndichiti, ‘Uyo, anouya shure kwangu, akavapo mberi kwangu; nokuti akanditangira.’ ”" 
John1:16 Nokuti pakuzara kwake isu tose takapiwa nyasha pamusoro penyasha. 
John1:17 Nokuti murairo wakapiwa naMosesi, nyasha nechokwadi zvakauya naJesu Kristu." 
John1:18 Hakuna munhu akatongoona Mwari; mwanakomana akabereka ari mumwe oga, ari pachifuva chaBaba, ndiye akamuzivisa isu." 
John1:19 Uku ndiko kupupura kwaJohani, musi vaJudha vakatumira kwaari vapristi navaRevhi, vachibva Jerusaremu, kundomubvunza, kuti, “Iwe ndiwe aniko?”" 
John1:20 Akatenda pachena, haana kuramba, akatenda pachena, achiti, “Handisi Kristu.”" 
John1:21 Vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Asi kudiniko? Ndiwe Eriya here?” Akati, “Handisi iye.” “Ko uri uya muporofita here?” Akapindura, akati, “Kwete.”" 
John1:22 Zvino vakati kwaari, “Ndiwe aniko? Tigondopindura vakatituma. Unozviti aniko?”" 
John1:23 Akati, “Ndini izwi roanodana murenje, richiti, ‘Ruramisai nzira yaIshe; sezvakarehwa nomuporofita Isaya.’ ”" 
John1:24 Ava vakanga vatumwa vaiva vaVaFarisi. 
John1:25 Vakamubvunza, vakati kwaari, “Kana usiri Kristu, kana Eriya, kana muporofita uya, unogobhabhatidzireiko?”" 
John1:26 Johani akapindura, akati, “Ini ndinobhabhatidza nemvura; asi pakati penyu pamire mumwe wamusingazivi;" 
John1:27 ndiye anouya shure kwangu, wandisina kufanira kuti ndisunungure rukanda rweshangu yake.”" 
John1:28 Izvozvi zvakaitwa paBhetania, mhiri kwaJodhani, kwaibhabhatidza Johani." 
John1:29 Ava mangwana akaona Jesu achiuya kwaari, akati, “Tarirai, Hwayana yaMwari, inobvisa zvivi zvenyika." 
John1:30 Ndiye wandaireva, ndichiti, ‘Shure kwangu kunouya mumwe, akavapo mberi kwangu, nokuti akanditangira.’" 
John1:31 Neni ndakanga ndisingamuzivi; asi ndizvo zvandakauyira, ndichibhabhatidza nemvura, kuti aoneswe kuVaIsiraeri.”" 
John1:32 Johani akapupura, akati, “Ndakaona Mweya achiburuka kudenga senjiva akagara pamusoro pake." 
John1:33 Neni ndakanga ndisingamuzivi; asi akandituma kubhabhatidza nemvura, ndiye akati kwandiri, ‘Uyo waunoona Mweya achiburuka pamusoro pake, akagara pamusoro pake, ndiye anobhabhatidza noMweya Mutsvene.’" 
John1:34 “Ini ndikaona, ndikapupura kuti uyu ndiye Mwanakomana waMwari.”" 
John1:35 Ava mangwanazve Johani akanga amire navadzidzi vake vaviri; 
John1:36 akatarisisa Jesu achifamba, akati, “Tarirai, Hwayana yaMwari!”" 
John1:37 Ivavo vadzidzi vaviri, vakamunzwa achitaura, vakatevera Jesu." 
John1:38 Jesu akatendeuka akavaona vachitevera, akati kwavari, “Munotsvakeiko?” Vakati kwaari, “Rabhi” (ndokuti, “Mudzidzisi, kana zvichishandurwa,”) munogarepiko?" 
John1:39 Akati kwavari, “Uyai, muone.” Vakaenda, vakandoona kwaaigara, vakagara naye zuva iro; yakanga iri nguva inenge yegumi." 
John1:40 Mumwe waivavo vaviri, vakanga vanzwa Johani, vakamutevera, waiva Andireya, munun'una waSimoni Petirosi." 
John1:41 Iye akatanga kuwana Simoni, mukoma wake, akati kwaari, “Tawana Mesiya” (ndokuti, “Kristu, kana zvichishandurwa.”)" 
John1:42 Akamuisa kuna Jesu. Jesu akamutarira, akati, “Ndiwe Simoni, mwanakomana waJona, uchanzi Kefasi zvinoshandurwa, dombo.”" 
John1:43 Ava mangwana akada kuenda Gareriya, akawana Firipi; Jesu akati kwaari, “Nditevere.”" 
John1:44 Firipi akanga ari weBhetisaidha, guta raAndireya naPetirosi." 
John1:45 Firipi akawana Nataneri, akati kwaari, “Tamuwana iye, akanyorwa zvake naMosesi mumurairo navaporofita, iye Jesu weNazareta, mwanakomana waJosefa.”" 
John1:46 Nataneri akati kwaari, “Kune chinhu chakanaka chingabva Nazareta here?” Firipi akati kwaari, “Uya, uone.”" 
John1:47 Jesu akaona Nataneri achiuya kwaari, akamuti, “Tarirai, muIsiraeri wechokwadi, asina kunyengera maari.”" 
John1:48 Nataneri akati kwaari, “Mandizivirepiko?” Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Firipi asati akudana, uri munyasi momuonde, ndakakuona.”" 
John1:49 Nataneri akamupindura, akati, “Rabhi, ndimi Mwanakomana waMwari, ndimi Ishe waIsiraeri.”" 
John1:50 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Unotenda iwe, nokuti ndakati kwauri, ndakakuona munyasi momuonde here? Uchazoona zvikuru kuna izvozvi.”" 
John1:51 Akati kwaari, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwauri, uchaona kudenga kwazarurwa, navatumwa vaMwari vachikwira, nokuburukira pamusoro poMwanakomana womunhu.”" 
John2:1 Nezuva retatu muchato waivapo paKana yeGareriya; namai vaJesu vakanga varipo. 
John2:2 NaJesu navadzidzi vake vakanga vadanwawo kumuchato. 
John2:3 Waini yakati ichizoshayikwa, mai vaJesu vakati kwaari, “Havachine waini.”" 
John2:4 Jesu akati kwavari, “Ndineiko nemi, mai? Nguva yangu ichigere kusvika.”" 
John2:5 Mai vake vakati kuvaranda, “Itai zvose zvaanokuudzai.”" 
John2:6 Zvino kwakanga kuna makate matanhatu amabwe, akanga aiswapo netsika yavaJudha yokuzvinatsa, rimwe nerimwe raizadzwa nezviero zviviri kana zvitatu." 
John2:7 Jesu akati kwavari, “Zadzai makate nemvura.” Ivo vakaazadza kusvikira pamiromo." 
John2:8 Akati kwavari, “Cherai zvino muise kumukuru womuchato.” Vakandoisa." 
John2:9 Zvino mukuru womuchato wakati aravira mvura yakasanduka waini, asingazivi payabva, (asi varanda, vakanga vachera mvura, vaiziva), mukuru womuchato akadana muwani," 
John2:10 akati kwaari, “Munhu mumwe nomumwe anositanga abudisa waini yakanaka, neisinganaki kana vanwa kwazvo; asi iwe wachengeta waini yakanaka kusvikira zvino.”" 
John2:11 Ichi chiratidzo chake chokutanga Jesu akaita paKana yeGareriya, akaratidza kubwinya kwake; vadzidzi vake vakatenda kwaari." 
John2:12 Shure kwaizvozvo akaburukira Kapenaume, iye namai vake navanun'una, navadzidzi vake; akagarapo mazuva mashomanane." 
John2:13 Pasika yavaJudha yakanga yava pedyo; zvino Jesu akakwira Jerusaremu. 
John2:14 Akawana mutemberi vaitengesa mombe namakwai nenjiva, navaitsinhanha mari, vageremo." 
John2:15 Akaruka tyava yetambo, akabudisa mutemberi makwai nemombe zvose; akaparadza mari yavaitsinhanha, nokuwisa matafura avo." 
John2:16 Akati kuna vaitengesa njiva, “Bvisai zvinhu izvozvo muno; musaita imba yaBaba vangu imba yokutengesera.”" 
John2:17 Vadzidzi vake vakarangarira kuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, “Kushingairira imba yenyu kuchandipedza.”" 
John2:18 Zvino vaJudha vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Ungatiratidza chiratidzo cheiko, zvaunoita zvinhu izvozvo?”" 
John2:19 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Putsai temberi iyi, ini ndichaimutsazve namazuva matatu.”" 
John2:20 Zvino vaJudha vakati, “Temberi iyi yakavakwa namakore ana makumi mana namatanhatu, zvino iwe ungaimutsa namazuva matatu here?”" 
John2:21 Asi iye akanga achireva temberi yomuviri wake. 
John2:22 Zvino akati amutswa kuvakafa, vadzidzi vake vakayeuka, kuti akanga areva izvozvo; vakatenda Rugwaro neshoko rakanga rarehwa naJesu." 
John2:23 Zvino nguva yaakanga ari Jerusaremu pamutambo wePasika, vazhinji vakatenda kuzita rake, vachiona zviratidzo zvaaiita." 
John2:24 Asi Jesu haana kutendeseka navo, nokuti akanga achivaziva vose." 
John2:25 Akanga asingatsvaki kuti munhu mumwe apupure zvomunhu; nokuti akanga achiziva iye zviri mumunhu. 
John3:1 Kwaivapo mumwe wavaFarisi, ainzi Nikodhimo, mukuru wavaJudha." 
John3:2 Iye akauya kwaari usiku, akati kwaari, “Rabhi, tinoziva kuti muri Mudzidzisi akabva kuna Mwari; nokuti hakuna munhu anogona kuita zviratidzo izvozvo zvamunoita, kana Mwari asiri naye.”" 
John3:3 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwauri, kana munhu asingaberekwi kutsva, haangaoni ushe hwaMwari.”" 
John3:4 Nikodhimo akati kwaari, “Munhu angagoberekwa seiko ava mukuru? Angapindazve mudumbu ramai vake rwechipiri, akaberekwa here?”" 
John3:5 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwauri, kana munhu asingaberekwi nemvura noMweya, haangagoni kupinda muushe hwaMwari." 
John3:6 Chakaberekwa nenyama inyama, chakaberekwa noMweya, mweya." 
John3:7 Usashamiswa, nokuti ndakati kwauri, munofanira kuberekwa kutsva." 
John3:8 Mhepo inovhuvhuta painoda napo, unonzwa izwi rayo, asi hauzivi painobva napainoenda; mumwe nomumwe akaberekwa naMweya akadaro.”" 
John3:9 Nikodhimo akapindura, akati kwaari, “Zvinhu izvi zvingagoitwa seiko?”" 
John3:10 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Iwe uri mudzidzisi waVaIsiraeri, haunzwisisi zvinhu izvozvi here?" 
John3:11 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwauri, tinotaura zvatinoziva, tinopupura zvatakaona; asi imi hamugamuchiri kupupura kwedu." 
John3:12 “Kana ndakakuudzai zvinhu zvenyika, mukasatenda, mungagotenda seiko, kana ndichikuudzai zvinhu zvokudenga?" 
John3:13 “Hakuna munhu akakwira kudenga, asi iye akaburuka kudenga, iye Mwanakomana womunhu.”" 
John3:14 Mosesi sezvaakasimudza nyoka murenje, saizvozvo Mwanakomana womunhu anofanira kusimudzwawo," 
John3:15 kuti ani naani anotenda kwaari, ave noupenyu husingaperi." 
John3:16 Nokuti Mwari akada nyika nokudaro, kuti akapa Mwanakomana wake akaberekwa mumwe woga, kuti ani naani anotenda kwaari, arege kufa, asi ave noupenyu husingaperi." 
John3:17 Nokuti Mwari haana kutumira Mwanakomana wake panyika, kuti atonge nyika, asi kuti nyika iponeswe naye." 
John3:18 Anotenda kwaari, haatongwi; asi asingatendi kwaari, atotongwa, nokuti haana kutenda kuzita roMwanakomana waMwari akaberekwa mumwe woga." 
John3:19 Kutongwa ndokuku, kuti chiedza chakasvika panyika, asi vanhu vakada rima kupfuura chiedza, nokuti mabasa avo akanga akaipa." 
John3:20 Nokuti mumwe nomumwe, anoita zvakaipa, anovenga chiedza, haauyi pachiedza, kuti mabasa ake arege kubudiswa pachena." 
John3:21 Asi anoita chokwadi, anouya kuchiedza, kuti mabasa ake aonekwe, kuti akaitwa muna Mwari." 
John3:22 Shure kwaizvozvo Jesu akasvika munyika yeJudhiya, navadzidzi vake, akagarako navo achibhabhatidza." 
John3:23 NaJohani akanga achibhabhatidzawo paAinoni, pedyo neSarimu, nokuti kwaiva nemvura zhinji ipapo; vakauya, vakabhabhatidzwa." 
John3:24 Nokuti Johani akanga achigere kuiswa mutorongo. 
John3:25 Zvino nharo dzikamuka pamusoro pokuzvinatsa pakati pavadzidzi vaJohani nomumwe muJudha. 
John3:26 Vakauya kuna Johani, vakati kwaari, “Rabhi, uya aiva nemi mhiri kwaJodhani, wamaimbopupurira, tarirai, iye anobhabhatidza, uye vose vanouya kwaari.”" 
John3:27 Johani akapindura, akati, “Munhu haangagamuchiri chinhu, kana asina kuchipiwa chichibva kudenga." 
John3:28 Imi mumene mungandipupurira, kuti ndakati, ‘Handisi Kristu ini, asi kuti ndakatumwa pamberi pake.’" 
John3:29 Ano mwenga ndiye muwani; asi shamwari yemuwani inomira ichimunzwa, inofara zvikuru nezwi romuwani. Naizvozvo kufara kwangu uku kwazadzika." 
John3:30 Iye anofanira kukura, asi ini ndinofanira kudukupiswa.”" 
John3:31 Anobva kumusoro ndiye uri pamusoro pavose; noanobva panyika ndowenyika, anotaura zvenyika; anobva kudenga ndiye ari pamusoro pavose." 
John3:32 Zvaakaona nezvaakanzwa, ndizvo zvaanopupura; asi hakuna munhu anogamuchira kupupura kwake." 
John3:33 Uyo akagamuchira kupupura kwake, akasimbisa kuti Mwari ndowechokwadi." 
John3:34 Nokuti akatumwa naMwari, ndiye anotaura mashoko aMwari; nokuti haapi Mweya asina mwero." 
John3:35 Baba vanoda Mwanakomana, vakamupa zvose muruoko rwake." 
John3:36 Anotenda Mwanakomana, ano upenyu husingaperi; asi asingatereri Mwanakomana, haangaoni upenyu, asi kutsamwa kwaMwari kunogara pamusoro pake." 
John4:1 Zvino Ishe akati aziva kuti VaFarisi vakanga vanzwa kuti Jesu akaita nokubhabhatidza vadzidzi kupfuura Johani," 
John4:2 kunyangwe Jesu akanga asingabhabhatidzi amene, asi vadzidzi vake," 
John4:3 akabva Judhiya, akaendazve Gareriya." 
John4:4 Akanga achifanira kupfuura neSamaria. 
John4:5 Zvino akasvika paguta reSamaria, rainzi Sikari, pedyo nemunda wakanga wapa Jakobho mwanakomana wake Josefa." 
John4:6 Tsime raJakobho rakanga riripo. Zvino Jesu aneta nokufamba, ndokungogara zvake patsime. Yaiva nguva inenge yechitanhatu." 
John4:7 Zvino mumwe mukadzi weSamaria akasvikapo kuzochera mvura. Jesu akati kwaari, “Ndipeiwo, ndinwe.”" 
John4:8 Nokuti vadzidzi vake vakanga vaenda muguta kundotenga zvokudya. 
John4:9 Ipapo mukadzi muSamaria akati kwaari, “Ko iwe muJudha, unokumbira seiko kwandiri kunwa, ini mukadzi muSamaria?” (Nokuti vaJudha havafambidzani navaSamaria)." 
John4:10 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Dai waiziva chipo chaMwari, uye kuti ndiani anoti kwauri, ndipeiwo ndinwe, ungadai waikumbira kwaari, akakupa mvura mhenyu.”" 
John4:11 Mukadzi akati kwaari, “Ishe, hamuna chamungachera nacho, tsime rakadzika, zvino mvura mhenyu mungaiwanepiko?" 
John4:12 Ko muri mukuru kuna Baba vedu Jakobho, vakatipa tsime iri, vakanwa pariri vamene navanakomana vavo nezvipfuwo zvavo?”" 
John4:13 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Mumwe nomumwe, anonwa mvura iyi, achava nenyotazve." 
John4:14 Asi ani naani, anonwa mvura yandichamupa ini, haachazovi nenyota nokusingaperi; asi mvura, yandichamupa, ichava mukati make tsime remvura, inovhaira kuupenyu husingaperi.”" 
John4:15 Mukadzi akati kwaari, “Ishe, ndipei mvura iyi, kuti ndirege kuzova nenyota, kana kuuya kuchera pano.”" 
John4:16 Jesu akati kwaari, “Enda, undodana murume wako, ugouya pano.”" 
John4:17 Mukadzi akapindura, akati kwaari, “Handina murume.” Jesu akati kwaari, “Wareva zvakanaka, zvawati, ‘Handina murume.’" 
John4:18 “Nokuti watova navarume vashanu; uyo waunaye zvino, haasi murume wako; apo wareva chokwadi.”" 
John4:19 Mukadzi akati kwaari, “Ishe, ndinoona kuti muri muporofita." 
John4:20 Madzibaba edu ainamata pagomo iri; imi munoti muJerusaremu ndimo munofanira kunamatwa.” 
John4:21 Jesu akati kwaari, “Mai, nditende kuti nguva inouya, yamusingazonamati Baba pagomo iri, kana muJerusaremu." 
John4:22 Imi munonamata chamusingazivi; isu tinonamata chatinoziva, nokuti ruponeso runobva kuvaJudha." 
John4:23 Asi nguva inouya, nazvino yatovapo, yokuti vanonamata nechokwadi vachanamata Baba mumweya nechokwadi; nokuti Baba vanotsvaka vakadaro kuzomunamata." 
John4:24 “Mwari ndiMweya; vanomunamata, vanofanira kumunamata mumweya nechokwadi.”" 
John4:25 Zvino mukadzi akati kwaari, “Ndinoziva kuti Mesiasi anouya, anonzi Kristu; kana iye asvika, uchatiudza zvose.”" 
John4:26 Jesu akati kwaari, “Ini, ndinotaura newe, ndini iye.”" 
John4:27 Zvino vadzidzi vake vakasvika, vakashamiswa vachiona kuti anotaurirana nomukadzi; kunyangwe zvakadaro hakuna mumwe akati, “Munotsvakeiko kwaari?” Kana, “Munotaurireiko naye?”" 
John4:28 Ipapo mukadzi akasiya chirongo chake, akaenda muguta, akati kuvanhu," 
John4:29 “Uyai muone munhu, akandiudza zvose zvandakaita. Ko uyu handiti ndiye Kristu here?”" 
John4:30 Vakabuda muguta, vakaenda kwaari." 
John4:31 Nenguva iyo vadzidzi vake vakafanomunyengetera, vachiti, “Rabhi, chidyai.”" 
John4:32 Iye akati kwavari, “Ini ndine zvokudya, zvandinodya, zvamusingazivi.”" 
John4:33 Zvino vadzidzi vakataurirana, vachiti, “Kasi mumwe amuvigira zvokudya kanhi?”" 
John4:34 Jesu akati kwavari, “Zvokudya zvangu ndizvo, kuti ndiite kuda kwoakandituma, nokupedza basa rake." 
John4:35 Ko imi hamuti, ‘Kwasara mwedzi mina, kukohwa kwasvika?’ Tarirai, ini ndinoti kwamuri, simudzai meso enyu, onai minda, kuti yatochena kuti ikohwiwe." 
John4:36 Anocheka anopiwa mubairo, anounganidza mbesanwa muupenyu husingaperi; kuti anokusha naanocheka vafare vose." 
John4:37 Nokuti tsumo ndeyechokwadi, inoti, ‘Mumwe anokusha, mumwe achikohwa.’" 
John4:38 Ndakakutumai kundokohwa zvamusina kubindukira; vamwe vakabindukira, zvino imi mapinda pane zvavakabindukira ivo.”" 
John4:39 Zvino vaSamaria vazhinji veguta iro vakatenda kwaari neshoko romukadzi, akapupura, achiti, “Andiudza zvose zvandakaita.”" 
John4:40 Zvino vaSamaria vakati vachisvika kwaari, vakamunyengetera kuti agare navo; akagarapo mazuva maviri." 
John4:41 Navamwe vazhinji vakatenda neshoko rake. 
John4:42 Vakati kumukadzi, “Hatichatendi nokureva kwako; tazvinzwira timene, tinoziva kuti uye ndiye Muponesi wapasi pose.”" 
John4:43 Mazuva maviri akati apfuura, akabvapo; akaenda Gareriya." 
John4:44 Nokuti Jesu amene akapupura, kuti muporofita haakudzwi munyika yake." 
John4:45 Zvino akati achisvika Gareriya, vaGareriya vakamugamuchira, nokuti vakanga vaona zvose zvaakaita Jerusaremu pamutambo wePasika, nokuti naivo vakanga vaendawo kumutambo wePasika." 
John4:46 Zvino Jesu akasvikazve paKana yeGareriya, paakanga ashandura mvura ikaita waini. Ipapo pakanga panorimwe gurukota raishe, mwanakomana wake akanga achirwara paKapenaume." 
John4:47 Iye akati achinzwa kuti Jesu abva Judhiya, asvika Gareriya, akaenda kwaari, akamunyengetera kuti aburuke kundoporesa mwanakomana wake; nokuti akanga achitandadza." 
John4:48 Zvino Jesu akati kwaari, “Kana musingaoni zviratidzo nezvishamiso, hamungatongotendi.”" 
John4:49 Gurukota raishe rakati kwaari, “Ishe, burukai henyu, mwana wangu asati afa.”" 
John4:50 Jesu akati kwaari, “Enda hako, mwanakomana wako mupenyu.” Munhu uyu akatenda shoko rakarehwa naJesu kwaari, akaenda." 
John4:51 Akati achaburuka, varanda vake vakasangana naye, vakati, “Mwana wenyu mupenyu.”" 
John4:52 Zvino akavabvunza nguva yaakatanga kunaya nayo. Vakati kwaari, “Zuro nenguva yechinomwe fivha yakabva kwaari.”" 
John4:53 Zvino Baba vakaziva kuti ndiyo nguva Jesu yaakati kwaari, “Mwanakomana wako mupenyu.” Iye akatenda nemhuri yake yose." 
John4:54 Ichi ndicho chiratidzo chechipiri chakaitwa naJesu, abva Judhiya, asvika Gareriya." 
John5:1 Shure kwaizvozvo, mutambo wavaJudha waivapo; Jesu akakwira Jerusaremu." 
John5:2 Zvino kuJerusaremu pedyo nesuwo ramakwai kwaiva nedziva rainzi Bhetisaidha neChiHebheru, raiva namabiravira mashanu." 
John5:3 Mukati mawo makanga muvete vazhinji vairwara namapofu, nezvirema, navakaonyana, [vaigarira kubvongodzwa kwemvura." 
John5:4 Nokuti mutumwa waiburukira mudziva iro neimwe nguva, achibvongodza mvura; zvino uyo aitanga kupinda mumvura yabvongodzwa aiporeswa, kunyangwe akanga akabatwa nokurwara kupi nokupi.]" 
John5:5 Zvino kwaivapo mumwe munhu, akanga abatwa nokurwara kwake makore makumi matatu namasere." 
John5:6 Jesu akati aona munhu uyo avete pasi, zvaaiziva kuti akanga akadaro nguva refu, akati kwaari, “Unoda kuporeswa here?”" 
John5:7 Murwere akamupindura, akati, “Ishe, ndinoshayiwa munhu anondiwisira mudziva, kana mvura ichibvongodzwa; asi ndinoti kana ndoenda, mumwe onditangira kupinda.”" 
John5:8 Jesu akati kwaari, “Simuka, tora nhoo dzako, ufambe.”" 
John5:9 Pakarepo munhu uyo akaporeswa, akatora nhoo dzake, akafamba. Musi uyo waiva weSabata." 
John5:10 Zvino vaJudha vakati kune akaporeswa. “ISabata, hautenderwi kutakura nhoo dzako.”" 
John5:11 Iye akapindura, akati, “Uyo andiporesa ndiye akati kwandiri, tora nhoo dzako, ufambe.”" 
John5:12 Vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Ndianiko munhu uyo akati kwauri, tora nhoo dzako, ufambe?”" 
John5:13 Zvino akanga aporeswa, haana kuziva kuti ndiani; nokuti Jesu akanga abva, zvakwaiva navanhu vazhinji panzvimbo iyo." 
John5:14 Shure kwaizvozvo Jesu akamuwana mutemberi, akati kwaari, “Tarira, waporeswa; usatadzazve, kuti urege kubatwa nechinhu chakaipa chinokunda ichi.”" 
John5:15 Zvino munhu uyo akandoudza vaJudha, kuti ndiJesu akamuporesa." 
John5:16 Saka vaJudha vakatambudza Jesu, nokuti wakazviita izvozvo neSabata." 
John5:17 Asi iye akapindura, akati, “Baba vangu vachabata kusvikira zvino, neni ndinobatawo.”" 
John5:18 Saka zvino vaJudha vakatsvaka zvikuru kumuuraya, nokuti akanga asingatyori murairo weSabata bedzi, asi akatiwo Mwari ndiBaba vake, achizvienzanisa naMwari." 
John5:19 Zvino Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, mwanakomana haagoni kuita chinhu oga, kana asingaoni Baba vachichiita; nokuti zvose zvavanoita ivo, Mwanakomana unozviita saizvozvowo." 
John5:20 “Nokuti Baba vanoda Mwanakomana, vanomuratidza zvose zvavanoita vamene; vachamuratidza mabasa makuru kuna iwawa, kuti mushamiswe." 
John5:21 Nokuti Baba sezvavanomutsa vakafa, vachivararamisa, saizvozvo Mwanakomana anoraramisawo vaanoda kuraramisa." 
John5:22 Nokuti naBaba havatongi munhu, asi vakapa Mwanakomana kutonga kwose," 
John5:23 kuti vose vakudze Mwanakomana sezvavanokudza Baba. Asingakudzi Mwanakomana, haakudzi naBaba, vakamutuma." 
John5:24 “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, anonzwa shoko rangu, nokutenda akandituma, ano upenyu husingaperi; haauyi mukutongwa, asi abva murufu, aenda muupenyu." 
John5:25 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, nguva inouya, nazvino yatovapo, nayo vakafa vachanzwa izwi roMwanakomana waMwari; vanonzwa vachararama." 
John5:26 Nokuti Baba sezvavano upenyu mavari, saizvozvowo vakapa Mwanakomana, kuti ave noupenyu maari." 
John5:27 Vakamupa simba rokutonga, zvaari Mwanakomana womunhu." 
John5:28 “Musashamiswa naizvozvo; nokuti nguva inouya, nayo vose vari mumahwiro vachanzwa izwi rake," 
John5:29 vachabuda; avo vakaita zvakanaka, kukumuka kwoupenyu, avo vakaita zvakaipa, kukumuka kwokutongwa." 
John5:30 “Handigoni kuita chinhu ndoga; ndinotonga sezvandinonzwa; kutonga kwangu kwakarurama, nokuti handitsvaki kuda kwangu, asi kuda kwoakandituma." 
John5:31 Kana ndichizvipupurira, kupupura kwangu hakusi kwechokwadi." 
John5:32 “Mumwe aripo anondipupurira; ndinoziva kuti kupupura kwake kwaanondipupurira ndokwechokwadi. 
John5:33 Makatuma kuna Johani, iye akapupurira chokwadi." 
John5:34 Ini handigamuchiri kupupura kunobva kumunhu, asi ndinoreva izvozvo kuti muponeswe." 
John5:35 Iye akanga ari mwenje unopfuta nounovheneka; imi makanga muchida kufara nguva duku muchiedza chake. 
John5:36 Ini ndine chapupu chikuru kuna Johani; nokuti mabasa andakapiwa naBaba kuti ndiapedze, iwo mabasa andinoita, ndiwo anondipupurira kuti Baba vakandituma." 
John5:37 Naivo Baba, vakandituma, ndivo vakandipupurirawo. Hamuna kutongonzwa izwi ravo, kana kuona mufananidzo wavo." 
John5:38 Shoko ravo harigari mukati menyu, nokuti hamutendi avakatuma." 
John5:39 Munonzvera Magwaro, nokuti munoti upenyu husingaperi munahwo maari; ndiwo anondipupurira ini." 
John5:40 “Asi hamudi kuuya kwandiri, kuti muve noupenyu." 
John5:41 “Handigamuchiri kukudzwa kunobva kuvanhu; 
John5:42 asi ndinokuzivai, kuti hamuna rudo rwaMwari mukati menyu." 
John5:43 Ndakauya nezita raBaba vangu, asi hamundigamuchiri; kana mumwe akasvika nezita rake amene, muchamugamuchira iye." 
John5:44 Mungatenda seiko imi, iyemi munogamuchira kukudzwa mumwe kune mumwe, asi kukudzwa kunobva kuna Mwari, ari oga, hamukutsvaki?" 
John5:45 Musati ndichakupomerai mhosva kuna Baba; mumwe ariko anokupomerai mhosva, ndiye Mosesi, wamakavimba naye." 
John5:46 Nokuti dai maitenda Mosesi, mungadai mainditenda ini, nokuti iye akanyora zvangu." 
John5:47 Asi kana musingatendi manyoro ake, mungatenda seiko mashoko angu?”" 
John6:1 Shure kwaizvozvo Jesu akaenda mhiri kweGungwa reGareriya, ndiro reTibheriasi." 
John6:2 Vanhu vazhinji zhinji vakamutevera, nokuti vakaona zviratidzo zvaaiita kuvarwere." 
John6:3 Jesu akakwira mugomo, akagaramo navadzidzi vake." 
John6:4 Pasika, mutambo wavaJudha, wakanga uri pedyo." 
John6:5 Zvino Jesu akati achitarira, akaona vanhu vazhinji zhinji vachiuya kwaari, akati kuna Firipi, “Tingatengepiko zvingwa, kuti vanhu ava vadye?”" 
John6:6 Akareva izvozvo kuti amuedze, nokuti iye akaziva amene zvaakanga achida kuita." 
John6:7 Firipi akamupindura, achiti, “Zvingwa zvamadhinari ana mazana maviri hazvingavaringani, kuti mumwe nomumwe atore zvishoma.”" 
John6:8 Zvino mumwe wavadzidzi vake, Andireya, munun'una waSimoni Petirosi, akati kwaari," 
John6:9 “Pano pano mukomana, ane zvingwa zvishanu zvebhari nehove mbiri; asi izvi zvingakwanira sei vanhu vazhinji?”" 
John6:10 Jesu akati, “Garisai vanhu pasi.” Zvino kwakanga kuno uswa huzhinji ipapo. Naizvozvo varume vakagara pasi, kuwanda kwavo kunenge zviuru zvishanu." 
John6:11 Zvino Jesu akatora zvingwa; akavonga, akazvipa vakanga vagere pasi; nehovewo saizvozvo pavaida napo." 
John6:12 Zvino vakati vaguta, akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Unganidzai zvimedu zvakasara, kuti zvirege kurasika.”" 
John6:13 Ipapo vakazviunganidza, vakazadza matengu ane gumi namaviri nezvimedu zvezvingwa zvishanu zvebhari, zvakanga zvasara kuna vakadya." 
John6:14 Zvino vanhu vakati vaona chiratidzo chaakaita, vakati, “Zvirokwazvo uyu muporofita, anouya panyika.”" 
John6:15 Zvino Jesu, zvaakaziva kuti voda kuuya kumubata nesimba kuzomuita mambo, akabvazve, akaenda mugomo ari oga." 
John6:16 Zvino ava madekwana, vadzidzi vake vakaburukira kugungwa;" 
John6:17 vakapinda muigwa, vakatanga kuyambuka gungwa kuenda Kapenaume. Zvino kwakanga kwasviba, asi Jesu akanga asati asvika kwavari." 
John6:18 Gungwa rikatanga kumutswa nemhepo huru yaivhuvhuta. 
John6:19 Zvino vakati vakwasva zvikuru masitadhia anenge makumi maviri namashanu, kana makumi matatu, vakaona Jesu achifamba pamusoro pemvura, achiswedera pedyo negwa; vakatya." 
John6:20 Asi iye akati kwavari, “Ndini, musatya.”" 
John6:21 Zvino vakafara kumugamuchira muigwa, igwa rikasvika pakarepo kunyika kwavakanga vachienda." 
John6:22 Ava mangwana vanhu vazhinji, vakanga vamire mhiri kwegungwa, vakaona kuti pakanga pasina rimwe igwa duku ipapo, asi iro rimwe makanga mapinda vadzidzi vake, mariri, uye kuti Jesu haana kupinda muigwa navadzidzi vake, asi kuti vadzidzi vake vakanga vaenda voga." 
John6:23 (Asi mamwe magwa maduku akanga abva Tibheriasi, akasvika pedyo pavakadyira zvingwa, Ishe ambovonga)." 
John6:24 Zvino vanhu vazhinji vakati vaona, kuti Jesu haapo, navadzidzi vake, vakapinda vamene mumagwa maduku, vakasvika Kapenaume, vachitsvaka Jesu." 
John6:25 Zvino vakati vamuwana mhiri kwegungwa, vakati kwaari, “Rabhi, mauya pano rinhiko?”" 
John6:26 Jesu akavapindura, akati, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, hamunditsvaki nokuti makaona zviratidzo, asi nokuti makadya zvingwa mukaguta." 
John6:27 Musabatira basa kutsvaka zvokudya zvinopera, asi batirai basa kuti muwane zvokudya zvinogara kuupenyu husingaperi, zvamuchapiwa naMwanakomana womunhu; nokuti Baba, Mwari, vakaisa chisimbiso kwaari.”" 
John6:28 Zvino vakati kwaari, “Tichaiteiko, kuti tibate mabasa aMwari?”" 
John6:29 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Basa raMwari ndiro, kuti mutende kuna iye waakatuma.”" 
John6:30 Zvino vakati kwaari, “Munoita chiratidzo chipiko, kuti tione, tikutendei?" 
John6:31 Madzibaba edu akadya mana murenje, sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, ‘Akavapa chingwa chikabva kudenga, kuti vadye.’ ”" 
John6:32 Zvino Jesu akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo ndinoti kwamuri, akanga asi iye Mosesi, akakupai chingwa chakabva kudenga, asi ndiBaba vangu vanokupai chingwa chechokwadi, chinobva kudenga." 
John6:33 Nokuti chingwa chaMwari ndicho chinoburuka kudenga, chinopa pasi upenyu.”" 
John6:34 Zvino vakati kwaari, “Ishe, tipei chingwa ichi misi yose.”" 
John6:35 Jesu akati kwavari, “Ndini chingwa choupenyu; anouya kwandiri, haangatongovi nenzara, noanotenda kwandiri haangatongovi nenyota." 
John6:36 Asi ndakakuudzai, kuti makandiona, asi hamutendi." 
John6:37 “Zvose Baba zvavanondipa zvichauya kwandiri; noanouya kwandiri, handingatongomurasiri kunze." 
John6:38 Nokuti handina kuburuka kudenga, kuti ndiite kuda kwangu, asi kuda kwoakandituma." 
John6:39 Kuda kwoakandituma ndiko, kuti pazvose zvaakandipa, ndirege kurasikirwa nomumwechete waakanditurira, asi kuti ndivamutse nezuva rokupedzisira." 
John6:40 Nokuti kuda kwababa vangu ndiko, kuti mumwe nomumwe, anotarira Mwanakomana, nokutenda kwaari, ave noupenyu husingaperi; neni ndichamumutsa nezuva rokupedzisira.”" 
John6:41 Zvino vaJudha vakagun'un'una pamusoro pake, nokuti akati, “Ndini chingwa chakaburuka kudenga.”" 
John6:42 Vakati, “Uyu haasi Jesu, Mwanakomana waJosefa, watinoziva baba namai vake here? Zvino angagoti seiko, ndakaburuka kudenga?”" 
John6:43 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Musagun'un'una pakati penyu." 
John6:44 “Hakuna munhu angauya kwandiri, kana Baba, vakandituma, vasingamukwevi; neni ndichamumutsa nezuva rokupedzisira." 
John6:45 Muvaporofita makanyorwa, muchinzi, ‘Vachadzidziswa vose naMwari.’ Mumwe nomumwe akazvinzwa kuna Baba, akadzidza, anouya kwandiri." 
John6:46 Handirevi kuti kune munhu akaona Baba; asi uyo anobva kuna Mwari, ndiye akaona Baba." 
John6:47 “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, anotenda, ano upenyu usingaperi." 
John6:48 Ndini chingwa choupenyu. 
John6:49 “Madzibaba enyu akadya mana murenje, akafa." 
John6:50 Ichi ndicho chingwa, chinoburuka kudenga, kuti munhu achidye, arege kufa." 
John6:51 Ndini chingwa chipenyu, chakaburuka kudenga; kana munhu achidya chingwa ichi, achararama nokusingaperi; chingwa chandichapa, inyama yangu, yandinopira upenyu hwapasi.”" 
John6:52 Zvino vaJudha vakakakavara pakati pavo, vachiti, “Munhu uyu angatipa seiko nyama yake, tidye?”" 
John6:53 Jesu akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, kana musingadyi nyama yoMwanakomana womunhu, nokunwa ropa rake, hamuna upenyu mamuri." 
John6:54 “Anodya nyama yangu, naanonwa ropa rangu, ane upenyu husingaperi; ini ndichamumutsa nezuva rokupedzisira." 
John6:55 Nokuti nyama yangu ndicho chokudya chaicho, neropa rangu chokunwa chaicho." 
John6:56 Anodya nyama yangu, naanonwa ropa rangu, anogara mandiri, neni maari." 
John6:57 Baba vapenyu, sezvavakandituma, neni ndichirarama naBaba; saizvozvo anondidya, achararama neni." 
John6:58 Ichi ndicho chingwa chakaburuka kudenga; hazvina kuita samadzibaba akadya, akafa; anodya chingwa ichi achararama nokusingaperi.”" 
John6:59 Akareva zvinhu izvi musinagoge, achidzidzisa paKapenaume." 
John6:60 Zvino vazhinji vavadzidzi vake vakati vachizvinzwa, vakati, “Iri shoko igukutu; ndianiko angarinzwa?”" 
John6:61 Asi Jesu, zvaakanga achiziva mumwoyo make kuti vadzidzi vake vanogun'un'una neshoko irero, akati kwavari, “Iri shoko rinokugumbusai kanhi?" 
John6:62 Muchagodiniko kana muchiona Mwanakomana womunhu achikwira kwaaiva pakutanga? 
John6:63 Mweya ndiye anoraramisa, nyama haina maturo; mashoko andakataura kwamuri, ndiwo mweya noupenyu." 
John6:64 Asi vamwe venyu variko vasingatendi;” nokuti Jesu akanga achiziva kubva pakutanga, kuti vaisatenda ndivanaani, uye kuti ndiani aizomupandukira." 
John6:65 Akati, “Nemhaka iyi ndakati kwamuri, kuti hakuna munhu angauya kwandiri, kana asina kuzvipiwa naBaba.”" 
John6:66 Ipapo vadzidzi vake vazhinji vakadzokera shure, vakasazofamba naye." 
John6:67 Jesu akati kuna vane gumi navaviri, “Nemi munoda kubvawo here?”" 
John6:68 Simoni Petirosi akamupindura, akati, “Ishe, tichagoenda kuna aniko? Ndimi muna mashoko oupenyu husingaperi." 
John6:69 “Isu takatenda, tikaziva kuti ndimi Mutsvene waMwari.”" 
John6:70 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Handina kukutsanangurai, imi muri gumi navaviri here? Asi mumwe wenyu ndowaDhiabhori.”" 
John6:71 Akareva Judhasi, mwanakomana waSimoni Isikarioti, nokuti ndiye aizomupandukira, aiva mumwe wavane gumi navaviri." 
John7:1 Shure kwaizvozvo Jesu akafamba muGareriya; nokuti akanga asingadi kufamba muJudhiya, nokuti vaJudha vakanga vachida kumuuraya." 
John7:2 Zvino mutambo wavaJudha wamatumba wakanga uri pedyo. 
John7:3 Naizvozvo vanun'una vake vakati kwaari, “Ibva pano, uende Judhiya, kuti vadzidzi vako vaonewo mabasa ako aunoita." 
John7:4 Nokuti hakuna munhu anoita chinhu chinyararire, kana iye amene achida kuzikanwa; kana iwe uchiita izvi, uzviratidze kunyika.”" 
John7:5 Nokuti navanun'una vake vakanga vasingatendi kwaari. 
John7:6 Ipapo Jesu akati kwavari, “Nguva yangu ichigere kusvika; asi nguva yenyu inogara yakagadzirwa." 
John7:7 “Nyika haingakuvengi imi; asi inondivenga ini, nokuti ndinoipupurira, kuti mabasa ayo akaipa." 
John7:8 Kwirai kumutambo imi; ini handiti ndokwira kumutambo, nokuti nguva yangu ichigere kusvika kwazvo.”" 
John7:9 Akati areva izvozvo kwavari, akagara Gareriya." 
John7:10 Zvino vanun'una vake vakati vakwira kumutambo, iye akabva okwirawo, asingaendi pachena, asi panenge sapakavanda." 
John7:11 Zvino vaJudha vakamutsvaka pamutambo, vakati, “Aripiko iye?”" 
John7:12 Kugun'un'una kukuru kukavapo pakati pavazhinji pamusoro pake, vamwe vachiti, “Akanaka;” vamwe vachiti, “Kwete, anotsausa vanhu vazhinji.”" 
John7:13 Kunyangwe zvakadaro kwakanga kusina munhu aitaura pachena pamusoro pake, nokuti vakatya vaJudha." 
John7:14 Zvino kwakati pava pakati pomutambo, Jesu akakwira kutemberi, akatanga kudzidzisa." 
John7:15 Naizvozvo vaJudha vakashamiswa, vachiti, “Munhu uyu anoziva seiko mabhuku, zvaasina kumbodzidza?”" 
John7:16 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Kudzidzisa kwangu hakusi kwangu, asi ndokwoakandituma." 
John7:17 Kana munhu achida kuita kuda kwake, achaziva kana kudzidzisa uku kuchibva kuna Mwari, kana ndichizvitaurira ndimene." 
John7:18 “Anozvitaurira, anotsvaka kukudzwa kwake; asi anotsvaka kukudzwa kwoakamutuma, ndiye wechokwadi, hapana kusarurama maari." 
John7:19 Mosesi haana kukupai murairo here? Asi hakuna mumwe wenyu anoita murairo. Munotsvakireiko kundiuraya?” 
John7:20 Vanhu vazhinji vakapindura, vachiti, “Uno mweya wakaipa iwe; ndianiko anotsvaka kukuuraya?”" 
John7:21 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Ndakaita basa rimwe, mukashamiswa mose." 
John7:22 Nemhaka iyi Mosesi akakupai dzingiso, (handiti ndeyaMosesi, asi yamadzibaba); zvino imi munodzingisa munhu neSabata." 
John7:23 “Zvino kana munhu angadzingiswa neSabata, kuti murairo waMosesi urege kutyorwa, ko imi monditsamwira nokuti ndakaporesa munhu wose neSabata here?" 
John7:24 Musatonga nezvinoonekwa, asi tongai nokutonga kwakarurama.”" 
John7:25 Zvino vamwe veJerusaremu vakati, “Ko haasi iye avaitsvaka kuuraya here?" 
John7:26 Tarirai, anotaura pachena, vasingarevi chinhu kwaari. Ko vakuru vanoziva kwazvo kanhi kuti ndiye Kristu?" 
John7:27 Zvino uyu tinoziva kwaanobva, asi Kristu kana achisvika, hakuna munhu angaziva kwaanobva.”" 
John7:28 Zvino Jesu akadanidzira mutemberi, akadzidzisa, achiti, “Munondiziva, munoziva napandakabva; handina kuuya ini ndimene, asi akandituma ndiye wechokwadi, wamusingazivi imi." 
John7:29 Ini ndinomuziva, nokuti ndinobva kwaari; ndiye akandituma.”" 
John7:30 Naizvozvo vakatsvaka kumubata, asi kwakanga kusina munhu akaisa ruoko kwaari, nokuti nguva yake yakanga isati yasvika." 
John7:31 Asi vamwe vazhinji vakatenda kwaari, vakati, “Kana Kristu achizosvika, angaita zviratidzo zvizhinji kunezvizvi zvakaitwa nouyu here?”" 
John7:32 Zvino VaFarisi vakanzwa vanhu vazhinji vachigun'un'una izvozvo pamusoro pake; vapristi vakuru navaFarisi vakatuma mapurisa kundomubata. 
John7:33 Ipapo Jesu akati kwavari, “Ndichiri nemi nguva duku, ndigoenda kune akandituma." 
John7:34 Muchanditsvaka, asi hamungandiwani; uye apo pandiri, imi hamungasvikipo.”" 
John7:35 Zvino vaJudha vakataurirana, vachiti, “Uyo anoda kuendepiko, kwatisingazomuwani? Ko anoda kuenda kuna vakapararira pakati pavaGiriki, kuti anodzidzisa vaGiriki here?" 
John7:36 Rinoti kudiniko shoko iri raareva, rokuti, ‘Muchanditsvaka, asi hamungandiwani, uye, apo pandiri, imi hamungasvikipo?’ ”" 
John7:37 Zvino nezuva rokupedzisira, zuva guru romutambo, Jesu akamira, akadanidzira, akati, “Ani naani, kana ane nyota, ngaauye kwandiri, anwe." 
John7:38 ‘Anotenda kwandiri, sezvazvakarehwa noRugwaro, nzizi dzemvura mhenyu dzichayerera dzichibva mukati make.’ ”" 
John7:39 Asi izvi akareva Mweya, aizopiwa avo vaitenda kwaari, nokuti Mweya akanga asati avapo, nokuti Jesu akanga asati akudzwa." 
John7:40 Zvino vamwe pakati pavanhu vazhinji vakati vachinzwa mashoko awa, vakati, “Zvirokwazvo uyu muporofita.”" 
John7:41 Vamwe vakati, “Uyu ndiye Kristu.” Asi vamwe vakati, “Ko Kristu angabva Gareriya here?" 
John7:42 Rugwaro haruna kureva here, kuti Kristu achabva kurudzi rwaDhavhidhi, napamusha weBhetirehemu, paiva naDhavhidhi?”" 
John7:43 Naizvozvo kupesana kwakamuka pamusoro pake pakati pavazhinji. 
John7:44 Vamwe vakanga vachida kumubata; asi kwakanga kusina akaisa maoko kwaari. 
John7:45 Zvino mapurisa akauya kuvapristi vakuru nokuvaFarisi, ivo vakati kwavari, “Makaregereiko kuuya naye?”" 
John7:46 Mapurisa akapindura, akati, “Hakuna munhu akatongotaura nokutaura kwomunhu uyo.”" 
John7:47 Naizvozvo VaFarisi vakavapindura, vakati, “Nemiwo matsauswa kanhi?" 
John7:48 Kuvakuru nokuvaFarisi kuno mumwe akatongotenda kwaari here? 
John7:49 Asi vanhu ava vazhinji, vasingazivi murairo, vakatukwa.”" 
John7:50 Nikodhimo, (uya akambouya kwaari, aiva mumwe wavo), akati kwavari," 
John7:51 “Murairo wedu unotonga munhu, vasati vambomunzwa, nokuziva chaanoita here?”" 
John7:52 Vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Ko newewo uri weGareriya here? Nzvera, uone kuti hakuna muporofita, anobva Gareriya.” [" 
John7:53 Ipapo mumwe nomumwe akaenda kumba kwake. 
John8:1 Jesu akaenda kugomo reMiorivhi. 
John8:2 Mangwanani akadzokerazve kutemberi, vanhu vose vakauya kwaari; akagara pasi akavadzidzisa." 
John8:3 Vanyori naVaFarisi vakauya kwaari nomukadzi akanga abatwa achifeva vakamuisa pakati pavo. 
John8:4 Vakati kwaari, “Mudzidzisi, mukadzi uyu wakabatwa achifeva, ipapo pamene." 
John8:5 “Zvino Mosesi akatirayira mumurairo kuti vakadzi vakadaro vatakwe namabwe; zvino imi munoti kudiniko?” 
John8:6 Vakareva izvozvo, vachimuedza, kuti vawane chavangamupomera mhosva nacho. Asi Jesu akakotama, akanyora pasi nomunwe." 
John8:7 Zvino ivo vakati vachiramba vachimubvunza, akakotoroka, akati kwavari, “Asina chivi pakati penyu, ngaatange kukanda bwe kwaari.”" 
John8:8 Akakotamazve, akanyora pasi." 
John8:9 Zvino ivo vakati vachizvinzwa, hana dzavo dzikavarova, vakabuda mumwe–mumwe, kutanga vakuru kusvikira kunowokupedzisira; Jesu akasara ari oga, nomukadzi akanga amire pakati pavo." 
John8:10 Jesu akatwasanukazve; zvino asingaoni munhu, asi mukadzi oga, akati kwaari, “Mai, vaya vakupomera mhosva varipiko? Hakuna akutonga here?”" 
John8:11 Iye akati, “Hakuna, Ishe!” Jesu akati kwaari, “Neniwo handikupi mhosva. Enda hako, usatadzazve.”]" 
John8:12 Zvino Jesu akataurazve navo, akati, “Ndini chiedza chenyika; anonditevera haangatongofambi murima, asi achava nechiedza choupenyu.”" 
John8:13 Naizvozvo VaFarisi vakati kwaari, “Anozvipupurira iwe; kupupura kwako hakusi kwechokwadi.”" 
John8:14 Jesu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Kunyangwe ndichizvipupurira, kupupura kwangu ndokwechokwadi; nokuti ndinoziva kwandakabva, nokwandinoenda; asi imi hamuzivi kwandakabva, nokwandinoenda." 
John8:15 “Imi munotonga nenyama; ini handitongi munhu. 
John8:16 Asi kunyangwe ndichitonga, kutonga kwangu ndokwechokwadi; nokuti handisi ndoga, asi ini naBaba vakandituma." 
John8:17 Uye mumurairo wenyu makanyorwa, kuti kupupura kwavanhu vaviri ndokwechokwadi." 
John8:18 Ndini ndinozvipupurira, naBaba vakandituma, vanondipupurirawo.”" 
John8:19 Zvino vakati kwaari, “Baba vako varipiko?” Jesu akapindura, akati, “Hamundizivi ini, kunyangwe naBaba vanguo; dai maindiziva ini, maizivawo naBaba vangu.”" 
John8:20 Akataura mashoko awa paichengeterwa mari achidzidzisa mutemberi; kwakanga kusina munhu akamubata, nokuti nguva yake yakanga isati yasvika." 
John8:21 Zvino akatizve kwavari, “Ndinoenda, muchanditsvaka, mukafira muzvivi zvenyu; pandinoenda, imi hamungauyipo.”" 
John8:22 Zvino vaJudha vakati, “Achazviuraya kanhi, zvaanoti, pandinoenda, imi hamungauyipo?”" 
John8:23 Akati kwavari, “Imi muri vapasi, ini ndiri wokumusoro; imi muri venyika ino, ini handisi wenyika ino." 
John8:24 Naizvozvo ndakati kwamuri, muchafira muzvivi zvenyu, nokuti kana musinganditendi, kuti, ‘Ndini iye, muchafira muzvivi zvenyu.’ ”" 
John8:25 Zvino vakati kwaari, “Iwe ndiwe aniko?” Jesu akati kwavari, “Izvo zvandinongoramba ndichikuudzai kubva pakutanga." 
John8:26 Ndine zvizhinji zvandinoda kureva nokutonga pamusoro penyu; asi akandituma ndowechokwadi; izvo zvandakanzwa kwaari, ndizvo zvandinoudza nyika.”" 
John8:27 Asi havana kunzwisisa kuti anovaudza zvaBaba. 
John8:28 Naizvozvo Jesu akati, “Kana masimudza Mwanakomana womunhu, ipapo muchaziva kuti ndini iye, uye kuti ini handiiti chinhu ndimene, asi ndinotaura izvozvo zvandakadzidziswa naBaba." 
John8:29 “Akandituma aneni. Haana kundisiya ndiri ndoga; nokuti ini ndinoita nguva dzose zvinomufadza.” 
John8:30 Akati areva izvozvo, vazhinji vakatenda kwaari." 
John8:31 Zvino Jesu akati kuvaJudha avo, vakanga vamutenda, “Kana imi muchigara mushoko rangu, muri vadzidzi vangu zvirokwazvo." 
John8:32 Muchaziva chokwadi, nechokwadi chichakusunungurai.”" 
John8:33 Vakamupindura, vakati, “Tiri vorudzi rwaAbhurahamu isu, hatina kutongova varanda vomunhu; zvino iwe ungareva seiko kuti, ‘Muchasunungurwa?’ ”" 
John8:34 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, mumwe nomumwe anoita zvivi, ndiye muranda wezvivi." 
John8:35 Muranda haagari mumba nokusingaperi; mwanakomana ndiye anogara nokusingaperi. 
John8:36 Naizvozvo kana Mwanakomana achikusunungurai, muchava vakasununguka kwazvo." 
John8:37 Ndinoziva kuti muri rudzi rwaAbhurahamu; asi munotsvaka kundiuraya, nokuti shoko rangu hariwani nzvimbo mamuri." 
John8:38 “Ini ndinotaura zvandakaona kuna Baba vangu; imi munoitawo zvamanzwa kuna baba venyu.” 
John8:39 Vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Baba vedu ndiAbhurahamu.” Jesu akati kwavari, “Dai maiva vana vaAbhurahamu, maiita mabasa aAbhurahamu." 
John8:40 Asi zvino munotsvaka kundiuraya, ini munhu wakakuudzai chokwadi, chandakanzwa kuna Mwari. Abhurahamu haana kuita izvozvo." 
John8:41 Imi munoita mabasa ababa venyu.” Vakati kwaari, “Hatina kuberekwa noupombwe; tina Baba vamwechete, iye Mwari.”" 
John8:42 Jesu akati kwavari, “Dai Mwari aiva Baba venyu, maindida ini; nokuti ndakabuda, ndikabva kuna Mwari. Nokuti handina kuuya nokuda kwangu ini, asi ndiye akandituma." 
John8:43 Hamunzwisisi seiko kutaura kwangu? Nokuti hamugoni kunzwa shoko rangu. 
John8:44 Imi muri vababa venyu Dhiabhori, munoda kuita kuda kwakaipa kwababa venyu. Iye akanga ari muurayi kubva pakutanga; haamiri muchokwadi, nokuti maari hamuna chokwadi. Kana achireva nhema, anoreva zvake, nokuti ndiye wenhema, uye baba vadzo." 
John8:45 Asi ini, zvandinoreva chokwadi, hamunditendi." 
John8:46 Ndianiko kwamuri angakonese kuti ndine zvivi? Kana ndichireva chokwadi, munoregereiko kunditenda?" 
John8:47 Ari waMwari, anonzwa mashoko aMwari; imi hamunzwi nemhaka iyi, nokuti hamusiri muri vaMwari.”" 
John8:48 VaJudha vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Hatina kureva here, tichiti, uri muSamaria, une mweya wakaipa?”" 
John8:49 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Handina mweya wakaipa, asi ndinokudza Baba vangu, zvino imi mondizvidza." 
John8:50 Ini handitsvaki kuti ndikudzwe; ariko mumwe anozvitsvaka, achitonga." 
John8:51 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, kana munhu akachengeta shoko rangu, haangatongooni rufu.”" 
John8:52 VaJudha vakati kwaari, “Tinoziva zvino kuti unemweya wakaipa; Abhurahamu akafa, navaporofitawo; zvino iwe unoti, kana munhu akachengeta shoko rangu, haangatongooni rufu." 
John8:53 “Ko iwe uri mukuru kuna baba vedu Abhurahamu, vakafa, kanhi? Navaporofita vakafa? Unozviita aniko?”" 
John8:54 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Kana ini ndichizvikudza, kuzvikudza kwangu hakuna maturo; anondikudza ndivo Baba, avo vamunoti ndiMwari wenyu." 
John8:55 Hamuna kuvaziva imi, asi ini ndinovaziva; kana ini ndikati handivazivi, ndava murevi wenhema semi; asi ndinovaziva ini, ndinochengeta shoko ravo." 
John8:56 “Abhurahamu, baba venyu, vakafara, vachiti, vachaona zuva rangu; vakariona, vakafara.”" 
John8:57 Ipapo vaJudha vakati kwaari, “Iwe ugere kusvika makore ana makumi mashanu, wakaona Abhurahamu sei?”" 
John8:58 Jesu akati kwavari, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, ‘Abhurahamu asati avapo, ini ndaivapo.’ ”" 
John8:59 Ipapo vakanonga mabwe kuti vamutake nawo; asi Jesu akazvivanza, akabuda mutemberi." 
John9:1 Akati achipfuura, akaona munhu akanga ari bofu kubva pakuberekwa kwake." 
John9:2 Vadzidzi vake vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Rabhi, ndianiko akatadza, uyu kana vabereki vake, zvaakaberekwa riri bofu?”" 
John9:3 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Uyu haana kutadza, kunyangwe navabereki vake; asi izvi zvakaitwa kuti mabasa aMwari aoneswe maari." 
John9:4 Ndinofanira kubata basa rowakandituma, achiri masikati; usiku hunouya, husingagoni munhu kubata basa nahwo." 
John9:5 Ndichiri panyika, ndiri chiedza chenyika.”" 
John9:6 Akati areva izvozvo, akapfira mate pasi, akakanya dope namate, akazodza dope pameso pake," 
John9:7 akati kwaari, “Enda undoshamba mudziva reSiroamu,” (ndokuti, kana zvichishandurwa, “Kutumwa.”) Ipapo akaenda, akandoshamba, akadzoka achiona." 
John9:8 Vakanga vagere naye, navaimuona kare, kuti ndiye waikumbira, vakati, “Ko uyu haasi iye aigara achikumbira here?”" 
John9:9 Vamwe vakati, “Ndiye;” vamwe vakati, “Kwete, asi akatodzana naye.” Iye akati, “Ndini.”" 
John9:10 Zvino vakati kwaari, “Meso ako akagosvinudzwa seiko?”" 
John9:11 Akapindura, akati, “Munhu anonzi Jesu akakanya dope, akazodza meso angu, akati kwandiri, enda Siroamu, undoshamba; naizvozvo ndakaenda, ndikashamba, ndikaona.”" 
John9:12 Vakati kwaari, “Iye aripiko?” Akati, “Handizivi.”" 
John9:13 Vakamuisa kuvaFarisi, iye akanga ari bofu kare." 
John9:14 Zvino raiva Sabata zuva iro Jesu raakakanya dope naro, akasvinudza meso ake." 
John9:15 Zvino VaFarisi vakamubvunzazve, kuti wakaoneswa sei. Akati kwavari, “Akaisa dope pameso pangu, ndikandoshamba, ndikaona.”" 
John9:16 Zvino vamwe vavaFarisi vakati, “Munhu uyu haasi waMwari, nokuti haachengeti Sabata.” Asi vamwe vakati, “Ko munhu mutadzi angaita seiko zviratidzo zvakadai?” Ipapo kupesana kwakamuka pakati pavo." 
John9:17 Zvino vakatizve kubofu, “Iwe unoti kudiniko pamusoro pake, zvaakasvinudza meso ako?” Akati, “Muporofita.”" 
John9:18 Naizvozvo vaJudha havana kutenda pamusoro pake, kuti akanga ari bofu, akazoona, kusvikira vadana vabereki vowakaoneswa," 
John9:19 vakavabvunza, vachiti, “Uyu ndiye mwanakomana wenyu, wamunoti akaberekwa riri bofu here? Zvino anogoona seiko?”" 
John9:20 Vabereki vake vakapindura, vakati, “Tinoziva kuti uyu mwanakomana wedu, uye kuti akaberekwa riri bofu;" 
John9:21 asi hatizivi kuti zvino woona sei; noakasvinudza meso ake, hatimuzivi; mubvunzei henyu; ayaruka, achazvirevera hake.”" 
John9:22 Vabereki vake vakareva izvozvo, nokuti vaitya vaJudha, nokuti vaJudha vakanga vatotenderana, kuti kana kuchinge kune munhu anotenda kuti ndiye Kristu, abudiswe musinagoge." 
John9:23 Naizvozvo vabereki vake vakati, “Ayaruka hake, mubvunzei henyu.”" 
John9:24 Zvino vakamudanazve rwechipiri, iye munhu akanga ari bofu, vakati kwaari, “Rumbidza Mwari; isu tinoziva kuti munhu uyu mutadzi.”" 
John9:25 Ipapo iye akapindura, akati, “Kana ari mutadzi ini handizivi; ndinoziva chinhu chimwe, kuti ndaiva bofu, zvino ndoona.”" 
John9:26 Ipapo vakati kwaari, “Akakuiteiko? Akasvinudza meso ako sei?”" 
John9:27 Akavapindura, akati, “Ndatokuudzai, mukasanzwa. Munoda kunzwazve nemhaka yeiko? Nemi munoda kuva vadzidzi vakewo kanhi?”" 
John9:28 Vakamunyomba, vachiti, “Iwe ndiwe mudzidzi wake, asi isu tiri vadzidzi vaMosesi." 
John9:29 Tinoziva kuti Mwari wakataura naMosesi; asi uyu hatizivi kwaakabva.” 
John9:30 Iye munhu akapindura, akati kwavari, “Nyambera chinhu ichi chinoshamisa, kuti imi hamuzivi kwaanobva, kunyangwe akasvinudza meso angu." 
John9:31 Tinoziva kuti Mwari haanzwi vatadzi; asi kana munhu achishandira Mwari, achiita kuda kwake, anomunzwa iye." 
John9:32 Kubvira pakutanga hakuna kumbonzwika, kuti mumwe akasvinudza meso omunhu, akaberekwa riri bofu." 
John9:33 Dai uyu asati ari waMwari, haasaigona kuita chinhu.”" 
John9:34 Vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Iwe wakaberekerwa muzvivi chose, zvino iwe wotidzidzisa isu?” Vakamudzingira kunze." 
John9:35 Jesu akanzwa kuti vamudzingira kunze; akati amuwana, akati kwaari, “Iwe unotenda kuMwanakomana waMwari here?”" 
John9:36 Akapindura, akati, “Iye ndianiko Ishe, kuti nditende kwaari?”" 
John9:37 Jesu akati kwaari, “Wamuona, uye, ndiye unotaura newe.”" 
John9:38 Ipapo akati, “Ndinotenda, Ishe.” Akamupfugamira." 
John9:39 Jesu akati, “Kutonga ndiko kwandauyira panyika ino, kuti vasingaoni, vaone; navanoona vave mapofu.”" 
John9:40 Avo vavaFarisi vaiva naye, vakazvinzwa, vakati kwaari, “Ko nesuwo tiri mapofu here?”" 
John9:41 Jesu akati kwavari, “Dai maiva mapofu, hamusaiva nezvivi, asi zvino munoti, tinoona; zvivi zvenyu zvinoramba zviripo.”" 
John10:1 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, “Asingapindi napamusuwo mudanga ramakwai, asi anokwira napamwe, imbavha negororo." 
John10:2 Asi anopinda nopamusuwo, ndiye mufudzi wamakwai." 
John10:3 Murindi womusuwo anomuzarurira iye, makwai anonzwa izwi rake, anodana makwai ake namazita awo, nokuaperekedzera kunze." 
John10:4 Kana abudisa makwai ake ose, anoatungamirira; makwai anomutevera, nokuti anoziva izwi rake." 
John10:5 Asi mweni haangatongomuteveri, asi anomutiza; nokuti haazivi izwi ravaeni.”" 
John10:6 Jesu akareva mufananidzo uyu kwavari, asi havana kunzwisisa, kuti zvaakavataurira ndezvei." 
John10:7 Zvino Jesu akati kwavarizve, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, ndini musuwo wamakwai." 
John10:8 Vose vakanditangira kuuya, imbavha namakororo, asi makwai haana kuvanzwa." 
John10:9 “Ndini musuwo kana munhu apinda neni, achaponeswa, achapinda, achabuda, achawana mafuro." 
John10:10 Mbavha inongouya, kuti ibe nokuuraya nokuparadza. Ini ndakauya, kuti ave noupenyu, uye ave nohwakawanda." 
John10:11 “Ndini mufudzi akanaka; mufudzi akanaka anorasira makwai ake upenyu hwake. 
John10:12 Muranda, asati ari mufudzi wamakwai, makwai asati ari ake, anoti kana achiona bere richiuya, anosiya makwai, ndokutiza; bere rinoabvuta, nokuaparadza;" 
John10:13 anotiza, zvaari muranda; haana hanya namakwai." 
John10:14 Ndini mufudzi akanaka, ndinoziva makwai angu, namakwai angu anondiziva ini," 
John10:15 Baba sezvavanondiziva, neni ndichiziva Baba; ndinorashira makwai angu upenyu hwangu." 
John10:16 Namamwe makwai ndinawo, asati ari edanga rino. Naiwo ndinofanira kuuya nawowo, achanzwa izwi rangu; richava boka rimwe, nomufudzi mumwe." 
John10:17 “Saka Baba vanondida, nokuti ndinorasha upenyu hwangu, ndigohutorazve." 
John10:18 Hakuna munhu anganditorera upenyu; asi ndinohurasha ndimene. Ndine simba rokuhurasha, uye ndine simba rokuhutorazve. Uyu murairo ndakaupiwa nababa vangu.”" 
John10:19 Ipapo kupesana kukamukazve pakati pavaJudha pamusoro pamashoko iwayo. 
John10:20 Vazhinji vavo vakati, “Ane mweya wakaipa, anopenga; munomuteerereiko?”" 
John10:21 Vamwe vakati, “Mashoko awa haati ari omunhu akabatwa nomweya wakaipa; ko mweya wakaipa ungagona kusvinudza meso amapofu here?”" 
John10:22 Yaiva nguva yomutambo wokuvandudzwa kwetemberi paJerusaremu; chaiva chando. 
John10:23 Jesu akafamba mutemberi pabiravira raSoromoni. 
John10:24 Zvino vaJudha vakamukomba, vakati kwaari, “Uchatinetsa kusvikira rinhiko? Kana uri Kristu iwe, tiudze pachena.”" 
John10:25 Jesu akavapindura, akati, “Ndakakuudzai, mukasatenda. Mabasa andinoita nezita raBaba, ndiwo anondipupurireni." 
John10:26 Asi imi hamutendi, nokuti hamusi vamakwai angu." 
John10:27 Makwai angu anonzwa izwi rangu; neni ndinoaziva, uye anonditevera." 
John10:28 Ndinoapa upenyu husingaperi; haangafi nokusingaperi, uye hakuna munhu angaabvuta muruoko rwangu." 
John10:29 Zvandakapiwa naBaba vangu zvikuru kuna zvose; hakuna munhu ungaabvuta muruoko rwaBaba vangu. 
John10:30 “Ini naBaba tiri vamwe.” 
John10:31 Zvino vaJudha vakanongazve mabwe, kuti vamutake." 
John10:32 Jesu akavapindura, akati, “Ndakakuratidzai mabasa mazhinji akanaka akabva kuna Baba; munonditakira basa ripiko kuna iwaya?”" 
John10:33 VaJudha vakamupindura, vakati, “Hatikutakiri basa rakanaka; asi nokuti wamhura Mwari; uye, nokuti iwe munhu, unozviita Mwari.”" 
John10:34 Jesu akavapindura, akati, “Hazvina kunyorwa here mumurairo wenyu, zvichinzi, ndakati, ‘Muri vamwari?’" 
John10:35 “Zvino kana akavaidza vamwari, ivo shoko raMwari rakasvika kwavari, (Rugwaro harungaputswi);" 
John10:36 imi moti seiko kuna iye akaitwa mutsvene naBaba, nokutumwa panyika, unomhura Mwari, zvandakati, ndiri Mwanakomana waMwari?" 
John10:37 Kana ndisingaiti mabasa aBaba vangu, regai kunditenda ini;" 
John10:38 asi kana ndichiaita, kunyangwe musinganditendi ini, tendai mabasa, mugoziva nokunzwisisa, kuti Baba vari mandiri, neni ndiri muna Baba.”" 
John10:39 Zvino vakatsvakazve kumubata, asi iye akapukunyuka pamaoko avo." 
John10:40 Zvino akaendazve mhiri kwaJodhani, paya paibhabhatidza Johani pakutanga; akagarapo." 
John10:41 Vazhinji vakauya kwaari, vakati, “Johani haana kuita chiratidzo, asi zvose zvakareva Johani pamusoro pouyu ndezvechokwadi.”" 
John10:42 Vazhinji vakatenda kwaari ipapo. 
John11:1 Mumwe munhu wakanga achirwara, ainzi Razaro weBhetania, musha waMaria nomukoma wake Marita." 
John11:2 Ndiye Maria uya, akazodza Ishe namafuta, akapukuta tsoka dzake nevhudzi rake; hanzvadzi yake Razaro, akanga achirwara." 
John11:3 Zvino hanzvadzi dzake dzakatuma shoko kwaari, dzichiti, “Ishe, tarirai uyo anodikanwa nemi anorwara.”" 
John11:4 Jesu akati azvinzwa, akati, “Kurwara uku hakusi kwokufa, asi kuti Mwari akudzwe, noMwanakomana waMwari akudzwewo nazvo.”" 
John11:5 Jesu akanga achida Marita, nomunun'una wake, naRazaro." 
John11:6 Zvino akati anzwa kuti anorwara, akambogara mazuva maviri paakanga ari." 
John11:7 Shure kwaizvozvo akati kuvadzidzi vake, “Hendeizve Judhiya.”" 
John11:8 Vadzidzi vakati kwaari, “Rabhi, vaJudha vakanga vachikutsvakai iko zvino, kuti vakutakei namabwe; zvino moendazve ikoko here?”" 
John11:9 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Nguva hadzisi gumi nembiri pazuva here? Kana munhu achifamba masikati, haagumburwi, nokuti anoona chiedza chenyika ino." 
John11:10 Asi kana munhu achifamba usiku, anogumburwa, nokuti hakuna chiedza maari.”" 
John11:11 Ndizvozvo zvaakareva, akazoti kwavari, “Razaro, hama yedu, avata; asi ndinoenda, kuti ndimumutse pahope.”" 
John11:12 Zvino vadzidzi vakati kwaari, “Ishe, kana achivata, achanaya.”" 
John11:13 Jesu akanga areva kufa kwake, asi ivo vakanga vachiti anoreva kuvata hope." 
John11:14 Ipapo Jesu akavaudza pachena, “Razaro afa." 
John11:15 Ndinofara nokuda kwenyu, kuti ndakanga ndisipo, kuti mugotenda; asi zvino hendei kwaari.”" 
John11:16 Ipapo Tomasi, ainzi Dhidhimo, akati kuna vamwe vadzidzi, “Hendei nesuwo, kuti tindofa naye.”" 
John11:17 Zvino Jesu akati achisvika, akamuwana atova muhwiro mazuva mana." 
John11:18 Bhetania rakanga riri pedyo neJerusaremu, masitadhia anenge gumi namashanu;" 
John11:19 vazhinji vavaJudha vakanga vauya kuna Marita naMaria, kuti vavabate ruoko pamusoro pehanzvadzi yavo." 
John11:20 Zvino Marita akati achinzwa kuti Jesu wouya, akaenda kunomuchingamidza; asi Maria akagara mumba." 
John11:21 Marita akati kuna Jesu, “Ishe, dai maiva pano, hanzvadzi yangu ingadai isina kufa." 
John11:22 Kunyangwe zvino ndinoziva, kuti zvose zvamunokumbira kuna Mwari, Mwari achakupai.”" 
John11:23 Jesu akati kwaari, “Hanzvadzi yako ichamukazve.”" 
John11:24 Marita akati kwaari, “Ndinoziva kuti achamukazve pakumuka nezuva rokupedzisira.”" 
John11:25 Jesu akati kwaari, “Ndini kumuka noupenyu; anotenda kwandiri, kunyangwe akafa, achararama." 
John11:26 “Mumwe nomumwe ari mupenyu, anotenda kwandiri, haangatongofi. Unotenda izvozvo here?”" 
John11:27 Akati kwaari, “Hongu, Ishe, ndakatenda kuti ndimi Kristu, Mwanakomana waMwari, uyo ainzi anouya panyika.”" 
John11:28 Akati areva izvovo, akandodana Maria, munun'una wake, akati kwaari vari voga, “Mudzidzisi asvika, anokudana.”" 
John11:29 Iye akati achizvinzwa, akakurumidza kusimuka, akaenda kwaari." 
John11:30 (Zvino Jesu akanga asati asvika pamusha, asi akanga achiri paya paakachingamidzwa naMarita.)" 
John11:31 Zvino vaJudha, vakanga vari mumba naye vachimubata ruoko, vakati vachiona Maria achikurumidza kusimuka achibuda, vakamutevera, vachiti unoenda kuhwiro kundochemako." 
John11:32 Zvino Maria akati achisvika kuna Jesu, achimuona, akawira pasi patsoka dzake, akati kwaari; “Ishe, dai maiva pano, hanzvadzi yangu ingadai isina kufa.”" 
John11:33 Zvino Jesu akati achimuona achichema, navaJudha vakanga vauya naye, vachichemawo, akafa neshungu mumweya, akatambudzika," 
John11:34 akati, “Mamuisepiko?” Vakati kwaari, “Ishe, uyai muone.”" 
John11:35 Jesu akachema misodzi. 
John11:36 Ipapo vaJudha vakati, “Tarirai, aimuda sei!”" 
John11:37 Asi vamwe vavo vakati, “Uyu akasvinudza meso ebofu, haasaigona kudzivisa kuti uyu munhu arege kufa here?”" 
John11:38 Ipapo Jesu akafazve neshungu mukati make, akasvika pahwiro. Iro raiva bako, nebwe rakanga riri pamusoro paro." 
John11:39 Jesu akati, “Bvisai ibwe!” Marita, hanzvadzi yoakafa, akati kwaari, “Ishe, otonhuwa zvino, nokuti ava namazuva mana okufa kwake.”" 
John11:40 Jesu akati kwaari, “Handina kukuudza here, kuti kana ukatenda, uchaona kubwinya kwaMwari?”" 
John11:41 Ipapo vakabvisa ibwe. Zvino Jesu akatarira kudenga, akati, “Baba, ndinovongai, nokuti mandinzwa." 
John11:42 Asi ndakanga ndichiziva, kuti munosindinzwa nguva dzose; asi ndakazvireva nokuda kwavazhinji vakandikomba, kuti vatende kuti makandituma.”" 
John11:43 Akati areva izvozvo, akadanidzira nezwi guru, akati, “Razaro, buda!”" 
John11:44 Akanga afa akabuda, akapombwa makumbo namaoko nemicheka yomuhwiro, nechiso chake chakapombwa nomucheka. Jesu akati kwavari, “Musunungurei, aende.”" 
John11:45 Naizvozvo vazhinji vavaJudha, vakanga vauya kuna Maria, vakati vaona zvaaita, vakatenda kwaari." 
John11:46 Asi vamwe vavo vakaenda kuvaFarisi, vakandovaudza zvakanga zvaitwa naJesu." 
John11:47 Naizvozvo vapristi vakuru navaFarisi vakaunganidza makurukota, vakati, “Todiniko? Nokuti uyu anoita zviratidzo zvizhinji." 
John11:48 Kana tikamurega achidaro, vanhu vose vachatenda kwaari; navaRoma vachauya vakatitorera nzvimbo yedu norudzi rwedu.”" 
John11:49 Zvino mumwe wavo, Kaifasi, akanga ari Mupristi Mukuru gore iro, akati kwavari, “Hamuzivi chinhu, imi," 
John11:50 uye hamurangariri kuti zviri nani kwamuri, kuti munhu mumwe afire vanhu, rudzi rwose rurege kufa.”" 
John11:51 Haana kureva izvozvo pachake, asi zvaakanga ari Mupristi Mukuru gore iro, akaporofita kuti Jesu aifanira kufira rudzi;" 
John11:52 rusati ruri rudzi rwoga, asi kuti aunganidze pamwechete vana vaMwari vakapararira." 
John11:53 Zvino kubva pazuva iro vakarangana, kuti vamuuraye." 
John11:54 Naizvozvo Jesu haana kuzofamba pachena pakati pavaJudha, asi akabvapo, akaenda kunyika iri pedyo nerenje, kuguta rainzi Efuremu; akagarako navadzidzi vake." 
John11:55 Zvino Pasika yavaJudha yakanga yava pedyo, vanhu vazhinji venyika iyo vakakwira Jerusaremu, Pasika isati yasvika, kuti vazvinatse." 
John11:56 Zvino vakatsvaka Jesu, vakataurirana vamire mutemberi, vachiti, “Munoti kudiniko? Munoti haangauyi kumutambo here?”" 
John11:57 Zvino vapristi vakuru navaFarisi vakanga varayira, kuti, ani naani kana achiziva kwaari, avazivise, kuti vandomubata." 
John12:1 Zvino mazuva matanhatu Pasika ichigere kusvika, Jesu akasvika Bhetania, paiva naRazaro, wakadeya kumutswa naJesu kuvakafa." 
John12:2 Vakamuitirapo chirariro; Marita akavashandira; naRazaro akanga ari mumwe wavakanga vagere naye pakudya. 
John12:3 Zvino Maria akatora paundi yamafuta enaridho, anomutengo mukuru, akazodza tsoka dzaJesu, akapukuta tsoka dzake nevhudzi rake; imba ikazadzwa nokunhuwira kwamafuta." 
John12:4 Ipapo mumwe wavadzidzi vake, Judhasi Isikarioti akanga achazomupandukira, akati," 
John12:5 “Mafuta awa akaregereiko kutengeswa namadhinari mazana matatu, akapiwa varombo?”" 
John12:6 Asi haana kureva izvozvo kuri kuti akarangarira varombo, asi nokuti aiva mbavha; aigara nechikwama, achisiba zvaiiswamo." 
John12:7 Asi Jesu akati, “Muregei, azvichengetere zuva rokuvigwa kwangu." 
John12:8 Nokuti varombo munavo nguva dzose; asi ini hamuneni nguva dzose.” 
John12:9 Zvino vanhu vazhinji zhinji vokuvaJudha vakanzwa kuti aripo; vakauya, asi havana kuuya nokuda kwaJesu bedzi, asi kuti vaonewo Razaro, waakanga amutsa kuvakafa." 
John12:10 Asi vapristi vakuru vakarangana kuti vauraye naRazarowo," 
John12:11 nokuti nokuda kwake vaJudha vazhinji vakanga vachibva kwavari, vachitenda kuna Jesu." 
John12:12 Zvino ava mangwana vanhu vazhinji zhinji, vakanga vauya kumutambo, vakati vanzwa kuti Jesu auya Jerusaremu," 
John12:13 vakatora mashizha emichindwi, vakabuda kundomuchingamidza, vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Hosana! Ngaarumbidzwe anouya muzita raIshe, Mambo waVaIsiraeri.”" 
John12:14 Jesu akati awana mwana wembongoro, akagara pamusoro payo, sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi," 
John12:15 “Usatya, mukunda weZioni; tarira Mambo wako anouya, agere pamusoro pemhuru yembongoro.”" 
John12:16 Vadzidzi vake havana kunzwisisa izvozvi pakutanga; asi Jesu akati akudzwa, vakazoyeuka, kuti izvozvo zvakanga zvanyorwa pamusoro pake, uye kuti vakanga vamuitira izvozvo." 
John12:17 Zvino vanhu vazhinji vaiva naye pakudana kwake Razaro kuti abve muhwiro, nokumumutsa kuvakafa, vakapupura." 
John12:18 Saka vazhinji vakamuchingamidzawo, nokuti vakanga vanzwa, kuti akaita chiratidzo ichocho." 
John12:19 Ipapo VaFarisi vakataurirana, vachiti, “Munoona henyu kuti hamugoni chinhu; tarirai, nyika yose yamutevera.”" 
John12:20 Zvino kwaiva navamwe vaGiriki pakati pavakanga vakwira kumutambo kundonamatako; 
John12:21 ivo vakauya kuna Firipi weBhetisaidha reGareriya, vakakumbira kwaari, vachiti, “Ishe, tinoda kuona Jesu.”" 
John12:22 Firipi akaenda, akandoudza Andireya; Andireya akaenda naFiripi, vakandoudza Jesu." 
John12:23 Jesu akavapindura, akati, “Nguva yasvika, kuti Mwanakomana womunhu akudzwe." 
John12:24 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, kana tsanga yezviyo ikasawira muvhu, ikafa, ichagara iri yoga; asi kana ikafa, inobereka zvibereko zvizhinji." 
John12:25 Anoda upenyu hwake, acharasikirwa nahwo; noanovenga upenyu hwake panyika ino, achahuchengeta kuupenyu husingaperi." 
John12:26 Kana munhu achindishumira, ngaanditevere; napandinenge ndiri, nomuranda wangu achavapowo. Kana munhu achindishumira, Baba vachamukudza." 
John12:27 “Zvino mweya wangu unomanikidzwa; ndichatiiko? Baba ndiponesei panguva ino. Asi ndizvo zvandauyira panguva ino. 
John12:28 Baba, kudzai zita renyu.” Ipapo izwi rakauya, richibva kudenga, richiti, “Ndatorikudza, ndicharikudzazve.”" 
John12:29 Zvino vanhu vazhinji, vakanga vamirepo, vachizvinzwa, vakati, “Kwatinhira.” Vamwe vakati, “Mutumwa ataura naye.”" 
John12:30 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Izwi iri harina kuuya nokuda kwangu asi nokuda kwenyu." 
John12:31 Zvino kutongwa kwenyika ino kwavapo, zvino muchinda wenyika ino achadzingwa." 
John12:32 Neni, kana ndasimudzwa panyika, ndichakwevera vose kwandiri.”"
