John12:33 Wakareva izvozvi, achiratidza kufa, kwaaizofa nako." 
John12:34 Zvino vanhu vazhinji vakamupindura, vakati, “Isu takanzwa pamurairo kuti Kristu uchagara nokusingaperi; zvino moreva seiko imi, kuti Mwanakomana womunhu anofanira kusimudzwa? Uyu Mwanakomana womunhu ndianiko?”" 
John12:35 Ipapo Jesu akati kwavari, “Chiedza chichipo pakati penyu chinguva chiduku. Fambai muchine chiedza, kuti murege kukundwa nerima; anofamba murima haazivi kwaanoenda." 
John12:36 “Muchine chiedza, tendai kuchiedza, mugoitwa vana vechiedza.” Jesu akareva izvozvi, akabva, akazvivanza kwavari." 
John12:37 Zvino kunyangwe akanga aita zviratidzo zvizhinji zvakadaro pamberi pavo, havana kutenda kwaari;" 
John12:38 kuti shoko romuporofita Isaya riitike, raakareva, achiti, “Ishe, ndianiko akatenda chavakanzwa kwatiri? Noruoko rwaIshe rwakaratidzwa kuna aniko?”" 
John12:39 Saka vakanga vasingagoni kutenda, nokuti Isaya akatizve," 
John12:40 “Akapofumadza meso avo, akaomesa mwoyo yavo; Kuti varege kuona nameso avo, nokunzwisisa nemwoyo yavo, Vadzoke Ndivaporese.”" 
John12:41 Isaya akareva izvozvi, nokuti akaona kubwinya kwake; akamureva iye." 
John12:42 Asi kunyangwe zvakadaro vazhinji vavabati vakatenda kwaari; asi vakanga vasingamureururi nokuda kwavaFarisi, kuti varege kubudiswa musinagoge;" 
John12:43 nokuti vakanga vachida kukudzwa navanhu kupfuura kukudzwa naMwari. 
John12:44 Zvino Jesu akadana, akati, “Anotenda kwandiri, haatendi kwandiri, asi kune akandituma." 
John12:45 Anondiona, anoona akandituma." 
John12:46 Ini ndakauya munyika, ndiri chiedza, kuti ani naani anotenda kwandiri arege kugara murima." 
John12:47 Kana munhu achinzwa mashoko angu, akasaachengeta, handimutongi ini, nokuti handina kuuya kuzotonga nyika, asi kuti ndiponese nyika." 
John12:48 Anondiramba, asingagamuchiri mashoko angu, ano mumwe, anomutonga; shoko randakareva ndiro richamutonga nezuva rokupedzisira." 
John12:49 “Nokuti handina kureva pachangu, asi Baba, vakandituma, ndivo vakandipa murairo, zvandichareva nezvandichataura." 
John12:50 Ndinoziva kuti murairo wavo ndihwo upenyu husingaperi; naizvozvi zvandinotaura, ndinotaura sezvandakaudzwa naBaba.”" 
John13:1 Zvino mutambo wePasika usati wasvika, Jesu akaziva kuti nguva yake yasvika, kuti abve munyika ino, aende kuna Baba, zvaakanga aida vanhu vake vaiva munyika, akavada kusvikira pakuguma." 
John13:2 Zvino vakati voravira, Dhiabhori atoisa mumwoyo maJudhasi Isikarioti, mwanakomana waSimoni, kuti amupandukire;" 
John13:3 Jesu achiziva kuti Baba vakamupa zvinhu zvose mumaoko ake, uye kuti akabva kuna Mwari, uye kuti anoenda kuna Mwari;" 
John13:4 akasimuka pakurayira, akabvisa nguo dzake, akatora mucheka, akazvisunga chiuno." 
John13:5 Zvino akadira mvura mumudziyo, akatanga kushambidza tsoka dzavadzidzi vake, akadzipukuta nomucheka, waakanga akazvisunga nawo." 
John13:6 Akasvika kuna Simoni Petirosi, iye akati kwaari, “Ishe, imi moshambidza tsoka dzangu kanhi?”" 
John13:7 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Chandinoita hauchizivi zvino; asi uchazvinzwisisa pashure.”" 
John13:8 Petirosi akati kwaari, “Hamungatongoshambidzi tsoka dzangu nokusingaperi.” Jesu akamupindura, akati, “Kana ndisingakushambidzi, hauna mugove neni.”" 
John13:9 Simoni Petirosi akati kwaari, “Dzirege kuva tsoka dzangu dzoga, asi maoko angu nomusoro wanguo.”" 
John13:10 Jesu akati kwaari, “Akashambidzwa muviri wose, anofanira woga kuti ashambidzwe tsoka dzake, zvino wanaka kwazvo; imi makanaka, asi hamusi mose.”" 
John13:11 Nokuti akanga achiziva uyo aizomupandukira saka akati, “Hamuna kunaka mose.”" 
John13:12 Zvino akati ashambidza tsoka dzavo, akatora nguo dzake, akagarazve, akati kwavari, “Munoziva zvandakakuitirai here?" 
John13:13 Munondiidza Mudzidzisi, uye Ishe; munoreva zvakanaka, nokuti ndini iye." 
John13:14 Zvino kana ini, Ishe noMudzidzisi, ndakashambidza tsoka dzenyu, nemiwo munofanira kushambidzana tsoka dzenyu." 
John13:15 “Ndakakuratidzai makwara kuti muite imi sezvandakakuitirai ini. 
John13:16 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, Muranda haasi mukuru kuna ishe wake, uye wakatumwa mukuru kune akamutuma." 
John13:17 Kana muchizviziva izvi, makaropafadzwa kana muchizviita." 
John13:18 “Handirevi imi mose; ini ndinoziva avo vandakasanangura; asi kuti Rugwaro ruitike, runoti, ‘Anodya chingwa changu, akandisimudzira chitsitsinho chake.’" 
John13:19 Kubva zvino ndinokuudzai zvisati zvaitika, kuti kana zvichiitwa, mugotenda kuti ndini." 
John13:20 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, anogamuchira wandinotuma, unogamuchireni, noanondigamuchira ini, anogamuchira akandituma.”" 
John13:21 Zvino Jesu akati areva kudaro, akamanikidzwa mumweya, akapupura, akati, “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, mumwe wenyu achandipandukira.”" 
John13:22 Vadzidzi vakatarirana, vasingazivi kuti wareva ani." 
John13:23 Zvino mumwe wavadzidzi vake akanga akasendamira pachipfuva chaJesu, aidikanwa naJesu." 
John13:24 Simoni Petirosi akamuninira, akati kwaari, “Tiudzei kuti ndianiko waanoreva.”" 
John13:25 Iye akavata pachipfuva chaJesu, akati kwaari, “Ishe, ndianiko?”" 
John13:26 Ipapo Jesu akapindura, akati, “Ndiye wandichapa chimedu, kana ndachiseva.” Zvino akati aseva chimedu, akachitora, akapa Judhasi, mwanakomana waSimoni Isikarioti." 
John13:27 Iye akati agamuchira chimedu, Satani akapinda maari. Ipapo Jesu akati kwaari, “Zvaunoita, ita uchikurumidza.”" 
John13:28 Asi kwakanga kusina mumwe kuna vakanga vagere naye pakudya, akaziva kuti akareverei izvozvi kwaari." 
John13:29 Vamwe vakanga vachiti, Judhasi zvaaigara ane chikwama, kuti Jesu akati kwaari, “Tenga zvatinoda pamutambo; kana kuti ape varombo chinhu.”" 
John13:30 Iye akati agamuchira chimedu, akabuda pakarepo; hwakanga huri usiku." 
John13:31 Zvino akati abuda, Jesu akati, “Zvino Mwanakomana akudzwa maari;" 
John13:32 kana Mwari akudzwa maari, Mwari achamukudza iye maari, uchamukudza pakarepo." 
John13:33 Vana vaduku, ndichiri nemi chinguva chiduku; muchanditsvaka, asi sezvandakareva kuvaJudha, ndichiti, ‘Pandinoenda, imi hamungauyipo, saizvozvo zvino ndinoreva kwamuriwo.’" 
John13:34 “Ndinokupai murairo mutsva, wokuti mudane; sezvandakakudai imi, nemi mudanewo saizvozvo." 
John13:35 Vose vachaziva naizvozvi kuti muri vadzidzi vangu, kana muno rudo pakati penyu.”" 
John13:36 Simoni Petirosi akati kwaari, “Ishe, munoendepiko?” Jesu akapindura, akati, “Kwandinoenda, haunganditeveri zvino; asi uchanditevera pashure.”" 
John13:37 Petirosi akati kwaari, “Ishe, handingakutevereyi zvino neiko? Ndichakufirai ini.”" 
John13:38 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Uchandifira here? Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwauri, Jongwe haringariri, usati wandiramba katatu." 
John14:1 “Mwoyo yenyu irege kumanikidzwa; tendai kuna Mwari, mutendewo kwandiri." 
John14:2 Mumba maBaba vangu mune nzvimbo zhinji dzokugara; dai kusaiva kudaro, ndingadai ndaikuudzai; nokuti ndinoenda kundokugadzirirai pokugara." 
John14:3 “Kana ndaenda kundokugadzirirai pokugara, ndinozouyazve, ndikugamuchirei kwandiri; kuti apo pandiri, nemi mugovapowo." 
John14:4 Napandinoendanapo, imi munoziva nzira.”" 
John14:5 Tomasi akati kwaari, “Ishe, hatizivi pamunoenda; nzira tingaiziva seiko?”" 
John14:6 Jesu akati kwaari, “Ndini nzira, nechokwadi, noupenyu; hapana munhu unouya kuna Baba, asi nokwandiri." 
John14:7 Dai makanga muchindiziva mungadai maizivawo Baba vangu; kubva zvino munovaziva, makavaona.”" 
John14:8 Firipi akati kwaari, “Ishe, tiratidzei Baba zvigotiringana.”" 
John14:9 Jesu akati kwaari, “Ndakava nemi nguva refu yakadai, ko hausati wandiziva here, Firipi? Andiona ini, aona Baba; zvino unoreva seiko, uchiti, ‘Tiratidzei Baba?’" 
John14:10 Hautendi here kuti ndiri muna Baba naBaba vari mandiri? Mashoko andinoreva kwamuri, handiarevi pachangu; asi Baba, vanogara mandiri, ndivo vanoita mabasa avo." 
John14:11 Nditendei kuti ndiri muna Baba, naBaba vari mandiri; kana kusi kudaro, nditendei nokuda kwamabasa amene." 
John14:12 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, Anotenda kwandiri, mabasa andinoita, iye achaaitawo, achaita makuru kunaawa; nokuti ndinoenda kuna Baba." 
John14:13 Chinhu chipi nechipi chamunokumbira muzita rangu, ndichachiita, kuti Baba vakudzwe muMwanakomana." 
John14:14 Kana muchikumbira chinhu kwandiri muzita rangu, ndichachiita." 
John14:15 “Kana muchindida, muchachengeta mirairo yangu." 
John14:16 Neni ndichakumbira Baba, vachakupai mumwe Munyaradzi, kuti agare nemi nokusingaperi;" 
John14:17 ndiye Mweya wechokwadi; nyika haigoni kumugamuchira, nokuti haimuoni, kana kumuziva; imi munomuziva, nokuti agere nemi, achava mukati menyu." 
John14:18 “Handingakusiyi muri nherera; ndinouya kwamuri. 
John14:19 “Kuchine nguva duku, nyika haichazondioni; asi imi munondiona, nokuti ini ndiri mupenyu, nemiwo muchava vapenyu." 
John14:20 Nezuva iro muchandiziva, kuti ndiri muna Baba, nemi mandiri, neni mamuri." 
John14:21 “Ane mirairo yangu, akaichengeta, ndiye anondida; anondida achadikanwa naBaba vangu; neni ndichamudawo, ndichazviratidza kwaari.”" 
John14:22 Judhasi (asati ari iye Isikarioti) akati kwaari, “Ishe, ndokudiniko kuti muchazviratidza kwatiri, musingazviratidzi kunyika?”" 
John14:23 Jesu akapindura, akati kwaari, “Kana munhu achindida, achachengeta shoko rangu; naBaba vangu vachamuda, tichauya kwaari, tikaita ugaro hwedu maari." 
John14:24 Asingandidi, haachengeti mashoko angu; shoko ramunonzwa, harisi rangu, asi nderaBaba vakandituma." 
John14:25 “Zvinhu izvozvi ndakakuudzai ndichigere nemi. 
John14:26 Asi Munyaradzi, Mweya Mutsvene, achatumwa naBaba muzita rangu, iye achakudzidzisai zvose, nokukuyeuchidzai zvose, zvandakareva kwamuri." 
John14:27 “Ndinokusiyirai rugare; ndinokupai rugare rwangu; handikupiyi sokupa kwenyika. Mwoyo yenyu irege kumanikidzwa, irege kutya." 
John14:28 Makanzwa kuti ndakati kwamuri, ‘Ndinoenda, ndigodzokerazve kwamuri.’ Dai maindida, mungadai maifara, nokuti ndinoenda kuna Baba; nokuti Baba vakuru kwandiri." 
John14:29 Zvino ndakuudzai zvisati zvaitika, kuti musi wazvinoitika mugotenda." 
John14:30 Handichazotauri zvizhinji nemi, nokuti muchinda wenyika anouya; asi haana chinhu kwandiri;" 
John14:31 asi izvi zvinoitika kuti nyika izive kuti ndinoda Baba, uye kuti sezvandakarairwa naBaba, ndizvo zvandinoita. Simukai, ngatibve pano." 
John15:1 “Ndini muzambiringa wechokwadi, Baba vangu murimi." 
John15:2 Davi rimwe nerimwe riri mandiri, risingabereki michero, vanoribvisa; rimwe nerimwe, rinobereka michero, vanorinatsa, kuti riwedzere michero." 
John15:3 Imi matonatswa neshoko randakareva kwamuri. 
John15:4 Garai mandiri, neni mamuri. Sedavi risingagoni kubereka michero roga, kana risingagari mumuzambiringa; saizvozvo nemiwo, kana musingagari mandiri." 
John15:5 “Ini ndiri muzambiringa, imi muri matavi. Anogara mandiri, neni maari, ndiye anobereka michero yakawanda; nokuti kunze kwangu hamugoni kuita chinhu." 
John15:6 Kana munhu asingagari mandiri, anoraswa kunze sedavi, ndokuoma; anounganidzwa, ndokukandirwa mumoto, atsve." 
John15:7 Kana muchigara mandiri, namashoko angu achigara mamuri, kumbirai zvamunoda, muchazviitirwa." 
John15:8 Baba vangu vanokudzwa naizvozvi, kuti mubereke michero yakawanda; uye muchava vadzidzi vangu." 
John15:9 Baba sezvavakandida, neni ndakakudai; garai murudo rwangu." 
John15:10 Kana muchichengeta mirairo yangu, muchagara murudo rwangu, seni ndaichengeta mirairo yaBaba vangu, ndichigara murudo rwavo." 
John15:11 “Zvinhu izvozvi ndakazvitaura kwamuri, kuti mufaro wangu ugare mamuri, nomufaro wenyu uzadzike." 
John15:12 Uyu ndiwo murairo wangu, kuti mudane, seni ndakakudai imi." 
John15:13 Hakuna munhu ano rudo rukuru kune urwu, kuti munhu arasire hama dzake upenyu hwake." 
John15:14 Imi muri hama dzangu, kana muchiita zvandinokurayirai ini." 
John15:15 Handichakuidzii varanda; nokuti muranda haazivi zvinoitwa naishe wake; asi ndinokuidzai hama; nokuti zvose zvandakanzwa kuna Baba vangu, ndakakuzivisai izvo." 
John15:16 “Imi hamuna kundisanangura, asi ini ndakakusanangurai imi, ndikakuisai kuti muende mubereke michero, uye kuti michero yenyu igare; kuti chinhu chipi nechipi chamunenge muchikumbira kuna Baba muzita rangu, vakupei icho." 
John15:17 “Ndizvozvi zvandinokurayirai, kuti mudane." 
John15:18 “Kana nyika ichikuvengai, muzive kuti yakandivenga ini, isati yakuvengai imi." 
John15:19 Kana maiva venyika, nyika yaidana vayo; zvino zvamusati muri venyika, asi ini ndakakusanangurai panyika, saka nyika inokuvengai." 
John15:20 Rangarirai shoko randakareva kwamuri, ndichiti, ‘Muranda haasi mukuru kuna ishe wake.’ Kana vakanditambudza ini, vachakutambudzai nemiwo; kana vakachengeta shoko rangu, vachachengeta nerenyuwo." 
John15:21 Asi izvi zvose vachakuitirai nokuda kwezita rangu, nokuti havazivi akandituma." 
John15:22 Dai ndisina kuuya, ndikataura navo, vangadai vasina zvivi; asi zvino havana pembedzo yezvivi zvavo." 
John15:23 Anondivenga, anovenga naBaba vanguo." 
John15:24 “Dai ndisina kuita pakati pavo mabasa asina kumboitwa nomumwe munhu, vangadai vasina zvivi; asi zvino vakaona, nokundivenga ini naBaba vangu." 
John15:25 “Asi zvakaitwa, kuti shoko rakanyorwa mumurairo wavo, riitike, rinoti, ‘Vakandivenga ndisina mhosva.’" 
John15:26 “Kana Munyaradzi auya, wandichatuma kwamuri, achibva kuna Baba, iye Mweya wechokwadi, anobuda kuna Baba, achandipupurira." 
John15:27 Nemiwo pupurai, nokuti maiva neni kubva pakutanga." 
John16:1 “Zvinhu izvi ndakakuudzai, kuti murege kugumburwa." 
John16:2 Vachakubudisai mumasinagoge; asi nguva inosvika, mumwe nomumwe wakakuurayai, achati anobatira Mwari basa." 
John16:3 Zvinhu izvi vachaita, nokuti havana kuziva Baba, kana ini." 
John16:4 “Asi ndakakuudzai izvi, kuti kana nguva yazvo yasvika, mugozviyeuka, kuti ndakakuudzai. Handina kukuudzai izvi kubva pakutanga, nokuti ndaiva nemi." 
John16:5 Asi zvino ndinoenda kune akandituma; hakuna mumwe wenyu anondibvunza, achiti, ‘Munoendepiko?’" 
John16:6 Asi zvino mwoyo yenyu yafa neshungu zvandakakuudzai izvi. 
John16:7 Asi ini ndinokuudzai zvechokwadi, kana ndichiti, zviri nani kwamuri, kuti ndiende, nokuti kana ndisingaendi, Munyaradzi haangauyi kwamuri; asi kana ndikaenda, ndichamutumira kwamuri." 
John16:8 “Iye kana asvika achazivisa nyika pamusoro pezvivi, napamusoro pokururama, napamusoro pokutongwa;" 
John16:9 pamusoro pezvivi, nokuti havatendi kwandiri;" 
John16:10 pamusoro pokururama, nokuti ndinoenda kuna Baba, hamungazondioni;" 
John16:11 pamusoro pokutongwa, nokuti muchinda wenyika ino atongwa kare." 
John16:12 “Ndine zvizhinji zvandinoda kukuudzai; asi hamugoni kuzvigamuchira zvino. 
John16:13 “Asi kana asvika, iye Mweya wechokwadi, achakutungamirirai muchokwadi chose; nokuti haangatauri zvake, asi zvaakanzwa, ndizvo zvaachataura, uye achakuparidzirai zvinouya." 
John16:14 Achandikudza, nokuti achatora pane zvangu achikuparidzai izvo." 
John16:15 Zvose Baba zvavanazvo, ndezvangu; naizvozvo ndakati, achatora pane zvangu, achikuparidzai izvo." 
John16:16 “Chinguva chiduku chasara, hamuchazondioni; uyezve chinguva chiduku, muchandiona.”" 
John16:17 Zvino vamwe vavadzidzi vake vakataurirana, vachiti, “Chiiko ichi chaanoreva kwatiri, kuti, ‘Chinguva chiduku chasara, hamuchazondioni; uyezve, chinguva chiduku, muchandiona, uye, nokuti, ndinoenda kuna Baba?’" 
John16:18 Naizvozvo vakati, Chiiko chaanoti, ‘Chasara chinguva chiduku?’ Hatizivi chaanotaura.”" 
John16:19 Jesu akaziva kuti vanoda kumubvunza, akati kwavari, “Munobvunzana here pamusoro pechinhu ichi chandareva, ndichiti, ‘Chasara chinguva chiduku, hamuchazondioni; uyezve, chinguva chiduku, muchandiona?’" 
John16:20 “Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, mucharira nokuchema imi, asi nyika ichafara; imi muchanzwa shungu, asi shungu dzenyu dzichasanduka mufaro." 
John16:21 “Mukadzi kana achipona, anonzwa shungu, nokuti nguva yake yasvika; asi kana apona mwana, haachafungi kutambudzika, nokufara kwake nokuti munhu aponwa panyika." 
John16:22 Nemi zvino mune shungu; asi ndichakuonaizve, nomwoyo yenyu ichafara; hakuna munhu angakutorerai mufaro wenyu." 
John16:23 “Nezuva iro hamungazondibvunzi chinhu. Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwamuri, zvose zvamunenge muchakumbira kuna Baba, vachakupai izvo muzita rangu." 
John16:24 Kusvikira zvino hamuna kukumbira chinhu muzita rangu; kumbirai, muchapiwa, mufaro wenyu uzadzike." 
John16:25 “Izvi ndakataura kwamuri nemifananidzo, nguva inouya yandisingazotauri kwamuri nemifananidzo; asi ndichakuparidzira pachena zvaBaba." 
John16:26 “Nezuva iro muchakumbira muzita rangu; handikuudzii, kuti ndichakunyengeterera ini kuna Baba;" 
John16:27 nokuti Baba vemene vanokudai, nokuti makandida ini, mukatenda, kuti ini ndakabva kuna Baba." 
John16:28 Ndakabva kuna Baba, ndikauya panyika; ndinobvazve panyika, ndichienda kuna Baba.”" 
John16:29 Vadzidzi vake vakati, “Tarirai, zvino motaura pachena, hamucharevi nemifananidzo." 
John16:30 Zvino toziva, kuti munoziva zvose, hamutsvaki kuti munhu akubvunzei; tinotenda izvozvi kuti makabva kuna Mwari.”" 
John16:31 Jesu akavapindura akati, “Motenda zvino here?" 
John16:32 Tarirai, nguva inouya, yatosvika, yamuchaparadzirwa, mumwe nomumwe kune zvake mukandisiya ndiri ndoga; asi handisi ndoga, nokuti Baba vaneni." 
John16:33 Ndakareva izvozvi kwamuri, kuti muve norugare mandiri. Panyika munotambudzika; asi tsungai mwoyo, ini ndakakunda nyika.”" 
John17:1 Jesu akataura izvozvi, akatarira kudenga, akati, “Baba, nguva yasvika; kudzai Mwanakomana wenyu, kuti Mwanakomana akukudzei imi," 
John17:2 sezvamakamupa simba pamusoro pevanhu vose, kuti vose vamakamupa, avape upenyu husingaperi." 
John17:3 Upenyu husingaperi ndihwo, kuti vakuzivei imi, Mwari ari oga wechokwadi, naJesu Kristu, wamakatuma." 
John17:4 Ndakakukudzai panyika, ndapedza basa ramakandipa kuti ndiriite." 
John17:5 Zvino imi Baba, mundikudzei pamberi penyu nokukudzwa kwandaiva nako kwamuri, nyika isati yavapo." 
John17:6 “Ndakaratidza vanhu, vamakandipa panyika, zita renyu. Vakanga vari venyu, mukandipa ivo, vakachengeta shoko renyu." 
John17:7 Zvino vanoziva kuti zvose–zvose, zvamakandipa, zvinobva kwamuri." 
John17:8 Nokuti ndakavapa mashoko amakandipa, vakaagamuchira, vakaziva zvirokwazvo kuti ndakabva kwamuri, vakatenda kuti ndakatumwa nemi." 
John17:9 “Ndinovanyengeterera ivo; handinyengetereri nyika, asi ivo vamakandipa, nokuti ndivo venyu." 
John17:10 Zvose zvangu ndezvenyu, nezvenyu ndezvangu; ndakudzwa mavari." 
John17:11 Ini handichiri munyika, asi ivo vari munyika; ini ndinouya kwamuri. Baba vatsvene, muvachengete muzita renyu, ramakandipa, kuti vave vamwe, sesu." 
John17:12 Ndichiri navo, ini ndaivachengeta muzita renyu, ramakandipa; hapana mumwe wavo wakarasika, asi mwanakomana wokuraswa, kuti Rugwaro ruitike." 
John17:13 Asi zvino ndouya kwamuri; ndinotaura izvi panyika, kuti vave nomufaro wangu, wakazadzika mavari." 
John17:14 “Ini ndakavapa shoko renyu nyika ikavavenga, nokuti havasi venyika, seni ndisi wenyika." 
John17:15 Handinyengeteri kuti muvabvise panyika, asi kuti muvachengete pane wakaipa." 
John17:16 Havasi venyika, seni ndisi wenyika." 
John17:17 “Muvaite vatsvene muchokwadi; shoko renyu ichokwadi. 
John17:18 Sezvamakandituma panyika imi, saizvozvo neni ndakavatuma panyika." 
John17:19 Ndinozviita mutsvene nokuda kwavo, kuti naivo vaitwe vatsvene muchokwadi." 
John17:20 “Handinyengetereri ava bedzi, asi naivo vanotendawo kwandiri neshoko ravo," 
John17:21 kuti vose vave vamwe; semi Baba muri mandiri, neni mamuri; kuti naivo vave matiri, kuti nyika itende kuti makandituma." 
John17:22 “Neni ndakavapa kubwinya kwamakandipa; kuti vave vamwe, sesu tiri vamwe;" 
John17:23 ini mavari, nemi mandiri, vakwaniswe kuva vamwe; kuti nyika izive kuti makandituma, uye kuti makavada sezvamakandida ini." 
John17:24 “Baba ndinoda kuti avo vamakandipa, vavewo neni apo pandiri, kuti vaone kubwinya kwangu, kwamakandipa, nokuti makandida nyika isati yavambwa." 
John17:25 “Baba vakarurama, nyika haina kukuzivai; asi ini ndakakuzivai, naivava vakaziva kuti makandituma." 
John17:26 Ndakavazivisa zita renyu, uye ndicharizivisa, kuti rudo, rwamakandida narwo, ruve mavari, neni ndive mavari.”" 
John18:1 Jesu akati areva izvozvi, akabuda navadzidzi vake, akaenda mhiri kworukova runonzi Kedhironi, paiva nomunda, akapinda mauri, iye navadzidzi vake." 
John18:2 Zvino Judhasi, akamupandukira, akanga achizivawo nzvimbo iyo; nokuti Jesu kazhinji waiunganapo navadzidzi vake." 
John18:3 Naizvozvo Judhasi akatora boka ravarwi, navatariri, vaibva kuvapristi vakuru navaFarisi, akaendapo nemwenje namazhenje, nezvokurwa nazvo." 
John18:4 Zvino Jesu, zvaakanga achiziva zvose zvaifanira kumuwira, akabuda, akati kwavari, “Munotsvaka aniko?”" 
John18:5 Vakamupindura, vakati, “Jesu weNazareta.” Jesu akati kwavari, “Ndini.” NaJudhasi, akamupandukira, akanga amirewo navo." 
John18:6 Zvino akati areva kwavari, achiti, “Ndini,” vakasudurukira shure vakawira pasi." 
John18:7 Zvino akavabvunzazve, achiti, “Munotsvaka aniko?” Vakati, “Jesu weNazareta.”" 
John18:8 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Ndakuudzai, kuti ndini. Kana muchinditsvaka ini, regai ava vaende;”" 
John18:9 kuti shoko, raakareva, riitike, rokuti, “Handina kurasikirwa nomumwe kuna ivavo vamakandipa.”" 
John18:10 Zvino Simoni Petirosi, akanga ano munondo, akauvhomora, akatema muranda womupristi mukuru, akamugura nzeve yorudyi. Zita romuranda uyo rainzi Marikosi." 
John18:11 Zvino Jesu akati kuna Petirosi, “Dzorera munondo wako mumuhara; mukombe wandakapiwa naBaba, handingaunwi here?”" 
John18:12 Zvino boka ravarwi, nomukuru wechiuru chezana, navatariri vavaJudha vakabata Jesu, vakamusunga" 
John18:13 vakatanga kumuisa kuna Anasi; nokuti akanga ari tezvara waKaifasi, aiva mupristi mukuru gore iro." 
John18:14 Zvino Kaifasi ndiye akanga apa vaJudha zano, kuti zviri nani kuti munhu mumwe afire vanhu vose." 
John18:15 Zvino Simoni Petirosi akanga achitevera Jesu, nomumwe mudzidziwo. Mudzidzi uyu aizikanwa nomupristi mukuru, akapinda naJesu muruvazhe rwomupristi mukuru." 
John18:16 Asi Petirosi akanga amire panze pamusuwo. Zvino uya mumwe mudzidzi, aizikanwa nomupristi mukuru, akabuda, akataura nomurindi womusuwo, akapinza Petirosi." 
John18:17 Zvino musikana, wairinda musuwo, akati kuna Petirosi, “Newewo uri mumwe wavadzidzi vomunhu uyu here?” Akati, “Handisati.”" 
John18:18 Zvino varanda navatariri vakanga vamirepo, vambovesa moto wamazimbe, nokuti kwaitonhora; vakadziya moto. NaPetirosi akamirawo navo achidziya moto." 
John18:19 Zvino mupristi mukuru akabvunza Jesu zvavadzidzi vake, nezvokudzidzisa kwake." 
John18:20 Jesu akamupindura, akati, “Ndaitaura pachena kunyika; ndaidzidzisa nguva dzose mumasinagoge nomutemberi, panoungana vaJudha vose; handina kureva chinhu pakavanda." 
John18:21 “Munondibvunzireiko ini? Bvunzai ava vainzwa zvandaitaura kwavari; tarirai, ava vanoziva zvandaireva.”" 
John18:22 Akati areva izvozvo, mumwe wavatariri, akanga amirepo, akarova Jesu noruoko, achiti, “Unopindura mupristi mukuru uchidaro nhai?”" 
John18:23 Jesu akamupindura, akati, “Kana ndareva zvakaipa, pupura kuti zvakaipa ndezvipi; kana ndareva zvakanaka, wagondirovereiko?”" 
John18:24 Zvino Anasi akamutumira akasungwa kuna Kaifasi, Mupristi Mukuru." 
John18:25 Zvino Simoni Petirosi akanga amirepo, achidziya moto. Vakati kwaari, “Newewo uri mumwe wavadzidzi vake here?” Akaramba, akati, “Handisati.”" 
John18:26 Mumwe muranda woMupristi Mukuru, hama yowakanga agurwa nzeve naPetirosi, akati, “Ini handina kukuona unaye mumunda here?”" 
John18:27 Petirosi akarambazve. Pakarepo jongwe rikarira. 
John18:28 Zvino vakabva kuna Kaifasi, vakaenda naJesu kuimba yomubati; aiva mangwanani. Asi ivo havana kupinda mumba momubati, kuti varege kusvibiswa, kuti vagodya Pasika." 
John18:29 Ipapo Pirato akabudira kwavari, akati, “Munoti, munhu uyu ane mhosva yeiko?”" 
John18:30 Vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Dai munhu uyu asaiva mutadzi, tingadai tisina kumuisa kwamuri.”" 
John18:31 Zvino Pirato akati kwavari, “Chimutorai imi, mumutonge nomurairo wenyu.” VaJudha vakati kwaari, “Hatina kutenderwa isu kuti tiuraye munhu;”" 
John18:32 kuti shoko raJesu raakareva riitike, achidudzira kufa kwaaifanira kufa nako." 
John18:33 Zvino Pirato akapindazve mumba momubati, akadana Jesu, akati kwaari, “Ndiwe mambo wavaJudha here?”" 
John18:34 Jesu akapindura, akati, “Unozvireva izvi pachako here, kana wazviudzwa navamwe pamusoro pangu?”" 
John18:35 Pirato akapindura, akati, “Ini ndiri muJudha su? Rudzi rwako navapristi vakuru vakakuisa kwandiri; waiteiko?”" 
John18:36 Jesu akapindura akati, “Ushe hwangu hahusi hwenyika ino; dai ushe hwangu hwaiva hwenyika ino, varanda vangu vangadai vairwa, kuti ndirege kuiswa kuvaJudha; asi zvino ushe hwangu hahusi hwapano.”" 
John18:37 Ipapo Pirato akati kwaari, “Iwe uri mambo su?” Jesu akapindura akati, “Unoreva iwe kuti ndiri mambo. Ndakaberekerwa izvo, ndakauyira izvozvo panyika, kuti ndipupure chokwadi. Mumwe nomumwe wechokwadi anonzwa izwi rangu.”" 
John18:38 Pirato akati kwaari, “Chokwadi Chiiko?” Akati areva izvozvi, akabudirazve kuvaJudha, akati kwavari, “Ini handiwani mhosva kwaari." 
John18:39 Asi imi mune tsika kuti ndikusunungurirei mumwe nePasika; zvino munoda kuti ndikusunungurirei mambo wavaJudha here?” 
John18:40 Ipapo vakadanidzira vose, vachiti, “Munhu uyu kwete, asi Bharabhasi!” Zvino Bharabhasi akanga ari gororo." 
John19:1 Zvino Pirato akatora Jesu, akamurovesa." 
John19:2 Varwi vakaruka ndaza yeminzwa, vakaiisa pamusoro wake, vakamupfekedza nguo tsvuku," 
John19:3 vakauya kwaari, vachiti, “Kwaziwai, Mambo wavaJudha!” Vakamurova namaoko." 
John19:4 Ipapo Pirato akabudazve, akati kwavari, “Tarirai, ndamubudisa kwamuri, muzive kuti handiwani mhosva kwaari.”" 
John19:5 Jesu akabuda, akadzikwa ndaza yeminzwa, ane nguo tsvuku. Pirato akati kwavari, “Tarirai munhu!”" 
John19:6 Zvino vapristi vakuru navatariri vakati vachimuona vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Roverai pamuchinjikwa, roverai pamuchinjikwa!” Pirato akati kwavari, “Chimutorai imi, mumuroverere pamuchinjikwa; nokuti ini handiwani mhosva kwaari.”" 
John19:7 VaJudha vakamupindura, vakati, “Isu tine murairo, zvino nomurairo wedu anofanira kufa, nokuti akazviita Mwanakomana waMwari.”" 
John19:8 Zvino Pirato akati anzwa shoko iri, akanyanya kutya." 
John19:9 Akapindazve mumba momubati, akati kuna Jesu, “Uri wepiko?” Asi Jesu haana kumupindura." 
John19:10 Ipapo Pirato akati kwaari, “Hautauri neni here? Hauzivisu kuti ndine simba rokukusunungura, nesimba rokukurovera pamuchinjikwa?”" 
John19:11 Jesu akamupindura, akati, “Haungatongovi nesimba pamusoro pangu, kana usina kuripiwa richibva kumusoro; naizvozvo akandiisa kwauri, ane zvivi zvinokunda zvako.”" 
John19:12 Zvino Pirato akatsvaka kumusunungura; asi vaJudha vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Kana mukasunungura munhu uyu, hamusi shamwari yaKesari; mumwe nomumwe, anozviita mambo, anoramba Kesari.”" 
John19:13 Zvino Pirato akati anzwa mashoko iwayo, akabudisa Jesu, akagara pachigaro chokutonga, panzvimbo yainzi “Pakarongwa naMabwe,” asi neChiHebheru “Gabhata.”" 
John19:14 Zvino wakanga uri musi wokugadzirira Pasika; yaiva nguva inenge yechitanhatu. Akati kuvaJudha, “Tarirai Mambo wenyu!”" 
John19:15 Ivo vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Bvisai, bvisai, mumurovere pamuchinjikwa!” Pirato akati kwavari, “Ndorovera Mambo wenyu pamuchinjikwa here?” Vapristi vakuru vakapindura, vachiti, “Hatina mambo, asi Kesari chete.”" 
John19:16 Ipapo akamuisa kwavari, kuti aroverwe pamuchinjikwa. Zvino vakaenda naJesu;" 
John19:17 akabuda, achitakura muchinjikwa wake, akaenda kunzvimbo yainzi, “Dehenya,” neChiHebheru ichinzi, “Gorogota,”" 
John19:18 pavakamurovera pamuchinjikwa, navamwe vaviri naye, mumwe kune rumwe rutivi, mumwe kune rumwe rutivi, Jesu pakati." 
John19:19 Pirato akanyorawo rugwaro, pamuchinjikwa; kwakanga kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, “JESU WENAZARETA, MAMBO WAVAJUDHA.”" 
John19:20 Zvino vaJudha vazhinji vakarava rugwaro urwo; nokuti nzvimbo iyo pakanga pakaroverwa Jesu pamuchinjikwa, yaiva pedyo neguta; rwakanga rwakanyorwa neChiHebheru, nechiRoma, nechiGiriki." 
John19:21 Ipapo vapristi vakuru vavaJudha vakati kuna Pirato, “Musanyora muchiti, ‘Mambo wavaJudha,’ asi kuti, ‘Iye akati, ndiri mambo wavaJudha.’ ”" 
John19:22 Pirato akapindura, akati, “Zvandanyora, ndanyora.”" 
John19:23 Zvino varwi vakati varovera Jesu pamuchinjikwa, vakatora nguo dzake, vakaita migove mina, murwi mumwe nomumwe mugove wake; nenguo yapasiwo. Zvino nguo iyi yakanga isina pakasonwa, asi yakanga yakarukwa yose kubva kumusoro kwayo." 
John19:24 Zvino vakataurirana, vachiti, “Ngatirege kuibvarura, asi tikande mijenya pamusoro payo, tione kuti ichava yaani;” kuti Rugwaro ruitike, runoti, “Vakagovana nguo dzangu pakati pavo, Vakakanda mijenya pamusoro pechokufuka changu.” Ndizvo zvakaitwa navarwi." 
John19:25 Zvino pamuchinjikwa waJesu pakanga pamire mai vake, nomunun'una wamai vake, Maria, mukadzi waKiropasi, naMaria Magadharina." 
John19:26 Zvino Jesu akati achiona mai vake, nomudzidzi waaida, amirepo, akati kuna mai vake, “Mai tarirai, mwana wenyu.”" 
John19:27 Ipapo akati kumudzidzi, “Tarira mai vako.” Kubva panguva iyo mudzidzi akavatora, akavaisa kumba kwake." 
John19:28 Shure kwaizvozvo, Jesu akati achiziva kuti zvose zvapera, kuti Rugwaro ruitike, akati, “Ndine nyota.”" 
John19:29 Pakanga pamirepo hari izere nevhiniga; zvino vakaisa chifovefove chizere nevhiniga parutanda rwehisopi, vakaruisa kumuromo wake." 
John19:30 Zvino Jesu akati agamuchira vhiniga, akati, “Zvapera!” Akakotamisa musoro wake, akapa Mwari mweya wake." 
John19:31 Zvino zvawaiva musi woKugadzirira Pasika, vaJudha vakakumbira kuna Pirato kuti makumbo avo avhunwe, vabviswe, kuti mitumbi irege kugara pamuchinjikwa neSabata, nokuti zuva iro reSabata raiva guru." 
John19:32 Naizvozvo varwi vakauya, vakavhuna makumbo owokutanga, noomumwe akanga aroverwa pamuchinjikwa pamwechete naye;" 
John19:33 asi vakati vachisvika kuna Jesu, vachiona kuti atofa hake, havana kuvhuna makumbo ake," 
John19:34 asi mumwe murwi wakabaya rutivi rwake nepfumo, pakarepo ropa nemvura zvikabuda." 
John19:35 Uyo akaona, ndiye akapupura, uye kupupura kwake ndokwechokwadi; iye anoziva kuti anoreva zvechokwadi, kuti nemiwo mutende." 
John19:36 Nokuti izvozvo zvakaitwa, kuti Rugwaro ruitike, runoti, “Pfupa rake haringavhunwi.”" 
John19:37 Norumwe Rugwaro runoti, “Vachatarira uyo wavakabowora.”" 
John19:38 Shure kwaizvozvo Josefa weArimatia, aiva mudzidzi waJesu, asi chinyararire nokutya vaJudha, akakumbira kuna Pirato kuti abvise chitunha chaJesu; Pirato akamutendera. Ipapo akauya, akabvisa chitunha chake." 
John19:39 NaNikodhimowo, iye akambouya kwaari pakutanga usiku, akauya ane mura nearosi zvakavhenganiswa, mapaundi anenge zana." 
John19:40 Ipapo vakatora chitunha chaJesu, vakachiputira nemicheka pamwechete nezvinonhuwira, sezvinoita vaJudha pakuviga kwavo." 
John19:41 Panzvimbo iyo, paakaroverwa pamuchinjikwa, pakanga pano munda; mumunda imomo maiva nohwiro hutsva, makanga musina kumboiswa munhu." 
John19:42 Zvino vakaisa Jesu ipapo, zvawakanga uri musi woKugadzirira kwavaJudha, (nokuti hwiro hwakanga huri pedyo.)" 
John20:1 Zvino nomusi wokutanga wevhiki Maria Magadharina akaenda kuhwiro mangwanani kuchakasviba; akaona ibwe rabviswa pahwiro. 
John20:2 Akamhanya, akaenda kuna Simoni Petirosi nokuno mumwe mudzidzi, aidikanwa naJesu, akati kwavari, “Vabvisa Ishe muhwiro, hatizivi pavakamuisa.”" 
John20:3 Zvino Petirosi akabuda nouya mumwe mudzidzi, vakaenda kuhwiro." 
John20:4 Vakamhanya vose vari vaviri; uya mumwe mudzidzi akamhanyisa akakunda Petirosi, akatanga kusvika pahwiro," 
John20:5 akakotama achidongorera, akaona micheka iri pasi, asi haana kupinda." 
John20:6 Zvino Simoni Petirosi akasvikawo, akapinda muhwiro, akaona micheka iri pasi;" 
John20:7 nomucheka muduku, wakanga uri mumusoro wake, usati uri kune mimwe micheka, asi wakapetwa uri pamwe woga." 
John20:8 Zvino uye mumwe mudzidzi akapindawo, iye akatanga kusvika pahwiro, akaona, akatenda." 
John20:9 Nokuti vakanga vachigere kunzwisisa Rugwaro, runoti anofanira kumuka kuvakafa." 
John20:10 Zvino vadzidzi vakadzokerazve kumusha kwavo. 
John20:11 Asi Maria akaramba amire kunze kwehwiro, achichema; zvino achichema, akakotama, akadongorera muhwiro." 
John20:12 Akaona vatumwa vaviri, vane nguo chena, vagere mumwe kumusoro, mumwe kumakumbo, ipapo pakanga paiswa chitunha chaJesu." 
John20:13 Ivo vakati kwaari, “Mai, munochemeiko?” Akati kwavari, “Nokuti vakabvisa Ishe wangu, zvino handizivi kwavakamuisa.”" 
John20:14 Zvino akati achireva izvozvo, akatendeukira shure, akaona Jesu amire; asi haana kuziva kuti ndiJesu." 
John20:15 Jesu akati kwaari, “Mai, munochemeiko? Munotsvaka aniko?” Iye achiti ndiye murimi womunda, akati kwaari, “Ishe, kana muri imi mamubvisa, ndiudzei pamamuisa, ndindomutora.”" 
John20:16 Jesu akati kwaari, “Maria!” Iye akatendeuka, akati kwaari neChiHebheru, “Rabhoni;” ndokuti, “Mudzidzisi.”" 
John20:17 Jesu akati kwaari, “Usandibata, nokuti ndichigere kukwira kuna Baba vangu; asi enda kuhama dzangu, uti kwavari, ndinokwira kuna Baba vangu naBaba venyu, kuna Mwari wangu naMwari wenyu.”" 
John20:18 Maria Magadharina akaenda, akaudza vadzidzi, achiti, “Ndaona Ishe,” uye kuti akanga audzwa zvinhu izvi naye." 
John20:19 Zvino ava madeko pazuva iro rokutanga revhiki, misuwo yapfigwa pavakanga vari vadzidzi nokutya vaJudha, Jesu akauya, akamira pakati pavo, akati kwavari, “Rugare kwamuri!”" 
John20:20 Zvino akati areva izvozvo, akavaratidza zvanza zvake norutivi rwake. Vadzidzi vakafara vachiona Ishe." 
John20:21 Jesu akatizve kwavari, “Rugare kwamuri! Baba sezvavakandituma, neni ndinokutumaiwo.”" 
John20:22 Zvino akati areva izvozvo, akafemera kwavari, akati kwavari, “Gamuchirai Mweya Mutsvene." 
John20:23 Avo, vanoregerera zvivi zvavo, varegererwa; avo, vamunobata zvivi zvavo, zvabatwa.”" 
John20:24 Zvino Tomasi, ainzi Dhidhimo, mumwe wavane gumi navaviri, akanga asipo, pakuuya kwaJesu." 
John20:25 Zvino vamwe vadzidzi vakati kwaari, “Taona Ishe.” Iye akati kwavari, “Kana ndikasaona mavanga embambo muzvanza zvake, nokuisa munwe wangu paiva nembambo, nokuisa ruoko rwangu murutivi rwake, handingatongotendi.”" 
John20:26 Zvino mazuva masere akati apfuurazve, vadzidzi vakanga varimo mukati, naTomasi anavo. Jesu akauya, misuwo yapfigwa, akamira pakati pavo, akati, “Rugare kwamuri!”" 
John20:27 Ipapo akati kuna Tomasi, “Uya pano nomunwe wako, uone zvanza zvangu; uya noruoko rwako, uruise murutivi rwangu; usava usingatendi, asi unotenda.”" 
John20:28 Tomasi akapindura, akati kwaari, “Ishe wangu, naMwari wangu!”" 
John20:29 Jesu akati kwaari, “Watenda, nokuti wandiona? Vacharopafadzwa vanotenda, kunyangwe vasina kuona.”" 
John20:30 Zvino Jesu akaita zvimwe zviratidzo zvizhinji pamberi pavadzidzi vake, zvisina kunyorwa mubhuku iyi;" 
John20:31 asi izvi zvakanyorwa, kuti mutende kuti Jesu ndiye Kristu Mwanakomana waMwari; uye kuti, muchitenda, muve noupenyu muzita rake." 
John21:1 Shure kwaizvozvo Jesu akazviratidzazve kuvadzidzi vake pagungwa reTibheriasi; akazviratidza kudai: 
John21:2 VanaSimoni Petirosi, naTomasi, ainzi Dhidhimo, naNataneri, weKana yeGareriya, navanakomana vaZebhedhi, navamwe vaviri vadzidzi vake, vakanga vari pamwechete." 
John21:3 Simoni Petirosi akati kwavari, “Ndonobata hove.” Vakati kwaari, “Nesu tinoendawo newe.” Vakabuda, vakapinda muigwa; asi usiku uhwo havana kubata chinhu." 
John21:4 Zvino kwakati kwaedza, Jesu akamira pamhenderekedzo, asi vadzidzi vakanga vasingazivi kuti ndiJesu." 
John21:5 Zvino Jesu akati kwavari, “Vana, mune hove here?” Vakamupindura, vachiti, “Kwete.”" 
John21:6 Akati kwavari, “Kandai usvasvi kurutivi rworudyi rwegwa mugowana.” Ipapo vakakanda, vakasagona zvino kuhukweva nokuwanda kwehove." 
John21:7 Zvino mudzidzi uya, aidikanwa naJesu, akati kuna Petirosi, “NdiIshe.” Ipapo Simoni Petirosi akati achinzwa kuti ndiIshe, akasunga nguo yake, nokuti akanga asina, akazviwisira mugungwa." 
John21:8 Asi vamwe vadzidzi vakauya nekagwa, vachikweva usvasvi hune hove, nokuti vakanga vasiri kure nenyika asi makubhiti anenge mazana maviri." 
John21:9 Zvino vakati vasvika panyika, vakaona moto wamazimbe waveswa, nehove yakaiswa pamusoro pawo, nechingwa." 
John21:10 Jesu akati kwavari, “Uyai nedzimwe hove dzamakabata zvino.”" 
John21:11 Simoni akakwira muigwa, akakwevera usvasvi kumucheto, hwakanga huzere nehove huru, zana namakumi mashanu nenhatu; asi kunyangwe dzaiva zhinji dzikadai usvasvi hahuna kubvaruka." 
John21:12 Jesu akati kwavari, “Uyai, musvusvure.” Kwakanga kusina mumwe wavadzidzi vake akatsunga kumubvunza, kuti, “Ndimi aniko?” Vachiziva kuti ndiye Ishe." 
John21:13 Zvino Jesu akaenda, akatora chingwa, akavapa, nehovewo saizvozvo." 
John21:14 Urwu rwaiva rwechitatu, Jesu rwaakazviratidza kuvadzidzi vake amuka kuvakafa." 
John21:15 Zvino vakati vasvusvura, Jesu akati kuna Simoni Petirosi, “Simoni, mwanakomana waJona uno rudo neni kupfuura ava here?” Akati kwaari, “Hongu, Ishe; munoziva kuti ndinokudai.” Jesu akati kwaari, “Fudza hwayana dzangu.”" 
John21:16 Akati kwaarizve rwechipiri, “Simoni, mwanakomana waJona, une rudo neni here?” Akati kwaari, “Hongu, Ishe; munoziva kuti ndinokudai.” Jesu akati kwaari, “Chengeta makwai angu.”" 
John21:17 Akati kwaari rwechitatu, “Simoni, mwanakomana waJona, Unondida here?” Petirosi akarwadziwa mwoyo, nokuti akati kwaari rwechitatu, “Unondida here?” Akati kwaari, “Ishe, munoziva zvose; munoziva kuti ndinokudai.” Jesu akati kwaari, “Fudza hwai dzangu." 
John21:18 Zvirokwazvo, zvirokwazvo, ndinoti kwauri, uchiri jaya, waizvisunga chiuno, uchifamba kwawaida; asi kana wakwegura, uchatambanudza maoko ako, mumwe achakusunga chiuno, achikuisa kwausingadi.”" 
John21:19 Akareva izvozvo, achifananidza kufa kwaaizokudza Mwari nako. Zvino akati areva izvozvo, akati kwaari, “Nditevere.”" 
John21:20 Petirosi akatendeuka, akaona uya mudzidzi, aidikanwa naJesu, achitevera; ndiyewo akasendamira pachipfuva chake pachirariro, achiti, “Ishe, ndianiko achakupandukirai?”" 
John21:21 Zvino Petirosi akati achimuona, akati kuna Jesu, “Ishe, ko uyu uchaitweiko?”" 
John21:22 Jesu akati kwaari, “Kana ndikada kuti agare kusvikira ndichiuya, uneiko nazvo iwe? Unditevere iwe.”" 
John21:23 Zvino shoko iro rakapararira pakati pehama, kuti mudzidzi uyu haangazofi. Asi Jesu haana kureva kwaari, kuti haangazofi, asi kuti, “Kana ndikada kuti agare kusvikira ndichiuya, uneiko nazvo iwe?”" 
John21:24 Ndiwoyu mudzidzi anopupura izvozvi, wakazvinyorawo; tinoziva kuti kupupura kwake ndokwechokwadi." 
John21:25 Zvimwe zvizhinji zviriko zvakaitwawo naJesu; kana zvainyorwa chimwe nechimwe, ndinoti kunyangwe nenyika yose haingaringani bhuku dzinganyorwa." 
Acts1:1 Teofiro, ndakanyora rugwaro rwokutanga rwezvose zvakatanga kuitwa nokudzidziswa naJesu," 
Acts1:2 kusvikira zuva raakakwidzwa, amborayira naMweya Mutsvene vapostori vaakanga atsanangura." 
Acts1:3 Akazviratidzawo kwavari nezviratidzo zvizhinji, ari mupenyu, shure kwokutambudzika kwake, achionekwa navo mazuva ana makumi mana, achitaura zvoushe hwaMwari;" 
Acts1:4 akavaraira, aungana navo, kuti varege kubva Jerusaremu, asi vagarire chipikirwa chaBaba, achiti, chiya chamakanzwa kwandiri;" 
Acts1:5 nokuti Johani, zvirokwazvo, akabhabhatidza nemvura; asi imi muchabhabhatidzwa naMweya Mutsvene, mazuva mazhinji asati apera." 
Acts1:6 Zvino ivo, vakati vaungana, vakamubvunza, vachiti, “Ishe, modzosera ushe kuna VaIsiraeri nenguva ino here?”" 
Acts1:7 Akati kwavari, “Hazvina kufanira kuti muzive nguva kana misi yakatarwa naBaba vomene nesimba ravo." 
Acts1:8 Asi muchapiwa simba, kana Mweya Mutsvene auya pamusoro penyu; ipapo muchava zvapupu zvangu muJerusaremu, nomuJudhiya yose, nomuSamaria, kusvikira kumugumo wenyika.”" 
Acts1:9 Zvino akati areva izvozvi, akakwidzwa, vachitaririra; gore rikamubvisa, vakasazomuona." 
Acts1:10 Zvino vachitarisisa kudenga, iye achikwira, tarira, varume vaviri vamira navo vakafuka nguo chena;" 
Acts1:11 ivo vakati, “Imi varume veGareriya, makamirireiko makatarira kudenga? Uyu Jesu, akabva kwamuri, akakwidzwa kudenga, achauya saizvozvo, sezvamamuona achienda kudenga.”" 
Acts1:12 Zvino vakadzokera Jerusaremu, vachibva pagomo rinonzi reMiorivhi, riri pedyo neJerusaremu, nhambo yorwendo rweSabata." 
Acts1:13 Vakati vapinda, vakakwira muimba yaiva pamusoro, pavakanga vagere, vaiti: Petirosi, naJohani, naJokobho, naAndireya, naFiripi, naTomasi, naBhatoromiyo, naMateu, naJakobho, mwanakomana waArifeusi, naSimoni Zeroti, naJudhasi, mwanakomana waJakobho." 
Acts1:14 Ava vose vakatsungirira nomwoyo mumwe pakunyengetera, vana vakadzi, naMaria, mai vaJesu, navanun'una vake." 
Acts1:15 Namazuva iwayo Petirosi akasimuka pakati pehama, vanhu vazhinji vaivapo pamwechete, vanenge zana namakumi maviri, akati," 
Acts1:16 “Varume, hama, rugwaro rwakafanira kuitika, rwakaporofitwa naMweya Mutsvene nomuromo waDhavhidhi, pamusoro paJudhasi, akanga ari muperekedzi wavaya vakabata Jesu." 
Acts1:17 Nokuti akanga averengwa pamwechete nesu, akapiwa mugove wake pabasa iri.”" 
Acts1:18 Zvino munhu uyu akatenga munda nomubairo wezvisakarurama, akawira pasi nechiso, akaputika napakati, ura hwake hukabuda hwose." 
Acts1:19 Zvikanzwika navose vaigara Jerusaremu; naizvozvo munda uyu ukatumidzwa Akeridhama norurimi rwavo, ndokuti, “Munda weropa.”" 
Acts1:20 “Nokuti mubhuku raMapisarema makanyorwa, zvichinzi, ‘Musha wake ngauitwe dongo, Kurege kuva nomunhu anogaramo;’ ‘Uye mumwe ngaapinde pautariri hwake.’" 
Acts1:21 “Zvino pakati pavarume vaiungana nesu nguva yose, Ishe Jesu yaakapinda nokubuda nayo pakati pedu," 
Acts1:22 kutanga pakubhabhatidza kwaJohani, kusvikira pazuva raakabva kwatiri, achikwidzwa, mumwe wavo anofanira kuva chapupu chokumuka kwake pamwechete nesu.”" 
Acts1:23 Zvino vakaisapo vaviri, vaiti: Josefa, ainzi Bhasabhasi, akatumidzwawo Jusuto, naMatia." 
Acts1:24 Vakanyengetera, vachiti, “Imi Ishe, munoziva mwoyo yavanhu vose, ratidzai kuti wamakatsanangura kuna ivava vaviri ndoupi;" 
Acts1:25 kuti apiwe nzvimbo pabasa iri noupostori uhwu, hwaakarasikirwa nahwo iye Judhasi, kuti iye aende kunzvimbo yake.”" 
Acts1:26 Zvino vakavakandira mijenya, mujenya ukabata Matia; iye akaverengwa pamwechete navapostori vane gumi nomumwe." 
Acts2:1 Zvino zuva rePendekositi rakati rasvika, vakanga vakaungana vose pamwechete panzvimbo imwechete." 
Acts2:2 Pakarepo kutinhira sokwemhepo inovhuvhuta nesimba kwakabva kudenga, kukazadza imba yose mavakanga vagere." 
Acts2:3 Vakaonawo marimi achiparadzana, anenge emoto; ndokumhara pamusoro womumwe nomumwe wavo." 
Acts2:4 Vose vakazadzwa naMweya Mutsvene, vakatanga kutaura nedzimwe ndimi, pavakapiwa napo naMweya kureva." 
Acts2:5 Zvino paJerusaremu pakanga pagere vaJudha, varume vakarurama, vaibva kumarudzi ose pasi pedenga." 
Acts2:6 Zvino kutinhira uku kwakati kwanzwika, vanhu vazhinji vakaungana, vakakanganiswa, nokuti mumwe nomumwe akavanzwa, vachitaura norurimi rwake." 
Acts2:7 Vakakatyamara vose, nokushamiswa, vachiti, “Tarirai, ava vose vanotaura havazi vaGareriya here?" 
Acts2:8 Zvino tinogovanzwa seiko mumwe nomumwe norurimi rwedu, rwatakaberekwa narwo?" 
Acts2:9 VaPatiya, navaMidhia, navaEramu, navanogara Mesopotamia, neJudhiya, neKapadhosia, nePondusi, neEzhia," 
Acts2:10 neFirigia, nePamufiria, neIjipiti, namativi enyika dzeRibhia, dziri pedyo neKurine, navaeni vabva Roma, navaJudha, vanyakupandukira kuchipinda," 
Acts2:11 navaKiriti, navaArabhia, tinovanzwa vachitaura nendimi dzedu mabasa makuru aMwari.”" 
Acts2:12 Vakakatyamara vose, vakakanganiswa, ndokutaurirana, vachiti, “Izvi zvinoti kudiniko?”" 
Acts2:13 Asi vamwe vakaseka, vachiti, “Vaguta waini itsva.”" 
Acts2:14 Zvino Petirosi amire navane gumi nomumwe, akadanidzira, akaparidza kwavari, achiti, “Varume veJudhiya, nemi mose mugere Jerusaremu, chinhu ichi ngachizikanwe nemi, muteerere mashoko angu," 
Acts2:15 nokuti ava havana kubatwa, sezvamunofunga imi, zvaichiri nguva yechitanhatu yezuva," 
Acts2:16 asi ichi ndicho chakarehwa nomuporofita Joeri achiti," 
Acts2:17 ‘Mwari anoti, namazuva okupedzisira, Ndichadurura Mweya wangu pamusoro penyama yose; Vanakomana venyu navanasikana venyu vachaporofita; Majaya enyu achaona zviratidzo, Navatana venyu vacharota hope." 
Acts2:18 Napamusoro pavaranda vangu napamusoro pavashandiri vangu, Ndichadurura Mweya wangu namazuva iwayo; vachaporofita." 
Acts2:19 Ndichaita zvinoshamisa kudenga kumusoro, Nezviratidzo pasi pano; Ropa, nomoto, nemhute yohutsi." 
Acts2:20 Zuva richashandurwa rima, Nomwedzi uchashandurwa ropa. Zuva guru raIshe rinobwinya risati rasvika.’" 
Acts2:21 “Zvino kuchaitika kuti ani naani anodana zita raIshe achaponeswa. 
Acts2:22 Varume veIsiraeri, donzwai mashoko awa, Jesu weNazareta, murume akaratidzwa naMwari kwamuri namabasa esimba, nezvishamiso, nezviratidzo zvakaitwa naMwari pakati penyu naye, sezvamunoziva imi mumene;" 
Acts2:23 iye, akaiswa kwamuri nomutemo nokuziva zviri mberi kwaMwari, imi makamurovera pamuchinjikwa, mukamuuraya namaoko avanhu vasingateereri murairo;" 
Acts2:24 iye akamutswa naMwari, amusunungura pakurwadziwa kworufu; nokuti zvakanga zvisingabviri kuti abatwe narwo." 
Acts2:25 Nokuti Dhavhidhi akataura pamusoro pake, achiti, ‘Ndakaona Ishe pamberi pangu misi yose, Nokuti ari kurudyi rwangu, kuti ndirege kuzununguswa." 
Acts2:26 Naizvozvo mwoyo wangu wakafara, norurimi rwangu rwakafarisisa; Uyezve, nenyama yangu ichazorora netariro." 
Acts2:27 Nokuti hamungasiyi mweya wangu muHadhesi; Hamungaisi Mutsvene wenyu kuti aone kuora. 
Acts2:28 Makandizivisa nzira dzoupenyu; Muchandizadzisa nomufaro ndichiona chiso chenyu.’ 
Acts2:29 “Varume, hama, ndingakuudzai pachena zvatateguru Dhavhidhi, kuti vakafa, vakavigwa, hwiro hwavo huri pakati pedu kusvikira nhasi." 
Acts2:30 Zvino zvaakanga ari muporofita, achizivawo kuti Mwari akamupikira nemhiko kuti achagadza pachigaro chake choushe mumwe wezvibereko zvechiuno chake," 
Acts2:31 zvaaiona zviri mberi, akareva pamusoro pokumuka kwaKristu, kuti haana kuora." 
Acts2:32 Uyu Jesu akamutswa naMwari, isu tiri zvapupu zvake tose." 
Acts2:33 “Zvino akati asimudzirwa kurudyi rwaMwari, apiwa naBaba chipikirwa chaMweya Mutsvene, akadurura izvi zvamunoona nezvamunonzwa." 
Acts2:34 Nokuti Dhavhidhi haana kukwira kudenga, asi anoti amene, ‘Ishe akati kuna Ishe wangu, Gara kurudyi rwangu," 
Acts2:35 Kusvikira ndichiita vavengi vako vave chitsiko chetsoka dzako.’ 
Acts2:36 “Zvino imba yose yaVaIsiraeri ngaizive kwazvo, kuti uyu Jesu wamakarovera pamuchinjikwa, Mwari akamuita Ishe naKristu.”" 
Acts2:37 Zvino vakati vachinzwa izvozvo, vakabayiwa pamwoyo, vakati kuna Petirosi nokuna vamwe vapostori, “Varume, hama, tichaiteiko?”" 
Acts2:38 Petirosi akati kwavari, “Tendeukai, mumwe nomumwe wenyu abhabhatidzwe nezita raJesu, kuti muregererwe zvivi, mupiwe chipikirwa choMweya Mutsvene." 
Acts2:39 Nokuti chipikirwa ndechenyu, navana venyu, navose vari kure, vanozodanwa naIshe, Mwari wedu.”" 
Acts2:40 Akapupura kwazvo namamwe mashoko mazhinji, akavaraira, achiti, “Muzviponese parudzi urwu rwakakombama.”" 
Acts2:41 Zvino avo vakagamuchira shoko rake, vakabhabhatidzwa; nezuva iro vanhu vanenge zviuru zvitatu vakawedzerwa." 
Acts2:42 Vakatsungirira pakudzidzisa kwavapostori, napakuyanana kwavo, napakumedura chingwa, napaminyengetero." 
Acts2:43 Vanhu vose vakabatwa nokutya; zvinoshamisa zvizhinji nezviratidzo zvikaitwa navapostori. 
Acts2:44 Navaitenda vose, vaiva pamwechete, vakati zvinhu zvose ndezvavose;" 
Acts2:45 vakatengesa pfuma yavo nenhumbi, vakagovana navose, mumwe nomumwe paakashayiwa napo." 
Acts2:46 Zuva rimwe nerimwe vakanga vachitsungirira mutemberi nomwoyo mumwe, vachimedura chingwa mudzimba dzavo, vachidya zvokudya zvavo nomufaro nomwoyo wakanaka," 
Acts2:47 vachirumbidza Mwari, vachidikanwa navanhu vose. Ishe akawedzera kwavari zuva rimwe nerimwe avo vaiponeswa." 
Acts3:1 Zvino Petirosi naJohani vakakwira kutemberi nenguva yokunyengetera yepfumbamwe. 
Acts3:2 Zvino mumwe murume, chirema kubva padumbu ramai vake, akanga achitakurwa; vaimuisa zuva rimwe nerimwe pamusuwo wetemberi, wainzi Wakanaka, kuti akumbire zvipo kuna vaipinda mutemberi." 
Acts3:3 Iye akati achiona Petirosi naJohani voda kupinda mutemberi, akakumbira kuti apiwe chipo." 
Acts3:4 Zvino Petirosi akamutarisisa, naJohaniwo, akati, “Titarire.”" 
Acts3:5 Akavatarira, achiti ndichapiwa chinhu navo." 
Acts3:6 Asi Petirosi akati, “Sirivha nendarama handina; asi chandinacho ndinokupai. Nezita raJesu weNazareta, chifamba.”" 
Acts3:7 Akamubata ruoko rworudyi, akamusimudza; pakarepo tsoka dzake nezviziso zvetsoka dzake zvakasimba." 
Acts3:8 Akakwakuka, akamira, ndokufamba; ndokupinda navo mutemberi, akafamba achipembera, achirumbidza Mwari." 
Acts3:9 Vanhu vose vakamuona achifamba, achirumbidza Mwari." 
Acts3:10 Vakamuziva, kuti ndiye aigarira zvipo pamusuwo Wakanaka wetemberi; vakakatyamara zvikuru nokushamiswa nezvaakaitirwa." 
Acts3:11 Zvino akati achakabata Petirosi naJohani, vanhu vose vakamhanyira kwavari pabiravira, rainzi raSoromoni, vakashamiswa kwazvo." 
Acts3:12 Zvino Petirosi akati achiona izvozvo, akapindura vanhu, akati, “Varume VaIsiraeri, mashamiswa neiko pamusoro pouyu? Munotitarisisa neiko, setinenge tamufambisa nesimba redu, kana nokunamata kwedu Mwari?" 
Acts3:13 Mwari waAbhurahamu, nowaIsaka, nowaJakobho, Mwari wamadzibaba edu, ndiye akakudza Muranda wake Jesu, amakaisa kuvatongi mukaramba pamberi paPirato, iye atonga kuti asunungurwe." 
Acts3:14 Asi imi makaramba uyo Mutsvene, akarurama, mukakumbira kuti mupiwe muurayi;" 
Acts3:15 mukauraya Muvambi woupenyu; iye akamutswa naMwari kuvakafa; iye, watiri zvapupu zvake isu." 
Acts3:16 Nokutenda kuzita rake, zita rake rakasimbisa munhu uyu wamunoona, nowamunoziva; uye, kutenda kunobva kwaari, ndiko kwakamuporesa zvakanaka kudai pamberi penyu mose." 
Acts3:17 “Asi zvino, hama dzangu, ndinoziva kuti makazviita nokusaziva, savabati venyuwo;" 
Acts3:18 asi saizvozvo Mwari akapedzisa zvaakamboreva nomuromo wavaporofita vose, kuti Kristu wake achazotambudzika." 
Acts3:19 Naizvozvo tendeukai, mudzoke, kuti zvivi zvenyu zvidzimwe, kuti nguva dzokusimbiswa dzinobva kuna Ishe, dzisvike;" 
Acts3:20 atume Kristu, iye Jesu, akagadzwa kare nokuda kwenyu;" 
Acts3:21 iye anofanira kugamuchirwa kudenga kusvikira nguva yokugadzirwa kwezvinhu zvose, yakarehwa naMwari nomuromo wavaporofita vake vatsvene kubva pakutanga." 
Acts3:22 Nokuti Mosesi akati, ‘Ishe, Mwari wenyu, achakumutsirai Muporofita pakati pehama dzenyu, akafanana neni; muchamuteerera pana zvose, zvaanotaura kwamuri." 
Acts3:23 Zvino mumwe nomumwe kana asingateereri Muporofita uyo, achaparadzwa kwazvo pakati pavanhu.’" 
Acts3:24 Navaporofita vose kubva kuna Samueri, navakamutevera, naivo vose vakataura nokuparidza zvamazuva ano." 
Acts3:25 Imi muri vana vavaporofita, navesungano, yakaitwa naMwari namadzibaba enyu, achiti kuna Abhurahamu, ‘Marudzi ose enyika acharopafadzwa muvana vako.’" 
Acts3:26 Mwari akatanga kukumutsirai imi Muranda wake, akamutuma kukuropafadzai, achidzora mumwe nomumwe wenyu pazvakaipa zvenyu.”" 
Acts4:1 Vakati vachataura navanhu, vapristi nomukuru wetemberi navaSadhusi vakauya kwavari," 
Acts4:2 vafa neshungu, nokuti vakanga vachidzidzisa vanhu, vachiparidza kumuka kwavakafa muna Jesu." 
Acts4:3 Vakavabata, vakavaisa mutorongo kusvikira mangwana; nokuti akanga ava madekwana." 
Acts4:4 Asi vazhinji kuna vakanzwa shoko vakatenda; varume vakazosvika zviuru zvinenge zvishanu pakuverengwa kwavo. 
Acts4:5 Zvino fume mangwana vabati vavo, navakuru, navanyori vakaungana paJerusaremu;" 
Acts4:6 naAnasi, mupristi mukuru, naKaifasi, naJohani, naArekizanda, nehama dzose dzoMupristi Mukuru," 
Acts4:7 vakavaisa pakati pavo, vakavabvunzisisa, vachiti, “Makazviita izvozvi nesimba rei, kana nezita ripiko?”" 
Acts4:8 Zvino Petirosi, azere naMweya Mutsvene, akati kwavari, “Imi vabati vavanhu," 
Acts4:9 kana tikabvunzwa nhasi pamusoro pebasa rakanaka, rakaitirwa munhu chirema, napaakaponeswa napo;" 
Acts4:10 muzive imi mose, navanhu vose VaIsiraeri, kuti nezita raJesu Kristu weNazareta, wamakarovera pamuchinjikwa, iye akamutswa naMwari kuvakafa, nezita iri munhu uyu amire pano pamberi penyu apora." 
Acts4:11 Ndiye ibwe rakazvidzwa nemi vavaki, rikaitwa musoro wekona." 
Acts4:12 Nokuti hakuna kuponeswa kuno mumwe; nokuti hakuna nerimwe zita pasi pedenga, rakapiwa pakati pavanhu, ratingasunungurwa naro.”" 
Acts4:13 Zvino vakati vachiona kusatya kwaPetirosi naJohani, vachinzwisisa kuti vaiva vanhu vasina kudzidza, vasingazivi chinhu, vakashamiswa; vakavaziva kuti vaiva naJesu." 
Acts4:14 Vakaonawo munhu, akanga aporeswa, amire navo, vakashayiwa chavangapindura nacho." 
Acts4:15 Zvino vakati vavarayira kuti vabude paungano, vakarangana pakati pavo," 
Acts4:16 vachiti, “Vanhu ava tichavaita seiko? Nokuti vanhu vose vagere Jerusaremu vaona kwazvo kuti chiratidzo chaitwa navo; hatigoni kuramba isu." 
Acts4:17 Asi ngativanyevere kuti varege kuzotaura nomunhu upi noupi nezita iri, kuti zvirege kuramba zvichaparadzirwa pakati pavanhu.”" 
Acts4:18 Vakavadana vakavarayira kuti varege chose kutaura kana kudzidzisa nezita raJesu. 
Acts4:19 Asi Petirosi naJohani vakapindura, vakati kwaari, “Tongai henyu imi, kana zvingava zvakarurama pamberi paMwari, kuti titeerere imi kupfuura Mwari." 
Acts4:20 Nokuti hatigoni kurega kutaura zvatakaona, nezvatakanzwa.”" 
Acts4:21 Zvino vakati vawedzera kuvanyevera, vakavaregedza, vasingawani mhosva yavangavarova nayo nokuda kwavanhu; nokuti vose vairumbidza Mwari pamusoro pezvakaitwa;" 
Acts4:22 nokuti munhu akanga aitirwa chiratidzo ichi akanga ana makore makumi mana ane mirawudzo. 
Acts4:23 Vakati varegedzwa, vakaenda kunovokwavo, vakandovaudza zvose zvavakanga vaudzwa navapristi vakuru navakuru." 
Acts4:24 Ivo vakati vazvinzwa, vakadana kuna Mwari nomwoyo mumwe, vachiti, “Tenzi, ndimi makaita denga napasi, negungwa, nezvose, zviri mukati mazvo;" 
Acts4:25 makareva naMweya Mutsvene, nomuromo waBaba vedu Dhavhidhi, muranda wenyu, muchiti, ‘Vahedheni vakaitireiko hasha, Navanhu vakafungireiko zvisina maturo?" 
Acts4:26 Madzimambo enyika akamuka, Navabati vakaungana pamwechete, Kurwa naIshe naKristu wake.’" 
Acts4:27 “Nokuti zvirokwazvo Herodhi, naPontio Pirato, navahedheni, navanhu VaIsiraeri vakaunganira muguta iri, kuzorwa naJesu Muranda wenyu mutsvene, wamakazodza;" 
Acts4:28 kuti vaite zvose zvakanga zvatemwa noruoko rwenyu, napakufunga kwenyu, kuti zviitwe." 
Acts4:29 Zvino, Ishe, tarirai kunyevera kwavo, mubatsire varanda venyu kuti vataure shoko renyu vasingatyi," 
Acts4:30 mutambanudze ruoko rwenyu kuzoporesa; nezviratidzo nezvishamiso zviitwe nezita raJesu, Muranda wenyu mutsvene.”" 
Acts4:31 Zvino vakati vanyengetera, nzvimbo yavakanga vakaungana ikazununguswa; vakazadzwa vose naMweya Mutsvene, vakataura shoko raMwari vasingatyi." 
Acts4:32 Zvino vazhinji vose vavaitenda vaiva nomwoyo mumwe nomweya mumwe; kwakanga kusina mumwe aiti chimwe chaaiva nacho ndechake, asi zvinhu zvose vakati ndezvavose." 
Acts4:33 Vapostori vaipupurira kumuka kwaJesu nesimba guru; nyasha huru ikavapo pamusoro pavo vose. 
Acts4:34 Nokuti pakanga pasina aishaiwa pakati pavo, nokuti vose vaiva neminda kana dzimba, vakazvitengesa, vakauya nomutengo wezvakatengeswa," 
Acts4:35 vakazviisa pamberi pavapostori; mumwe nomumwe akagoverwa paakashayiwa napo. 
Acts4:36 NaJosefa, akatumidzwa navapostori achinzi Bhanabhasi, ndokuti, “Mwanakomana wokunyaradza, kana zvichishandurwa,” muRevhi, munhu weSaipurasi parudzi rwake," 
Acts4:37 aiva nomunda; akautengesa, akauya nemari, akaiisa pamberi pavapostori." 
Acts5:1 Zvino mumwe murume, ainzi Ananiasi, akatengesa pfuma yake, ana Safira mukadzi wake," 
Acts5:2 akazvikamurira zvimwe pamutengo, mukadzi wake achizivawo, akauya nomumwe mugove, ndokuuisa pamberi pavapostori." 
Acts5:3 Asi Petirosi akati, “Ananiasi, Satani wazadzireiko mwoyo wako, kuti ureve nhema kuMweya Mutsvene, nokuzvikamurira zvimwe pamutengo womunda?" 
Acts5:4 Iwo uchiripo, wakanga usi wako here? Watengeswa, wakanga usina simba nazvo here? Waita seiko, zvawafunga chinhu ichi mumwoyo mako? Hauna kureva nhema kuvanhu, asi kuna Mwari.”" 
Acts5:5 Ananiasi, akati achinzwa mashoko iwayo, akawira pasi, akabudisa mweya wake; kutya kukuru kukawira vose vakazvinzwa." 
Acts5:6 Majaya akasimuka, akamuputira, ndokumutakurira kunze, ndokumuviga." 
Acts5:7 Nguva dzinenge senhatu dzakati dzapfuura, mukadzi wake akapinda, asingazivi zvaitwa." 
Acts5:8 Petirosi akapindura kwaari akati, “Ndiudze kana makatengesa munda nemari yakadai?” Iye akati, “Hongu, neyakadai.”" 
Acts5:9 Petirosi akati kwaari, “Maita seiko zvamarangana kuedza Mweya waIshe? Tarira, tsoka dzavakaviga murume wako, dzichiri pamusuwo, vachakutakurirawo kunze.”" 
Acts5:10 Ipapo akawira pasi pakarepo patsoka dzake, akabudisa mweya wake; majaya akapinda, akamuwana afa, ndokumutakurira kunze, ndokumuviga kumurume wake." 
Acts5:11 Kutya kukuru kukawira Chechi yose navose vakazvinzwa. 
Acts5:12 Zviratidzo nezvinoshamisa zvizhinji zvikaitwa pakati pavanhu namaoko avapostori; vose vaiva nomwoyo mumwe pabiravira raSoromoni. 
Acts5:13 Asi pakati pavamwe kwakanga kusina munhu akatsunga kuzviisa kwavari; asi vanhu vaivakudza. 
Acts5:14 Vatendi vazhinji kwazvo, varume navakadzi, vairamba vachiwedzerwa kuna Ishe." 
Acts5:15 Nokudaro vakatakurira varwere munzira dzomumusha, vakavaradzika pamibhedha napanhoo, kuti kana Petirosi achiswederapo, kunyangwe nomumvuri wake bedzi udzikatire mumwe wavo." 
Acts5:16 Navazhinji vamaguta akapoteredza Jerusaremu vakaungana, vachiuya navarwere, navaitambudzika nemweya yetsvina, vakaporeswa." 
Acts5:17 Zvino mupristi mukuru akasimuka, navose vaiva naye (vaiva vedzidziso yavaSadhusi), vane godo kwazvo;" 
Acts5:18 vakabata vapostori vakavaisa mutorongo maipinzwa vanhu vose. 
Acts5:19 Asi mutumwa waIshe wakazarura misuwo yetorongo usiku, akavabudisa akati," 
Acts5:20 “Endai, mumire mutemberi muchitaura kuvanhu mashoko ose oupenyu uhwu.”" 
Acts5:21 Vakati vachizvinzwa, vakapinda mutemberi mangwanani, vakadzidzisa. Zvino Mupristi Mukuru navaiva naye, vakasvika, vakakokera makurukota neungano yose yavakuru vavana vaIsiraeri; vakatumira vanhu kutorongo kuzouya navo." 
Acts5:22 Asi varanda vakati vachisvikapo, vakawana vasimo mutorongo vakadzoka, vakavaudza izvozvo, vachiti," 
Acts5:23 “Torongo takaiwana yakazarirwa zvakasimba kwazvo, navarindi vakarindira pamisuwo; asi takati tichizarura, tikasawana munhu mukati.”" 
Acts5:24 Zvino mukuru wetemberi, navapristi vakuru, vakati vachinzwa mashoko iwayo, vakakanganiswa pamusoro pazvo, vasingazivi kuti zvinozodini." 
Acts5:25 Ipapo mumwe munhu akasvika, akavaudza, achiti, “Tarirai, varume vamakaisa mutorongo, vava mutemberi, vamire vachidzidzisa vanhu.”" 
Acts5:26 Zvino mukuru navatariri akaenda, akauya navo, vasingaiti nesimba, nokuti vakanga vachitya vanhu, kuti vangatakwa namabwe." 
Acts5:27 Vakati vasvika navo, vakavaisa kumakurukota. Mupristi Mukuru akavabvunza," 
Acts5:28 achiti, “Takakurairai zvikuru kuti murege kudzidzisa nezita iri, zvino tarirai, mazadza Jerusaremu nokudzidzisa kwenyu, muchida kuti ropa romunhu uyu riuye pamusoro pedu.”" 
Acts5:29 Zvino Petirosi navapostori vakapindura, vakati, “Tinofanira kuteerera Mwari kupfuura vanhu." 
Acts5:30 Mwari wamadzibaba edu akamutsa Jesu, iye wamakauraya muchimuturika pamuti." 
Acts5:31 Mwari akamusimudza iye noruoko rwake rworudyi, ave Mutungamiri noMusununguri, kuti ape VaIsiraeri kutendeuka nekanganwiro yezvivi." 
Acts5:32 Isu tiri zvapupu zvamashoko iwayo; naMweya Mutsvenewo, wavakapiwa naMwari ivo vanomuteerera.”" 
Acts5:33 Zvino ivo vakati vachizvinzwa, vakafa neshungu, vakada kuvauraya." 
Acts5:34 Ipapo mumwe muFarisi, ainzi Gamarieri, mudzidzisi womurairo, aikudzwa navanhu vose, akasimuka pamakurukota, akarayira kuti vanhu vabudiswe chinguva chiduku;" 
Acts5:35 akati kwavari, “Varume VaIsiraeri, chenjerai zvamunoda kuitira vanhu ava." 
Acts5:36 Nokuti kare kwakambomuka Tudhasi, achiti, ndiri munhu mukuru, vanhu vanenge mazana mana vakamutevera; iye akaurayiwa, navose vaimuteerera vakaparadzirwa, nokuparadzwa." 
Acts5:37 Shure kwomunhu uyu Judhasi weGareriya akamuka, pamazuva okuverengwa, akatsausa vanhu kuti vamutevere; iye akaparara, navose vakamuteerera, vakaparadzirwa." 
Acts5:38 Zvino ndinoti kwamuri, musabata vanhu ava, muvarege, nokuti kana kufunga uku nebasa iri zviri zvavanhu, zvichaparadzwa." 
Acts5:39 Asi kana zviri zvaMwari, hamungagoni kuzviparadza; kuti zvimwe mungadai muchirwa naMwariwo.”" 
Acts5:40 Vakamunzwa; ipapo vakati vadana vapostori, vakavarova, vakavarayira kuti varege kutaura nezita raJesu; vakavaregedza." 
Acts5:41 Ipapo vakabuda pamakurukota, vachifara, zvavakanzi vakafanirwa ivo kuzvidzwa nokuda kwezita rake." 
Acts5:42 Havana kurega kudzidzisa, nokuparidza mazuva ose zvaKristu Jesu, mutemberi kana kudzimba dzavo." 
Acts6:1 Zvino namazuva iwayo, vadzidzi vachiwanda, vaJudha, vaitaura ChiGiriki, vakanyunyutira VaHebheru, nokuti chirikadzi dzavo dzaidarikwa pakugoverwa kwomusi mumwe nomumwe." 
Acts6:2 Zvino vane gumi navaviri vakadana vadzidzi vazhinji, vakati, “Hakuzakafanira kuti isu tirege kuparidza shoko raMwari, tishumire pamatafura." 
Acts6:3 Zvino hama dzangu, tsanangurai pakati penyu varume vanomwe, vanopupurirwa zvakanaka, vazere naMweya nouchenjeri, vatingaisa pabasa iri." 
Acts6:4 Asi isu tichatsungirira pakunyengetera napabasa rokuparidza shoko.” 
Acts6:5 Shoko iri rikafadza vazhinji vose, vakatsanangura Sitefani, murume akanga azere nokutenda naMweya Mutsvene, naFiripi, naPirokoro, naNikano, naTimoni, naPamenasi, naNikorasi, nyakupindukira kuchiJudha weAndiyoki." 
Acts6:6 Vakavaisa pamberi pavapostori; vakanyengetera, vakaisa maoko pamusoro pavo." 
Acts6:7 Shoko raMwari rikakura, vadzidzi vakawanda zvikuru muJerusaremu; navapristi vazhinji vakagamuchira kutenda." 
Acts6:8 Zvino Sitefani, azere nenyasha nesimba, akaita zvinoshamisa nezviratidzo zvikuru pakati pavanhu." 
Acts6:9 Ipapo vamwe vavo, vaiva vesinagoge rainzi ravasununguki, navaKurene, navaArekizandiria, naveSirisia, naveEzhia, vakasimuka vakaita nharo naSitefani." 
Acts6:10 Asi vakanga vasingagoni kukunda kuchenjera kwake, naMweya waaitaura naye." 
Acts6:11 Ipapo vakamutsa varume, vaiti, “Takamunzwa achitaura mashoko anomhura Mosesi naMwari.”" 
Acts6:12 Vakakurudzira vanhu, navakuru, navanyori; vakamuwira, vakamubata, vakamuisa kumakurukota," 
Acts6:13 vakaisapo zvapupu zvenhema, zvaiti, “Munhu uyu haaregi kutaura mashoko anomhura imba iyi tsvene nomurairo." 
Acts6:14 “Nokuti takamunzwa achiti, ‘Uyu Jesu weNazareta achaparadza nzvimbo iyi nokusandura tsika dzatakapiwa naMosesi.’ ”" 
Acts6:15 Zvino vose vakanga vagere pamakurukota, vakamutarisisa, vakaona chiso chake chakaita sechiso chomutumwa." 
Acts7:1 Mupristi Mukuru akati, “Zvinhu izvi ndizvo nhai?”" 
Acts7:2 Iye akati, “Varume, hama, namadzibaba, inzwai, Mwari wokubwinya akazviratidza kuna baba vedu Abhurahamu, vachiri Mesopotamia, vasati vagara Harani," 
Acts7:3 akati kwavari, ‘Ibva munyika yako, nokuhama dzako, uende kunyika yandinozokuratidza.’" 
Acts7:4 Ipapo akabuda munyika yavaKaridhia, akagara Harani. Zvino baba vake vakati vafa, Mwari akamutamisa ipapo kunyika ino yamugere zvino." 
Acts7:5 Asi haana kumupa nhaka imomo, kunyangwe paangatsika norutsoka rwake, asi akamupikira kuti achamupa iyo, ive yake neyavana vake vaizomutevera, asati atongova nomwana." 
Acts7:6 Mwari akataura, achiti, vana vake vachava vatorwa kunyika yavamwe; vachavaita varanda, nokuvaonesa nhamo makore ana mazana mana." 
Acts7:7 Rudzi rwavachava varanda varwo, ndicharutongesa, ndizvo zvinoreva Mwari; shure kwaizvozvo vachabuda, vachandishumira panzvimbo iyi." 
Acts7:8 Akamupa sungano yedzingiso. Zvino Abhurahamu akabereka Isaka, akamudzingisa nezuva rorusere; Isaka akabereka Jakobho; naJakobho akabereka matateguru ane gumi namaviri." 
Acts7:9 “Matateguru zvaakanga achigodora Josefa, vakamutengesa, akaiswa Ijipiti; Mwari akava naye." 
Acts7:10 Akamurwira panhamo dzake dzose, akamubatsira kuti adikanwe naFarao, mambo weIjipiti, ave nokuchenjera pamberi pake; iye akamuita mutariri weIjipiti noweimba yake yose." 
Acts7:11 Zvino nzara ikasvika paIjipiti yose neKenani, nenhamo huru; madzibaba edu akashayiwa zvokudya." 
Acts7:12 Zvino Jakobho, akati anzwa kuti kuIjipiti kune zviyo, pakutanga akatuma madzibaba edu." 
Acts7:13 Parwendo rwechipiri Josefa akazikanwa navakuru vake; rudzi rwaJosefa rukaonekwa naFarao. 
Acts7:14 Zvino Josefa akavatuma kundodana Jakobho, baba vake, nehama dzake dzose, vanhu vaiva namakumi manomwe navashanu." 
Acts7:15 Jakobho akaburukira Ijipiti; akazofa, iye namadzibaba edu;" 
Acts7:16 vakaiswa Ishekemu vakavigwa pahwiro hwakanaka hwakatengwa naAbhurahamu nomutengo wesirivha kuvanakomana vaEmori paIshekemu. 
Acts7:17 “Zvino nguva yechipikirwa chakanga chapikirwa Abhurahamu naMwari, yakati ichiswedera, vanhu vakawanda, vakaita vazhinji muIjipiti;" 
Acts7:18 kusvikira mumwe mambo akamuka muIjipiti, akanga asina kuziva Josefa." 
Acts7:19 “Iye akabata rudzi rwedu namano, akatambudza madzibaba edu, akavaraira kuti varase vacheche vavo, kuti varege kuraramiswa." 
Acts7:20 Nenguva iyo Mosesi akaberekwa, akanga akaisvonaka kwazvo; akarerwa mwedzi mitatu mumba mababa vake;" 
Acts7:21 zvino akati araswa, mukunda waFarao akamunonga, akamurera kuti ave mwanakomana wake." 
Acts7:22 Mosesi akadzidziswa uchenjeri hwose hwaVaIjipiti; akava nesimba pamashoko napamabasa ake. 
Acts7:23 “Zvino akati asvika makore ana makumi mana, mwoyo wake ukada kushanyira hama dzake, vana VaIsiraeri." 
Acts7:24 Akaona mumwe achiitirwa zvisakarurama, ndokumurwira, akauraya muIjipiti, achitsiva akanga achitambudzwa." 
Acts7:25 Akati, zvimwe hama dzake dzichanzwisisa kuti Mwari akanga achida kuvaponesa noruoko rwake; asi havana kunzwisisa." 
Acts7:26 Fume mangwana akavaona vachikakavara, akaedza kuvayananisa, achiti, ‘Varume, muri hama, munoitirana zvisakarurama neiko?’" 
Acts7:27 “Zvino iye akanga achiitira wokwake zvisakarurama akamusundira kure, achiti, ‘Ndianiko akakuita mubati nomutongi wedu?" 
Acts7:28 Unoda kundiuraya, sezvawakauraya muIjipiti zuro kanhi?’" 
Acts7:29 Mosesi akatiza achinzwa shoko iri, akandova mutorwa kunyika yeMidhiani, kwaakandobereka vanakomana vaviri." 
Acts7:30 “Zvino makore makumi mana akati apera, mutumwa akaonekwa naye murenje regomo reSinai, mumurazvo womoto mugwenzi." 
Acts7:31 Mosesi akati achizviona, akashamiswa nezvaakaona; zvino akati achiswedera kuzocherechedza, izwi raIshe rikanzwika, richiti," 
Acts7:32 ‘Ndini Mwari wamadzibaba ako, Mwari waAbhurahamu, nowaIsaka, nowaJakobho.’ Ipapo Mosesi akadedera, akatya kucherechedza." 
Acts7:33 Ishe akati kwaari, ‘Bvisa shangu patsoka dzako, nokuti apo paunomira ivhu dzvene." 
Acts7:34 Ndakaona hangu kwazvo kutambudzika kwavanhu vangu vari muIjipiti, ndakanzwa kugomera kwavo, ndaburuka kuzovarwira; zvino uya ndikutume Ijipiti.’" 
Acts7:35 “Uyu Mosesi wavakaramba, vachiti, ‘Ndiani wakakuita mubati nomutongi?’ Ndiye akatumwa naMwari nomutumwa akaonekwa naye mugwenzi, kuti ave mubati nomudzikinuri." 
Acts7:36 “Iye akavabudisa, akaita zvinoshamisa nezviratidzo munyika yeIjipiti, nomuGungwa Dzvuku, nomurenje, makore ana makumi mana." 
Acts7:37 Ndiyeye Mosesi akati kuvana VaIsiraeri, ‘Mwari achakumutsirai Muporofita pakati pehama dzenyu, akafanana neni.’" 
Acts7:38 Ndiyeye akanga ari kuungano murenje, anomutumwa akataura naye mugomo reSinai, anamadzibaba eduwo, akagamuchira mashoko mapenyu kuzotipa." 
Acts7:39 “Ndiye, wavakanga vasingadi kumuteerera ivo madzibaba edu; vakamuramba, vakadzokera Ijipiti nemwoyo yavo." 
Acts7:40 “Vakati kuna Aroni, ‘Tiitire vamwari, vangatitungamirira; nokuti kana ari Mosesi uyu, akatibudisa munyika yeIjipiti, hatizivi zvakaitika naye.’" 
Acts7:41 Zvino vakaita mhuru namazuva iwayo, vakauya nechibayiro kuchifananidzo chavo, vakafarira mabasa amaoko avo." 
Acts7:42 Zvino Mwari akavafuratira, akavarega kuti vashumire hondo yokudenga, sezvazvakanyorwa mubhuku yavaporofita, zvichinzi, ‘Ko makandivigira zvipfuwo zvakabayiwa nezvibairo Makore makumi mana murenje, imi, imba yaVaIsiraeri here?" 
Acts7:43 Makatakura tabhenakeri yaMoroki, Nenyenyedzi yamwari wenyu Remifani, Zvifananidzo zvamakaita kuti muzvinamate; Ndichakutamisai mberi kweBhabhironi.’" 
Acts7:44 “Madzibaba edu aiva netabhenakeri youchapupu murenje, yakanga yakavakwa sezvaakarayira iye, akataura naMosesi, achiti aiite nomufananidzo waakaona." 
Acts7:45 Yakati yagamuchirwa namadzibaba edu, vakapinda nayo naJoshua munyika yavahedheni, vakadzingwa naMwari pamberi pamadzibaba edu, kusvikira pamazuva aDhavhidhi;" 
Acts7:46 iye akanzwirwa nyasha pamberi paMwari, akakumbira kuvakira Mwari waJakobho pokugara." 
Acts7:47 Soromoni akamuvakira imba. 
Acts7:48 “Asi Wokumusoro–soro haagari mudzimba dzakavakwa namaoko, sezvazvakarehwa nomuporofita, achiti," 
Acts7:49 ‘Denga ndicho chigaro changu choushe, Nenyika chitsiko chetsoka dzangu; Muchandivakira imba yakadiniko? Ndizvo zvinoreva Ishe; Kana nzvimbo yandingazorora pairi ndeipi?" 
Acts7:50 Ko ruoko rwangu haruna kuita izvovi zvose here?’ 
Acts7:51 “Imi vemitsipa mikukutu, musina kudzingiswa pamwoyo nenzeve, munogara muchidzivisa Mweya Mutsvene; samadzibaba enyu, nemiwo." 
Acts7:52 Ndoupiko pavaporofita asina kutambudzwa namadzibaba enyu? Vakauraya avo vaiparidza kuuya kwoWakarurama, iye wamakapandukira nokumuuraya zvino." 
Acts7:53 Iyemi, makapiwa murairo sezvawakarayiwa navatumwa, mukasauchengeta.”" 
Acts7:54 Zvino vakati vachinzwa izvozvo, vakafa neshungu kwazvo, vakamugeda–gedera meno." 
Acts7:55 Asi iye azere naMweya Mutsvene, akatarisisa kudenga, akaona kubwinya kwaMwari, naJesu amire kuruoko rworudyi rwaMwari," 
Acts7:56 akati, “Tarirai, ndinoona denga rakazarurwa, noMwanakomana womunhu amire kuruoko rworudyi rwaMwari.”" 
Acts7:57 Zvino vakadanidzira nezwi guru, vakadzivira nzeve dzavo, vakamhanyira kwaari vose pamwechete;" 
Acts7:58 vakamubudisira kunze kweguta, ndokumutaka namabwe; zvapupu zvikaisa nguo dzazvo patsoka dzejaya, rainzi Sauro." 
Acts7:59 Vakataka Sitefani, achidana achiti, “Ishe Jesu, gamuchirai mweya wangu.”" 
Acts7:60 Akapfugama, akadanidzira nezwi guru, achiti, “Ishe, musavapa mhosva yechivi ichi.” Akati areva izvozvo, akabva afa." 
Acts8:1 Sauro akanga achitenda kuurayiwa kwake. Zvino nenguva iyo Chechi yapaJerusaremu yakatambudzwa zvikuru, vakaparadzirwa vose kunyika yeJudhiya neSamaria, vakasara vapostori bedzi." 
Acts8:2 Varume vakarurama vakaviga Sitefani, vakamuchema zvikuru." 
Acts8:3 Zvino Sauro akaparadza Chechi, achipinda mudzimba dzose, achikakata varume navakadzi, nokuvaisa mutorongo." 
Acts8:4 Zvino avo vakaparadzirwa, vakapota nyika, vachiparidza shoko." 
Acts8:5 NaFiripi akaburukira kuguta reSamaria, akavaparidzira Kristu." 
Acts8:6 Vanhu vazhinji vakateerera nomwoyo mumwe zvairehwa naFiripi, vachinzwa nokuona zviratidzo zvaakanga achiita." 
Acts8:7 Nokuti mweya yetsvina yakabuda kuvazhinji vaiva nayo, ichidanidzira nezwi guru; navazhinji vakanga vakafa mitezo navaikamhina vakaporeswa." 
Acts8:8 Mufaro mukuru ukavapo paguta iro. 
Acts8:9 Zvino kwakanga kuno mumwe murume, ainzi Simoni, aiva n'anga kare paguta iro, aishamisa vanhu veSamaria, achizviita munhu mukuru." 
Acts8:10 Vose, vaduku navakuru, vakamuteerera, vachiti, “Uyu munhu isimba guru raMwari.”" 
Acts8:11 Vakamuteerera, nokuti akanga avashamisa noun'anga hwake nguva huru." 
Acts8:12 Zvino vakati vatenda Firipi, aiparidza mashoko oushe hwaMwari nezita raJesu Kristu, vakabhabhatidzwa varume navakadzi." 
Acts8:13 Naiye Simoni akatendawo, ndokubhabhatidzwawo, akagara naFiripi; akashamiswa, achiona zviratidzo namabasa emasimba makuru, akanga achiitwa." 
Acts8:14 Zvino vapostori vaiva paJerusaremu, vakati vanzwa kuti vaSamaria vakanga vagamuchira shoko raMwari, vakatuma Petirosi naJohani kwavari." 
Acts8:15 Ivo vakaburukirako, vakavanyengeterera kuti vapiwe Mweya Mutsvene;" 
Acts8:16 nokuti akanga asina kuburukira pamusoro pomumwe wavo; vakanga vangobhabhatidzwa muzita raIshe Jesu bedzi. 
Acts8:17 Ipapo vapositori vakaisa maoko avo pamusoro pavo, vakapiwa Mweya Mutsvene." 
Acts8:18 Zvino Simoni akati achiona kuti Mweya Mutsvene apiwa nokuiswa kwamaoko avapostori, akauya kwavari nemari," 
Acts8:19 achiti, “Ndipei neniwo simba iri, kuti wandinenge ndichiisa maoko pamusoro pake, apiwe Mweya Mutsvene.”" 
Acts8:20 Zvino Petirosi akati kwaari, “Sirivha yako ngaiparadzwe newe, nokuti wakafunga kutenga chipo chaMwari nemari." 
Acts8:21 Hauna mugove, kana chikamu, pachinhu ichi, nokuti mwoyo wako hauna kururama pamberi paMwari." 
Acts8:22 Naizvozvo tendeuka pakuipa kwako, ukumbire kuna Ishe, kuti zvimwe uregererwe marangariro omwoyo wako." 
Acts8:23 “Nokuti ndinoona kuti wapinda munduru inovava, napakusungwa kusakarurama.”" 
Acts8:24 Simoni akapindura, akati, “Mundikumbirire zvikuru imi kuna Ishe, kuti ndirege kuwirwa nechimwe chaizvozvo zvamareva.”" 
Acts8:25 Zvino vakati vapupura kwazvo nokutaura shoko raIshe, vakadzokerazve Jerusaremu, vachiparidza Vhangeri mumisha mizhinji yavaSamaria." 
Acts8:26 Zvino mutumwa waIshe akataura naFiripi, akati, “Simuka, uende Zasi kunzira inobva Jerusaremu ichiburukira Gaza; iyo nyika irenje.”" 
Acts8:27 Akasimuka, akaenda; zvino kwakanga kuno murume weItiopia, muranda mukuru kwazvo waKandase, mambokadzi weItiopia, aichengeta pfuma yake yose, akanga auya Jerusaremu kuzonamata;" 
Acts8:28 akanga achidzoka, agere mungoro yake achirava muporofita Isaya." 
Acts8:29 Mweya akati kuna Firipi, “Swedera, urambire pangoro iyo.”" 
Acts8:30 Firipi akamhanyirako, akamunzwa achirava muporofita Isaya, akati, “Unonzwisisa zvaunorava here?”" 
Acts8:31 Iye akati, “Ndingagona seiko, kana mumwe asingandidudziri?” Akakumbira zvikuru kuna Firipi kuti akwire, agare naye." 
Acts8:32 Zvino paakanga achirava muRugwaro paiti, “Akaiswa pakubayiwa segwai; Segwayana rinyerere pamberi pomuveuri waro, Saizvozvo haana kushamisa muromo wake;" 
Acts8:33 Pakuzvidzwa kwake kutongwa kwake kwakabviswa; Ndianiko acharondedzera rudzi rwake? Nokuti upenyu hwake hunobviswa panyika.” 
Acts8:34 Muranda akapindura Firipi, akati, “Ndinokumbira kwauri, undiudze kuti muporofita anoreva aniko achidaro? Anozvireva iye amene, kana mumwe?”" 
Acts8:35 Ipapo Firipi akashamisa muromo wake, akatanga parugwaro urwu, akamuparidzira Jesu." 
Acts8:36 Zvino vakati vachifamba munzira, vakasvika pane mvura; muranda akati, “Heyi mvura; chiiko chingadzivisa ndirege kubhabhatidzwa?” [" 
Acts8:37 Firipi akati, “Kana uchitenda nomwoyo wako wose, zvingaitwa.” Akapindura, akati, “Ndinotenda kuti Jesu ndiye Mwanakomana waMwari.”]" 
Acts8:38 Akarayira kuti ngoro imire; vakaburukira vose mumvura, iye Firipi nomuranda; akamubhabhatidza." 
Acts8:39 Zvino vakati vachibuda mumvura, Mweya waIshe akabvisa Firipi; muranda akasazomuonazve; nokuti akafamba rwendo rwake, achifara." 
Acts8:40 Asi Firipi akawanika paAzoto, akapota nyika achiparidza Vhangeri pamaguta ose, kusvikira paSizaria." 
Acts9:1 Asi Sauro achingorangarira kutyisa nokuuraya vadzidzi vaIshe, akaenda kuMupristi Mukuru," 
Acts9:2 akakumbira kwaari magwaro okuenda nawo Dhamasikosi kumasinagoge, kuti kana awana vamwe vaiva veNzira iyo, varume kana vakadzi, auye navo Jerusaremu vakasungwa." 
Acts9:3 Zvino akati ari parwendo, oswedera pedyo neDhamasikosi, kamwe–kamwe chiedza chakabva kudenga chikamupenyera pamativi ose," 
Acts9:4 akawira pasi, akanzwa izwi richiti kwaari, “Sauro, Sauro, unonditambudzireiko?”" 
Acts9:5 Iye akati, “Ndimi aniko, Ishe?” Akati, “Ndini Jesu waunotambudza; zvinokuremera kupfura zvibayiso.”" 
Acts9:6 Iye achidedera nokutya, akati, “Ishe, munoda kuti ndiiteiko?” Ishe akati kwaari, “Simuka, uende muguta, uchandoudzwa zvaunofanira kuita.”" 
Acts9:7 Varume vaiva parwendo naye, vakamira vanyerere, vachinzwa izwi, asi vasingaoni munhu." 
Acts9:8 Zvino Sauro akasimuka; asi achisvinudza meso ake, haana kuona chinhu; vakamubata ruoko, vakaenda naye Dhamasikosi." 
Acts9:9 Akaita mazuva matatu, asingaoni, asingadyi, asinganwi chinhu." 
Acts9:10 Zvino paDhamasikosi pakanga pano mumwe mudzidzi, ainzi Ananiasi; Ishe akati kwaari nezvaakaratidzwa, “Ananiasi!” Iye akati, “Ndiri pano Ishe!”" 
Acts9:11 Ishe akati kwaari, “Simuka, uende munzira yomuguta inonzi Yakarurama, ubvunze mumba maJudhasi, munhu anonzi Sauro weTasasi; nokuti tarira, anonyengetera;" 
Acts9:12 naiye akaona murume, anonzi Ananiasi achipinda, achiisa maoko ake pamusoro pake, kuti aonezve.”" 
Acts9:13 Zvino Ananiasi akapindura, akati, “Ishe, ndakanzwa navanhu vazhinji zvomunhu uyu, kuti akaitira vatsvene venyu paJerusaremu zvakaipa zvizhinji;" 
Acts9:14 napano ane simba raakapiwa navapristi vakuru, kuti asunge vose vanonamata nezita renyu.”" 
Acts9:15 Asi Ishe akati kwaari, “Enda, nokuti iye mudziyo wakasanangurwa neni, kuti aende nezita rangu kuvahedheni, namadzimambo, nokuvana VaIsiraeri;" 
Acts9:16 nokuti ndichamuratidza zvose, zvaachafanira kutamburira nokuda kwezita rangu.”" 
Acts9:17 Ipapo Ananiasi akaenda akapinda mumba, akaisa maoko ake pamusoro pake, akati, “Sauro, hama, Ishe Jesu, akazviratidza kwauri munzira yawakauya nayo, akandituma, kuti uonezve, uzadzwe naMweya Mutsvene.”" 
Acts9:18 Pakarepo pameso ake pakabva zvinhu zvinenge mafunhurwa, akaonazve; akasimuka, ndokubhabhatidzwa;" 
Acts9:19 akadya zvokudya, ndokusimbiswa. Akagara navadzidzi paDhamasikosi mamwe mazuva." 
Acts9:20 Pakarepo akaparidza Jesu mumasinagoge, kuti ndiye Mwanakomana waMwari." 
Acts9:21 Vose vakazvinzwa vakashamiswa, vakati, “Ko uyu haazi iye aiparadza vaidana zita iri paJerusaremu here, akauira izvozvo pano, kuti aende navo vakasungwa kuvapristi vakuru?”" 
Acts9:22 Asi Sauro akaramba achisimbiswa, akakunda vaJudha vakanga vagere Dhamasikosi, achiratidza kuti Jesu ndiye Kristu." 
Acts9:23 Zvino mazuva mazhinji akati apera, vaJudha vakarangana kuti vamuuraye." 
Acts9:24 Asi kurangana kwavo kwakazikanwa naSauro. Vakarindawo masuwo masikati nousiku, kuti vamuuraye." 
Acts9:25 Zvino vadzidzi vake vakamutora usiku, vakamuburusa naparusvingo, vamuisa mudengu." 
Acts9:26 Zvino akati asvika Jerusaremu, akaedza kufambidzana navadzidzi; asi ivo vakamutya vose, vasingatendi kuti ava mudzidzi." 
Acts9:27 Zvino Bhanabhasi akamutora, akaenda naye kuvapostori, ndokuvarondedzera kuti akaona Ishe munzira, uye kuti akataura naye, uye kuti akaparidza nezita raJesu paDhamasikosi asingatyi." 
Acts9:28 Akagara navo paJerusaremu, achifambidzana navo," 
Acts9:29 akaparidza nezita raIshe asingatyi. Akataura navaJudha vaitaura ChiGiriki; asi ivo vakaedza kumuuraya. 
Acts9:30 Zvino hama dzakati dzichizviziva, dzakamuburusira Sizaria, ndokumutumira Tasasi." 
Acts9:31 Zvino Chechi yakanga ino rugare paJudhiya rose, reGareriya, neSamaria, ikasimbiswa; ikawedzerwa, ichifamba ichitya Ishe, ichinyaradzwa naMweya Mutsvene." 
Acts9:32 Zvino Petirosi akati achipota nyika kwose, akaburukirawo kuvatsvene vakanga vagere Ridha." 
Acts9:33 Akawanapo mumwe munhu, ainzi Eniyasi, akanga avete panhoo makore masere, mitezo yake yakafa." 
Acts9:34 Petirosi akati kwaari, “Eniyasi, Jesu Kristu anokuporesa; simuka, uzviwarire nhoo dzako!” Akasimuka pakarepo." 
Acts9:35 Zvino vose vakanga vagere Ridha neSaroni vakamuona, vakatendeukira kuna Ishe." 
Acts9:36 Zvino paJopa pakanga pano mukadzi aiva mudzidzi, ainzi Tabhita, ndokuti, Dhokasi, kana zvichishandurwa. Iye aishingaira zvikuru pamabasa akanaka ezvipo." 
Acts9:37 Zvino namazuva iwayo iye akarwara, ndokufa. Vakati vamushambidza, vakamuisa muimba yokumusoro." 
Acts9:38 Zvino Ridha zvayakanga iri pedyo neJopa, vadzidzi vakati vanzwa kuti Petirosi aripo, vakatumira kwaari vanhu vaviri, kuti vandokumbira zvikuru kwaari, vachiti, “Usanonoka hako kuuya kwatiri.”" 
Acts9:39 Ipapo Petirosi akasimuka, akaenda navo. Akati asvika, vakamuisa kuimba yokumusoro; chirikadzi dzose dzikamira naye dzichichema, vakamuratidza zvokufuka nenguo, dzavakanga vaitirwa naDhokasi, achiri navo." 
Acts9:40 Zvino Petirosi akavabudisira panze vose, akapfugama, akanyengetera, ndokutendeukira kumutumbi, akati, “Tabhita, muka!” Akasvinura meso ake; zvino akati achiona Petirosi, akagara." 
Acts9:41 Akamubata noruoko rwake, akamusimudza; akadana vatsvene nechirikadzi, akamuisa pamberi pavo ari mupenyu." 
Acts9:42 Zvikazikanwa navose paJopa; vazhinji vakatenda kuna Ishe. 
Acts9:43 Ipapo akagara mazuva mazhinji paJopa, kuno mumwe Simoni, musuki wamatehwe." 
Acts10:1 Zvino kwakanga kuno mumwe murume paSizaria, ainzi Koniriasi, mukuru wezana wehondo yainzi Itari," 
Acts10:2 munhu, ainamata noaitya Mwari, iye naveimba yake yose, aipa vanhu zvipo zvizhinji, nokunyengetera kuna Mwari misi yose." 
Acts10:3 Zvino nenguva inenge yepfumbamwe yezuva akaona kwazvo, nezvaakaratidzwa, mutumwa waMwari achipinda kwaari, achiti kwaari, “Koniriasi!”"
