Acts10:4 Iye akamutarisisa, akatya, akati, “Chiiko Ishe?” Akati kwaari, “Minyengetero yako nezvipo zvako zvakwira pamberi paMwari, zvarangarirwa." 
Acts10:5 Zvino tuma varume Jopa kundodana Simoni, anotumidzwa Petirosi." 
Acts10:6 Anogara nomumwe anonzi Simoni, musuki wamatehwe, imba yake iri pagungwa.”" 
Acts10:7 Zvino mutumwa, akataura naye, akati abva, akadana varanda vake vaviri nomurwi wakarurama pakati pavaisimushumira," 
Acts10:8 akavaudza zvose, ndokuvatumira Jopa." 
Acts10:9 Zvino fume mangwana vachiri parwendo, vava pedyo neguta, Petirosi akakwira pamusoro peimba kundonyengetera nenguva inenge yechitanhatu." 
Acts10:10 Akaziya kwazvo, akada kudya; zvino vakati vachagadzira, akabatwa mweya;" 
Acts10:11 akaona denga razarurwa nechimwe chinhu chichiburuka somucheka mukuru unoburusirwa pasi wakasungwa miromo mina. 
Acts10:12 Maiva nemhuka dzose dzina makumbo mana nezvinokambaira zvenyika, neshiri dzedenga." 
Acts10:13 Izwi rikauya kwaari, richiti, “Simuka Petirosi, baya, udye.”" 
Acts10:14 Asi Petiro akati, “Kwete, Ishe, nokuti handina kutongodya chinhu chisakanaka, chine tsvina.”" 
Acts10:15 Ipapo izwi rikauyazve kwaari rwechipiri, richiti, “Chakanatswa naMwari, usati, chine tsvina iwe.”" 
Acts10:16 Izvozvo zvakaitwa katatu, chinhu chikakwidzwa pakarepo kudenga." 
Acts10:17 Zvino Petirosi akati achakanganiswa mumwoyo make, kuti chiratidzo chaakanga aona chairevei, tarira varume vakanga vatumwa naKoniriasi, vamira pasuwo vachibvunza imba yaSimoni;" 
Acts10:18 vakadana, vakabvunza kana Simoni, anonzi Petirosi, agerepo." 
Acts10:19 Zvino Petirosi, achafunga chiratidzo, Mweya akati kwaari, “Tarira, varume vatatu vanokutsvaka." 
Acts10:20 Zvino simuka, uburuke, uende navo, usinganyunyuti, nokuti ndini ndavatuma.”" 
Acts10:21 Ipapo Petirosi akaburukira kuvarume avo, akati kwavari, “Tarirai, ndini wamunotsvaka; shoko ramauyira ndereiko?”" 
Acts10:22 Vakati, “Koniriasi, mukuru wezana, murume akarurama, anotya Mwari, anorumbidzwa norudzi rwose rwavaJudha, akarayirwa naMwari nomutumwa mutsvene, kuti akudanei kuzouya kumba kwake, kuti anzwe mashoko kwamuri.”" 
Acts10:23 Ipapo akavadana mumba, akati vagarepo. Fume mangwana akasimuka akaenda navo; nedzimwe hama dzapaJopa dzikamuperekedza." 
Acts10:24 Fumezve mangwana akapinda Sizaria. Zvino Koniriasi akanga akavamirira, akakokera hama dzake neshamwari dzake dzaidikanwa." 
Acts10:25 Zvino Petirosi akati achipinda, Koniriasi akamuchingamidza, akawira pasi petsoka dzake, akamupfugamira." 
Acts10:26 Asi Petirosi akamusimudza, akati, “Simuka, neni ndiri munhuwo.”" 
Acts10:27 Zvino akati achataura naye, akapinda, akawana vazhinji vakaungana," 
Acts10:28 akati kwavari, “Imi munoziva kuti hazvina kufanira kuti muJudha afambidzane nomunhu worumwe rudzi, kana kuuya kwaari. Asi Mwari akandiratidza, kuti ndirege kuti munhu haana kunaka, kana kuti ane tsvina;" 
Acts10:29 naizvozvo ndauya, ndisingaramba, zvandadanwa; zvino ndinobvunza kuti mandidanireiko.”" 
Acts10:30 Koniriasi akati, “Ava mazuva mana kusvikira nguva ino, ini ndakanga ndichinyengetera mumba mangu nenguva yepfumbamwe; ipapo ndikaona murume amire pamberi pangu, ane nguo dzinopenya," 
Acts10:31 akati, ‘Koniriasi, kunyengetera kwako kwanzwikwa, nezvipo zvako zvarangarirwa naMwari." 
Acts10:32 Naizvozvo chitumira vanhu Jopa, udane Simoni, anonzi Petirosi; anogara mumba maSimoni musuki wamatehwe, pagungwa.’" 
Acts10:33 Naizvozvo ndakakurumidza kutuma kwamuri; zvino maita zvakanaka, zvamauya. Zvino isu tose tiri pano pamberi paMwari kuti tinzwe zvose zvamarayirwa naIshe.”" 
Acts10:34 Ipapo Petirosi akashamisa muromo wake akati, “Zvirokwazvo, ndinoona kuti Mwari haazi mutsauri wavanhu," 
Acts10:35 asi parudzi rupi norupi, munhu, anomutya, achiita zvakarurama, anogamuchirwa naye." 
Acts10:36 “Ndiro shoko, raakatuma kuvana VaIsiraeri, achiparidza mashoko akanaka orugare naJesu Kristu (ndiye Ishe wavose)." 
Acts10:37 Imi munoziva shoko iro rakaparidzwa paJudhiya rose, rakatanga paGareriya, shure kwokubhabhatidza kwakaparidzwa naJohani;" 
Acts10:38 raJesu weNazareta, kuti Mwari akamuzodza naMweya Mutsvene nesimba; iye aipota nyika, achiita zvakanaka, achiporesa vose vakamanikidzwa naDhiabhori; nokuti Mwari aiva naye." 
Acts10:39 Nesu tiri zvapupu zvazvose, zvaakaita munyika yavaJudha nomuJerusaremu; ndiye wavakauraya, vachimuturika pamuti." 
Acts10:40 “Ndiye akamutswa naMwari nezuva retatu, akamupa simba kuti aonekwe pachena;" 
Acts10:41 akasaonekwa navanhu vose, asi nezvapupu zvakagara zvatsaurwa naMwari, iyesu, taidya nokunwa naye, amuka kuvakafa." 
Acts10:42 Akatirayira kuti tiparidzire vanhu, nokupupura kwazvo kuti ndiye akagadzwa naMwari, kuti ave Mutongi wavapenyu navakafa." 
Acts10:43 “Vaporofita vose vanomupupurira kuti nezita rake mumwe nomumwe anotenda kwaari achapiwa ruregerero rwezvivi.” 
Acts10:44 Petirosi akati achataura mashoko awa, Mweya Mutsvene akaburuka pamusoro pavose, vakanzwa shoko." 
Acts10:45 Zvino vatendi vokudzingisa, vakanga vauya naPetirosi, vakashamiswa, kuti chipo chaMweya Mutsvene chakanga chadururwa pamusoro pavahedheniwo;" 
Acts10:46 nokuti vakavanzwa vachitaura nedzimwe ndimi, vachirumbidza Mwari. Ipapo Petirosi akapindura, akati," 
Acts10:47 “Kuno munhu here angadzivisa mvura, kuti ava, vakapiwa Mweya Mutsvene sesu, varege kubhabhatidzwa?”" 
Acts10:48 Zvino akarayira kuti vabhabhatidzwe muzita raJesu Kristu. Ipapo vakakumbira kwaari, kuti ambogara mamwe mazuva." 
Acts11:1 Zvino vapostori nehama, vaiva paJudhiya, vakanzwa kuti vahedheni vakagamuchirawo shoko raMwari." 
Acts11:2 Zvino Petirosi akati akwira Jerusaremu, vatendi vokudzingisa vakaita nharo naye," 
Acts11:3 vachiti, “Wakapinda iwe kuvarume vasina kudzingiswa, ukadya navo.”" 
Acts11:4 Zvino Petirosi akatanga kuvarondedzera zvose, zvichitevedzana, achiti," 
Acts11:5 “Ndakanga ndiri muguta reJopa, ndichinyengetera; ndikabatwa mweya, ndikaona chiratidzo; chimwe chinhu chakaburuka, chinenge mucheka mukuru unoburuswa kudenga wakasungwa miromo mina, chikasvika pandiri;" 
Acts11:6 ndakati ndachitarisisa, nokucherechedza, ndikaona mhuka dzenyika dzina makumbo mana nezvikara, nezvinokambaira, neshiri dzedenga," 
Acts11:7 ndikanzwawo izwi richiti kwandiri, ‘Simuka Petirosi, baya, udye.’" 
Acts11:8 Asi ini ndikati, ‘Kwete Ishe, nokuti mumuromo mangu hamuna kumbopinda chinhu chisakanaka, chine tsvina.’" 
Acts11:9 Asi izwi rakapindura rwechipiri, richibva kudenga, richiti, ‘Icho chakanatswa naMwari, iwe usati, hachina kunaka.’" 
Acts11:10 “Izvozvo zvakaitwa katatu, zvose zvikakwidzwazve kudenga." 
Acts11:11 Ipapo, tarira, pakarepo varume vatatu vamira pamberi peimba, matakanga tiri, vakanga vatumirwa kwandiri, vachibva Sizaria." 
Acts11:12 “Ipapo Mweya akandiudza, kuti ndiende navo, ndisinganyunyuti. Nehama idzi nhanhatuwo dzakandiperekedza, tikapinda mumba momurume uyu." 
Acts11:13 Iye akatiudzawo kuti akaona mutumwa amire mumba make, achiti, ‘Tumira Jopa, udane Simoni, anonzi Petirosi;" 
Acts11:14 iye achakuudza mashoko auchaponeswa nawo, iwe nemhuri yako yose.’" 
Acts11:15 Zvino ndakati ndichatanga kutaura, Mweya Mutsvene akaburuka pamusoro pavo, sapamusoro peduwo pakutanga." 
Acts11:16 Ini ndikarangarira shoko raIshe, rokuti, ‘Johani akabhabhatidza nemvura, asi imi muchabhabhatidzwa naMweya Mutsvene.’" 
Acts11:17 “Zvino kana Mwari akavapa chipo icho chaakatipa isu, pakutenda kwedu kuna Ishe Jesu Kristu, ini ndaigova ani, aigona kudzivisa Mwari?”" 
Acts11:18 Zino vakati vanzwa izvozvo, vakanyarara, vakakudza Mwari, vachiti, “Zvirokwazvo, Mwari akapa vahedheniwo kutendeuka kwoupenyu.”" 
Acts11:19 Zvino avo vakaparadzirwa nokutambudzika kwakamuka pamusoro paSitefani, vakaenda kusvikira paFonikia, neSaipurasi, neAndiyoku, vasingatauri shoko kumunhu, asi kuna vaJudha bedzi." 
Acts11:20 Zvino pakati pavo paiva navamwe varume veSaipurasi neKurene; ivo vakati vasvika Andiyoku, vakataura kuvaGirikiwo, vachiparidza Ishe Jesu." 
Acts11:21 Ruoko rwaIshe rukava navo, vazhinji vakatenda, vakatendeukira kuna Ishe." 
Acts11:22 Mashoko avo akanzwika nechechi muJerusaremu, vakatuma Bhanabhasi kuti aende Andiyoku." 
Acts11:23 Iye akati asvika, akaona nyasha dzaMwari, akafara; akarayira vose kuti vanamatire Ishe nomwoyo wakasimba;" 
Acts11:24 nokuti waiva murume akanaka, azere naMweya Mutsvene nokutenda; vazhinji zhinji vakawedzerwa kuna Ishe." 
Acts11:25 Iye akaenda Tasasi achindotsvaka Sauro. 
Acts11:26 Zvino akati amuwana, akauya naye Andiyoku. Ipapo vakaungana nechechi gore rose, vakadzidzisa vanhu vazhinji zhinji; paAndiyoku vadzidzi vakatanga kunzi VaKristu." 
Acts11:27 Namazuva iwayo vaporofita vakaburuka vachibva Jerusaremu, vakaenda Andiyoku." 
Acts11:28 Mumwe wavo ainzi Agabho, akasimuka, ndokuvazivisa naMweya kuti nzara huru ichavapo panyika yose; iyo ikasvika panguva yaKiraudhiyo." 
Acts11:29 Ipapo vadzidzi vakatenderana, kuti mumwe nomumwe paaigona napo atume zvingabatsira hama dzigere Judhiya." 
Acts11:30 Vakaita kudaro, vakazvitumira naBhanabhasi naSauro kuvakuru." 
Acts12:1 Zvino nenguva inenge iyeyo mambo Herodhi akatambanudza maoko ake kuti atambudze vamwe vechechi; 
Acts12:2 akauraya Jakobho, mukuru waJohani, nomunondo." 
Acts12:3 Zvino akati achiona kuti zvafadza vaJudha, ndokupfuura akabatawo Petirosi. Aiva mazuva ezvingwa zvisina mbiriso." 
Acts12:4 Zvino akati amubata, akamusunga akamuisa mutorongo, kumapoka mana, rimwe nerimwe rina varwi vana, kuti vamurinde, achiti amuise pamberi pavanhu, kana Pasika yapfuura." 
Acts12:5 Naizvozvo Petirosi akachengetwa mutorongo; asi akanga achinyengetererwa zvikuru nechechi kuna Mwari. 
Acts12:6 Zvino Herodhi akati oda kumubudisa, usiku ihwohwo Petirosi akanga avete pakati pavarwi vaviri, akasungwa namangetani maviri; navarindi vakanga vachirinda torongo pamberi pomusuwo." 
Acts12:7 Ipapo tarira, mutumwa waIshe akamirapo, chiedza chikapenya mumba; akarova Petirosi parutivi, ndokumumutsa, achiti, “Muka, ukurumidze.” Ipapo ngetani dzakawa pamaoko ake." 
Acts12:8 Mutumwa akati kwaari, “Zvisunge chiuno, usungire shangu dzako.” Akaita saizvozvo. Akati kwaari, “Fuka nguo yako, unditevere.”" 
Acts12:9 Akabuda, akamutevera, asingazivi kuti zvirokwazvo zvinoitwa nomutumwa; asi akati ndinoona chiratidzo." 
Acts12:10 Zvino vakati vapfuura murindi wokutanga nowechipiri, vakasvika pasuwo ramatare, pavaipinda napo paguta; rikangovazarukira roga; vakabuda, vakapfuura neimwe nzira, mutumwa ndokubva kwaari pakarepo." 
Acts12:11 Petirosi akati apengenuka, akati, “Zvino ndinoziva zvirokwazvo kuti Ishe akatuma mutumwa wake, akandirwira paruoko rwaHerodhi napazvose zvakanga zvichifungwa navanhu vavaJudha.”" 
Acts12:12 Zvino akati arangarira izvozvo, akaenda kumba kwaMaria, mai vaJohani, ainzi Mako; vazhinji vakanga vakaunganapo, vachinyengetera." 
Acts12:13 Zvino akati agogodza pagonhi resuwo, musikana ainzi Rodha akauya kuzoteerera." 
Acts12:14 Iye akati achinzwa izwi raPetirosi, akasazarura suwo nomufaro, asi akamhanyira mukati akavaudza kuti Petirosi amire pasuwo." 
Acts12:15 Ivo vakati kwaari, “Unopenga.” Asi iye akasimbisa achiti, “Ndizvozvo.” Ivo vakati, “Mutumwa wake.”" 
Acts12:16 Asi Petirosi akaramba achigogodza; vakazozarura, vakamuona, vakashamiswa." 
Acts12:17 Zvino iye akavaninira noruoko kuti vanyarare, akavarondedzera mutoo waakabudiswa nawo naIshe patorongo. Akati, “Udzai Jakobho nehama zvinhu izvozvi; ndokubva akaenda kumwe.”" 
Acts12:18 Zvino kwakati kwaedza, bope guru rikavapo pakati pavarwi, vachiti, “Petirosi aitwa sei.”" 
Acts12:19 Herodhi akati amutsvaka, akamushayiwa, ndokubvunzisisa varindi, akarayira kuti vanourayiwa. Zvino akaburuka Judhiya, akaenda Sizaria, akandogarako." 
Acts12:20 Zvino akatsamwira zvikuru vanhu veTaya neSidhoni; ivo ndokuuya kwaari vose pamwechete, vakaita ushamwari naBhurasito, mutariri weimba yamambo, vakakumbira rugare, nokuti nyika yavo yaipiwa zvokudya nenyika yamambo." 
Acts12:21 Ipapo nezuva rakanga ratarwa, Herodhi akafuka nguo dzoumambo, akagara pachigaro chake choushe, akataura kwavari." 
Acts12:22 Ipapo vanhu vakadanidzira vachiti, “Izwi raMwari, harizi romunhu.”" 
Acts12:23 Pakarepo mutumwa waIshe akamurova, nokuti akanga asina kukudza Mwari; akadyiwa nehonye, akafa." 
Acts12:24 Asi shoko raMwari rakakura, rikawanda." 
Acts12:25 Zvino Bhanabhasi naSauro, vakati vapedzisa basa ravo, vakadzokera Jerusaremu, vakaenda naJohani, ainzi Mako." 
Acts13:1 Zvino pachechi yapaAndiyoku paiva navaporofita navadzidzisi, vaiti: Bhanabhasi naSimeoni, ainzi Nigeri, naRukio weKurene, naManaeni akanga arerwa pamwechete naHerodhi mubati, naSauro." 
Acts13:2 Vakati vachishumira Ishe, nokuzvinyima zvokudya, Mweya Mutsvene akati, “Nditsaurirei Bhanabhasi naSauro kubata basa randakavadanira.”" 
Acts13:3 Ipapo vakazvinyima zvokudya, vakanyengetera, vakaisa maoko pamusoro pavo, ndokuvaendesa." 
Acts13:4 Naizvozvo vakati vatumwa noMweya Mutsvene, vakaburukira Serusia; vakabvapo, vakaenda Saipurasi nechikepe." 
Acts13:5 Vachisvika paSaramisi, vakaparidza shoko raMwari mumasinagoge avaJudha. Vakanga vana Johaniwo, aiva mubatsiri wavo." 
Acts13:6 Vakati vagura chivi chose kusvikira paPafosi, vakawana mumwe munhu wamashiripiti, aiva muporofita wenhema, muJudha, zita rake rainzi BhariJesu." 
Acts13:7 Aigara pamubati wenyika, ainzi Segio Pauro, munhu akachenjera. Iye ndokudana Bhanabhasi naSauro, achitsvaka kunzwa shoko raMwari." 
Acts13:8 Asi n'anga iyo Erimasi (nokuti ndiro zita rake, kana richishandurwa), akavadzivisa, achitsvaka kutsausa mubati pakutenda." 
Acts13:9 Asi Sauro (ndiye Paurowo), azere noMweya Mutsvene, akamutarisisa, akati," 
Acts13:10 “Iwe, uzere nokunyengera kwose namano akaipa ose, mwanakomana waDhiabhori, muvengi wokururama kwose, hauregi here kutsausa nzira dzakarurama dzaIshe?" 
Acts13:11 Zvino, tarira, ruoko rwaIshe ruri pamusoro pako; uchava bofu, uchaita nguva usingaoni zuva.” Pakarepo mhute nerima zvikamuwira; akapota–pota, achitsvaka vangamusesedza noruoko." 
Acts13:12 Zvino mubati akati achiona zvaitika, akatenda, akashamiswa nedzidziso yaIshe." 
Acts13:13 Zvino Pauro navaiva naye, vakabva Pafosi, ndokusvika Pega muPamufiria; Johani akabva kwavari, ndokudzokera Jerusaremu." 
Acts13:14 Asi ivo vakabva Pega, vakasvika Andiyoku paPisidhia; vakapinda musinagoge nezuva reSabata, ndokugara pasi." 
Acts13:15 Zvino murairo navaporofita zvakati zvarawa, vabati vesinagoge vakatuma shoko kwavari, vachiti, “Varume, hama, kana mune shoko rokuvaraidza vanhu, taurai henyu.”" 
Acts13:16 Ipapo Pauro akasimuka, akavaninira noruoko akati, “Varume VaIsiraeri, nemi munotya Mwari, teererai," 
Acts13:17 Mwari wavanhu ava VaIsiraeri akatsanangura madzibaba edu, akaudza vanhu ava, vachiti vatorwa munyika yeIjipiti; akavabudisa mairi noruoko rune simba," 
Acts13:18 akava nomwoyo murefu nemitoo yavo murenje makore anenge makumi mana," 
Acts13:19 akaparadza marudzi manomwe munyika yeKenani, akavagovera nyika yavo nemijenya, ive nhaka yavo makore anenge mazana mana namakumi mashanu." 
Acts13:20 Shure kwaizvozvo akavapa vatongi kusvikira kumuporofita Samueri. 
Acts13:21 Pashure vakakumbira mambo; Mwari akavapa Sauro, mwanakomana waKisi murume worudzi rwaBhenjamini, makore makumi mana." 
Acts13:22 “Akamubvisa akamutsa Dhavhidhi, kuti ave mambo wavo, waakapupura, achiti, ‘Ndawana Dhavhidhi, mwanakomana waJese murume womwoyo wangu, achaita kuda kwangu kwose.’" 
Acts13:23 Parudzi rwaiyeyo, Mwari akamutsira VaIsiraeri Muponesi Jesu, sezvaakanga avapikira;" 
Acts13:24 iye asati asvika, Johani akamboparidzira vanhu VaIsiraeri rubhabhatidzo rwokutendeuka." 
Acts13:25 Zvino Johani akati opedzisa basa rake, akati, ‘Munoti, ndini aniko? Handizi iye. Asi tarirai, shure kwangu mumwe anouya, wandisakafanira kuti ndisunungure shangu dzetsoka dzake.’" 
Acts13:26 “Varume, hama, vana vorudzi rwaAbhurahamu, navari pakati penyu vanotya Mwari, shoko roruponeso urwu rakatumirwa isu." 
Acts13:27 Nokuti vaigara Jerusaremu navabati vavo, zvavakanga vasingamuzivi iye, kana mazwi avaporofita, anorawa Sabata rimwe nerimwe, vakaazadzisa pakumupa mhaka kwavo." 
Acts13:28 “Kunyangwe vasina kuwana mhosva yorufu kwaari, vakakumbira kuna Pirato kuti auraiwe." 
Acts13:29 Zvino vakati vapedza zvose zvakanyorwa pamusoro pake, vakamuturura pamuti, vakamuviga muhwiro." 
Acts13:30 Asi Mwari wakamumutsa kuvakafa; 
Acts13:31 akaonekwa mazuva mazhinji navakanga vakwira naye Jerusaremu, vachibva Gareriya, avo vari zvapupu zvake zvino kuvanhu." 
Acts13:32 Isu tinokuparidzirai chipikirwa chakaitirwa madzibaba edu. 
Acts13:33 Kuti Mwari akachiita kuvana vedu, achimutsa Jesu; sezvakanyorwawo paPisarema rechipiri, panoti, ‘Ndiwe Mwanakomana wangu, nhasi ndakakubereka.’" 
Acts13:34 Uye kuratidza kuti akamumutsa kuvakafa, kuti arege kuzodzokerazve kuora, akareva kudai, ‘Ndichakupai mikomborero mitsvene inotendwa yaDhavhidhi.’" 
Acts13:35 “Ndokuti anoreva pane rimwe Pisarema, achiti, ‘Hamungaisi Mutsvene wenyu kuti aone kuora.’" 
Acts13:36 Nokuti Dhavhidhi akati aita kuda kwaMwari parudzi rwake, akavata rufu, akavigwa kuna madzibaba ake, akaona kuora." 
Acts13:37 Asi uyu, akamutswa naMwari haana kuora." 
Acts13:38 Naizvozvo varume hama muzive imi, kuti kuregererwa zvivi nouyu, inokuparidzirwai imi." 
Acts13:39 Nouyu, mumwe nomumwe anotenda, anoruramiswa pazvose, zvamakanga musingagoni kururamiswa pazviri nomurairo waMosesi." 
Acts13:40 Naizvozvo chenjerai, kuti murege kuwirwa nezvakarehwa navaporofita, zvinoti," 
Acts13:41 ‘Tarirai, imi vazvidzi, mushamiswe, muparare; Nokuti ndinobata basa pamazuva enyu, basa ramucharamba kutongotenda, kana muchizviudzwa nomunhu.’ ”" 
Acts13:42 Zvino vakati vachibuda musinagoge, vakakumbira zvikuru kuti vaparidzirwezve mashoko iwayo neSabata rinotevera." 
Acts13:43 Zvino vesinagoge vakati vapararira, vaJudha vazhinji navapanduki vainamata Mwari, vakatevera Pauro naBhanabhasi; ivo vakataurirana navo, vakavarayira kuti varambire panyasha dzaMwari." 
Acts13:44 NeSabata rakatevera guta rinenge rose rakaungana kuzonzwa shoko raMwari. 
Acts13:45 Zvino vaJudha vakati vachiona vanhu vazhinji, vakazara negodo, vakaramba zvakarehwa naPauro, vachimhura Mwari." 
Acts13:46 Ipapo Pauro naBhanabhasi vakataura vasingatyi vakati, “Zvakanga zvakafanira kuti shoko raMwari ritange kutaurirwa imi, asi zvamariramba, muchiti, hamufanirwi noupenyu husingaperi, tarirai, zvino toenda kuvahedheni." 
Acts13:47 Nokuti Ishe wakatirayira saizvozvo, achiti, ‘Ndakakuisa kuti uve chiedza chavahedheni, Kuti uve ruponeso kusvikira kumugumo wenyika.’ ”" 
Acts13:48 Zvino vahedheni vakati vachinzwa izvozvo, vakafara, vakakudza shoko raIshe; navose vakanga vatarirwa upenyu husingaperi vakatenda." 
Acts13:49 Shoko raIshe rikaparidzirwa kunyika yose. 
Acts13:50 Asi vaJudha vakakurudzira vakadzi vainamata Mwari, vaikudzwa, navakuru veguta; vakamutsira Pauro naBhanabhasi dambudziko, vakavadzinga munyika yavo." 
Acts13:51 Asi ivo vakazunza guruva patsoka dzavo, vakaenda Ikoniumu." 
Acts13:52 Vadzidzi vakaramba vachizadzwa nomufaro noMweya Mutsvene. 
Acts14:1 Zvino paIkoniumu vakapinda kamwe vose musinagoge ravaJudha, vakataura nokudaro kuti vazhinji zhinji vavaJudha navaGiriki vakatenda." 
Acts14:2 Asi vaJudha vasina kuteerera, vakamutsa mwoyo yavahedheni, kuti vavenge hama." 
Acts14:3 Naizvozvo vakagarapo nguva refu, vachitaura muna Ishe vasingatyi; iye akapupurira shoko renyasha dzake, akavapa simba kuti zviratidzo nezvishamiso zviitwe namaoko avo." 
Acts14:4 Asi vanhu vazhinji veguta vakapesana, vamwe vakava kuvaJudha, vamwe kuvapostori." 
Acts14:5 Zvino vahedheni, navaJudha, navabati vavo vakati vachivavarira kuvaitira zvakaipa nokuvataka namabwe;" 
Acts14:6 ivo vakazviziva, vakatizira Risitira neDhebhe, aiva maguta eRikonia, nokunyika yakapoteredza;" 
Acts14:7 vakaparidzira Vhangeri ikoko. 
Acts14:8 Zvino paRisitira paigara mumwe murume akanga asina simba patsoka dzake, chirema kubva padumbu ramai vake, asina kutongofamba." 
Acts14:9 Iye akanzwa Pauro achitaura; zvino iye akati achimutarisisa, akaona kuti anokutenda kuti angaporeswa," 
Acts14:10 akati nezwi guru, “Mira kwazvo netsoka dzako.” Iye akavazuka, akafamba." 
Acts14:11 Vanhu vazhinji vakati vaona zvaitwa naPauro, vakadanidzira norurimi rwavaRikonia, vachiti, “Vamwari vaburukira kwatiri, vaita savanhu.”" 
Acts14:12 Bhanabhasi vakamutumidza Jupiteri, naPauro Merikuro, nokuti ndiye aiva mutauri mukuru." 
Acts14:13 Ipapo mupristi waJupiteri aiva netemberi yake pamberi peguta, akauya pamusuwo nenzombe namaruva okushonga, achida kuvabayira, ana vanhu vazhinji naye." 
Acts14:14 Zvino vapostori, Bhanabhasi naPauro, vakati vachinzwa izvozvo, vakabvarura nguo dzavo, vakamhanyira pakati pavanhu vazhinji, vakadanidzira," 
Acts14:15 vachiti, “Varume, munoitireiko izvozvi? Nesu tiri vanhu semiwo; tinokuparidzirai mashoko akanaka, kuti mubve pana izvozvo zvisina maturo, mutendeukire kuna Mwari mupenyu akaita denga napasi; negungwa, nezvose zviri mukati mazvo." 
Acts14:16 Iye, panguva dzakapfuura akatendera vahedheni vose kufamba nenzira dzavo." 
Acts14:17 Asi haana kurega kuzvipupurira, achiita zvakanaka, achikupai mvura yokudenga, nenguva yezviyo zvizhinji, achizadza mwoyo yenyu nezvokudya nomufaro.”" 
Acts14:18 Nokutaura kwavo saizvozvo, vakatambura kwazvo kudzivisa vanhu kuti varege kuvabayira." 
Acts14:19 Ipapo vaJudha vakabva Andiyoku neIkoniumu, vakasvika, vakamutsa mwoyo yavanhu, vakataka Pauro namabwe, vakamukwevera kunze kweguta vachiti wafa." 
Acts14:20 Asi vadzidzi vakati vamukomba iye akasimuka, akapinda muguta. Fume mangwana akaenda Dhebhe naBhanabhasi." 
Acts14:21 Vakati vaparidza Vhangeri paguta iro, vakaita vadzidzi vazhinji, ndokudzokera Risitira, neIkoniumu, neAndiyoku," 
Acts14:22 vachisimbisa mweya yavadzidzi, vachivarayira kuti vatsungirire pakutenda, vachiti, “Tinofanira kupinda ushe hwaMwari namatambudziko mazhinji.”" 
Acts14:23 Vakavasanangurira vakuru pachechi imwe neimwe, vakanyengetera, vachizvinyima zvokudya, vakavaisa kuna Ishe, wavaitenda." 
Acts14:24 Vakagura nePisidhia, ndokusvika Pamufiria." 
Acts14:25 Vakati vaparidza shoko paPega, vakaburukira Ataria." 
Acts14:26 Vakabvapo, vakaenda Andiyoku nechikepe, apo pavakanga vaiswa panyasha dzaMwari kubata basa ravakanga vapedzisa zvino." 
Acts14:27 Vakati vasvika, vakaunganidza Chechi, vakarondedzera zvose zvakanga zvaitwa naMwari navo, uye kuti akanga azarurira vahedheni musuwo wokutenda." 
Acts14:28 Vakagara nguva huru navadzidzi. 
Acts15:1 Zvino vamwe vakaburuka Judhiya, vakadzidzisa hama, vachiti, “Kana musingadzingiswi netsika yaMosesi, hamungaponeswi.”" 
Acts15:2 Asi Pauro naBhanabhasi vakapesana kwazvo navo, nokuita nharo navo, vakazotenderana kuti Pauro naBhanabhasi navamwe vavo vakwire Jerusaremu kuvapostori navakuru pamusoro peshoko iri." 
Acts15:3 Naizvozvo vakaperekedzwa nechechi, vakagura neFonishia neSamaria, vakataura zvokutendeuka kwavahedheni; vakafadza zvikuru hama dzose." 
Acts15:4 Zvino vakati vasvika Jerusaremu, vakagamuchirwa nechechi, navapostori, navakuru; vakarondedzera zvose zvakaitwa naMwari navo." 
Acts15:5 Asi vamwe vedzidziso yavaFarisi, vaitenda, vakasimuka, vakati, “Vanofanira kudzingiswa nokurayirwa kuti vachengete murairo waMosesi.”" 
Acts15:6 Ipapo vapostori navakuru vakaungana kuti varangane pamusoro peshoko iri. 
Acts15:7 Zvino nharo huru dzakati dzavapo, Petirosi akasimuka akati kwavari, “Varume, hama munoziva kuti kubva pamazuva akare Mwari akanditsanangura pakati penyu, kuti vahedheni vanzwe shoko reVhangeri nomuromo wangu vatende." 
Acts15:8 Zvino Mwari, muzivi womwoyo, wakavapupurira, akavapa Mweya Mutsvene sesu;" 
Acts15:9 haana kutsaura pakati pedu navo, zvaakanatsa mwoyo yavo nokutenda." 
Acts15:10 Naizvozvo zvino, munoedzireiko Mwari, muchiisa pamitsipa yavadzidzi joko, rakanga risingagoni kutakurwa namadzibaba edu kunyangwe nesu?" 
Acts15:11 Asi tinotenda kuti isu tichaponeswa nenyasha dzaIshe Jesu nomutoo mumwe navo.” 
Acts15:12 Ipapo vanhu vazhinji vose vakaramba vanyerere, vakateerera vanaBhanabhasi naPauro vachirondedzera zviratidzo nezvishamiso, zvakaitwa naMwari navo pakati pavahedheni." 
Acts15:13 Zvino vakati vanyarara, Jakobho akapindura akati, “Varume, hama, nditeererei." 
Acts15:14 Simoni akarondedzera matangiro aMwari kumutsa vahedheni, kuti atore kwavari vanhu vezita rake." 
Acts15:15 Naizvozvo mashoko avaporofita anobvumira izvozvi; sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi," 
Acts15:16 ‘Shure kwaizvozvi ndichadzoka, Ndivake tabhenakeri yaDhavhidhi, yakawa; Ndichavakazve matongo ayo, Ndichiimutsa;" 
Acts15:17 Kuti vakasara kuvanhu vatsvake Ishe, Navahedheni vose vakadanwa nezita rangu," 
Acts15:18 Ndizvo zvinotaura Ishe, unozivisa izvozvi zvose kubva pakutanga kwenyika.’" 
Acts15:19 “Naizvozvi ini ndinoti, ngatirege kugumbusa avo pakati pavahedheni vakatendeukira kuna Mwari;" 
Acts15:20 asi tivanyorere kuti varege zvakashatiswa nezvifananidzo, noupombwe, nezvakadzipwa, neropa." 
Acts15:21 Nokuti Mosesi kubva pamarudzi ekare, aiva navanomuparidza paguta rimwe nerimwe, achiverengwa mumasinagoge Sabata rimwe nerimwe.”" 
Acts15:22 Ipapo vapostori, navakuru, nechechi yose, vakati zvakanaka kuti vatsanangure varume pakati pavo, vavatumire Andiyoku pamwechete naPauro naBhanabhasi, vaiti: Judhasi ainzi Bhasabhasi, naSirasi, vakuru pakati pehama." 
Acts15:23 Vakanyora tsamba, vakaituma navo, yaiti, “Vapostori navakuru pahama, kuhama dzokuvahedheni paAndiyoku, napaSiria, napaSirisia; mufaro!" 
Acts15:24 Zvatakanzwa, kuti vamwe vakabva kwatiri, vatisina kurayira, vakakukanganisai namashoko, vachidziyanisa mweya yenyu," 
Acts15:25 takati nomwoyo mumwe zvakanaka kuti titsanangure varume, tivatumire kwamuri, pamwechete naBhanabhasi naPauro, vadikanwi vedu;" 
Acts15:26 vanhu vakazvidza upenyu hwavo nokuda kwezita raIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu." 
Acts15:27 Zvino tatuma Judhasi naSirasi, ivo vanozokuudzai vamene izvozvi nomuromo." 
Acts15:28 Nokuti Mweya Mutsvene nesu takati zvakanaka, kuti tirege kukutakudzai mutoro mukuru kune zvinhu izvi zvakafanira," 
Acts15:29 zvinoti: Regai zvakabayirwa zvifananidzo, neropa, nezvakadzipwa, noupombwe; kana mukazvidzora pazviri, muchaita zvakanaka. Sarai zvakanaka.”" 
Acts15:30 Zvino vakati vaendeswa, vakaburukira Andiyoku; vakaunganidza vanhu vazhinji, vakavapa tsamba." 
Acts15:31 Ivo vakati vairava, vakafara zvikuru pamusoro pokuvaraidzwa." 
Acts15:32 Judhasi naSirasi, vaiva vaporofita vamene, vakavaraidza hama namashoko mazhinji, nokuvasimbisa." 
Acts15:33 Vakati vagarako nguva, vakaendeswa nehama nomufaro, vakaenda kuna vakanga vavatuma. [" 
Acts15:34 Asi Sirasi akati zvakanaka kusarapo.] 
Acts15:35 Pauro naBhanabhasi vakagara Andiyoku, vachidzidzisa nokuparidza shoko raIshe, navamwe vazhinjiwo." 
Acts15:36 Zvino mamwe mazuva akati apfuura, Pauro akati kuna Bhanabhasi, “Ngatidzokezve tindoshanyira hama muguta rimwe nerimwe matakaparidza shoko raIshe, tione kuti vakadini.”" 
Acts15:37 Zvino Bhanabhasi akanga achida kutora Johaniwo, ainzi Mako;" 
Acts15:38 asi Pauro akati hazvina kunaka kumutora iye, akambovasiya Pamufiria, akasaenda navo kubasa." 
Acts15:39 Ipapo kutsamwirana kukavapo, nokudaro vakaparadzana, Bhanabhasi akatora Mako, akaenda Saipurasi nechikepe;" 
Acts15:40 asi Pauro wakatsanangura Sirasi; akaenda, akaiswa nehama panyasha dzaIshe;" 
Acts15:41 akagura neSiria neKirikia, achisimbisa Chechi." 
Acts16:1 Akasvikawo paDhebhe neRisitira. Zvino ipapo paiva nomumwe mudzidzi, ainzi Timoti, mwanakomana womukadzi mutendi, aiva muJudha; asi baba vake vaiva muGiriki." 
Acts16:2 Iye aipupurirwa zvakanaka nehama dzapaRisitira neIkoniumu. 
Acts16:3 Pauro akada kuti aende naye, akamutora, akamudzingisa nokuda kwavaJudha vaiva kunzvimbo idzo; nokuti vose vakanga vachiziva kuti baba vake muGiriki." 
Acts16:4 Vakafamba namaguta, vakavapa zvirevo zvakatemwa navapostori navakuru vapaJerusaremu, kuti vazvichengete." 
Acts16:5 Naizvozvo Chechi dzakasimbiswa pakutenda, dzikawanda pakuverengwa kwadzo zuva rimwe nerimwe." 
Acts16:6 Vakagura nenyika yeFirigiya neyeGaratiya, vambodziviswa naMweya Mutsvene kuparidza shoko paEzhia." 
Acts16:7 Zvino vakati vasvika pakatarisana neMisia, vakaedza kuenda Bhitinia, asi Mweya waJesu haana kuvatendera." 
Acts16:8 Vakati vapfuura Misia, vakaburukira Tiroasi." 
Acts16:9 Chiratidzo chikaonekwa naPauro usiku; murume weMakedhonia akanga amire, akakumbira zvikuru kwaari, achiti, “Yambukirai Masedhonia, utibatsire.”" 
Acts16:10 Zvino akati aona chiratidzo, pakarepo tikatsvaka kuenda Masedhonia, tichiti, Mwari atidana kuti tindovaparidzira Vhangeri." 
Acts16:11 Naizvozvo takabva Tiroasi nechikepe, tikaruramira Samotirasi; fume mangwana tikasvika Neaporisi;" 
Acts16:12 tikabvapo, tikaenda Firipi, guta guru renyika yeMasedhonia, raiva koroni yeRoma; tikagara mamwe mazuva muguta iro." 
Acts16:13 Nezuva reSabata tikabuda kunze kwesuwo kurwizi, pataiti vanenge vanonyengeterapo; tikagara pasi, tikaparidzira vakadzi vakanga vaunganapo." 
Acts16:14 Zvino mumwe mukadzi, ainzi Ridhia, mutengesi wenguo tsvuku, womusha weTiatira, ainamata Mwari, akatinzwa; Ishe akazarura mwoyo wake, kuti ateerere zvaitaurwa naPauro." 
Acts16:15 Akati abhabhatidzwa, iye naveimba yake, akakumbira zvikuru, achiti, “Kana muchiti ndakatenda kuna Ishe, pindai mumba mangu mugare.” Akatitendisa." 
Acts16:16 Zvino takati tichipinda panzvimbo yokunyengetera, tikasangana nomumwe musikana aiva nomweya wokuuka, aiwanira vatenzi vake mari zhinji nokuuka kwake." 
Acts16:17 Iye akatevera Pauro nesu, akadanidzira, achiti, “Vanhu ava varanda vaMwari Wokumusoro–soro, vanokuparidzirai nzira yokuponeswa nayo.”" 
Acts16:18 Akaita izvozvo mazuva mazhinji. Zvino Pauro akafa neshungu, akatendeuka, akati kumweya, “Ndinokurayira muzita raJesu Kristu kuti ubude kwaari.” Ukabuda nenguva iyeyo." 
Acts16:19 Zvino vatenzi vake vakati vachiona kuti tariro yokufumiswa kwavo yaenda, vakabata Pauro naSirasi, vakavakakatira kudare pamberi pavabati," 
Acts16:20 vakaenda navo kuvatongi, vakati, “Vanhu ava vaJudha, vanopesanisa guta redu," 
Acts16:21 vachiparidza tsika dzatisina kutenderwa kugamuchira, kana kuita, isu vaRoma.”" 
Acts16:22 Ipapo vanhu vazhinji vakavamukira vose, vatongi vakavabvarurira nguo dzavo, vakarayira kuti varohwe neshamhu." 
Acts16:23 Zvino vakati vavarova zvikuru, vakavaisa mutorongo, vakarayira murindi wetorongo kuti avachengete kwazvo." 
Acts16:24 Iye akati arayirwa kudaro, akavaisa mutorongo yomukati, akasunga makumbo avo mumatanda." 
Acts16:25 Zvino panenge pakati pousiku, Pauro naSirasi vakanga vachinyengetera nokuimbira Mwari nziyo; vakanga vakasungwa vakavateerera." 
Acts16:26 Pakarepo kudengenyeka kwenyika kukuru kukavapo, naizvozvo nheyo dzeimba dzikazununguswa; pakarepo misuwo yose yeimba ikazarurwa, nemisungo yavose ikasununguka." 
Acts16:27 Ipapo murindi wetorongo akapepuka, ndokuona mikova yetorongo yakazaruka, akavhomora munondo wake, akada kuzviuraya, achiti vasungwa vatiza." 
Acts16:28 Ipapo Pauro akadanidzira nezwi guru, akati, “Usazvikuvadza, nokuti tiri muno tose.”" 
Acts16:29 Zvino akati akumbira mwenje, akamhanyiramo, ndokuwira pasi pamberi paPauro naSirasi, achibvunda;" 
Acts16:30 akavabudisira kunze, akati, “Vatenzi, ndinofanira kuitei kuti ndiponeswe?”" 
Acts16:31 Vakati, “Tenda kuna Ishe Jesu, ugoponeswa, iwe nemhuri yako.”" 
Acts16:32 Vakaparidza shoko raMwari kwaari navose vaiva mumba make. 
Acts16:33 Akavatora nenguva iyoyo yousiku, akakupa mavanga avo, ndokubhabhatidzwa pakarepo, iye navose vake." 
Acts16:34 Akaenda navo mumba make, ndokuisa zvokudya pamberi pavo, akafara zvikuru, iye nemhuri yake yose, achitenda kuna Mwari." 
Acts16:35 Zvino kwakati kwaedza vatongi vakatuma mapurisa, vachiti, “Sunungurai vanhu vaya.”" 
Acts16:36 Murindi wetorongo akaudza Pauro mashoko iwayo, achiti, “Vatongi vatuma shoko kuti musunungurwe; naizvozvo budai henyu zvino, muende norugare.”" 
Acts16:37 Asi Pauro akati kwavari, “Vakatirova pachena, isu vanhu vaRoma tisina kutongwa, vakatiisa mutorongo; zvino voda kutibudisa chinyararire here? Haiwa kwete! Ngavauye vomene vatibudise.”" 
Acts16:38 Mapurisa akaudza vatongi mashoko iwayo; vakatya vachinzwa kuti vaRoma; 
Acts16:39 vakasvika, vakakumbira zvikuru kwavari; vakavabudisa, mutorongo ndokuvakumbira kuti vabve muguta ravo." 
Acts16:40 Ipapo vakabuda mutorongo, vakapinda mumba maRidhia; vakaona hama, vakavanyaradza, ndokuenda." 
Acts17:1 Zvino vakati vagura neAmifiporisi neAporonia, vakasvika paTesaronika paiva nesinagoge ravaJudha." 
Acts17:2 Zvino Pauro, sezvaaisiita, akapinda kwavari; akataurirana navo zvaMagwaro maSabata matatu," 
Acts17:3 achivazarurira nokuvazivisa, kuti, “Kristu aifanira kutambudzika nokumuka kuvakafa, uye kuti Jesu uyu, wandinokuparidzirai, ndiye Kristu.”" 
Acts17:4 Vamwe vavo vakatendera, vakatevera Pauro naSirasi, navazhinji vavaGiriki, vainamata Mwari, navakadzi vaikudzwa vazhinji." 
Acts17:5 Asi vaJudha vaiva negodo, vakatora vamwe varume vakaipa, dzaiva simbe, vakaunganidza vanhu vazhinji, vakakanganisa guta; vakawira imba yaJasoni, vachida kuvabudisira kuvanhu." 
Acts17:6 Vakati vachivashayiwa, vakakakatira Jasoni nedzimwe hama pamberi pavabati veguta, vakadana, vachiti, “Ava vakakanganisa nyika yose, vakasvika napanowo," 
Acts17:7 Jasoni akavagamuchira; mumba make ava vose vanoita zvinopesana nezvirevo zvaKesari, vachiti, mumwe mambo uripiko, anonzi Jesu.”" 
Acts17:8 Vakapesanisa vanhu navabati veguta, vachinzwa izvozvo." 
Acts17:9 Zvino, vakati vatora rubatso kuna Jasoni navamwe, vakavarega." 
Acts17:10 Pakarepo hama dzikatuma Pauro naSirasi Bheria usiku. Ivo vakati vachisvikapo, vakapinda musinagoge ravaJudha." 
Acts17:11 Ava vakanga vakanaka kukunda veTesaronika, vakagamuchira shoko nomwoyo wose, vachinzvera Magwaro zuva rimwe nerimwe, kana zvinhu izvozvo zviri izvo." 
Acts17:12 Naizvozvo vazhinji vavo vakatenda, navakadzi vaikudzwa vavaGiriki, navarume vazhinji." 
Acts17:13 Asi vaJudha veTesaronika, vakati vachinzwa kuti shoko raMwari roparidzwa naPauro paBheria, vakasvikawo ipapo, vakamutsa nokupesanisa vazhinji." 
Acts17:14 Ipapo hama dzakatuma Pauro pakarepo kusvikira kugungwa, asi Sirasi naTimoti vakasarapo." 
Acts17:15 Zvino avo vakaperekedza Pauro, vakamusvitsa Ateni; vakati varayirwa kuudza Sirasi naTimoti, kuti vakurumidze kuuya kwaari, vakabva." 
Acts17:16 Zvino Pauro, achakavagarira paAteni, akanzwa shungu pamwoyo, achiona kuti guta rizere nezvifananidzo." 
Acts17:17 Naizvozvo akataurirana musinagoge navaJudha, navainamata Mwari, napadare zuva rimwe nerimwe, navaakasangana navo." 
Acts17:18 Zvino vamwe vakachenjera vavaEpikure navaSitoiki, vakaita nharo naye; vamwe vakati, “Ko uyu mutauri wezvisina maturo anoda kureveiko?” Vamwezve vakati, “Anenge muparidzi wavamwari vasingazikanwi; nokuti wakavaparidzira Jesu nokumuka kwavakafa.”" 
Acts17:19 Ipapo vakamubata, vakamuisa paAreopago, vakati, “Ngatinzwewo kuti kudzidzisa uku kutsva, kunotaurwa newe, ndokweiko?" 
Acts17:20 Nokuti unoreva zvimwe zvinoshamisa panzeve dzedu; naizvozvo tinoda kunzwa, kuti zvinhu izvi ndezveiko?”" 
Acts17:21 (Zvino vaAteni vose, navatorwa vaigarapo, vaingofarira chinhu chimwechete, kutaura kana kunzwa chinhu chitsva.)" 
Acts17:22 Zvino Pauro, amire pakati peAreopago akati, “Imi varume veAteni, pazvinhu zvose ndinoona kuti munonamata zvikuru." 
Acts17:23 Nokuti ndakati ndichipfuura, ndichicherechedza zvamunonamata, ndakawanawo atari yakanyorwa, ‘KUNA MWARI ASINGAZIKANWI.’ Zvino chamunonamata musingachizivi, ndicho chandinokuparidzirai." 
Acts17:24 Mwari akasika nyika nezvose zviri mairi, iye Tenzi wedenga napasi, haagari mutemberi dzakaitwa namaoko." 
Acts17:25 Haashumirwi namaoko avanhu, saachinge achishayiwa chinhu, zvaari iye amene anopa vose upenyu, nokufema, nezvose;" 
Acts17:26 akaita marudzi ose avanhu, achibva kuno mumwechete, kuti agare pose panyika; ambotara nguva dzavakatemerwa, nemiganhu yokugara kwavo;" 
Acts17:27 kuti vatsvake Mwari, zvimwe vamutsvangadzire, vamuwane, kunyangwe asiri kure nomumwe nomumwe wedu." 
Acts17:28 Nokuti maari tino upenyu, tinofamba, tiripo; sezvavakareva vamwe vanyori venziyo vokwenyu, vachiti, ‘Nokuti tiri rudzi rwakewo.’" 
Acts17:29 “Zvatiri rudzi rwaMwari, hatifaniri kuti uMwari hwakafanana nendarama, kana sirivha, kana ibwe, zvakavezwa noumhizha kana nokuchenjera kwomunhu." 
Acts17:30 Naizvozvo Mwari akarega hake kurangarira nguva dzokusaziva; asi zvino anoraira vanhu vose kwose–kwose kuti vatendeuke. 
Acts17:31 Nokuti akatara zuva, raachatonga nyika naro nokururama, nomurume waakagadza; akasimbisa shoko iro kuna vose, pakumumutsa kuvakafa.”" 
Acts17:32 Zvino vakati vachinzwa zvokumuka kwavakafa, vamwe vakaseka, asi vamwe vakati, “Tichazokunzwazve pamusoro paizvozvi.”" 
Acts17:33 Naizvozvo Pauro akabuda pakati pavo. 
Acts17:34 Asi vamwe varume vakamunamatira, vakatenda; pakati pavo kwaiva naDhionisio, muAreopago, nomukadzi ainzi Dhamari, navamwe pamwechete navo." 
Acts18:1 Shure kwaizvozvo, Pauro akabva Ateni, akasvika Korinde;" 
Acts18:2 akawana mumwe muJudha, ainzi Akwira, worudzi rwavePondusi, achangobva Itariya, naPirisira mukadzi wake; (nokuti Kiraudhio akanga arayira kuti vaJudha vose vabve Roma); akaenda kwavari;" 
Acts18:3 zvino zvaakanga ane basa rimwe navo, akagara navo vachibata; nokuti basa ravo raiva rokuita matende." 
Acts18:4 Sabata rimwe nerimwe akataurirana navo musinagoge, akaedza kugombedzera vaJudha navaGiriki." 
Acts18:5 Zvino Sirasi naTimoti vakati vachizoburuka vachibva Masedhonia, Pauro akamanikidzwa neshoko, achipupurira vaJudha kwazvo kuti Jesu ndiye Kristu." 
Acts18:6 Zvino vakati vachimudzivisa, nokumutuka, akazunza nguo dzake, akati kwavari, “Ropa renyu ngarive pamusoro penyu; ndakachena, kubva zvino ndichaenda kuvahedheni.”" 
Acts18:7 Akabvapo, akapinda mumba momumwe, ainzi Tito Jusuto, ainamata Mwari, imba yake yaiva pedyo nesinagoge." 
Acts18:8 NaKirisipo, mukuru wesinagoge, akatenda kuna Ishe naveimba yake yose; navazhinji veKorinde vakanzwa, vakatenda, vakabhabhatidzwa." 
Acts18:9 Zvino Ishe akati kuna Pauro usiku nechiratidzo, “Usatya hako, asi taura, usanyarara;" 
Acts18:10 nokuti ini ndinewe; hapana munhu angakumukira akakuitira zvakaipa, nokuti ndina vanhu vazhinji muguta rino.”" 
Acts18:11 Akagarapo gore rimwe nemwedzi mitanhatu, achidzidzisa shoko raMwari pakati pavo." 
Acts18:12 Zvino Gario akati ava mubati weAkaya, vaJudha vakamukira Pauro nomwoyo mumwe, vakauya naye pachigaro chokutonga," 
Acts18:13 vachiti, “Uyu anogombedzera vanhu kuti vanamate Mwari nenzira isingatenderwi nomurairo.”" 
Acts18:14 Zvino Pauro akati oda kushamisa muromo wake, Gario akati kuvaJudha, “Dai yaiva mhosva yezvisakarurama, kana kutadza kwakaipa, ndaifanira kuva nomwoyo murefu kwamuri, imi vaJudha." 
Acts18:15 Asi kana dziri nharo pamusoro pamashoko namazita nomurairo wenyu, tambai henyu imi mhosva iyo; ini handidi kuva mutongi waizvozvo.”" 
Acts18:16 Akavadzinga pachigaro chokutonga. 
Acts18:17 Zvino vose vakabata Sositeni, mukuru wesinagoge, vakamurova pamberi pechigaro chokutonga; asi Gario haana kuva nehanya nechinhu chimwe chaizvozvo." 
Acts18:18 Pauro akati agarapo mazuva mazhinji, akaonekana nehama, akabvapo, akaenda Siria nechikepe, ana Pirisira naAkwira, aveura musoro wake paKenikiria, nokuti akanga apika." 
Acts18:19 Vakasvika Efeso, akavasiyapo; asi iye amene akapinda musinagoge akataurirana navaJudha." 
Acts18:20 Zvino vakati vachikumbira kuti agare navo nguva refu, haana kutenda;" 
Acts18:21 asi wakaonekana navo, achiti, “Ndichadzokerazve kwamuri, kana Mwari achida,” akabva Efeso nechikepe." 
Acts18:22 Akati asvika Sizaria, akakwira kundokwazisa Chechi, akaburukira Andiyoku." 
Acts18:23 Akati agarapo nguva, akabva, akagura nenyika dzeGaratia neFirigia achidzitevedzanisa, achisimbisa vadzidzi vose." 
Acts18:24 Zvino mumwe muJudha ainzi Aporo, worudzi rwapaArekizandiria, murume akanga akadzidza zvikuru, akasvika Efeso; akanga ane simba pamagwaro." 
Acts18:25 Uyu akanga adzidziswa nzira yaIshe, akashingaira nomweya, achitaura nokunatsodzidzisa zvaJesu, achiziva rubhabhatidzo rwaJohani bedzi." 
Acts18:26 Iye akatanga kutaura musinagoge asingatyi. Zvino Pirisira naAkwira vakati vamunzwa, vakamutora, vakanatsomududzira nzira yaMwari." 
Acts18:27 Zvino akati achida kuyambukira Akaya, hama dzikamusimbisa, vakanyorera vadzidzi kuti vamugamuchire. Zvino akati asvika, akabatsira zvikuru ivo vakatenda nenyasha." 
Acts18:28 Nokuti akakunda vaJudha nesimba pachena, achiratidza naMagwaro, kuti Jesu ndiye Kristu." 
Acts19:1 Zvino Aporo achiri paKorinde, Pauro wakati agura namativi enyika okumusoro, akasvika Efeso, akawana vamwe vadzidzi," 
Acts19:2 akati kwavari, “Makagamuchira Mweya Mutsvene pakutenda kwenyu here?” Vakati kwaari, “Kwete, hatina kutongonzwa kuti Mweya Mutsvene aripo.”" 
Acts19:3 Akati, “Ko makabhabhatidzwa norubhabhatidzo rupiko?” Vakati, “Norubhabhatidzo rwaJohani.”" 
Acts19:4 Zvino Pauro akati, “Johani akabhabhatidzwa norubhabhatidzo rwokutendeuka, achiudza vanhu kuti vatende kuna iye anozouya shure kwake, iye Jesu.”" 
Acts19:5 Vakati vazvinzwa izvozvo, vakabhabhatidzwa muzita raIshe Jesu." 
Acts19:6 Zvino Pauro akati aisa maoko ake pamusoro pavo, Mweya Mutsvene akauya pamusoro pavo, vakataura nendimi, vakaporofita." 
Acts19:7 Ivavo vose vaiva varume vanenge gumi navaviri. 
Acts19:8 Zvino akapinda musinagoge, akataura asingatyi mwedzi mitatu, achitaurirana navo, achivagombedzera namashoko oushe hwaMwari." 
Acts19:9 Asi vamwe vakati vachiomesa mwoyo, vasingateereri, vachizvidza Nzira iyo pamberi pavazhinji, akabva kwavari, akatsaura vadzidzi, akataurirana navo zuva rimwe nerimwe muchikoro chaTirano." 
Acts19:10 Izvozvo zvikaitwa makore maviri; nokudaro vose vakanga vagere paEzhia vakanzwa shoko raIshe, vaJudha navaGiriki." 
Acts19:11 NaMwari akaita masimba anoshamisa namaoko aPauro," 
Acts19:12 nokudaro micheka nenguo, zvaibva pamuviri wake, zvaiiswa kuvarwere, zvirwere zvikabva kwavari, nemweya yakaipa ikabuda." 
Acts19:13 Zvino vamwe vaJudha, vauki, vaipota–pota, vakaidza kudana zita raIshe Jesu pamusoro pavaiva nemweya yakaipa, vachiti, “Ndinokupikirai naJesu unoparidzwa naPauro.”" 
Acts19:14 Vaiva vanakomana vanomwe vomumwe muJudha, ainzi Sikeva, Mupristi Mukuru, vaiita izvozvo." 
Acts19:15 Mweya wakaipa ukapindura, ukati kwavari, “Jesu ndinomuziva, naPauro ndinomuziva, asi imi ndimi vanaaniko?”" 
Acts19:16 Ipapo munhu aiva nomweya wakaipa akavamukira simba, akavakurira vose vari vaviri, akavakunda; nokudaro vakatiza mumba imomo, vasina nguo, vakuvadzwa." 
Acts19:17 Izvozvo zvikazikanwa navose, vaJudha navaGiriki, vakanga vagere Efeso vakatya vose, zita raIshe rikakudzwa." 
Acts19:18 Zvino vazhinji vavakanga vatenda vakauya, vakareurura, nokurondedzera zvamabasa avo." 
Acts19:19 Navamwe vazhinji vaiita zveun'anga, vakaunganidza mabhuku avo, vakadzipisa pamberi pavose; vakaverenga mutengo wadzo, vakawana kuti waiva masirivha ane zviuru zvina makumi mashanu." 
Acts19:20 Naizvozvo shoko raIshe rikakura nesimba, rikakunda." 
Acts19:21 Izvozvo zvakati zvapedziswa, Pauro akafunga mumwoyo make kuenda Jerusaremu, kana ambogura napaMasedhonia neAkaa, achiti, “Kana ndamboenda ikoko, ndinofanira kundowana Romawo.”" 
Acts19:22 Zvino akatumira Masedhonia vaviri vavaimushumira, vanaTimoti naErasito, iye amene akagara Ezhia nguva duku." 
Acts19:23 Zvino nenguva iyo bope guru rikavapo pamusoro peNzira iyo. 
Acts19:24 Nokuti mumwe, ainzi Dhemetirio, mupfuri wesirivha, waiita zvitemberi zvaDhiyana zvesirivha, waifumisa zvikuru mhizha dzapo." 
Acts19:25 Akavaunganidza ivo pamwechete navamwe vabati vezvakadaro, akati, “Varume, munoziva kuti nebasa iri tinowana pfuma yedu." 
Acts19:26 Zvino munoona, nokunzwa, kuti Pauro uyu akatendisa nokutsausa vazhinji, pasati pari paEfeso bedzi, asi panenge paEzhia yose, achiti, zvakaitwa namaoko havazi vamwari." 
Acts19:27 Zvino njodzi ndiyo kuti hahuzi humhizha hwedu bedzi hungazvidzwa, asi kuti temberi yamwarikadzi mukuru Dhiyana ichashorwa, naiye amene, anonamatwa paEzhia yose nenyika yose, abviswe paukuru hwake.”" 
Acts19:28 Zvino vakati vachinzwa izvozvo, vakafa neshungu kwazvo, vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Dhiana wavaEfeso mukuru!”" 
Acts19:29 Guta rikakanganiswa kwazvo; vakamhanyira nomwoyo mumwe panzvimbo paitambwa, vabata Gayo naArisitakusi, varume veMasedhonia, vaiperekedza Pauro." 
Acts19:30 Zvino Pauro akada kupinda kuvanhu, vadzidzi vakasamutendera." 
Acts19:31 Navamwe vakuru veEzhia, vaiva shamwari dzake, vakatuma shoko kwaari, vachikumbira zvikuru kwaari kuti arege kupinda panzvimbo paitambwa." 
Acts19:32 Zvino vamwe vakadanidzira zvimwe, vamwe zvimwezve; nokuti ungano yakanga yanyonganiswa, vazhinji vasingazivi zvavakaunganira." 
Acts19:33 Ipapo vakabudisa Arekizanda mukati mavanhu vazhinji, vaJudha vachimusundira mberi; zvino Arekizanda akaninira noruoko, achida kuzvidavirira pamberi pavanhu." 
Acts19:34 Ipapo vakati vachiona kuti iye muJudha, izwi rimwe rikamuka kuna vose, vakadanidzira nguva dzinenge mbiri, vachiti, “Dhiyana wavaEfeso mukuru!”" 
Acts19:35 Zvino munyori weguta akanyaradza vanhu, akati, “Varume veEfeso, munhu ndoupiko asingazivi, kuti guta ravaEfeso ndiwo muchengeti wetemberi yaDhiyana mukuru nowomufananidzo akaburuka kudenga?" 
Acts19:36 Zvazvisingagoni kurambwa izvozvi, maifanira kunyarara musingaiti chinhu nokusarangarira kwazvo." 
Acts19:37 Nokuti mauya navarume ava, vasati vari mbavha dzetemberi kana vashori vamwarikadzi wedu." 
Acts19:38 Zvino kana Dhemetirio nedzimwe mhizha naye vane mhosva nomunhu, misi yokutonga iripo, navatongi varipo; ngavakwirirane havo." 
Acts19:39 “Asi kana muchitsvaka chimwe chinhu pamusoro pedzimwe mhosva, zvingatemwa paungano yakafanira." 
Acts19:40 Nokuti njodzi ndiyo kuti tingakwirirwa pamusoro pebope ranhasi, zvakusina mhosva; kana chiri chinhu ichi hatingagoni kupindura pamusoro pemhere–mhere iyi.”" 
Acts19:41 Akati ataura izvozvo, akaendesa ungano." 
Acts20:1 Bopoto rakati ranyarara, Pauro akadana vadzidzi, akavaraira, ndokuonekana navo, akabva achida kuenda Masedhonia." 
Acts20:2 Akagura namativi enyika idzo, akarayira vatendi namashoko mazhinji, ndokusvika panyika yavaGiriki." 
Acts20:3 Akati agara mwedzi mitatu, rangano yakaipa ikaitwa navaJudha pamusoro pake, oda kuenda Siria nechikepe, akati ndodzokera napaMasedhonia." 
Acts20:4 Akaperekedzwa naSopato weBhereya, mwanakomana waPiro; naArisitakusi naSekundo veTesaronika; naGayo weDhebhe, naTimotio; uye Tikiko naTirofimo veEzhia." 
Acts20:5 Ivo vakatungamira, vakatimirira paTiroasi." 
Acts20:6 Isu tikabva Firipi nechikepe mazuva ezvingwa zvisina mbiriso apfuura; tikasvika kwavari paTiroasi namazuva mashanu; tikagarapo mazuva manomwe. 
Acts20:7 Zvino nomusi wokutanga wevhiki, takaungana kuti timedure chingwa, Pauro akataurirana navo, achida kuenda mangwana; akaramba achiparidza shoko kusvikira pakati pousiku." 
Acts20:8 Kwakanga kune mwenje mizhinji muimba yokumusoro, matakanga taungana." 
Acts20:9 Zvino pahwindo pakanga pagere rimwe jaya, rainzi Yutiko, rikabatwa nehope kwazvo; zvino Pauro, akati achingoramba achiparidza, iye akabatwa nehope, akawira pasi, achibva paimba yechitatu yokumusoro, akasimudzwa afa." 
Acts20:10 Ipapo Pauro akaburuka, akazviwisira pamusoro pake, akamufungatira, akati, “Musaita bopoto, nokuti mweya wake uchiri maari.”" 
Acts20:11 Akakwira, akamedura chingwa, akadya, akataura navo nguva refu kusvikira kuchiedza, ndokuenda." 
Acts20:12 Vakauya nomukomana ari mupenyu, vakanyaradzwa kwazvo." 
Acts20:13 Asi isu takatungamirira kuchikepe, tikaenda Asosi, tichida kutora Pauro ipapo, nokuti akanga arayira saizvozvo, iye achida kufamba namakumbo." 
Acts20:14 Tikati tasangana naye paAsosi, tikamutora, tikandosvika Mitirene;" 
Acts20:15 tikabva ipapo nechikepe, fume mangwana tikasvika pakatarisana neKiosi; fume mangwana tikapfuura napaSamosi; fume mangwanazve tikasvika Miretusi." 
Acts20:16 Nokuti Pauro akanga ati, ndichapfuura Efeso nechikepe, kuti arege kunonoka paEzhia; nokuti akanga achikurumidza kuti kana aizvigona ave Jerusaremu nezuva rePendekositi." 
Acts20:17 Zvino iye ari paMiretusi, akatumira Efeso kundodana vakuru vechechi." 
Acts20:18 Vakati vasvika kwaari, akati kwavari, “Imi munoziva mugariro wangu pakati penyu nguva dzose, kubva pazuva rokutanga randakasvika naro paEzhia;" 
Acts20:19 ndichibatira Ishe nokuzvininipisa zvikuru, nemisodzi, namatambudziko akandiwira nerangano dzakaipa dzavaJudha;" 
Acts20:20 kuti handina kutya kukuparidzirai zvingakubatsirai nokukudzidzisai pachena padzimba dzose; 
Acts20:21 ndichipupurira kwazvo vaJudha navaGiriki, kuti vatendeukire kuna Mwari, nokutenda kuna Ishe wedu Jesu." 
Acts20:22 “Zvino tarirai, ndinoenda Jerusaremu, ndasungwa mweya wangu, ndisingazivi zvichandiwira ikoko;" 
Acts20:23 asi kuti Mweya Mutsvene unondipupurira kwazvo muguta rimwe nerimwe, kuti kusungwa nenhamo zvakandigarira." 
Acts20:24 Asi handina hanya noupenyu hwangu, handihudi, kuti ndipedze rwendo rwangu nebasa randakapiwa naIshe Jesu, rokupupura kwazvo Vhangeri yenyasha dzaMwari." 
Acts20:25 Zvino tarirai, ndinoziva kuti imi mose, vandakafamba pakati penyu, ndichiparidza ushe hwaMwari, hamuchazooni chiso changu." 
Acts20:26 Naizvozvo ndinokupupurirai nhasi kuti ndakachena paropa ravanhu vose. 
Acts20:27 Nokuti handina kutya kukuparidzirai kuda kwose kwaMwari. 
Acts20:28 Zvichenjerei imi, neboka rose ramakaitirwa vatariri varo naMweya Mutsvene, kuti mufudze Chechi yaMwari, yaakatenga neropa rake." 
Acts20:29 “Ini ndinoziva kuti kana ndaenda, mapere anoparadza achapinda pakati penyu, asingaregi boka." 
Acts20:30 Uye, napakati penyu chaipo pachamuka varume, vachataura zvinopesanisa, kuti vatsause vadzidzi vavatevere." 
Acts20:31 Naizvozvo rindai, murangarire kuti makore matatu handina kurega usiku namasikati kurayira mumwe nomumwe nemisodzi." 
Acts20:32 “Zvino ndinokuisai kuna Ishe, neshoko renyasha dzake, iye ane simba rokukuvakisai, nokukupai nhaka pakati pavakaitwa vatsvene vose." 
Acts20:33 Handina kuchochora sirivha, kana ndarama, kana nguo dzomunhu mumwe." 
Acts20:34 Munoziva imi mumene, kuti maoko awa akabatsira kushayiwa kwangu nokwavanhu vandaiva navo." 
Acts20:35 Pazvinhu zvose ndakakuratidzai, kuti muchibata muchidai, munofanira kubatsira vasina simba, nokurangarira mashoko aIshe Jesu, sezvakataura amene achiti, ‘Kupa kuno mufaro chaiwo kupfuura kugamuchira.’ ”" 
Acts20:36 Akati ataura izvozvo, akapfugama, akanyengetera navo vose." 
Acts20:37 Vakachema zvikuru vose; vakawira pamutsipa waPauro, vakaonekana naye nokumutsvoda," 
Acts20:38 vane shungu kwazvo neshoko raakataura rokuti havachazooni chiso chake. Ipapo vakamuperekedzera kuchikepe. 
Acts21:1 Zvino takati taparadzana navo, tikabva nechikepe, tikarurama, tikasvika Kose; fume mangwana tikasvika Rodhe; tikabvapo, tikasvika Patara." 
Acts21:2 Takati tawanapo chikepe, chaiyambukira Fonisha, tikapinda mukati macho, tikaenda." 
Acts21:3 Takati taona Saipurasi, tikaisiya kuruboshwe, tichienda Siria, tikasvika Taya; nokuti chikepe chaifanira kututunura mutoro ipapo;" 
Acts21:4 zvino takati tawanapo vadzidzi, tikagarapo mazuva manomwe; ivo vakati nomweya kuna Pauro kuti arege kukwira Jerusaremu." 
Acts21:5 Zvino takati tapedzapo mazuva, tikabva, tikaenda; ivo vose, navakadzi navana, vakatiperekedza kusvikira tabuda paguta; ipapo tikafugama pamhenderekedzo, tikanyengetera." 
Acts21:6 Tikaonekana, isu tikaenda kuchikepe, ivo vakadzokera kumusha kwavo." 
Acts21:7 Isu takati tapedza rwendo tichibva Taya, tikasvika Toremaisi, tikakwazisa hama, ndokuswera zuva rimwe navo." 
Acts21:8 Fume mangwana tikabvapo, tikasvika Sizaria; ipapo tikapinda mumba maFiripi, Muvhangeri, mumwe wavanomwe, tikagara naye." 
Acts21:9 Iye akanga ana vakunda vana, mhandara, vaiporofita." 
Acts21:10 Zvino takati tichigarapo mazuva mazhinji, mumwe muporofita, ainzi Akabho, akaburuka achibva Judhiya," 
Acts21:11 akauya kwatiri, akatora bhanhire raPauro, akazvisunga makumbo namaoko ake, akati, “Mweya Mutsvene anoreva kudai, saizvozvo vaJudha paJerusaremu vachasunga murume, mwene webhandi iri, nokumuisa pamaoko avahedheni.”" 
Acts21:12 Takati tichinzwa izvozvo, isu navamwe vaipapo tikakumbira zvikuru kwaari, kuti arege kukwira Jerusaremu." 
Acts21:13 Ipapo Pauro akapindura, akati, “Munoiteiko, muchichema nokuputsa mwoyo wangu? Nokuti ini handina kuzvigadzirira kusungwa bedzi, asi kunyangwe kufira zita raIshe Jesu paJerusaremu.”" 
Acts21:14 Zvino akati achiramba kukundwa, tikanyarara, tikati, “Kuda kwaIshe ngakuitwe.”" 
Acts21:15 Mazuva iwayo akati apera, tikarongedza, tikakwira Jerusaremu." 
Acts21:16 Navamwe vadzidzi veSizaria vakaenda nesu, vakauyawo nomumwe, ainzi Minasoni, mudzidzi wakare, weSaipurasi, wataindogara naye." 
Acts21:17 Zvino takati tichisvika Jerusaremu, hama dzikatigamuchira nomufaro." 
Acts21:18 Fume mangwana Pauro akapinda nesu kuna Jakobho; navakuru vakanga varipo vose. 
Acts21:19 Akavakwazisa, ndokuvarondedzera, chimwe nechimwe, zvakaitwa naMwari pakati pavahedheni nebasa rake." 
Acts21:20 Ivo vakati vazvinzwa, vakakudza Mwari, vakati kwaari, “Hama, unoona kuti varipo vane zviuru zvamazana zvizhinji zvavaJudha vakatenda; vose vanoshingairira murairo;" 
Acts21:21 zvino vakaudzwa kuti iwe unodzidzisa vaJudha vose, vari pakati pavahedheni, kuti varambe Mosesi, uchiti, varege kudzingisa vana vavo, kana kufamba netsika dzomurairo." 
Acts21:22 Zvino todiniko? Vachanzwa havo kuti wasvika. 
Acts21:23 Naizvozvo ita izvi zvatinotaura kwauri, tina varume vana vakazvisunga nokupika;" 
Acts21:24 uvatore, uzvinatse pamwechete navo, uvaripire, vagoveura misoro yavo; ipapo vose vachaziva, kuti haazi mashoko ezvokwadi, avakaudzwa pamusoro pako; asi kuti iwewo unofamba zvakanaka, uchichengeta murairo umene." 
Acts21:25 Asi kana vari vahedheni vakatenda, takavanyorera, tichiti vazvidzore pane zvakabayirwa zvifananidzo, neropa, nezvakadzipwa, noupombwe.”" 
Acts21:26 Ipapo Pauro akatora varume avo, akazvinatsa pamwechete navo nezuva rakatevera, akapinda mutemberi, kuti azivise kupera kwamazuva okunatsa, kusvikira mumwe nomumwe abayirwa chibayiro." 
Acts21:27 Zvino mazuva manomwe akati opera, vaJudha veEzhia vakamuona mutemberi, vakamutsa vanhu vazhinji, vakamubata," 
Acts21:28 vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Varume VaIsiraeri, batsirai! Uyu ndiye munhu anodzidzisa vanhu kwose–kwose zvinopesana navanhu, nomurairo, nenzvimbo ino; uyezve akauya navaGiriki mutemberi, akasvibisa nzvimbo ino tsvene.”" 
Acts21:29 Nokuti vakanga vaona Tirofimo muEfeso, anaye muguta, vakati zvimwe Pauro apinda naye mutemberi." 
Acts21:30 Ipapo guta rose rakanyonganiswa, vanhu vakamhanyira pamwechete; vakabata Pauro, vakamukwevera kunze kwetemberi, misuwo ikazarirwa pakarepo." 
Acts21:31 Zvino vakati vachitsvaka kumuuraya, shoko rikakwira kumukuru wechiuru chamazana, kuti Jerusaremu rose ranyonganiswa." 
Acts21:32 Iye akatora pakarepo varwi vakuru vezana, akaburuka achimhanyira kwavari; ivo vakati vachiona mukuru wechiuru chamazana navarwi, vakarega kurova Pauro." 
Acts21:33 “Zvino mukuru wechiuru chamazana akaswedera, akamubata, ndokurayira kuti asungwe nengetani mbiri; akabvunza kuti ndiani, uye kuti aiteiko.”" 
Acts21:34 Zvino vamwe pakati pavazhinji vakadanidzira chimwe chinhu, vamwe chimwe chinhu; zvino iye asingagoni kuziva chokwadi nokuda kwebopoto, akarayira kuti vamuise kuimba yavarwi." 
Acts21:35 Akati achisvika pazvikwiriso, akaita sokutakurwa navarwi;" 
Acts21:36 nokuti vanhu vazhinji vakatevera, vachidanidzira, vachiti, “Mubvise!”" 
Acts21:37 Zvino oda kupinzwa muimba yavarwi, Pauro akati kumukuru wechiuru chamazana, “Ndingataura chimwe nemi here?” Iye akati, “Unoziva chiGiriki here?" 
Acts21:38 Ko hauzi uya muIjipiti, akadeya kukanganisa vanhu panguva yapfuura, akaenda navaurayi vane zviuru zvina kurenje here?”" 
Acts21:39 Ipapo Pauro akati, “Ini ndiri muJudha weTasasi muSirisia, munhu weguta rakakurumbira. Ndinokumbira kuti munditendere nditaure navanhu.”" 
Acts21:40 Zvino akati amutendera, Pauro akamira pazvikwiriso, akaninira vanhu noruoko rwake; zvino vakati vanyarara kwazvo, akataura norurimi rweChiHebheru akati." 
Acts22:1 “Varume, hama, namadzibaba, inzwai kuzvidavirira kwangu pamberi penyu zvino.”" 
Acts22:2 Ivo vakati vachinzwa, kuti wotaura navo norurimi rweChiHebheru, vakanyanya kunyarara. Iye akati," 
Acts22:3 “Ini ndiri muJudha, ndakaberekwa paTasasi muSirisia, asi ndakarerwa muguta rino, pamakumbo aGamarieri, ndikadzidziswa netsika kwadzo dzomurairo wamadzibaba edu, ndichishingairira Mwari, semi mose nhasi;" 
Acts22:4 ndikatambudza veNzira iyi kusvikira pakuuraya, ndichisunga varume navakadzi nokuvaisa mutorongo," 
Acts22:5 Mupristi Mukuru sezvaangandipupurirawo namakurukota ose; ndikapiwa tsamba navo kuhama, ndikaenda Dhamasikosi kuti ndiise Jerusaremu avo vaigarako, vakasungwa, kuti varohwe." 
Acts22:6 “Zvino ndakati ndichifamba, ndoswedera Dhamasikosi, anenge masikati, pakarepo ndikapenyerwa kwose nechiedza chikuru, chaibva kudenga." 
Acts22:7 Ndikawira pasi, ndikanzwa izwi richiti kwandiri, ‘Sauro, Sauro, unonditambudzireiko?’" 
Acts22:8 “Ndikapindura, ndikati, ‘Ndimi aniko Ishe?’ Akati kwandiri, ‘Ndini Jesu weNazareta, waunotambudza.’" 
Acts22:9 Zvino vaiva neni vakaona chiedza, asi havana kunzwa izwi rowakataura neni." 
Acts22:10 “Ndikati, ‘Ndodiniko, Ishe?’ Ishe akati kwandiri, ‘Simuka, uende Dhamasikosi, apo uchaudzwa zvose zvakatarwa kuti uzviite.’" 
Acts22:11 Zvino zvandakanga ndisingagoni kuona nokupenya kwechiedza icho, ndikasesedzwa noruoko navaiva neni, ndikasvika Dhamasikosi." 
Acts22:12 “Zvino mumwe murume, ainzi Ananiasi, munhu ainamata Mwari sezvinoreva murairo, aipupurirwa zvakanaka navaJudha vose vakanga vagerepo," 
Acts22:13 akauya kwandiri, akamira, akati kwandiri, ‘Sauro, hama, chiona!’ Nenguva iyo ndikamuona." 
Acts22:14 Iye akati, ‘Mwari wamadzibaba edu akakutsanangura, kuti uzive kuda kwake, nokumuona iye wakarurama, nokunzwa izwi, rinobva mumuromo make." 
Acts22:15 Nokuti iwe uchava chapupu chake kuvanhu vose chezvawakaona nezvawakanzwa. 
Acts22:16 Zvino uchanonokereiko? Simuka, ubhabhatidzwe, usukwe zvivi zvako, udane zita rake.’" 
Acts22:17 “Zvino ndakati ndadzokera Jerusaremu, ndichinyengetera mutemberi, ndikaita sokubatwa mweya," 
Acts22:18 ndikamuona, achiti kwandiri, ‘Kurumidza, ubve Jerusaremu zvino–zvino, nokuti havangagamuchiri kupupura kwako pamusoro pangu.’" 
Acts22:19 Ipapo ndikati, ‘Ishe, vanoziva vamene kuti ini ndaiisa mutorongo, nokurova mumasinagoge, avo vaitenda kwamuri;" 
Acts22:20 uye, musi wakadururwa ropa raSitefani, chapupu chenyu, neniwo ndakanga ndimirepo, ndichibvumira, ndikachengeta nguo dzavaimuuraya.’" 
Acts22:21 “Ipapo akati kwandiri, ‘Enda, ndichakutuma kure kuvahedheni.’ ”" 
Acts22:22 Vakamuteerera kusvikira pashoko iro; ipapo vakadanidzira, vachiti, “Akadai ngaabviswe panyika; nokuti haafaniri kurarama.”" 
Acts22:23 Vakadanidzira, vakakandira nguo dzavo pasi, vachikushira ivhu kudenga," 
Acts22:24 mukuru wechiuru chamazana akarayira, kuti aiswe kuimba yavarwi, achiti abvunzwe nokurohwa zvikuru, kuti azive mhosva yavakanga vamupopoterera kudai." 
Acts22:25 Zvino vakati vamusunga namakashu, Pauro akati kumukuru wezana, akanga amirepo, “Makatenderwa kurova munhu ari muRoma, asina kutongwa here?”" 
Acts22:26 Zvino mukuru wezana wakati achizvinzwa, akaenda kumukuru wechiuru chamazana, akamuudza akati, “Munoda kuiteiko? Nokuti munhu uyu muRoma.”" 
Acts22:27 Mukuru wechiuru chamazana akauya akati kwaari, “Ndiudze, uri muRoma here?” Akati, “Hongu.”" 
Acts22:28 Mukuru wechiuru chamazana akati, “Ini ndakatenga simba iri rokuva muRoma nomutengo mukuru.” Pauro akati, “Ini ndakaberekwa ndiri muRoma.”" 
Acts22:29 Zvino vakanga vomubvunzisisa, vakabva kwaari pakarepo, nomukuru wechiuru chamazana akatyawo achiziva kuti iye muRoma, uye nokuti akanga amusunga." 
Acts22:30 Zvino fume mangwana, achida kuziva kwazvo kuti vaJudha vakamupomera mhosva yei, akamusunungura, akarayira kuti vapristi vakuru namakurukota ose vaungane, akaburusa Pauro, ndokumuisa pamberi pavo." 
Acts23:1 Zvino Pauro akati achitarisisa kumakurukota, akati, “Varume, hama, ini ndakafamba pamberi paMwari nehana yakarurama kusvikira zuva ranhasi.”" 
Acts23:2 Ipapo Ananiasi, Mupristi Mukuru, akarayira vakanga vamire naye, kuti vamurove muromo." 
Acts23:3 Ipapo Pauro akati kwaari, “Mwari achakurova iwe, rusvingo rwakacheneswa; ugerepo kuti unditonge nomurairo, zvino worayira kuti ndirohwe, uchidarika murairo here?”" 
Acts23:4 Vakanga vamirepo vakati, “Ko unotuka Mupristi Mukuru waMwari here?”" 
Acts23:5 Pauro akati, “Hama dzangu, ndakanga ndisingazivi kuti ndiye Mupristi Mukuru; nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, ‘Usataura zvakaipa pamusoro pomubati wavanhu vako.’ ”" 
Acts23:6 Zvino Pauro akati achiona kuti vamwe ndivaSadhusi navamwe VaFarisi, akadanidzira mumakurukota, akati, “Varume, hama, ini ndiri muFarisi, mwanakomana wavaFarisi, ndinotongwa pamusoro petariro nokumuka kwavakafa.”" 
Acts23:7 Akati adaro, kupesana kukavapo pakati pavaFarisi navaSadhusi; ungano ikaparadzana." 
Acts23:8 Nokuti vaSadhusi vaiti hapana kumuka kwavakafa, kana mutumwa, kana mweya; asi VaFarisi vaitenda izvozvo zvose." 
Acts23:9 Zvino bope guru rikavapo; vamwe vanyori vokuvaFarisi vakasimuka vakaita nharo, vachiti, “Hationi chinhu chakaipa kumunhu uyu; zvimwe mweya akataura naye, kana mutumwa.”" 
Acts23:10 Zvino kupesana kukuru kuchida kumuka, mukuru wechiuru chamazana akatya kuti Pauro angabvamburwa navo, akarayira varwi kuti vaburuke, vamubvute pakati pavo, vamuise muimba yavarwi." 
Acts23:11 Usiku hwakatevera, Ishe akamira naye, akati, “Tsunga mwoyo, sezvawakandipupurira kwazvo paJerusaremu, unofanira kupupura paRomawo.”" 
Acts23:12 Zvino kwakati kwaedza, vaJudha vakaita rangano, vakazvisunga nokupika, vachiti, havangadyi kana kunwa kusvikira vauraya Pauro." 
Acts23:13 Vakanga vaita rangano iyo, vakapfuura makumi mana." 
Acts23:14 Ava vakaenda kuvapristi vakuru navakuru, vakati, “Tazvisunga nokupika kukuru, kuti hatingadyi chinhu, kusvikira tauraya Pauro." 
Acts23:15 “Naizvozvo zvino imi, namakurukota, muzivise mukuru wechiuru chamazana, kuti amuburusire kwamuri, muchiita somunoda kunatsobvunzisisa mhosva yake; isu tazvigadzira kuti timuuraye, asati aswedera.”" 
Acts23:16 Zvino mwanakomana wehanzvadzi yaPauro akanzwa zvokuvandira kwavo, akaenda, akapinda mumba mavarwi, akaudza Pauro." 
Acts23:17 Ipapo Pauro akadana mumwe wavakuru vezana, akati, “Isa jaya iri kumukuru wechiuru chamazana; nokuti ane shoko raanoda kumuudza.”" 
Acts23:18 Naizvozvo akamutora, akaenda naye kumukuru wechiuru chamazana, akati, “Pauro musungwa, akandidana, akakumbira, kuti ndiuye nejaya iri kwamuri; ane shoko raanoda kukuudzai.”" 
Acts23:19 Mukuru wechiuru chamazana akabata ruoko rwake, akaenda naye vari voga, akamubvunza vari voga, akati, “Une shoko reiko, raunoda kundiudza?”" 
Acts23:20 Iye akati, “VaJudha vakatenderana kukumbira kwamuri, kuti muburuse Pauro kumakurukota mangwana, muchiita somunoda kunatsobvunzisisa mhosva yake." 
Acts23:21 Naizvozvo musavatenda; nokuti pakati pavo kuna varume vanopfuura makumi mana vanomuvandira vakazvisunga nokupika, kuti havangadyi, kana kunwa, kusvikira vamuuraya; zvino vakazvigadzira, vakatarira tendero inobva kwamuri.”" 
Acts23:22 Naizvozvo mukuru wechiuru chamazana akaendesa jaya, akamurayira, achiti, “Usaudza munhu, kuti wandizivisa izvozvo.”" 
Acts23:23 Zvino akadana vakuru vezana vaviri, akati, “Gadzirai varwi vana mazana maviri, navanotasva mabhiza vana makumi manomwe, navana mapfumo vana mazana maviri, vaende Sizaria nenguva yechitatu yousiku;" 
Acts23:24 muvatsvakire zvipfuo, kuti vatasvise Pauro, vagonatsomuisa kumubati Ferikisi.”" 
Acts23:25 Akanyora tsamba yakanga ichiti," 
Acts23:26 “Kiraudhio Risiya, kuna Ferikisi, mubati wakakurumbira kwazvo, kwaziwai!" 
Acts23:27 Uyu munhu akabatwa navaJudha, akanga oda kuurayiwa navo, ini ndikasvika navarwi, ndikamurwira, zvandakanzwa kuti muRoma." 
Acts23:28 Zvino ndakati ndichida kuziva mhosva yavakamukwirira nayo, ndikamuburusira kumakurukota avo;" 
Acts23:29 ndikawana kuti wakwirirwa pamusoro pamashoko omurairo wavo, asi asina mhosva yechinhu chingafanira rufu kana kusungwa." 
Acts23:30 “Zvino ndakati ndaudzwa, kuti voda kuvandira munhu uyu, ndikamutumira kwamuri pakarepo, ndikarayira vanomukwirira kuti vataure pamberi penyu mhosva yake.”" 
Acts23:31 Zvino varwi vakatora Pauro sezvavakarayirwa, vakamuisa Andipatisi usiku." 
Acts23:32 Fume mangwana vakarega vatasvi vamabhiza, kuti vaende naye, ivo vakadzokera kuimba yavarwi." 
Acts23:33 Vaya vakati vasvika Sizaria, vakapa mubati tsamba, vakaisawo Pauro pamberi pake." 
Acts23:34 Akati arava, akabvunza kuti ndowenyika ipi; zvino akati anzwa kuti ndoweSizaria," 
Acts23:35 akati, “Ndichakunzwa kwazvo, kana vanokukwirira vasvikawo;” akarayira kuti achengetwe mumba maHerodhi." 
Acts24:1 Zvino mazuva mashanu akati apfuura, Ananiasi, Mupristi Mukuru, akaburuka navamwe vakuru, nomumwe mureveri, ainzi Terituro; vakamhan'arira Pauro kumubati." 
Acts24:2 Iye akati adanwa, Terituro akatanga kumupomera mhosva achiti, “Zvatinoona rugare rukuru nemi, norudzi urwu zvarunoruramisirwa mhosva nokubata kwenyu kwakanaka;" 
Acts24:3 tinozvigamuchira nemitoo yose napanzvimbo dzose nokuvonga kukuru, imi, Ferikisi akakurumbira zvikuru." 
Acts24:4 Asi, zvandisingadi kukunonotsai, ndinokumbira kwamuri, kuti mutinzwe nengoni dzenyu zvishomanene." 
Acts24:5 Nokuti takaona kuti murume uyu wakashata kwazvo, anomutsa bope pavaJudha vose panyika dzose, ari mutungamiriri weboka ravaNazareni." 
Acts24:6 Iye akaidzawo kushatisa temberi, tikamubata, [tichida kumutonga nomurairo wedu." 
Acts24:7 Asi Risiya, mukuru wechiuru chamazana, ndokuuya, akamubvisa mumaoko edu nesimba guru," 
Acts24:8 akarayira vanomupomera kuti vauye pamberi penyu.] Kana mukamubvunzisisa mumene, muchagona kuziva izvozvo zvose zvatakamukwirira nazvo.”" 
Acts24:9 NavaJudha vakabvumirawo pakumhan'ara, vakasimbisa kuti zvinhu izvozvo ndizvo." 
Acts24:10 Zvino mubati akati amuninira, kuti ataure, Pauro akapindura, akati, “Zvandinoziva kuti mava mutongi wavanhu ava makore mazhinji, ndinozvidavirira nomufaro," 
Acts24:11 nokuti munzwe kuti mazuva achigere kupfuura gumi namaviri, kubvira panguva yandakakwira Jerusaremu kundonamata." 
Acts24:12 “Havana kundiwana ndichiita nharo mutemberi nomunhu, kana muguta;" 
Acts24:13 havangagoniwo kusimbisa kwamuri izvo zvavanondipomera nazvo zvino. 
Acts24:14 Asi ndinotenda hangu kwamuri, kuti ndinoshumira Mwari wamadzibaba edu neNzira, yavanoti idzidziso yakatsauka, ndichitenda zvose zvomurairo nezvakanyorwa pavaporofita;" 
Acts24:15 ndine tariro kuna Mwari, iyo yavanotendawo vamene, kuti kuchavapo kumuka kwavakafa kwavakarurama navasakarurama." 
Acts24:16 “Pachinhu ichi ndinoedza zvikuru kuti misi yose ndive nehana isina mhosva kuna Mwari nokuvanhu. 
Acts24:17 “Zvino makore mazhinji akati apfuura, ndakauya nezvipo nezvibairo kuvanhu vangu." 
Acts24:18 “Ndizvozvo zvavakandiwana ndichiita mutemberi, ndanatswa, ndisina vanhu vazhinji, kana bopoto;" 
Acts24:19 asi vamwe vaJudha veEzhia vaivapo, ivo vaifanira kuva pano pamberi penyu, kundipomera mhosva, kana vaiva nechinhu neni." 
Acts24:20 “Kunyangwe navava ngavareve vomene chisakarurama chavakawana, musi wandakamira pamberi pamakurukota," 
Acts24:21 asi shoko iri bedzi, randakadanidzira, ndimire pakati pavo, ndichiti, ‘Ndinotongwa nhasi pamusoro pokumuka kwavakafa.’ ”" 
Acts24:22 Asi Ferikisi, zvaakazivisisa zvakanaka Nzira iyo, akavavetsa, achiti, “Kana Risiya, mukuru wechiuru chamazana aburukira pano ndichanatsobvunzisisa mhaka yenyu.”" 
Acts24:23 Akarayira mukuru wezana kuti Pauro achengetwe, arerusirwe, uye kuti varege kudzivisa mumwe wokwake kumushumira." 
Acts24:24 Zvino mamwe mazuva akati apfuura, Ferikisi akasvika, nomukadzi wake Dhurusira, aiva muJudha, akadana Pauro, akamunzwa pamusoro pokutenda kuna Kristu Jesu." 
Acts24:25 Zvino akati achitaura zvokururama, nokuzvidzora, nokutonga kunouya, Ferikisi akatya zvikuru, akapindura, akati, “Enda hako zvino; kana ndikazova nenguva yakanaka, ndichakudana.”" 
Acts24:26 Akatiwo zvimwe achazopiwa mari naPauro; naizvozvo akamudana kazhinji, achitaura naye." 
Acts24:27 Asi makore maviri akati apera, Pokio Fesito akapinda panzvimbo yaFerikisi, zvino Ferikisi achida kufadza vaJudha, akasiya Pauro akasungwa." 
Acts25:1 Zvino Fesito akati asvika panyika iyo, mazuva matatu apfuura, akakwira Jerusaremu, achibva Sizaria," 
Acts25:2 vapristi vakuru navakuru vavaJudha vakamhan'arira Pauro kwaari vakamunyengetera," 
Acts25:3 vakakumbira kuti avafadze pamusoro pake, amudanire Jerusaremu, kuti vamuvandire vamuuraye panzira." 
Acts25:4 Asi Fesito akapindura, achiti, “Pauro akachengetwa Sizaria, uye kuti iye amene akanga okurumidza kuendako." 
Acts25:5 Akati, avo vane simba pakati penyu, ngavaburuke neni; kana kune chinhu chisakafanira kumunhu uyu, ngavamupomere mhosva.”" 
Acts25:6 Akagara pakati pavo mazuva asingapfuuri masere kana gumi, ndokuburukira Sizaria; fume mangwana akagara pachigaro chokutonga, akarayira kuti vauye naPauro." 
Acts25:7 Akati asvika, vaJudha vakabva Jerusaremu, vakamukomba, vakamupomera mhosva zhinji dzakaipa, dzavakanga vasingagoni kusimbisa." 
Acts25:8 Zvino Pauro akazvidavirira, akati, “Handina kutadzira murairo wavaJudha, kana temberi, kana Kesari.”" 
Acts25:9 Zvino Fesito achida kufadza vaJudha, akapindura Pauro akati, “Unoda here kukwira Jerusaremu, undotongwako pamberi pangu pamusoro pezvinhu izvi?”" 
Acts25:10 Ipapo Pauro akati, “Ndinomira pamberi pechigaro chokutonga chaKesari, pandinofanira kutongwa; handina kuitira vaJudha zvisakarurama, sezvamunoziva nemiwo zvakanaka." 
Acts25:11 Zvino kana ndinenge ndisakarurama, ndaita chinhu chinofanira rufu, handirambi kufa; asi kana pasina chinhu chezvokwadi pazvinhu zvavanondipomera, hakuna munhu angandiisa kwavari. Ndinozviisa kuna Kesari.”" 
Acts25:12 Ipapo Fesito akataurirana namakurukota, akapindura, akati, “Wazviisa kuna Kesari; kuna Kesari uchaenda.”" 
Acts25:13 Zvino mamwe mazuva akati apfuura, mambo Agiripa naBherinike vakasvika Sizaria kuzokwazisa Fesito." 
Acts25:14 Vakati vagara mazuva mazhinji, Fesito akaisa mhosva yaPauro kuna mambo, achiti, “Kuno mumwe murume akasiyiwa pano naFerikisi, akasungwa;" 
Acts25:15 ndichiri paJerusaremu, vapristi vakuru navakuru vavaJudha vakamumhan'arira, vachikumbira kuti atongerwe rufu." 
Acts25:16 Ndikavapindura, ndikati haizi tsika yavaRoma kuisa kumutongi munhu apomerwa, asati ava navapomeri pamberi pake, akatenderwa kuzvidavirira pamusoro pemhosva yaanopomerwa nayo." 
Acts25:17 Zvino vakati vaungana pano, handina kunonoka, asi fume mangwana ndakagara pachigaro chokutonga, ndikarayira kuti vauye nomurume uyo." 
Acts25:18 Zvino vapomeri vakasimuka, asi havana kumupomera mhosva yezvinhu zvakaipa zvandakanga ndichiti vachamupomera nazvo;" 
Acts25:19 asi vakanga vanamamwe mashoko okupira kwavo, noomumwe Jesu akanga afa, ainzi naPauro mupenyu." 
Acts25:20 “Zvino ini, zvandakanga ndisingazivi mubvunziro wezvinhu zvakadai, ndikabvunza kana achida kuenda Jerusaremu kundotongwa ikoko pamusoro pezvinhu izvozvo." 
Acts25:21 Asi Pauro akati akumbira kuti achengetwe kuzotongwa namambo mukuru, ndikarayira kuti achengetwe kusvikira ndichimutumira kuna Kesari.”" 
Acts25:22 Ipapo Agiripa akati kuna Fesito, “Neni ndinoda kunzwa munhu uyu ndimene.” Iye akati, “Mangwana muchamunzwa.”" 
Acts25:23 Fume mangwana Agiripa akati asvika naBherinike, vashonga kwazvo, vapinda mumba maitambirwa mhaka, navakuru vechiuru chamazana, navakuru veguta, vakauya naPauro varayirwa naFesito." 
Acts25:24 Zvino Fesito akati, “Mambo Agiripa, nemi varume vose vaneni, munoona munhu uyu, wandakanyengeterwa navaJudha vose paJerusaremu napano, vakadanidzira, vachiti, ‘Haafaniri kuva mupenyu.’" 
Acts25:25 Asi ini ndakawana kuti haana kuita chinhu chakafanira rufu, uye zvaakakumbira kuiswa kuna mambo mukuru, ndakati, ndichamutuma." 
Acts25:26 Asi handina shoko kwaro rezvokwadi randinganyorera ishe pamusoro pake; saka ndauya naye pamberi penyu, zvikuru pamberi penyu, imi mambo Agiripa, kuti kana abvunziswa nemi, ndigova nezvandinganyora." 
Acts25:27 Nokuti kwandiri zvakaita sezvisina kufanira kutuma musungwa, mhosva dzaakakwirirwa nadzo dzisingaziviswiwo.”" 
Acts26:1 Zvino Agiripa akati kuna Pauro, “Unotenderwa kuzvidavirira.” Ipapo Pauro akatambanudza ruoko rwake, akazvidavirira, achiti," 
Acts26:2 “Mambo Agiripa, ndinozvikorokotedza, zvandingazvidavirira nhasi pamberi penyu pamusoro pezvose zvandinokwirirwa nazvo navaJudha;" 
Acts26:3 zvikuru nokuti munoziva tsika dzose namashoko ose pakati pavaJudha; naizvozvo ndinokumbira kwamuri, kuti mundinzwe nomwoyo murefu." 
Acts26:4 “VaJudha vose vanoziva mafambiro angu, kubva pauduku hwangu, aiva pakati porudzi rwangu napaJerusaremu, kubva pakutanga;" 
Acts26:5 vakandiziva kare, kana vachida kupupura, kuti ndaiva muFarisi, nedzidziso yokupira kwedu yakaisvorurama." 
Acts26:6 Nazvino ndinomira pano, kuti nditongwe nokuda kwokutarira chipikirwa chakapikirwa madzibaba edu naMwari." 
Acts26:7 Marudzi edu ane gumi namaviri anoshumira Mwari usiku namasikati, achiti achasvika pachipikirwa icho. Pamusoro pokutarira uku, imi mambo, ndinokwirirwa navaJudha." 
Acts26:8 Munofungireiko imi kuti hazvingatendwi kuti Mwari angamutsa vakafa? 
Acts26:9 “Zvino neni ndaiti ndinofanira kuita zvinhu zvizhinji zvinopesana nezita raJesu weNazareta. 
Acts26:10 Ndakazviitawo paJerusaremu, ndikapfigira vatsvene vazhinji mutorongo, ndapiwa simba navapristi vakuru; uye kana vaiurayiwa, neni ndaibvumirawo." 
Acts26:11 Nomumasinagoge ose ndaivatambudza, ndichivaroverera kuti vashonhe Mwari; ndikanyanya kuvapengera, ndikavatambudza kusvikira kumaguta ari kure nenyika ino." 
Acts26:12 “Ndakati ndichaita izvozvi, ndikaenda Dhamasikosi nesimba uye nomurairo wavapristi vakuru," 
Acts26:13 zvino, mambo, masikati makuru, ndiri munzira, ndikaona chiedza chaibva kudenga, chaikunda kupenya kwezuva, chichindipenyera kumativi ose navandaifamba navo." 
Acts26:14 Zvino takati tawira pasi tose, ndikanzwa izwi richiti kwandiri norurimi rweChiHebheru, ‘Sauro! Sauro! Unonditambudzireiko? Zvinokuremera kupfura zvibayiso.’" 
Acts26:15 “Ndikati, ‘Ndimi aniko, Ishe?’ Ishe akati, ‘Ndini Jesu, waunotambudza." 
Acts26:16 Asi simuka, umire namakumbo ako; nokuti ndazviratidza kwauri nezvizvi, kuti ndikuite munyai nechapupu chezvawakaona, nezvandichazviratidza nazvo kwauri;" 
Acts26:17 ndichakurwira kuvanhu nokuvahedheni, vandinokutumira kwavari;" 
Acts26:18 kuti usvinudze meso avo, vabve murima, vaende kuchiedza, nokubva pasimba raSatani, vaende kuna Mwari, kuti vagamuchire ruregerero rwezvivi zvavo, nenhaka pakati pavakaitwa vatsvene, nokutenda kwandiri.’" 
Acts26:19 “Naizvozvo, mambo Agiripa handina kuramba kuteerera chiratidzo chokudenga;" 
Acts26:20 asi ndakatanga kuparidza kuna veDhamasikosi, nokuna veJerusaremu, nenyika yose yeJudhiya, nokuvahedheni, kuti vatendeuke, varingire kuna Mwari, vaite mabasa akafanira kutendeuka." 
Acts26:21 Pamusoro paizvozvi vaJudha vakandibata mutemberi, vakaedza kundiuraya." 
Acts26:22 Asi ndakabatsirwa naMwari, ndikamira kusvikira zuva ranhasi, ndichipupurira vaduku navakuru, ndisingarevi zvimwe zvinhu asi zvakataurwa navaporofita naMosesi, kuti zvichaitika;" 
Acts26:23 zvokuti Kristu akafanira kutambudzika, nokutanga kumuka kuvakafa, aparidzire vanhu navahedheni chiedza.”" 
Acts26:24 Zvino akati achizvidavirira saizvozvo, Fesito akati nezwi guru, “Pauro, unopenga; kudzidza kwako kukuru kunokupenza.”" 
Acts26:25 Asi Pauro akati, “Handipengi, Fesito akakurumbira; asi ndinotaura mashoko amazvokwadi noouchenjeri." 
Acts26:26 Nokuti mambo andinotaura naye ndisingatyi, vanoziva izvozvi, nokuti chinhu ichi hachina kuitwa pakavanda." 
Acts26:27 “Mambo Agiripa, munotenda vaporofita here? Ndinoziva kuti munotenda.”" 
Acts26:28 Agiripa akati kuna Pauro, “Unenge unoda kundiita muKristu nenguva duku.”" 
Acts26:29 Pauro akati, “Ndinonyengetera kuna Mwari kana nenguva duku, kana nehuru, kuti musava imi moga, asi vose vanondinzwa nhasi, vaitwe seni, asi vasina zvisungo izvi.”" 
Acts26:30 Ipapo mambo akasimuka, nomubati, naBherinike, navakanga vagere navo;" 
Acts26:31 vakabuda vakataurirana, vakati, “Munhu uyu haaiti chinhu chakafanira rufu kana kusungwa.”" 
Acts26:32 Ipapo Agiripa akati kuna Fesito, “Munhu uyu dai asina kuzviisa kuna Kesari angadai asunungurwa.”" 
Acts27:1 Zvino kwakati kwatemwa kuti tiende Itaria nechikepe, vakaisa Pauro navamwe vasungwa kumukuru wezana, ainzi, “Jurio, wehondo yaAugusto.”" 
Acts27:2 Zvino takati tapinda muchikepe cheAdhiramitiumu, chakanga choenda napamisha yemhenderekedzo dzeEzhia, tikabva tina Arisitakusi muMasedhonia, aibva Tesaronika." 
Acts27:3 Fume mangwana tikasvika Sidhoni, Jurio akaitira Pauro zvakanaka, akamutendera kuti aende kushamwari dzake, achengetwe navo." 
Acts27:4 Tikabva ipapo, tikapfuura nenyasi kweSaipurasi, nokuti mhepo yakatidzivisa." 
Acts27:5 Zvino tikayambuka gungwa reSirisia nePamufiria, tikasvika Mira, musha weRikiya." 
Acts27:6 Mukuru wezana akawanapo chikepe cheArekizandiria, chaienda Itari, ndokutipinzamo." 
Acts27:7 Zvino takanatsofamba mazuva mazhinji, tikasvika pakatarisana neKinidhusi tichitambudzika, mhepo zvayakanga isingatitenderi kufamba, tikapfuura nenyasi kweKiriti, pakatarisana neSarimoni." 
Acts27:8 Tikapfuura napo tichitambudzika, ndokusvika pamwe painzi Zororo Rakanaka, pedyo neguta reRasea." 
Acts27:9 Zvino nguva huru yakati yapfuura, nokufamba negungwa kwava nenjodzi, nokuti nguva yokuzvinyima zvokudya yakanga yatopfuura, Pauro akavaraira," 
Acts27:10 akati kwavari, “Varume, ndinoona kuti rwendo rwedu ruchava nokutambudzika nokurasikirwa kukuru, zvisati zviri zvomutoro nechikepe bedzi, asi nokwoupenyu hweduwo.”" 
Acts27:11 Asi mukuru wezana akaterera mufambisi wechikepe, nomwene wacho, kupfuura zvakarehwa naPauro," 
Acts27:12 nokuti zororo zvarakanga risina kunaka kuti vagarepo chando, vamwe vazhinji vakati zviri nani kuti vabvepo, kuti zvimwe vangasvika Fenika vagarepo chando; ndiro zororo reKiriti, rakanga rakatarira mabvazuva kumusoro nezasi." 
Acts27:13 Zvino mhepo yezasi yakati ichirira zvishoma, vakati tawana zvatakanga tichivinga, vakabvapo, vakafamba pedyo neKiriti." 
Acts27:14 Zvino gare–gare mhepo ine simba, yainzi, “Yurakuro,” ikaburuka ichibva kwairi, ikatiwira." 
Acts27:15 Zvino chikepe chakati chichibatwa, tisingagoni kufamba takatarira mhepo, tikachirega, tikaramba tichingotorwa." 
Acts27:16 Zvino tikafamba nyasi kwechimwe chiwi chiduku, chainzi Kaudha, tikanga tokoniwa kusunga igwa." 
Acts27:17 Vakati varisimudza, vakatora zvibatsiro, vakasunga chikepe nenyasi; zvino zvavakatya kuti vachakandirwa pajecha reSiritisi, vakaderedza masaira, ndokungotorwa." 
Acts27:18 Fume mangwana, zvakatambura kwazvo nedutu remhepo, vakakandira nhumbi kunze;" 
Acts27:19 nezuva retatu, vakakandira zvinhu zvechikepe kunze namaoko avo." 
Acts27:20 Zvino zvatakanga tisina kubudirwa nezuva kana nyenyedzi mazuva mazhinji, nedutu guru remhepo richirambira riripo, takatorerwa kutarira kwose kwokuti tichaponeswa." 
Acts27:21 Zvino vakati vagara nguva refu vasingadyi, Pauro akamira pakati pavo, akati, “Varume, maifanira kunditeerera, mukasabva Kiriti, mukasawirwa nokutambudzika nokurasikirwa uku." 
Acts27:22 Asi zvino ndinokurairai kuti mutsunge mwoyo; nokuti hakuna angarasikirwa noupenyu hwake pakati penyu, asi chikepe bedzi." 
Acts27:23 Nokuti usiku huno mutumwa waMwari, wandiri wake, nowandinoshumirawo, akamira neni," 
Acts27:24 akati, ‘Pauro, usatya; unofanira kumira pamberi paKesari; tarira, Mwari akakupa vose vanofamba newe muchikepe.’" 
Acts27:25 Naizvozvo, varume, tsungai mwoyo, nokuti ndinotenda Mwari, kuti zvichaitika sezvandakaudzwa." 
Acts27:26 Asi tinofanira kukandirwa pane chimwe chiwi.” 
Acts27:27 Zvino usiku hwegumi nouna hwakati hwasvika, tichangotorwa–torwa muGungwa reAdhiria, pakati pousiku vafambisi vechikepe vakati voswedera kune imwe nyika." 
Acts27:28 Vakayera kudzika kwemvura, vakawana pakaita mafadhomi makumi maviri; vakapfuura zvishoma, ndokuyerazve, vakawana pakaita mafadhomi ane gumi namashanu." 
Acts27:29 Zvino vakatya kuti zvimwe tichawira pamabwe, vakakanda zvimiso zvina neshure kwechikepe, vakachema vachiti kuedze." 
Acts27:30 Zvino vafambisi vakati vachida kutiza muchikepe, vakaburusira igwa mugungwa, vachiita savanenge vokanda zvimiso kumuromo wacho." 
Acts27:31 Pauro akati kumukuru wezana navarwi, “Hamungararami kana ava vasingagari muchikepe.”" 
Acts27:32 Ipapo varwi vakagura mabote egwa, vakarirega, rikawa." 
Acts27:33 Zvino kwakati kwoedza, Pauro akakumbira zvikuru kwavari vose kuti vadye, achiti, “Nhasi rava zuva regumi nerechina, ramakagara muchizvinyima kudya, musingadyi chinhu." 
Acts27:34 “Saka ndinokumbira zvikuru kuti mudye, nokuti ndizvo zvichakuponesai; nokuti hakuna ruvhudzi rumwe ruchaparadzwa pamusoro womumwe wenyu.”"
