Acts27:35 Akati areva izvozvo, akatora chingwa, akavonga Mwari pamberi pavo vose, akachimedura, ndokutanga kudya iye." 
Acts27:36 Ipapo vakatsunga mwoyo vose, vakadyawo vamene." 
Acts27:37 Isu tose taiva muchikepe, taiva mazana maviri namakumi manomwe navatanhatu." 
Acts27:38 Zvino vakati vaguta, vakarerusa chikepe, vachikandira zviyo mugungwa." 
Acts27:39 Kwakati kwoedza, vakasaziva nyika; asi vakaona zororo raiva nejecha, vakarangana kana zvaibvira kuitika, kuti vaise chikepe pariri." 
Acts27:40 Ipapo vakagura zvimiso, vakazvisiya mugungwa, vakasunungura zvisungo zvaisunga zvokudzoresa nazvo, vakasimudzira seiri rapamberi kumhepo, vakaruramira kumhenderekedzo." 
Acts27:41 Zvino vakati vachisvika paidira makungwa maviri, vakagumirisa chikepe pasi; muromo wacho ukabatwa kwazvo usingazununguki, asi rutivi rwacho rweshure rukavhunika nesimba remvura." 
Acts27:42 Zvino varwi vakati zviri nani kuti vasungwa vauraiwe, kuti vamwe varege kutiza vachishambira." 
Acts27:43 Asi mukuru wezana akada kuponesa Pauro, akavadzivisa zvavakanga vachida kuita; akarayira kuti vanogona kushambira, vatange kuzviwisira mumvura, vabude kunyika;" 
Acts27:44 vamwe, vasara, vabude vamwe pamatanda, vamwe panezvimwe zvinhu zvechikepe. Naizvozvo zvakaitika kuti vose vakasvika kunyika vari vapenyu." 
Acts28:1 Zvino takati taponeswa, tikaziva kuti chiwi chinonzi Morota." 
Acts28:2 Vanhu venyika iyo vakatiitira unyoro kwazvo; nokuti vakabatidza moto, vakatigamuchira tose, nokuda kwemvura yakanga ichinaya, uye nokuda kwechando." 
Acts28:3 Zvino Pauro akati aunganidza svinga routsotso, akahuisa pamoto, kukabuda nyoka nokudziya, ikanamatira paruoko rwake." 
Acts28:4 Vanhu venyika iyo vakati vachiona chikara chakaremberera paruoko rwake, vakataurirana, vachiti, “Zvirokwazvo munhu uyu muurayi, nokuti kunyangwe adoponeswa hake pagungwa, Kururama hakumutenderi kuti ave mupenyu.”" 
Acts28:5 Asi iye wakazunzira chikara mumoto, akasanzwa kurwadzwa." 
Acts28:6 Ivo vakati achazvimba, kana kuwira pasi pakarepo, akafa; zvino vakati vatarira nguva refu, vakaona kuti haana kusvikirwa nenjodzi, vakashanduka voti, “Iye Mwari.”" 
Acts28:7 Zvino pedyo ipapo paiva neminda yomukuru wechiwi, ainzi Pubhuriyo; iye akatigamuchira, akatigarisa zvakanaka mazuva matatu." 
Acts28:8 Zvino baba vaPubhuriyo vakanga vavete pasi, vakabatwa nefivha nokubudisa ropa; Pauro akapinda kwavari, akanyengetera, ndokuisa maoko ake pamusoro pake, akamuporesa." 
Acts28:9 Izvo zvakati zvaitwa, navamwewo vechiwi, vairwara, vakauya, vakaporeswa." 
Acts28:10 Vakatikudza nokukudza kukuru; tichizoenda, vakaisa pachikepe zvinhu zvatakanga tichishayiwa." 
Acts28:11 Mwedzi mitatu yakati yapfuura, tikaenda nechikepe cheArekizandiria, chakanga chagara chando pachiwi, chaiva nechiratidzo chokuti “Dhiokuri.”" 
Acts28:12 Zvino tikaenda napaSirakuse, tikagarapo mazuva matatu." 
Acts28:13 Tikabvapo, tikapota, ndokusvika Rhegiumu; zuva rimwe rikati rapfuura, mhepo yaibva zasi ikamuka, tikasvika Puteori nezuva repiri;" 
Acts28:14 tikawanapo hama, dzakakumbira zvikuru kuti tigare nadzo mazuva manomwe; naizvozvo tikasvika Roma." 
Acts28:15 Zvino hama dzakati dzatinzwa, dzikabvapo, dzikauya kuzotichingamidza, dzikasvika Apio Foro napaTabherini Nhatu; Pauro akati adziona idzo, akavonga Mwari, akatsunga mwoyo." 
Acts28:16 Zvino takati tapinda Roma, Pauro akatenderwa kugara ari oga, anomurwi aimurinda." 
Acts28:17 Mazuva matatu akati apfuura, akakokera avo, vakanga vari vakuru vavaJudha. Vakati vaungana, akati kwavari, “Varume, hama, ini kunyangwe ndisina kuita chinhu chakatadzira vanhu, kana tsika dzamadzibaba edu, ndakabva Jerusaremu ndakasungwa, ndaiswa pamaoko avaRoma;" 
Acts28:18 ivo, vakati vandibvunzisisa, vakada kundisunungura, nokuti pakanga pasina mhosva yorufu kwandiri." 
Acts28:19 Asi vaJudha vakaramba, ndikarovererwa kuzviisa kuna Kesari; kusi kuti ndaiva nechinhu chokupomera rudzi rwangu." 
Acts28:20 Zvino ndakakudanai pamusoro pemhosva iyi, kuti ndikuonei, nditaurirane nemi, nokuti ndakasungwa nengetani iyi nokuda kwetariro yaVaIsiraeri.”" 
Acts28:21 Vakati kwaari, “Hatina kugamuchira tsamba pamusoro pako, dzaibva Judhiya, uye hakuna mumwe wehama akasvika akatiudza zvako, kana kutaura zvakaipa pamusoro pako." 
Acts28:22 Asi tinoda kunzwa kwauri zvaunofunga; nokuti kana iri dzidziso iyi, tinoziva kuti inorambwa kwose–kwose.”" 
Acts28:23 Zvino vakati vamutarira zuva, vakauya kwaari vari vazhinji, kwaakanga agere, akavadudzira, achivapupurira kwazvo ushe hwaMwari, akavagombedzera pamusoro paJesu, nomurairo waMosesi navaporofita, kubva mangwanani kusvikira madekwana." 
Acts28:24 Vamwe vakatenda zvakataurwa, asi vamwe havana kutenda." 
Acts28:25 Zvino zvavakanga vasinganzwani, vakaenda, Pauro ataura shoko rimwechete kwavari rokuti, “Mweya Mutsvene akataura zvakanaka nomuporofita Isaya kuna madzibaba enyu," 
Acts28:26 achiti, ‘Enda kuvanhu ava uti, Nokunzwa muchanzwa, musingatongonzwisisi; Nokuona, muchaona, musingaonesesi." 
Acts28:27 Nokuti mwoyo yavanhu ava yava mikukutu, Nzeve dzavo hadzinzwi zvakanaka, Vakatsinzina meso avo; Kuti varege kutongoona nameso avo, Nokunzwa nenzeve dzavo, Nokunzwisisa nemwoyo yavo, Vatendeuke, Ndivaporese.’ ”" 
Acts28:28 Zvino zivai imi, kuti ruponeso urwu rwakatumirwa vahedheni; ivo vachanzwawo. [" 
Acts28:29 Akati ataura izvozvo, vaJudha vakaenda, vachiita nyaya huru pakati pavo.]" 
Acts28:30 Iye akapedza makore maviri agere muimba yake yairipirwa mari, akagamuchira vose vaipinda kwaari," 
Acts28:31 achiparidza ushe hwaMwari, achidzidzisa zvaIshe Jesu Kristu, asingatongotyi, asingadziviswi nomunhu." 
Romans1:1 Pauro, muranda waKristu Jesu, akadanwa kuti ave mupostori, akatsaurirwa Vhangeri yaMwari," 
Romans1:2 yaakapira kare navaporofita vake muMagwaro matsvene," 
Romans1:3 zvoMwanakomana wake, akabva kurudzi rwaDhavhidhi panyama," 
Romans1:4 akaratidzwa nesimba paMweya woutsvene, kuti ndiye Mwanakomana waMwari, nokumuka kwake kuvakafa; ndiye Jesu Kristu, Ishe wedu," 
Romans1:5 watakagamuchira naye nyasha nohupostori, kuti pakati pavahedheni vose, pave nokuteerera kwokutenda nokuda kwezita rake;" 
Romans1:6 nemiwo muri pakati pavo, makadanwa kuti muve vaJesu Kristu;" 
Romans1:7 kuna vose vari muRoma, vadikanwi vaMwari, vakadanwa kuti vave vatsvene, Nyasha ngadzive nemi norugare, zvinobva kuna Mwari, Baba vedu, nokuna Ishe Jesu Kristu." 
Romans1:8 Pakutanga, ndinovonga Mwari wangu muna Jesu Kristu, pamusoro penyu mose, nokuti kutenda kwenyu kunoparidzirwa panyika yose." 
Romans1:9 Nokuti Mwari chapupu changu, iye wandinoshumira mumweya wangu muVhangeri yoMwanakomana wake, kuti handiregi kukurangarirai," 
Romans1:10 ndichikumbira nguva dzose pakunyengetera kwangu, kuti zvimwe ndifambiswe hangu zvakanaka ndiuye kwamuri nokuda kwaMwari." 
Romans1:11 Nokuti ndinoda zvikuru kukuonai, kuti ndikupei chimwe chipo chomweya, kuti musimbiswe." 
Romans1:12 Ndokuti ini ndinyaradzwe pamwechete nemi pakati penyu, mumwe nomumwe nokutenda kwomumwe, kwenyu nokwangu." 
Romans1:13 Handidi kuti musaziva, hama dzangu, kuti kazhinji ndaida kuuya kwamuri, (ndikadziviswa kusvikira zvino), kuti ndive nezvibereko kwamuriwo, sapakati pavamwe vahedheni." 
Romans1:14 Ndine ngava kuvaGiriki nokuvatorwa, kuvakachenjera navasina kuchenjera." 
Romans1:15 Naizvozvo, kana ndirini, ndakazvigadzira kukuparidziraiwo Vhangeri, imi muri paRoma." 
Romans1:16 Nokuti handinyari pamusoro peVhangeri; nokuti isimba raMwari rokuponesa mumwe nomumwe anotenda, kutanga muJudha, uye muGirikiwo." 
Romans1:17 Nokuti mairi kururama kwaMwari kunoratidzwa kunobva pakutenda kuchienda kukutenda; sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Akarurama achararama nokutenda.”" 
Romans1:18 Nokuti kutsamwa kwaMwari kunoratidzwa, kuchibva kudenga, pamusoro pokusada Mwari kwose nokusarurama kwavanhu, vanodzivisa chokwadi nokusarurama;" 
Romans1:19 nokuti izvo zvingazikanwa zvaMwari zvinoonekwa mukati mavo, nokuti Mwari akazviratidza izvo kwavari." 
Romans1:20 Nokuti kubvira pakusikwa kwenyika izvo zvake zvisingaonekwi, iro simba rake risingaperi nohuMwari hwake, zvinoonekwa kwazvo, zvichizikanwa pazvinhu zvakaitwa; kuti varege kuva nepembedzo;" 
Romans1:21 nokuti vaiziva Mwari, asi havana kumukudza saMwari, kana kumuvonga; asi vakafunga zvisina maturo nemwoyo yavo isina zivo, ikasvibiswa." 
Romans1:22 Vachiti, takachenjera, vakava mapenzi;" 
Romans1:23 vakashandura kubwinya kwaMwari asingafi, vakakuita mufananidzo wakafanana nomunhu anofa, neshiri, nemhuka dzina makumbo mana, nezvinokambaira." 
Romans1:24 Saka Mwari, mukuchiva kwemwoyo yavo, akavaisa kutsvina, kuti vanyadzise miviri yavo pakati pavo." 
Romans1:25 Avo vakatsinhanha zvokwadi yaMwari nenhema, vakanamata nokushumira zvisikwa kupfura Musiki, iye anokudzwa nokusingaperi. Ameni." 
Romans1:26 Saka Mwari akavaisa pakuchiva kunonyadzisa; nokuti vanhukadzi vavo vakashandura basa ravakasikirwa, rive basa ravasina kusikirwa;" 
Romans1:27 saizvozvo vanhurumewo vakasiya basa rakasikirwa munhukadzi, vakakundwa nokuchiva pakati pavo, vanhurume vachiita zvinonyadza navanhurume, vakapiwa mukati mavo mubairo wakafanira wokurasika kwavo." 
Romans1:28 Sezvavakanga vasingadi kugara vachiziva Mwari, Mwari akavaisa kumurangariro wakarasika, kuti vaite zvisakafanira;" 
Romans1:29 vakazadzwa nokusarurama kwose; nokuipa, noruchiva, nokuvenga; vakazara negodo, nokuuraya, norukave, nokunyengera, nechinya; vanhu vanoita zeve–zeve," 
Romans1:30 navacheri, navanovenga Mwari, navanodada navanozvikudza, navanozvirumbidza, navavambi vezvakaipa, navasingateereri vabereki," 
Romans1:31 namapenzi, navanoputsa sungano, navasina rudo kwarwo, vasina ngoni." 
Romans1:32 Avo, kunyangwe vachiziva havo chirevo chaMwari, kuti vanoita zvakadai vakafanirwa norufu, havaiti izvo bedzi, asi vanotenderana navanozviita." 
Romans2:1 Saka hauna pembedzo iwe munhu, upi noupi, unotonga vamwe; nokuti pachinhu icho chaunotonga mumwe nacho, unozvipa mhosva iwe, nokuti iwe, unotonga, unoita zvinhu izvozvo." 
Romans2:2 Tinoziva kuti kutonga kwaMwari ndokwazvokwadi kunovanoita zvinhu zvakadai. 
Romans2:3 Iwe munhu, unotonga vamwe vanoita zvinhu zvakadai, iwe uchizviitawo, ko unoti ungatiza kutonga kwaMwari here?" 
Romans2:4 Unozvidza kanhi pfuma younyoro hwake, nomwoyo wake munyoro, nomwoyo wake murefu, usingazivi here kuti unyoro hwaMwari hunokuisa pakutendeuka?" 
Romans2:5 Asi noukukutu hwako nomwoyo usingadi kutendeuka, unozviunganidzira kutsamwa nezuva rokutsamwa, nokuratidzwa kwokutonga kwakarurama kwaMwari;" 
Romans2:6 iye achapa mumwe nomumwe paakaita napo," 
Romans2:7 Vanotsvaka kubwinya, nokukudzwa, nokusafa, vachitsungirira pakuita zvakanaka, achavapa upenyu husingaperi." 
Romans2:8 Asi kuna vane nharo, vasingateereri chokwadi, vanoteerera zvisakarurama, kuchavapo kutsamwa nehasha," 
Romans2:9 nokutambudzika nenhamo kumweya mumwe nomumwe womunhu anoita zvakaipa, pakutanga womuJudha, nowomuGiriki;" 
Romans2:10 asi kubwinya, nokukudzwa, norugare kune mumwe nomumwe anoita zvakanaka, kumuJudha pakutanga, nomuGirikiwo." 
Romans2:11 Nokuti Mwari haatendi zvinoonekwa zvomunhu. 
Romans2:12 Nokuti vose vakatadza vasina murairo, vachaparadzwawo vasina murairo; vose vakatadza vanomurairo, vachatongwa nomurairo;" 
Romans2:13 nokuti vanzwi vomurairo havazi ivo vakarurama pamberi paMwari, asi vaiti vomurairo ndivo vanoruramiswa;" 
Romans2:14 (nokuti kana vahedheni vasina murairo vachiita pachavo zvinhu zvomurairo, vava murairo wavo vamene;" 
Romans2:15 nokuti vanoratidza basa romurairo wakanyorwa mumwoyo yavo, hana yavo ichipupura pamwechete nazvo, nezvavanofunga pakati pavo zvichivapa mhosva kana kuvapembedza;)" 
Romans2:16 nezuva iro, Mwari raanozotonga naro zvakavanzika zvavanhu, naJesu Kristu, sezvinoreva Vhangeri yangu." 
Romans2:17 Zvino kana iwe unonzi muJudha, unovimba nomurairo, unozvirumbidza muna Mwari," 
Romans2:18 unoziva kuda kwake, nokutsaura kuti zvakanaka ndezvipi, uchidzidziswa nomurairo," 
Romans2:19 unozviti iwe uri mutungamiriri wamapofu, nechiedza chavari murima," 
Romans2:20 nomurayiri wamapenzi, nomudzidzisi wavacheche, zvauno mufananidzo wokuziva nowechokwadi pamurairo;" 
Romans2:21 zvino iwe unodzidzisa mumwe, unoregereiko kuzvidzidzisa? Iwe unoparidza kuti, “Munhu arege kuba,” unobireiko iwe?" 
Romans2:22 Iwe unoti munhu arege kuita, “Upombwe,” unoitireiko upombwe iwe? Iwe unosema zvifananidzo, unobireiko iwe temberi dzavo?" 
Romans2:23 Iwe unozvirumbidza nomurairo, unoshoora Mwari nokudarika murairo neiko?" 
Romans2:24 Nokuti, sezvazvakanyorwa, zita raMwari rinomhurwa pakati pavahedheni nokuda kwenyu." 
Romans2:25 Nokuti kudzingiswa kunobatsira, kana iwe uri muiti womurairo; asi kana uri mudariki womurairo, kudzingiswa kwako kwava kusadzingiswa." 
Romans2:26 Zvino, kana iye asina kudzingiswa achichengeta zvirevo zvomurairo, ko kusadzingiswa kwake hakunganzi kudzingiswa here?" 
Romans2:27 Neasina kudzingiswa kubva pakuzvarwa kwake, kana achichengeta murairo, haangakutongi here iwe unodarika murairo, iwe unomurairo wakanyorwa, uyewo kudzingiswa?" 
Romans2:28 Nokuti uyo haazi muJudha, ari muJudha pakuonekwa chete; nokudzingiswa hakuzi iko kunoonekwa, kuri panyama;" 
Romans2:29 asi muJudha ndiye uri muJudha nechomukati; nokudzingiswa ndiko kwomwoyo, mumweya, kusati kuri kwezvakanyorwa; iye haarumbidzwi navanhu, asi naMwari." 
Romans3:1 Ko muJudha anopfuura vamwe neiko? Kana kudzingiswa kunobatsireiko? 
Romans3:2 Zvizhinji, nemitowo yose, Pakutanga, kuti ndivo vakapiwa mashoko aMwari." 
Romans3:3 Nokuti zvinodiniko kana vamwe vasina kutenda? Ko kusatenda kwavo kuchakonesa kutendeka kwaMwari here? 
Romans3:4 Haisva! Mwari ngaave wachokwadi, asi vanhu vose vave venhema; sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Kuti mururamiswe pamashoko enyu, Mukunde pakutonga kwenyu.”" 
Romans3:5 Asi kana kusarurama kwedu kuchiratidza kururama kwaMwari, tichatiiko? Kuti Mwari haana kururama here, zvaanoita nehasha? (Ndinotaura nokutaura kwomunhu.)" 
Romans3:6 Haisva! Mwari angagozotonga nyika seiko? 
Romans3:7 Zvino kana chokwadi chaMwari chawanzwa nenhema dzangu, iye akakudzwa nazvo, ko neniwo ndichatongerwei somutadzi?" 
Romans3:8 Ticharegereiko kutaura (sezvatinopomerwa, uye sezvinoreva vamwe vachiti tinodaro), tichiti, “Ngatiite zvakaipa, kuti zvakanaka zvibudepo?” Kutongwa kwavo kwakarurama." 
Romans3:9 Zvino todiniko? Tinovapfuura here? Kwete napaduku; nokuti tambopa vose mhosva, vaJudha navaGiriki, tichiti vose vakasungwa nezvivi;" 
Romans3:10 sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Hakuna akarurama, kunyangwe nomumwe;" 
Romans3:11 Hakuna anonzwisisa, Hakuna anotsvaka Mwari;" 
Romans3:12 Vakatsauka vose, vakava vanhu vasina maturo, Hakuna anoita zvakanaka, kunyangwe nomumwechete;" 
Romans3:13 Huro dzavo hwiro hwakashama; Vakanyengera nendimi dzavo; Uturu hwenyoka huri mumiromo yavo; 
Romans3:14 Muromo wavo uzere nokutuka nokuvava; 
Romans3:15 Tsoka dzavo dzinokurumidza kuteura ropa; 
Romans3:16 Kuparadza nenhamo zviri munzira dzavo; 
Romans3:17 Nenzira yorugare havana kuiziva 
Romans3:18 Kutya Mwari hakupo pamberi pavo.” 
Romans3:19 Zvino tinoziva kuti zvose zvinorehwa nomurairo, anozvitaura kuna vose vari pasi pomurairo; kuti miromo yose idzivirwe, nenyika yose ive nemhosva pamberi paMwari." 
Romans3:20 Nokuti hakuna nyama ingaruramiswa pamberi pake namabasa omurairo; nokuti zvivi zvinoziviswa nomurairo. 
Romans3:21 Asi zvino kururama kwaMwari kwakaratidzwa kunze kwomurairo, kuchipupurirwa nomurairo navaporofita;" 
Romans3:22 ndiko kururama kwaMwari kunouya nokutenda kuna Jesu Kristu kuna vose vanotenda; nokuti havasiyani," 
Romans3:23 nokuti vose vakatadza, vakasasvika pakubwinya kwaMwari." 
Romans3:24 Vanongoruramiswa nenyasha dzake nokudzikinura kuri muna Kristu Jesu; 
Romans3:25 iye akagadzwa naMwari, kuti ave muyananiso nokutenda muropa rake, kuti kururama kwake kuratidzwe, nokuti zvivi zvakaitwa kare zvakaregerwa, Mwari achivaitira mwoyo murefu;" 
Romans3:26 kuti kururama kwake kuratidzwe nenguva ino, kuti arurama iye amene, uye aruramise uyo unotenda kuna Jesu." 
Romans3:27 Zvino kuzvikudza kuripiko? Kwabviswa. Nomurairo upiko? Wamabasa here? Kwete, asi nomurairo wokutenda." 
Romans3:28 Naizvozvo tinoti, munhu anoruramiswa nokutenda kunze kwamabasa omurairo." 
Romans3:29 Ko Mwari ndiye wavaJudha voga here? Haazi wavahedheniwo here? Hongu, wavahedheniwo." 
Romans3:30 Mwari zvaari mumwechete, acharuramisa vakadzingiswa pamusoro pokutenda, navasina kudzingiswa nokutenda." 
Romans3:31 Zvino tinokonesa murairo nokutenda here? Haisva! Asi tinosimbisa murairo. 
Romans4:1 Zvino tichati Abhurahamu, tateguru vedu panyama, akawaneiko?" 
Romans4:2 Nokuti dai Abhurahamu akaruramiswa namabasa ake, angadai ane chinhu chaangazvirumbidza nacho; asi haana pamberi paMwari." 
Romans4:3 Nokuti Rugwaro runoti kudiniko? Runoti, “Abhurahamu akatenda Mwari, kukanzi kwaari ndiko kururama.”" 
Romans4:4 Zvino kuno anobata basa, mubairo haunzi ndowenyasha, asi ndowengava." 
Romans4:5 Kunoasingabati, asi anotenda kuna iye anoruramisa munhu asingadi Mwari, kutenda kwake kunonzi kwaari ndiko kururama." 
Romans4:6 Sezvinorevawo Dhavhidhi, kuti akaropafadzwa munhu anonzi naMwari akarurama, kunze kwamabasa," 
Romans4:7 achiti, “Vakaropafadzwa vakaregererwa zvisakarurama zvavo, Navakafukidzirwa zvivi zvavo;" 
Romans4:8 Wakaropafadzwa munhu asinganzi naIshe ane zvivi.” 
Romans4:9 Zvino kuropafadzwa uku ndokwavakadzingiswa, kana kwavasina kudzingiswa here? Nokuti tinoti, kuna Abhurahamu, “Kutenda kwake kwakanzi ndiko kururama.”" 
Romans4:10 Zvino zvakanzarwo seiko? Atodzingiswa, kana asina kudzingiswa here? Hazvina kunzarwo adzingiswa, asi asina kudzingiswa;" 
Romans4:11 akapiwa chiratidzo chokudzingiswa, kuti chive chisimbiso chokururama kwokutenda, kwaakanga anako asati adzingiswa; kuti ave baba vavose vanotenda, kunyangwe vasina kudzingiswa, kuti vagonzi vakarurama;" 
Romans4:12 ave baba vokudzingiswa kuna ivo vasina kudzingiswa bedzi, asi vanofambawo mumakwara okutenda kwababa vedu Abhurahamu, kwavaiva nako vasati vadzingiswa." 
Romans4:13 Nokuti chipikirwa chokuti uchava mugari wenhaka yenyika hachina kupiwa Abhurahamu kana rudzi rwake nomurairo, asi nokururama kwokutenda." 
Romans4:14 Nokuti dai vomurairo vari vagari venhaka, kutenda hakuna maturo, nechipikirwa chinokoneswa;" 
Romans4:15 nokuti murairo unouyisa kutsamwa; asi pasina murairo hapana kudarikawo. 
Romans4:16 Saka ndezvokutenda, kuti, zvive zvenyasha; kuti chipikirwa chive nesimba kurudzi rwose; rusati ruri rwomurairo bedzi, asi norwokutenda kwaAbhurahamuwo, iye baba vedu tose," 
Romans4:17 (sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Ndakakuita baba vamarudzi mazhinji”) pamberi paiye waakatenda, iye Mwari anopa vakafa upenyu, nokudana zvisipo sezvinenge zviripo." 
Romans4:18 Akatenda netariro pasina tariro, kuti ave baba vamarudzi mazhinji, sezvakanga zvarehwa, zvichinzi, “Rudzi rwako ruchadaro.”" 
Romans4:19 Haana kushayiwa simba pakutenda, achifunga muviri wake wakanga watofa hawo (zvaaiva namakore anenge zana), nokufa kwechizvaro chaSara;" 
Romans4:20 akatarira chipikirwa chaMwari, haana kunyunyuta nokusatenda, asi akasimbiswa pakutenda, akakudza Mwari," 
Romans4:21 achiziva kwazvo, kuti icho chaakapikira, akanga ane simba rokuchiitawo." 
Romans4:22 Saka zvakanzi kwaari, “Ndiko kururama.”" 
Romans4:23 Zvino hazvina kunyorwa nokuda kwake bedzi, kuti “Zvikanzarwo kwaari;”" 
Romans4:24 asi nokuda kweduwo; nesu tichanzarwo; iyesu, tinotenda kuno akamutsa Jesu, Ishe wedu, kuvakafa" 
Romans4:25 iye akaiswa kurufu nokuda kwokudarika kwedu, akamutswa nokuda kwokururamiswa kwedu." 
Romans5:1 Naizvozvo zvatinoruramiswa nokutenda ngative norugare kuna Mwari naIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu;" 
Romans5:2 watakawana naye mapindiro nokutenda munyasha idzi, dzatinomira madziri; ngatifare netariro yokuona kubwinya kwaMwari." 
Romans5:3 Zvisati zviri izvo bedzi, asi ngatifarewo mumatambudziko, tichiziva kuti kutambudzika kunouyisa kutsungirira;" 
Romans5:4 kutsungirira kunouyisa kuedzwa; kuedzwa kunouyisa tariro; 
Romans5:5 tariro hainyadzisi; nokuti rudo rwaMwari rwakadirwa mumwoyo yedu noMweya Mutsvene watakapiwa. 
Romans5:6 Nokuti tichiri pakushayiwa simba, Kristu panguva yakafanira akafira vasingadi Mwari." 
Romans5:7 Nokuti zvinorema kuti munhu afire akarurama; nokuti zvimwe mumwe angatsunga kufira akanaka. 
Romans5:8 Asi Mwari anoratidza rudo rwake kwatiri pakuti Kristu akatifira, tichiri vatadzi." 
Romans5:9 Zvino, zvatakaruramiswa muropa rake, tichaponeswa zvikuru sei naye pakutsamwa." 
Romans5:10 Nokuti zvatakayananiswa naMwari nokufa kwoMwanakomana wake, tichiri vavengi vake, zvikuru tichaponeswa kana tayananiswa noupenyu hwake;" 
Romans5:11 zvisati zviri izvo bedzi, asi tinofara zvikuruwo muna Mwari naIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, watakapiwa zvino naye iko kuyananiswa." 
Romans5:12 Saka, zvivi sezvazvakapinda munyika nomunhu mumwe, norufu rukapinda nezvivi; saizvozvo rufu rwakasvika kuvanhu vose, nokuti vose vakatadza;" 
Romans5:13 nokuti murairo usati wavapo, zvivi zvakanga zviri panyika; asi zvivi hazviverengerwi munhu, kana kusina murairo." 
Romans5:14 Asi rufu rwakabata ushe kubva kuna Adhamu kusvikira kuna Mosesi, kunyangwe napakatiwo pavasina kutadza nokudarika kwaAdhamu, waiva mufananidzo waakanga achizouya." 
Romans5:15 Asi chipo chokungopiwa hachifanani nokudarika. Nokuti kana vazhinji vakafa nokudarika kwomumwe, zvikuru nyasha dzaMwari nechipo chakauya nenyasha dzomunhu mumwe, Jesu Kristu, zvakawandira vazhinji." 
Romans5:16 Uye chipo hachifanani nezvivi zvomunhu mumwe akatadza; nokuti kutonga kwakauya nomunhu mumwe kuti vapiwe mhosva; asi chipo chokungopiwa chakauya nokudarika kuzhinji, kuti varuramisirwe." 
Romans5:17 Nokuti kana nokudarika kwomumwe rufu rwakabata ushe nomunhu uyu mumwe; zvikuru avo, vakapiwa kuwanda kwenyasha nokwechipo chokururama, vachabata ushe paupenyu nomumwe, iye Jesu Kristu." 
Romans5:18 Naizvozvo, kutonga sezvakwakauya kuvanhu vose nokudarika kumwe, kuti vapiwe mhosva; saizvozvo nokururamisa kumwe chipo chokungopiwa chakauya kuvanhu vose, kururamisirwa kwoupenyu kukavapo." 
Romans5:19 Nokuti vazhinji sezvavakaitwa vatadzi nokusateerera kwomumwe, saizvozvo vazhinji vachaitwa vakarurama nokuteerera kwomumwe." 
Romans5:20 Murairo wakapindawo kuti kudarika kuwande; zvino zvivi pazvakawanda, nyasha dzakawanda nokupfuurisa;" 
Romans5:21 kuti zvivi sezvazvakabata ushe parufu, saizvozvo nyasha dzibate ushe nokururama, zviise kuupenyu husingaperi naJesu Kristu Ishe wedu." 
Romans6:1 Zvino tichatiiko? Torambira muzvivi kuti nyasha dziwande here? 
Romans6:2 Haisva! Isu takafa kuzvivi, tichagara seiko mukati mazvo?" 
Romans6:3 Ko hamuzivi here kuti isu takabhabhatidzwa muna Kristu Jesu, takabhabhatidzwa murufu rwake?" 
Romans6:4 Naizvozvo pakubhabhatidzwa takavigwa pamwechete naye murufu; kuti saiye Kristu akamutswa kuvakafa nokubwinya kwaBaba, saizvozvo nesuwo tifambe noupenyu hutsva." 
Romans6:5 Nokuti kana takava vamwe naye pakufanana naye parufu rwake, tichadarowo pakumuka kwake;" 
Romans6:6 tichiziva izvi, kuti munhu wedu wekare wakaroverwa pamuchinjikwa pamwechete naye, kuti muviri wezvivi ushaiswe simba, tirege kuzova varanda vezvivi;" 
Romans6:7 nokuti akafa, aruramiswa pazvivi." 
Romans6:8 Zvino kana takafa pamwechete naKristu, tinotenda kuti tichararamawo pamwechete naye;" 
Romans6:9 tichiziva kuti Kristu, amutswa kuvakafa, haachazofi; rufu haruchavi nesimba pamusoro pake." 
Romans6:10 Nokuti pakufa kwake, akafa kamwe kwazvo kuzvivi; zvino pakurarama kwake, anorarama kuna Mwari." 
Romans6:11 Saizvozvo nemiwo muzviti makafa kuzvivi, asi kuti muri vapenyu kuna Mwari, muna Kristu Jesu." 
Romans6:12 Naizvozvo zvivi ngazvirege kubata ushe mumuviri wenyu unofa, kuti muteerere kuchiva kwawo;" 
Romans6:13 uye musapa zvivi mitezo yenyu, kuti dzive nhumbi dzokuita zvisakarurama; asi muzvipe imi kuna Mwari, savanhu vakararama kuvakafa, nemitezo yenyu kuti dzive nhumbi dzokururama kuna Mwari." 
Romans6:14 Nokuti zvivi hazvingavi nesimba pamusoro penyu; nokuti hamuzi pasi pomurairo asi pasi penyasha. 
Romans6:15 Zvino tichatiiko? Titadze, nokuti hatizi pasi pomurairo here, asi pasi penyasha? Haisva!" 
Romans6:16 Hamuzivi here, kuti uyo wamunozvipa kwaari kuti muve varanda vake kumuteerera, kuti muri varanda vaiye wamunoteerera; kana vezvivi zvinoisa kurufu, kana wokuteerera kunoisa kukururama?" 
Romans6:17 Asi Mwari ngaavongwe, nokuti imi maiva varanda vezvivi, mukazoteerera nomwoyo rudzi urwu rwedzidziso yamakaiswa kwairi." 
Romans6:18 Makasunungurwa pazvivi, mukava varanda vokururama." 
Romans6:19 Ndinotaura nokutaura kwavanhu, nokuda kwokushayiwa simba kwenyama yenyu; nokuti sezvamakapa mitezo yenyu kuti ive varanda vetsvina, navezvisakarurama zvinoisa kune zvisakarurama, saizvozvo ipai mitezo yenyu zvino ive varanda vokururama kunoisa kuutsvene." 
Romans6:20 Nokuti panguva iyo muchiri varanda vezvivi, makanga makasununguka pakururama." 
Romans6:21 Zvino maiva nezvibereko zveiko panguva iyo pazvinhu izvo zvamunonyadziswa nazvo zvino? Nokuti kuguma kwazvo ndirwo rufu. 
Romans6:22 Asi zvino makasunungurwa pazvivi, mava varanda vaMwari, mune zvibereko zvenyu zvinoisa kuutsvene, uye kuguma kwazvo ndihwo upenyu husingaperi." 
Romans6:23 Nokuti mubairo wezvivi ndirwo rufu; asi chipo chokungopiwa chaMwari ndihwo upenyu husingaperi muna Kristu Jesu, Ishe wedu." 
Romans7:1 Hamuzivi here, hama dzangu, (nokuti ndinotaura navanhu vanoziva murairo), kuti murairo unobata munhu nguva yose youpenyu hwake?" 
Romans7:2 Nokuti mukadzi, ano murume, akasungwa nomurairo kumurume wake, iye achiri mupenyu; asi kana murume afa, asunungurwa pamurairo womurume." 
Romans7:3 Naizvozvo zvino kana akawanikwa nomumwe murume, murume wake achiri mupenyu, achanzi chipfeve asi kana murume wake afa, asununguka pamurairo, zvino haazi chipfeve kunyangwe akawanikwa nomumwe murume." 
Romans7:4 Saka, hama dzangu nemiwo makaitwa vakafa kumurairo nomuviri waKristu; kuti muve womumwe, iye akamutswa muvakafa, kuti tiberekere Mwari zvibereko." 
Romans7:5 Nokuti panguva iyo tichiri munyama, kuchiva kwezvivi, kwakamutswa nomurairo, kwakabata mumitezo yedu kuti kubereke zvibereko zvinoisa kurufu." 
Romans7:6 Asi zvino takasunungurwa pamurairo, takafa kuna izvozvo zvatakanga takasungwa nazvo; naizvozvo tinobatira Mwari nomweya mutsva, tisingabatiri nezvakanyorwa zvakare." 
Romans7:7 Zvino tichatiiko? Murairo zvivi here? Haisva! Asi handizaiziva zvivi kana murairo usaivapo; nokuti handizaiziva kuchiva, kana murairo usina kuti, “Usachiva;”" 
Romans7:8 zvino zvivi zvakawana nzira nomurairo, zvikaita mandiri mitoo yose yokuchiva; nokuti kunze kwomurairo zvivi zvakafa." 
Romans7:9 Ini ndaiva mupenyu kare kunze kwomurairo, asi mutemo uchizosvika, zvivi zvakamuka, ini ndikafa;" 
Romans7:10 nomutemo iwo waifanira kuisa kuupenyu, ndakauwana uchiisa kurufu;" 
Romans7:11 nokuti zvivi zvakawana nzira nomutemo, zvikandinyengera, zvikandiuraya nawo." 
Romans7:12 Naizvozvo murairo mutsvene, nomutemo mutsvene, wakarurama, wakanaka." 
Romans7:13 Ko zvino zvakanaka zvakazova rufu kwandiri here? Haisva! Asi ndizvo zvivi, kuti zviratidzwe kuti zvivi, zvakandiitira rufu nezvakanaka; kuti nomutemo zvivi zvive zvakaipa kwazvo–kwazvo." 
Romans7:14 Nokuti tinoziva kuti murairo ndowemweya; asi ini ndiri wenyama, ndakatengeswa pasi pezvivi." 
Romans7:15 Nokuti zvandinoita handizvizivi; nokuti zvandinoita hazvizi zvandinoda; asi zvandinovenga, ndizvo zvandinoita." 
Romans7:16 Zvino kana ndichiita zvandisingadi, ndinobvumira kuti murairo wakanaka" 
Romans7:17 Zvino handichini ndinozviita, asi zvivi zvinogara mandiri." 
Romans7:18 Nokuti ndinoziva kuti mukati mangu, imo munyama yangu, hamugari chinhu chakanaka; nokuti kuda kuripo kwandiri, asi kuita zvakanaka hakupo." 
Romans7:19 Nokuti zvakanaka, zvandinoda, handizviiti; asi zvakaipa, zvandisingadi, ndizvo zvandinoita." 
Romans7:20 Zvino kana ndichiita zvandisingadi, handichini ndinozviita, asi zvivi zvinogara mandiri." 
Romans7:21 Naizvozvo ndinowana murairo uyu kuti kana ndichida kuita zvakanaka, zvakaipa zviripo kwandiri." 
Romans7:22 Nokuti ndinofarira murairo waMwari nomunhu womukati; 
Romans7:23 asi ndinoona mumwe murairo pamitezo yangu, unorwa nomurairo womurangariro wangu, unonditapira kumurairo wezvivi uri pamitezo yangu." 
Romans7:24 Ndiri munhu uri pakutambudzika! Ndianiko achandisunungura pamuviri worufu urwu? 
Romans7:25 Mwari ngaavongwe, naJesu Kristu, Ishe wedu. Naizvozvo nomurangariro ndinobatira Mwari, asi nenyama murairo wezvivi." 
Romans8:1 Naizvozvo hakuchina kupiwa mhosva kuna vari muna Kristu Jesu. 
Romans8:2 Nokuti murairo woMweya woupenyu muna Kristu Jesu wakandisunungura pamurairo wezvivi noworufu. 
Romans8:3 Nokuti, zvakanga zvisingakwaniswi nomurairo, pakushaiwa kwawo simba nokuda kwenyama, Mwari pakutuma kwake Mwanakomana wake nomufananidzo wenyama yezvivi, nokuda kwezvivi, akapa mhosva zvivi zviri munyama;" 
Romans8:4 kuti zvakarehwa nomurairo zviitike matiri, isu tisingafambi nenyama, asi nomweya." 
Romans8:5 Nokuti vari venyama vanofunga zvenyama; asi vari vomweya, vanofunga zvomweya." 
Romans8:6 Nokuti kufunga kwenyama ndirwo rufu; asi kufunga kwomweya ndihwo upenyu norugare; 
Romans8:7 nokuti kufunga kwenyama kunovengana naMwari; nokuti hakuzviisi pasi pomurairo waMwari; hakugoniwo; 
Romans8:8 zvino vari munyama havagoni kufadza Mwari. 
Romans8:9 Asi imi hamuzi munyama, asi mumweya, kana Mweya waMwari achigara zvirokwazvo mukati menyu. Asi kana munhu asina Mweya waKristu, haazi wake." 
Romans8:10 Kana Kristu ari mukati menyu, muviri wakafa nokuda kwezvivi, asi mweya mupenyu nokuda kwokururama." 
Romans8:11 Zvino kana Mweya waiyeyo akamutsa Jesu kuvakafa achigara mukati menyu, iye akamutsa Kristu Jesu kuvakafa, achaponesa miviri yenyu inofa noMweya wake, unogara mukati menyu." 
Romans8:12 Naizvozvo, hama dzangu, hatina mungava nenyama, kuti tirarame netsika dzenyama." 
Romans8:13 Nokuti kana muchifamba netsika dzenyama, muchafa; asi kana muchiuraya mabasa omuviri noMweya, muchararama;" 
Romans8:14 nokuti vose vanotungamirirwa naMweya waMwari, ndivo vana vaMwari." 
Romans8:15 Nokuti hamuna kupiwa mweya wouranda kuti mutyezve, asi makapiwa mweya wokuitwa vana, watinodana nawo, tichiti, “Aba, baba.”" 
Romans8:16 Mweya amene anopupurirana nomweya wedu, kuti tiri vana vaMwari;" 
Romans8:17 zvino kana tiri vana, tiri vadyi venhaka; vadyi venhaka yaMwari, vadyi venhaka pamwechete naKristu; kana tichitambudzika pamwechete naye, tigokudzwawo pamwechete naye." 
Romans8:18 Nokuti ndinoti matambudziko enguva ino haana kufanira kuenzaniswa nokubwinya kuchazoratidzwa kwatiri. 
Romans8:19 Nokuti zvisikwa zvinotarisisa zvikuru zvichimirira kuratidzwa kwavanakomana vaMwari. 
Romans8:20 Nokuti zvisikwa zvakaiswa pasi pezvisingagari, zvisingadi hazvo, asi nokuda kwaiye wakazviisa pasi pazvo," 
Romans8:21 zvichitarira kuti zvisikwa zvimene zvisunungurwewo pauranda hwokuora, zviiswe pakusunungurwa kwokubwinya kwavana vaMwari." 
Romans8:22 Nokuti tinoziva kuti zvisikwa zvose zvinogomera nokurwadziwa pamwechete kusvikira zvino. 
Romans8:23 Zvisati zviri izvo bedzi, asi nesuwo, kunyangwe tine zvibereko zvokutanga zvoMweya, nesu timene tinogomera mukati medu, tichimirira kuitwa kwedu vana, ndiko kudzikinurwa kwomuviri wedu." 
Romans8:24 Nokuti takaponeswa netariro; asi tariro inoonekwa, haizi tariro; nokuti ndiani anotarira chaanoona?" 
Romans8:25 Asi kana tichitarira chatisingaoni, tinochimirira nokutsungirira." 
Romans8:26 Saizvozvo Mweya anobatiranawo nokusava nesimba kwedu; nokuti hatizivi kunyengetera zvakafanira; asi Mweya amene unotinyengeterera nokugomera kusingataurwi; 
Romans8:27 uyo anonzvera mwoyo, ndiye anoziva kufunga kwoMweya, nokuti anonyengeterera vatsvene sezvinoda Mwari." 
Romans8:28 Tinoziva kuti zvinhu zvose zvinobatirana kuti zviitire zvakanaka avo vanoda Mwari, avo vakadanwa sezvaakafunga." 
Romans8:29 Nokuti vaakafanoziva kare, ndivo vaakatemerawo kare, kuti vafanane nomufananidzo woMwanakomana wake, kuti ave dangwe pakati pehama zhinji;" 
Romans8:30 avo vaakatemera kare, ndivo vaakadanawo; vaakadana, ndivo vaakaruramisawo; vaakaruramisa, ndivo vaakakudzawo." 
Romans8:31 Zvino tichatiiko pazvinhu izvi? Kana Mwari achitirwira, ndianiko achatirwisa?" 
Romans8:32 Iye asina kuramba kunyangwe noMwanakomana wake, asi akamupa chose nokuda kwedu tose, angarega seiko kutipawo zvose pamwechete naye?" 
Romans8:33 Ndianiko achakwirira vasanangurwa vaMwari? Mwari ndiye anoruramisa. 
Romans8:34 Ndianiko achavapa mhosva? Kristu Jesu ndiye akafa, zvikuru ndiye akamutswa kuvakafa, ari kurudyi rwaMwari, anotinyengetererawo." 
Romans8:35 Ndianiko achatiparadzanisa norudo rwaKristu? Kutambudzika, kana nhamo, kana kuvengwa, kana nzara, kana kushayiwa zvokufuka, kana njodzi, kana munondo here?" 
Romans8:36 Sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Nokuda kwenyu tinourayiwa zuva rose; Takanzi tiri makwai anobayiwa.”" 
Romans8:37 Kwete, pazvinhu izvi zvose tiri vakundi nokupfuurisa naiye wakatida." 
Romans8:38 Nokuti ndinoziva kwazvo kuti kunyangwe rufu, kana upenyu, kana vatumwa, kana vakuru, kana zvazvino, kana zvinouya, kana masimba," 
Romans8:39 kana kwakakwirira, kana kwakadzika, kana chinhu chimwe chakasikwa, hazvingagoni kutiparadzanisa norudo rwaMwari, ruri muna Kristu Jesu, Ishe wedu." 
Romans9:1 Ndinotaura zvirokwazvo muna Kristu, handirevi nhema, hana yangu ichindipupurira muMweya Mutsvene," 
Romans9:2 kuti ndine shungu kwazvo nokuchema kusingaperi mumwoyo mangu. 
Romans9:3 Nokuti ndaida kuti ini ndimene ndive munhu akatukwa, akaparadzaniswa naKristu nokuda kwehama dzangu, ivo vorudzi rwangu panyama;" 
Romans9:4 ndivo VaIsiraeri; kuva vana, nokubwinya, nesungano, nokupiwa murairo, nokunamata Mwari, nezvipikirwa, ndezvavo;" 
Romans9:5 madzibaba ndaavo, naKristu akabva kwavari panyama, ari pamusoro pavose, Mwari anokudzwa nokusingaperi. Ameni." 
Romans9:6 Asi handiti shoko raMwari rakakona. Nokuti vakabva kuVaIsiraeri havazi VaIsiraeri vose; 
Romans9:7 navari vorudzi rwaAbhurahamu havazi vana vake vose; asi zvinonzi, “Kuna Isaka ndiko kuchatumidzwa rudzi rwako.”" 
Romans9:8 Ndokuti havazi vana venyama vari vana vaMwari; asi vana vokupikirwa, ndivo vanonzi rudzi." 
Romans9:9 Nokuti shoko rakapikirwa ndirori, “Nenguva yakaita seino ndichauya, Sara achava nomwanakomana.”" 
Romans9:10 Hazvizi izvozvo bedzi; asi Rabhekawo, wakati ava nemimba kuno mumwe, iye Isaka, baba vedu." 
Romans9:11 Nokuti vana vasati vaberekwa, vasati vaita zvakanaka kana zvakaipa, kuti kufunga kwaMwari pakutsanangura kwake kusimbiswe, kusingabvi pamabasa, asi kuna iye anodana," 
Romans9:12 zvakanzi kwaari, “Mukuru achava muranda womuduku.”" 
Romans9:13 Sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Jakobho ndakamuda, asi Esau ndakamuvenga.”" 
Romans9:14 Zvino tichatiiko? Kusarurama kuripo kuna Mwari here? Haisva! 
Romans9:15 Nokuti anoti kuna Mosesi, “Ndichanzwira ngoni wandinonzwira tsitsi.”" 
Romans9:16 Naizvozvo hazvibvi kunoanoda, kana kunoanomhanya, asi kuna Mwari, munzwiri wengoni." 
Romans9:17 Nokuti Rugwaro runoti kuna Farao, “Ndizvo zvandakakumutsira, kuti ndiratidze simba rangu kwauri, uye kuti zita rangu riparidzwe panyika yose.”" 
Romans9:18 Naizvozvo anonzwira ngoni waanoda; uye anoomesera mwoyo waanoda. 
Romans9:19 Zvino iwe ungati kwandiri, “Iye achapireiko mhosva? Nokuti ndianiko anoramba kuda kwake?”" 
Romans9:20 Ko zvino iwe munhu, ndiwe aniko, unopindura Mwari? Ko chakaumbwa chingati kuno akachiumba, “Wandiitireiko kudai?”" 
Romans9:21 Ko muwumbi wehari haana simba pamusoro pevhu here, kuti nebundu rimwe aite midziyo mumwe wakakudzwa, nomumwe usina kukudzwa?" 
Romans9:22 Zvino tichatiiko kuna Mwari, kana akanga achida kuratidza kutsamwa kwake, nokuzivisa simba rake, akaita nomwoyo murefu zvikuru pamusoro pemidziyo yokutsamwirwa, yakagadzirirwa kuparadzwa," 
Romans9:23 kuti azivise kufuma kwokubwinya kwake pamusoro pemidziyo yengoni, yaakanga agadzirira kubwinya," 
Romans9:24 iyesu vakadanwawo naye, tisingabvi kuvaJudha bedzi, asi kuvahedheniwo?" 
Romans9:25 Sezvaanorevawo muBhuku yaHosiya, achiti, “Avo vakanga vasi vanhu vangu, ndichavaidza, ‘Vanhu vangu;’ Naiye akanga asi mudikanwi, ndichamuidza, ‘Mudikanwi.’" 
Romans9:26 Zvichaitika kuti paya pakanga parehwa kwavari, ‘Hamuzi vanhu vangu,’ Ipapo vachaidzwa vanakomana vaMwari mupenyu.”" 
Romans9:27 NaIsaya anodana pamusoro paVaIsiraeri, achiti, “Kana kuwanda kwavana VaIsiraeri kwakaita sejecha regungwa, vakasara ndivo vachaponeswa;" 
Romans9:28 nokuti Ishe achaita panyika shoko rake, nokuripedzisa nokukurumidza.”" 
Romans9:29 Sezvaakamboreva Isayawo, achiti, “Dai Ishe wehondo asina kutisiyira rudzi, Tingadai takava seSodhoma, takaitwa seGomora.”" 
Romans9:30 Zvino tichatiiko? Tichati, vahedheni vasina kutsvaka kururama, ndivo vakawana kururama, iko kururama kwokutenda;" 
Romans9:31 asi VaIsiraeri vakati vachitsvaka murairo wokururama, havana kusvika pamurairo iwoyo." 
Romans9:32 Neiko? Nokuti havana kuutsvaka nokutenda, asi zvinenge namabasa avo. Vakagumburwa nebwe rinogumbusa." 
Romans9:33 Sezvazvakanyorwa zvichinzi, “Tarira, ndinoisa paZioni ibwe rokugumbusa, nedombo rokupinganidza; Anotenda kwaari, haanganyadziswi.”" 
Romans10:1 Hama dzangu, kuda kwomwoyo wangu nokukumbira kwangu kuna Mwari pamusoro pavo ndiko, kuti vaponeswe." 
Romans10:2 Nokuti ndinovapupurira kuti vanoshingairira Mwari, asi havaiti nokuziva." 
Romans10:3 Nokuti, zvavakanga vasingazivi kururama kwaMwari, vakatsvaka kumisa kururama kwavo vomene, vakasazviisa pasi pokururama kwaMwari." 
Romans10:4 Nokuti Kristu ndimugumo womurairo, kuti mumwe nomumwe anotenda aruramiswe." 
Romans10:5 Nokuti Mosesi anonyora achiti, “Munhu, anoita kururama, kunorehwa nomurairo, achararama nazvo.”" 
Romans10:6 Asi kururama kunobva pakutenda, kunoreva kudai, “Usati mumwoyo mako, ndianiko achakwira kudenga?” (Ndiko kuburusa Kristu;)" 
Romans10:7 kana, “Ndianiko achaburukira kwakadzika–dzika?” (Ndiko kubudisa Kristu kuvakafa.)" 
Romans10:8 Asi kunoreveiko? “Shoko riri pedyo newe, mumuromo mako, ndiro shoko rokutenda ratinoparidza;”" 
Romans10:9 kana, kuti uchipupura nomuromo wako kuti Jesu ndiye Ishe, nokutenda mumwoyo mako, kuti Mwari akamumutsa kuvakafa, uchaponeswa;" 
Romans10:10 nokuti munhu anotenda nomwoyo, ndokururamiswa; anopupura nomuromo, ndokuponeswa." 
Romans10:11 Nokuti Rugwaro runoti, “Ani naani anotenda kwaari, haanganyadziswi.”" 
Romans10:12 Nokuti muJudha nomuGiriki havasiyani; nokuti mumwe ndiye Ishe wavose, akapfuma kuna vose vanodana kwaari;" 
Romans10:13 nokuti aninaani anodana kuzita raIshe, achaponeswa." 
Romans10:14 Zvino vachagodana seiko kuna iye, wavasina kutenda kwaari? Vachatenda seiko kuna iye, wavasina kunzwa? Vachanzwa seiko kana kusina muparidzi?" 
Romans10:15 Vachaparidza seiko, kana vasingatumwi? Sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Dzakanaka sei tsoka dzavanouya namashoko omufaro ezvinhu zvakanaka?”" 
Romans10:16 Asi vose havana kuteerera mashoko omufaro. Nokuti Isaya anoti, “Ishe, ndianiko akatenda zvatakaparidza?”" 
Romans10:17 Naizvozvo kutenda kunouya nokunzwa, nokunzwa kunouya neshoko raKristu." 
Romans10:18 Asi ndinoti, “Havana kunzwa here? Izwi ravo rakabuda kunyika yose, Namashoko avo kumigumo yenyika.”" 
Romans10:19 Asi ndinoti, VaIsiraeri havana kuziva here? Pakutanga Mosesi anoti, “Ndichamutsa godo renyu norudzi rusati ruri rudzi, Ndichamutsa kutsamwa kwenyu norudzi rusinganzwisisi.”" 
Romans10:20 NaIsaya, asingatyi, anoti, “Ndakawanikwa navasina kunditsvaka, Ndakaonekwa navasina kundibvunza.”" 
Romans10:21 Asi kuVaIsiraeri anoti, “Ndakatambanudzira maoko angu zuva rose kuvanhu vasingateereri, navanokakavara.”" 
Romans11:1 Zvino ndinoti, Ko Mwari wakarasa vanhu vake here? Haisva! Nokuti neniwo ndiri muIsiraeri, worudzi rwaAbhurahamu, weimba yaBhenjamini." 
Romans11:2 Mwari haana kurasa vanhu vake vaakaziva pakutanga. Ko hamuzivi kuti Rugwaro runoti kudini pamashoko aEriya here? Kuti anokumbira kuna Mwari pamusoro paVaIsiraeri, achiti," 
Romans11:3 “Ishe, vakauraya vaporofita venyu, vakaputsa atari dzenyu; ini ndakasiyiwa ndoga, zvino vanotsvaka kundiuraya?”" 
Romans11:4 Asi Mwari anomupindureiko? Anoti, “Ndakazvisiyira varume vane zviuru zvinomwe vasina kupfugamira Bhaari.”" 
Romans11:5 Zvino, saizvozvo nenguva inowo variko vakasara, vakatsanangurwa nenyasha." 
Romans11:6 Zvino kana kutsanangura kuri kwenyasha, hakusati kuchiri kwamabasa; kana zvisakadaro, nyasha hadzichiri nyasha." 
Romans11:7 Zvino tichatiiko? VaIsiraeri havana kuwana zvavakanga vachitsvaka, asi vakatsanangurwa ndivo vakazviwana; vamwe vakaomeswa," 
Romans11:8 sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Mwari akavapa mweya wehope; kuti varege kunzwa, kusvikira zuva ranhasi.”" 
Romans11:9 NaDhavhidhiwo anoti, “Tafura yavo ngaiitwe musungo, neriva, Nechigumbuso, nechinotsiva kwavari," 
Romans11:10 Meso avo ngaasvibirwe, varege kuona; Mukotamise misana yavo misi yose.”" 
Romans11:11 Zvino ndinoti, Vakagumbuswa kuti vawe here? Haisva! Asi nokuwa kwavo ruponeso rwakasvika kuvahedheni, kuti vamutsirwe godo." 
Romans11:12 Zvino kana kuwa kwavo kwakafumisa nyika, nokutapudzwa kwavo kwakafumisa vahedheni, zvikuru sei kuzara kwavo?" 
Romans11:13 Ndinotaura kwamuri, imi vahedheni. Zvandiri mupostori wavahedheni, ndinokudza basa rangu." 
Romans11:14 Zvimwe ndingamutsa godo kuna venyama yangu, ndiponese vamwe vavo." 
Romans11:15 Nokuti kana kuraswa kwavo kuri kuyananiswa kwenyika, kugamuchirwa kwavo kuchagoveiko, asi upenyu pakufa?" 
Romans11:16 Zvino kana chibereko chokutanga chiri chitsvene, bundu rose rakadarowo; kana mudzi uri mutsvene, matavi akadarowo." 
Romans11:17 Zvino, kana mamwe matavi akavhuniwa, iwe, muorivhi wokudondo ukabatanidzwa pakati pawo, ukava nomugove pamwechete nawo pamudzi napamafuta omuorivhi;" 
Romans11:18 usazvikudza pamusoro pamatavi; kana uchizvikudza, hauzi iwe unotakura mudzi, asi mudzi ndiwo unokutakura iwe." 
Romans11:19 Zvino iwe uchati, “Matavi akavhuniwa, kuti ini ndibatanidzwe.”" 
Romans11:20 Ndizvozvo; vakavhuniwa nokusatenda kwavo iwe unomira nokutenda kwako. Usazvikudza, asi utye;" 
Romans11:21 nokuti kana Mwari asina kurega matavi okutanga, haangakuregi newewo." 
Romans11:22 Zvino tarira unyoro nokukasharara kwaMwari; kukasharara kuna vakawa, asi kwauri unyoro hwaMwari, kana uchigara paunyoro hwake; kana zvisakadaro newe uchatemwawo." 
Romans11:23 Naivowo, kana vasingagari pakusatenda kwavo, vachabatanidzwa; nokuti Mwari anogona kuvabatanidzazve." 
Romans11:24 Nokuti kana iwe wakatemwa kumuorivhi, uri wokudondo pakusikwa kwawo, ukabatanidzwa pamuorivhi wakanaka, zvichipesana nokusikwa kwazvo zvikuru sei ava vari vomuti iwoyo umene, vangabatanidzwa pamuorivhi wavo!" 
Romans11:25 Nokuti hama dzangu, handidi kuti musaziva chavanzika ichi, kuti murege kuva namanyawi; kuti kuomeswa kwomwoyo kwakauya pamusoro pavamwe vaVaIsiraeri kusvikira kuzara kwavahedheni kwapinda;" 
Romans11:26 naizvozvo rudzi rwose rwaVaIsiraeri ruchaponeswa; sezvazvakanyorwa zvichinzi, “PaZioni pachabuda Musununguri; Achabvisa kusada Mwari kuna Jakobho;" 
Romans11:27 Iyi ndiyo sungano yangu navo, Musi wandichabvisa zvivi zvavo.”" 
Romans11:28 Kana iri Vhangeri, ivo vavengi vaMwari nokuda kwenyu; asi kana kuri kutsanangurwa, vadikanwi nokuda kwamadzibaba." 
Romans11:29 Nokuti zvipo zvaMwari nokudana kwake hazvishandurwi. 
Romans11:30 Nokuti semi kare makanga musingateereri Mwari, asi zvino makanzwirwa ngoni nokusateerera kwavo," 
Romans11:31 saizvozvo naivo zvino havana kuterera, kuti nengoni dzakaitirwa imi naivo vanzwirwewo ngoni." 
Romans11:32 Nokuti Mwari akavapfigira vose pakusateerera kwavo, kuti avanzwire ngoni vose." 
Romans11:33 Aiwa kupfuma kwokuchenjera nokuziva kwaMwari kwakadzika sei! Kutonga kwake hakunganzverwi, nenzira dzake hadzingarondwi!" 
Romans11:34 Nokuti ndianiko akaziva murangariro waIshe? Ndianiko akanga ari chipangamazano wake? 
Romans11:35 Ndianiko akatanga kumupa, kuti aripirwezve?" 
Romans11:36 Nokuti zvose zvinobva kwaari, zviripo naye, zviripo nokuda kwake. Ngaave nokubwinya nokusingaperi. Ameni." 
Romans12:1 Naizvozvo ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri, hama dzangu, netsitsi dzaMwari, kuti muise miviri yenyu, chive chibayiro chipenyu, chitsvene, chinofadza Mwari, ndiko kunamata kwenyu kwomwoyo." 
Romans12:2 Musaenzaniswa nenyika ino; asi mushandurwe murangariro wenyu uchivandudzwa, kuti muedze muzive kuda kwaMwari kwakanaka, kunofadza, kwakakwana." 
Romans12:3 Nokuti nenyasha dzandakapiwa, ndinoudza mumwe nomumwe ari pakati penyu, kuti arege kuzvifunga mukuru kupfuura paanofanira kufunga napo; asi afunge nokufunga kwakachenjera, mumwe nomumwe nechiyero chokutenda, sezvaakagoverwa naMwari." 
Romans12:4 Nokuti sezvatine mitezo mizhinji pamuviri mumwe, asi mitezo yose haina basa rimwechete;" 
Romans12:5 saizvozvo isu, tiri vazhinji, tiri muviri mumwechete muna Kristu, mumwe nomumwe ari mutezo wavamwe." 
Romans12:6 Tine zvipo zvakasiyana, patakapiwa nyasha napo; kana kuri kuporofita, ngatiporofite zvakaenzana nokutenda kwedu;" 
Romans12:7 kana kuri kushumira, ngazvionekwe pakushumira kwedu; kana kuri kudzidzisa, pakudzidzisa kwedu;" 
Romans12:8 kana kuri kurayira, pakurayira kwedu; anopa, ngaape nomwoyo wose; ari mukuru, ngaabate nokushingaira; anoitira ngoni, ngaaite nomufaro." 
Romans12:9 Rudo ngarurege kuva nokunyengera. Vengai zvakaipa; namatirai zvakanaka. 
Romans12:10 Kana ruri rudo pakati pavatendi, danai norudo rukuru; pakukudzana tungamiriranai." 
Romans12:11 Regai kuva nousimbe pakushingaira; pisai pamweya; batirai Ishe; 
Romans12:12 farai patariro; tsungirirai pakutambudzika; rambai muchinyengetera; 
Romans12:13 govanai navatsvene pakushayiwa kwavo; itirai vaeni rudo. 
Romans12:14 Ropafadzai vanokutambudzai; ropafadzai, musatuka." 
Romans12:15 Farai navanofara; chemai navanochema. 
Romans12:16 Ivai nomwoyo mumwe pakati penyu. Musatsvaka zvinorumbidzwa, asi mufambidzane navanozvininipisa. Musati pamwoyo yenyu makachenjera." 
Romans12:17 Musatsiva munhu chakaipa kana akuitirai chakaipa. Tsvakai zvakarurama pamberi pavanhu vose. 
Romans12:18 Kana zvichibvira, pamunogona napo, ivai norugare navanhu vose." 
Romans12:19 Musatsiva, vadikanwi, asi mudziurire kutsamwa; nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, “Kutsiva ndokwangu, ini ndicharipira ndizvo zvinoreva Ishe.”" 
Romans12:20 Asi kana muvengi wako aziya, umupe kudya; kana afa nenyota, umupe kunwa; nokuti kana uchiita izvozvo, uchatutira mazimbe omoto pamusoro wake." 
Romans12:21 Usakundwa nezvakaipa, asi ukunde zvakaipa nezvakanaka." 
Romans13:1 Munhu mumwe nomumwe ngaazviise pasi pamasimba makuru; nokuti hakuna simba risina kubva kuna Mwari; iwo aripo akaiswapo naMwari. 
Romans13:2 Saka anoramba simba, anodzivisa zvakaiswapo naMwari; zvino ivo vanodzivisa, vanozvitorera mhosva." 
Romans13:3 Nokuti vabati havatyisi anobata basa rakanaka, asi rakaipa. Unoda kusatya simba here? Ita zvakanaka, ugorumbidzwa naro;" 
Romans13:4 nokuti ndiye mushumiri waMwari kwauri, kuti akuitire zvakanaka. Asi kana uchiita zvakaipa, chitya; nokuti iye haabati munondo pasina; nokuti ndiye mushumiri waMwari, mutsivi wokutsamwa kunoanoita zvakaipa." 
Romans13:5 Naizvozvo munofanira kuzviisa pasi pavo, musingadaro nokuda kwokutsamwa bedzi, asi nokuda kwehanawo." 
Romans13:6 Nokuti nemhaka iyo munoripawo mutero; nokuti ndiwo varanda vaMwari, vanoramba vachingobatira chinhu icho." 
Romans13:7 Ripirai vose zvavanofanira kuripirwa, Mutero kuna vanofanira kutererwa; kutya kuna vanofanira kutyiwa; kukudza kuna vanofanira kukudzwa." 
Romans13:8 Musava nechikwereti nomunhu, asi chokudana; nokuti anoda mumwe, azadzisa murairo." 
Romans13:9 Nokuti izvo zvokuti, “Usaita upombwe, usauraya, usaba, usachiva; kana murairo upi noupi,” zvakaunganidzwa pashoko rokuti, “Ude wokwako sezvaunozvida iwe.”" 
Romans13:10 Rudo haruitiri wokwako zvakaipa; naizvozvo rudo runozadzisa murairo. 
Romans13:11 Zvikuru ndinoreva izvozvi, zvatinoziva nguva, kuti zvino yatova nguva yokumuka kwenyu pahope; nokuti zvino kuponeswa kwedu kwava pedyo kupfuura zuva ratakatanga kutenda naro." 
Romans13:12 Usiku hwapfuura, kwoedza; naizvozvo ngatirashe mabasa erima, ngatishonge nhumbi dzokurwa dzechiedza." 
Romans13:13 Ngatifambe nenzira yakafanira sapamasikati; tisingafambi nokutamba kwakaipa, nokubatwa, kana noupombwe, noutere, kana negakava, negodo." 
Romans13:14 Asi pfekai Ishe Jesu Kristu, musatsvaka kufadza nyama pakuchiva kwayo." 
Romans14:1 Zvino gamuchirai asina simba pakutenda kwake musingaiti gakava naye pamusoro pokufunga kwake. 
Romans14:2 Mumwe munhu anokutenda kuti angadya zvose; asi asina simba anodya miriwo. 
Romans14:3 Anodya ngaarege kuzvidza asingadyi; asingadyi ngaarege kupa mhosva anodya; nokuti Mwari akamugamuchira. 
Romans14:4 Iwe ndiwe aniko unopa muranda womumwe munhu mhosva? Iye anomira kana anowa pamberi paIshe wake. Achamiswa hake, nokuti Ishe ane simba rokumumisa." 
Romans14:5 Mumwe munhu anoti zuva rimwe rinopfuura rimwe; mumwe anoti mazuva ose akafanana. Mumwe nomumwe ngaazive kwazvo mumwoyo make. 
Romans14:6 Uyo anochengeta zuva, anorichengeta nokuda kwaIshe; uyo anodya, anodya nokuda kwaIshe, nokuti anovonga Mwari; uyo asingadyi, haadyi nokuda kwaIshe, naiye anovonga Mwari." 
Romans14:7 Nokuti hakuna mumwe wedu anozviraramira iye oga, hakuna anozvifira iye oga." 
Romans14:8 Nokuti kana tichirarama tinoraramira Ishe; kana tichifa, kana tichifa tinofira Ishe; zvino kana tichirarama, kana tichifa, tiri vaIshe." 
Romans14:9 Nokuti Kristu akafira izvozvi, akararamazve kuti ave Ishe wavose vakafa navapenyu." 
Romans14:10 Zvino iwe, unopireiko hama yako mhosva? Kana newewo, unozvidzireiko hama yako? Nokuti isu tose tichamira pachigaro chokutonga chaMwari." 
Romans14:11 Nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, “Noupenyu hwangu ndizvo zvinoreva Ishe ibvi rimwe nerimwe richandipfugamira, Rurimi rumwe norumwe ruchakudza Mwari.”" 
Romans14:12 Naizvozvo mumwe nomumwe wedu achazvidavirira kuna Mwari. 
Romans14:13 Naizvozvo ngatirege kuramba tichitongana; asi zviri nani kuti mutonge, kuti munhu arege kuisa chigumbuso kana chinopinganidza pamberi pehama yake." 
Romans14:14 Ndinoziva, nokuzivisisa kwazvo muna Ishe Jesu, kuti hakuna chinhu chine tsvina." 
Romans14:15 Nokuti kana hama yako ichisvibiswa mwoyo nokuda kwezvokudya, iwe hauchafambi norudo. Usaparadza nezvokudya zvako uyo akafirwa naKristu." 
Romans14:16 Naizvozvo kunaka kwenyu ngakurege kuzvidzwa. 
Romans14:17 Nokuti ushe hwaMwari hazvizi zvokudya kana zvokunwa, asi kururama, norugare, nomufaro muMweya Mutsvene." 
Romans14:18 Nokuti unobatira Kristu pazvinhu izvi, anofadza Mwari, uye anotendwa navanhu." 
Romans14:19 Naizvozvo ngatitsvake izvo zvinouyisa rugare nezvatingasimbisana nazvo. 
Romans14:20 Regai kuparadza basa raMwari nokuda kwezvokudya. Zvinhu zvose zvakanaka hazvo, asi zvakaipira munhu anodya achigumbusa vamwe." 
Romans14:21 Zvakanaka kusadya nyama, kana kusanwa waini, kana kusaita chimwe chinhu chingagumbusa hama yako." 
Romans14:22 Kana uri iwe, kutenda kwaunako uve nako umene pamberi paMwari. Akaropafadzwa munhu uyo asingazvipi mhosva pazvinhu zvaanozvitendera." 
Romans14:23 Asi uyo anonyunyuta ava nemhosva kana achidya, nokuti haadyi nokutenda; zvose zvisingabvi pakutenda, zvivi." 
Romans15:1 Zvino isu, tine simba, tinofanira kutakura utera hwavasina simba, tisingazvifadzi." 
Romans15:2 Mumwe nomumwe wedu ngaafadze wokwake pane zvakanaka zvinosimbisa. 
Romans15:3 Nokuti Kristuwo haana kuzvifadza; asi sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Kuzvidza kwavakakuzvidza nako kwakawira pamusoro pangu.”" 
Romans15:4 Nokuti zvose zvakanyorwa kare, zvakanyorwa kuti isu tidzidze kuti tive netariro inobva pakutsungirira napakunyaradza kwaMagwaro." 
Romans15:5 Zvino Mwari wokutsungirira nowokunyaradza ngaakupei mwoyo mumwe pakati penyu, sezvinoda Kristu Jesu;" 
Romans15:6 kuti mukudze Mwari, baba vaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, nomwoyo mumwe uye nomuromo mumwe." 
Romans15:7 Saka gamuchirai, Kristu sezvaakatigamuchira, kuti Mwari akudzwe." 
Romans15:8 Nokuti ndinoti, Kristu akaitwa mushumiri wokudzingiswa kuratidza zvokwadi yaMwari, kuti asimbise zvakapikirwa madzibaba." 
Romans15:9 Uye, kuti vahedheni vakudze Mwari nokuda kwengoni dzake; sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Naizvozvo ndichakurumbidzai pakati pavahedheni, Nokukuimbirai zita renyu.”" 
Romans15:10 Uyezve unoti, “Farai imi vahedheni, navanhu vake.”" 
Romans15:11 Uyezve, “Rumbidzai Ishe, imi vahedheni vose; Marudzi ose ngaamukudze.”" 
Romans15:12 Uyezve, Isaya anoti, “Mudzi waJese uchavapo, Naiye unomuka, kuti abate vahedheni; Vahedheni vachamutarira iye.”" 
Romans15:13 Zvino Mwari wetariro ngaakuzadzei nomufaro wose norugare pakutenda kwenyu, kuti muve netariro yakawandisa, nesimba roMweya Mutsvene." 
Romans15:14 Zvino, hama dzangu, ini ndimene ndinoziva kwazvo pamusoro penyu, kuti imi mumene muzere nokunaka, makazadzwa nokuziva kwose, munogonawo kurayirana." 
Romans15:15 Asi ndinokunyorerai zvimwe ndichinyanya kutsunga, ndichiita sendinokuyeudzai nenyasha dzandakapiwa naMwari," 
Romans15:16 kuti ndive muranda waKristu Jesu kuvahedheni, ndichiita basa roupristi muVhangeri yaMwari, kuti chibayiro chavahedheni chifadze Mwari, chakaitwa chitsvene noMweya Mutsvene." 
Romans15:17 Naizvozvo ndingazvirumbidza muna Kristu Jesu pazvinhu zvaMwari. 
Romans15:18 Nokuti ndingatya kutaura zvimwe zvinhu, asi izvo Kristu zvaakaita neni, kuti vahedheni vaterereswe neshoko namabasa," 
Romans15:19 nesimba rezviratidzo nezvinoshamisa, nesimba roMweya Mutsvene; nokuda kubva Jerusaremu nenyika yakapoteredza, kusvikira Iririko, ndakaparidza kwazvo Vhangeri yaKristu;" 
Romans15:20 ndichishingairira chinhu ichi kuti ndiparidze Vhangeri, apo pasina kumborehwa zita raKristu, kuti ndirege kuvaka pamusoro penheyo dzomumwe munhu;" 
Romans15:21 asi, sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Avo, vasina kuudzwa zvake, vachaona; Naivo vasina kunzwa vachanzwisisa.”" 
Romans15:22 Naizvozvo ndakadziviswawo kazhinji kuuya kwamuri; 
Romans15:23 zvino zvandisina pokubata panyika idzi, uye zvaava makore mazhinji ndichida zvikuru kuuya kwamuri," 
Romans15:24 kana ndichienda Sipeini, ndichauya kwamuri; (nokuti ndinotarira kukuonai parwendo rwangu, ndiperekedzwe nemi ikoko, kana ndamboguta zvishoma kuonana nemi)." 
Romans15:25 Asi zvino ndomboenda Jerusaremu kundoshumira vatsvene. 
Romans15:26 Nokuti veMasedhonia naveAkaia vakati zvakanaka kuti vagovane navarombo pavatsvene vari muJerusaremu. 
Romans15:27 Nokuti vakati zvakanaka; vane ngava navo. Nokuti kana vahedheni vakaitwa vagovani navo pazvinhu zvoMweya, vane ngavawo rokuvashumira pazvinhu zvenyama." 
Romans15:28 Naizvozvo kana ndapedza chinhu ichi, ndikavavigira chibereko ichi, ndichaenda Sipeini nokwenyu." 
Romans15:29 Ndinoziva kuti kana ndichiuya kwenyu, ndichauya nokuropafadza kwakazara kwaKristu." 
Romans15:30 Zvino ndinokumbira zvikuru, hama dzangu, naIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu, uye norudo rwoMweya, kuti murwe pamwechete neni pakunyengetera kwenyu kuna Mwari pamusoro pangu;" 
Romans15:31 kuti ndisunungurwe kuna vasingateereri muJudhiya, uye kuti kushumira kwangu kuna veJerusaremu kufadze vatsvene;" 
Romans15:32 kuti ndiuye kwamuri nomufaro nokuda kwaMwari, ndiwane zororo pamwechete nemi." 
Romans15:33 Zvino Mwari worugare ngaave nemi mose. Ameni. 
Romans16:1 Ndinoreverera kwamuri Fibhi, hanzvadzi yedu, mushandiri wechechi iri paKenikiria." 
Romans16:2 Kuti mumugamuchire muna Ishe, sezvinofanira vatsvene, nokumubatsira pazvinhu zvose zvaangashayiwa; nokuti iye amene akabatsira vazhinji, neniwo ndimene." 
Romans16:3 Ndikwazisirei Pirisika naAkwira, vanobata neni muna Kristu Jesu," 
Romans16:4 vakaisa mitsipa yavo kurwira upenyu hwangu; vandisingavongi ini ndoga, asi nechechi dzose dzavahedheni." 
Romans16:5 Ndikwazisireiwo Chechi iri paimba yavo. Ndikwazisirei Epeneto, mudikanwi wangu, ndiye chibereko chokutanga muna Kristu paEzhia." 
Romans16:6 Ndikwazisirei Maria, akakubatsirai zvikuru." 
Romans16:7 Ndikwazisirei Andironiko naJunia, worudzi rwangu, vakasungwa pamwechete neni, vakakurumbira pakati pavapostori, vakanditangirawo kuva muna Kristu." 
Romans16:8 Ndikwazisirei Amupiriato, mudikanwi wangu muna Ishe." 
Romans16:9 Ndikwazisirei Uribhano, anobata nesu muna Kristu, naSitako, mudikanwi wangu." 
Romans16:10 Ndikwazisirei Apere, akatendwa muna Kristu. Ndikwazisirei vokwaArisitobhuro." 
Romans16:11 Ndikwazisirei Herodhio worudzi rwangu. Ndikwazisirei vokwaNarikiso, vari muna Ishe." 
Romans16:12 Ndikwazisirei Tirifaina naTirifosa, vanobata muna Ishe. Ndikwazisirei Pesisi, mudikanwi, akabata zvikuru muna Ishe." 
Romans16:13 Ndikwazisirei Rufosi, musanangurwi muna Ishe, naamai vake, navangu." 
Romans16:14 Ndikwazisirei Asinikiroto, naFiregoni, naHerimesi, naPatirobhasi, naHerimasi, nehama dziri kwavari." 
Romans16:15 Ndikwazisirei Firorogosi, naJuria, naNerea, nehanzvadzi yake, naOrimipasi, navatsvene vose vari kwavari." 
Romans16:16 Kwazisanani nokutsvoda kutsvene. Chechi dzose dzaKristu dzinokukwazisai. 
Romans16:17 Zvino ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri, hama dzangu, kuti mucherekedze avo vanopesanisa, navanogumbusa, vachiita zvinopesana nedzidziso yamakadzidza imi; muvanzvenge." 
Romans16:18 Nokuti vakadaro havabatiri Ishe wedu Kristu, asi dumbu ravo; vanonyengera mwoyo yavasina zvakaipa namashoko avo akanaka, anobata kumeso." 
Romans16:19 Nokuti kuteerera kwenyu kwakasvika kuvanhu vose. Naizvozvo ndinofara pamusoro penyu; asi ndinoda kuti muve vakachenjera kune zvakanaka, asi vasina njere kune zvakaipa." 
Romans16:20 Zvino Mwari worugare achakurumidza kupwanya Satani pasi petsoka dzenyu. Nyasha dzaIshe wedu Jesu ngadzive nemi. 
Romans16:21 Timoti, anobata neni, anokukwazisai; naRukio, naJasoni, naSosipatirosi, vorudzi rwangu." 
Romans16:22 Ini Teritiosi, anonyora tsamba iyi, ndinokukwazisai muna Ishe." 
Romans16:23 Gayo, akandigamuchira ini nechechi yose, anokukwazisai." 
Romans16:24 Erasitosi, muchengeti wemari yeguta, anokukwazisai, naKwaritosiwo, hama." 
Romans16:25 Zvino iye, anogona kukusimbisai, sezvinoreva Vhangeri yangu, nokuparidzwa kwaJesu Kristu, nokuzarurwa kwezvakavanzika, zvisina kurehwa nguva dzisingaperi," 
Romans16:26 asi zvino zvinoratidzwa nokuziviswa kumarudzi ose, naMagwaro avaporofita, sezvakarayirwa naMwari asingaperi, kuti vateerere nokutenda;" 
Romans16:27 iye Mwari wakachenjera oga, ngaave nokubwinya naJesu Kristu nokusingaperi. Ameni." 
1Corinthians1:1 Pauro, akadanwa nokuda kwaMwari, kuti ave mupostori waKristu Jesu, naSositene, hama yedu," 
1Corinthians1:2 kuchechi yaMwari iri muKorinde, kuna vakaitwa vatsvene muna Kristu Jesu, vakadanwa kuti vave vatsvene pamwechete navose vanodana pose pose zita raJesu Kristu Ishe wedu, wavo nowedu." 
1Corinthians1:3 Nyasha ngadzive nemi, norugare runobva kuna Mwari, Baba vedu, naIshe Jesu Kristu." 
1Corinthians1:4 Ndinogara ndichivonga Mwari nguva dzose nokuda kwenyu, pamusoro penyasha dzaMwari dzamakapiwa muna Kristu Jesu;" 
1Corinthians1:5 kuti makapfumiswa pazvose maari, pakutaura kwose, napakuziva kwose;" 
1Corinthians1:6 nokudaro uchapupu hwaKristu hwakasimbiswa mamuri; 
1Corinthians1:7 kuti hamushayiwi chipo chimwe; muchimirira kuratidzwa kwaIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu;" 
1Corinthians1:8 achakusimbisai kusvikira pakuguma, muve vasingapomerwi mhosva pazuva raIshe Jesu Kristu." 
1Corinthians1:9 Mwari ndiye akatendeka, wamakadanwa naye kuyanana noMwanakomana wake, Jesu Kristu, Ishe wedu." 
1Corinthians1:10 Zvino ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri, hama dzangu, nezita raIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu, kuti imi mose mutaure chinhu chimwe, kuti pakati penyu kurege kuva nokupesana; asi kuti musanganiswe zvakanaka pamurangariro mumwe nokufunga kumwe." 
1Corinthians1:11 Nokuti ndakaudzwa pamusoro penyu, hama dzangu, navarwi vokwaKirowe, kuti kune gakava pakati penyu." 
1Corinthians1:12 Zvandinoreva ndizvokuti, mumwe nomumwe wenyu anoti, “Ini ndiri waPauro,” “Ini waAporo,” “Ini waKefasi,” “Ini waKristu.”" 
1Corinthians1:13 Ko Kristu akaparadzaniswa here? Ko Pauro akaroverwa pamuchinjikwa nokuda kwenyu here? Ko makabhabhatidzwa muzita raPauro here? 
1Corinthians1:14 Ndinovonga Mwari, kuti handina kubhabhatidza mumwe wenyu, asi Kirisipo naGayo;" 
1Corinthians1:15 kuti kurege kuva nomunhu angati, makabhabhatidzwa muzita rangu." 
1Corinthians1:16 Ndakabhabhatidzawo veimba yaSitefana; asi vamwe, handizivi kana ndakabhabhatidza mumwe." 
1Corinthians1:17 Nokuti Kristu haana kundituma kubhabhatidza, asi kuti ndiparidze Vhangeri; ndisingaiti nenjere dzamashoko, kuti muchinjikwa waKristu urege kukoneswa." 
1Corinthians1:18 Nokuti shoko romuchinjikwa upenzi kuna vanoparadzwa; asi kwatiri, isu tinoponeswa, isimba raMwari." 
1Corinthians1:19 Nokuti kwakanyorwa kuchinzi, “Ndichaparadza uchenjeri hwavakachenjera, Ndichakonesa kuziva kwavanoziva.”" 
1Corinthians1:20 Akachenjera aripiko? Munyori aripiko? Muiti wenharo wenyika ino aripiko? Mwari haana kuita uchenjeri hwenyika huve upenzi here? 
1Corinthians1:21 Nokuti nouchenjeri hwaMwari, nyika nouchenjeri hwayo zvaisina kuziva Mwari, Mwari akafadzwa nazvo kuti vanotenda avaponese noupenzi hwokuparidza." 
1Corinthians1:22 Nokuti vaJudha vanokumbira zviratidzo, navaGiriki vanotsvaka uchenjeri;" 
1Corinthians1:23 asi isu tinoparidza Kristu, akaroverwa pamuchinjikwa, chigumbuso kuVaJudha, noupenzi kuvahedheni;" 
1Corinthians1:24 asi kuna vakadanwa, vaJudha navaGiriki, Kristu isimba raMwari, nouchenjeri hwaMwari." 
1Corinthians1:25 Nokuti upenzi hwaMwari hunopfuura vanhu nouchenjeri; noutera hwaMwari hunopfuura vanhu pasimba. 
1Corinthians1:26 Nokuti tarirai kudanwa kwenyu, hama dzangu, kuti havazi vazhinji vakachenjera panyama vakadanwa; havazi vazhinji vane simba, havazi vazhinji vanokudzwa;" 
1Corinthians1:27 asi Mwari akatsaura zvinhu zvisina simba zvenyika, kuti anyadzise izvo zvine simba;" 
1Corinthians1:28 Mwari akatsaura zvinhu zvinozvidzwa zvenyika, nezvinoshorwa, nezvinhu zvisipo, kuti ashayise zviripo simba razvo," 
1Corinthians1:29 kuti kurege kuva nomunhu angazvikudza pamberi paMwari. 
1Corinthians1:30 Asi naye muri muna Kristu Jesu, iye akatiitirwa isu uchenjeri hunobva kuna Mwari, nokururama, noutsvene, norudzikinuro." 
1Corinthians1:31 Kuti anozvirumbidza, ngaazvirumbidze muna Ishe, sezvazvakanyorwa." 
1Corinthians2:1 Zvino ini, hama dzangu, pakuuya kwangu kwamuri, handina kuuya ndichikuparidzirai uchapupu hwaMwari nokunaka kwamashoko, kana kwouchenjeri." 
1Corinthians2:2 Nokuti ndakati, handingazivi chinhu pakati penyu, asi Jesu Kristu iye akaroverwa pamuchinjikwa." 
1Corinthians2:3 Ndakanga ndiri pakati penyu noutera, nokutya, nokudedera kukuru," 
1Corinthians2:4 neshoko rangu nokuparidza kwangu hazvizaiva namashoko okugombedzera ouchenjeri; asi nokuratidza kwoMweya nokwesimba; 
1Corinthians2:5 kuti kutenda kwenyu kurege kuva muuchenjeri hwavanhu, asi musimba raMwari." 
1Corinthians2:6 Zvino tinotaura uchenjeri pakati pavakakura; asi uchenjeri husati huri hwenyika ino, kana hwavabati venyika ino vanoshayiswa simba." 
1Corinthians2:7 Asi tinotaura uchenjeri hwaMwari hwakavanzika, hwakafukidzwa, hwakatemerwa kubwinya kwedu naMwari, nyika isati yavapo;" 
1Corinthians2:8 husina kuzikanwa nomumwe wavabati venyika ino; nokuti dai vaihuziva, vangadai vaisarovera Ishe wokubwinya pamuchinjikwa." 
1Corinthians2:9 Asi sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Izvo zvisina kuonekwa neziso, kana kunzwika nenzeve, Nezvisina kupinda mumwoyo womunhu, Ndizvo Mwari zvaakagadzirira vanomuda.”" 
1Corinthians2:10 Nokuti Mwari akazviratidza izvo kwatiri isu naMweya; nokuti Mweya anonzvera zvose, nezvakadzika zvaMwari." 
1Corinthians2:11 Nokuti munhu ndoupiko anoziva zvomunhu, asi mweya womunhu uri maari? Saizvozvo hukuna munhu anoziva zvaMwari, asi Mweya waMwari." 
1Corinthians2:12 Zvino isu hatina kugamuchira mweya wenyika, asi Mweya unobva kuna Mwari; kuti tizive izvo zvatakangopiwa hedu naMwari." 
1Corinthians2:13 Ndizvo zvatinotaurawo, tisingatauri namashoko atinodzidziswa nouchenjeri hwomunhu, asi anodzidziswa naMweya; tichidudzira zvinhu zvoMweya kuvanhu voMweya." 
1Corinthians2:14 Zvino munhu sezvaakaberekwa haagamuchiri zvinhu zvoMweya waMwari; nokuti upenzi kwaari; haazvinzwisisi, nokuti zvinonzwisiswa naMweya." 
1Corinthians2:15 Asi ari woMweya anonzwisisa zvose, asi iye amene haanzwisiswi nomunhu." 
1Corinthians2:16 Nokuti, “Ndianiko akaziva murangariro waIshe, kuti amudzidzise?” Asi isu tinomurangariro waKristu." 
1Corinthians3:1 Ini, hama dzangu, ndakanga ndisingagoni kutaura nemi sokuna voMweya, asi sokuna venyama, sokuna vacheche muna Kristu." 
1Corinthians3:2 Ndakakupai mukaka munwe, handina kukupai zvokudya; nokuti makanga musingagoni kudya, nazvino hamugoni." 
1Corinthians3:3 Nokuti muchiri venyama; nokuti zvapachine godo pakati penyu, negakava, ko hamuzi venyama, muchifamba nomutoo wavanhu here?" 
1Corinthians3:4 Nokuti kana mumwe achiti, “Ini ndiri waPauro;” mumwe, “Ini ndiri waAporo;” ko hamuzi vanhu here?" 
1Corinthians3:5 Zvino Aporo Chiiko? Pauro Chiiko? Vashumiri vamakatenda navo, mumwe nomumwe sezvaakapiwa naIshe." 
1Corinthians3:6 Ini ndakasima, Aporo akadiridza; asi Mwari akameresa." 
1Corinthians3:7 Naizvozvo anosima haazi chinhu, kana anodiridza; asi Mwari anomeresa." 
1Corinthians3:8 Zvino anosima noanodiridza ndavamwe; asi mumwe nomumwe achapiwa mubairo wake, sezvaakabata basa." 
1Corinthians3:9 Nokuti tiri vabati pamwechete naMwari; muri munda waMwari, muri imba yaMwari." 
1Corinthians3:10 Nenyasha dzaMwari dzandakapiwa, ndakaronga nheyo somuvaki akachenjera; mumwe anovaka pamusoro padzo. Zvino mumwe nomumwe ngaachenjere kuti anovaka sei pamusoro padzo." 
1Corinthians3:11 Nokuti hakuna mumwe angaronga dzimwe nheyo, asi idzo dzakarongwa kare, ndiye Jesu Kristu." 
1Corinthians3:12 Zvino kana munhu achivaka pamusoro penheyo idzi, ndarama, kana sirivha, kana mabwe anokosha, kana matanda, kana uswa, kana mashanga;" 
1Corinthians3:13 basa romumwe nomumwe richaonekwa; nokuti zuva iro richazvibudisa pachena, nokuti richaratidzwa nomoto; moto uchaedza basa romumwe nomumwe kuti rakadini." 
1Corinthians3:14 Kana basa romunhu raakavaka pamusoro padzo, richigara, achapiwa mubairo." 
1Corinthians3:15 Kana basa romunhu rikapiswa, ucharasikirwa, asi iye amene achaponeswa, asi soakabuda pamoto." 
1Corinthians3:16 Ko hamuzivi kuti muri temberi yaMwari, uye kuti Mweya waMwari anogara mukati menyu here?" 
1Corinthians3:17 Kana munhu achitadzira temberi yaMwari, Mwari achamuparadza; nokuti temberi yaMwari itsvene, ndimi iyo." 
1Corinthians3:18 Kurege kuva nomunhu anozvinyengera. Kana munhu achiti ndakachenjera pakati penyu panyika ino, ngaave benzi, kuti ave akachenjera." 
1Corinthians3:19 Nokuti uchenjeri hwenyika ino upenzi kuna Mwari. Nokuti kwakanyorwa kuchinzi, “Anobata vakachenjera pamano avo.”" 
1Corinthians3:20 Uyezve, “Ishe anoziva ndangariro dzavakachenjera, kuti hadzina maturo.”" 
1Corinthians3:21 Naizvozvo ngakurege kuva nomunhu anovimba navanhu. Nokuti zvinhu zvose dzezvenyu; 
1Corinthians3:22 kana Pauro, kana Aporo, kana Kefasi, kana nyika, kana upenyu, kana rufu, kana zvazvino, kana zvinouya; zvose ndezvenyu;" 
1Corinthians3:23 imi muri vaKristu; naKristu ndowaMwari. 
1Corinthians4:1 Munhu upi noupi ngaatirangarire saizvozvo kuti tiri varanda vaKristu, vachengeti vezvakavanzika zvaMwari." 
1Corinthians4:2 Zvino, pazvinhu izvi, pavatariri panotsvakwa, kuti munhu awanikwe akatendeka." 
1Corinthians4:3 Zvino chinhu chiduku–duku kwandiri, kuti nditongwe nemi, kana nokutonga kwomunhu; handizvitongi ini ndimene." 
1Corinthians4:4 Nokuti handizivi mhosva yandinayo; asi handiruramiswi naizvozvo; asi anonditonga ndiye Ishe. 
1Corinthians4:5 Saka regai kutonga chinhu nguva isati yasvika, kusvikira Ishe auya, iye achabudisa pachena zvinhu zvakavanzika zverima, nokuratidza mifungo yomwoyo; ipapo munhu mumwe nomumwe acharumbidzwa naMwari." 
1Corinthians4:6 Zvino, hama dzangu, zvinhu izvi ndakanyora ndichizvifananidzira ini naAporo, nokuda kwenyu; kuti mudzidze kwatiri kusapfuura izvo zvakanyorwa, kuti, “Mumwe arege kuzvikudza, achitsaura mumwe kuno mumwe.”" 
1Corinthians4:7 Nokuti ndianiko akakutsaura iwe? Chiiko chaunacho chausina kupiwa? Zvino kana wakapiwa, unozvikudzireiko sousina kupiwa?" 
1Corinthians4:8 Matoguta, matopfuma, mabata ushe kunze kwedu; dai maibata ushe hwenyu, kuti isu tibatewo pamwechete nemi." 
1Corinthians4:9 Nokuti ndinoti Mwari akatigadza isu vapostori pakupedzisira, savanhu vakatongerwa rufu; nokuti takaitwa chinhu chinoshamisa nyika, navatumwa, navanhu." 
1Corinthians4:10 Isu tiri mapenzi nokuda kwaKristu, asi imi makachenjera muna Kristu; isu tinoshayiwa simba, asi imi mune simba; imi munokudzwa, asi isu tinozvidzwa." 
1Corinthians4:11 Kusvikira nguva ino isu tine nzara, tine nyota, hatina chatingafuka, tinorohwa netsiva, hatina nzvimbo kwayo yokugara;" 
1Corinthians4:12 tinotambudzika, tichibata namaoko edu; kana tichitukwa, tinoropafadza, kana tichitambudzwa, tinotsunga mwoyo;" 
1Corinthians4:13 kana tichipomerwa mhosva, tinovarayidza; takaitwa setsvina yenyika, marara avose kusvikira zvino." 
1Corinthians4:14 Handikunyoreri zvinhu izvi, kuti ndikunyadzisei, asi kuti ndikurayirei savana vangu vanodikanwa." 
1Corinthians4:15 Nokuti kunyangwe maiva navadzidzisi vane zviuru zvine gumi muna Kristu, hamuna madzibaba mazhinji; nokuti muna Jesu Kristu ini ndakakuberekai neVhangeri." 
1Corinthians4:16 Naizvozvo ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri, kuti muve vateveri vangu." 
1Corinthians4:17 Nemhaka iyi ndakatuma Timoti kwamuri, mwana wangu anodikanwa, akatendeka muna Ishe; iye achakuyeuchidzai mitoro yangu iri muna Kristu Jesu, sezvandinodzidzisa kwose pachechi dzose." 
1Corinthians4:18 Zvino vamwe vanozvikudza, vachiti ndinenge handiuyi kwamuri." 
1Corinthians4:19 Ndichakurumidza kuuya kwamuri, kana Ishe achida; handingazivi shoko raivavo vanozvikudza, asi simba ravo." 
1Corinthians4:20 Nokuti ushe hwaMwari hahuzi pamashoko, asi pasimba." 
1Corinthians4:21 Munotsvakeiko? Ndiuye kwamuri neshamu, kana norudo nomweya wounyoro here?" 
1Corinthians5:1 Vanhu vose vanoti upombwe huripo pakati penyu, upombwe hwakadaro husingazikanwi kunyangwe pakati pavahedheni, hwokuti mumwe anogara nomukadzi wababa vake." 
1Corinthians5:2 Munozvikudza, hazvizaiva nani here kana makachema, kuti uyo akabata basa iri abviswe pakati penyu?" 
1Corinthians5:3 Nokuti ini, zvirokwazvo, kunyangwe ndisipo nomuviri, asi ndiripo hangu nomweya, ndatotongesa uyo akaita chinhu ichi, sendinenge ndiripo," 
1Corinthians5:4 nemi, makaungana pamwechete nomweya wangu nezita raIshe Jesu Kristu, nesimba raIshe wedu Jesu," 
1Corinthians5:5 kuti munhu akadai aiswe kuna Satani, nyama iparadzwe, kuti mweya uponeswe pazuva raIshe." 
1Corinthians5:6 Kuzvirumbidza kwenyu hakuna kunaka. Ko hamuzivi kuti mbiriso shoma inovirisa bundu rose here? 
1Corinthians5:7 Bvisai mbiriso yekare, kuti muve bundu idzva, sezvamusina kuviriswa. Nokuti Pasika yedu, yakatibayirwa, ndiKristu;" 
1Corinthians5:8 saka ngatiite mutambo, tisingaiti nembiriso yekare, kana nembiriso yokushata nokuipa; asi nechingwa chisina kuviriswa chokururama nezvokwadi." 
1Corinthians5:9 Ndakakunyorerai netsamba yangu, kuti murege kufambidzana nemhombwe;" 
1Corinthians5:10 handiti nemhombwe dzose dzenyika ino, kana vanoruchiva, kana makororo, kana vanonamata zvifananidzo, nokuti kana zvakadaro maifanira kubva panyika." 
1Corinthians5:11 Asi zvino ndinokunyorerai, kuti murege kufambidzana nomunhu anoidzwa hama, kana ari mhombwe, kana anoruchiva, kana anonamata zvifananidzo, kana mutuki, kana anosinwa doro, kana gororo; musadya nowakadai." 
1Corinthians5:12 Nokuti ini ndichatongereiko vari kunze? Ko imi hamutongi vari pakati penyu here? 
1Corinthians5:13 Asi avo vari kunze. Mwari anovatonga. Bvisai pakati penyu munhu uyo wakaipa. 
1Corinthians6:1 Ko kana mumwe wenyu ane mhosva nomumwe, angatsunga kumukwirira kuna vasakarurama, akasamukwirira kuna vatsvene here?" 
1Corinthians6:2 Hamuzivi here kuti vatsvene vachatonga nyika? Zvino kana nyika ichitongwa nemi, ko imi hamufaniri kutonga mhosva duku–duku here?" 
1Corinthians6:3 Hamuzivi here kuti tichatonga vatumwa? Zvikuru sei izvo zvoupenyu huno! 
1Corinthians6:4 Zvino kana mune mhosva dzoupenyu huno dzinofanira kutongwa, munogadza seiko avo vanozvidzwa pachechi, kuti ivo vatonge?" 
1Corinthians6:5 Ndinodaro kuti munyadziswe. Ko hakuna akachenjera pakati penyu angagona kutonga pakati pehama nehama yake here? 
1Corinthians6:6 Asi hama inokwirira hama, achizviita pamberi pavasingatendi here?" 
1Corinthians6:7 Zvino matova nemhosva kwazvo pakati penyu, zvamunokwirirana. Munoregereiko kutenda kuitirwa zvisakarurama? Munoregereiko kutenda kubirwa?" 
1Corinthians6:8 Asi imi munoita zvisakarurama, munonyengera, muchizviitira hama." 
1Corinthians6:9 Ko hamuzivi kuti vasakarurama havangagari nhaka youshe hwaMwari here? Musarasika; nokuti mhombwe, kana vanonamata zvifananidzo, kana vanofeva, kana vakapata, kana vanoita zvakaipa navarume," 
1Corinthians6:10 kana mbavha, kana vanoruchiva, kana vanosinwa doro, kana vatuki, kana makororo, havangagari nhaka youshe hwaMwari." 
1Corinthians6:11 Vamwe venyu vakanga vakadaro; asi makashambidzwa, asi makaitwa vatsvene, asi makaruramiswa nezita raIshe Jesu Kristu, noMweya waMwari wedu." 
1Corinthians6:12 Ndakatenderwa zvinhu zvose; asi zvinhu zvose hazvindibatsiri. Ndakatenderwa zvinhu zvose, asi handidi kukundwa nechinhu chimwe." 
1Corinthians6:13 Zvokudya ndezvedumbu, nedumbu nderezvokudya; asi Mwari achaparadza iro naizvo, zvose. Asi muviri hauzi woupombwe, asi ndowaIshe; naIshe ndowomuviri;" 
1Corinthians6:14 Mwari akamutsa Ishe, uye achatimutsa isu nesimba rake." 
1Corinthians6:15 Hamuzivi kuti miviri yenyu mitezo yaKristu here? Zvino ndobvisa mitezo yaKristu, ndiite mitezo yemhombwe here? Haisva!" 
1Corinthians6:16 Hamuzivi kuti akasanganiswa nemhombwe wava muviri mumwe naye here? Nokuti iye anoti, “Ava vaviri vachava nyama imwe.”" 
1Corinthians6:17 Asi akasanganiswa naIshe, wava mweya mumwe naye." 
1Corinthians6:18 Tizai upombwe. Zvivi zvose, zvinoitwa nomunhu, zviri kunze kwomuviri; asi anoita upombwe, anotadzira muviri wake." 
1Corinthians6:19 Hamuzivi here kuti muviri wenyu itemberi yaMweya Mutsvene, ari mukati menyu, wamakapiwa naMwari? Hamuzi venyu;" 
1Corinthians6:20 nokuti makatengwa nomutengo; naizvozvo kudzai Mwari mumuviri wenyu. 
1Corinthians7:1 Zvino kana zviri zvamakandinyorera, ndinoti, Zvakanaka kuti munhu arege kuwana mukadzi." 
1Corinthians7:2 Asi nokuda kwoupombwe, murume mumwe nomumwe ngaave nomukadzi wake, nomukadzi mumwe nomumwe ngaave nomurume wake." 
1Corinthians7:3 Murume ngaape mukadzi zvakafanira; nomukadzi adarowo kumurume. 
1Corinthians7:4 Mukadzi haana simba pamusoro pomuviri wake, asi murume; saizvozvowo murume haana simba pamusoro pomuviri wake, asi mukadzi." 
1Corinthians7:5 Musanyimana, asi muchiita nguva duku, mambotenderana, kuti muve nenguva yokunyengetera, ndokusanganazve, kuti Satani arege kukuedzai pakusagona kwenyu kuzvidzora." 
1Corinthians7:6 Asi ndinotaura izvi, ndichikutenderai, ndisingarayiri." 
1Corinthians7:7 Nokuti ndinoda kuti vanhu vose vave seni. Asi munhu mumwe nomumwe ane chipiwa chake, chinobva kuna Mwari, mumwe chorudzi urwu, mumwe chorumwe rudzi." 
1Corinthians7:8 Asi ndinoti kuna vasina kuwana, nokuchirikadzi, Zvakanaka kuti vagare seni." 
1Corinthians7:9 Asi kana vasingagoni kuzvidzora, ngavawane; nokuti zviri nani kuti vawane pakutsva." 
1Corinthians7:10 Zvino vakawana ndinovarayira, asi handizini, ndiIshe, kuti mukadzi arege kubva kumurume wake," 
1Corinthians7:11 (kana achibva, ngaagare asingawanikwi, kana ayanane nomurume wake); nomurume ngaarege kuramba mukadzi wake." 
1Corinthians7:12 Zvino kuna vamwe ndinoti ini, haazi Ishe: Kana hama inomukadzi asingatendi, kana iye achida hake kugara naye, ngaarege kumuramba." 
1Corinthians7:13 Nomukadzi ano murume asingatendi, kana iye achida hake kugara naye, ngaarege kumuramba murume wake," 
1Corinthians7:14 nokuti murume asingatendi anoita mutsvene nomukadzi wake, nomukadzi asingatendi anoitwa mutsvene nomurume; kana zvisina kudaro, vana venyu vaiva netsvina; asi zvino vatsvene." 
1Corinthians7:15 Zvino kana asingatendi achienda, ngaaende hake. Hama, kana iri murume kana mukadzi, haisungwi nezvakadaro; asi Mwari akakudanai kuti muve norugare." 
1Corinthians7:16 Nokuti iwe mukadzi unoziva seiko kuti uchaponesa murume wako? Kana iwe murume, unoziva seiko kuti uchaponesa mukadzi wako?" 
1Corinthians7:17 Asi, mumwe nomumwe sezvaakagoverwa naIshe, mumwe nomumwe sezvaakadanwa naMwari ngaafambe saizvozvo. Ndizvo zvandinorayira pachechi dzose." 
1Corinthians7:18 Kana mumwe achinge akadanwa akadzingiswa, ngaarege kuitwa asakadzingiswa; kana mumwe achinge akadanwa asakadzingiswa, ngaarege kudzingiswa." 
1Corinthians7:19 Kudzingiswa hachizi chinhu, nokusadzingiswa hachizi chinhu, asi kuchengeta mirairo yaMwari." 
1Corinthians7:20 Mumwe nomumwe ngaagare pakudanwa kwaakadanwa nako. 
1Corinthians7:21 Wakadanwa uri muranda here? Usazvidya mwoyo; asi kana ungasunungurwa, zviri nani kuti udaro hako." 
1Corinthians7:22 Nokuti akadanwa muna Ishe, ari muranda, wava musunungurwa waIshe; saizvozvowo, akadanwa akasununguka, wava muranda waKristu." 
1Corinthians7:23 Makatengwa nomutengo; regai kuva varanda vavanhu. 
1Corinthians7:24 Hama dzangu, mumwe nomumwe ngaagare pamberi paMwari ipapo paakadanwa napo." 
1Corinthians7:25 Zvino, pamusoro pemhandara, handina murairo waIshe; asi ndinotaura somunhu wakapiwa ngoni naIshe kuti ave akatendeka." 
1Corinthians7:26 Naizvozvo ndinoti kuda kwenhamo ino, zvakanaka kuti munhu agare akadaro." 
1Corinthians7:27 Wakabatanidzwa nomukadzi here? Usatsvaka kusunungurwa. Wakasunungurwa pamukadzi here? Usatsvaka mukadzi. 
1Corinthians7:28 Zvino kana wawana, hauna kutadza; nemhandara kana yawanikwa, haina kutadza. Asi vakadaro vachava nedambudziko panyama; asi ini ndinoda kukutavirirai." 
1Corinthians7:29 Zvino ndinozvitaura izvi, hama dzangu, nokuti nguva ipfupi; kuti kubva zvino vana vakadzi vave savasina;" 
1Corinthians7:30 navanochema vave savasingachemi; navanofara savasingafari; navanotenga savasina chinhu; 
1Corinthians7:31 navanobata nezvenyika, savasingabatisisi nazvo; nokuti mugariro wenyika ino unopfuura." 
1Corinthians7:32 Zvino ndinoda kuti murege kuva nokufunganya. Asina kuwana, anofunga zvaIshe, kuti angafadza Ishe wake sei." 
1Corinthians7:33 Asi akawana, anofunga zvenyika, kuti angafadza mukadzi wake sei." 
1Corinthians7:34 Nomukadzi asina kuwanikwa nemhandara anofunga zvaIshe, kuti ave mutsvene pamuviri napamweya; asi akawanikwa anofunga zvenyika, kuti angafadza murume wake sei." 
1Corinthians7:35 Izvi ndinotaura kuti mubatsirwe imi; ndisingadi kukusungai nomusungo, asi nokuda kwezvakafanira, uye kuti munamatire Ishe, musingakanganiswi." 
1Corinthians7:36 Asi kana mumwe achifunga kuti haaitiri mukunda wake, yava mhandara, zvakafanira, iye zvaatokura kwazvo hake, ngaaite nokuda kwake, haatadzi; ngavawaniswe havo." 
1Corinthians7:37 Asi uyo anomira akasimba pamwoyo pake, asingamanikidzwi nechinhu, asi ane simba pamusoro pokuda kwake, akatema mumwoyo make chinhu ichi, kuti achachengeta mhandara yake, iye anoita zvakanaka." 
1Corinthians7:38 Naizvozvo, anomuwanisa anoita zvakanaka; noasingamuwanisi, anoita zvinopfuura nokunaka." 
1Corinthians7:39 Mukadzi akasungwa nomurairo, murume wake achiri mupenyu; zvino kana murume wake afa, asununguka, kuti awanikwe nowaanoda; asi ngazviitwe muna Ishe." 
1Corinthians7:40 Asi anganyanya kufara kana achigara akadaro, pakufunga kwangu ini; zvino ndinoti neniwo ndinaMweya waMwari." 
1Corinthians8:1 Zvino, pamusoro pezvakabayirwa zvifananidzo, tinoziva kuti tose tinako kuziva. Kuziva kunouyisa kuzvikudza, asi rudo runosimbisa." 
1Corinthians8:2 Kana munhu achiti, “Ndinoziva chinhu,” agere kutongoziva sezvaakafanira kuziva." 
1Corinthians8:3 Asi kana munhu achida Mwari, iye anozikanwa naye." 
1Corinthians8:4 Zvino kana kuri kudya zvinhu zvakabayirwa zvifananidzo, tinoziva kuti chifananidzo hachizi chinhu panyika, uye kuti hakuna mumwe Mwari, asi iye mumwechete." 
1Corinthians8:5 Nokuti kunyangwe varipo vanonzi “Vamwari,” kana kudenga kana panyika; sezvavaripo “Vamwari vazhinji, namadzishe mazhinji;”" 
1Corinthians8:6 asi isu tinongova naMwari mumwe bedzi, ndivo Baba; zvinhu zvose zvinobva kwaari, nesu tiripo nokuda kwake; uye Ishe mumwe, Jesu Kristu; zvinhu zvose zviripo naye, nesu tiripo naye." 
1Corinthians8:7 Asi vose havana kuziva ikoko; nokuti vamwe, vakarovera chifananidzo kusvikira zvino, vanodya vachiti zvakabayirwa zvifananidzo; hana yavo zvaisina simba, inoshatiswa." 
1Corinthians8:8 Zvino zvokudya hazvingatisvitsi kuna Mwari; nokuti kana tisingadyi, hatiipiswi, kana tichidya, hatinatswi." 
1Corinthians8:9 Asi chenjerai, kuti simba renyu iri rirege kuva chigumbuso kuna vasina simba."
