1Corinthians8:10 Nokuti kana mumwe achikuona iwe, unako kuziva, ugere pakudya mutemberi yechifananidzo, ko hana yaiyeye asina simba haingatsungiswi, kuti adye izvo zvakabayirwa zvifananidzo here?" 
1Corinthians8:11 Nokuti nokuziva kwako uyo asina simba anoparadzwa, iri hama yakafirwawo naKristu." 
1Corinthians8:12 Zvino kana muchitadzira hama saizvozvo, muchirwadzisa hana yavo isina simba munotadzira Kristu." 
1Corinthians8:13 Saka kana zvokudya zvichigumbusa hama yangu, handingatongodyi nyama nokusingaperi, kuti ndirege kugumbusa hama yangu." 
1Corinthians9:1 Handizi wakasununguka here? Handizi mupostori here? Handina kuona Jesu, Ishe wedu here? Imi hamuzi basa rangu muna Ishe here?" 
1Corinthians9:2 Kana ndisati ndiri mupostori kuna vamwe, kunyangwe zvakadaro zvirokwazvo ndiri mupostori kwamuri hangu; nokuti imi muri chisimbiso chohupostori hwangu muna Ishe." 
1Corinthians9:3 Kuzvidavirira kwangu kuna ivo vanonditonga ndikoku: 
1Corinthians9:4 Hatina simba rokudya nokunwa here? 
1Corinthians9:5 Hatina simba rokufamba nomukadzi iri hama, savamwe vapostori navanun'una vaIshe, naKefasi here?" 
1Corinthians9:6 Ko ini ndoga naBhanabhasi hatina simba rokurega kubata basa here? 
1Corinthians9:7 Ndianiko angandorwa achizviripira mubairo? Ndianiko anorima munda wemizambiringa, akasadya zvibereko zvawo? Ndianiko anofudza boka, akasadya mukaka weboka?" 
1Corinthians9:8 Izvi ndinozvitaura nokutaura kwavanhu here? Ko murairo haurevi saizvozvowo here? 
1Corinthians9:9 Nokuti pamurairo waMosesi pakanyorwa, pachiti, “Usasunga muromo wenzombe inopura zviyo.” Ko Mwari ane hanya nenzombe here?" 
1Corinthians9:10 Kana anoreva saizvozvo nokuda kwedu kwoga here? Zvirokwazvo, zvakanyorwa nokuda kwedu, nokuti anorima anofanira kurima netariro; noanopura, achitarira kuti uchagoverwawo." 
1Corinthians9:11 Kana isu takakudyarirai zvinhu zvomweya, chingava chinhu chikuru here kana tichicheka zvinhu zvenyu zvenyama?" 
1Corinthians9:12 Kana vamwe vachipiwa simba pamusoro penyu, ko isu hatipiwi iro zvikuru here? Asi hatina kuzvibatira nesimba iro; asi tinotambudzika pazvose, kuti tirege kudzivisa Vhangeri yaKristu." 
1Corinthians9:13 Hamuzivi here kuti vanoshumira pazvinhu zvitsvene, vanodya zvetemberi? Uye kuti vanobata basa paatari, vanogovana neatari here?" 
1Corinthians9:14 Saizvozvowo Ishe wakarayira kuti vanoparidza Vhangeri, vararame neVhangeri." 
1Corinthians9:15 Asi ini handina kuzvibatira nechimwe chezvinhu izvo. Handinyori izvi kuti ndiitirwe saizvozvo ini; nokuti zviri nani kuti ndife, pakuti mumwe akonese icho chandinozvirumbidza nacho." 
1Corinthians9:16 Nokuti kana ndichiparidza Vhangeri, handina chandingazvirumbidza nacho, nokuti ndinorovererwa; ndine nhamo, kana ndisingaparidzi Vhangeri." 
1Corinthians9:17 Nokuti kana ndichizviita ndichida ini, ndino mubairo; asi kana ndichizviita ndisingadi, ndakapiwa hangu utariri." 
1Corinthians9:18 Zvino mubairo wangu ndoweiko? Ndiwo, kuti kana ndichiparidza Vhangeri, ndivigire vanhu Vhangeri vasingaripi, kuti ndirege kuzvibatira pandaigona napo nesimba randinaro reVhangeri." 
1Corinthians9:19 Nokuti kunyangwe ndakasununguka kuna vose, ndakazviita muranda wavose, kuti ndiwane vazhinji kwazvo." 
1Corinthians9:20 KuVaJudha ndakava somuJudha, kuti ndiwane vaJudha; kuna vari pasi pomurairo, kunyangwe ndisati ndiri pasi pomurairo hangu, kuti ndiwane vari pasi pomurairo;" 
1Corinthians9:21 kuna vasina murairo, ndakava somunhu asina murairo, kunyangwe ndisati ndiri munhu asina murairo waMwari, asi pasi pomurairo waKristu, kuti ndiwane vasina murairo." 
1Corinthians9:22 Kuna vasina simba ndakava asina simba, kuti ndiwane vasina simba; ndakava zvose kuvanhu vose, kuti ndiponese vamwe nemitoo yose." 
1Corinthians9:23 Zvinhu zvose ndinozviita nokuda kweVhangeri, kuti ndigoverwe iyo pamwechete navamwe." 
1Corinthians9:24 Hamuzivi here kuti avo vanoita nhangemutange, vanomhanya vose, asi mumwechete anopiwa mubairo? Mhanyai saizvozvo, kuti muuwane." 
1Corinthians9:25 Mumwe nomumwe, anoshingaira pakutamba, anozvidzora pazvose. Zvino ivo vanozviita kuti vawane korona inoora, asi isu kuti tiwane isingaori." 
1Corinthians9:26 Zvino ini handimhanyi somunhu asingazivi; handirwi somunhu anorova mhepo; 
1Corinthians9:27 asi ndinorwadzisa muviri wangu, ndichiuita muranda; kuti zvimwe ini, ndamboparidzira vamwe, ndirege kuva akaraswa ndimene." 
1Corinthians10:1 Nokuti handidi, hama dzangu, kuti murege kuziva kuti madzibaba edu ose akanga ari pasi pegore, uye kuti vose vakayambuka gungwa;" 
1Corinthians10:2 vose vakabhabhatidzwa muna Mosesi mugore nomugungwa; 
1Corinthians10:3 vose vakadya zvokudya zvimwe zvomweya; 
1Corinthians10:4 vose vakanwa zvokunwa zvimwe zvomweya; nokuti vakanwa padombo romweya rakavatevera; dombo iro rakanga riri Kristu. 
1Corinthians10:5 Asi Mwari haana kufadzwa navazhinji vavo; nokuti vakaparadzwa murenje. 
1Corinthians10:6 Zvino, zvinhu izvi zvakanga zviri zviratidzo kwatiri, kuti isu tirege kuchiva zvakaipa, sezvavakachiva ivo." 
1Corinthians10:7 Imi regai kunamata zvifananidzo, savamwe vavo; sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Vanhu vakagara pasi pakudya nokunwa, vakamuka kuti vatambe.”" 
1Corinthians10:8 Zvino ngatirege kuita upombwe, savamwe vavo vakaita upombwe, vakafa nezuva rimwe vane zviuru zvina makumi maviri nezvitatu." 
1Corinthians10:9 Ngatirege kuedza Ishe, savamwe vavo vakamuedza, vakaparadzwa nenyoka." 
1Corinthians10:10 Murege kugunun'una savamwe vavo vakagun'una, vakaparadzwa nomuparadzi." 
1Corinthians10:11 Zvino, izvi zvakavawira, kuti vave zviratidzo; zvakanyorwa kuti tinyeverwe isu, tikasvikirwa nokuguma kwenyika." 
1Corinthians10:12 Naizvozvo, anoti ndinomira, ngaachenjere kuti arege kuwa." 
1Corinthians10:13 Hakuna muedzo wakakubatai imi, asi wavanhu vose; asi Mwari, akatendeka, haangatenderi kuti muedzwe kupfuura pamunogona napo; asi pamwechete nomuedzo, iye achakupaiwo nzira yokubuda nayo, muve nesimba rokutsunga." 
1Corinthians10:14 Naizvozvo, vadikanwi vangu, tizai kunamata zvifananidzo." 
1Corinthians10:15 Ndinotaura sokuna vakachenjera; fungai zvandinotaura. 
1Corinthians10:16 Mukombe wokuvonga watinovonga, hakuzi kusangana neropa raKristu here? Chingwa chatinomedura, hakuzi kusangana nomuviri waKristu here?" 
1Corinthians10:17 Zvachiri chingwa chimwechete, isu vazhinji tiri muviri mumwe; nokuti tinogovana tose pachingwa chimwe." 
1Corinthians10:18 Tarirai VaIsiraeri panyama; avo vanodya zvibairo havagovani neatari here? 
1Corinthians10:19 Zvino ndotiiko? Kuti chinobayirwa zvifananidzo chinhu here, kana chifananidzo chinhu here?" 
1Corinthians10:20 Kwete, asi ndinoti izvo zvinobayirwa navahedheni, havazvibayiri Mwari, asi mweya yakaipa; zvino handidi kuti muyanane nemweya yakaipa." 
1Corinthians10:21 Hamunganwiri mumukombe waIshe, nomumukombe wemweya yakaipa; hamungadyiri patafura yaIshe napatafura yemweya yakaipa." 
1Corinthians10:22 Ko tinoda kumutsa godo raIshe here? Tinomukunda nesimba here? 
1Corinthians10:23 “Ndakatenderwa zvinhu zvose; asi zvose hazvindibatsiri.” “Ndakatenderwa zvinhu zvose; asi zvose hazvisimbisi.” 
1Corinthians10:24 Munhu ngaarege kuzvitsvakira zvake, asi zvomumwe." 
1Corinthians10:25 Idyai zvose zvinotengwa panotengeswa nyama, musingabvunzi chinhu nokuda kwehana;" 
1Corinthians10:26 nokuti nyika ndeyaIshe nokuzara kwayo. 
1Corinthians10:27 Kana mumwe wavasingatendi akakukokerai kuzodya, kana mukada kuenda, idyai zvose zvinoiswa pamberi penyu, musingabvunzi chinhu nokuda kwehana." 
1Corinthians10:28 Asi kana mumwe akati kwamuri, “Ichi chakabayirwa zvifananidzo,” regai kudya nokuda kwaiye akakuratidzai, uye nokuda kwehana;" 
1Corinthians10:29 handirevi hana yako, asi yomumwe; nokuti kusununguka kwangu kunotongerweiko nehana yomumwe?" 
1Corinthians10:30 Kana ini ndichidya ndichivonga, ndingagotukirweiko nokuda kwechinhu chandinovonga pamusoro pacho?" 
1Corinthians10:31 Naizvozvo, kana muchidya, kana muchinwa, kana muchiita chinhu chipi nechipi, itai zvose kuti Mwari akudzwe." 
1Corinthians10:32 Regai kugumbusa kana vaJudha, kana vaGiriki, kana chechi yaMwari." 
1Corinthians10:33 Seniwo ndinofadza vanhu vose pazvinhu zvose, ndisingatsvaki zvingandibatsira ini, asi zvingabatsira vazhinji, kuti vaponeswe." 
1Corinthians11:1 Ivai vateveri vangu, seni ndiri muteveri waKristu." 
1Corinthians11:2 Zvino, ndinokurumbidzai, nokuti munondirangarira pazvinhu zvose, muchichengeta tsika, sezvandakakupai idzo." 
1Corinthians11:3 Asi ndinoda kuti muzive kuti musoro womumwe nomumwe ndiye Kristu; uye musoro womukadzi ndiye murume; uye musoro waKristu ndiye Mwari. 
1Corinthians11:4 Murume mumwe nomumwe, anonyengetera kana kuporofita musoro wake wakafukidzwa, anoninipisa musoro wake." 
1Corinthians11:5 Asi mukadzi mumwe nomumwe, anonyengetera kana kuporofita musoro wake usina kufukidzwa, anoninipisa musoro wake; nokuti ndizvo zvimwe nokuveurwa." 
1Corinthians11:6 Nokuti kana mukadzi asingafukidzwi, ngaachekerwe vhudzi rakewo; asi kana zvisingafaniri kuti mukadzi achekerwe vhudzi, kana aveurwe, ngaafukidzwe." 
1Corinthians11:7 Nokuti murume haafaniri kufukidza musoro, zvaari mufananidzo nokubwinya kwaMwari; asi mukadzi ndiye kubwinya kwomurume." 
1Corinthians11:8 Nokuti murume haabvi kumukadzi; asi mukadzi anobva kumurume; 
1Corinthians11:9 uye murume haana kusikirwa mukadzi, asi mukadzi akasikirwa murume;" 
1Corinthians11:10 nokuda kwaizvozvo mukadzi anofanira kuva nechiratidzo chesimba pamusoro wake, nokuda kwavatumwa." 
1Corinthians11:11 Kunyangwe zvakadaro muna Ishe mukadzi haazi kunze kwomurume, nomurume haazi kunze kwomukadzi." 
1Corinthians11:12 Nokuti mukadzi seanobva kumurume, nokudarowo murume unoberekwa nomukadzi; asi zvose zvinobva kuna Mwari." 
1Corinthians11:13 Tongai imi mumene: Zvakafanira kuti mukadzi anyengetere kuna Mwari asina kufukidzwa here? 
1Corinthians11:14 Ko hamudzidziswi naiwo musikirwo wavanhu kuti kana murume ane vhudzi refu, anonyadziswa nazvo here?" 
1Corinthians11:15 Asi kana mukadzi ane vhudzi refu, ndiko kubwinya kwake; nokuti akapiwa vhudzi rake chive chifukidzo." 
1Corinthians11:16 Zvino kana mumwe anenge achida kuita gakava, hatina tsika yakadaro isu, kunyangwe Chechi dzaMwari." 
1Corinthians11:17 Zvino kana ndichikuudzai izvi, handikurumbidzii, nokuti hamuunganiri zvinopfuura nokunaka, asi zvakaipa." 
1Corinthians11:18 Nokuti shoko rokutanga, kana muchiungana muchechi, ndinonzwa kuti kupesana kuripo pakati penyu; pamwe ndinotenda kuti ndizvo." 
1Corinthians11:19 Nokuti dzidziso dzakatsauka dzinofanira kuva pakati penyu, kuti avo vakatendeka vaonekwe pakati penyu." 
1Corinthians11:20 Zvino kana muchiungana pamwechete, hakuzi kuti mudye chirariro chaIshe;" 
1Corinthians11:21 nokuti kana modya, mumwe nomumwe anotangira vamwe kudya chirariro chake; mumwe ane nzara, mumwe anodhakwa." 
1Corinthians11:22 Ko hamuna dzimba kwamungadyira nokunwira here? Munozvidza Chechi yaMwari, muchinyadzisa avo vasina chinhu here? Ndichaiteiko kwamuri? Ndingakurumbidzai here? Handingakurumbidzii." 
1Corinthians11:23 Nokuti ini ndakagamuchira kuna Ishe icho chandakakupaiwo, kuti Ishe Jesu nousiku hwaakapandukirwa, akatora chingwa;" 
1Corinthians11:24 akati avonga, akachimedura, akati, “Uyu ndiwo muviri wangu unomedurirwa imi; itai izvi muchindirangarira.”" 
1Corinthians11:25 Saizvozvowo, vakati vapedza kurarira, akatora mukombe, akati, “Mukombe uyu ndiyo sungano itsva muropa rangu; itai izvi, nguva dzose kana muchinwa, muchindirangarira.”" 
1Corinthians11:26 Nokuti nguva dzose, kana muchidya chingwa ichi, kana kunwa mukombe uyu, munoparidza rufu rwaIshe, kusvikira achiuya." 
1Corinthians11:27 Naizvozvo mumwe nomumwe anodya chingwa ichi, kana kunwa mukombe waIshe, nomutoo asina kufanira, achava nemhosva yomuviri neropa raIshe." 
1Corinthians11:28 Zvino munhu ngaazviedze, kuti adye chingwa ichi achidaro, nokunwa mukombe uyu." 
1Corinthians11:29 Nokuti anodya nokunwa, asinganatsi kunzwisisa muviri waIshe, anozvidyira nokuzvinwira kurohwa." 
1Corinthians11:30 Nemaka iyi vazhinji varipo pakati penyu vasina simba, vanorwara; vazhinji vavete." 
1Corinthians11:31 Nokuti dai taizviedza isu timene, hatizairohwa." 
1Corinthians11:32 Zvino kana tichitongwa, tinorangwa naIshe, kuti tirege kutongerwa kuraswa pamwechete nenyika." 
1Corinthians11:33 Naizvozvo, hama dzangu, kana muchiunganira pakudya, miriranai." 
1Corinthians11:34 Kana munhu ane nzara, ngaadye kumusha kwake; kuti murege kuunganira kutongwa. Zvimwe zvakasara ndichazvigadzira kana ndichisvika." 
1Corinthians12:1 Zvino, kana zviri zvipo zvoMweya, hama dzangu, handidi kuti muve vasingazivi." 
1Corinthians12:2 Munoziva kuti panguva yamaiva vahedheni, makanga muchikweverwa kuzvifananidzo, zvisingagoni kutaura, sezvamaitungamirirwa." 
1Corinthians12:3 Saka ndinokuzivisai kuti hakuna munhu anotaura naMweya waMwari, angati, “Jesu ngaatukwe!” Uye, hakuna munhu angati, “Jesu ndiye Ishe, asi naMweya Mutsvene.”" 
1Corinthians12:4 Zvino marudzi mazhinji ezvipo aripo, asi Mweya ndomumwe." 
1Corinthians12:5 Marudzi mazhinji okushumira aripo, asi Ishe mumwe." 
1Corinthians12:6 Marudzi mazhinji amabasa aripo, asi Mwari mumwe, iye anobata zvose muna vose." 
1Corinthians12:7 Asi mumwe nomumwe anopiwa kuratidzwa kwoMweya, kuti vose vabatsirwe." 
1Corinthians12:8 Nokuti mumwe anopiwa naMweya shoko rouchenjeri, mumwe shoko rokuziva naMweya iwoyu;" 
1Corinthians12:9 mumwe, kutenda muMweya iwoyu; mumwe, zvipo zvokuporesa muMweya iwoyu;" 
1Corinthians12:10 mumwe, kuita mabasa esimba; mumwe; kuporofita; mumwe, kuzivisisa mweya; mumwe, marudzi endimi; mumwe, kududzira ndimi;" 
1Corinthians12:11 asi izvi zvose zvinoitwa naMweya iwoyu mumwechete, unogovera mumwe nomumwe sezvaanoda." 
1Corinthians12:12 Nokuti somuviri uri mumwe, une mitezo mizhinji, nemitezo yose yomuviri, kunyangwe iri mizhinji, muviri ndomumwechete; wakadarowo Kristu." 
1Corinthians12:13 Nokuti muMweya mumwe isu tose takabhabhatidzwa mumuviri mumwe; kana tiri vaJudha, kana vaGiriki, kana varanda, kana vakasununguka; isu tose takanwiswa paMweya mumwe." 
1Corinthians12:14 Nokuti muviri hauzi mutezo mumwe, asi mizhinji." 
1Corinthians12:15 Kana rutsoka rukati, “Zvandisati ndiri ruoko, handizi womuviri;” ko haruzi rwomuviri, zvarwadaro here?" 
1Corinthians12:16 Nenzeve kana ikati, “Zvandisati ndiri ziso, handizi womuviri;” ko haizi yomuviri here?" 
1Corinthians12:17 Kana muviri wose raiva ziso, kunzwa kwaivepiko? Kana wose kwaiva kunzwa, kunhuwidza kwaivepiko?" 
1Corinthians12:18 Asi zvino Mwari akaisa mutezo mumwe nomumwe pamuviri sezvaakada. 
1Corinthians12:19 Kana yose waiva mutezo mumwe, muviri waivepiko?" 
1Corinthians12:20 Asi zvino kune mitezo mizhinji, asi muviri mumwe." 
1Corinthians12:21 Ziso haringati kuruoko, “Handikudi,” kana musorowo kutsoka, “Handikudiyi imi.”" 
1Corinthians12:22 Kwete, zvikuru mitezo iyo yomuviri inenge isina simba, ndiyo inodikanwa," 
1Corinthians12:23 nemitezo iyo yomuviri yatinoti haikudzwi, ndiyo yatinokudza kwazvo; nemitezo iyo yedu isina kunaka, ndiyo yova nokunaka kunopfuurisa;" 
1Corinthians12:24 asi mitezo yedu yakanaka, haishaiwi kukudzwa. Asi Mwari akabatanidza muviri wose, akakudza nokupfuurisa mitezo inoshayiwa kunaka;" 
1Corinthians12:25 kuti pamuviri parege kuva nokupesana; asi kuti mitezo ichengetane zvakaenzana. 
1Corinthians12:26 Kana mutezo mumwe uchitambudzika, mitezo yose inotambudzika pamwechete nawo; kana mutezo mumwe uchikudzwa, mitezo yose inofara pamwechete nawo." 
1Corinthians12:27 Zvino, imi muri muviri waKristu, nomumwe nomumwe mitezo yawo." 
1Corinthians12:28 Mwari akaisa vamwe muchechi, pakutanga vapostori, vechipiri vaporofita, vechitatu vadzidzisi, tevere vaiti vamabasa esimba, tevere zvipo zvokuporesa, navabatsiri, navabati, namarudzi mazhinji endimi." 
1Corinthians12:29 Vose vapostori here? Vose vaporofita here? Vose vadzidzisi here? Vose vaiti vamabasa esimba here? 
1Corinthians12:30 Vose vane zvipo zvokuporesa here? Vose vanotaura nendimi here? Vose vanodudzira here? 
1Corinthians12:31 Asi shingairirai zvipo zvikuru. Ndinokuratidzaiwo nzira yakaisvonaka inopfuura dzose. 
1Corinthians13:1 Kunyangwe ndikataura nendimi dzavanhu nedzavatumwa, ndisina rudo, ndava sendarira dzinorira, nedare rinongoti, Ngwerengwere!" 
1Corinthians13:2 Kunyangwe ndine chipo chokuporofita, ndichinzwisisa zvakavanzika zvose, nokuziva kwose; kunyangwe ndinokutenda kwose, kuti ndibvise makomo, ndisina rudo, handizi chinhu." 
1Corinthians13:3 Kunyangwe ndagovera varombo zvose zvandinazvo, kunyangwe ndikaisa muviri wangu kuti ndipiswe, ndisina rudo, handibatsiri chinhu." 
1Corinthians13:4 Rudo runo mwoyo murefu, runo mwoyo munyoro; rudo haruna godo; rudo haruna manyawi haruzvikudzi;" 
1Corinthians13:5 haruiti zvisingafaniri, haruzvitsvakiri zvarwo; harutsamwi, haruna zvishura;" 
1Corinthians13:6 harufariri zvisakarurama, asi runofarira chokwadi;" 
1Corinthians13:7 runofukidza zvose, runotenda zvose, rune tariro pazvose, runotsungirira pazvose." 
1Corinthians13:8 Rudo harutongoperi; zvino kana kuri kuporofita, kuchabviswa; kana dziri ndimi, dzichaguma; kana kuri kuziva, kuchabviswa." 
1Corinthians13:9 Nokuti tinoziva zvisakakwana, tinoporofita zvisakakwana;" 
1Corinthians13:10 asi kana zvakwana zvasvika, izvo zvisakakwana zvichabviswa." 
1Corinthians13:11 Ini ndichiri mwana, ndaitaura somwana, ndaifunga somwana, ndairangarira somwana; zvino zvandava murume, ndabvisa zvinhu zvomwana." 
1Corinthians13:12 Nokuti zvino tinoona pachioni–oni, tisingaoni kwazvo; asi nenguva iyo tichaona neziso zvakatarisana; zvino ndinoziva zvisakakwana, asi nenguva iyo ndichaziva sezvandakazikanwa neniwo." 
1Corinthians13:13 Zvino kutenda, netariro, norudo, zvitatu izvi, ndizvo zvinogara; asi chikuru pakati pazvo ndirwo rudo." 
1Corinthians14:1 Teverai rudo; shingairirai zvipo zvoMweya, asi zvikuru kuti muporofite." 
1Corinthians14:2 Nokuti anotaura norumwe rurimi haatauri kuvanhu, asi kuna Mwari; nokuti hakuna anomunzwa; asi anotaura zvakavanzika muMweya." 
1Corinthians14:3 Asi anoporofita, anotaura kuvanhu, kuti vasimbiswe nokurayirwa, nokunyaradzwa." 
1Corinthians14:4 Anotaura norurimi, anozvisimbisa iye; asi anoporofita, anosimbisa Chechi." 
1Corinthians14:5 Zvino ndinoda kuti imi mose mutaure nendimi, asi zvikuru kuti muporofite; anoporofita mukuru kunoanotaura nendimi, asi kana achidudzira, kuti Chechi isimbiswe." 
1Corinthians14:6 Asi zvino, hama dzangu, kana ndichiuya kwamuri, ndichitaura nendimi, ndingakubatsirai neiko, kana ndisingatauri nokuzarurirwa, kana nokuziva, kana nokuporofita, kana nokudzidzisa?" 
1Corinthians14:7 Kunyangwe zvinhu zvisina upenyu zvinorira kana iri nyere, kana rudimbwa, kana zvisingasiyani pakurira kwazvo, zvingazikanwa seiko chinoridzwa nenyere kana norudimbwa?" 
1Corinthians14:8 Nokuti kana hwamanda isingariri kwazvo, ndianiko angazvigadzira kundorwa?" 
1Corinthians14:9 Zvakadarowo nemi, kana musingatauri mashoko norurimi anonatsozikanwa, zvinotaurwa zvichazikanwa seiko? Nokuti muchangotaura henyu mumhepo." 
1Corinthians14:10 Mazwi anamarudzi mazhinji sei panyika, hakuna chinhu chisina izwi racho." 
1Corinthians14:11 Zvino kana ndisingazivi kuti izwi rinorevei, ini ndichava somunhu worumwe rurimi kune anotaura, noanotaura achava kwandiri somunhu worumwe rurimi." 
1Corinthians14:12 Saizvozvowo imi, zvamunoshingairira zvinhu zvoMweya, tsvakai zvikuru kuti musimbise Chechi." 
1Corinthians14:13 Saka anotaura norumwe rurimi, ngaanyengetere kuti adudzirewo." 
1Corinthians14:14 Nokuti kana ndichinyengetera norumwe rurimi, mweya wangu unonyengetera, asi kufunga kwangu kunoshaiwa zvibereko." 
1Corinthians14:15 Zvino chiiko? Ndichanyengetera nomweya wangu, uye ndichanyengetera nokufunga kwanguo; ndichaimba nomweya wangu, uye ndichaimba nokufunga kwanguo." 
1Corinthians14:16 Kana zvisakadaro, kana iwe uchivonga nomweya, ko uyo agere pachigaro chavasina kudzidza, achati Ameni seiko pakuvonga kwako, zvaasingazivi chaunotaura iwe?" 
1Corinthians14:17 Nokuti iwe unovonga hako zvakanaka, asi mumwe haasimbiswi." 
1Corinthians14:18 Ndinovonga Mwari, kuti ini ndinotaura nendimi zhinji kukunda imi mose;" 
1Corinthians14:19 asi pachechi ndinoda zvikuru kutaura mashoko mashanu nokufunga kwangu, kuti ndidzidzise vamwewo, pakutaura norumwe rurimi mashoko ane zviuru zvine gumi." 
1Corinthians14:20 Hama dzangu, musava vana pakuziva, asi muve vacheche pazvakaipa, asi pakuziva muve vakuru." 
1Corinthians14:21 Pamurairo pakanyorwa, pachiti, “Ndichataura kuvanhu ava, ndichireva navanhu vedzimwe ndimi nemimwe miromo; kunyangwe zvakadaro, havanganditeereri, ndizvo zvinoreva Ishe.”" 
1Corinthians14:22 Saka ndimi hadzizi chiratidzo kuna vanotenda, asi kuna vasingatendi; nokuporofita hakuzi kuna vasingatendi, asi kuna vanotenda." 
1Corinthians14:23 Naizvozvo, kana Chechi yose yaungana, vose vakataura nendimi, vasina kudzidza kana vasina kutenda vakapinda, havati munopenga here?" 
1Corinthians14:24 Asi kana vose vakaporofita, mumwe asingatendi kana asina kudzidza akapinda, achatendiswa navose, achatongwa navose;" 
1Corinthians14:25 zvakavanzika zvomwoyo wake zvinoratidzwa; naizvozvo achawira pasi nechiso chake, achinamata Ishe nokupupura kuti Mwari ari pakati penyu zvirokwazvo." 
1Corinthians14:26 Zvino tichatiiko, hama dzangu? Kana muchiungana, mumwe nomumwe ane pisarema, ane chokudzidzisa, ane chakamuzarurirwa, anorumwe rurimi, ane chokududzira. Ngazviitwe zvose, kuti musimbiswe." 
1Corinthians14:27 Kana mumwe achitaura norurimi, ngazviitwe navaviri, kana varege kupfuura vatatu, vachiravana; nomumwe ngaadudzire." 
1Corinthians14:28 Asi kana pasina anodudzira, ngaanyarare muchechi; ngaazvitaurire iye, nokuna Mwari." 
1Corinthians14:29 Vaporofita ngavataure vaviri, kana vatatu, navamwe ngavatsoropodze." 
1Corinthians14:30 Zvino kana chimwe chinhu chikazarurirwa mumwe agerepo, wokutanga ngaanyarare." 
1Corinthians14:31 Nokuti mungaporofita mose, muchiita mumwe–mumwe, kuti vose vadzidze, vose vanyaradzwe." 
1Corinthians14:32 Mweya yavaporofita inozviisa pasi pavaporofita; 
1Corinthians14:33 nokuti Mwari haazi Mwari wenyonganiso, asi worugare, sapachechi dzose dzavatsvene." 
1Corinthians14:34 Vakadzi ngavanyarare pachechi; nokuti havatenderwi kutaura; asi ngavazviise pasi, sezvinorevawo murairo." 
1Corinthians14:35 Kana vachida kudzidza chinhu, ngavabvunze varume vavo kumusha; nokuti hazvifaniri kuti mukadzi ataure muchechi." 
1Corinthians14:36 Ko shoko raMwari rakabva kwamuri here? Kana rakasvika kwamuri moga here? 
1Corinthians14:37 Kana munhu achiti, ndiri muporofita, kana ndiri womweya, ngaatende kuti izvo zvandinokunyorerai, murairo waIshe." 
1Corinthians14:38 Asi kana munhu asingazivi, ngaave asingazivi hake." 
1Corinthians14:39 Saka, hama dzangu, shingairirai kuporofita, musingadzivisi mumwe kutaura nendimi." 
1Corinthians14:40 Asi zvinhu zvose ngazviitwe nomutoo wakafanira zvine mirairo yazvo. 
1Corinthians15:1 Zvino, hama dzangu, ndinokuzivisai Vhangeri yandakakuparidzirai, iyo yamakagamuchirawo, neyamunomirawo mairi;" 
1Corinthians15:2 iyo yamunoponeswawo nayo, kana muchiibatisa nomutoo wandakaiparidza kwamuri, kana musina kutenda pasina." 
1Corinthians15:3 Nokuti pakutanga ndakakupai izvo zvandakagamuchirawo, kuti Kristu akafira zvivi zvedu, sezvakanyorwa muMagwaro;" 
1Corinthians15:4 uye kuti akavigwa, akamutswa nezuva retatu, sezvakanyorwa muMagwaro;" 
1Corinthians15:5 akazviratidza kuna Kefasi, ipapo kuna vane gumi navaviri;" 
1Corinthians15:6 ipapo akazviratidza kuhama dzinopfuura mazana mashanu kamwe vazhinji vavo vapenyu kusvikira zvino, asi vamwe vakavata." 
1Corinthians15:7 Ipapo akazviratidza kuna Jakobho; ipapo kuna vapostori vose; 
1Corinthians15:8 pakupedzisira akazviratidza kwandiriwo, sokunoakazvarwa nguva isati yasvika." 
1Corinthians15:9 Nokuti ini ndiri muduku kuvapostori vose, handifaniri kuti ndinzi muapostora, nokuti ndakatambudza Chechi yaMwari." 
1Corinthians15:10 Asi nenyasha dzaMwari ndiri munhu akadai zvino; nenyasha dzake kwandiri hadzina kuva pasina; asi ndakashanda zvikuru kupfuura vose; handizini, asi inyasha dzaMwari dzaiva neni." 
1Corinthians15:11 Naizvozvo, kana ndirini, kana vari ivo, tinoparidza kudai, nemi makatenda kudai." 
1Corinthians15:12 Zvino kana Kristu achiparidzwa, kuti akamutswa kuvakafa, vamwe pakati penyu vanoreva seiko, kuti hakuna kumuka kwavakafa?" 
1Corinthians15:13 Zvino, dai pasina kumuka kwavakafa, naKristu angadai asina kumutswawo;" 
1Corinthians15:14 uye, dai Kristu asina kumutswa, kuparidza kwedu kungadai kuchiva pasina, nokutenda kwenyu kungadai kuchiva pasinawo." 
1Corinthians15:15 Nesu taiwanikwa tiri zvapupu zvaMwari zvenhema; nokuti takapupura kuti Mwari akamutsa Kristu, iye waasina kumumutsa, kana zviri izvo kuti vakafa havamutswi." 
1Corinthians15:16 Nokuti kana vakafa vasingamutswi, naKristu haana kumutswawo;" 
1Corinthians15:17 kana Kristu asina kumutswa, kutenda kwenyu hakuna maturo; muchiri muzvivi zvenyu." 
1Corinthians15:18 Zvino naivo vakafa muna Kristu vakarasikawo. 
1Corinthians15:19 Kana tine tariro kuna Kristu muupenyu uhwu bedzi, tinonzwisa urombo kukunda vanhu vose." 
1Corinthians15:20 Asi zvino Kristu akamutswa kuvakafa, akava chibereko chokutanga chavavata." 
1Corinthians15:21 Nokuti rufu zvarwakauya nomunhu, kumuka kwavakafa kwakauya nomunhuwo." 
1Corinthians15:22 Nokuti vose sezvavanofa muna Adhamu, saizvozvowo vose vachararamiswa muna Kristu." 
1Corinthians15:23 Asi mumwe nomumwe padzoro rake: wokutanga ndiye Kristu chibereko chokutanga; tevere, avo vari vaKristu pakuuya kwake." 
1Corinthians15:24 Ipapo kuguma kunosvika, panguva yaachazopa Mwari, Baba, ushe, panguva yaachaparadza kubata kwose, noushe hwose, nesimba." 
1Corinthians15:25 Nokuti anofanira kubata ushe, kusvikira aisa vavengi vake vose pasi petsoka dzake." 
1Corinthians15:26 Muvengi wokupedzisira, achaparadzwa, ndirwo rufu." 
1Corinthians15:27 Nokuti akaisa zvinhu zvose pasi petsoka dzake. Zvino kana achiti, “Zvose zvakaiswa pasi pake, zvinoonekwa pachena kuti iye, akaisa zvose pasi pake, haaiswipo.”" 
1Corinthians15:28 Zvino kana zvose zvaiswa pasi pake, ipapo noMwanakomanawo amene achaiswa pasi paiye akaisa zvose pasi pake, kuti Mwari ave zvose kuna vose." 
1Corinthians15:29 Kana zvisina kudaro, ko avo vanobhabhatidzirwa vakafa, vachagoita seiko? Kana vakafa vasingatongomutswi, vakagobhabhatidzirweiko ivo vakafa?" 
1Corinthians15:30 Nesu tiri panjodzi nguva dzose neiko? 
1Corinthians15:31 Ndinopika, hama dzangu, nokuzvirumbidza kwandinako pamusoro penyu muna Kristu Jesu, Ishe wedu, kuti ndinofa zuva rimwe nerimwe." 
1Corinthians15:32 Kana ndakarwa nezvikara paEfeso somunhu zvaindibatsireiko? Kana vakafa vasingamutswi, ngatidye, ngatinwe, nokuti mangwana tinofa." 
1Corinthians15:33 Musanyengerwa; ushamwari hwakaipa hunoodza tsika dzakanaka. 
1Corinthians15:34 Pengenukai zvakarurama, “Murege kutadza, nokuti vamwe havazivi Mwari; ndinotaura izvi kuti munyadziswe.”" 
1Corinthians15:35 Asi mumwe angati, “Vakafa vanogomutswa seiko? Vachauya nomuviri wakaita sei?”" 
1Corinthians15:36 Iwe benzi, icho chaunodyara hachimeri, kana chisingafi." 
1Corinthians15:37 Chaunodyara, haudyari muviri uchavapo, asi tsanga bedzi, kana yamapfunde, kana yezvimwe;" 
1Corinthians15:38 asi Mwari anoipa muviri paanoda napo, nembeu imwe neimwe muviri wayo." 
1Corinthians15:39 Nyama yose haizi nyama imwe; asi imwe ndeyavanhu, imwe inyama yemhuka, imwe inyama yeshiri, imwe ndeyehove." 
1Corinthians15:40 Kune miviri yokudenga, nemiviri yenyika; asi kubwinya kweyokudenga ndokumwe, nokwenyika ndokumwe." 
1Corinthians15:41 Kubwinya kwezuva ndokumwe, nokubwinya kwomwedzi ndokumwe, nokubwinya kwenyenyedzi ndokumwe; nokuti nyenyedzi imwe haifanani neimwe nyenyedzi pakubwinya." 
1Corinthians15:42 Ndizvo zvakaitawo kumuka kwavakafa. Muviri unodyarwa pakuora; unomutswa pakusaora; 
1Corinthians15:43 unodyarwa pakuzvidzwa, unomutswa pakubwinya; unodyarwa pautera, unomutswa pasimba." 
1Corinthians15:44 Unodyarwa uri muviri wokuberekwa, unomutswa uri muviri womweya. Muviri wokuberekwa uripo, nomuviri womweya uripo." 
1Corinthians15:45 Zvakanyorwawo saizvozvo, zvichinzi, “Munhu wokutanga, Adhamu, akaitwa munhu mupenyu;” Adhamu wokupedzisira akaitwa mweya, unopa upenyu." 
1Corinthians15:46 Asi zvomweya hazvizi zvokutanga, asi zvokuberekwa; tevere zvomweya." 
1Corinthians15:47 Munhu wokutanga ndowenyika, wevhu; munhu wechipiri akabva kudenga." 
1Corinthians15:48 Saiye wevhu, ndizvo zvakaitawo avo vevhu; saiye wokudenga, ndizvo zvakaitawo ivo vokudenga." 
1Corinthians15:49 Uye, sezvatakanga tinomufananidzo womunhu wevhu, tichavawo nomufananidzo waiye wokudenga." 
1Corinthians15:50 Zvino, hama dzangu, ndinoreva ndichiti, nyama neropa hazvingagari nhaka youshe hwaMwari; nokuora hakungagari nhaka yokusaora." 
1Corinthians15:51 Tarirai, ndinokuudzai chakavanzika, Hatingavati tose, asi tichashandurwa tose;" 
1Corinthians15:52 pakarepo, nokubwaira kweziso, nehwamanda yokupedzisira; nokuti hwamanda icharira, ipapo vakafa vachamutswa nokusaora; nesu tichashandurwa;" 
1Corinthians15:53 nokuti ichi chinoora chinofanira kufuka kusafa. 
1Corinthians15:54 Zvino kana ichi chinoora chafuka kusaora, nechichi chinofa chafuka kusafa, ipapo shoko rakanyorwa richaitika, rinoti, “Rufu rwakamedzwa nokukunda.”" 
1Corinthians15:55 “Iwe rufu, kukunda kwako kuripiko? Iwe rufu, rumborera rwako ruripiko?”" 
1Corinthians15:56 Rumborera rworufu ndizvo zvivi; nesimba rezvivi ndiwo murairo. 
1Corinthians15:57 Zvino Mwari ngaavongwe, uyo anotipa kukunda naIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu." 
1Corinthians15:58 Saka, hama dzangu dzinodikanwa, mirai makasimba, murege kuzununguswa, mushandire Ishe zvikuru nguva dzose, muchiziva kuti kubata basa kwenyu hakungavi pasina muna Ishe." 
1Corinthians16:1 Zvino, kana zviri zvipo zvakaunganidzirwa vatsvene, sezvandakaraira Chechi yeGaratia, itai nemiwo saizvozvo." 
1Corinthians16:2 Nomusi wokutanga wevhiki, mumwe nomumwe wenyu ngaakamure zvimwe kumba kwake, aunganidze, paakawana napo, kuti zvipo zvirege kuunganidzwa, kana ndichisvika." 
1Corinthians16:3 Kana ndasvika, ndichatuma avo vamunotenda netsamba, vagondoisa zvipo zvenyu Jerusaremu." 
1Corinthians16:4 Kana zvakafanira kuti ini ndiendewo, vangaenda neni." 
1Corinthians16:5 Zvino ndichauya kwamuri, kana ndagura neMasedhonia; nokuti ndinogura neMasedhonia." 
1Corinthians16:6 Zvimwe ndichagara nemi, kunyangwe ndipedze chando, kuti mugondiperekedza pose pandinoenda." 
1Corinthians16:7 Nokuti handidi kukuonai zvino ndiri parwendo; nokuti ndinoti ndichazogara nemi chinguva, kana Ishe achinditendera." 
1Corinthians16:8 Asi ndichagara paEfeso kusvikira paPendekositi. 
1Corinthians16:9 Nokuti ndazarurirwa musuwo mukuru, une basa guru; navadzivisi vazhinji varipo." 
1Corinthians16:10 Zvino kana Timoti achisvika, chenjerai kuti agare nemi asingatyi; nokuti anobata basa raIshe, sezvandinoita neniwo." 
1Corinthians16:11 Naizvozvo ngakurege kuva nomunhu anomuzvidza. Asi muperekedzei norugare, kuti auye kwandiri; nokuti ndakamutarira pamwechete nehama." 
1Corinthians16:12 Zvino kana ari Aporo, hama yedu, ndakakumbira kwaari zvikuru, kuti auye kwamuri pamwechete nedzimwe hama; asi akanga asingatongodi kuuya zvino, achauya hake kana awana nguva yakanaka." 
1Corinthians16:13 Rindai, mirai nesimba pakutenda, itai savarume, musimbiswe." 
1Corinthians16:14 Zvose zvamunoita ngazviitwe norudo. 
1Corinthians16:15 Ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri, hama dzangu, munoziva mhuri yaSitefani, kuti ndicho chibereko chokutanga paAkia, vakazviisa kuti vashumire vatsvene." 
1Corinthians16:16 Kuti nemiwo muzviise pasi pavakadaro, napasi pavose vanotibatsira navanobata basa iri." 
1Corinthians16:17 Ndinofara nokuuya kwaSitefani, naFochunatosi, naAkayikosi; nokuti ivo vakandiitira zvamakanga musingagoni kuita imi." 
1Corinthians16:18 Nokuti vakazorodza mweya wangu nowenyu; naizvozvo kudzai vakadaro. 
1Corinthians16:19 Chechi dzapaEzhia dzinokukwazisai. Akwira naPirisira vanokukwazisai zvikuru muna Ishe, pamwechete nechechi iri mumba mavo." 
1Corinthians16:20 Hama dzose dzinokukwazisai. Kwazisanai nokutsvoda kutsvene. 
1Corinthians16:21 Ndiko kukwazisa kwangu, ini Pauro, noruoko rwangu." 
1Corinthians16:22 Kana munhu asingadi Ishe, ngaave akatukwa. Ishe anouya!" 
1Corinthians16:23 Nyasha dzaIshe Jesu ngadzive nemi. 
1Corinthians16:24 Rudo rwangu ngaruve nemi mose muna Kristu Jesu. 
2Corinthians1:1 Pauro, mupostori waKristu Jesu, nokuda kwaMwari, naTimoti, hama yedu kuchechi yaMwari iri muKorinde, pamwechete navatsvene vose vari paAkia yose." 
2Corinthians1:2 Nyasha ngadzive nemi, norugare runobva kuna Mwari, Baba vedu, naIshe Jesu Kristu." 
2Corinthians1:3 Mwari ngaavongwe, ivo Baba vaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, Baba vengoni, Mwari wokunyaradza kwose;" 
2Corinthians1:4 iye anotinyaradza pakutambudzika kwedu kwose, kuti isu tive nesimba rokunyaradza vari mukutambudzika kupi nokupi, nokunyaradzwa kwatinonyaradzwa nako naMwari." 
2Corinthians1:5 Nokuti matambudziko aKristu sezvaakava mazhinji kwatiri, saizvozvowo kunyaradzwa kwedu kwakava kuzhinji naKristu." 
2Corinthians1:6 Zvino kana tichitambudzika hedu isu, zvinoitwa nokuda kwokunyaradzwa nokuponeswa kwenyu; kana tichinyaradzwa isu, zvinoitwa nokuda kwokunyaradzwa kwenyu, kunokusimbisai kutsungirira pamatambudziko iwayo atinotambudzikawo nawo." 
2Corinthians1:7 Tariro yedu pamusoro penyu yakasimba, nokuti tinoziva kuti sezvamunosangana nesu pamatambudziko, saizvozvowo pakunyaradzwa." 
2Corinthians1:8 Nokuti hatidi hama dzangu, kuti murege kuziva kutambudzika kwakatiwira paEzhia, kuti takaremerwa kwazvo–kwazvo kukunda simba redu, nokudaro takarasa mwoyo tichiti hatingararami;" 
2Corinthians1:9 asi pamwoyo pedu isu takanga tatozvitongera rufu, kuti tirege kuvimba nesimba redu, asi naMwari anomutsa vakafa;" 
2Corinthians1:10 iye akatisunungura parufu rukuru rwakadai, uye achatisunungurazve; iye watinotenda kuti acharamba achitisunungura;" 
2Corinthians1:11 nemiwo muchibatsirana pakutikumbirira kwenyu, kuti vanhu vazhinji vavonge pamusoro pedu nokuda kwechipo chedu chenyasha chatakapiwa nokunyengetera kwavazhinji." 
2Corinthians1:12 Nokuti kuzvirumbidza kwedu ndikoku: Kupupura kwehana yedu, kuti takafamba panyika, zvikuru kwamuri, noutsvene nechokwadi chaMwari, tisingafambi nouchenjeri hwenyama, asi nenyasha dzaMwari." 
2Corinthians1:13 Nokuti hatikunyorerei zvimwe zvinhu, asi izvo zvamunorava nezvamunotenda; ndinoti dai muchizvitenda kusvikira pakuguma;" 
2Corinthians1:14 sezvamakatitendawo pane zvimwe, kuti isu tiri kurumbidzwa kwenyu, semiwo muchava kurumbidzwa kwedu nezuva raIshe Jesu." 
2Corinthians1:15 Ndichiziva izvozvi, ndakanga ndichida kutanga kuuya kwamuri, kuti mukomborerwe rwechipiri;" 
2Corinthians1:16 ndipfuure nokwenyu ndichienda Masedhonia, nokuuya nokwenyuzve, ndichibva Masedhonia, ndiperekedzwe nemi ndichienda Judhiya." 
2Corinthians1:17 Zvino zvandakanga ndichida kuita izvozvo, ndakaita nokusanduka mwoyo here? Kana, zvandinoda kuita ndinozvida nenyama here, kuti ini pamwe nditi, “Hongu, hongu,” pamwe, “Kwete, kwete?”" 
2Corinthians1:18 NaMwari akatendeka, shoko redu kwamuri harizi “Hongu” kana “Kwete.”" 
2Corinthians1:19 Nokuti Mwanakomana waMwari, Jesu Kristu, uyo akaparidzwa pakati penyu nesu neni naSirivhano naTimoti akanga asiri, “Hongu” kana “Kwete,” asi akanga ari, “Hongu maari.”" 
2Corinthians1:20 Nokuti zvipikirwa zvaMwari, kunyangwe zviri zvizhinji sei, maari ndi “Hongu,” naizvozvo naiyewo ndi “Ameni,” kuti Mwari akudzwe nesu." 
2Corinthians1:21 Zvino, uyo anotisimbisa muna Kristu pamwechete nemi, nokutizodza, ndiMwari;" 
2Corinthians1:22 uyo akatiisirawo chisimbiso, akatipa rubatso rwoMweya mumwoyo medu." 
2Corinthians1:23 Asi ndinodana Mwari, ave chapupu pamwoyo wangu, kuti handina kuzouya Korinde, nokuti ndakakunzwirai tsitsi." 
2Corinthians1:24 Hatiiti simba nokutenda kwenyu, asi tinokubatsirai kuti mufare; nokuti mumire nokutenda." 
2Corinthians2:1 Asi ndakati mumwoyo mangu, kuti handidi kuuyazve kwamuri nokuchema." 
2Corinthians2:2 Nokuti kana ndichikuchemedzai, ndianiko achandifadza, kana asiri iye akachemedzwa neni?" 
2Corinthians2:3 Zvino ndakanyora chinhu ichi kuti kana ndasvika ndirege kuchemedzwa naivo vaifanira kundifadza; ndichikutendai mose, kuti kufara kwangu ndokwenyu mose." 
2Corinthians2:4 Nokuti ndakakunyorerai nemisodzi mizhinji pakutambudzika kukuru nenhamo yomwoyo; ndisingati muchemedzwe, asi kuti muzive rudo rukuru rwandinokudai narwo." 
2Corinthians2:5 Zvino kana mumwe akachemedza hake, haana kundichemedza ini, asi ndingati zvimwe ndirege kunyanyisa imi mose." 
2Corinthians2:6 Kurova uku kwavanhu vazhinji kunoringana munhu wakadai. 
2Corinthians2:7 Naizvozvo zviri nani kuti mumukanganwire nokumunyaradza, kuti arege kuodzwa mwoyo kwazvo neshungu huru." 
2Corinthians2:8 Naizvozvo ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri kuti musimbise rudo rwenyu kwaari. 
2Corinthians2:9 Nokuti ndakanyorawo izvi, kuti ndikuedzei, ndizive kana munoteerera pazvinhu zvose." 
2Corinthians2:10 Zvino iye wamunoregerera, neni ndinomuregererawo; nokuti izvo zvandakaregererwa ini, kana ndinenge ndakaregererwa chinhu, ndakazviita nokuda kwenyu pamberi paKristu;" 
2Corinthians2:11 kuti tirege kunyengerwa naSatani; nokuti mano ake tinoaziva. 
2Corinthians2:12 Zvino, ndakati ndichisvika paTiroasi kuparidza Vhangeri yaKristu, ndichizarurirwa musuwo muna Kristu," 
2Corinthians2:13 ndakanga ndisina zororo pamweya wangu, nokuti handina kuwanapo Tito, hama yangu; asi ndakaonekana navo, ndikaenda Masedhonia." 
2Corinthians2:14 Asi Mwari ngaavongwe, anotikundisa nguva dzose muna Kristu, anoratidza nesu kwose–kwose hwema hwokuziva kwake." 
2Corinthians2:15 Nokuti isu tiri hwema hwakanaka hwaKristu kuna Mwari, pakati paivo vanoponeswa navanoparara." 
2Corinthians2:16 Kuna vamwe tiri hwema hworufu hunoisa kurufu; kuna vamwe hwema hwoupenyu hunoisa kuupenyu. Zvino ndianiko angakwanisa zvinhu zvakadai? 
2Corinthians2:17 Nokuti hatifanani navamwe vazhinji vanokanganisa shoko raMwari; asi tinotaura muna Kristu nechokwadi, sechinobva kuna Mwari, pamberi paMwari." 
2Corinthians3:1 Tinotangazve kuzvirumbidza kwamuri here? Tinotsvaka here savamwe tsamba dzinoenda kwamuri, kana dzinobva kwamuri, dzingatirumbidza?" 
2Corinthians3:2 Imi muri tsamba yedu yakanyorwa mumwoyo medu, inozikanwa nokurahwa navanhu vose;" 
2Corinthians3:3 makaonekwa kuti muri tsamba yaKristu, yakagadzirwa nesu, isina kunyorwa neingi, asi naMweya waMwari mupenyu; isina kunyorwa pamahwendefa emabwe, asi pamahwendefa emwoyo yavanhu." 
2Corinthians3:4 Kutenda kwakadai tinako naKristu, kuna Mwari;" 
2Corinthians3:5 hatiti takakwana isu timene, kuti titeme chinhu timene; asi kukwana kwedu kunobva kuna Mwari;" 
2Corinthians3:6 iye akatikwanisa kuti tive vashumiri vesungano itsva, isati iri yezvakanyorwa asi yoMweya; nokuti zvakanyorwa zvinouraya, asi Mweya anopa upenyu." 
2Corinthians3:7 Zvino kana kushumira, kwakauyisa rufu, kwakanga kwakatemwa namabhii pamabwe, kwakauya nokubwinya, kwakanga kwadaro kuti vana VaIsiraeri vakakoniwa kutarisisa chiso chaMosesi nokuda kwokubwinya kwechiso chake kwakanga kuchipfuura hako" 
2Corinthians3:8 ko kushumira kwoMweya hakungavi nokubwinya kukuru here? 
2Corinthians3:9 Nokuti kana kushumira, kwakauyisa kutongeswa, kwakanga kunokubwinya, zvikuru sei kushumira, kunouyisa kururama, kuchakunda pakubwinya." 
2Corinthians3:10 Nokuti naicho chakabwinyiswa, hachina kubwinyiswa, kana pachinhu ichi tichichifananidza nokubwinya kunokunda." 
2Corinthians3:11 Nokuti kana icho chinopfuura chaiva nokubwinya, zvikuru sei icho chinogara ndicho chiri pakubwinya." 
2Corinthians3:12 Naizvozvo, zvatine tariro yakadai, tinotaura tisingatyi napaduku," 
2Corinthians3:13 tisingaiti saMosesi, waiisa chifukidziro pachiso chake, kuti vana VaIsiraeri varege kutarisisa kuguma kwezvinopfuura." 
2Corinthians3:14 Asi ndangariro dzavo dzakakokomara; nokuti kusvikira zuva ranhasi, kana sungano yakare ichirawa, chifukidziro icho chiripo, chisingaratidzwi kuti muna Kristu zvinopfuura." 
2Corinthians3:15 Asi kusvikira nhasi, kana Mosesi achiverengwa, chifukidziro chiripo pamwoyo yavo." 
2Corinthians3:16 Zvino kana munhu achitendeukira kuna Ishe, chifukidziro chinobviswa." 
2Corinthians3:17 Ishe ndiMweya; zvino panoMweya waIshe, pane sununguko." 
2Corinthians3:18 Zvino isu tose tinoti tichitarira nechiso chisina kufukidzirwa kubwinya kwaIshe sapachionioni, tinosandurwa tichifanana nomufananidzo iwoyo, tichibva pakubwinya kumwe tichienda kunokumwe kubwinya, sezvichibva kuna Ishe, Mweya." 
2Corinthians4:1 Saka, zvatinako kushumira uku, patakanzwirwa ngoni napo, hatineti;" 
2Corinthians4:2 asi takaramba zvinhu zvakavanzika zvinonyadza, tisingafambi nokunyengera, tisingashatisi shoko raMwari; asi pakuratidza kwedu zvokwadi, tinozvitendisa kuhana dzavanhu vose pamberi paMwari." 
2Corinthians4:3 Zvino kana Vhangeri yedu yakafukidzwa, yakafukidzwa kuna vanorasika;" 
2Corinthians4:4 kuna vasingatendi vakapofumadzirwa ndangariro namwari wenyika ino, kuti varege kuvhenekerwa nechiedza cheVhangeri yokubwinya kwaKristu, uri mufananidzo waMwari." 
2Corinthians4:5 Nokuti hatizviparidzi isu, asi Kristu Jesu kuti ndiye Ishe; nesu kuti tiri varanda venyu nokuda kwaJesu." 
2Corinthians4:6 Nokuti Mwari, akareva kuti, “Chiedza chibude parima,” ndiye akavhenekera mumwoyo yedu, kuti atipe chiedza chokuziva kubwinya kwaMwari kunoonekwa pachiso chaJesu Kristu." 
2Corinthians4:7 Asi pfuma iyi tinayo mumidziyo yevhu, kuti ukuru hwesimba huve hwaMwari, hurege kuva hwedu." 
2Corinthians4:8 Tinotambudzika pamativi ose, asi hatimanikidzwi; tinokanganiswa, asi hatina kurasa mwoyo;" 
2Corinthians4:9 tinotambudzwa, asi hatina kusiyiwa; takawisirwa pasi, asi hatina kuparadzwa;" 
2Corinthians4:10 tinoramba tichitakura nguva dzose mumuviri wedu kufa kwaJesu, kuti noupenyuwo hwaJesu huratidzwe mumuviri wedu." 
2Corinthians4:11 Nokuti isu vapenyu tinogara tichingoiswa pakufa nokuda kwaJesu, kuti noupenyuwo hwaJesu huratidzwe munyama yedu inofa." 
2Corinthians4:12 Saizvozvo kufa kunobata matiri, asi upenyu mamuri." 
2Corinthians4:13 Zvino zvatino mweya iwoyu wokutenda, sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Ndakatenda, saka ndakataura;” nesuwo tinotenda, saka tinotaurawo;" 
2Corinthians4:14 tichiziva kuti iye akamutsa Ishe Jesu, achatimutsawo isu pamwechete naJesu; agotiisa pamberi pake pamwechete nemi." 
2Corinthians4:15 Nokuti zvinhu zvose zvinoitwa nokuda kwenyu, kuti nyasha zvadzakawanzwa navazhinji, dziwanze kuvonga, kuti Mwari akudzwe." 
2Corinthians4:16 Saka hatineti, asi kunyangwe munhu wedu wokunze uchipera hawo, munhu womukati unovandudzwa zuva rimwe nerimwe." 
2Corinthians4:17 Nokuti kutambudzika kwedu, kwakareruka, kuripo chinguva chiduku, kunotiitira kubwinya kukuru kwakaisvonaka kusingaperi;" 
2Corinthians4:18 tisingatariri zvinoonekwa, asi zvisingaonekwi; nokuti zvinoonekwa zvinopfuura, asi zvisingaonekwi ndezvokusingaperi." 
2Corinthians5:1 Nokuti tinoziva kuti kana imba yedu yenyika, tabhenakeri yedu, ichiputswa, tine chakavakwa chinobva kuna Mwari, imba isina kuvakwa namaoko, isingaperi, iri kudenga." 
2Corinthians5:2 Nokuti tinogomerawo mairi, tichishuva kuti tifukidzwe neimba yedu inobva kudenga;" 
2Corinthians5:3 kuti kana takafukidza hedu, hatingawanikwi tisina chatakafuka." 
2Corinthians5:4 Nokuti nesu, tiri mutabhenakeri iyi tinogomera, tichiremerwa; tisingadi kuti tikutunurwe, asi kuti tifukidzwe, kuti chinofa chimedzwe noupenyu." 
2Corinthians5:5 Zvino, uyo akatigadzirira chinhu ichi ndiMwari, akatipawo rubatso rwoMweya." 
2Corinthians5:6 Naizvozvo tinotsunga mwoyo nguva dzose, tichiziva kuti kana tichigara mumuviri hatigari kuna Ishe;" 
2Corinthians5:7 nokuti tinofamba nokutenda, hatifambi nokuona;" 
2Corinthians5:8 tinotsunga mwoyo, tichiti zviri nani tirege kugara mumuviri, kuti tigare kuna Ishe." 
2Corinthians5:9 Saka tinoshingaira kuti timufadze iye, kunyangwe tichigaramo, kunyangwe tisingagarimo." 
2Corinthians5:10 Nokuti isu tose tinofanira kuratidzwa pamberi pechigaro chokutonga chaKristu; kuti mumwe nomumwe apiwe zvaakaita nomuviri, sezvaakaita, kana zvakanaka kana zvakaipa." 
2Corinthians5:11 Naizvozvo zvatinoziva kutya kwaIshe, tinogombedzera vanhu; asi tinoratidzwa hedu kuna Mwari; uye zvino ndinoti dai tichiratidzwawo muhana dzenyu." 
2Corinthians5:12 Hatizvirumbidzizve kwamuri, asi tinokupai nzira yokurumbidza nokuda kwedu, kuti mugone kupindura avo vanovimba nezvinoonekwa, vasingavimbi nezvomwoyo." 
2Corinthians5:13 Nokuti kana tichipenga, tinodaro nokuda kwaMwari; kana tiri vanhu kwavo, tinodaro nokuda kwenyu." 
2Corinthians5:14 Nokuti rudo rwaKristu runotimanikidza; zvatinoziva chinhu ichi kuti mumwe akafira vose, zvino vose vakafa;" 
2Corinthians5:15 zvino iye akafira vose, kuti avo vanorarama varege kuzozviraramira ivo, asi uyo akafa nokumutswa nokuda kwavo." 
2Corinthians5:16 Naizvozvo kubvira zvino hatitongozivi munhu panyama; uye kunyangwe takaziva Kristu panyama, kubvira zvino hatichamuzivi saizvozvo." 
2Corinthians5:17 Saka kana munhu ari muna Kristu, ava chisikwa chitsva; zvinhu zvakare zvapfuura; tarirai, zvose zvava zvitsva." 
2Corinthians5:18 Asi zvinhu zvose zvakabva kuna Mwari, wakatiyananisa naye naKristu, akatipa kushumira kwokuyananisa;" 
2Corinthians5:19 ndiko kuti Mwari akanga achiyananisa nyika naye muna Kristu, akasavaverengera kudarika kwavo, akatipa isu shoko rokuyananisa." 
2Corinthians5:20 Naizvozvo tiri nhume nokuda kwaKristu, Mwari saanenge achikumbira zvikuru nesu; tinokumbira nokuda kwaKristu, tichiti, “Yananiswai naMwari.”" 
2Corinthians5:21 Uyo, akanga asingazivi zvivi, akamuita kuti ave zvivi nokuda kwedu; kuti isu tive kururama kwaMwari maari." 
2Corinthians6:1 Zvino zvatinobatsirana naye, tinokumbira zvikuru kuti murege kugamuchira nyasha dzaMwari pasina." 
2Corinthians6:2 (Nokuti iye anoti, “Ndakakunzwa iwe nenguva yakafanira, Ndakakubatsira pazuva rokuponeswa.” Tarirai, zvino inguva yakafanira; tarirai, zvino ndiro zuva rokuponeswa.)" 
2Corinthians6:3 Hatigumbusi vamwe nechinhu, kuti kushumira kwedu kurege kuzvidzwa;" 
2Corinthians6:4 asi pazvinhu zvose tinozviratidza savashumiri vaMwari, pakutsungirira kukuru, panhamo, pakushayiwa, pamatambudziko," 
2Corinthians6:5 pakurohwa, pakusungwa, pakunyonganiswa, pamabasa, pakusavata, pakuzvinyima zvokudya;" 
2Corinthians6:6 pakuchema kwomwoyo, pakuziva, pamwoyo murefu, paunyoro, paMweya Mutsvene, parudo rusinganyengeri;" 
2Corinthians6:7 pashoko rechokwadi, pasimba raMwari, nenhumbi dzokurwa dzokururama, kurudyi nokurubhoshwe" 
2Corinthians6:8 nokukudzwa, nokusakudzwa, neguhu rakaipa, neguhu rakanaka; savanyengeri, asi tiri vechokwadi hedu;" 
2Corinthians6:9 savasingazikanwi, asi tichizikanwa hedu zvikuru; savanofa, asi, tarirai, tiri vapenyu; savanorohwa, asi tisingaurawi;" 
2Corinthians6:10 savanochema, asi tichigara tichifara hedu; savarombo, asi tichipfumisa vazhinji; savasina chinhu, asi tinazvo zvose." 
2Corinthians6:11 Imi, vaKorinde, muromo wedu wakashama kwamuri, mwoyo wedu wakuriswa." 
2Corinthians6:12 Hamumanikidzwi nesu, asi munomanikidzwa mumwoyo menyu." 
2Corinthians6:13 Zvino, mundidzosere saizvozvo (ndinotaura sokuna vana vangu), imiwo mukuriswe mwoyo." 
2Corinthians6:14 Musasungwa zvisina kufanira pajoko pamwechete navasingatendi; nokuti kururama kungava noukama hweiko nokusarurama? Chiedza chingayanana seiko nerima? 
2Corinthians6:15 Kristu anganzwana seiko naBheriari? Anotenda angava nomugove weiko noasingatendi? 
2Corinthians6:16 Temberi yaMwari ingatenderana seiko nezvifananidzo? Nokuti isu tiri temberi yaMwari mupenyu; Mwari sezvaakareva, achiti, “Ndichagara mukati mavo, nokufamba mukati mavo; ndichava Mwari wavo, ivo vachava vanhu vangu." 
2Corinthians6:17 Saka budai pakati pavo, muzviraure, ndizvo zvinotaura Ishe, Musabata chinhu chine tsvina; Ini ndichakugamuchirai," 
2Corinthians6:18 Ndichava Baba venyu, Nemi muchava vanakomana navanasikana vangu, ndizvo zvinotaura Ishe ane simba rose.”" 
2Corinthians7:1 Zvino, vadikanwi, zvatine zvipikirwa izvi, ngatizvinatse pamatsvina ose enyama noomweya, tikwanise utsvene pakutya Mwari." 
2Corinthians7:2 Mutizarurire mwoyo yenyu; hatina kuitira munhu zvisakarurama, hatina kutadzira munhu, hatina kunyengera munhu." 
2Corinthians7:3 Handirevi izvi, kuti ndikupei mhosva; nokuti ndamboreva kuti imi muri mumwoyo medu, kuti tife nokurarama pamwechete nemi." 
2Corinthians7:4 Kusatya kwangu kukuru pakutaura kwamuri, nokuzvirumbidza kwangu kukuru pamusoro penyu; ndizere nokunyaradzwa, ndinofara kwazvo pakutambudzika kwedu kwose." 
2Corinthians7:5 Nokuti takati tasvika Masedhonia, nyama yedu haina kuzorora, asi takatambudzika pamativi ose; kunze kwaiva nokukakavara, mukati maiva nokutya." 
2Corinthians7:6 Asi Mwari, anonyaradza vakaora mwoyo, akatinyaradza nokusvika kwaTito;" 
2Corinthians7:7 handiti nokusvika kwake bedzi, asiwo nokunyaradzwa, kwaakanyaradzwa nako pamusoro penyu, achitiudza zvechishuo chenyu, nokuchema kwenyu, nokushingaira kwenyu pamusoro pangu; saka ndakanyanya kufara." 
2Corinthians7:8 Nokuti kunyangwe ndakakuchemedzai netsamba yangu, handizvidyi mwoyo; kunyangwe ndakanga ndichizvidya mwoyo hangu, ndinoona kuti tsamba iyo yakakuchemedzai, asi yakanga iri nguva duku hayo." 
2Corinthians7:9 Zvino, handifari kuti makachemedzwa, asi nokuti makachemedzwa mukatendeuka; nokuti makachemedzwa sezvinoda Mwari, kuti murege kurasikirwa nechinhu nokuda kwedu." 
2Corinthians7:10 Nokuti kuchema sezvinoda Mwari kunouyisa kutendeuka, kunoisa kukuponwa kusingazvidyi mwoyo; asi kuchema kwenyika kunouyisa rufu." 
2Corinthians7:11 Nokuti tarirai kuti chinhu icho chokuti makachemedzwa sezvinoda Mwari, chakauyisa mukati menyu kushingaira kukuru sei, nokuzvidavirira, nokutsamwa, nokutya, nechisuwo, nokurwadza mwoyo, nokutsiva. Pazvinhu zvose makazviratidza kuti makachena pachinhu ichi." 
2Corinthians7:12 Zvino, kana ndakakunyorerai, handina kuzviita nokuda kwaiye akaita zvisakarurama, kana nokuda kwaiye akaitirwa zvisakarurama, asi kuti kushingaira kwenyu nokuda kwedu kuonekwe nemi mumene pamberi paMwari." 
2Corinthians7:13 Nemhaka iyi isu tinonyaradzwa; zvino pakunyaradzwa kwedu takafara zvikuru kwazvo pamusoro pomufaro waTito, nokuti mweya wake wakasimbiswa nemi mose." 
2Corinthians7:14 Nokuti kana ndakazvirumbidza nechinhu kwaari pamusoro penyu, handina kunyadziswa; asi sezvatakataura kwamuri zvose nechokwadi, saizvozvowo kuzvirumbidza kwedu pamberi paTito kwakaonekwa kuti ndokwechokwadi." 
2Corinthians7:15 Nehanya dzake dzawedzerwa kwamuri, achirangarira kuteerera kwenyu mose, pamakamugamuchira napo nokutya nokudedera." 
2Corinthians7:16 Ndinofara kuti pazvinhu zvose ndingakutendai. 
2Corinthians8:1 Zvino tinokuzivisai, hama dzangu, nyasha dzaMwari dzakapiwa pachechi dzeMasedhonia;" 
2Corinthians8:2 kuti pakati pokuedzwa kukuru kwokutambudzika, mufaro wavo mukuru, pamwechete nourombo hwavo hukuru, zvakawanza zvikuru kusanyima kwavo." 
2Corinthians8:3 Nokuti ndinopupura, kuti vakapa nokuda kwavo pavakagona napo, kunyangwe kupfuura pavakagona napo;" 
2Corinthians8:4 vakakumbira nokunyengetera kukuru kwatiri kuti tivatendere kuita basa iri renyasha nokusangana pakushumira vatsvene; 
2Corinthians8:5 havana kuita sezvatakafunga bedzi, asi ivo vakatanga kuzvipa kuna ishe, nokwatiri, nokuda kwaMwari." 
2Corinthians8:6 Naizvozvo takakumbira zvikuru kuna Tito, kuti sezvaakanga atanga, apedzise basa iri renyasha pakati penyuwo." 
2Corinthians8:7 Zvino sezvamakapfuurira pazvinhu zvose, pakutenda, napakutaura, napakuziva, napakushingaira kwose, naparudo rwenyu kwatiri, tarirai kuti mupfuure pabasa iri renyashawo." 
2Corinthians8:8 Handirevi ndichirayira, asi kuti ndiedze ndizive nokushingaira kwavamwe kana rudo rwenyu nderwechokwadiwo." 
2Corinthians8:9 Nokuti munoziva nyasha dzaIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu, kuti kunyangwe akanga akapfuma, akava murombo nokuda kwenyu, kuti imi nourombo hwake muve vapfumi." 
2Corinthians8:10 Pachinhu ichi ndinokuudzai kufunga kwangu; nokuti zvichakubatsirai, nokuti ndimi makatangira vamwe makei, musingaiti bedzi, asi muchidawo." 
2Corinthians8:11 Asi zvino pedzisai kuitawo; sezvamakanga muno mwoyo unoda, saizvozvo pedzisaiwo pamunogona napo." 
2Corinthians8:12 Nokuti kana mwoyo wokupa uripo, chipo chinofadza paanapo, kusati kuri paanoshaiwa napo." 
2Corinthians8:13 Nokuti handirevi kudaro ndichiti vamwe varerukirwe, imi muremerwe; asi kuti muenzane;" 
2Corinthians8:14 kuti panguva ino kuwanda kwenyu kubatsire kushayiwa kwavo, kuti kuwanda kwavo kubatsire kushayiwa kwenyuwo; kuti kuve nokuenzana;" 
2Corinthians8:15 sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Wakaunganidza zvizhinji, haana kusarirwa nechinhu; naiye akaunganidza zvishoma, haana kushayiwa.”" 
2Corinthians8:16 Zvino Mwari ngaavongwe, wakaisa mumwoyo maTito kushingaira kwakadaro kwamuri." 
2Corinthians8:17 Nokuti akanzwa hake kurayira kwedu, asi zvaakanga achishingaira zvikuru, akaenda kwamuri, nokuda kwake hake." 
2Corinthians8:18 Zvino takatuma pamwechete naye hama iya, inorumbidzwa paVhangeri pachechi dzose;" 
2Corinthians8:19 zvisati zviri izvozvo bedzi, asi iye akasanangurwawo nechechi kuti atiperekedze pabasa iri renyasha, rinoitwa nesu, kuti iye Mwari akudzwe;" 
2Corinthians8:20 tichizvichenjerera, kuti kurege kuva nomunhu angatipa mhosva pamusoro pezvakawanda izvi, zvatinobata nazvo." 
2Corinthians8:21 Nokuti hatitsvaki zvinhu zvakanaka pamberi paIshe bedzi, asi pamberi pavanhuwo." 
2Corinthians8:22 Takatumawo navo hama yedu, yatakaedza kazhinji tikaona kuti anoshingaira pazvinhu zvizhinji; asi zvino anonyanya kushingaira nokuda kwokutenda kukuru kwaanako kwamuri." 
2Corinthians8:23 Kana ari Tito, ndiye shamwari yangu, nomubatsiri wangu kwamuri; kana dziri hama dzedu, ndivo vapostori vechechi, uye kukudzwa kwaKristu." 
2Corinthians8:24 Naizvozvo muvaratidze pamberi pechechi chiratidzo chorudo rwenyu, nechokurumbidza kwedu pamusoro penyu." 
2Corinthians9:1 Nokuti kana kuri kushumira vatsvene, handifaniri kuti ndikunyorerei;" 
2Corinthians9:2 nokuti ndinoziva kuda kwomwoyo yenyu, kwandinozvirumbidza nako kuna vaMasedhonia kuti, “VaAkaia vakanga vazvigadzira kubvira makei; nokushingaira kwenyu kwakamutsa vazhinji.”" 
2Corinthians9:3 Zvino, ndakatuma hama idzi, kuti kuzvirumbidza kwedu pamusoro penyu kurege kuitwa pasina chinhu ichi; kuti, sezvandakareva, mugare makazvigadzira;" 
2Corinthians9:4 kuti zvimwe kana vamwe veMasedhonia vachiuya neni, vakakuwanai musina kuzvigadzira, isu (hatirevi imi) tirege kunyadziswa pakutenda uku." 
2Corinthians9:5 Naizvozvo ndakati zvakafanira kuti ndirayire hama idzi, kuti vatange kuenda kwamuri, vatange kumbogadzira chipo chokuvonga chamakapikira kare, kuti ichi chigare chakagadzirwa chiri chipo chokuvonga, chirege kuva chinhu chakatorwa nesimba." 
2Corinthians9:6 Zvino rangarirai chinhu ichi: Anodyara zvishoma, achachekawo zvishoma; anodyara zvizhinji, achachekawo zvizhinji." 
2Corinthians9:7 Mumwe nomumwe ngaaite sezvaakafunga mumwoyo; arege kuita nokuchema, kana nokurovererwa; nokuti Mwari anoda munhu anopa nomufaro." 
2Corinthians9:8 Mwari anogona kukuwanzirai nyasha dzose kuti nguva dzose muve nokuringana kwose pazvose, kuti muwanze mabasa ose akanaka;" 
2Corinthians9:9 sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Iye akaparadzira, iye akapa varombo; Kururama kwake kunogara nokusingaperi.”" 
2Corinthians9:10 Zvino iye, anopa mudyari mbeu nechingwa, kuti zvive zvokudya, achakupaiwo mbeu dzokudyara achidziwanza, nokuwedzera zvibereko zvokururama kwenyu;" 
2Corinthians9:11 muchifumiswa pazvose mugoziva kupa zvakawanda, zvinoti, kana zvichiitwa nesu, Mwari anovigirwa nazvo kuvonga." 
2Corinthians9:12 Nokuti kushumira kwokubatsira uku hakuzadzisi kushayiwa kwavatsvene bedzi, asi kunowanzisawo kuvonga kuna Mwari;" 
2Corinthians9:13 nokuda kwezvinoonekwa pakushumira uku vanorumbidza Mwari, pamusoro pokupupura kwenyu kwakateerera Vhangeri yaKristu, napamusoro pokupa kwenyu zvakawanda kwavari nokuna vose." 
2Corinthians9:14 Naivo vomene vanokushuvai, vachikukumbirirai, nokuda kwenyasha huru–huru dzaMwari pamusoro penyu." 
2Corinthians9:15 Mwari ngaavongwe pamusoro pechipo chake, chisingagoni kurondedzerwa." 
2Corinthians10:1 Zvino ini Pauro ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri nounyoro netsitsi dzaKristu ini muduku kana ndiri pakati penyu, asi ndinotsunga kwamuri kana ndisipo." 
2Corinthians10:2 Ndinokumbira kwamuri, kuti kana ndavapo, ndirege kuzotsunga, nokutenda kwandinoti zvino ndichatsunga nako kuna vamwe vanoti tinofamba nenzira yenyama." 
2Corinthians10:3 Nokuti, kunyangwe tichifamba nenzira yenyama, hatirwi nemitoo yenyama;" 
2Corinthians10:4 nokuti nhumbi dzedu dzokurwa nadzo hadzizi dzenyama, asi dzine simba pamberi paMwari rokuputsa nhare;" 
2Corinthians10:5 isu tinoti tichiputsa njere, nezvakakwirira zvose zvinomutswa kuzorwa nokuziva Mwari, tinopa mifungo yose kuti iteerere Kristu;" 
2Corinthians10:6 takazvigadzira kuranga kusateerera kwose, kana kuteerera kwenyu kwazadziswa." 
2Corinthians10:7 Imi munotarira zvinhu zviri pamberi penyu. Kana munhu achivimba nazvo achiti ndiri waKristu, ngaarangarirezve chinhu ichi mumwoyo make, kuti sezvaari waKristu iye, saizvozvo nesuwo." 
2Corinthians10:8 Nokuti kunyangwe ndainyanya kuzvirumbidza pamusoro pesimba redu ratakapiwa naIshe kukusimbisai, risati riri rokukuputsai, handinganyadziswi;" 
2Corinthians10:9 kuti ndirege kuita sendinokutyisai netsamba dzangu. 
2Corinthians10:10 Nokuti vanoti, “Tsamba dzake dzina mashoko makuru, dzine simba, asi muviri wake kana aripo, uno utera, nokutaura kwake kunozvidzwa.”" 
2Corinthians10:11 Munhu akadaro ngaarangarire chinhu ichi, kuti sezvatinoreva mutsamba kana tisipo, ndizvo zvatakaitawo pakuita kwedu kana tiripo." 
2Corinthians10:12 Nokuti tinotya kuzvienzanisa nokuzvifananidza navamwe vanozvikudza; asi ivo havana njere, zvavanozvienzanisa naivo vamene, nokuzvifananidza naivo vomene." 
2Corinthians10:13 Zvino isu hatingazvirumbidzi tichipfuura chiyero, asi nechiyero chinosvika pachitanda chatakagoverwa naMwari, kuti chive chiyero, chisvikirewo kwamuri." 
2Corinthians10:14 Nokuti hatinyanyi kuzvitambanudza, sezvatisingasvikiri kwamuri; nokuti tisu takatanga kusvikira kwamuri neVhangeri yaKristu;" 
2Corinthians10:15 hatizvirumbidzi tichipfuura chiyero pamusoro pebasa ravamwe; asi tine tariro kuti, kana kutenda kwenyu kuchikura, isu tichakuriswa pakati penyu kusvikira pachitanda chedu nokupfuurisa;" 
2Corinthians10:16 tigoparidza Vhangeri panyika dziri mberi kwenyu, tirege kuzvirumbidza pachitanda chomumwe pamusoro pezvatoitwa hazvo." 
2Corinthians10:17 Asi anozvirumbidza, ngaazvirumbidze muna Ishe." 
2Corinthians10:18 Nokuti akatendeka haazi iye anozvirumbidza, asi ndiye anorumbidzwa naIshe." 
2Corinthians11:1 Dai muchindiitira mwoyo murefu paduku paupenzi hwangu; asi munondiitira henyu mwoyo murefu. 
2Corinthians11:2 Nokuti ndine godo pamusoro penyu negodo raMwari; nokuti ndakakuwanisai nomurume mumwe, kuti ndikuisei kuna Kristu semhandara yakachena." 
2Corinthians11:3 Asi ndinotya kuti, senyoka yakanyengera Evha namano ayo, zvimwe saizvozvo ndangariro dzenyu dzingasvibiswa, dzitsauke pakururama nokuchena kwomwoyo kuri kuna Kristu." 
2Corinthians11:4 Nokuti kana mumwe achiuya anoparidza mumwe Jesu, watisina kumboparidza isu, kana zvimwe muchigamuchira mumwe mweya, wamusina kumbogamuchira, kana imwe vhangeri, yamusina kumbotenda, zvino momuitira mwoyo murefu kwazvo." 
2Corinthians11:5 Nokuti ndinoti handizi muduku napaduku–duku kuvapostori vanopfuura vamwe vose. 
2Corinthians11:6 Zvino kunyangwe ndisinganatsi pakutaura, handina kudaro pakuziva; asi pazvinhu zvose takaratidza izvozvo kwamuri pamberi pavose." 
2Corinthians11:7 Ndakatadza here zvandakazvininipisa kuti imi mukudzwe, zvandakakuparidzirai Vhangeri yaMwari ndisingapiwi mubairo?" 
2Corinthians11:8 Dzimwe Chechi ndakadzitorera, ndichireva mubairo, kuti ndikushumirei imi." 
2Corinthians11:9 Uye, panguva yandakanga ndiri kwamuri, ndichishayiwa, handina kuremedza munhu; nokuti zvandakashaiwa ndakapiwa nehama dzaibva Masedhonia; pazvinhu zvose ndakachenjera kuti ndirege kukuremedzai, uye ndicharamba ndichichenjera." 
2Corinthians11:10 Chokwadi chaKristu chiri mandiri, ndinoti kuzvirumbidza uku hakungandidzivisirwi kunyika yeAkaia." 
2Corinthians11:11 Nemhaka yeiko? Nokuti handikudi here? Mwari anoziva. 
2Corinthians11:12 Asi chinhu ichi chandinoita, ndinochiita, kuti ndishayise nzira ivo vanotsvaka nzira; kuti vawanikwe vakaita sesu pazvinhu izvozvo zvavanozvirumbidza nazvo." 
2Corinthians11:13 Nokuti vakadaro vapostori venhema, vanobata nokunyengera, vanozvishandura vachizviita vapostori vaKristu." 
2Corinthians11:14 Naizvozvi hazvishamisi; nokuti kunyangwe naSataniwo anozvishandura, achizviita somutumwa wechiedza." 
2Corinthians11:15 Naizvozvo hachizi chinhu chikuru, kana vashumiri vake vachishandurawo, vachizviita savashumiri vokururama; kuguma kwavo kuchava sezvavakabata basa." 
2Corinthians11:16 Ndinopamhidza, ndichiti: Ngakurege kuva nomunhu anoti ndiri benzi; asi kana muchidaro henyu, ndigamuchirei sebenzi, kuti ndizvirumbidze hangu zvishomawo." 
2Corinthians11:17 Zvandinotaura, handizvitauri sezvinobva kuna Ishe, asi sapaupenzi hwangu, pakuzvitenda uku kwatinozvirumbidza nako." 
2Corinthians11:18 Vazhinji zvavanozvirumbidza panyama, neniwo ndichazvirumbidza." 
2Corinthians11:19 Nokuti munoitira mapenzi mwoyo murefu nomufaro, imi muri vakachenjera;" 
2Corinthians11:20 nokuti munoita nomwoyo murefu kana munhu achikuitai varanda, kana achikuparadzai, kana achikutapai, kana achizvikudza, kana achikurovai kumeso." 
2Corinthians11:21 Ndinoreva ndichizvishora, ndichiti takanga tisina simba kudaro. Zvino kana kuno munhu anotsunga, (ndinotaura sebenzi), neni ndinotsungawo." 
2Corinthians11:22 Ivo vaHebheru here? Neniwo. Ivo VaIsiraeri here? Neniwo. Ivo vana vaAbhurahamu here? Neniwo. 
2Corinthians11:23 Ivo vashumiri vaKristu here? (Ndinotaura somunhu anopenga), zvikuru ini; pamabasa ndinovapfuura, pakurohwa zvikuru–kuru, parufu kazhinji." 
2Corinthians11:24 Ndakarohwa navaJudha kashanu shamhu dzina makumi matatu nepfumbamwe. 
2Corinthians11:25 Katatu ndakarohwa netsvimbo, kamwe ndakatakwa namabwe, katatu ndakaputsikirwa nechikepe, usiku humwe namasikati ndakanga ndiri mugungwa;" 
2Corinthians11:26 panzendo kazhinji, panjodzi dzenzizi, panjodzi dzamakororo, panjodzi dzovorudzi rwangu, panjodzi dzavahedheni, panjodzi muguta, panjodzi murenje, panjodzi mugungwa, panjodzi pakati pehama dzenhema;" 
2Corinthians11:27 pakubata basa napakutambura, pakuvata kazhinji takarindira, panzara nenyota, pakuzvinyima zvokudya kazhinji, pachando napakushayiwa zvokufuka." 
2Corinthians11:28 Kunze kwaizvozvi, ndinoremedzwa zuva rimwe nerimwe nokurangarira Chechi dzose." 
2Corinthians11:29 Ndianiko asina simba, neni ndikasava nesimba? Ndianiko anogumburwa, neni ndikasarwadziwa?" 
2Corinthians11:30 Kana ndikafanira kuzvirumbidza, ndichazvirumbidza nezvinhu zvoutera hwangu." 
2Corinthians11:31 Mwari, Baba vaIshe Jesu, anokudzwa nokusingaperi, anoziva kuti handirevi nhema." 
2Corinthians11:32 PaDhamasikosi mubati pasi pamambo Areta akarinda guta raveDhamasikosi, achitsvaka kundibata;" 
2Corinthians11:33 ndikaburuswa ndiri mudengu napahwindo parusvingo, ndikatiza pamaoko ake." 
2Corinthians12:1 Ndinofanira hangu kuzvirumbidza, kunyangwe zvisina kunaka, asi ndichasvika pazviratidzo nezvakazarurwa zvaIshe." 
2Corinthians12:2 Ndinoziva munhu ari muna Kristu, ava makore ane gumi namana apfuura, (kana zvakaitwa mumuviri, kana kunze kwomuviri, handizivi; Mwari anoziva), munhu akadai akakwidzwa kudenga rechitatu." 
2Corinthians12:3 Uye ndinoziva munhu akadai (kana zvakaitwa mumuviri kana kunze kwomuviri, handizivi; Mwari anoziva)," 
2Corinthians12:4 kuti akakwidzwa muparadhiso, akanzwa mashoko asingagoni kutaurwa, asina kutenderwa munhu kuti aareve." 
2Corinthians12:5 Pamusoro pomunhu akadai ndichazvirumbidza; asi pamusoro pangu handizvirumbidzi; asi pamusoro poutera hwangu bedzi. 
2Corinthians12:6 Nokuti kana ndichida kuzvirumbidza, handingavi benzi; nokuti ndichareva zvamazvokwadi; asi ndinorega hangu, kuti kurege kuva nomunhu, angati ndiri mukuru kune zvaakaona kana zvaakanzwa kwandiri;" 
2Corinthians12:7 zvino, kuti ini ndirege kunyanya kuzvikudza nokuda kwoukuru kwazvo hwezvakandizarurirwa, ndakapiwa munzwa munyama yangu, nhume yaSatani, andirove, kuti ndirege kunyanya kuzvikudza." 
2Corinthians12:8 Pamusoro pechinhu ichi ndakakumbira Ishe zvikuru katatu, kuti chibve kwandiri." 
2Corinthians12:9 Iye akati kwandiri, “Nyasha dzangu dzinokuringana; nokuti simba rangu rinozadziswa pautera hwako.” Naizvozvo zviri nani kuti ndizvirumbidze nomufaro mukuru noutera hwangu, kuti simba raKristu rigare pamusoro pangu." 
2Corinthians12:10 Naizvozvo ndinofara noutera, nokuzvidzwa, nokushaiwa, nokutambudzika, nenhamo nokuda kwaKristu; nokuti kana ndino utera, ipapo ndine simba." 
2Corinthians12:11 Ndava benzi; imi mandiroverera. Nokuti ini ndaifanira kurumbidzwa nemi; nokuti handizi muduku napaduku kuvapostori vanopfuura vose, kunyangwe ndisi chinhu." 
2Corinthians12:12 Zvirokwazvo, zviratidzo zvomupostori zvakaitwa pakati penyu nokutsungirira kukuru, nezviratidzo, nezvishamiso, namabasa esimba." 
2Corinthians12:13 Nokuti makapfuurwa neiko nedzimwe Chechi, asi pakuti ini handina kukuremedzai? Ndikanganwirei henyu kusarurama uku." 
2Corinthians12:14 Tarirai, ino ndiyo nguva yechitatu yandakazvigadzira kuuya kwamuri; handingakuremedzii; nokuti handitsvaki zvenyu, asi ndinokutsvakai imi; nokuti vana havafaniri kuchengetera vabereki, asi vabereki vanofanira kuchengetera vana." 
2Corinthians12:15 Nokuti ndingafara zvikuru kupedza zvose zvangu, nokupedzwa ini nokuda kwemweya yenyu. Kana ini ndichikudai zvikuru, ini ndodikanwa zvishoma here?" 
2Corinthians12:16 Zvino, ngazvive saizvozvo hazvo, ini handina kukuremedzai; asi zvandakanga ndine njere, ndakakubatai namano." 
2Corinthians12:17 Ndakakutorerai chinhu here nomumwe waivo vandakatuma kwamuri? 
2Corinthians12:18 Ndakarayira Tito, ndikatuma hama iya naye; ko Tito akakutorerai chinhu here? Hatina kufamba nomweya mumwe here? Uye namakwara mamwe here?" 
2Corinthians12:19 Nguva yose makanga muchiti tinozvidavirira kwamuri here? Tinotaura pamberi paMwari muna Kristu; asi tinotaura izvi zvose, vadikanwi, kuti musimbiswe." 
2Corinthians12:20 Nokuti ndinotya kuti zvimwe kana ndichisvika, ndingakuwanai musina kuita sezvandinoda, neni ndingawanikwa nemi ndakaita sezvamusingadi; zvimwe kungavapo gakava, negodo, nokutsamwa, nokupesana, nokuchera, namakuhwa, namanyawi, nenyonganiso;" 
2Corinthians12:21 kuti kana ndichisvikazve, Mwari wangu arege kundininipisa pamberi penyu, ndicheme pamusoro pavazhinji vavo vatotadza, vakasatendeuka patsvina yavo, noupombwe, noutere hwavakaita." 
2Corinthians13:1 Iyi inguva yechitatu, yandinouya kwamuri. “Mumiromo yezvapupu zviviri kana zvitatu mashoko ose achasimbiswa.”" 
2Corinthians13:2 Avo, vatotadza, navamwe vose, ndambovaudza, zvino ndovaudzazve, sezvandakaita parwendo rwechipiri, nokudaro zvino ndinonyora ndisipo kuti kana ndichisvikazve, handingavaitiri mwoyo murefu;" 
2Corinthians13:3 zvamunotsvaka chiratidzo chaKristu, anotaura mandiri, iye asingashayiwi simba kwamuri, asi ane simba paanenge aine chokuita nemi." 
2Corinthians13:4 Nokuti akaroverwa pamuchinjikwa nokushayiwa simba maari, asi anorarama nesimba raMwari. Nokuti nesuwo tinouterawo maari, asi tichararama kwamuri pamwechete naye nesimba raMwari." 
2Corinthians13:5 Zviedzei imi mumene, muone kana muri makasimba pakutenda; muzvinzverei imi mumene. Hamuzivi here imi mumene kuti Jesu Kristu ari mukati menyu? Kana zvimwe mava vakaraswa henyu." 
2Corinthians13:6 Asi ndinoti muchaziva henyu kuti isu hatina kuva vakaraswa. 
2Corinthians13:7 Zvino tinonyengetera Mwari kuti murege kuita chinhu chimwe chakaipa; handidaro kuti isu tiwanikwe kuti takatendeka, asi kuti imi muite zvakarurama, kunyangwe isu takaita savakaraswa." 
2Corinthians13:8 Nokuti hatigoni kuita chinhu chinopesana nechokwadi, asi chinobatsira chokwadi." 
2Corinthians13:9 Nokuti tinofara kana isu tiine utera, imi muchiva nesimba; ndizvo zvatinokumbirawo, kuti mukwaniswe." 
2Corinthians13:10 Saka ndinonyora izvi ndisipo, kuti kana ndavapo, ndirege kuita nehasha, sezvandakapiwa naIshe simba rokusimbisa, risati riri rokuputsa." 
2Corinthians13:11 Pakupedzisira, hama dzangu, farai, mukwaniswe, munyaradzwe, ivai nomwoyo mumwe, garai norugare; Mwari worudo norugare achava nemi." 
2Corinthians13:12 Kwazisanai nokusveta kutsvene. 
2Corinthians13:13 Vatsvene vose vanokukwazisai. 
2Corinthians13:14 Nyasha dzaIshe Jesu Kristu, norudo rwaMwari, nokuyanana kwoMweya Mutsvene, ngazvive nemi mose." 
Galatians1:1 Pauro, mupostori, asina kubva kuvanhu, kana kutumwa nomunhu, asi naJesu Kristu, naMwari Baba, akamumutsa kuvakafa," 
Galatians1:2 nehama dzose dziri kwandiri, kusangano reGaratia." 
Galatians1:3 Nyasha norugare ngazvive nemi, zvinobva kuna Mwari, Baba vedu, naIshe Jesu Kristu," 
Galatians1:4 akazvipa nokuda kwezvivi zvedu, kuti atisunungure kunyika yakaipa yazvino, nokuda kwaMwari, Baba vedu;" 
Galatians1:5 ngaave nokubwinya nokusingaperi. Ameni. 
Galatians1:6 Ndinoshamiswa kuti munokurumidza mukadai kushandukira uyo akakudanai munyasha dzaKristu, kuti mutsaukire kune imwe Vhangeri;" 
Galatians1:7 isati iri imwe hayo; asi kuti vamwe varipo vanokukanganisai, vachida kushandura Vhangeri yaKristu." 
Galatians1:8 Asi kunyangwe isu, kana mutumwa anobva kudenga, akakuparidzirai imwe Vhangeri, inopesana neyatinokuparidzirai isu, ngaave akatukwa." 
Galatians1:9 Sezvatakamboreva, zvino ndinorevazve saizvozvo: Kana kuno munhu anokuparidzirai imwe Vhangeri, inopesana neiyo yamakagamuchira, ngaave akatukwa." 
Galatians1:10 Nokuti zvino ndinoita ushamwari navanhu here, kana naMwari? Kana ndinotsvaka kufadza vanhu here? Kana ndaifadza vanhu nazvino, handizaiva muranda waKristu." 
Galatians1:11 Nokuti ndinokuzivisai, hama dzangu, kuti Vhangeri yakaparidzwa neni, haina kuita seyavanhu." 
Galatians1:12 Nokuti handina kuipiwa kana kuidzidziswa nomunhu, asi ndakairatidzwa naJesu Kristu." 
Galatians1:13 Nokuti makanzwa zvomufambiro wangu kare pakunamata kwavaJudha, kuti ndaitambudza sangano yaMwari zvikuru kwazvo, ndikaiparadza;" 
Galatians1:14 pakunamata kwavaJudha ndaipfuura vazhinji vezero rangu parudzi rwangu, ndichinyanya kushingairira tsika dzamadzibaba angu." 
Galatians1:15 Zvino Mwari, iye akanditsanangura kubva padumbu ramai vangu, akandidana nenyasha dzake, akati afadzwa nazvo," 
Galatians1:16 kuti aratidze Mwanakomana wake mandiri, ndimuparidze pakati pavahedheni, pakarepo; handina kurangana nenyama neropa;" 
Galatians1:17 handina kukwira Jerusaremu kunaavo vakanditangira kuva vapostori, asi ndakaenda Arabhiya, ndikadzokera Dhamasikosi zve." 
Galatians1:18 Ipapo, makore matatu akati apfuura, ndikakwira Jerusaremu kundoona Kefasi, ndikagara naye mazuva ane gumi namashanu." 
Galatians1:19 Asi handina kuona mumwe wavapostori, asi Jakobho bedzi, munun'una waIshe." 
Galatians1:20 Izvi zvandinokunyorerai, tarirai, pamberi paMwari, handirevi nhema." 
Galatians1:21 Ipapo ndakasvika kunyika dzeSiria neSirisia. 
Galatians1:22 Asi ndakanga ndisingazikanwi pachiso nesangano reJudhiya riri muna Kristu; 
Galatians1:23 asi vakanga vanzwa bedzi, kuti “Uya, waititambudza kare, zvino ava kuparidza kutenda kwaaiparadza kare;”" 
Galatians1:24 vakarumbidza Mwari nokuda kwangu. 
Galatians2:1 Zvino, makore ane gumi namana akati apfuura, ndikakwirazve Jerusaremu naBhanabhasi, ndikaendawo naTitosi." 
Galatians2:2 Ndakakwira nokuda kwokuratidzwa; ndikarondedzera pamberi pavo Vhangeri yandinoparidza pakati pavahedheni, asi kuna vakanga vachikudzwa vari voga, kuti zvimwe ndirege kumhanyira pasina, kana kuti zvimwe ndatomhanyira pasina." 
Galatians2:3 Asi naTito, waiva neni, ari muGiriki, haana kurovererwa kuti adzingiswe;" 
Galatians2:4 nokuda kwehama dzenhema, vakanga vapinzwa nokunyanga, vakanga vapinda pakavanda, kuti vashore kusununguka kwedu kwatinako muna Kristu Jesu, kuti vatisunge;" 
Galatians2:5 hatina kuvatsedukira ivava, tichivateerera kunyangwe nguva imwechete; kuti chokwadi cheVhangeri chirambe chichigara nemi." 
Galatians2:6 Zvino kana vari ivo vanonzi vakuru handina mhaka kuti vaiva vakadini kare; Mwari haatendi zvinoonekwa zvomunhu kana vari ivo vanonzi vakuru, havana kundiwedzera chinhu;" 
Galatians2:7 asi ivo vakati vaona kuti ini ndakapiwa Vhangeri kuna vasina kudzingiswa, saPetirosi kuna vakadzingiswa;" 
Galatians2:8 nokuti iye akapa Petirosi simba rokuva mupostori kuna vakadzingiswa, ndiye akapawo ini simba rokuva mupostori kuvahedheni;" 
Galatians2:9 vakati vaona nyasha dzandakanga ndapiwa, Jakobho, naKefasi, naJohani avo vainzi mbiru vakatibata isu tose naBhanabhasi namaoko orudyi okuyanana, kuti isu tiende kuvahedheni, ivo kuna vakadzingiswa;" 
Galatians2:10 vakada chete kuti tirangarire varombo; ndizvo zvandakashingairirawo kuti ndizviite. 
Galatians2:11 Zvino Kefasi akati asvika Andiyoku ndakamudzivisa pachena, nokuti akanga ane mhosva." 
Galatians2:12 Nokuti vamwe, vakanga vabva kuna Jakobho; asi vasati vasvika, iye aidya navahedheni asi vakati vasvika akadzoka, akazviraura, achitya vakadzingiswa." 
Galatians2:13 Navamwe vaJudha vakaita mano–manowo pamwechete naye; zvikaitwa kuti naiye Bhanabhasiwo akatsauswa namano–mano avo. 
Galatians2:14 Asi ndakati ndichiona kuti havafambi zvakarurama nechokwadi cheVhangeri, ndakati kuna Kefasi pamberi pavose: “Kana iwe, uri muJudha, uchifamba savahedheni usingaiti savaJudha, unoreverera seiko vahedheni, kuti vafambe savaJudha?”" 
Galatians2:15 Isu vaJudha pakuzvarwa kwedu, tisati tiri vatadzi vanobva kuvahedheni," 
Galatians2:16 zvatinoziva kuti munhu haaruramiswi namabasa omurairo, asi nokutenda kuna Kristu Jesu, nesuwo takatenda kuna Kristu Jesu, kuti tiruramiswe nokutenda kuna Kristu, tirege kururamiswa namabasa omurairo; nokuti hakuna munhu acharuramiswa namabasa omurairo." 
Galatians2:17 Zvino kana isu pakutsvaka kwekururamiswa muna Kristu, tikawanikwa tiri vatadziwo timene, ko Kristu wava mushumiri wezvivi here? Haisva!" 
Galatians2:18 Nokuti kana ndikavakazve izvo zvandamboputsa, ndinozviita mudariki." 
Galatians2:19 Nokuti nomurairo ini ndakafa kumurairo, kuti ndirarame kuna Mwari." 
Galatians2:20 Ndakaroverwa pamuchijikwa pamwechete naKristu; handichiri ini ndinorarama, asi Kristu anorarama mandiri; kurarama uku, kwandinorarama nako munyama zvino, ndinorarama nokutenda kuri muMwanakomana waMwari, akandida, akazvipa nokuda kwangu." 
Galatians2:21 Handikonesi nyasha dzaMwari; nokuti kana kururamiswa kuchibva kumurairo, Kristu akafa pasina." 
Galatians3:1 Imi vaGaratia vokusafunga, ndianiko wakakurunzirai, iyemi, makaratidzwa Jesu Kristu pachena pamberi pameso enyu akaroverwa pamuchinjikwa?" 
Galatians3:2 Ichochi bedzi ndinoda kunzwa kwamuri: Makapiwa Mweya namabasa omurairo here, kana nokunzwa kwokutenda?" 
Galatians3:3 Muri vokusafunga vakadaro seiko? Makatanga muMweya, ko zvino mopedzisa munyama here?" 
Galatians3:4 Makatambudzika zvikuru mukadai pasina here? Kana zvaiva pasina hazvo! 
Galatians3:5 Naizvozvo uyo anokupai Mweya, nokuita mabasa esimba pakati penyu, anozviita izvo namabasa omurairo here, kana nokunzwa kwokutenda?" 
Galatians3:6 Abhurahamu sezvaakatenda kuna Mwari, kukanzi kwaari ndiko kururama." 
Galatians3:7 Naizvozvo zivai kuti vokutenda ndivo vana vaAbhurahamu. 
Galatians3:8 NoRugwaro, zvarwakaziva zviri mberi, kuti Mwari acharuramisa vahedheni nokutenda, rwakaparidza Vhangeri kare kuna Abhurahamu, ruchiti, “Mauri marudzi ose acharopafadzwa.”" 
Galatians3:9 Naizvozvo vokutenda vanoropafadzwa pamwechete naAbhurahamu, akatenda." 
Galatians3:10 Nokuti vose vari vamabasa omurairo, vari pakutukwa; nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, “Vakatukwa vose vasingarambiri pazvinhu zvose zvakanyorwa muBhuku yoMurairo, kuti vazviite.”" 
Galatians3:11 Zvino, zvinoonekwa kuti hakuna munhu anoruramiswa nomurairo pamberi paMwari, nokuti, “Akarurama achararama nokutenda.”" 
Galatians3:12 Zvino murairo haubvi pakutenda; asi uyo akaita zvinhu izvozvi achararama nazvo. 
Galatians3:13 Kristu akatidzikinura pakutuka kwomurairo, iye akaitwa chakatukwa nokuda kwedu, nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, “Vakatukwa vose vanoturikwa pamuti!”" 
Galatians3:14 Kuti kuropafadzwa kwaAbhurahamu kusvike kuvahedheni muna Jesu Kristu; kuti tipiwe nokutenda chipikirwa choMweya. 
Galatians3:15 Hama dzangu, ndinoreva nokureva kwavanhu, ndichiti: Kunyangwe iri sungano yavanhu hayo, kana yasimbiswa, hakuna munhu anoikonesa kana kuwedzera kwairi." 
Galatians3:16 Zvino, izvo zvipikirwa zvakarehwa kuna Abhurahamu nokumwana wake. Haarevi, achiti, “Kuvana vako,” savanenge vari vazhinji; asi saanenge ari mumwe, unoti, “Kumwana wako;” uyu ndiye Kristu." 
Galatians3:17 Zvino ndinoreva chinhu ichi, ndichiti, Sungano yakasimbiswa kare naMwari haitorerwi simba rayo nomurairo wakazotevera makore mazana mana namakumi matatu apfuura, kuti chipikirwa chikoneswe." 
Galatians3:18 Nokuti kana nhaka ichibva kumurairo, haichabvi kuchipikirwa; asi Mwari akaipa Abhurahamu nokupikira." 
Galatians3:19 Naizvozvo murairo chiiko? Wakazowedzerwa nokuda kwezvivi, kusvikira mwana akapikirwa izvozvo achizouya; iwo wakarayirwa navatumwa noruoko rwomurevereri." 
Galatians3:20 Zvino murevereri haazi womumwechete; asi Mwari ndomumwe. 
Galatians3:21 Naizvozvo asi murairo unorwisa zvipikirwa zvaMwari here? Haisva! Nokuti dai vakanga vapiwa murairo waigona kuraramisa, zvirokwazvo kururamiswa kwaibva kumurairo." 
Galatians3:22 Asi Rugwaro rwakapfigira zvose pasi pezvivi, kuti chipikirwa chinobva pakutenda muna Jesu Kristu chipiwe vanotenda." 
Galatians3:23 Asi kutenda kusati kwasvika, taichengetwa pasi pomurairo, takapfigirwa nokuda kwokutenda kwaizoratidzwa." 
Galatians3:24 Saizvozvo murairo wakanga uri muperekedzi wedu, kutiisa kuna Kristu kuti tiruramiswe nokutenda." 
Galatians3:25 Zvino kutenda zvakwakasvika, hatichiri pasi pomuperekedzi." 
Galatians3:26 Nokuti imi mose muri vana vaMwari nokutenda muna Kristu Jesu; 
Galatians3:27 nokuti vose pakati penyu, vakabhabhatidzwa muna Kristu, makapfeka Kristu." 
Galatians3:28 Hakuchina muJudha kana muGiriki, hakuchina akasungwa kana akasununguka, hakuchina munhurume kana munhukadzi; nokuti imi mose muri vamwe muna Kristu Jesu." 
Galatians3:29 Zvino kana muri vaKristu, muri vana vaAbhurahamu, vadyi venhaka sezvamakapikirwa." 
Galatians4:1 Zvino ndinoti, mudyi wenhaka, kana achiri mwana, haatongosiyani nomuranda, kunyangwe ari ishe wazvose;" 
Galatians4:2 asi ari pasi pavatariri navachengeti kusvikira panguva yakatarwa nababa. 
Galatians4:3 Saizvozvo nesuwo, tichiri vana, takanga takasungwa pasi pezvokuvamba zvenyika;" 
Galatians4:4 zvino nguva yakati yazara kwazvo, Mwari akatuma Mwanakomana wake, akaberekwa nomukadzi, akaberekwa pasi pomurairo," 
Galatians4:5 kuti adzikinure vari pasi pomurairo, kuti tipiwe umwana hwedu." 
Galatians4:6 Zvino zvamuri vanakomana, Mwari akatuma Mweya woMwanakomana wake mumwoyo medu unodana, achiti, “Abha, Baba!”" 
Galatians4:7 Saka iwe hauchiri muranda, asi mwanakomana, kana wava mwanakomana, wava mudyi wenhaka naMwari." 
Galatians4:8 Asi nenguva iyo, zvamakanga musingazivi Mwari, maiva varanda vavamwari vasati vari vezvokwadi;" 
Galatians4:9 asi zvino, zvamunoziva Mwari, zvikuru zvamunozikanwa naMwari, modzokerazve seiko kune zvokuvamba zvisina simba, zvourombo, muchidazve kutanga kuva varanda vazvo?" 
Galatians4:10 Munochengeta misi nemwedzi, nenguva namakore." 
Galatians4:11 Ndinotya pamusoro penyu, kuti zvimwe ndakabata basa kwamuri pasina." 
Galatians4:12 Ndinokumbira kwamuri, hama dzangu, kuti muve seni, nokuti ini ndakaita semi. Hamuna kundiitira chinhu chimwe chisakarurama;" 
Galatians4:13 zvino munoziva kuti ndakakuparidzirai Vhangeri pakutanga nokuda kwokurwara panyama; 
Galatians4:14 nechinhu icho panyama yangu, chakanga chiri muedzo kwamuri, hamuna kuchizvidza, kana kuchisema; asi makandigamuchira somutumwa waMwari, saiye Kristu Jesu." 
Galatians4:15 Zvino kufara kwenyu kuripiko? Nokuti ndinokupupurirai, kuti kana maigona, maitumbura meso enyu mukandipa iwo." 
Galatians4:16 Zvino ndava muvengi wenyu, zvandakakuudzai chokwadi here?" 
Galatians4:17 Vanokushingairirai nomutoo usakanaka; asi vanoda kukupfigirai kunze, kuti imi muvashingairire." 
Galatians4:18 Zvino zvakanaka kuti pachinhu chakanaka kushingairirwe nguva dzose, zvirege kuitwa kana ndiri kwamuri bedzi." 
Galatians4:19 Vana vangu vaduku, vandinotamburirazve kubereka, kusvikira Kristu aumbwa mukati menyu." 
Galatians4:20 Ndaida kuti ndive nemi zvino, ndishandure izwi rangu; nokuti ndinokanganiswa nokuda kwenyu." 
Galatians4:21 Ndiudzei, imi munoda kuva pasi pomurairo, hamuteereri murairo here?" 
Galatians4:22 Nokuti kwakanyorwa kuti Abhurahamu akanga ana vanakomana vaviri, mumwe womurandakadzi, mumwe womukadzi akasununguka."
