Galatians4:23 Zvino womurandakadzi akaberekwa nenzira yenyama; asi womukadzi akasununguka akaberekwa sezvaakapikirwa. 
Galatians4:24 Zvinhu izvi zvinofananidzira; nokuti vakadzi ava vaviri isungano mbiri; imwe inobva pagomo reSinai, inobereka vana vouranda ndiye Agari;" 
Galatians4:25 zvino Agari ndiro gomo reSinai muArabhia, rakaenzana neJerusaremu razvino; nokuti uri muuranda iye navana vake." 
Galatians4:26 Zvino Jerusaremu riri kumusoro rakasununguka, ndivo mai vedu;" 
Galatians4:27 nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, “Fara, iwe usingabereki, usingazvari, Pururudza, udanidzire, iwe usingatamburi nokubereka, Nokuti vana vomusiyiwa vazhinji kuno waiye ano murume.”" 
Galatians4:28 Zvino imi, hama dzangu, muri vana vokupikirwa saIsaka." 
Galatians4:29 Asi sapanguva iyo, uyo wakaberekwa nenzira yenyama wakatambudza akaberekwa nenzira yoMweya, zvakadarowo nazvino." 
Galatians4:30 Asi Rugwaro runotiiko? “Dzinga murandakadzi nomwanakomana wake; nokuti mwanakomana womurandakadzi haangadyi nhaka pamwechete nomwanakomana wowakasununguka.” 
Galatians4:31 Saka, hama dzangu, hatizi vana vomurandakadzi, asi vowakasununguka." 
Galatians5:1 Kristu akatisunungura kuti tive vakasununguka; naizvozvo mirai nesimba, murege kusungwazve nejoko rouranda." 
Galatians5:2 Tarirai, ini Pauro, ndinoti kwamuri, kana muchidzingiswa, Kristu haangakubatsiriyi chinhu." 
Galatians5:3 Ndinopupurira mumwe nomumwe anodzingiswa, kuti iye ane ngava rokuti achengete murairo wose." 
Galatians5:4 Makaparadzaniswa naKristu, iyemi munoda kururamiswa nomurairo; mabudiswa panyasha." 
Galatians5:5 Nokuti isu noMweya tinomirira nokutenda tariro yokururamiswa. 
Galatians5:6 Nokuti muna Kristu Jesu kudzingiswa kana kusadzingiswa hazvibatsiri chinhu; asi kutenda kunobata norudo. 
Galatians5:7 Makanga muchimhanya zvakanaka; ndianiko akakudzivisai kuti murege kuteerera chokwadi? 
Galatians5:8 Hamuna kugombedzerwa naiye akakudanai. 
Galatians5:9 “Mbiriso shoma inovirisa mukanyiwa wose.” 
Galatians5:10 Ndinotenda pamusoro penyu muna Ishe, kuti hamungatongorangariri chimwe chinhu; asi uyo, anokupesanisai achafanira hake kutongwa, kunyangwe ari ani naani." 
Galatians5:11 Asi ini, hama dzangu, kana ndichiparidza kuti vanhu vadzingiswe, ndinoramba ndichitambudzwa neiko? Naizvozvo kugumbusa kwomuchinjikwa kwabviswa." 
Galatians5:12 Dai avo vanokupesanisai vachizvigadzirawo pachavo. 
Galatians5:13 Nokuti imi, hama dzangu, makadanirwa kusununguka; asi kusununguka kwenyu ngakurege kuva nzira yenyama, asi batiranai norudo." 
Galatians5:14 Nokuti murairo wose unozadziswa neshoko rimwechete, rokuti, “Ida wokwako sezvaunozvida iwe;”" 
Galatians5:15 asi kana muchirumana nokudyana, chenjerai kuti murege kupedzana." 
Galatians5:16 Zvino ndinoti: Fambai noMweya, ipapo hamungaiti kuchiva kwenyama." 
Galatians5:17 Nokuti nyama inochiva ichirwa noMweya; noMweya uchirwa nenyama; nokuti izvi zvinorwisana; kuti murege kuita zvamunoda. 
Galatians5:18 Asi kana muchitungamirirwa noMweya, hamuzi pasi pomurairo." 
Galatians5:19 Zvino mabasa enyama anoonekwa, anoti: Upombwe, netsvina, nokukara" 
Galatians5:20 nokunamata zvifananidzo, nouroyi, nokuvengana, negakava, negodo, nokutsamwa, nokupesana, nokuparadzana, nedzidziso dzakatsauka," 
Galatians5:21 nokugodorana, nokuraradza, nokutamba kwakaipa, nezvinhu zvakadai; izvo zvandinokuudzai zvino, sezvandakambokuudzai kare, kuti vanoita zvakadai havangadyi nhaka youshe hwaMwari." 
Galatians5:22 Zvino chibereko choMweya ndirwo rudo, norufaro, rugare, mwoyo murefu, mwoyo munyoro, kunaka, kutendeka," 
Galatians5:23 unyoro, nokuzvidzora; hakuna murairo unodzivisa zvinhu zvakadai." 
Galatians5:24 Asi avo vari vaKristu Jesu vakarovera pamuchinjikwa nyama yavo, pamwechete nokuda kwayo, nokuchiva kwayo." 
Galatians5:25 Kana tichirarama noMweya, ngatifambewo noMweya," 
Galatians5:26 tirege kuzvikudza, tichimutsana mwoyo, tichigodorana." 
Galatians6:1 Hama dzangu, kunyangwe munhu akabatwa panokumwe kudarika, imi voMweya mudzose wakadai nomwoyo wounyoro; uchizvichenjerera iwe, kuti urege kuedzwawo." 
Galatians6:2 Takuriranai mitoro yenyu, mugozadzisa murairo waKristu saizvozvo." 
Galatians6:3 Nokuti kana munhu achiti, ndiri chinhu, asati ari chinhu, anozvinyengera iye." 
Galatians6:4 Zvino munhu mumwe nomumwe ngaaedze basa rake amene, ipapo angazvirumbidza pamusoro pake iye amene oga, asingazviiti pamusoro pomumwe." 
Galatians6:5 Nokuti munhu mumwe nomumwe achafanira kutakura mutoro wake. 
Galatians6:6 Zvino anodzidziswa Shoko, ngaagovane noanodzidzisa pazvinhu zvose zvakanaka." 
Galatians6:7 Musanyengerwa; Mwari haasekwi; nokuti izvo zvinodyarwa nomunhu, ndizvo zvaanochekazve." 
Galatians6:8 Nokuti anodyarira nyama yake, achacheka kuora, kunobva panyama; asi anodyarira Mweya, achacheka upenyu husingaperi, hunobva kuMweya." 
Galatians6:9 Zvino ngatirege kuneta pakuita zvakanaka; nokuti tinozocheka nenguva yakafanira, kana tisingaori mwoyo." 
Galatians6:10 Zvino zvatine nguva, ngatiitire vose zvakanaka, zvikuru kuna veimba yokutenda." 
Galatians6:11 Tarirai, kukura kwamabhii andinokunyorerai nawo noruoko rwangu." 
Galatians6:12 Vose vanoda kunzi vakanaka pane zvinoonekwa panyama, ndivo vanokurovererai kuti mudzingiswe; vanodaro bedzi kuti varege kutambudzwa nokuda kwomuchinjikwa waKristu." 
Galatians6:13 Nokuti kunyangwe vakadzingiswa, havachengeti murairo vamene; asi vanoda kuti imi mudzingiswe, kuti vazvirumbidze panyama yenyu." 
Galatians6:14 Asi kana ndirini, ngandirege kutongozvirumbidza napaduku, asi bedzi mumuchinjikwa waIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu; naye nyika yakaroverwa pamuchinjikwa kwandiri, neni ndakaroverwa kunyika." 
Galatians6:15 Nokuti kudzingiswa kana kusadzingiswa hachizi chinhu, asi chisikwa chitsva." 
Galatians6:16 Vose vanofamba nomurairo uyu, rugare ngaruve pamusoro pavo, nenyasha, napamusoro paVaIsiraeri vaMwari." 
Galatians6:17 Kubvira zvino ngakurege kuva nomunhu anonditambudza; nokuti ndina mavanga aJesu pamuviri wangu. 
Galatians6:18 Nyasha dzaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, ngadzive nomweya wenyu, hama dzangu. Ameni." 
Ephesians1:1 Pauro, mupostori waKristu Jesu, nokuda kwaMwari, kuvatsvene vari paEfeso, nokuna vanotenda muna Kristu Jesu." 
Ephesians1:2 Nyasha ngadzive nemi, norugare runobva kuna Mwari; Baba vedu, naIshe Jesu Kristu." 
Ephesians1:3 Ngaavongwe Mwari naBaba vaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, akatiropafadza nokuropafadza kwose kwoMweya, kudenga muna Kristu," 
Ephesians1:4 sezvaakatitsanangura maari nyika isati yavambwa, kuti tive vatsvene, vasina mhosva, pamberi pake murudo;" 
Ephesians1:5 akatitemera kare, kuti naJesu Kristu tiitwe vanakomana vake, sezvaakafadzwa pakuda kwake," 
Ephesians1:6 kuti kunaka kukuru kwenyasha dzake dzakangotipa hake muMudikanwi wake, kurumbidzwe;" 
Ephesians1:7 uyo watine dzikinuro maari neropa rake, iko kukanganwirwa kwokudarika kwedu, nokuwanda kwenyasha dzake;" 
Ephesians1:8 dzakawanza kwatiri nokuchenjera kwose nokuziva; 
Ephesians1:9 akatizivisa zvakavanzika zvokuda kwake, sezvaakafadzwa pakufunga kwake maari;" 
Ephesians1:10 kuti afambise kuzara kwenguva, aunganidzwe muna Kristu zvose zviri kudenga, nezviri pasi;" 
Ephesians1:11 muna iye, watakaitwawo nhaka maari, yatakatemerwa kare nokurayira kwaiye, anoita zvose nokufunga kwokuda kwake;" 
Ephesians1:12 kuti tirumbidze kubwinya kwake, isu takatarira kare muna Kristu;" 
Ephesians1:13 muna iye, nemiwo, makanzwa shoko rechokwadi maari, iyo Vhangeri yokuponeswa kwenyu; muna iye, wamakatenda kwaari, mukaisirwa chisimbiso noMweya Mutsvene wamakapikirwa;" 
Ephesians1:14 uri rubato rwenhaka yedu, kuratidza kudzikinurwa kwavanhu vaMwari chaivo, kuti kubwinya kwake kurumbidzwe." 
Ephesians1:15 Saka neniwo, ndakati ndanzwa kutenda muna Ishe Jesu kuri pakati penyu, norudo kuvatsvene vose," 
Ephesians1:16 handiregi kuvonga pamusoro penyu, ndichikurangarirai paminyengetero yangu;" 
Ephesians1:17 kuti Mwari waIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, Baba vokubwinya kukuru, akupei mweya wokuchenjera nowokuzarurirwa pakumuziva," 
Ephesians1:18 mavhenekerwa meso omwoyo wenyu, kuti muzive kuti kudana kwake kune tariro yei, nepfuma yokubwinya kwenhaka yake pakati pavatsvene," 
Ephesians1:19 noukuru hwakapfuurisa hwesimba rake kwatiri isu tinotenda, nokubata kwesimba rake guru," 
Ephesians1:20 raakabata muna Kristu, achimumutsa kuvakafa, nokumugarisa kurudyi rwake kudenga," 
Ephesians1:21 kumusoro–soro kwamadzishe ose, noukuru, nesimba, noushe, namazita ose anorehwa, pasati pari panyika ino bedzi, asi pane inozouyawo;" 
Ephesians1:22 akaisa zvose pasi petsoka dzake, akapa sangano iye, kuti ave musoro wazvose," 
Ephesians1:23 ndiwo muviri wake kuzara kwaiye anozadzisa zvose muna vose. 
Ephesians2:1 Akakuraramisai imi, makanga makafa nokudarika kwenyu nezvivi zvenyu," 
Ephesians2:2 izvo zvamaifamba mukati mazvo kare, netsika dzenyika ino, nenzira dzomuchinda wesimba redenga, dzomweya anobata zvino muvana vokusateerera;" 
Ephesians2:3 vataifamba tose pakati pavo kare, mukuchiva kwenyama yedu, tichiita kuda kwenyama nokwokufunga kwedu, nopakuzvarwa kwedu isu navamwe vose taiva vana vokutsamwirwa." 
Ephesians2:4 Zvino Mwari ane nyasha zhinji zhinji, nokuda kworudo rwake rukuru, rwaakatida narwo," 
Ephesians2:5 kunyangwe takanga takafa mukudarika kwedu, akatiraramisa pamwechete naKristu makaponeswa nenyasha;" 
Ephesians2:6 akatimutsa pamwechete naye, akatigarisa kudenga pamwechete naye muna Kristu Jesu;" 
Ephesians2:7 kuti nenguva dzinouya aratidze pfuma huru–huru yenyasha dzake paunyoro hwake kwatiri muna Kristu Jesu; 
Ephesians2:8 nokuti makaponeswa nenyasha, nokutenda; izvo zvisingabvi kwamuri, asi chipo chaMwari;" 
Ephesians2:9 hazvibvi pamabasa, kuti kurege kuva nomunhu anozvikudza." 
Ephesians2:10 Nokuti tiri basa rake, takasikwa kuti muna Kristu Jesu tiite mabasa akanaka, akagadzirwa kare naMwari kuti tifambe maari." 
Ephesians2:11 Naizvozvo rangarirai, kuti imi vahedheni munyama, mainzi “Vasina, kudzingiswa” naivo vanonzi, “Vokudzingiswa,” kuri munyama, kunoitwa namaoko;" 
Ephesians2:12 kuti nenguva iyo makanga musina Kristu, muri vatorwa paushe hwaVaIsiraeri, muri vaeni pasungano dzechipikirwa, musina tariro, musina Mwari panyika." 
Ephesians2:13 Asi zvino muna Kristu Jesu imi, makanga muri kure kare, makaswededzwa muropa raKristu." 
Ephesians2:14 Nokuti ndiye rugare rwedu, iye akaita zvinhu zviviri kuti chive chinhu chimwe, akaputsa rusvingo rwapakati rwaiparadzanisa;" 
Ephesians2:15 zvaakaparadza munyama yake kuvengana, iwo murairo wezvakarayirwa pazvirevo; kuti asike ava vaviri vave munhu mutsva maari, aite rugare saizvozvo;" 
Ephesians2:16 kuti mumuchinjikwa ayananisezve vose vaviri, vave muviri mumwe kuna Mwari, zvaakauraya kuvengana naiwo muchinjikwa;" 
Ephesians2:17 akasvika, akaparidza rugare kwamuri, imi maiva kure, norugare kuna ivo vaiva pedyo;" 
Ephesians2:18 nokuti isu tose tinopinda naiye noMweya mumwe kuna Baba. 
Ephesians2:19 Naizvozvo, hamuzati muchiri vaeni navatorwa, asi matova pamwechete navatsvene, neveimba yaMwari." 
Ephesians2:20 Makavakwa pamusoro penheyo dzavapostori navaporofita, Kristu Jesu amene ari ibwe rapakona." 
Ephesians2:21 Maari imba yose yakasanganiswa kwazvo, inokura, ive temberi tsvene muna Ishe." 
Ephesians2:22 Maari nemiwo makavakwa pamwechete, kuti muve ugaro hwaMwari muMweya." 
Ephesians3:1 Nemhaka iyi, ini Pauro, ndiri musungwa waKristu Jesu nokuda kwenyu, imi vahedheni," 
Ephesians3:2 kana makanzwa henyu kugoverwa kwenyasha dzaMwari dzandakapiwa pamusoro penyu; 
Ephesians3:3 kuti zvakanga zvakavanzika zvakandizivisa pakuzarurirwa, sezvandakambokunyorerai namashoko mashoma;" 
Ephesians3:4 kana muchiarava iwo, mungaona kuziva kwangu pane zvakavanzika zvaKristu;" 
Ephesians3:5 zvakanga zvisina kuziviswa vanakomana vavanhu pane dzimwe nguva, sezvazvakazarurirwa vapostori vatsvene, navaporofita zvino muMweya;" 
Ephesians3:6 zvokuti: Vahedheni, vadyi venhaka pamwechete nesu, nemitezo yomuviri pamwechete nesu, vakagoverwawo pamwechete nesu chipikirwa muna Kristu Jesu neVhangeri;" 
Ephesians3:7 yandakaitwa mushandiri wayo nechipo chenyasha dzaMwari, chandakapiwa nokushanda kwesimba rake." 
Ephesians3:8 Ini, muduku kwazvo kuvatsvene vose, ndakapiwa nyasha idzi, kuti ndiparidzire vahedheni pfuma isinganzverwi yaKristu," 
Ephesians3:9 nokuratidza vose kuti kugoverwa kwakadiniko kwezvakavanzika, zvakanga zvakafukidzwa muna Mwari, akasika zvose, kubva panguva yokutanga;" 
Ephesians3:10 kuti zvino madzishe navane simba kudenga vaziviswe nesungano kuchenjera kukuru kwaMwari; 
Ephesians3:11 sechirevo chokutanga–tanga chaakatema muna Kristu Jesu, Ishe wedu;" 
Ephesians3:12 maari tinokutsunga kwedu nokupinda kwedu tisingatyi, nokutenda kwake." 
Ephesians3:13 Saka ndinokumbira kuti murege kupera mwoyo nokutambudzika kwangu pamusoro penyu; ndiko kukudzwa kwenyu. 
Ephesians3:14 Nemhaka iyi ndinopfugama namabvi angu kuna Baba," 
Ephesians3:15 rudzi rwose kudenga napanyika runotumidzwa nezita ravo," 
Ephesians3:16 kuti vakupei papfuma yokubwinya kwavo kukuru, simba kuti musimbiswe noMweya wavo mumunhu womukati;" 
Ephesians3:17 kuti Kristu agare mumwoyo yenyu nokutenda; kuti imi, mune midzi yenyu nenheyo dzenyu murudo;" 
Ephesians3:18 muve nesimba rokunzwisisa pamwechete navatsvene vose, kuti kufara, nokureba, nokukwirira, nokudzika kwakadiniko," 
Ephesians3:19 nokuziva rudo rwaKristu, runopfuura kuziva, kuti muzadziswe nokuzara kwose kwaMwari." 
Ephesians3:20 Zvino, iye ane simba rokuita zvikuru kwazvo zvinopfuura zvose zvatinokumbira kana zvatinofunga, nesimba rinobata mukati medu," 
Ephesians3:21 ngaave nokubwinya musangano muna Kristu Jesu, kusvikira kumarudzi ose nokusingaperi–peri, Ameni." 
Ephesians4:1 Naizvozvo ini musungwa muna Ishe, ndinokumbira zvikuru kuti mufambe zvakafanira kudanwa kwamakadanwa nako," 
Ephesians4:2 nokuzvininipisa kwose nounyoro, nomwoyo murefu, muchiitirana mwoyo murefu murudo;" 
Ephesians4:3 muchishingaira kuchengeta umwe hwoMweya muchisungo chorugare. 
Ephesians4:4 Kuno muviri mumwe, noMweya mumwe, sezvamakadanwawo mutariro imwe yokudanwa kwenyu;" 
Ephesians4:5 Ishe mumwe, nokutenda kumwe; norubhabhatidzo rumwe," 
Ephesians4:6 naMwari mumwe, naBaba vavose, ari pamusoro pavose, anoshanda muna vose, ari mukati mavose." 
Ephesians4:7 Asi mumwe nomumwe wedu akapiwa nyasha nechiyero chechipo chaKristu. 
Ephesians4:8 Naizvozvo anoti, “Akakwira kumusoro akatapa vatapwa, Akapa vanhu zvipo.”" 
Ephesians4:9 Zvino kuti, “Akakwira, Chiiko,” asi kuti, akaburukawo kumativi ari pasi penyika?" 
Ephesians4:10 Akaburuka ndiye akakwirawo kumusoro–soro kwedenga rose, kuti azadzise zvose." 
Ephesians4:11 Zvino akapa vamwe kuti vave vapostori, vamwe vaporofita, vamwe vaparidzi, vamwe vafudzi navadzidzisi;" 
Ephesians4:12 kuti vatsvene vakwanisirwe basa ravo rokushumira, nerokuvaka muviri waKristu;" 
Ephesians4:13 kudzamara isu tose tisvike paumwe hwokutenda nokuziva Mwanakomana waMwari, napamunhu wakura, napachiyero choukuru hokuzara kwaKristu;" 
Ephesians4:14 kuti tirege kuramba tichingova vacheche, tichizununguswa nokudzingwa nemhepo ipi neipi yokudzidzisa nokunyengera kwavanhu, namano, kuti vatsause nokunyengera;" 
Ephesians4:15 asi tireve chokwadi murudo, tigokura maari pazvose, iye Kristu, Musoro;" 
Ephesians4:16 muviri wose wakasanganiswa zvakanaka maari nokubatanidzwa nenhengo dzose dzinosimbisa, mutezo mumwe nomumwe uchibata basa nechiyero chawo kuti muviri ukuriswe pakuvakwa kwawo murudo." 
Ephesians4:17 Naizvozvo ndinoreva nokupupura chinhu ichi muna Ishe, ndichiti, musaramba muchifamba savahedheni, vanofambawo noupenzi hwokurangarira kwavo," 
Ephesians4:18 vakasvibirwa pakunzwisisa kwavo, vari vatorwa paupenyu hwaMwari nokuda kwokusaziva kuri mukati mavo nokuda kwoukukutu hwomwoyo yavo;" 
Ephesians4:19 vakazvipa vasina hanya kuutere, kuti vabate mabasa ose etsvina nookuchiva." 
Ephesians4:20 Asi imi hamuna kudzidza Kristu saizvozvo," 
Ephesians4:21 kana ari iye hake wamakanzwa, nokudzidziswa maari, seiri chokwadi muna Jesu:" 
Ephesians4:22 kuti pamufambiro wenyu wokutanga mubvise munhu wekare; unoodzwa nokuchiva kwokunyengetera; 
Ephesians4:23 muvandudzwe mumweya wokurangarira kwenyu," 
Ephesians4:24 mupfeke munhu mutsva, akasikwa akafanana naMwari pakururama, noutsvene hwechokwadi." 
Ephesians4:25 Naizvozvo bvisai nhema, mutaure chokwadi, mumwe nomumwe kunowokwake; nokuti tiri mitezo, mumwe womumwe." 
Ephesians4:26 Tsamwai, musingatadzi; zuva ngarirege kuvira muchakatsamwa;" 
Ephesians4:27 musapa Dhiabhori nzvimbo. 
Ephesians4:28 Akaba, ngaarege kubazve; asi zviri nani kuti atambudzike abate namaoko ake basa rakanaka, kuti ave nechaangapa anoshaiwa." 
Ephesians4:29 Mumuromo menyu murege kubuda shoko rakaora, asi rakanaka, ringasimbisa pakafanira, rivigire nyasha avo vanonzwa." 
Ephesians4:30 Regai kuchemedza Mweya Mutsvene waMwari, wamakaisirwa chisimbiso maari kusvikira pazuva rokudzikinurwa." 
Ephesians4:31 Shungu dzose, nokutsamwa, nehasha, nokupopota, nokutuka, nezvakaipa zvose, ngazvibviswe kwamuri;" 
Ephesians4:32 muitirane mwoyo munyoro, munzwirane tsitsi, mukanganwirane, sezvamakakanganwirwa naMwari muna Kristu." 
Ephesians5:1 Naizvozvo ivai vateveri vaMwari savana vanodikanwa; 
Ephesians5:2 fambai murudo, Kristu sezvaakakudaiwo, akazvipa nokuda kwedu, kuti ave chipo nechibayiro kuna Mwari, zviite hwema hunonhuwira." 
Ephesians5:3 Asi upombwe, netsvina yose, kana kuchiva, ngazvirege kurehwa pakati penyu, sezvinofanira vatsvene;" 
Ephesians5:4 nezvakaipa, nokutaura zvoupenzi, nokunemera, izvo zvisina kufanira; asi zviri nani kuvonga." 
Ephesians5:5 Nokuti munoziva kwazvo, kuti hakuna mhombwe, kana munhu une tsvina, kana anochiva, ndiye anonamata zvifananidzo, angadya nhaka muushe hwaKristu naMwari." 
Ephesians5:6 Ngakurege kuva nomunhu anokunyengerai namashoko asina maturo; nokuti nemhaka yezvinhu izvi kutsamwa kwaMwari kunouya pamusoro pavanakomana vokusateerera. 
Ephesians5:7 Naizvozvo regai kushamwaridzana navo; 
Ephesians5:8 nokuti kare maiva rima, asi zvino muri chiedza muna Ishe; fambai savana vechiedza." 
Ephesians5:9 Nokuti chibereko chechiedza chiri mukunaka kwose, nokururama, nechokwadi," 
Ephesians5:10 muchiedza muzive zvinofadza Ishe. 
Ephesians5:11 Regai kuyanana namabasa erima asina zvibereko, asi zviri nani kuti muarayire;" 
Ephesians5:12 nokuti izvo, zvinoitwa navo pakavanda, zvinonyadza kana zvichirehwa." 
Ephesians5:13 Asi zvinhu zvose, kana zvarayirwa, zvinoratidzwa, chava chiedza." 
Ephesians5:14 Saka iye anoti, “Muka iwe uvete, muka kuvakafa, Kristu achakuvhenekera.”" 
Ephesians5:15 Naizvozvo chenjerai kwazvo pakufamba kwenyu, kuti murege kufamba savasina kuchenjera asi savakachenjera;" 
Ephesians5:16 mungwarire nguva yenyu, nokuti mazuva akaipa." 
Ephesians5:17 Saka musava mapenzi, asi muzive kuda kwaIshe." 
Ephesians5:18 Regai kudhakwa newaini, nokuti ndipo panokusazvidzora, asi muzadzwe noMweya;" 
Ephesians5:19 mutaurirane pakati penyu namapisarema, nenziyo, nezviimbo zvoMweya, muimbire, muridzire Ishe mumwoyo yenyu;" 
Ephesians5:20 muchivonga Mwari, Baba, nguva dzose pamusoro pezvinhu zvose, muzita raIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu;" 
Ephesians5:21 muchizviisa mumwe pasi pomumwe, muchitya Kristu." 
Ephesians5:22 Imi vakadzi, muzviise pasi pavarume venyu chaivo, sezvamunoita kuna Ishe." 
Ephesians5:23 Nokuti murume musoro womukadzi, saKristuwo musoro wesangano; iye amene ndiye muponesi womuviri." 
Ephesians5:24 Asi sangano sezvariri pasi paKristu, vakadzi ngavadaro pazvinhu zvose kuvarume vavo." 
Ephesians5:25 Imi varume, idai vakadzi venyu, Kristu sezvaakadawo sangano, akazvipa nokuda kwaro;" 
Ephesians5:26 kuti ariite dzvene achirinatsa nokushambidza nemvura neshoko," 
Ephesians5:27 kuti azviisire pamberi pake sangano, rinobwinya, risina gwapa, kana kuonyana, kana chinhu chakadai; asi rive dzvene, risina chipomerwa." 
Ephesians5:28 Saizvozvowo varume vanofanira kuda vakadzi vavo semiviri yavo. Anoda mukadzi wake, anozvida;" 
Ephesians5:29 nokuti hakuna munhu akatongovenga nyama yake; asi anoipa zvokudya nokuichengeta, Kristu sezvaanoitira sangano;" 
Ephesians5:30 nokuti isu tiri mitezo yomuviri wake. 
Ephesians5:31 Naizvozvo munhu achasiya baba vake namai vake, anamatire mukadzi wake; ivavo vaviri vachava nyama imwe." 
Ephesians5:32 Chakavanzika ichi, chikuru; asi ndinotaura zvaKristu nezvesangano." 
Ephesians5:33 Asi imiwo, mumwe nomumwe ngaade mukadzi wake sezvaanozvida iye; nomukadzi ngaatye murume wake." 
Ephesians6:1 Imi vana, teererai vabereki venyu muna Ishe; nokuti ndizvo zvakarurama." 
Ephesians6:2 Kudza baba vako namai ndiwo murairo wokutanga une chipikirwa 
Ephesians6:3 kuti uitirwe zvakanaka, ugare nguva refu panyika." 
Ephesians6:4 Nemi madzibaba, regai kutsamwisa vana venyu; asi varerei pakuranga nokurayira kwaIshe." 
Ephesians6:5 Imi varanda, teererai avo vari vatenzi venyu panyama, nokutya nokudedera, nemwoyo yakarurama, muchizviita sokuna Kristu;" 
Ephesians6:6 musingabati basa kana muchionekwa bedzi, savafadzi vavanhu, asi savaranda vaKristu, vanoita kuda kwaMwari nomwoyo wose;" 
Ephesians6:7 muchibata basa nomwoyo wakanaka, muchizviita sokuna Ishe, musingaitiri vanhu;" 
Ephesians6:8 muchiziva kuti chinhu chipi nechipi chakanaka, chinoitwa nomunhu mumwe nomumwe, achapiwazve naIshe, kana akasungwa kana akasununguka." 
Ephesians6:9 Nemi madzishe, muvaitire saizvozvo, murege kuvatyisa; nokuti munoziva kuti Ishe wavo nowenyu ari kudenga; haatendi zvinoonekwa zvomunhu." 
Ephesians6:10 Pakupedzisira ivai nesimba muna Ishe, nomusimba rake guru." 
Ephesians6:11 Shongai nhumbi dzose dzokurwa nadzo dzaMwari, mugone kumira muchirwa namano aDhiabhori." 
Ephesians6:12 Nokuti hatirwi nenyama neropa, asi navabati, navane simba, namadzishe enyika erima rino, nemweya yakaipa yedenga." 
Ephesians6:13 Saka torai nhumbi dzose dzokurwa nadzo dzaMwari, kuti mugone kudzivisa pazuva rakaipa, nokuramba mumire mapedza zvose." 
Ephesians6:14 Naizvozvo mirai makasunga zviuno zvenyu nechokwadi, makapfeka chidzitiro chechipfuva chokururama," 
Ephesians6:15 makasunga patsoka dzenyu kugadzirwa kweVhangeri yorugare; 
Ephesians6:16 pamusoro paizvozvi makatora nhoo huru yokutenda, yamungagona kudzima nayo miseve yose yomoto yowakaipa." 
Ephesians6:17 Torai ngowani yoruponeso, nomunondo woMweya, iro shoko raMwari." 
Ephesians6:18 Munyengetere nguva dzose nokunyengetera kwose nokukumbira muMweya, muchirinda pazvinhu izvi nokutsunga kwose nokukumbirira vatsvene vose," 
Ephesians6:19 neniwo, kuti ndipiwe shoko kuti ndidudzire ndisingatyi zvakavanzika zveVhangeri," 
Ephesians6:20 yandiri nhume yayo yakasungwa nengetani; kuti ndizvitaure ndisingatyi, sezvandinofanira kutaura." 
Ephesians6:21 Zvino kuti muzivewo zvangu, kuti ndakadiniko, Tikiko, hama inodikanwa, nomushumiri akatendeka muna Ishe, uchakuzivisai zvose;" 
Ephesians6:22 ndakamutuwa kwamuri neshoko iri, kuti muzive zvinhu zvedu, anyaradze mwoyo yenyu." 
Ephesians6:23 Rugare ngaruve nehama, norudo pamwechete nokutenda, zvinobva kuna Mwari, Baba, naIshe Jesu Kristu." 
Ephesians6:24 Nyasha ngadzive navose vanoda Ishe wedu, Jesu Kristu, norudo rusingaori." 
Philippians1:1 Pauro naTimoti, varanda vaKristu Jesu, kuvatsvene vose muna Kristu Jesu, vari muFiripi, navatariri navaranda vesangano." 
Philippians1:2 Nyasha ngadzive nemi, norugare runobva kuna Mwari, Baba vedu, naIshe Jesu Kristu." 
Philippians1:3 Ndinovonga Mwari wangu nguva imwe neimwe kana ndichikufungai," 
Philippians1:4 ndichikumbira nomufaro nguva dzose pakukumbira kwangu kwose, pamusoro penyu mose" 
Philippians1:5 nokuda kwokusangana kwenyu paVhangeri kubva pazuva rokutanga kusvikira zvino; 
Philippians1:6 ndichiziva chinhu ichi, kuti iye akatanga basa rakanaka mukati menyu, acharipedzisa kusvikira pazuva raKristu Jesu;" 
Philippians1:7 sezvazvakanaka kwandiri kuti ndifunge saizvozvo pamusoro penyu mose, zvandinokurangarirai mumwoyo mangu, nokuti pakusungwa kwangu napakudavirira nokusimbisa Vhangeri, imi makagoverwa nyasha pamwechete neni." 
Philippians1:8 Nokuti Mwari chapupu changu kuti ndinokushuvai mose zvikuru netsitsi dzaKristu Jesu. 
Philippians1:9 Ndizvo zvandinonyengetera, kuti rudo rwenyu rurambe ruchingowanda pakuziva nokunzwisisa kwose;" 
Philippians1:10 kuti muedze muzive kuti zvinhu zvakanaka ndezvipi, kuti muve vakarurama, vasina mhosva, kusvikira pazuva raKristu;" 
Philippians1:11 muzere nechibereko chokururama, chinouya naJesu Kristu, kuti ave nokubwinya nokurumbidzwa." 
Philippians1:12 Zvino ndinoda kuti muzive, hama dzangu, kuti izvo zvakandiwira zvakatofambisa Vhangeri;" 
Philippians1:13 nokudaro kuti kusungwa kwangu kwakazikanwa muimba yashe yose, nokuna vamwe vose kuti kuri muna Kristu." 
Philippians1:14 Nehama zhinji muna Ishe, dzakasimbiswa nokusungwa kwangu, vonyanya kutsunga kuparidza shoko raMwari vasingatyi." 
Philippians1:15 Vamwe havo vanoparidza Kristu negodo negakava, vamwe nomwoyo wakanaka;" 
Philippians1:16 vamwe havo vanoita norudo, vachiziva kuti ndakagadzwa kuti ndidavirire Vhangeri." 
Philippians1:17 Asi vamwe vanoparidza Kristu nenharo, vasingaiti nomwoyo wakachena, vachiti vawedzere nhamo pakusungwa kwangu." 
Philippians1:18 Zvinei hazvo? Hazvina hazvo, asi kuti Kristu anoparidzwa hake nenzira dzose, kana namanomano, kana nechokwadi; ndinofara nazvo, uye ndichasifara hangu nazvo." 
Philippians1:19 Nokuti ndinoziva kuti nokuda kwokukumbira kwenyu nokusimbiswa kwoMweya waJesu Kristu, izvozvi zvichava kuponeswa kwangu," 
Philippians1:20 zvandinotarira zvikuru netariro, kuti handinganyadziswi pachinhu chimwe; asi kuti zvino, sapanguva dzose, nokusatya kwangu kwose Kristu achakudzwa mumuviri wangu, kana noupenyu, kana nokufa." 
Philippians1:21 Nokuti kwandiri kurarama ndiKristu, kufa kupfuma." 
Philippians1:22 Zvino kana ndichirarama panyama, izvo zvichandipa zvibereko zvokubata kwangu; handizivi chandichasanangura;" 
Philippians1:23 zvino ndinomanikidzwa nezvinhu zviviri: ndinoda kubva, kuti ndive naKristu, nokuti ndizvo zvinopfuura nokunaka;" 
Philippians1:24 asi nokuda kwenyu zvakanaka kuti ndigare panyama. 
Philippians1:25 Zvino ndichitenda chinhu ichi, ndinoziva kuti ndichagara, ndicharamba ndigere nemi mose, kuti mupfuurire mberi, mufare pakutenda;" 
Philippians1:26 kuti muzvirumbidze zvikuru muna Kristu Jesu pamusoro pangu nokuda kwokudzokera kwangu kwamuri. 
Philippians1:27 Asi fambai bedzi zvakafanira Vhangeri yaKristu; kuti kunyangwe ndikauya ndikakuonai, kunyangwe ndisipo, ndinzwe pamusoro penyu kuti mumire nesimba nomweya mumwe, nomwoyo mumwe, muchirwira kutenda kweVhangeri;" 
Philippians1:28 musingatyiswi pachinhu chimwe navanorwa nemi. Ndizvo zvichava chiratidzo chokuparadzwa kwavari, asi kwamuri chokuponeswa; chinhu ichi chinobva kuna Mwari." 
Philippians1:29 Nokuti nokuda kwaKristu imi makatenderwa kuti murege kutenda kwaari bedzi, asi kuti mutambudzikewo nokuda kwake;" 
Philippians1:30 imi muchirwawo nokurwa uku kwamakaona kwandiri, kwamunonzwa kuti ndinorwa nazvino." 
Philippians2:1 Zvino kana kuvaraidzwa kuripo kuna Kristu, kana kunyaradza kworudo, kana kuyanana kwoMweya, kana mwoyo munyoro nokunzwira tsitsi," 
Philippians2:2 zadzisai mufaro wangu, muve nokufunga kumwe, muchiva norudo rumwe, nomweya mumwe, nendangariro imwe," 
Philippians2:3 musingaiti chinhu nenharo, kana nokuzvikudza, asi mumwe nomumwe ngaati nomwoyo unozvininipisa, vamwe vanomupfuura iye pakunaka;" 
Philippians2:4 mumwe nomumwe ngaarege kutarira zvake, asi ngaatarire vamwewo." 
Philippians2:5 Ivai nomwoyo uyo, wakanga uri muna Kristu Jesu;" 
Philippians2:6 iye, kunyangwe akanga akafanana naMwari, haana kuti kuenzana naMwari ndochinhu chinofanira kubatisiswa;" 
Philippians2:7 asi wakazvidurura iye, akazviita muranda, akafanana navanhu;" 
Philippians2:8 akati awanikwa nomufananidzo womunhu, akazvininipisa, akateerera kusvikira parufu, irwo rufu rwomuchinjikwa." 
Philippians2:9 Saka Mwari akamukudza zvikuru, akamupa zita rinopfuura mazita ose;" 
Philippians2:10 kuti muzita raJesu mabvi ose apfugame, avari kudenga navari panyika, navari pasi penyika," 
Philippians2:11 kuti ndimi dzose dzibvumire dziti, Jesu Kristu ndiye Ishe, kuti Mwari, Baba, arumbidzwe." 
Philippians2:12 Naizvozvo, vadikanwi vangu, sezvamakateerera nguva dzose, ndisati ndiripo bedzi, asi zvikuru zvino kana ndisipo, pedzisai kuponeswa kwenyu nokutya nokudedera;" 
Philippians2:13 nokuti ndiye Mwari anoita mukati menyu kuda nokuita nokuda kwake kwakanaka. 
Philippians2:14 Itai zvose musinganyunyuti musina nharo; 
Philippians2:15 kuti muve vanhu vasina chavangapomerwa, navasina kusarurama, vana vaMwari vasina mhosva pakati porudzi rwakakombama, rwakatsauka, rwamunoonekwa pakati parwo sezviedza panyika;" 
Philippians2:16 makabatisisa shoko roupenyu, kuti ndive nechandingazvirumbidza nacho nezuva raKristu, ndizive kuti handina kumhanya pasina, kana kubata basa pasina." 
Philippians2:17 Kunyangwe ndikadururwa pamusoro pechibayiro nokushumira kwokutenda kwenyu, ndinofara nokufarisisa nemi mose." 
Philippians2:18 Nokuda kwaizvozvo nemiwo mufare nokufarisisa neni. 
Philippians2:19 Muna Ishe Jesu ndinoti ndichakurumidza kutuma Timoti kwamuri, kuti neni ndifare kana ndanzwa zvenyu." 
Philippians2:20 Nokuti handina mumwe munhu ano mwoyo wakaita sowake, achava nehanya kwazvo nezvenyu." 
Philippians2:21 Nokuti vose vanozvitsvakira zvavo, zvisati zviri zvaKristu Jesu." 
Philippians2:22 Asi munoziva kutendeka kwake, kuti akabata pamwechete neni paVhangeri, somwana anobatira baba vake." 
Philippians2:23 Zvino ndiye wandinoti ndichatuma kwamuri pakarepo, kana ndaona kuti zvangu zvakadini;" 
Philippians2:24 asi ndinotenda muna Ishe kuti neniwo ndimene ndichakurumidza kuuya. 
Philippians2:25 Asi ndakati ndinofanira kutuma kwamuri Epafirodhito, hama yangu, nomubatsiri wangu pamabasa napakurwa, nhume yenyu nomushumiri wangu pakushayiwa kwangu;" 
Philippians2:26 zvaakanga achikushuvai zvikuru imi mose, akatambudzika kwazvo, nokuti imi makanga manzwa kuti anorwara." 
Philippians2:27 Nokuti akanga achirwara kwazvo, ari pakufa; asi Mwari wakamunzwira tsitsi; asati ari iye bedzi, asi neniwo, kuti ini ndirege kuwedzerwa nhamo pamusoro penhamo." 
Philippians2:28 Naizvozvo ndakashingaira kumutuma kwamuri, kuti mumuone, mufarezve, neni ndirege kuva nenhamo." 
Philippians2:29 Naizvozvo mumugamuchire muna Ishe nomufaro wose, uye mukudze vakadai;" 
Philippians2:30 nokuti nokuda kwebasa raKristu akanga oda kufa, akasarangarira upenyu hwake, achida kukwanisa pamakanga musingagoni kundishumira imi." 
Philippians3:1 Pakupedzisira, hama dzangu, farai muna Ishe. Ini handinetswi nokukunyoreraizve zvinhu zviya, asi zvinokusimbisai imi." 
Philippians3:2 Ityai imbwa, ityai vabati vakaipa, ityai vokucheka;" 
Philippians3:3 nokuti isu tiri vokudzingiswa, tinonamata noMweya waMwari, tinozvirumbidza muna Kristu Jesu, tisingavimbi nenyama," 
Philippians3:4 kunyangwe ini hangu ndingavimba nenyama; kana kuno mumwe munhu anoti ndinovimba nenyama, zvikuru ini." 
Philippians3:5 Ndakadzingiswa nomusi worusere, ndiri worudzi rwaVaIsiraeri veimba yaBhenjamini, muHebheru wavaHebheru; pamurairo ndiri muFarisi;" 
Philippians3:6 pakushingaira kwangu, ndaitambudza sangano; pakururama kunorehwa nomurairo ndakanga ndisina chandingapomerwa." 
Philippians3:7 Asi izvozvo, zvaiva pfuma kwandiri, ndakati ndiko kurashikirwa hako nokuda kwaKristu." 
Philippians3:8 Hongu, zvirokwazvo, ndinototi zvinhu zvose kurashikirwa hako nokuda kwokunaka kwokuziva Kristu Jesu, Ishe wangu, wandakarasikirwa nezvinhu zvose nokuda kwake, ndikazviedza marara, kuti ndiwane Kristu;" 
Philippians3:9 ndiwanikwe maari, ndisina kururama kwangu kuri kwomurairo, asi kuri kwokutenda kuna Kristu, ndiko kururama kunobva kuna Mwari nenzira yokutenda;" 
Philippians3:10 kuti ndimuzive iye, nesimba rokumuka kwake, nokusangana naye pamatambudziko ake, ndifanane naye pakufa kwake;" 
Philippians3:11 kuti zvimwe ndisvike pakumuka kwavakafa. 
Philippians3:12 Handiti ndatochiwana, kana ndatokwaniswa, asi ndinoshingairirako, kuti zvimwe ndichibate, icho Kristu Jesu chaakambondibatira." 
Philippians3:13 Hama dzangu, ini handiti ndatochibata, asi ndinoita chinhu chimwe: ndinokanganwa zviri shure, ndichinanavira kune zviri mberi," 
Philippians3:14 ndinoshingairira kunharidzano, kuti ndipiwe mubairo wokudana kwaMwari kunobva kudenga, muna Kristu Jesu." 
Philippians3:15 Naizvozvo isu tose, takakura, ngative nomwoyo wakadaro; kana imi muno mumwe mwoyo, Mwari uchakuratidzai naizvozvowo." 
Philippians3:16 Asi, ngatirambe tichifamba bedzi nomurangariro iwoyu watasvika nawo patasvika." 
Philippians3:17 Hama dzangu, ivai vateveri vangu mose; natsai kurarira avo vanofamba saizvozvo sezvatakakutungamirirai isu." 
Philippians3:18 Nokuti vazhinji, vandakakuudzai zvizhinji, nazvino ndinokuudzaiwo nokuchema, vanofamba vari vavengi vomuchinjikwa waKristu;" 
Philippians3:19 kuguma kwavo ndiko kuparadzwa, mwari wavo idumbu ravo, vanozvirumbidza pamusoro pezvinonyadzisa zvavo, vanofunga zvenyika." 
Philippians3:20 Nokuti nyika yedu iri kudenga, uko kwatakatarira kuuya kwoMuponesi Ishe Jesu Kristu;" 
Philippians3:21 uyo achavandudza muviri wokuninipiswa kwedu, kuti ufanane nomuviri wokubwinya kwake, nesimba iro raanogonawo naro kuzviisira zvose pasi pake." 
Philippians4:1 Naizvozvo, hama dzangu, vadikani vandinoshuva kwazvo, mufaro wangu, nekorona yangu, mirai nesimba saizvozvo muna Ishe, vadikani." 
Philippians4:2 Ndinokumbira zvikuru Yuodhia, ndinokumbira zvikuru Sinitike, kuti vave nomwoyo mumwe muna Ishe." 
Philippians4:3 Hongu, newewo, shamwari yangu yazvokwadi pabasa, ndinokumbira kwauri kuti ubatsire vanhukadzi ava, nokuti vakabatirana neni paVhangeri, pamwechete naKiremenzi, navamwe vakabata basa pamwechete neni, mazita avo ari mubhuku roupenyu." 
Philippians4:4 Farai muna Ishe nguva dzose; ndichapamhidzazve: Farai. 
Philippians4:5 Unyoro hwenyu ngahuzikanwe navanhu vose. Ishe ari pedyo. 
Philippians4:6 Musafunganya pamusoro pechinhu; asi pazvinhu zvose, mikumbiro yenyu ngaiziviswe Mwari nokunyengetera nokukumbira, pamwechete nokuvonga." 
Philippians4:7 Zvino rugare rwaMwari runopfuura kunzwisisa kwose, rucharinda mwoyo yenyu nemifungo yenyu muna Kristu Jesu." 
Philippians4:8 Pakupedzisira, hama dzangu, zvose zvechokwadi, zvose zvinokudzwa, zvose zvakarurama, zvose zvakachena, zvose zvinodikanwa, zvose zvinorumbidzwa, kana kunaka kupi nokupi, kana chingarumbidzwe chipi nechipi, fungisisai izvozvo." 
Philippians4:9 Zvinhu izvo zvamakadzidza, nezvamakapiwa, nezvamakanzwa, nezvamakaona kwandiri, itai izvozvo; Mwari worugare ngaave nemi." 
Philippians4:10 Ndakafara zvikuru muna Ishe, nokuti zvino makapepukazve mukandirangarira; makanga marangarira henyu, asi makashayiwa nguva." 
Philippians4:11 Handirevi izvozvi nokuti ndinoshayiwa; nokuti ini ndakadzidza kutenda nezvose zvandinazvo. 
Philippians4:12 Ndinoziva urombo, ndinozivawo kuva nezvakawanda; pachinhu chipi nechipi napazvinhu zvose ndakadzidziswa kuti ndizive kuguta nokunzwa nzara, kuva nezvizhinji nokushayiwa." 
Philippians4:13 Ndingaita zvose naiye anondipa simba. 
Philippians4:14 Kunyangwe zvakadaro, makaita zvakanaka zvamakasangana neni pakutambudzika kwangu." 
Philippians4:15 Munozivawo, imi VaFiripi, kuti pakutanga kweVhangeri, ndichibva Masedhonia, pakanga pasina sangano rimwe rakasangana neni pashoko rokupa nokugamuchira, asi imi moga;" 
Philippians4:16 nokuti napaTesaronika makanditumira kamwe, norwechipirizve, pakushayiwa kwangu." 
Philippians4:17 Handirevi kudaro kuti nditsvake chipo, asi ndinotsvaka chibereko chamunozofumiswa nacho." 
Philippians4:18 Zvino ndava nezvose, ndapfumiswa; ndaguta, ndagamuchira kuna Epafirodhito izvo, zvinobva kwamuri, zvakaita sohwema hunonhuwira, nechibayiro chakafanira, chinofadza Mwari." 
Philippians4:19 Zvino Mwari wangu achazadzisa kushayiwa kwenyu kwose papfuma yake, mukubwinya, muna Kristu Jesu." 
Philippians4:20 Zvino Mwari, Baba vedu, ngaave nokubwinya nokusingaperi–peri. Ameni." 
Philippians4:21 Ndikwazisirei mutsvene mumwe nomumwe muna Kristu Jesu. Hama dzineni dzinokukwazisai. 
Philippians4:22 Vatsvene vose vanokukwazisai, zvikuru avo veimba yaKesari." 
Philippians4:23 Nyasha dzaIshe Jesu Kristu ngadzive nomweya wenyu. 
Colossians1:1 Pauro, mupostori waKristu Jesu nokuda kwaMwari, naTimoti, hama yedu," 
Colossians1:2 kuvatsvene nehama dzakatendeka muna Kristu vari paKorose: Nyasha ngadzive nemi, norugare zvinobva kuna Mwari; Baba vedu." 
Colossians1:3 Tinovonga Mwari, Baba vaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, nguva dzose kana tichikunyengetererai," 
Colossians1:4 zvatakanzwa zvokutenda kwenyu muna Kristu Jesu, norudo rwamunarwo kuvatsvene vose," 
Colossians1:5 pamusoro petariro yamakachengeterwa kudenga, yamakanzwa kare pashoko rechokwadi reVhangeri;" 
Colossians1:6 iyo yakasvika kwamuri, sezvayakasvika panyika yosewo; ichibereka zvibereko, ichikura, sezvainoita kwamuriwo, kubvira pazuva ramakanzwa nokuziva kwazvo nyasha dzaMwari muchokwadi;" 
Colossians1:7 sezvamakadzidza kuna Epafirasi, muranda pamwechete nesu, anodikanwa, mushumiri akatendeka waKristu nokuda kwenyu," 
Colossians1:8 iye akatiudzawo zvorudo rwenyu muMweya. 
Colossians1:9 Saka nesuwo, kubvira pazuva ratakanzwa, hatiregi kukunyengetererai, nokukumbira kuti muzadziswe nokuziva kwazvo kuda kwake, pakuchenjera nokunzwisisa kwose kwomweya;" 
Colossians1:10 kuti mufambe sezvinofanira Ishe, muchimufadza pazvose, muchibereka zvibereko pamabasa ose akanaka, muchikura pakuziva Mwari kwazvo;" 
Colossians1:11 muchisimbiswa nesimba rose, nesimba rokubwinya kwake, muve nomwoyo murefu, nomufaro;" 
Colossians1:12 muvonge Baba, vakatikwanisa kuti tipiwe nhaka yavatsvene muchiedza;" 
Colossians1:13 vakatisunungura pasimba rerima, vakatiisa muushe hwoMwanakomana worudo rwavo;" 
Colossians1:14 watine dzikinuro maari, ndiko kukanganwirwa kwezvivi zvedu." 
Colossians1:15 Ndiye mufananidzo waMwari usingaonekwi, dangwe rezvisikwa zvose;" 
Colossians1:16 nokuti maari zvinhu zvose zvakasikwa, zviri kudenga napanyika, zvinoonekwa nezvisingaonekwi, kana zviri zvigaro zvoushe, kana ushe, kana vabati, kana masimba; zvinhu zvose zvakasikwa naye, zviripo nokuda kwake." 
Colossians1:17 Ndiye anotangira zvose, zvose zvakabatana maari." 
Colossians1:18 Ndiye musoro womuviri, ndiyo sangano; ndiye wokutanga, dangwe ravakamuka kuvakafa; kuti iye ave mukuru pazvinhu zvose." 
Colossians1:19 Nokuti Baba vakafara nazvo, kuti kuzara kwose kugare maari," 
Colossians1:20 kuti naye ayananise zvinhu zvose kwaari, amboita rugare neropa rake rakaparadzirwa romuchinjikwa naiye, kunyangwe zviri panyika, kunyangwe zviri kudenga." 
Colossians1:21 Nemiwo, kare maiva vaeni navavengi pakufunga kwenyu pamabasa enyu akaipa," 
Colossians1:22 asi zvino wakakuyananisai nomuviri wenyama yake, nokufa kwake, kuti akuisei pamberi pake muri vatsvene, musina mhosva, musingapomerwi," 
Colossians1:23 kana muchingorambira pakutenda makateyiwa, mumire makasimba, musingabviswi patariro yeVhangeri yamakanzwa, yakaparidzirwa zvisikwa zvose pasi pokudenga; iyo Vhangeri yandakaitwa mushumiri wayo, ini Pauro." 
Colossians1:24 Zvino ndinofara pakutambudzika kwangu nokuda kwenyu, ndichizadzisa panyama yangu zvakasara pamatambudziko aKristu, nokuda kwomuviri wake, iro sangano;" 
Colossians1:25 iro randakaitwa mushumiri waro sezvandakagoverwa naMwari pamusoro penyu, kuti ndizadzise shoko raMwari;" 
Colossians1:26 ndicho chakavanzika, chakanga chakafukidzwa kubvira pakutanga kwenguva nendudzi, asi zvino chakaratidzwa vatsvene vake;" 
Colossians1:27 kuna ivo Mwari waakada kuvazivisa upfumi hwokubwinya kwechakavanzika ichochi pakati pavahedheni, chokuti, Kristu mukati menyu, tariro yokubwinya;" 
Colossians1:28 iye watinoparidza isu, tichirayira munhu mumwe nomumwe, tichidzidzisa munhu mumwe nomumwe nouchenjeri hwose, kuti tiise munhu mumwe nomumwe akakwana muna Kristu;" 
Colossians1:29 ndizvo zvandinobatirawo, ndichirwa, zvichiitwa nokubata kwake kunobata mukati mangu nesimba." 
Colossians2:1 Nokuti ndinoda kuti muzive kurwa kukuru kwandinako pamusoro penyu, navari paRaodhikia, navose vasina kumboona chiso changu panyama;" 
Colossians2:2 kuti mwoyo yavo isimbiswe, vasunganidzwe murudo, vave nepfuma yose yokunzwisisa kwakakwana, kuti vazive kwazvo chakavanzika chaMwari, iye Kristu;" 
Colossians2:3 maari pfuma yose youchenjeri nokuziva yakachengetwa. 
Colossians2:4 Ndinoreva izvi, kuti kurege kuva nomunhu anokurashai namashoko anonyengera." 
Colossians2:5 Nokuti kunyangwe ndisipo panyama, ndiripo nemi pamweya, ndinofara ndichiona kunzwana kwenyu, nokusimba kwokutenda kwenyu muna Kristu." 
Colossians2:6 Naizvozvo sezvamakagamuchira Kristu Jesu, Ishe, fambai maari," 
Colossians2:7 mune midzi yenyu nokuvakwa kwenyu maari, makasimbiswa pakutenda, sezvamakadzidziswa, muchinyanya kuvonga." 
Colossians2:8 Chenjerai, kuti murege kutapwa nomunhu nouchenjeri, nokunyengera kusina maturo, achitevera tsika dzavanhu nezvokuvamba zvenyika, asingateveri Kristu." 
Colossians2:9 Nokuti kuzara kwohuMwari kunogara maari pamuviri. 
Colossians2:10 Maari nemiwo makazadzwa, iye musoro wavabati vose namasimba;" 
Colossians2:11 iye wamakadzingiswawo maari nokudzingiswa kusingaitwi namaoko, muviri wenyama uchibviswa, nokudzingiswa kuri kwaKristu;" 
Colossians2:12 makavigwa pamwechete naye pakubhabhatidzwa, pamakamutswawo pamwechete naye nokutenda kwenyu simba raMwari akamumutsa kuvakafa." 
Colossians2:13 Nemi, imi makanga makafa pakudarika kwenyu napakusadzingiswa kwenyama yenyu, wakakupai upenyu pamwechete naye, akatikanganwira kudarika kwedu kwose," 
Colossians2:14 akadzima rugwaro rwakanga ruchirwa nesu pazvirevo zvarwo, ruchipesana nesu; akarubvisa irwo pakati pedu, akarurovera pamuchinjikwa;" 
Colossians2:15 akaparadza vabati namasimba, akavabudisa pachena, akavakunda mauri." 
Colossians2:16 Naizvozvo munhu ngaarege kuvapo anokutongai pazvokudya, kana zvokunwa, kana nokuda kwomusi womutambo, kana pakugara kwomwedzi, kana paSabata;" 
Colossians2:17 izvi mumvuri wezvichauya; asi muviri ndowaKristu. 
Colossians2:18 Munhu ngaarege kuvapo anokutorerai mubairo wenyu namawune, nokuzvininipisa nokunamata vatumwa, achivimba nezvaakaona, achizvikudza pasina nokufunga kwenyama," 
Colossians2:19 asingabatisisi Musoro, uyo, maari muviri wose unosimbiswa nokusunganidzwa nezvisungo namarunda, ndokukura nokukurisa kwaMwari." 
Colossians2:20 Zvino kana makafa pamwechete naKristu kunezvokuvamba zvenyika, munozviisireiko pasi pemirairo, somugere munyika?" 
Colossians2:21 Mirairo inoti, “Usabata,” “Usaravira,” “Usagunzva.”" 
Colossians2:22 Izvi zvose zvinofanira kuparadzwa kana zvobatwa nazvo; muchitevera mirairo nedzidziso dzavanhu? 
Colossians2:23 Zvinhu zvakadai zvakaita sezvino uchenjeri, pakunamata Mwari nokuda kwavo, nokuzvininipisa, nokutambudza muviri; asi hazvina simba rokukunda kuchiva kwenyama." 
Colossians3:1 Naizvozvo, kana makamutswa pamwechete naKristu, tsvakai zviri kumusoro, uko kuna Kristu, agere kurudyi rwaMwari." 
Colossians3:2 Fungai zviri kumusoro, musafunga zviri pasi." 
Colossians3:3 Nokuti makafa, upenyu hwenyu hwakavigwa pamwechete naKristu muna Mwari." 
Colossians3:4 Kana Kristu, iye upenyu hwedu, achionekwa, nemiwo muchaonekwa pamwechete naye pakubwinya." 
Colossians3:5 Naizvozvo urayai mitezo yenyu iri panyika, inoti: Upombwe, netsvina, nokushumba, nokuda zvakaipa, nokuchiva, ndiko kunamata zvifananidzo." 
Colossians3:6 Nokuda kwaizvozvi kutsamwa kwaMwari kunouya pamusoro pavana vokusateerera; 
Colossians3:7 nemiwo maifamba mazviri kare, maigara muzvinhu izvi." 
Colossians3:8 Asi zvino, imiwo, bvisai izvi zvose, zvinoti: Hasha, nokutsamwa, nokuvenga, nokutuka, nokutaura zvinonyadzisa nomuromo wenyu." 
Colossians3:9 Regai kureverana nhema, zvamakabvisa munhu wekare namabasa ake," 
Colossians3:10 mukafuka munhu mutsva, anovandudzwa pakuziva, afanane nowakamusika;" 
Colossians3:11 apo hapana muGiriki nomuJudha, akadzingiswa kana kusadzingiswa, mutorwa nomuSitia, musungwa nowakasununguka; asi Kristu ndiye zvose uye uri muna vose." 
Colossians3:12 Naizvozvo, savatsanangurwa vaMwari, vatsvene navanodikanwa, fukai mwoyo une tsitsi, nomwoyo munyoro, nokusazvikudza, nounyoro, nomwoyo murefu;" 
Colossians3:13 muitirane mwoyo murefu, muchikanganwirana, kana munhu ane mhosva nomumwe; Ishe sezvaakakukanganwirai, muite saizvozvo nemiwo." 
Colossians3:14 Zvino pamusoro pezvinhu izvi zvose fukai rudo, ndicho chisungo chinokwanisa." 
Colossians3:15 Norugare rwaKristu ngaruteme zvirevo mumwoyo yenyu, ndirwo rwamakadanirwawo mumuviri mumwe; ivai nokuvonga." 
Colossians3:16 Shoko raKristu ngarigare mukati menyu riwande; nokuchenjera kwose mudzidzisane, nokurayirana namapisarema, nenziyo, nezviimbo zvomweya, muimbire Mwari nenyasha mumwoyo menyu;" 
Colossians3:17 uye zvose zvamunoita, kana zviri zveshoko kana basa, itai zvose nezita raIshe Jesu, muchivonga Mwari Baba naye." 
Colossians3:18 Vakadzi, muzviise pasi pavarume venyu, sezvazvakafanira muna Ishe." 
Colossians3:19 Varume, idai vakadzi venyu, regai kuva nehasha navo." 
Colossians3:20 Vana, teererai vabereki venyu pazvinhu zvose, nokuti ndizvo zvakanaka muna Ishe." 
Colossians3:21 Madzibaba, regai kunetsa vana venyu, kuti varege kuora mwoyo." 
Colossians3:22 Varanda, teererai pazvinhu zvose vatenzi venyu panyama; regai kubata basa pamberi pameso avo, savafadzi vavanhu, asi nomwoyo wakarurama muchitya Ishe." 
Colossians3:23 Zvose zvamunoita, muzviite nomwoyo wose, sokuna Ishe, musingaitiri vanhu," 
Colossians3:24 muchiziva kuti muchapiwa naIshe mubairo wenhaka; nokuti munoshandira Ishe Kristu. 
Colossians3:25 Nokuti anoita zvisakarurama, achapiwa zvisakarurama zvaakaita; hazvizi zvinoonekwa zvomunhu zvinotendwa." 
Colossians4:1 Madzishe, itirai varanda venyu zvakarurama, zvakaringana; muzive kuti nemiwo muna Ishe kudenga." 
Colossians4:2 Tsungirirai pakunyengetera, murinde pahuri nokuvonga;" 
Colossians4:3 mutinyengeterere nesuwo kamwe, kuti Mwari atizarurire musuwo weshoko, titaure chakavanzika chaKristu, chandakasungirwa icho;" 
Colossians4:4 kuti ndichiratidze, sezvandinofanira kutaura." 
Colossians4:5 Fambai nokuchenjera kuna vari kunze, muchingwarira nguva yenyu." 
Colossians4:6 Kutaura kwenyu ngakuve nenyasha nguva dzose, kwakarungwa nomunyu, kuti muzive kupindura mumwe nomumwe sezvamunofanira kuita." 
Colossians4:7 Muchaziviswa zvangu zvose naTikiko, hama inodikanwa, mushumiri akatendeka, nomuranda pamwechete neni muna Ishe." 
Colossians4:8 Ndakamutuma iye kwamuri nemhaka iyi, kuti muzive zvedu, anyaradze mwoyo yenyu;" 
Colossians4:9 pamwechete naOnesimo, hama yakatendeka, inodikanwa, mumwe wokwenyu. Ivo vachakuzivisai zvose zvapano." 
Colossians4:10 Arisitakusi, musungwa pamwechete neni, anokukwazisai, naMako, hama yaBhanabhasi, mumugamuchire;" 
Colossians4:11 naJesu, anonzi Jusuto, vari vokudzingiswa; ndivava bedzi vanobata neni paushe hwaMwari, ivo vakandinyaradza." 
Colossians4:12 Epafirasi, mumwe wokwenyu, muranda waKristu Jesu, anokukwazisai, achirwa nguva dzose pakunyengetera nokuda kwenyu, kuti mumire makakwana, muchiziva kwazvo kuda kwose kwaMwari." 
Colossians4:13 Nokuti ndinomupupurira, kuti anotambudzika zvikuru nokuda kwenyu, naveRaodhikia, naveHerapori." 
Colossians4:14 Ruka, chiremba hwehutano inodikanwa, naDhemasi, vanokukwazisai." 
Colossians4:15 Ndikwazisirei hama dziri Raodhikia, naNimifa, nesangano riri mumba mavo." 
Colossians4:16 Kana tsamba iyi yarawa pakati penyu, ngairawewo musangano ravaRaodhikia; imiwo murave tsamba inobva Raodhikia." 
Colossians4:17 Udzai Arikipo muti, “Tarira basa rawakapiwa naIshe, kuti uripedzise kwazvo.”" 
Colossians4:18 Ndiko kukwazisa kwangu, ini Pauro, noruoko rwangu. Rangarirai kusungwa kwangu. Nyasha ngadzive nemi." 
1Thessalonians1:1 Pauro, naSirivhano, naTimoti, kuchechi yaVaTesaronika, iri muna Mwari Baba, naIshe Jesu Kristu: Nyasha ngadzive nemi norugare." 
1Thessalonians1:2 Tinovonga Mwari nguva dzose nokuda kwenyu mose, tichikurangarirai pakunyengetera kwedu;" 
1Thessalonians1:3 tichiramba tichirangarira basa renyu rinobva pakutenda, nokutamburira vamwe kunobva parudo, nokutsungirira kunobva patariro muna Ishe wedu, Jesu Kristu, pamberi paMwari, Baba vedu;" 
1Thessalonians1:4 tinoziva, hama dzinodikanwa naMwari, kusanangurwa kwenyu." 
1Thessalonians1:5 Nokuti Vhangeri yedu haina kuuya kwamuri neshoko bedzi, asi nesimbawo, nomuMweya Mutsvene, nokuziva kwazvo; sezvamunoziva kuti takanga takadini pakati penyu nokuda kwenyu." 
1Thessalonians1:6 Nemi makava vateveri vedu navaIshe, zvamakagamuchira Shoko mumatambudziko mazhinji, nomufaro woMweya Mutsvene;" 
1Thessalonians1:7 naizvozvo makatungamirira vose vanotenda muMasedhonia neAkaia. 
1Thessalonians1:8 Nokuti shoko raIshe, rakabva kwamuri, rakanzwika, kusati kuri kuMasedhonia neAkaia bedzi, asi kutenda kwenyu kuna Mwari kwakasvika kwose; naizvozvo hatifaniri kutaura chinhu." 
1Thessalonians1:9 Nokuti ivo vamene vanoparidza kupinda kwedu kwamuri, kuti kwakanga kwakadini; uye, kuti makatendeukira kuna Mwari, muchibva pazvifananidzo, kuti mubatire Mwari mupenyu wachokwadi," 
1Thessalonians1:10 nokumirira Mwanakomana wake pakubva kwake kudenga, iye waakamutsa kuvakafa, ndiye Jesu anotisunungura pakutsamwa kunouya." 
1Thessalonians2:1 Nokuti nemi, hama dzangu, munoziva kuti kupinda kwedu kwamuri hakuna kuva pasina." 
1Thessalonians2:2 Asi takati tatambudzika nokuitirwa zvakaipa muFiripi, sezvamunoziva, takatsunga muna Mwari wedu, tikakuparidzirai Vhangeri yaMwari pakati pokudziviswa kukuru." 
1Thessalonians2:3 Nokuti kurayira kwedu hakuna kubva pakurashika, kana pakufunga kwakaipa, kana pakunyengera;" 
1Thessalonians2:4 asi sezvatakatendiwa naMwari, kuti tipiwe Vhangeri, ndizvo zvatinotaura; tisingaiti kuti tifadze vanhu, asi Mwari anoedza mwoyo yedu." 
1Thessalonians2:5 Nokuti, sezvamunoziva, hatina kutongoreva namashoko okubata kumeso, kana namanomano okukarira pfuma, Mwari chapupu;" 
1Thessalonians2:6 tisingatsvaki kukudzwa navanhu kana nemi, kana navamwe, kunyangwe taigona kukuremedzai, zvatiri vapostori VaKristu." 
1Thessalonians2:7 Asi takanga tiri vanyoro pakati penyu, somureri kana achivaraidza vana vake;" 
1Thessalonians2:8 saizvozvo takakushuvai kwazvo, tikati zvakanaka kuti tirege kugovana nemi Vhangeri yaMwari bedzi, asi kunyangwe nemweya yeduwo, nokuti makanga madikanwa nesu kwazvo." 
1Thessalonians2:9 Nokuti, hama dzangu, munorangarira kutambudzika nokurwa kwedu; taibata basa usiku namasikati, kuti tirege kuremedza mumwe wenyu, tikakuparidzirai Vhangeri yaMwari." 
1Thessalonians2:10 Imi muri zvapupu, naMwariwo, kuti taifamba noutsvene nokururama, tisina chatingapomerwa kwamuri, imi vanotenda." 
1Thessalonians2:11 Sezvamunoziva kuti takaita nemi, mumwe nomumwe wenyu, sababa vanoita navana vavo," 
1Thessalonians2:12 tichikurairai, tichikusimbisai, tichikupupurirai, kuti mufambe zvakafanira Mwari, iye anokudanirai kuushe hwake nokubwinya kwake." 
1Thessalonians2:13 Saka isuwo tinoramba tichivonga Mwari, kuti panguva yamakagamuchira shoko, iro shoko raMwari, ramakanzwa kwatiri, hamuna kurigamuchira seshoko ravanhu, asi seshoko raMwari, (riri iro zvirokwazvo) rinobatawo mukati menyu, imi munotenda." 
1Thessalonians2:14 Nokuti imi, hama dzangu, makava vateveri veChechi yaMwari riri muJudhiya muna Kristu Jesu; nokuti nemiwo makatambudzwa saizvozvo novekwenyu, sezvavakatambudzwa ivo naVaJudha." 
1Thessalonians2:15 Ndivo vakauraya Ishe Jesu navaPorofita, vakatidzinga isu, vasingafadzi Mwari, vachirwa navanhu vose;" 
1Thessalonians2:16 vanotidzivisa kuti tirege kuparidzira vahedheni, kuti vaponeswa; kuti varambe vachizadzisa zvivi zvavo; asi kutsamwa kwakaburukira pamusoro pavo kusvikira pakuguma." 
1Thessalonians2:17 Zvino isu, hama dzangu, zvatakaparadzaniswa nemi chinguva chiduku pamuviri, pasati pari pamwoyo, takashingairira zvikuru nokushuva kukuru kuti tionane nemi pachiso;" 
1Thessalonians2:18 naizvozvo taida kuuya kwamuri, ini Pauro, kamwe uyezve rwechipiri, asi Satani akatidzivisa." 
1Thessalonians2:19 Nokuti tariro yedu ndeipiko, kana mufaro, kana korona yokuzvirumbidza nayo? Hamuzimi here, pamberi paIshe wedu Jesu pakuuya kwake?" 
1Thessalonians2:20 Nokuti imi muri kubwinya kwedu nomufaro wedu. 
1Thessalonians3:1 Saka zvatakanga tisingagoni kutsunga, takati zvakanaka kuti tisiyiwe tiri toga paAteni;" 
1Thessalonians3:2 tikatuma Timoti, hama yedu, mushumiri waMwari paVhangeri yaKristu, kuti akusimbisei, nokukutsungisai mwoyo pakutenda kwenyu;" 
1Thessalonians3:3 kuti kurege kuva nomunhu anozununguswa nenhamo idzi, nokuti munoziva mumene kuti takagadzirirwa izvozvo." 
1Thessalonians3:4 Nokuti tichiri kwamuri takambokuudzai kuti tichatambudzwa; sezvazvakaitika, nemi munoziva." 
1Thessalonians3:5 Saka iniwo, zvandakanga ndisingachagoni kutsunga, ndakamutuma kuti ndizive kutenda kwenyu, ndichiti zvimwe muedzo wakakuedzai, izvo zvatakabata zvikava pasina." 
1Thessalonians3:6 Asi zvino Timoti akati asvika kwatiri achangobva kwamuri, akatiudza mashoko akanaka okutenda kwenyu norudo rwenyu, uye kuti munongositifunga nomurangariro wakanaka, muchida kutiona isu sesuwo tichida kukuonai imi;" 
1Thessalonians3:7 saka, hama dzangu, takanyaradzwa pamusoro penyu pakutambudzika kwedu kwose nenhamo nokutenda kwenyu;" 
1Thessalonians3:8 nokuti zvino isu tinorarama, kana imi mumire makasimba muna Ishe." 
1Thessalonians3:9 Nokuti tingavonga Mwari neiko pamusoro penyu nomufaro wose watinofara nawo pamberi paMwari wedu nokuda kwenyu," 
1Thessalonians3:10 tichingokumbira zvikuru usiku namasikati kuti tione chiso chenyu, kuti tizadzise zvakatairira pakutenda kwenyu?" 
1Thessalonians3:11 Zvino iye Mwari, Baba vedu, naIshe wedu Jesu, ngaaruramisire nzira yedu kwamuri;" 
1Thessalonians3:12 ishe akukurisei, akuwanzisirei rudo pakati penyu nokuna vose, sezvatinoita isu kwamuri," 
1Thessalonians3:13 asimbise mwoyo yenyu kuti ive isina chaingapomerwa pautsvene pamberi paMwari, Baba vedu, pakuuya kwaIshe wedu Jesu pamwechete navatsvene vake vose." 
1Thessalonians4:1 Naizvozvo pakupedzisira, hama dzangu, tinokumbira kwamuri, nokukurayirai muna Ishe Jesu, kuti, sezvamadzidza kwatiri mutoo wamunofanira kufamba nokufadza Mwari nawo, sezvamunofambawo, kuti muwanze nokunzwisisa panaizvozvo." 
1Thessalonians4:2 Nokuti munoziva mirairo yatakakupai naIshe Jesu. 
1Thessalonians4:3 Nokuti kuda kwaMwari ndihwo utsvene hwenyu, murege upombwe;" 
1Thessalonians4:4 kuti mumwe nomumwe wenyu azive kuzviwanira mudziyo wake noutsvene nokukudzwa," 
1Thessalonians4:5 asingaiti nokukara kwokuchiva, savahedheni, vasingazivi Mwari;" 
1Thessalonians4:6 munhu ngaarege kuitira hama yake zvakaipa kana kumunyengera pachinhu ichi, nokuti Ishe ndiye mutsivi wezvinhu izvozvo zvose, sezvatakakuudzaiwo nokukupupurirai kwazvo." 
1Thessalonians4:7 Nokuti Mwari haana kutidanira tsvina, asi utsvene." 
1Thessalonians4:8 Naizvozvo anoramba izvozvo, haarambi munhu, asi Mwari, anokupai Mweya wake, iwo Mutsvene." 
1Thessalonians4:9 Zvino, kana ruri rudo pakati pehama, hamufaniri kuti munyorerwe, nokuti imi mumene makadzidziswa naMwari kuti mudane;" 
1Thessalonians4:10 nokuti ndizvo zvamunoitira hama dzose dzeMakedhonia yose, asi tinokurayirai, hama dzangu, kuti muwanze nokuwanzisisa panaizvozvi;" 
1Thessalonians4:11 shingairirai kuva norugare, mumwe nomumwe abate zvake, muchibata basa namaoko enyu, sezvatakakurairai;" 
1Thessalonians4:12 kuti mufambe nomutoo wakafanira kuna vari kunze, musingashayiwi chinhu." 
1Thessalonians4:13 Zvino, hama dzangu, hatidi kuti mushayiwe kuziva pamusoro pavavete, kuti murege kuchema savamwe vasina tariro." 
1Thessalonians4:14 Nokuti kana tichitenda kuti Jesu akafa, akamukazve, saizvozvowo avo vakavata muna Jesu, Mwari achavauyisa pamwechete naye." 
1Thessalonians4:15 Nokuti tinokuudzai neshoko raIshe, kuti isu vapenyu, vakasara kusvikira pakuuya kwaIshe, hatingatongotangiri vakavata." 
1Thessalonians4:16 Nokuti Ishe amene achaburuka kudenga nokudanidzira, nezwi romutumwa mukuru, nehwamanda yaMwari; vakafa muna Kristu vachatanga kumuka;" 
1Thessalonians4:17 zvino isu vapenyu, vakasara, tichatorwa pamwechete navo mumakore, kuti tichingamidze Ishe mudenga; naizvozvo tichava naIshe nguva dzose." 
1Thessalonians4:18 Naizvozvo nyaradzanai namashoko aya. 
1Thessalonians5:1 Asi kana dziri nguva nemisi, hama dzangu, hamufaniri henyu kuti munyorerwe chinhu;" 
1Thessalonians5:2 nokuti imi mumene munoziva kwazvo, kuti zuva raIshe rinosvika sembavha usiku." 
1Thessalonians5:3 Kana vachiti, Rugare, nokugarika ipapo kuparadzwa kuchakurumidza kuvawira, sokurwadziwa kunoita kwomukadzi ane pamuviri; havangatongopukunyuka." 
1Thessalonians5:4 Asi imi, hama dzangu, hamuzi murima, kuti zuva iro rikubatei sembavha." 
1Thessalonians5:5 Nokuti imi mose muri vana vechiedza, navana vamasikati; hatizi vousiku, kana verima." 
1Thessalonians5:6 Naizvozvo ngatirege kuvata savamwe, asi tirinde, tisvinuke." 
1Thessalonians5:7 Nokuti vanovata, vanovata usiku; vanobatwa nedoro, vanobatwa usiku." 
1Thessalonians5:8 Asi isu, zvatiri vamasikati, ngatisvinuke, takapfeka chidzitiro chechipfuva chokutenda norudo nengowani ive tariro yoruponeso." 
1Thessalonians5:9 Nokuti Mwari haana kutiisira kutsamwa, asi kuti tiwane ruponeso naIshe wedu Jesu Kristu;" 
1Thessalonians5:10 akatifira isu, kuti, kana tichirinda, kana tichivata, tirarame pamwechete naye." 
1Thessalonians5:11 Saka nyaradzanai, musimbisane, sezvamunoitawo." 
1Thessalonians5:12 Zvino tinokumbira kwamuri, hama dzangu, kuti muzive avo vanobata pakati penyu, vanokutungamirirai muna Ishe, vanokurairai;" 
1Thessalonians5:13 muvakudze zvikuru norudo, nokuda kwebasa ravo. Ivai norugare pakati penyu." 
1Thessalonians5:14 Tinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri, hama dzangu, kuti murayire vasingateereri murairo, musimbise vanopera mwoyo, mutsigire vasina simba, muve nomwoyo murefu kuna vose." 
1Thessalonians5:15 Chenjerai kuti mumwe arege kutsiva mumwe zvakaipa nezvakaipa; asi nguva dzose mutevere zvinhu zvakanaka, mumwe kuno mumwe, nokuna vose." 
1Thessalonians5:16 Farai nguva dzose. 
1Thessalonians5:17 Rambai muchinyengetera. 
1Thessalonians5:18 Vongai pazvinhu zvose; nokuti ndiko kuda kwaMwari kwamuri muna Kristu Jesu. 
1Thessalonians5:19 Musadzima Mweya; 
1Thessalonians5:20 musazvidza zvinoporofitwa; 
1Thessalonians5:21 edzai zvinhu zvose; mubatisise zvakanaka; 
1Thessalonians5:22 regai marudzi ose ezvakaipa. 
1Thessalonians5:23 Mwari worugare amene ngaakuitei vatsvene kwazvo; Mweya wenyu, nomwoyo, nomuviri, zvichengetwe kwazvo, zvisina zvazvingapomerwa pakuuya kwaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu." 
1Thessalonians5:24 Akatendeka ndiye anokudanai, achazviitawo." 
1Thessalonians5:25 Hama dzangu, tinyengetererei." 
1Thessalonians5:26 Kwazisai hama dzose nokutsvoda kutsvene. 
1Thessalonians5:27 Ndinokupikirai naIshe, kuti tsamba iyi iravirwe hama dzose." 
1Thessalonians5:28 Nyasha dzaIshe wedu Jesu ngadzive nemi. 
2Thessalonians1:1 Pauro, naSirivhano, naTimoti, kuchechi yaVaTesaronika muna Mwari Baba vedu, naIshe Jesu Kristu." 
2Thessalonians1:2 Nyasha ngadzive nemi, norugare runobva kuna Mwari Baba, naIshe Jesu Kristu." 
2Thessalonians1:3 Tinofanira kuvonga Mwari nguva dzose pamusoro penyu, hama dzangu, sezvazvakafanira, nokuti kutenda kwenyu kunokura kwazvo, norudo rwenyu mose, mumwe nomumwe kuna vamwe, runowanda;" 
2Thessalonians1:4 nokudaro isu timene tinozvirumbidza mamuri pachechi dzaMwari pamusoro pokutsungirira kwenyu, nokutenda kwenyu mukutambudzika kwenyu kwose nenhamo dzose dzamunadzo." 
2Thessalonians1:5 Ndizvo zvinoratidza kutonga kwakarurama kwaMwari; kuti mugonzi makafanirwa noushe hwaMwari hwamunotambudzikirawo; 
2Thessalonians1:6 zvakarurama kuna Mwari, kuti atsive nokutambudzika ivavo vanokutambudzai;" 
2Thessalonians1:7 nemi munotambudzwa, kuti mupiwe kuzorora pamwechete nesu pakuonekwa kwaIshe Jesu, kana achibva kudenga navatumwa vesimba rake," 
2Thessalonians1:8 mumoto unopfuta, achitsiva avo vasingazivi Mwari, navasingateereri Vhangeri yaIshe wedu, Jesu;" 
2Thessalonians1:9 ivo vacharohwa nokuparadzwa kusingaperi, kuti vabve pamberi paIshe, napakubwinya kwesimba rake," 
2Thessalonians1:10 kana achiuya kuzorumbidzwa muvatsvene vake, nokukanukirwa muna vose vanotenda nezuva irero; (nokuti kupupura kwedu kwamuri kwakatendwa)." 
2Thessalonians1:11 Naizvozvo tinokunyengetereraiwo nguva dzose, kuti Mwari wedu ati, makafanirwa nokudanwa kwenyu, akwanise nesimba rake kuda kwenyu kwose kuita zvakanaka namabasa ose okutenda;" 
2Thessalonians1:12 kuti zita raIshe wedu Jesu rirumbidzwe mamuri, nemi maari, sezvadzakaita nyasha dzaMwari wedu nedzaIshe Jesu Kristu." 
2Thessalonians2:1 Zvino tinokumbira kwamuri, hama dzangu, pamusoro pokuuya kwaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, nokuungana kwedu kwaari;" 
2Thessalonians2:2 kuti murege kukurumidza kuzununguswa pakufunga kwenyu, kana kuvunduswa, kana nomweya, kana neshoko, kana netsamba, inonzi inobva kwatiri, muchiti zuva raKristu ratosvika;" 
2Thessalonians2:3 ngakurege kuva nomunhu anokunyengerai nomutoo upi noupi; nokuti harisviki, kana kutsauka kusati kwatanga kuuya, nomunhu wezvivi, mwanakomana wokurashika, asati amboonekwa," 
2Thessalonians2:4 iye, anorwa achizvikudza pamusoro pezvose zvinonzi Mwari, kana zvinonamatwa; nokudaro kuti anogara muTemberi yaMwari, achizviita Mwari." 
2Thessalonians2:5 Hamurangariri here kuti, ndichiri kwamuri, ndakakuudzai izvozvi?" 
2Thessalonians2:6 Zvino munoziva chinodzivisa, kuti aratidzwe nenguva yake." 
2Thessalonians2:7 Nokuti chakavanzika chokusarurama chotobata basa racho; asi zvichaitwa bedzi kusvikira iye anodzivisa zvino achibviswa. 
2Thessalonians2:8 Ipapo iye asakarurama achaonekwa, iye achaurayiwa naIshe Jesu nomweya womuromo wake, achiparadza nokuonekwa kwokuuya kwake;" 
2Thessalonians2:9 kuuya kwake iye kwakaita sebasa raSatani nesimba rose, nezviratidzo, nezvinoshamisa zvenhema," 
2Thessalonians2:10 nokunyengera kwose kwokusarurama kuna vanorasika; nokuti havana kugamuchira rudo rwezvokwadi, kuti vaponeswe." 
2Thessalonians2:11 Saka Mwari anovatumira simba rokukanganisa, kuti vatende nhema," 
2Thessalonians2:12 kuti vose vasina kutenda chokwadi, asi vakafarira zvisakarurama, vatongwe." 
2Thessalonians2:13 Asi isu tinofanira kuvonga Mwari nguva dzose pamusoro penyu, hama dzangu, vadikanwi vaIshe, nokuti Mwari akakutsanangurai kubva pakutanga, kuti muponeswe muutsvene hwoMweya nokutenda chokwadi." 
2Thessalonians2:14 Izvo zvaakakudanirai neVhangeri yedu, kuti muwane kubwinya kwaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu." 
2Thessalonians2:15 Naizvozvo, hama dzangu, mirai makasimba, muchengete mirairo yamakadzidziswa, kana neshoko kana netsamba yedu." 
2Thessalonians2:16 Zvino, Ishe wedu Jesu Kristu amene, naMwari Baba vedu, vakatida, vakatipa nenyasha dzavo kuvaraidzwa kusingaperi netariro yakanaka," 
2Thessalonians2:17 ngavavaraidze mwoyo yenyu, vakusimbisei pamabasa ose namashoko ose akanaka." 
2Thessalonians3:1 Pakupedzisira, hama dzangu, mutinyengeterere, kuti shoko raIshe ripfuure, rikudzwe, sezvazvinoitwa kwenyuwo;" 
2Thessalonians3:2 uye, kuti tisunungurwe kuvanhu vasakarurama, vakaipa; nokuti havazi vose vanotenda." 
2Thessalonians3:3 Asi Ishe ndiye akatendeka, achakusimbisai, nokukuchengetai kune wakaipa." 
2Thessalonians3:4 Tinokutendai muna Ishe, kuti munoita, uye mucharamba muchiita, izvo zvatinokurayirai." 
2Thessalonians3:5 Ishe ngaaruramise mwoyo yenyu murudo rwaMwari, nomukutsungirira kwaKristu." 
2Thessalonians3:6 Zvino, hama dzangu, tinokurairai nezita raIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, kuti mubve pahama imwe neimwe isingafambi netsika dzakafanira, isingateereri mirairo yamakapiwa nesu;" 
2Thessalonians3:7 nokuti imi munoziva mumene, kuti munofanira kutitevera isu, nokuti hatina kufamba netsika dzisakafanira pakati penyu;" 
2Thessalonians3:8 hatina kutongodya zvokudya zvomunhu tisingaripi, asi takabata basa usiku namasikati, tichitambudzika nokushingaira, kuti tirege kuremedza mumwe wenyu;" 
2Thessalonians3:9 hakuzi kuti hatine simba, asi kuti tikutungamirirei, mutitevere." 
2Thessalonians3:10 Nokuti, nenguva yataiva kwamuri, takakurairai izvozvo, kuti, “Kana munhu achiramba kubata basa, ngaarege kudyawo.”" 
2Thessalonians3:11 Nokuti tinonzwa kuti vamwe pakati penyu havafambi netsika dzakafanira, vasina chavanobata, vasingaregi zvavamwe." 
2Thessalonians3:12 Vanhu vakadaro tinovarayira nokukumbira kwavari muna Ishe Jesu Kristu, kuti vabate nokunyarara, vadye zvokudya zvavo zvimene." 
2Thessalonians3:13 Asi imi, hama dzangu, musaneta pakuita zvakanaka." 
2Thessalonians3:14 Kana pano munhu asingateereri shoko redu remutsamba iyi, mutarisise munhu uyo, kuti murege kufambidzana naye, anyadzwe." 
2Thessalonians3:15 Regai henyu kumuedza muvengi, asi mumurayire sehama." 
2Thessalonians3:16 Zvino, Ishe worugare amene ngaakupei rugare misi yose nemitoo yose. Ishe ngaave nemi mose." 
2Thessalonians3:17 Ndiko kukwazisa kwangu, ini Pauro, noruoko rwangu, ndicho chiratidzo patsamba dzose; ndinonyora kudai." 
2Thessalonians3:18 Nyasha dzaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu ngadzive nemi mose. 
1Timothy1:1 Pauro, mupostori waKristu Jesu nokurayira kwaMwari, Muponesi wedu, naKristu Jesu, tariro yedu;" 
1Timothy1:2 kuna Timoti, mwana wangu chaiye pakutenda: Nyasha, nengoni, norugare, zvinobva kuna Mwari Baba, naKristu Jesu, Ishe wedu, ngazvive newe." 
1Timothy1:3 Sezvandakakumbira zvikuru kwauri, ini ndichienda Masedhonia, ndinoti, usare muEfeso, kuti urayire vamwe, varege kudzidzisa dzimwe dzidziso;" 
1Timothy1:4 kana kurangarira ngano namazita amadziteteguru asingaperi, zvinongomutsa nharo, zvisingatendesi zvakarayirwa naMwari, zviri mukutenda." 
1Timothy1:5 Asi chinovavarirwa nomurairo ndirwo rudo runobva pamwoyo wakachena, napahana yakanaka, napakutenda kusinganyengeri;" 
1Timothy1:6 vamwe vakarasika pazvinhu izvozvi, vakatsaukira kukutaura kusina maturo;" 
1Timothy1:7 vachitsvaka kuti vave vadzidzisi vomurairo, vasingazivi zvavanoreva kana zvavanosimbisa." 
1Timothy1:8 Asi tinoziva kuti murairo wakanaka, kana munhu achiita nawo sezvinoreva murairo," 
1Timothy1:9 achiziva kuti murairo hauna kuitirwa wakarurama, asi vasina hanya nomurairo, navasingateereri, navasingadi Mwari, navatadzi, navasi vatsvene, navasina hanya naMwari, navanorova madzibaba, navanorova madzimai, navanouraya vanhu;" 
1Timothy1:10 nemhombwe, navanopombora navarume, navanoba vanhu, navanoreva nhema, navanopika nhema, uye kana chimwe chiriko chinopesana nedzidziso yakarurama;" 
1Timothy1:11 sezvinoreva Vhangeri yokubwinya kwaMwari womufaro, yandakapiwa ini." 
1Timothy1:12 Ndinomuvonga iye Kristu Jesu, Ishe wedu, akandipa simba, nokuti akati ndakatendeka, akandiisa pabasa rake;" 
1Timothy1:13 kunyangwe ini ndaiva aishonha Mwari kare, nomutambudzi ndichiitira vanhu zvakaipa; asi ndakaitirwa ngoni, nokuti ndakanga ndichizviita nokusaziva pakusatenda;" 
1Timothy1:14 asi nyasha dzaIshe wedu dzakawanda zvikuru nokutenda, norudo ruri muna Kristu Jesu." 
1Timothy1:15 Ishoko rechokwadi, rinofanira kutendwa kwazvo, kuti Kristu Jesu akauya panyika kuzoponesa vatadzi; avo ini ndiri mukuru wavo;" 
1Timothy1:16 asi naizvozvo ndakaitirwa ngoni, kuti Jesu Kristu aratidze mwoyo wake wose murefu mandiri, ini mukuru wavatadzi, kuti ndive chiratidzo kuna vanozotenda kwaari, zvinovaisa kuupenyu husingaperi." 
1Timothy1:17 Zvino iye Ishe asingaperi, asingafi, asingaonekwi, Mwari woga, ngaave nokukudzwa nokubwinya nokusingaperi–peri. Ameni." 
1Timothy1:18 Basa iri, rakarayirwa, ndinokupa iro, iwe Timoti, mwana wangu, kuti sezvazvakaporofitwa kare pamusoro pako, urwe pfumo rakanaka mazviri;" 
1Timothy1:19 wakabata kutenda nehana yakarurama; iyo yakarashwa navamwe, vakarashikirwa nokutenda;" 
1Timothy1:20 vamwe vavo ndiHimenio naArekizanda, vandakaisa kuna Satani, vadzidziswe kuti varege kushonha Mwari." 
1Timothy2:1 Naizvozvo pakutanga kwezvose ndinorayira kuti vanhu vose vakumbirirwe, vanyengetererwe, varevererwe, vavongerwe;" 
1Timothy2:2 madzimambo, navose vari vakuru, kuti tigare norugare nokunyarara pakunamata Mwari kwose, nomugariro unokudzwa." 
1Timothy2:3 Ndizvo zvakanaka, zvinofadza pamberi paMwari, Muponesi wedu;" 
1Timothy2:4 uyo anoda kuti vanhu vose vaponeswe, vasvike pakuziva chokwadi." 
1Timothy2:5 Nokuti kunongova naMwari mumwechete, noMureveri mumwechetewo, pakati paMwari navanhu, ndiye munhu Kristu Jesu," 
1Timothy2:6 akazvipa iye, kuti ave rudzikinuro rwavose, chive chapupu panguva dzazvo," 
1Timothy2:7 icho chandakaitirwa muparidzi nomupostori (ndinoreva zvirokwazvo, handirevi nhema), nomudzidzisi wavahedheni pakutenda chokwadi." 
1Timothy2:8 Naizvozvo ndinoda kuti varume vanyengetere panzvimbo dzose, vachisimudza maoko matsvene, vasina kutsamwa nenharo." 
1Timothy2:9 Saizvozvowo, kuti vakadzi vashonge nguo dzakafanira, vanokunyara nokuzvidzora; vasava nevhudzi rakarukwa, nendarama, kana mapera, kana nguo dzinodya mari zhinji;" 
1Timothy2:10 asi ngavashonge mabasa akanaka, sezvinofanira vakadzi vanoti tinonamata Mwari." 
1Timothy2:11 Mukadzi ngaadzidze nokunyarara nokuzviisa pasi kwose. 
1Timothy2:12 Asi handitenderi mukadzi kuti adzidzise, kana kuti ave nesimba pamusoro pomurume, asi ngaanyarare." 
1Timothy2:13 Nokuti Adhamu akatanga kuumbwa, tevere Evha;" 
1Timothy2:14 naAdhamu haana kunyengerwa, asi mukadzi akanyengerwa akapinda pakudarika;" 
1Timothy2:15 asi achaponeswa nokubereka vana, kana vachirambira mukutenda norudo, noutsvene pamwechete nokuzvidzora." 
1Timothy3:1 Ishoko rechokwadi, rokuti, kana munhu achitsvaka basa romutariri, anoda basa rakanaka." 
1Timothy3:2 Naizvozvo mutariri anofanira kuva munhu asina chaangapomerwa, murume womukadzi mumwechete, akangwara, akachenjera, anomugariro wakafanira, anoitira vaeni rudo, anoziva kudzidzisa," 
1Timothy3:3 asingadi waini, asingarwi; asi munyoro, asina gakava, asingakariri mari;" 
1Timothy3:4 anobata imba yake zvakanaka, ana vana vanozviisa pasi nomugariro wose unokudzwa;" 
1Timothy3:5 (kana munhu asingazivi kubata imba yake, angachengeta seiko Chechi yaMwari?)" 
1Timothy3:6 Asava mutendi mutsva, kuti arege kuzozvikudza, atongwe saDhiabhori." 
1Timothy3:7 Uyezve, unofanira kupupurirwa zvakanaka navari kunze, kuti arege kuzvidzwa, nokubatwa mumusungo waDhiabhorosi." 
1Timothy3:8 Saizvozvowo vashumiri ngavave vanokudzwa, vasina mazwi maviri, vasingadi waini zhinji, vasingakariri pfuma yakaipa;" 
1Timothy3:9 vanochengeta zvakavanzika zvokutenda muhana yakanaka. 
1Timothy3:10 Naivo ngavatange kuedzwawo, ipapo vashumire, kana vasina chavangapomerwa." 
1Timothy3:11 Saizvozvo navakadzi ngavave vanokudzwa, vasingacheri vamwe, vakasvinuka, vakatendeka pazvose." 
1Timothy3:12 Vashumiri ngavave varume vanomukadzi mumwechete, vanobata vana vavo nedzimba dzavo zvakanaka;" 
1Timothy3:13 nokuti avo vakushumira zvakanaka, vanozviwanira zita rinokudzwa, nokutsunga kukuru pakutenda kwavo muna Kristu Jesu." 
1Timothy3:14 Zvinhu izvi zvose ndinokunyorera, ndichiti ndichakurumidza kuuya kwauri;" 
1Timothy3:15 zvino kana ndikanonoka, ndinoda kuti uzive kuti vanhu vanofanira kufamba sei mumba maMwari, iyo Chechi yaMwari mupenyu, mbiru nechitsigiro chechokwadi." 
1Timothy3:16 Hakuna angaramba kuti chakavanzika chokunamata chikuru kwazvo, chokuti: Iye akaratidzwa panyama, akaruramiswa pamweya, akaonekwa navatumwa, akaparidzwa pakati pavahedheni, akatendwa panyika, akakwidzwa mukubwinya." 
1Timothy4:1 Zvino Mweya anoreva pachena, kuti panguva dzinouya vamwe vachatsauka pakutenda, vachiteerera mweya inonyengera nedzidziso dzomweya yakaipa," 
1Timothy4:2 vachinyengerwa navanoreva nhema, vakapiswa pahana dzavo nedare rinopisa," 
1Timothy4:3 vachidzivisa vanhu kuwanana, nokurayira kuti zvimwe zvokudya zviregwe, zvakasikwa naMwari, kuti zvigamuchirwe nokuvonga navanotenda, vanoziva chokwadi." 
1Timothy4:4 Nokuti zvose zvakasikwa naMwari zvakanaka, hakuna chinhu chingafanira kurashwa, kana chichigamuchirwa nokuvonga;" 
1Timothy4:5 nokuti chinoitwa chitsvene neshoko raMwari nokunyengetera. 
1Timothy4:6 Kana uchiudzira hama zvinhu izvi, uchava mushumiri akanaka waKristu Jesu, wakarerwa namashoko okutenda needzidziso yakanaka, yawakatevera nomwoyo wose." 
1Timothy4:7 Asi urambe ngano dzisina hanya naMwari nedzechembere. Uzvirovedze kunamata Mwari. 
1Timothy4:8 Nokuti kurovedza muviri kunobatsira zvishoma hazvo, asi kunamata Mwari kunobatsira pazvinhu zvose, zvakune chipikirwa choupenyu hwazvino nohunouya." 
1Timothy4:9 Ishoko rachokwadi, rinofanira kutendwa kwazvo." 
1Timothy4:10 Nokuti ndizvo zvatinotambudzikira nokurwira, nokuti tariro yedu iri kuna Mwari mupenyu, Muponesi wavanhu vose, zvikuru wavanotenda." 
1Timothy4:11 Rayira nokudzidzisa zvinhu izvi. 
1Timothy4:12 Munhu ngaarege kuvapo anozvidza uduku hwako, asi uitire vanotenda makwara, pashoko napamufambiro, naparudo, napakutenda, napakuchena kwomwoyo." 
1Timothy4:13 Shingaira pakurava, napakurayira, napakudzidzisa, kusvikira ndichiuya." 
1Timothy4:14 Usarega kuchengeta chipiwa chiri mauri, chawakapiwa nokuporofita, nokuiswa maoko avakuru." 
1Timothy4:15 Shingairira zvinhu izvi, uzviite nomwoyo wose, kuti kupfuurira mberi kwako kuonekwe navanhu vose." 
1Timothy4:16 Uzvichengete iwe nedzidziso yako. Urambire pazvinhu izvi, nokuti kana uchiita izvozvi, uchazviponesa iwe navanokunzwa." 
1Timothy5:1 Usatuke mukuru, asi umuraire sababa, navaduku savanun'una," 
1Timothy5:2 navakadzi vakuru samadzimai, navaduku sehanzvadzi nokuchena kwomwoyo kwose." 
1Timothy5:3 Kudza chirikadzi, dziri chirikadzi chaidzo." 
1Timothy5:4 Asi kana chirikadzi ina vana kana vazukuru, ngavatange ivo kudzidza kunamata Mwari paimba yavo, vadzosere zvakafanira kuvabereki vavo, nokuti ndizvo zvinofadza Mwari." 
1Timothy5:5 Zvino kana iri chirikadzi chaiyo, yakasiyiwa iri yoga, ndiyo inovimba naMwari, inogara ichikumbira nokunyengetera usiku namasikati." 
1Timothy5:6 Asi iyo inokarira zvinofadza, yakafa ichiri mhenyu." 
1Timothy5:7 Rayirawo zvinhu izvi, kuti varege kuva nechavangapomerwa." 
1Timothy5:8 Asi kana munhu asingachengeti vokwake, zvikuru veimba yake, arasa kutenda, akaipa kukunda asingatendi." 
1Timothy5:9 Chirikadzi ngairege kunyorwa zita, asi kana yasvika makore makumi matanhatu, yaiva mukadzi womurume mumwechete," 
1Timothy5:10 ino rumbidzwa pamusoro pamabasa akanaka, kana yakarera vana, kana yaifarira vaeni, kana yaishambidza tsoka dzavatsvene, kana yaibatsira vari munjodzi, kana yaishingairira mabasa ose akanaka." 
1Timothy5:11 Asi urambe chirikadzi kana vachiri vakadzi vaduku, nokuti kana dzopesana naKristu, dzotsvaka kuwanikwa;" 
1Timothy5:12 dzava nemhosva, nokuti dzaramba kutenda kwokutanga;" 
1Timothy5:13 uyezve, dzinodzidza kuva nousimbe dzichipota nedzimba; hadzizi simbe bedzi, asi vaitiwo vamakuhwa, dzisingaregi zvavamwe, dzichitaura zvisakafanira." 
1Timothy5:14 Naizvozvo ndinoda kuti chirikadzi duku dziwanikwe, dzibereke vana, dzichengete dzimba dzadzo, kuti dzirege kutongopa muvengi nzira yokupomera nayo." 
1Timothy5:15 Nokuti vamwe vatotsauka vachitevera Satani. 
1Timothy5:16 Kana mukadzi mutendi ane chirikadzi, ngaadzibatsire, chechi irege kuremedzwa, kuti igobatsira chirikadzi chaidzo." 
1Timothy5:17 Vakuru vanobata Chechi zvakanaka ngavanzi vanofanirwa nokukudzwa kaviri, zvikuru avo vanobata pashoko napakudzidzisa." 
1Timothy5:18 Nokuti Rugwaro runoti, “Usasunga muromo wenzombe inopura;” uyezve, “Mubati wakafanirwa nomubairo wake.”" 
1Timothy5:19 Usangotenda mhaka inopomerwa mukuru, asi kana ichibva pamiromo yezvapupu zviviri kana zvitatu." 
1Timothy5:20 Vanotadza uvarange pamberi pavose, kuti vamwe vagotya." 
1Timothy5:21 Ndinokurayira kwazvo pamberi paMwari, naKristu Jesu, navatumwa vakasanangurwa, kuti uchengete zvinhu izvi usingatongi usati wambonzwa kwazvo, kana kuita chinhu uchitsaura vanhu." 
1Timothy5:22 Usakurumidza kuisa maoko pamusoro pomunhu, kana kusangana pazvivi zvavamwe; uzvichengete kuti uve wakachena." 
1Timothy5:23 Usaramba uchingonwa mvura bedzi, asi unwe waini shoma nokuda kwomudumbu mako noutera hwako huzhinji." 
1Timothy5:24 Zvivi zvavamwe vanhu zvinoonekwa pachena, zvinotungamirira kutongwa kwavo, vamwezve vanoteverwa nazvo." 
1Timothy5:25 Saizvozvowo kuna mabasa akanaka anoonekwa pachena, naasina kudaro haangavanzwi." 
1Timothy6:1 Vose vari varanda pasi pejoko, ngavati vatenzi vavo vanofanirwa nokukudzwa kwose, kuti zita raMwari nedzidziso zvirege kumhurwa." 
1Timothy6:2 Avo vana vatenzi vanotenda, ngavarege kuvazvidza zvadziri hama, asi zvikuru ngavavabatire, zvavari vatendi navanodikanwa vanobatsirwa nokubata kwavo kwakanaka. Dzidzisa zvinhu izvi, uzviraire." 
1Timothy6:3 Kana kune munhu anodzidzisa imwe dzidziso, asingabvumiri mashoko akarurama, mashoko aIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu, nedzidziso inonzwana nokunamata Mwari," 
1Timothy6:4 anongozvikudza, asingazivi chinhu, asi anongokarira mibvunzo nenharo dzinomutsa godo, negakava, nokutuka, nokufungidzira kwakaipa," 
1Timothy6:5 nokukakavadzana kusingaperi kwavanhu vanomurangariro wakaodzwa, vakatorerwa chokwadi, vachiti kunamata Mwari ndizvo zvinopfumisa." 
1Timothy6:6 Zvino kunamata Mwari pamwechete nokutenda nezvatinazvo ndizvo zvinopfumisa kwazvo; 
1Timothy6:7 nokuti hatina kuuya nechinhu panyika, hatigoniwo kubuda tine chinhu;" 
1Timothy6:8 asi kana tine zvokudya nezvokufuka, tichatenda nazvo." 
1Timothy6:9 Asi vanotsvaka kupfuma, vanowira mukuedzwa nomumusungo, nomukuchiva kwoupenzi kuzhinji kuno kuvadza, zvinonyudza vanhu mukuparadzwa nokuraswa." 
1Timothy6:10 Nokuti kuda mari ndiwo mudzi wezvakaipa zvose; vamwe vakati vachiida zvikuru vakatsauswa pakutenda, vakazvibaya neshungu zhinji." 
1Timothy6:11 Asi iwe, munhu waMwari, tiza zvinhu izvi; utevere kururama nokunamata Mwari, nokutenda, norudo, nokutsungirira, nohunyoro." 
1Timothy6:12 Urwe kurwa kwakanaka kwokutenda, ubatisise upenyu husingaperi, hwawakadanirwa kwahuri, ukapupura kupupura kwakanaka pamberi pezvapupu zvizhinji." 
1Timothy6:13 Ndinokurayira pamberi paMwari, anopa zvinhu zvose zvoupenyu hwazvo, napamberi paKristu Jesu, akapupura kupupura kwakanaka pamberi paPontio Pirato;" 
1Timothy6:14 kuti uchengete murairo, usina ruvara, usina chaungapomerwa, kusvikira pakuonekwa kwaIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu;" 
1Timothy6:15 kwaachazoratidza panguva dzake, iye oga akaropafadzwa nowaMasimbaose, Mambo wamadzimambo, Ishe wamadzishe;" 
1Timothy6:16 iye oga asingafi, agere pachiedza chisingaswederwi, asina kuonekwa; kukudzwa nesimba risingaperi ngazvive kwaari. Ameni." 
1Timothy6:17 Rayira vapfumi panyika yazvino, kuti varege kuzvikudza, kana kuvimba nepfuma isingagari, asi naMwari, anotipa zvose achiwanza, kuti tifare nazvo;" 
1Timothy6:18 kuti vaite zvakanaka, vave vapfumi pamabasa akanaka, vafarire kupa vamwe, nokugovana;" 
1Timothy6:19 vazvirongedzere nheyo dzakanaka dzenguva inouya, kuti vabatisise upenyu chaihwo." 
1Timothy6:20 Iwe, Timoti, chengeta icho chawakapiwa, ufuratire kutaura kusina hanya naMwari nokuramba kunobva pazivo inonzi zivo, dziri nhema hadzo;" 
1Timothy6:21 iyo yakapupurwa navamwe, vakazorasika pakutenda. Nyasha ngadzive nemi." 
2Timothy1:1 Pauro, mupostori waKristu Jesu, nokuda kwaMwari, nokuda kwechipikirwa choupenyu huri muna Kristu Jesu" 
2Timothy1:2 kuna Timoti, mwana wangu anodikanwa: Nyasha, nengoni, norugare, zvinobva kuna Mwari Baba, naKristu Jesu, Ishe wedu, ngazvive newe." 
2Timothy1:3 Ndinovonga Mwari, wandinoshumira samadziteteguru angu, nehana yakachena, kana ndichiramba ndichikurangarira pakukumbira kwangu usiku namasikati," 
2Timothy1:4 ndichishuva zvikuru kukuona, ndichirangarira misodzi yako, kuti ndizadzwe nomufaro;" 
2Timothy1:5 ndichiyeuchidzwa kutenda kusinganyengeri kuri mauri, kwaimbogara muna mbuya vako nomuna mai vako, vaJuniki, kwandinoziva kwazvo kuti kunogarawo mauri." 
2Timothy1:6 Nemhaka iyi ndinokuyeuchidza kuti ukuchidzire chipo chaMwari chiri mauri nokuiswa kwamaoko angu. 
2Timothy1:7 Nokuti Mwari haana kutipa mweya wokutya, asi wesimba, noworudo, nowokuzvidzora." 
2Timothy1:8 Naizvozvo usanyadziswa nokupupurira Ishe wedu, kana ini, musungwa wake, asi utambudzike pamwechete neni nokuda kweVhangeri nesimba raMwari," 
2Timothy1:9 akatiponesa, akatidana nokudana kutsvene, zvisingabvi pamabasa edu, asi nokufunga kwake, nenyasha dzaakatiitira muna Kristu Jesu nguva dzisati dzavapo," 
2Timothy1:10 asi kwakaratidzwa zvino nokuonekwa kwoMuponesi wedu, Kristu Jesu, iye akaparadza rufu, akabudisa pachena upenyu nokusaora nenzira yeVhangeri," 
2Timothy1:11 yandakaitwa muparidzi, nomupostori, nomudzidzisi wayo." 
2Timothy1:12 Nemhaka iyi ndinotambudzikawo nezvinhu izvi, asi handinyadziswi, nokuti ndinoziva wandakatenda, ndinoziva kwazvo kuti anogona kuchengeta chandakamupa kusvikira zuva irero." 
2Timothy1:13 Batisisa zvawakaratidzwa zvamashoko akarurama, izvo zvawakanzwa kwandiri mukutenda norudo ruri muna Kristu Jesu." 
2Timothy1:14 Icho chakanaka, chawakapiwa, uchichengete naMweya Mutsvene anogara matiri." 
2Timothy1:15 Unozviziva hako kuti vose vari paEzhia vakandifuratira; pakati pavo pana Figero naHerimogene.
