2Timothy1:16 Ishe ngaaitire imba yaOnesiforo ngoni, nokuti kazhinji akandisimbisa, asinganyadziswi neketani yangu." 
2Timothy1:17 Asi akati asvika Roma, akanditsvaka zvikuru, akandiwana." 
2Timothy1:18 (Ishe ngaamuitire chinhu ichi kuti awane ngoni kuna Ishe nezuva irero); newe unoziva kwazvo ukuru hwokushumira kwake paEfeso. 
2Timothy2:1 Naizvozvo iwe, mwana wangu, iva nesimba munyasha dziri muna Kristu Jesu." 
2Timothy2:2 Izvo zvawakanzwa kwandiri pamberi pezvapupu zvizhinji, uzvipe vanhu vakatendeka, vanogonawo kudzidzisa vamwe." 
2Timothy2:3 Utambudzike pamwechete neni, somurwi wakanaka waKristu Jesu." 
2Timothy2:4 Hakuna munhu anorwa papfumo anozvipinganidza namabasa oupenyu huno, kuti agone kufadza uyo wakakokera kuhondo." 
2Timothy2:5 Nemunhuwo kana achivhivhana navamwe, haashongedzwi korona, kana asina kuvhivhana sezvakarayirwa." 
2Timothy2:6 Murimi anobata basa ndiye anofanira kutanga kudya zvibereko. 
2Timothy2:7 Funga zvandinoreva, nokuti Ishe achakupa kunzwisisa pazvinhu zvose." 
2Timothy2:8 Rangarira Jesu Kristu akamuka kuvakafa, worudzi rwaDhavhidhi, sezvandinoparidza neVhangeri yangu;" 
2Timothy2:9 yandinotambudzikira kusvikira pakusungwa somunyangadzi; asi shoko raMwari harina kusungwa. 
2Timothy2:10 Saka ndinotsungirira pazvinhu zvose nokuda kwavakasanangurwa, kuti naivo vawane kuponeswa kuri muna Kristu Jesu, pamwechete nokubwinya kusingaperi." 
2Timothy2:11 Ishoko rechokwadi; “Nokuti kana tikafa pamwechete naye tichararamawo pamwechete naye. 
2Timothy2:12 Kana tikatsungirira, tichabata ushe pamwechete naye; kana tikamuramba, iye achatirambawo." 
2Timothy2:13 Kana isu tisakatendeka iye anoramba akatendeka, nokuti haangazvirambi iye.”" 
2Timothy2:14 Uvayeuchidze zvinhu izvi, uvarayire pamberi paMwari, kuti varege kuita nharo zvisina maturo, zvinongoparadza vanonzwa." 
2Timothy2:15 Shingaira kuti uzviratidze pamberi paMwari uri munhu akatendeka, mubati asingafaniri hake kunyadziswa, anonatsa kururamisa shoko rechokwadi." 
2Timothy2:16 Nzvenga kutaura kusina hanya naMwari; nokuti vanhu vacharamba vachingonyanya pakusanamata Mwari," 
2Timothy2:17 neshoko ravo richanyenga seronda; pakati pavo kuna Himenayo naFireto; 
2Timothy2:18 ivo vakarasika pachokwadi, vachiti, kumuka kwavakafa kwatopfuura, vachikanganisa kutenda kwavamwe." 
2Timothy2:19 Kunyangwe zvakadaro, nheyo dzakasimba dzaMwari dzinomira, dzine chisimbiso ichi, “Ishe anoziva vanhu vake;” uye “Mumwe nomumwe anoreva zita raIshe ngaabve pakusarurama.”" 
2Timothy2:20 Zvino muimba huru hamuna midziyo yendarama neyesirivha bedzi, asi mimwe yamatandawo, neyevhu; mimwe inokudzwa, mimwe isingakudzwi." 
2Timothy2:21 Naizvozvo kana munhu achizvinatsa kwazvo pazvinhu izvi, achava mudziyo unokudzwa, wakaitwa mutsvene, wakakwanira basa raTenzi, wakagadzirirwa mabasa ose akanaka." 
2Timothy2:22 Asi tiza kuchiva kwoujaya, uvinge kururama, nokutenda, norudo, norugare, pamwechete navanodana kuna Ishe nomwoyo wakachena." 
2Timothy2:23 Asi urambe mibvunzo youpenzi nokusaziva, uchiziva kuti zvinobereka kukakavara." 
2Timothy2:24 Zvino muranda washe haafaniri kukakavara, asi ave munyoro kuvanhu vose, anoziva kudzidzisa, anotsungirira pakuitirwa zvakaipa," 
2Timothy2:25 anodzidzisa nounyoro avo vanomudzivisa, kuti zvimwe Mwari avape kutendeuka vagoziva chokwadi," 
2Timothy2:26 vapengenukezve, vabve pamusungo waDhiabhori, wavakanga vakabatwa naye kuti vaite kuda kwake." 
2Timothy3:1 Zvino uzive chinhu ichi, kuti namazuva okupedzisira nguva dzokutambudzika dzichasvika." 
2Timothy3:2 Nokuti vanhu vachava vanozvida, vanoda mari, vanozvirumbidza, vanozvikudza, vanotuka, vasingateereri vabereki, vasingavongi, vasati vari vatsvene," 
2Timothy3:3 vasina rudo chairwo, vasingadi kuyanana, vanochera vamwe, vasingazvidzori, vane hasha, vasingadi zvinhu zvakanaka," 
2Timothy3:4 vanonyengera, vasingarangariri, vanoita manyawi, vanoda zvinofadza zvenyika kupfuura Mwari;" 
2Timothy3:5 vanomufananidzo bedzi wokunamata Mwari, asi vakarasa simba rako; ufuratire vanhu ivavawo." 
2Timothy3:6 Nokuti pakati pavo varipo vanopinda mudzimba vachiverevedza, vachitapa zvikadzi zvakaremedzwa nezvivi, zvinokwewa nokuchiva kuzhinji," 
2Timothy3:7 zvinongogara zvichidzidza, asi hazvitongogoni kusvika pakuziva chokwadi." 
2Timothy3:8 Janesi naJambiresi sezvavakadzivisa Mosesi, saizvozvo ivo vanodzivisa chokwadi, vari vanhu vane ndangariro dzakaodzwa, vakarasika pakutenda." 
2Timothy3:9 Asi havachapfuuriri mberi, nokuti upenzi hwavo huchaonekwa navose, sezvakazoita hwavo." 
2Timothy3:10 Asi iwe wakatevera kudzidzisa kwangu, nomufambiro, nokufunga, nokutenda, nomwoyo murefu, norudo, nokutsungirira," 
2Timothy3:11 natadambudziko, nenhamo, izvo zvakandiwira paAndiyoku, napaIkoniumu, napaRisitira; matambudziko makuru sei andakanzwa; pazvinhu izvozvo zvose Ishe akandisunungura." 
2Timothy3:12 Zvino, navose vanoda kunamata Mwari muna Kristu Jesu vachatambudzwa." 
2Timothy3:13 Asi vanhu vakaipa navanyengeri vachanyanyisa pakuipa, vachitsausa vamwe nokutsauswa ivo." 
2Timothy3:14 Asi iwe, rambira pane zvawakadzidza nezvawakatendiswa, uzive kuti wakazvidzidza kuna ani," 
2Timothy3:15 kuti kubvira paucheche hwako wakaziva Magwaro Matsvene anogona kukupa uchenjeri hunoisa kukuponeswa nokutenda kuri muna Kristu Jesu. 
2Timothy3:16 Rugwaro rwose rwakafemerwa naMwari, runobatsira pakudzidzisa, nokurayira, nokururamisa, nokuranga kuri mukururama," 
2Timothy3:17 kuti munhu waMwari akwane, agadzirirwa kwazvo mabasa ose akanaka." 
2Timothy4:1 Ndinokupupurira kwazvo pamberi paMwari, naKristu Jesu, iye achatonga vapenyu navakafa pakuonekwa kwake noushe hwake;" 
2Timothy4:2 paridza shoko; ramba uchidaro nenguva yakafanira, kunyangwe isakafanira; rayira, tuka, ranga nomwoyo murefu zvikuru nokudzidzisa." 
2Timothy4:3 Nokuti nguva ichasvika yavacharamba kutendera dzidziso yakarurama, asi, vachida kufadzwa panzeve dzavo, vachazviunganidzira vadzidzisi pakuchiva kwavo," 
2Timothy4:4 vachifuratidza nzeve dzavo pachokwadi, vachitsaukira kungano." 
2Timothy4:5 Asi iwe svinura pazvinhu zvose, tambudzika, bata basa romuvhangeri, upedzise basa rako kwazvo." 
2Timothy4:6 Nokuti ini ndotodururwa, nguva yokuenda kwangu yasvika." 
2Timothy4:7 Ndarwa kurwa kwakanaka, ndapedza rwendo rwangu, ndakachengeta kutenda;" 
2Timothy4:8 kubva zvino ndakachengeterwa korona yokururama, yandichapiwa naIshe, Mutongi wakarurama, nezuva irero; ndisini ndoga, asi navose vakada kuonekwa kwake." 
2Timothy4:9 Shingaira kuti ukurumidze kuuya kwandiri. 
2Timothy4:10 Nokuti Dhemasi akandisiya, akada nyika yazvino, akaenda Tesaronika; Kiresenzi akaenda Garatia, naTito akaenda Dharimatia." 
2Timothy4:11 Ruka oga aneni. Tora Mako uuye naye, nokuti anondibatsira kwazvo pabasa." 
2Timothy4:12 Asi Tikiko ndakamutuma Efeso. 
2Timothy4:13 Nguo yandakasiya paTiroa kuna Karipo, uuye nayo pakuuya kwako, nebhuku, zvikuru magwaro amatehwe." 
2Timothy4:14 Arekizanda, mupfuri wendarira, akandiitira zvakaipa zvizhinji; Ishe achamutsiva paakaita napo;" 
2Timothy4:15 newewo umuchenjere, nokuti akadzivisa zvikuru mashoko edu." 
2Timothy4:16 Pakuzvidavirira kwangu kwokutanga kwakanga kusina munhu akandibatsira, asi vose vakandisiya. Ngavarege kuravirwa izvozvi." 
2Timothy4:17 Asi Ishe akamira neni, akandisimbisa, kuti ndipedzise kwazvo kuparidza kwangu, vahedheni vose vanzwe; ndikarwirwa pamuromo weshumba." 
2Timothy4:18 Ishe achandirwira pamabasa ose akaipa, achandiponesa ndipinde ushe hwake hwokudenga; kubwinya ngakuve kwaari nokusingaperi–peri. Ameni." 
2Timothy4:19 Ndikwazisirei Pirisika naAkwira, neimba yaOnesiforo." 
2Timothy4:20 Erasito akasara paKorinde, asi Tirofimo ndakamusiya paMiretusi achirwara." 
2Timothy4:21 Shingaira kuuya, chando chisati chasvika. Yubhuro, naPudhe, naRino, naKiraudhiya nehama dzose vanokukwazisa." 
2Timothy4:22 Ishe ngaave nomweya wako. Nyasha ngadzive nemi. 
Titus1:1 Pauro, muranda waMwari, nomupostori waJesu Kristu, nokuda kwokutenda kwavakasanangurwa vaMwari, nokwokuzivisa chokwadi chiri pakunamata Mwari," 
Titus1:2 patariro youpenyu husingaperi, hwaakapikira iye Mwari, asingatongorevi nhema, nguva dzisingaperi dzisati dzavapo," 
Titus1:3 asi panguva dzazvo akazivisa shoko rake nokuparidza kwandakapiwa nomurairo waMwari, Muponesi wedu;" 
Titus1:4 kuna Tito, mwana wangu chaiye pakutenda kwedu tose: Nyasha norugare, zvinobva kuna Mwari Baba, naKristu Jesu, Muponesi wedu, ngazvive newe." 
Titus1:5 Ndakakusiya paKiriti nemhaka iyi, kuti upedzise kugadzira izvo zvakanga zvasara, nokugadza vakuru mumaguta ose, sezvandakakurayira." 
Titus1:6 Kana kuno munhu asina chaangapomerwa, murume womukadzi mumwechete, ana vana vanotenda, vasingapiwi mhosva yokuti havazvidzori, kana kuti havateereri." 
Titus1:7 Nokuti mutariri anofanira kuva munhu asina chaangapomerwa, somuchengeti wemhuri yaMwari; asingaiti kuda kwake, asingakurumidzi kutsamwa, asingadi waini, asingarwi, asingakariri pfuma yakaipa;" 
Titus1:8 asi anoitira vaeni rudo, anoda zvakanaka, akachenjera, akarurama, mutsvene, anozvidzora;" 
Titus1:9 anobatisisa shoko rechokwadi, sezvarinodzidziswa, kuti agone kurayira nedzidziso yakarurama, nokukunda vanokakavara." 
Titus1:10 Nokuti vazhinji varipo vasingateereri, vanotaura zvisina maturo, vanonyengera, zvikuru avo vokudzingiswa," 
Titus1:11 vanofanira kudzivirirwa miromo yavo; vanoparadza mhuri kwazvo, zvavanodzidzisa zvisakafanira nokuda kwepfuma yakaipa." 
Titus1:12 Mumwe wavo, muporofita wokwavo, akati, “VaKiriti vanogara vachireva nhema, zvikara zvakaipa, navanokara vane usimbe.”" 
Titus1:13 Kupupura uku ndokwechokwadi. Nemhaka iyi uvarange zvikuru, kuti varurame pakutenda," 
Titus1:14 varege kuteerera ngano dzavaJudha, nemirairo yavanhu vanofuratira chokwadi." 
Titus1:15 Kuna vakachena zvose zvakachena; asi kuna vakasvibiswa, vasingatendi, hakuna chinhu chakachena asi kufunga kwavo nehana yavo zvakasvibiswa." 
Titus1:16 Vanoti, tinoziva Mwari, asi vanomuramba namabasa avo, zvavari vanhu vanonyangadza, vasingateereri, vasakafanira pamabasa ose akanaka." 
Titus2:1 Zvino iwe, taura zvakafanira, dzidziso yakarurama." 
Titus2:2 Varume vakuru ngavave vakasvinuka, vanokudzwa, vakangwara, vakarurama pakutenda, naparudo, napakutsungirira;" 
Titus2:3 saizvozvowo vakadzi vakuru, ngavave nomufambire wakafanira vatsvene, vasingacheri, kana kuda waini zhinji, asi vave vadzidzisi vezvakanaka;" 
Titus2:4 kuti vadzidzise vakadzi vaduku, kuti vade varume vavo, nokuda vana vavo," 
Titus2:5 vave vakangwara, vakachena, vanochengeta mhuri, vanyoro, vanozviisa pasi pavarume vavo, kuti shoko raMwari rirege kumhurwa." 
Titus2:6 Saizvozvowo varume vaduku uvaraire kuti vave vakangwara; 
Titus2:7 pazvinhu zvose iwe umene uvaratidze makwara amabasa akanaka; uve nokusakanganisa pakudzidzisa, nomugariro unokudzwa," 
Titus2:8 nokutaura kwakarurama, kusingagoni kushoorwa, kuti anopesana nesu anyadziswe, asina chinhu chakaipa chaangareva pamusoro pedu." 
Titus2:9 Varanda ngavazviise pasi pavatenzi vavo, vavafadze pazvinhu zvose, vasingakakavari;" 
Titus2:10 vasingabi, asi varatidze kutendeka kwakanaka kwose, kuti vashongedze dzidziso yaMwari, Muponesi wedu, pazvinhu zvose." 
Titus2:11 Nokuti nyasha dzaMwari dzakaonekwa, dzinovigira vanhu vose kuponeswa," 
Titus2:12 dzichitidzidzisa isu kuti tirambe kusanamata Mwari nokuchiva zvenyika, tirarame nokungwara, nokururama, nokunamata Mwari panguva ino," 
Titus2:13 takatarira tariro inofadza, nokuonekwa kwokubwinya kwaMwari mukuru, noMuponesi wedu, Kristu Jesu," 
Titus2:14 wakazvipa nokuda kwedu, kuti atidzikinure pazvisakarurama zvose, kuti azvinatsire vanhu vave vake chaivo, vanhu vanoshingairira mabasa akanaka." 
Titus2:15 Taura zvinhu izvi, urayire, urange nesimba rose; ngakurege kuva nomunhu anokuzvidza." 
Titus3:1 Uvayeuchidze kuti vazviise pasi pavabati navane simba, kuti vateerere, kuti vave vanhu vakazvigadzira kubata mabasa ose akanaka," 
Titus3:2 varege kurevera mumwe zvakaipa, vaitire vanhu vose unyoro hwose." 
Titus3:3 Nokuti nesuwo kare taiva vokusafunga, tisingateereri, takarashika, tiri varanda, vokuchiva kuzhinji navezvose zvinofadza, tigere mukati mokushata negodo, tichivengwa, tichivengana." 
Titus3:4 Asi unyoro hwaMwari, Muponesi wedu, norudo rwake kuvanhu, zvakati zvaonekwa," 
Titus3:5 akatiponesa, asingazviiti nokuda kwamabasa akarurama, atakanga taita isu, asi nokuda kwenyasha dzake, nenzira yokushambidzwa kwokuberekwa kutsva nokuvandudzwa naMweya Mutsvene," 
Titus3:6 waakadurura achiwanza pamusoro pedu, naJesu Kristu Muponesi wedu," 
Titus3:7 kuti isu, taruramiswa nenyasha dzake, tiitwe vadyi venhaka nokuda kwetariro youpenyu husingaperi." 
Titus3:8 Ishoko rechokwadi, uye ndinoda kuti usimbise kwazvo zvinhu izvi, zvokuti avo vakatenda Mwari vachenjere kuti varambe vachiita mabasa akanaka. Ndizvo zvakanaka, zvinobatsira vanhu;" 
Titus3:9 asi unzvenge mibvunzo youpenzi, namazita amadziteteguru, negakava, nokukakavara pamusoro pomurairo, nokuti hazvina maturo, hazvine basa." 
Titus3:10 Munhu anodzidzisa zvakatsauka, kana arayirwa kamwe norwechipiri, umurambe," 
Titus3:11 zvaunoziva kuti akadaro akatsauka, anotadza, azvipa mhosva amene." 
Titus3:12 Kana ndichituma Aritema kwauri, kana Tikiko, ushingaire kuuya kwandiri Nikopori; nokuti ndakati ndichagara chando ikoko." 
Titus3:13 Zenasi, mududziri womurairo, naAporo, uvaise zvakanaka parwendo, varege kushayiwa chinhu." 
Titus3:14 Vanhu vedu ngavadzidzewo kuramba vachiita mabasa akanaka, kuti vabatsire panoshayikwa zvinofanira kuvapo, kuti varege kuva vanhu vasina zvibereko." 
Titus3:15 Vose vari kwandiri vanokukwazisa. Ndikwazisire avo vanotida pakutenda. Nyasha ngadzive nemi mose. 
Philemon1:1 Pauro, musungwa waKristu Jesu, naTimoti, hama yedu, kuna Firimoni, mudikanwi wedu noanobata nesu," 
Philemon1:2 nokunaAfia, hanzvadzi yedu, nokunaAkipo, murwi pamwechete nesu, nokuchechi iri mumba mako." 
Philemon1:3 Nyasha ngadzive nemi, norugare zvinobva kuna Mwari, Baba vedu, naShe Jesu Kristu." 
Philemon1:4 Ndinovonga Mwari wangu nguva dzose, kana ndichikurangarira pakunyengetera kwangu," 
Philemon1:5 zvandinonzwa zvorudo rwako nokutenda kwaunako kunaShe Jesu nokuvatsvene vose; 
Philemon1:6 kuti kugovana kwokutenda kwako kuve nesimba, kuti zvakanaka zvose zviri mukati medu kuna Kristu zvizikanwe;" 
Philemon1:7 nokuti ndakanga ndinomufaro mukuru nokunyaradzwa nokuda kworudo rwako, nokuti mwoyo yavatsvene yakazorodzwa newe, hama yangu." 
Philemon1:8 Naizvozvo, kunyangwe ndisingatongotyi muna Kristu kukurayira kuita zvakafanira," 
Philemon1:9 kunyangwe zvakadaro, nokuda kworudo ndinoita zvokukumbira zvikuru, zvandakadai hangu, ini Pauro, mutana, uye zvino musungwa waKristu Jesu." 
Philemon1:10 Ndinokumbira zvikuru kwauri pamusoro pomwana wangu, wandakabereka pakusungwa kwangu, Onesimo," 
Philemon1:11 akanga asingakubatsiri kare, asi zvino anobatsira zvikuru, iwe neni;" 
Philemon1:12 ndinomudzosera kwauri, iye amene, mwoyo wangu chaiwo;" 
Philemon1:13 ndaida kuti agare neni, kuti panzvimbo yako andishumire pakusungwa kwangu nokuda kweVhangeri;" 
Philemon1:14 asi ndakanga ndisingadi kuita chinhu, iwe usati watenda, kuti zvakanaka zvaungaita zvirege kuitwa nokurovererwa, asi nokuda kwako." 
Philemon1:15 Nokuti zvimwe wakaparadzaniswa newe chinguva nemhaka iyi, kuti ugozova naye nokusingaperi;" 
Philemon1:16 arege kuzova muranda, asi munhu anopfuura muranda, ave hama inodikanwa, panyama nomuna Ishe, zvikuru kwandiri, asi zvikuru kwazvo kwauri." 
Philemon1:17 Zvino kana uchiti ndiri mugovani newe, umugamuchire sezvaungandigamuchira ini." 
Philemon1:18 Asi kana akakuitira chinhu chisakarurama, kunyangwe ane ngava newe, undiravireni izvozvo." 
Philemon1:19 Ini Pauro, ndinozvinyora noruoko rwangu, ndicharipa; ndisingarevi hangu kuti pamusoro pezvose une ngava kwandiri, ndiyewe umene." 
Philemon1:20 Hongu, hama, ngandive nomufaro kwauri muna Ishe; uzorodze mwoyo wangu muna Kristu." 
Philemon1:21 Ndinokunyorera, nokuti ndinotenda kuteerera kwako, ndichiziva kuti uchaitawo kupfuura pandinoreva napo." 
Philemon1:22 Asi ndigadzirirewo pokugara, nokuti ndinotarira kuti muchandipiwa ini nokuda kwokunyengetera kwenyu." 
Philemon1:23 Epafirasi, musungwa pamwechete neni muna Kristu, anokukwazisa." 
Philemon1:24 NaMako, naArisitakusi, naDhemasi, naRuka, vanobata basa pamwechete neni." 
Philemon1:25 Nyasha dzaShe Jesu Kristu ngadzive nomweya wenyu. 
Hebrews1:1 Mwari akataura kare kuna madzibaba muvaporofita nemigove mizhinji, uye nemitoo mizhinji," 
Hebrews1:2 zvino pakupedzisira kwamazuva ano akataura kwatiri muMwanakomana wake, waakaita mudyi wenhaka yezvinhu zvose, waakaitawo naye nyika;" 
Hebrews1:3 iye chadzera chokubwinya kwake, nomufananidzo wake chaiye, anochengeta zvinhu zvose nezwi resimba rake, akati apedzisa kunatswa kwezvivi, akagara kurudyi rwoUmambo kudenga," 
Hebrews1:4 akapfuura vatumwa nokunaka saizvozvo, sezita raakagara nhaka yaro, rakanyanya kunaka kupfuura ravo." 
Hebrews1:5 Nokuti akambotaura kuna ani wavatumwa achiti, “Ndiwe Mwanakomana wangu, Nhasi ndakakubereka? Uyezve, Ndichava baba vake, Iye achava Mwanakomana wangu?”" 
Hebrews1:6 Uye, kana achizouyisazve dangwe rake panyika, anoti, “Vatumwa vose vaMwari ngavamunamate.”" 
Hebrews1:7 Napamusoro pavatumwa anoti, “Iye anoita vatumwa vake kuti vave mhepo, Navaranda vake, kuti vave murazvo womoto;”" 
Hebrews1:8 Asi pamusoro poMwanakomana, anoti, “Chigaro chenyu choushe, imi Mwari, chiripo nokusingaperi–peri, Netsvimbo yokururama ndiyo tsvimbo youshe hwako." 
Hebrews1:9 Makada kururama, mukavenga kusarurama; Saka Mwari, iye Mwari wenyu, akakuzodzai Namafuta okufara kupfuura shamwari dzenyu.”" 
Hebrews1:10 Uye, “Imi, Ishe, makateya nheyo dzenyika pakutanga, Nedenga ndiro basa ramaoko enyu;" 
Hebrews1:11 Iro richapera, asi imi mucharamba muripo; Richasakara rose senguo;" 
Hebrews1:12 Mucharipeta sechinofukwa, Senguo, rikashandurwa; Asi imi hamushanduki, namakore enyu haangagumi.”" 
Hebrews1:13 Asi akambotaura kuna ani wavatumwa, achiti, “Gara kurudyi rwangu, Kusvikira ndichiita vavengi vako vave chitsiko chetsoka dzako?”" 
Hebrews1:14 Ko havazi vose mweya inoshumira, yakatumwa kuzobata nokuda kwavanodya nhaka yokuponeswa here?" 
Hebrews2:1 Saka tinofanira kuteerera zvikuru izvo zvatakanzwa, kuti tirege kukukurwa." 
Hebrews2:2 Nokuti kana shoko rakanga rataurwa navatumwa, rakanga rakasimba, uye kana kudarika nokusateerera kwose kwakapiwa mubairo wakarurama," 
Hebrews2:3 ko isu tichatiza sei, kana tisina hanya nokuponeswa kukuru kwakadai? Uku kwakaparidzwa pakutanga naIshe, kukasimbiswa kwatiri naivo vakanzwa;" 
Hebrews2:4 naiye Mwariwo achipupurirana navo nezviratidzo nezvinoshamisa, namabasa esimba mazhinji, nezvipo zvoMweya Mutsvene, nokuda kwake." 
Hebrews2:5 Nokuti nyika inozouya, yatinoreva, haana kuiisa pasi pavatumwa." 
Hebrews2:6 Asi mumwe akapupura kwazvo pane imwe nzvimbo, achiti, “Ko munhu chiiko, zvamunomufunga? Kana Mwanakomana womunhu, zvamunomushanyira?" 
Hebrews2:7 Makamuita muduku zvishoma kuvatumwa, Makamushongedza korona yokubwinya nokukudzwa," 
Hebrews2:8 Mukaisa zvinhu zvose pasi petsoka dzake.” Nokuti pakuisa kwake zvinhu zvose pasi pake, haana kusiya chinhu chimwe, chisina kuiswa pasi pake. Asi zvino tigere kuona kuti zvinhu zvose zvakaiswa pasi pake." 
Hebrews2:9 Asi tinomuona, iye Jesu, akaitwa muduku zvishoma kuvatumwa, akashongedzwa korona yokubwinya nokukudzwa nokuda kwokutambudzika kworufu, kuti nenyasha dzaMwari anzwe rufu nokuda kwavose." 
Hebrews2:10 Nokuti zvakanga zvakafanira kuti iye, akaitirwa zvinhu zvose, uye akaita zvinhu zvose, pakuisa kwake vanakomana vazhinji pakubwinya, akwanise Mutungamiriri wokuponeswa kwavo nenzira yokutambudzika." 
Hebrews2:11 Nokuti uyo, anovaita vatsvene, naivo vanoitwa vatsvene, vose vakabva kuno mumwe; nemhaka iyi haana nyadzi kuvaidza hama," 
Hebrews2:12 Zvaanoti, “Ndichaparidzira hama dzangu zita renyu, Ndichakuimbirai pakati pechechi.”" 
Hebrews2:13 Uyezve, “Ndichatenda kwaari.” Uyezve, “Tarira, ndini navana vandakapiwa naMwari.”" 
Hebrews2:14 Naizvozvo, vana zvavakagoverwa ropa nenyama, naiyewo akagovana navo pana izvozvi; kuti nokufa kwake iye aparadze uyo ane simba rorufu, iye Dhiabhori;" 
Hebrews2:15 agosunungura avo vaiva varanda paupenyu hwavo hwose nokuda kwokutya rufu. 
Hebrews2:16 Nokuti zvirokwazvo, haabatsiri vatumwa, asi anobatsira vana vaAbhurahamu." 
Hebrews2:17 Naizvozvo akafanira kuti aenzaniswe nehama dzake pazvinhu zvose, kuti ave Mupristi Mukuru ane ngoni, akatendeka pazvinhu zvaMwari, kuti adzikinure zvivi zvavanhu." 
Hebrews2:18 Nokuti zvaakatambudzika iye amene pakuedzwa kwake, anogona kubatsira vanoedzwa." 
Hebrews3:1 Naizvozvo, hama tsvene, vagoverani neni pakudanwa kunobva kudenga, fungai zvakanaka Mupostori noMupristi Mukuru wokupupura kwedu, iye Jesu," 
Hebrews3:2 akanga akatendeka kuna iye akamugadza, saMosesiwo mumhuri yake yose." 
Hebrews3:3 Nokuti uyu akanzi akafanira kukudzwa kupfuura Mosesi, muvaki weimba wezvaanokudzwa kupfuura imba;" 
Hebrews3:4 nokuti imba imwe neimwe inovakwa nomunhu, asi iye, akavaka zvose, ndiye Mwari." 
Hebrews3:5 Zvino Mosesi akanga akatendeka muimba yake yose somuranda, kuti ave chapupu chezvinhu zvaifanira kuzotaurwa," 
Hebrews3:6 asi Kristu soMwanakomana, akaiswa pamusoro pemhuri yake; iye, tiri mhuri yake isu, kana tikabatisisa kusvika pakuguma kusatya kwedu netariro yatinozvirumbidza pamusoro payo." 
Hebrews3:7 Naizvozvo, sezvinotaura Mweya Mutsvene, achiti, “Nhasi, kana muchinzwa izwi rake," 
Hebrews3:8 Musaomesa mwoyo yenyu, sapanguva yokutsamwisa, Napazuva rokuedzwa murenje;" 
Hebrews3:9 Pandakaedzwa namadzibaba enyu vachindinetsa, Vakaona mabasa angu makore ana makumi mana." 
Hebrews3:10 Naizvozvo ndakanzwa shungu pamusoro porudzi urwu, Ndikati, ‘Vanogara vachitsauka pamwoyo yavo; Asi havana kuziva nzira dzangu;’" 
Hebrews3:11 Naizvozvo ndakapika pakutsamwa kwangu, ndikati, ‘Havangapindi pazororo rangu.’ ”" 
Hebrews3:12 Hama dzangu, chenjerai kuti mukati momumwe wenyu murege kuva nomwoyo wakashata usingatendi, mutsauke muchibva kuna Mwari mupenyu," 
Hebrews3:13 asi simbisanai zuva rimwe nerimwe, kana kuchanzi, “Nhasi;” kuti kurege kuva nomumwe wenyu anoomeswa nokunyengera kwezvivi." 
Hebrews3:14 Nokuti tava vagoverani pamwechete naKristu, kana tichibatisisa kuvamba kwokutenda kwedu kusvikira pakuguma;" 
Hebrews3:15 zvichinzi, “Nhasi, kana muchinzwa izwi rake, Musaomesa mwoyo yenyu, sapanguva yokutsamwisa.”" 
Hebrews3:16 Nokuti ndivanaani vakanzwa, vakamutsamwisa? Havazi ivo vose vakabva Ijipiti naMosesi here?" 
Hebrews3:17 Akanzwa shungu makore ana makumi mana pamusoro pavanaani? Havazi ivo vakatadza, mitumbi yavo ikawira murenje here?" 
Hebrews3:18 Akapika pamusoro pavanaani kuti havangapindi pazororo rake? Havazi ivo vasina kuteerera here? 
Hebrews3:19 Zvino tinoona kuti vakanga vasingagoni kupinda nokusatenda kwavo. 
Hebrews4:1 Naizvozvo, chipikirwa chokupinda muzororo rake zvachichipo, tinofanira kutya kuti zvimwe kurege kuva nomumwe wenyu achawanikwa asingasviki ikoko." 
Hebrews4:2 Nokuti nesuwo takaparidzirwa Vhangeri, saivo; asi shoko ravakanzwa, harina kuvabatsira, nokuti harina kuvenganiswa nokutenda kwaivo vakanzwa." 
Hebrews4:3 Nokuti isu takatenda, tinopinda pazororo irero, sezvaakareva, achiti, “Naizvozvo ndakapika pakutsamwa kwangu, ndikati, ‘Havangapindi muzororo rangu.’ ” Kunyangwe mabasa ake akanga akwaniswa kubva pakuvambwa kwenyika." 
Hebrews4:4 Nokuti paneimwe nzvimbo akataura pamusoro pezuva rechinomwe, achiti, “Mwari wakazorora nezuva rechinomwe pamabasa ake ose;" 
Hebrews4:5 napanozve; havangapindi muzororo rangu.” 
Hebrews4:6 Naizvozvo, shoko zvarichipo kuti vamwe vachapinda pariri, uye kuti avo vakaparidzirwa Vhangeri kare havana kupinda nokusateerera kwavo," 
Hebrews4:7 anotarazve rimwe zuva, rinonzi, “Nhasi” ndizvo zvaanotaura naDhavhidhi, nguva huru yakadai yapfuura, (sezvakwakambotaurwa kare, zvichinzi,) “Nhasi, kana muchinzwa izwi rake, Musaomesa mwoyo yenyu.”" 
Hebrews4:8 Nokuti dai Joshua akanga avapa zororo, haazaizoreva rimwe zuva pashure." 
Hebrews4:9 Zvino zororo reSabata ravanhu vaMwari richipo. 
Hebrews4:10 Nokuti uyo akapinda muzororo rake, akazorora iye amene pamabasa ake, saMwari pana ake." 
Hebrews4:11 Naizvozvo ngatishingaire kuti tipinde muzororo irero, kuti munhu arege kuvapo anozowa achitevera nzira iyo yokusateerera." 
Hebrews4:12 Nokuti shoko raMwari ibenyu, rine simba, rinopinza kukunda munondo unocheka kumativi maviri, rinobaya kusvikira panoparadzana mwoyo nomweya, namafundo nomongo; rinotonga mifungo nendangariro dzomwoyo." 
Hebrews4:13 Hakuna chisikwa chisingaonekwi naye, asi zvinhu zvose zvakafukurwa nokuzarurwa pameso aiye watinofanira kuzvidavirira kwaari." 
Hebrews4:14 Naizvozvo, zvatino Mupristi Mukuru kwazvo, akapinda napakati pokudenga, iye Jesu, Mwanakomana waMwari, ngatibatisise kupupura kwedu." 
Hebrews4:15 Nokuti hatina Mupristi Mukuru asingagoni kutinzwira tsitsi pautera hwedu, asi akaedzwa pazvinhu zvose sesu, asina zvivi." 
Hebrews4:16 Naizvozvo, ngatiswederei tisingatyi kuchigaro choushe chenyasha, kuti tinzwirwe ngoni, tiwane nyasha, tibatsirwe nenguva yakafanira." 
Hebrews5:1 Nokuti Mupristi Mukuru mumwe nomumwe, akatorwa kuvanhu, anogadzwa nokuda kwavanhu pazvinhu zvaMwari, kuti abayire zvipo nezvibairo pamusoro pezvivi;" 
Hebrews5:2 iye anogona kunzwira tsitsi avo vasingazivi navakatsauka, nokuti naiyewo amene akakomberedzwa noutera." 
Hebrews5:3 Nemhaka iyo iye amene anofanira kuzvibayira pamusoro pezvivi zvake, sezvaanobayira zvavanhu." 
Hebrews5:4 Hakuna munhu angazvitorera basa iri rinokudzwa, asi kana achidanwa naMwari saiye Aroni." 
Hebrews5:5 Saizvozvowo Kristu haana kuzvikudza iye, achiitwa Mupristi Mukuru, asi akakudzwa naiye, akati kwaari, “Ndiwe Mwanakomana wangu, Nhasi ndakakubereka;”" 
Hebrews5:6 Sezvaanorevawo pane imwe nzvimbo, achiti, “Ndiwe Mupristi nokusingaperi Unorudzi naMerekizedheki.”" 
Hebrews5:7 Iye, pamazuva enyama yake, akauya kuna iye akanga achigona kumurwira parufu, neminyengetero nemikumbiro, achichema nokuchema kukuru nemisodzi, akanzwika nokuda kwokutya kwake Mwari;" 
Hebrews5:8 kunyangwe aiva Mwanakomana, akadzidza kuteerera nezvaakatambudzika;" 
Hebrews5:9 akati akwaniswa, akazova muvambi wokuponeswa kusingaperi kuna vose vanomuteerera;" 
Hebrews5:10 akanzi naMwari Mupristi mukuru unorudzi naMerekizedheki. 
Hebrews5:11 Tina mashoko mazhinji atingataura pamusoro pake, anorema kududzira, zvamava vanhu vasingagoni kunzwisisa kwazvo." 
Hebrews5:12 Nokuti, kunyangwe maifanira kuva vadzidzisi zvino, kana tichitarira nguva, mofanirazve kuti muve nomumwe anokudzidzisai dzidzo dzokutanga dzokuvamba kwezvirevo zvaMwari; mava vanhu vanofanira kupiwazve mukaka, vasingapiwi zvokudya zvikukutu." 
Hebrews5:13 Nokuti mumwe nomumwe anodya mukaka haanzwisisi shoko rokururama, nokuti mucheche hake." 
Hebrews5:14 Asi zvokudya zvikukutu ndezvavakuru, vanokuziva kwakadzidziswa, nenzira yokurovedzwa, kuzivisisa zvakanaka nezvakaipa." 
Hebrews6:1 Naizvozvo ngatisiye shoko rokutanga kwaKristu, tipfuurire mberi pakukwaniswa, tisingaisizve nheyo dzokutendeuka pamabasa akafa, nedzokutenda kuna Mwari," 
Hebrews6:2 nedzedzidziso yokubhabhatidza, nedzokuisa maoko, nedzokumuka kwavakafa, nedzokutongwa kusingaperi." 
Hebrews6:3 Ndizvo zvatichaita, kana Mwari achitendera." 
Hebrews6:4 Nokuti kana vari ivo, vakambovhenekerwa, vakaravira chipo chokudenga, vakagoverwa Mweya Mutsvene," 
Hebrews6:5 vakaravira shoko rakanaka raMwari, namasimba enyika inouya," 
Hebrews6:6 kana vakazotsauka, hazvibviri kuvavandudzazve kuti vatendeuke, nokuti vanozvirovererazve Mwanakomana waMwari pamuchinjikwa, vachimunyadzisa pachena." 
Hebrews6:7 Nokuti nyika iyo, inoti kana yanwa mvura inosinaya pamusoro payo kazhinji, ikabereka miriwo yakafanirawo avo vainorimirwa, ndiyo inoropafadzwa naMwari;" 
Hebrews6:8 asi kana ikabereka minzwa norukato, inorakashwa, yobva yotukwa; kuguma kwayo ndiko kupiswa." 
Hebrews6:9 Asi vadikanwi, kunyangwe tichitaura kudai, tinoziva kwazvo pamusoro penyu zvinhu zvinopfuura nokunaka, zvinoisa kukuponeswa." 
Hebrews6:10 Nokuti Mwari haazati ari usakarurama, angakanganwa basa renyu norudo rwamakaratidza nokuda kwezita rake, zvamakashumira vatsvene, muchivashumira nazvino." 
Hebrews6:11 Zvino tinoda kuti mumwe nomumwe wenyu ashingaire saizvozvo, kuti muve netariro yakakwana kusvikira pakuguma." 
Hebrews6:12 Kuti murege kuva nousimbe, asi muve vateveri vaivo vanodya nhaka yezvipikirwa nenzira yokutenda nokutsungirira." 
Hebrews6:13 Nokuti Mwari pakupikira Abhurahamu, akapika naiye amene, nokuti akanga asina mukuru kwaari waangapika naye," 
Hebrews6:14 akati, “Zvirokwazvo nokuropafadza ndichakuropafadza, nokuwanza ndichakuwanza.”" 
Hebrews6:15 Nokudaro, akati atsungirira, akawana chipikirwa." 
Hebrews6:16 Nokuti vanhu vanopika nomukuru kwavari; nemhiko inosimbisa ndiyo inogumisa gakava rose pakati pavo. 
Hebrews6:17 Saizvozvo Mwari akati achida zvikuru kuratidza vadyi venhaka yechipikirwa, kuti chirevo chake hachishandurwi, akapinda pakati nokupika;" 
Hebrews6:18 kuti nezvinhu zviviri zvisingashandurwi, (nokuti pazviri Mwari haagoni kureva nhema), tive nesimbiso yakabata, iyesu, takatizira kutariro yakaiswa pamberi pedu, kuti tiibate;" 
Hebrews6:19 yatinayo sechibatiso choMweya, tariro isingazununguswi, yakasimba, inopinda kune zviri mukati mechidziro chetemberi;" 
Hebrews6:20 pakapinda mutungamiriri nokuda kwedu, iye Jesu akaitwa Mupristi Mukuru nokusingaperi, anorudzi naMerekizedheki." 
Hebrews7:1 Nokuti Merekizedheki uyo, mambo weSaremi, mupristi waMwari Wokumusorosoro, akasangana naAbhurahamu pakudzoka kwake andouraya madzimambo, akamuropafadza;" 
Hebrews7:2 Abhurahamu akamupawo chegumi chezvose; iye pakutanga ari mambo wokururama, kana zvichishandurwa, uyezve, mambo weSaremi, ndokuti, mambo worugare;" 
Hebrews7:3 asina baba, asina mai, asina madzisekuru, asina kutanga kwamadzisekuru, asina kutanga kwamazuva, kana kuguma kwoupenyu, asi akafananidzwa noMwanakomana waMwari, anogara ari mupristi nokusingaperi." 
Hebrews7:4 Zvino fungai kukura kwomunhu uyu, akapiwa natateguru Abhurahamu chegumi chezvaakapamba." 
Hebrews7:5 Zvino avo, vari vanakomana vaRevhi, vanopiwa basa roupristi, vakarayirwa nomurairo kuti vatore chegumi kuvanhu, iko kuhama dzavo, kunyangwe vakabva muchiuno chaAbhurahamu;" 
Hebrews7:6 asi uyu, asina kuravirwa rudzi rwake kwavari, akapiwa zvegumi naAbhurahamu, akamuropafadza iye akanga ane zvipikirwa." 
Hebrews7:7 Zvino hatingarambi kuti muduku ndiye anoropafadzwa noanopfuura nokunaka. 
Hebrews7:8 Uye pano, vanhu vanofa, vanopiwa zvegumi; asi apo uyo anopiwa, anopupurirwa zvichinzi mupenyu." 
Hebrews7:9 Zvino tingati, naRevhi anopiwa zvegumi, iyewo akapa zvegumi naAbhurahamu;" 
Hebrews7:10 nokuti akanga achiri muchiuno chababa vake, pakusangana kwaMerekizedheki naye." 
Hebrews7:11 Naizvozvo, kana kukwaniswa kwaivapo nenzira youpristi hwaRevhi (nokuti vanhu vakapiwa murairo nokuda kwahwo), ko mumwe mupristi aifanira kuzomuka seiko anorudzi naMerekizedheki, asinganzi ane rudzi naAroni?" 
Hebrews7:12 Nokuti kana upristi huchisandurwa, nomurairo unofanira kuti ushandurwewo." 
Hebrews7:13 Nokuti uyo anorehwa zvinhu izvi pamusoro pake, akanga ari worumwe rudzi, rwakanga rusina munhu akambobata basa paatari." 
Hebrews7:14 Nokuti zvinoonekwa pachena, kuti Ishe wedu akabva kuna Judha; pamusoro porudzi urwu, Mosesi haana kureva zvavapristi." 
Hebrews7:15 Izvi zvinoratidzwawo kwazvo, kana kuchimuka mumwe mupristi akafanana naMerekizedheki," 
Hebrews7:16 asina kuitwa mupristi nomurairo wokurayira kwenyama, asi nesimba roupenyu husingapedzwi." 
Hebrews7:17 Nokuti iye anopupurirwa, zvichinzi, “Iwe uri mupristi nokusingaperi, Anorudzi naMerekizedheki.”" 
Hebrews7:18 Nokuti murau wokutanga unokoneswa nokuda kwoutera hwawo, uye nokuti hauna maturo," 
Hebrews7:19 (nokuti murairo hauna kukwanisa chinhu), zvino tariro, inopfuura nokunaka, ikaiswapo, yatinoswedera nayo kuna Mwari." 
Hebrews7:20 Uyezve, zvaasina kuitwa mupristi kusina mhiko;" 
Hebrews7:21 nokuti ivo vakaitwa vapristi kusina mhiko, asi iye nokupika kwaiye, akati kwaari, “Ishe akapika, haangazvidyi mwoyozve, achiti, ‘Iwe uri mupristi nokusingaperi.’ ”" 
Hebrews7:22 Saizvozvo Jesu akaitwa rubatso rwesungano inopfuura nokunaka. 
Hebrews7:23 Ivo vaiva vapristi vazhinji, nokuti vakadziviswa norufu kugara nokusingaperi;" 
Hebrews7:24 asi iye, zvaanogara nokusingaperi, anoupristi husingapfuudzwi kuno mumwe." 
Hebrews7:25 Naizvozvo ane simba rokuponesa kwazvo–kwazvo avo vanoswedera kuna Mwari naye, zvaanorarama nokusingaperi kuti avareverere." 
Hebrews7:26 Nokuti Mupristi Mukuru akadai ndiye ataifanira kuva naye, mutsvene, asina chakaipa, asina kusvibiswa, akaparadzaniswa navatadzi, akakwidzwa kumusoro kwedenga;" 
Hebrews7:27 asingafaniri, savaya vapristi vakuru, kubayira zuva rimwe nerimwe, pakutanga pamusoro pezvivi zvavo, pashure pamusoro pezvivi zvavanhu; nokuti akaita izvozvi kamwechete, zvikapera, pakuzviita kwake chibayiro." 
Hebrews7:28 Nokuti murairo unogadza vanhu vanoutera, kuti vave vapristi vakuru; asi shoko rokupika, rakatevera murairo, rinogadza Mwanakomana, akakwaniswa nokusingaperi." 
Hebrews8:1 Zvino, shoko guru pana izvozvo zvatataura, ndiro kuti: Tino Mupristi Mukuru akadai akagara kurudyi rwechigaro choushe choUmambo kudenga;" 
Hebrews8:2 iye mushumiri wezvinhu zvitsvene, nowetabhenakeri chaiyo, yakamiswa naIshe, isina kumiswa nomunhu." 
Hebrews8:3 Nokuti Mupristi Mukuru mumwe nomumwe akagadzwa, kuti abayire Mwari zvipo nezvibairo; naizvozvo naiye aifanira kuti ave nechaangabayirawo;" 
Hebrews8:4 nokuti dai aiva panyika, angadai asina kuva mupristi, nokuti vapristi varipo, vanobayira Mwari zvipo sezvinorehwa nomurairo;" 
Hebrews8:5 ivo vanoshumira mufananidzo nomumvuri wezvokudenga, sezvaakarayirwa iye Mosesi oda kuita tabhenakeri; nokuti akati, “Tarira, uite zvose nomufananidzo, wawakaratidzwa mugomo.”" 
Hebrews8:6 Asi zvino akapiwa basa rakanyanya kunaka, sezvaari Murevereri wesungano inopfuura nokunaka, yakasimbiswa nezvipikirwa zvinopfuura nokunaka." 
Hebrews8:7 Nokuti dai iya yokutanga yakanga isina chaingapomerwa, yechipiri ingadai isina kutsvakirwa nzvimbo." 
Hebrews8:8 Nokuti anovapa mhosva, achiti, “Tarirai, mazuva anouya, ndizvo zvinotaura Ishe, Andichaita nawo sungano itsva neimba yaIsiraeri, uye neimba yaJudha;" 
Hebrews8:9 Isina kuita sesungano yandakaita namadzibaba avo, Pazuva randakabata ruoko rwavo, kuti ndivabudise munyika yeIjipiti; Nokuti havana kurambira musungano yangu, Neni ndakasava nehanya navo, ndizvo zvinotaura Ishe." 
Hebrews8:10 Nokuti ndiyo sungano yandichaita nemhuri yaIsiraeri Kana mazuva iwayo apfuura, ndizvo zvinotaura Ishe; Ndichaisa mirairo yangu pakufunga kwavo, Napamwoyo yavo ndichainyora, Ndichava Mwari wavo, Ivo vachava vanhu vangu;" 
Hebrews8:11 Mumwe nomumwe haangazodzidzisi wokwake, Kana mumwe nomumwe hama yake, ichiti, ‘Ziva Ishe;’ Nokuti vose vachandiziva, Kubva kumuduku kusvikira kumukuru pakati pavo." 
Hebrews8:12 Nokuti ndichava nengoni nokusarurama kwavo, Nezvivi zvavo handichazozvirangariri.”" 
Hebrews8:13 Zvaanoti: Sungano itsva, akasakadza yokutanga; zvino chinhu chosakara, chova chakare, choda kurova." 
Hebrews9:1 Zvino, neyiyi sungano yokutanga yakanga ine mirairo yokushumira Mwari nayo, neimba tsvene yenyika." 
Hebrews9:2 Nokuti tabhenakeri, yaiva yokutanga, yakagadzirwa, makanga mune chigadziko chemwenje, netafura, nezvingwa zvokuratidza; ndipo panonzi Patsvene." 
Hebrews9:3 Zvino mberi kweketeni rechipiri pakanga pane tabhenakeri yainzi Patsvene–tsvene; 
Hebrews9:4 pakanga pane ndiro yendarama yezvinonhuwira, neareka yesungano, yakanga yakanamwa nhivi dzose nendarama, imomo makanga mune hari yendarama, yakanga ine mana, netsvimbo yaAroni yakadeya kutungira, namahwendefa esungano;" 
Hebrews9:5 pamusoro payo pakanga pana makerubhi okubwinya, akadzikatidza chifunhiro chengoni; hatigoni kurondedzera izvozvo tichiita chimwe–chimwe zvino." 
Hebrews9:6 Zvinhu izvi zvakati zvagadzirwa saizvozvo, vapristi vaipinda mutabhenakeri yokutanga nguva dzose, vachibata mabasa okushumira Mwari;" 
Hebrews9:7 asi mune yechipiri Mupristi Mukuru aipinda ari oga, kamwechete pagore, asingapindi asina ropa, raaizvibayirira iye nezvivi zvavanhu;" 
Hebrews9:8 Mweya Mutsvene achiratidza chinhu ichi, kuti nzira inoenda kunzvimbo tsvene yakanga isati yataridzwa, tabhenakeri yokutanga ichimire;" 
Hebrews9:9 wakanga uri mufananidzo wenguva ino vanobayira nayo zvipo nezvibairo, zvisingagoni kukwanisa pahana yake iye anoshumira;" 
Hebrews9:10 nokuti yaingova mirairo yenyama, yezvokudya, nezvokunwa, nokushamba kuzhinji, yavakatemerwa kusvikira panguva yokuvandudzwa." 
Hebrews9:11 Asi Kristu akati asvika ari Mupristi Mukuru wezvinhu zvakanaka zvinozouya, akapinda nomutabhenakeri yakapfuura pakukura napakukwana, isina kuitwa namaoko, ndiko kuti, isati iri yokusikwa kuno," 
Hebrews9:12 haana kupinda neropa rembudzi kana remhuru, asi neropa rake chairo, kamwechete, zvikapera, panzvimbo tsvene, akatiwanira rudzikinuro rusingaperi." 
Hebrews9:13 Nokuti kana ropa rembudzi nerenzombe namadota etsiru, kana zvichisaswa pamusoro pavakasvibiswa, zvichivaita vatsvene, kuti vanatswe panyama," 
Hebrews9:14 zvikuru sei ropa raKristu iye wakazviita noMweya usingaperi chibayiro kuna Mwari, chisina chachingapomerwa, richanatsa hana dzedu pamabasa akafa, kuti tishumire Mwari mupenyu." 
Hebrews9:15 Nemhaka iyo, iye ndiMurevereri wesungano itsva, kuti, rufu zvarwakasvika kuzodzikinura avo vakadarika pasungano yokutanga, vakadanwa vagopiwa chipikirwa chenhaka isingaperi." 
Hebrews9:16 Nokuti apo pane chido chenhaka, panofanira kuvapowo rufu rwaiye wakachiita." 
Hebrews9:17 Nokuti chido chenhaka chine simba kana vanhu vafa; nokuti haitongovi nesimba kana akachiita achiri mupenyu. 
Hebrews9:18 Naizvozvo nesungano yokutanga haina kuvambwa pasina ropa. 
Hebrews9:19 Nokuti zvirevo zvose zvakati zvataurwa kuvanhu vose naMosesi sezvakareva murairo, iye akatora ropa remhuru nerembudzi, pamwechete nemvura namakushe matsvuku, nehisopi, akasasa bhuku imene navanhu vose," 
Hebrews9:20 achiti, “Iri iropa resungano, yamakarayirwa naMwari.”" 
Hebrews9:21 Uyezve, akasasa saizvozvo neropa tabhenakeri nemidziyo yose yokushumira nayo." 
Hebrews9:22 Zvirokwazvo, tingati pamurairo zvinhu zvinenge zvose zvinonatswa neropa; uye kana kusina ropa rinoteurwa, hakuna ruregerero." 
Hebrews9:23 Naizvozvo mifananidzo yezviri kudenga yaifanira kuti inatswe nezvibairo izvi; asi zvinhu zvokudenga zvimene kuti zvinatswe nezvibairo zvinopfuura izvi nokunaka. 
Hebrews9:24 Nokuti Kristu haana kupinda munzvimbo tsvene yakaitwa namaoko, inofananidza iyo iri chaiyo, asi akapinda kudenga kumene, kuti zvino azviise pamberi paMwari nokuda kwedu;" 
Hebrews9:25 uye haana kupinda kuti azviite chibayiro kazhinji, somupristi mukuru anopinda munzvimbo tsvene gore rimwe nerimwe, akabata ropa rezvimwe zvinhu;" 
Hebrews9:26 nokuti dai zvakanga zvakadaro, angadai aitambura kazhinji kubva pakuvambwa kwenyika; asi zvino akaonekwa kwamwechete pakupedzisira kwenguva, kuti aparadze zvivi, nokuzviita chibayiro kwake." 
Hebrews9:27 Uye vanhu zvavakatemerwa kuti vafe kamwechete, kutongeswa kugotevera," 
Hebrews9:28 saizvozvo Kristuwo, zvaakaitwa chibayiro kamwechete, kuti atakure zvivi zvavanhu vazhinji, achazoonekwa rwechipiri, asingatakuri zvivi, naivo vanomutarira kuti avaponese." 
Hebrews10:1 Nokuti murairo zvauno mumvuri wezvinhu zvakanaka zvinouya usati uri mufananidzo chaiwo wezvinhu izvozvo, haungatongogoni kukwanisa avo vanoswedera gore rimwe nerimwe naizvozvo zvibairo zvavanoramba vachibayira Mwari." 
Hebrews10:2 Dai zvakanga zvakadaro, zvingadai zvisina kupera kubayirwa here? Nokuti vanonamata, kana vakanga vanatswa kamwechete, vangadai vasina kuzoyeudzwa zvivi zvavo." 
Hebrews10:3 Asi nezvibairo izvozvi vanoyeudzirwa zvivi gore rimwe nerimwe. 
Hebrews10:4 Nokuti ropa renzombe nerembudzi haritongogoni kubvisa zvivi. 
Hebrews10:5 Saka pakusvika kwake panyika, anoti, “Chibayiro nechipo makazviramba, asi makandigadzirira muviri," 
Hebrews10:6 hamuna kuda zvibairo zvinopiswa, nezvibairo zvezvivi;" 
Hebrews10:7 Zvino ndikati, ‘Tarirai, ndauya, (Mubhuku yakapetwa makanyorwa nezvangu) Kuti ndiite kuda kwenyu, imi Mwari.’ ”" 
Hebrews10:8 Zvaanoti pakutanga, “Zvibairo nezvipo, nezvibairo zvinopiswa, nezvibairo zvezvivi hamuna kuzvida; hamuna kufadzwa nazvo,” (zviri izvo zvinobayirwa Mwari sezvinoreva murairo)," 
Hebrews10:9 ndokuzoti, “Tarirai, ndauya kuzoita kuda kwenyu.” Anobvisa chokutanga, kuti aise chechipiri." 
Hebrews10:10 Nokuda ikoku takaitwa vatsvene nechibayiro chomuviri waJesu Kristu, chakabayirwa kamwechete." 
Hebrews10:11 Mupristi mumwe nomumwe anomira zuva rimwe nerimwe achishumira, nokubayira kazhinji zvibairo izvozvo zvimwe, zvisingagoni kubvisa zvivi;" 
Hebrews10:12 asi iye akati abayira chibayiro chimwechete pamusoro pezvivi, akagara nokusingaperi kurudyi rwaMwari;" 
Hebrews10:13 kubva zvino achimirira kusvikira vavengi vake vaitwa chitsiko chetsoka dzake. 
Hebrews10:14 Nokuti nechibayiro chimwechete akakwanisa nokusingaperi avo vanoitwa vatsvene. 
Hebrews10:15 NoMweya Mutsvene anotipupurirawo; nokuti akatanga achiti," 
Hebrews10:16 “Iyi ndiyo sungano yandichaita navo shure kwamazuva iwayo, ndizvo zvinotaura Ishe. Ndichaisa mirairo yangu pamwoyo yavo, nokuinyora pakufunga kwavo.” Ndokuzoti," 
Hebrews10:17 “Zvivi zvavo nokudarika kwavo handichatongozvirangariri.” 
Hebrews10:18 Zvino, kana zvinhu izvi zvakaregererwa, zvivi hazvichabayirwi." 
Hebrews10:19 Naizvozvo, hama dzangu, zvatingatsunga kupinda panzvimbo tsvene neropa raJesu," 
Hebrews10:20 nenzira itsva mhenyu, yaakativambira iye nokupinda kwake paketeni retemberi, ndiyo nyama yake;" 
Hebrews10:21 uye zvatino Mupristi Mukuru pamhuri yaMwari," 
Hebrews10:22 ngatiswedere nomwoyo wachokwadi, nokutenda kwakasimba, mwoyo yedu yasaswa kuti inatswe pahana yakaipa, nemiviri yedu yakashambidzwa nemvura yakanaka." 
Hebrews10:23 Ngatichengete kwazvo kupupura kwetariro yedu, kuti irege kuzununguka; nokuti iye, akapikira, akatendeka;" 
Hebrews10:24 ngatirangarirane, timutsane mwoyo kuti tive norudo namabasa akanaka," 
Hebrews10:25 tisarega kuungana kwedu, sezvinoita vamwe, asi tirayirane; zvikuru zvamunoona kuti zuva roswedera." 
Hebrews10:26 Nokuti kana tichitadza tichida kana tambogamuchira nezivo zvechokwadi, hakuna chine chibayiro pamusoro pezvivi," 
Hebrews10:27 asi kungomirira tichitya kutongeswa nokutsamwa kunopfuta somoto, kuchapedza vavengi." 
Hebrews10:28 Munhu, akaramba murairo waMosesi, anofa asinganzwirwi tsitsi, kana pane zvapupu zviviri kana zvitatu;" 
Hebrews10:29 hamufungi here kuti munhu, akatsika Mwanakomana waMwari pasi petsoka dzake, akati ropa resungano raakaitwa mutsvene naro harina maturo zvaro, akazvidza Mweya wenyasha, kuti iye haanganzi akafanirwa nokurohwa kunopfuura uku kwazvo here?" 
Hebrews10:30 Nokuti tinomuziva iye akati, “Kutsiva ndokwangu, ini ndicharipira.” Uyezve, “Ishe achatonga mhosva dzavanhu vake.”" 
Hebrews10:31 Zvinotyisa kuwira pamaoko aMwari mupenyu. 
Hebrews10:32 Asi rangarirai mazuva okutanga, amakati mavhenekerwa, mukatsunga pakurwa kukuru kwedambudziko;" 
Hebrews10:33 pamwe nokuti makaitwa chinhu chinotarirwa nokuzvidzwa nokutambudzwa; pamwe nokuti makagovana naivo vakaitirwa izvozvo. 
Hebrews10:34 Nokuti makanzwira tsitsi avo vakasungwa, mukatendawo nomufaro kuti nhumbi dzenyu dzipambwe, muchiziva kuti imi mumene mune pfuma yakapfuura nokunaka, inogara." 
Hebrews10:35 Naizvozvo regai kurasha kusatya kwenyu kuno mubairo mukuru. 
Hebrews10:36 Nokuti munofanira kuva nokutsungirira, kuti, kana maita kuda kwaMwari, mugopiwa chipikirwa." 
Hebrews10:37 “Nokuti kanguva kaduku–duku kachiko, Iye anouya, achauya, asinganonoki." 
Hebrews10:38 Asi wakarurama wangu achaponeswa nokutenda; Zvino kana akadzokera shure, mwoyo wangu haungafari naye.”" 
Hebrews10:39 Zvino isu hatizi ivo vokudzokera shure, kuti tiparadzwe; asi tiri vokutenda kuti tiponeswe mweya." 
Hebrews11:1 Zvino kutenda ndirwo rusimbiso rwezvinhu zvatinotarisira, nechiratidzo chezvinhu zvatisingaoni." 
Hebrews11:2 Nokuti naiko vanhu vakare vakapupurirwa zvakanaka. 
Hebrews11:3 Nokutenda tinonzwisisa kuti nyika dzakanatsorongedzwa nezwi raMwari, naizvozvo zvinhu, zvinoonekwa, hazvina kuitwa nezvinhu zvinoonekwa." 
Hebrews11:4 Nokutenda Abheri akabayira Mwari chibayiro chakanaka kune chaKaini; akapupurirwa nacho kuti akanga akarurama, Mwari achipupurira zvipo zvake; naiko kutenda iye, kunyangwe afa hake, achangotaura nazvino." 
Hebrews11:5 Nokutenda Inoki akatorwa, kuti arege kuona rufu; akasaonekwa, nokuti Mwari akanga amutora; nokuti asati atorwa akapupurirwa kuti akanga achifadza Mwari." 
Hebrews11:6 Kana kusina kutenda hazvibviri kumufadza; nokuti anouya kuna Mwari, anofanira kutenda kuti iye aripo, uye kuti anopa vanomutsvaka mubairo wavo." 
Hebrews11:7 Nokutenda Nowa akati anyeverwa pamusoro pezvinhu zvichigere kuonekwa, akagadzira areka nokutya Mwari, kuti aponese mhuri yake; akapa nyika mhosva nazvo, akagara nhaka yokururama kunouya nokutenda." 
Hebrews11:8 Nokutenda Abhurahamu, akati adanwa, akateerera, akabuda, akaenda kunzvimbo yaakanzi achaipiwa ive nhaka yake; akabuda akaenda, asingazivi kwaanoenda." 
Hebrews11:9 Nokutenda akandogara somutorwa Munyika yeChipikirwa, sapanyika yavamwe, akagara mumatende naIsaka naJakobho, vadyi venhaka yechipikirwa chimwe pamwechete naye;" 
Hebrews11:10 nokuti akanga achitarira guta rine nheyo, Mwari ari mhizha nomuvaki waro." 
Hebrews11:11 Nokutenda naiye Sara akapiwa simba rokutora mimba, kunyangwe akanga achembera, nokuti akati iye akamupikira akatendeka." 
Hebrews11:12 Saka kumunhu mumwe, akanga akaita sowafa, kwakabva vana vakaita senyenyedzi dzokudenga nokuwanda kwavo, uye sejecha riri pamhenderekedzo dzegungwa risingaverengwi." 
Hebrews11:13 Ivava vose vakafa vachitenda, vasina kupiwa zvipikirwa, asi vakazviona zviri kure, vakazvikwazisa, vakatenda kuti ivo vaeni navafambi panyika." 
Hebrews11:14 Nokuti vanotaura zvakadaro, vanoratidza kuti vanotsvaka nyika yavo chaiyo." 
Hebrews11:15 Nokuti kana vairamba vachifunga nyika iyo yavakabva kwairi, vangadai vawana nguva yokudzoka." 
Hebrews11:16 Asi zvino vanoda imwe inopfuura nokunaka, ndiyo yokudenga; naizvozvo Mwari haana nyadzi pamusoro pavo kuti aidzwe Mwari wavo; nokuti wakavagadzirira guta." 
Hebrews11:17 Nokutenda Abhurahamu, achiedzwa, akabayira Isaka; iye akanga agamuchira kwazvo zvipikirwa, akanga achibayira mwana wake wakaberekwa mumwe woga;" 
Hebrews11:18 iye akanga audzwa, zvichinzi, “Muna Isaka vana vako vachatumidzwa;" 
Hebrews11:19 nokuti wakati Mwari anogona kumutsa munhu kunyangwe kuvakafa; ndipapowo, kana tichitaura nomufananidzo, paakamudzoserwa.”" 
Hebrews11:20 Nokutenda Isaka akaropafadza Jakobho naEsau pamusoro pezvinozoitwa. 
Hebrews11:21 Nokutenda Jakobho pakufa kwake akaropafadza mwanakomana mumwe nomumwe waJosefa; akanamata akasendamira pamusoro pomudonzvo wake. 
Hebrews11:22 Nokutenda Josefa, ofa, akataura zvokubuda kwavana VaIsiraeri, akavaraira pamusoro pamapfupa ake." 
Hebrews11:23 Nokutenda Mosesi pakuberekwa kwake akavanzwa navabereki vake mwedzi mitatu, nokuti vakaona kuti akanga ari mwana wakanaka; havana kutya murairo wamambo." 
Hebrews11:24 Nokutenda Mosesi akura, akaramba kunzi mwanakomana womukunda waFarao," 
Hebrews11:25 akati zviri nani kuitirwa zvakaipa pamwechete navanhu vaMwari pakufarira zvivi nguva duku; 
Hebrews11:26 akati kuzvidzwa kwaKristu ipfuma huru kupfuma kwose kweIjipiti; nokuti akatarira mubairo. 
Hebrews11:27 Nokutenda akabva Ijipiti, asingatyi kutsamwa kwamambo; nokuti akatsungirira somunhu anoona iye asingaonekwi." 
Hebrews11:28 Nokutenda, akavamba Pasika nokusasa ropa, kuti muurayi wamatangwe avarege ivo." 
Hebrews11:29 Nokutenda, vakayambuka Gungwa Dzvuku, sapanyika yakaoma; vaIjipiti vachiedza izvozvo, vakabitirirwa." 
Hebrews11:30 Nokutenda, masvingo eJeriko akawira pasi, apoteredzwa mazuva manomwe." 
Hebrews11:31 Nokutenda, Rakabhi chifeve, haana kufa pamwechete navasina kuteerera, nokuti akanga agamuchira vashori norugare." 
Hebrews11:32 Ndichataurireiko zvimwe? Nokuti ndichapererwa nenguva, kana ndikataura zvaGidheoni, naBharaki, naSamisoni, naJefita, naDhavhidhi, naSamueri, navaporofita;" 
Hebrews11:33 avo vakakunda ushe nokutenda kwavo vakaita zvakarurama, vakapiwa zvipikirwa, vakadzivira miromo yeshumba." 
Hebrews11:34 Vakadzima simba romoto, vakatiza minondo inopinza, vakasimbiswa muutera, vakava nesimba pakurwa, vakadzinga hondo dzamamwe marudzi." 
Hebrews11:35 Vakadzi vakapiwazve vakafa vavo, vamutswa; vamwe vakapurwa, vakaramba kusunungurwa, kuti vawane kumuka kwakapfuura nokunaka;" 
Hebrews11:36 vamwe vakaedzwa, vachisekwa, vachirohwa zvikuru, uyezve vachisungwa, vachiiswa mutorongo;" 
Hebrews11:37 vakatakwa namabwe, vakaedzwa, vakaurayiwa nomunondo; vakafamba vakafuka matehwe amakwai, nenguo dzembudzi; vasina chinhu, vachitambudzika, vachiitirwa zvakaipa;" 
Hebrews11:38 (nyika haina kufanirwa navo), vachidzungaira mumarenje, nomumakomo, nomumapako, nomumakomba enyika." 
Hebrews11:39 Ava vose vakanga vapupurirwa nokutenda kwavo, asi havana kupiwa zvipikirwa," 
Hebrews11:40 nokuti Mwari akanga atigadzirira, chimwe chinhu chinopfuura nokunaka, kuti ivo varege kukwaniswa kunze kwedu." 
Hebrews12:1 Naizvozvo, nesuwo, zvatakakomberedzwa negore rezvapupu rakakura rikadai, ngatibvisei zvose zvinoremedza, nezvivi zvinongotinamatira, ngatimhanye nokutsungirira nhangemutange yatakaisirwa," 
Hebrews12:2 tichitarira kuna Jesu, muvambi nomukwanisi wokutenda kwedu, iye akatsunga pamuchinjikwa nokuda kwomufaro akaiswa pamberi pake, akashora kunyadziswa kwawo, akandogara kurudyi rwechigaro choushe chaMwari." 
Hebrews12:3 Nokuti cherechedzai uyo akatsunga pakukakavara kwakadai kwavatadzi, kuti imi murege kuneta nokupera simba mumweya yenyu." 
Hebrews12:4 Muchigere kudzivirira kusvikira ropa richibuda pakurwa kwenyu nezvivi. 
Hebrews12:5 Uye makakanganwa kwazvo kurayira kunotaura kwamuri sokuvanakomana, kuchiti, “Mwanakomana wangu, usazvidza kuranga kwaIshe, Usapera mwoyo kana uchirayirwa naye;" 
Hebrews12:6 Nokuti waanoda Ishe anomuranga, Anorova zvikuru mwanakomana mumwe nomumwe waanogamuchira.”" 
Hebrews12:7 Tsungai henyu mwoyo kuti murangwe; Mwari anobata imi savanakomana; nokuti ndoupi mwanakomana asingarangwi nababa? 
Hebrews12:8 Asi kana musingarangwi, sezvinoitirwa vose, muri vana voupombwe, hamuzi vanakomana chaivo." 
Hebrews12:9 Uyezve isu taiva namadzibaba edu enyama, vaitiranga, tikavakudza; ko hatingazviisi zvikuru pasi paBaba vemweya, kuti tirarame here?" 
Hebrews12:10 Nokuti ivo, zvirokwazvo, vakatiranga mazuva mashoma, sezvavaifunga, asi iye anotiranga kuti tibatsirwe, tigogoverwa utsvene hwake." 
Hebrews12:11 Zvino kuranga kwose, kana kuchaitwa, kwakaita sokusingafadzi, kunochemedza; asi pashure kunoberekera ivo, vakadzidziswa nako, zvibereko zvorugare, ndizvo zvibereko zvokururama." 
Hebrews12:12 Saka simbisaizve maoko akarembera pasi, namabvi anoshaiwa simba;" 
Hebrews12:13 gadzirirai tsoka dzenyu nzira dzakarurama, kuti icho chinokamhina chirege kushodoka, asi chiporeswe." 
Hebrews12:14 Tsvakai rugare navanhu vose, noutsvene, nokuti kunze kwahwo hakuna munhu achaona Ishe;" 
Hebrews12:15 muchenjere kuti kurege kuva nomunhu anodzokera shure panyasha dzaMwari; kuti mudzi wokuvava urege kumuka, ukutambudzei, vazhinji vagosvibiswa nawo;" 
Hebrews12:16 kurege kuvapo nemhombwe, kana noasina hanya naMwari, saEsau akatengesa udangwe hwake nokudya kamwechete." 
Hebrews12:17 Nokuti munoziva kuti achizoda hake pashure kugara nhaka yokuropafadzwa, akarambwa; nokuti haana kuwana nguva yokutendeuka, kunyangwe akaitsvaka zvikuru nemisodzi." 
Hebrews12:18 Nokuti hamuna kuswedera kugomo ringabatwa namaoko, rinopfuta, uye kurima, nokusviba, nokudutu guru," 
Hebrews12:19 nokukurira kwehwamanda, nokuzwi ramashoko; ivo vakarinzwa vakakumbira kuti shoko rimwe rirege kuzovataurirwa;" 
Hebrews12:20 nokuti vakakoniwa kutevera chakanga charayirwa, chokuti, “Kunyangwe nemhuka kana ikabata gomo, ichatakwa namabwe;”" 
Hebrews12:21 icho chakaonekwa chatyisa kudai, kuti naMosesi akati, “Ndinotya kwazvo, ndinodedera;”" 
Hebrews12:22 asi imi makaswedera kugomo reZioni, nokuguta raMwari mupenyu, Jerusaremu riri kudenga, nokumazana namazana avatumwa vasingaverengwi," 
Hebrews12:23 nokuungano huru, nokuchechi yamatangwe akanyorwa kudenga, nokuna Mwari, mutongi wavose, nokumweya yavakarurama vakakwaniswa," 
Hebrews12:24 nokuna Jesu, Murevereri wesungano itsva, nokuropa rakasaswa, rinotaura zvakanaka kupfuura Abheri." 
Hebrews12:25 Chenjerai kuti murege kuramba anotaura; nokuti kana avo vakamuramba nguva yaakavarayira panyika, vasina kupukunyuka, zvikuru isu kana tikafuratira iye wokudenga;" 
Hebrews12:26 izwi rake rakazunungusa nyika nenguva iyo; asi zvino akapikira, achiti, “Ndichabvundisazve kamwechete, isati iri nyika bedzi, asi nedengawo.”" 
Hebrews12:27 Zvino shoko iri rokuti, “Kamwechete,” rinoratidza kubviswa kwezvinozununguka, sezvinhu zvakaitwa, kuti izvo zvisingazununguki zvigare." 
Hebrews12:28 Saka, zvatinopiwa ushe husingazununguki, ngative nokuvonga, kuti tishumire Mwari nako, tichimufadza nokukudza nokutya." 
Hebrews12:29 Nokuti Mwari wedu moto unoparadza. 
Hebrews13:1 Rudo pakati pehama ngarugare. 
Hebrews13:2 Musakanganwa kuitira vaeni rudo; nokuti vachidaro vamwe vakagarisa vatumwa mumba, vasingazvizivi." 
Hebrews13:3 Fungai vakasungwa, somunenge makasungwa pamwechete navo; naivo vanoitirwa zvakaipa, somunenge muri mumuviri imiwo." 
Hebrews13:4 Kuwanana ngakukudzwe navose, nenhoo ngairege kuva nemhosva; nokuti Mwari achatongesa mhombwe navanofeva." 
Hebrews13:5 Musakarira mari pamugariro wenyu; tendai nezvamunazvo; nokuti iye amene akati, “Handingatongokuregeri, handingatongokusiyi.”" 
Hebrews13:6 Naizvozvo tinotsunga mwoyo, tichiti, “Ishe ndiye mubatsiri wangu; handingatyi; Munhu angandiiteiko?”" 
Hebrews13:7 Rangarirai vatungamiriri venyu vaikuparidzirai shoko raMwari; cherechedzai kuguma kwokufamba kwavo, mugotevera kutenda kwavo." 
Hebrews13:8 Jesu Kristu anogara akadaro zuro, nanhasi, nokusingaperi." 
Hebrews13:9 Musatorwa nedzidziso dzimwe dzisingazikanwi; nokuti zvakanaka kuti mwoyo usimbiswe nenyasha; urege kusimbiswa nezvokudya zvisina kubatsira vakafamba mazviri. 
Hebrews13:10 Isu tine atari, pasingatenderwi kudyiwa navanoshumira tabhenakeri." 
Hebrews13:11 Nokuti mitumbi yezvipfuwo, zvakaisirwa ropa razvo panzvimbo tsvene noMupristi Mukuru nokuda kwezvivi, inopiswa kunze kwemisasa." 
Hebrews13:12 Saka naiye Jesu akatambudzika kunze kwesuwo kuti aite vanhu vave vatsvene neropa rake. 
Hebrews13:13 Naizvozvo ngatibudire kwaari kunze kwemisasa, titakure kunyadziswa kwake." 
Hebrews13:14 Nokuti pano hatina guta richagara, asi tinotsvaka richavapo." 
Hebrews13:15 Naizvozvo ngatirambe tichibayira Mwari naye chibayiro chokumurumbidza, ndicho chibereko chemiromo inopupura zita rake." 
Hebrews13:16 Asi musakanganwa kuita zvakanaka nokugovana; nokuti Mwari anofara nezvibairo zvakadai. 
Hebrews13:17 Tererai vatungamiriri venyu, muzviise pasi pavo; nokuti vanochengeta mweya yenyu, savanhu vanozobvunzwa pamusoro penyu, kuti vaite izvozvo nomufaro, vasingaiti neshungu; nokuti izvozvo hazvikubatsiriyi chinhu." 
Hebrews13:18 Tinyengetererei; nokuti tinoziva kwazvo kuti tine hana yakanaka, zvatinoda kufamba zvakanaka pazvinhu zvose." 
Hebrews13:19 Ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri kuti muite izvozvo, kuti ndikurumidze kudzoserwa kwamuri." 
Hebrews13:20 Zvino Mwari worugare, akadzosa kuvakafa mufudzi mukuru wamakwai, iye Ishe wedu Jesu Kristu, neropa resungano isingaperi," 
Hebrews13:21 ngaakukwanisei pazvinhu zvose zvakanaka, kuti muite kuda kwake, iye achiita mukati medu izvo zvinofadza pamberi pake, naJesu Kristu ngaave nokubwinya nokusingaperi–peri. Ameni." 
Hebrews13:22 Asi ndinokurayirai, hama dzangu, kuti mutende neshoko rokurayira, nokuti ndakakunyorerai mashoko mashoma." 
Hebrews13:23 Zivai kuti hama yedu Timoti akasunungurwa; kana akakurumidza kusvika, ndinozokuonai pamwechete naye." 
Hebrews13:24 Ndikwazisirei vatungamiri venyu vose navatsvene vose. VeItariya vanokukwazisai. 
Hebrews13:25 Nyasha ngadzive nemi mose. Ameni. 
James1:1 Jakobho, muranda waMwari nowaIshe Jesu Kristu, kumarudzi ane gumi namaviri akapararira: Farai!" 
James1:2 Hama dzangu, muti mufaro bedzi kana muchiwira mumiedzo mizhinji;" 
James1:3 muchiziva kuti kuedzwa kwokutenda kwenyu kunobereka kutsungirira. 
James1:4 Asi kutsungirira ngakuve nebasa rakakwaniswa, kuti mukwane, mururame kwazvo, musingashayiwi chinhu." 
James1:5 Zvino kana mumwe wenyu achishayiwa kuchenjera ngaakumbire kuna Mwari, anongopa vose asingazotuki; achapiwa hake." 
James1:6 Asi ngaakumbire nokutenda, asinganyunyuti napaduku; nokuti munhu anonyunyuta akaita sefungu regungwa rinosundwa nemhepo richimutswa–mutswa." 
James1:7 Munhu uyu ngaarege kufunga kuti achazowana chinhu kuna Ishe; 
James1:8 munhu, ane mwoyo miviri, anoshanduka–shanduka panzira dzake dzose." 
James1:9 Asi hama iri muduku zvayo ngaafare nokukudzwa kwake; 
James1:10 nomupfumi nokuninipiswa kwake, nokuti achapfuura seruva rouswa." 
James1:11 Nokuti zuva rinobuda pamwechete nemhepo inopisa, ndokuomesa uswa; ruva rahwo rinowira pasi, nokunaka kwahwo kwakanga kwaonekwa kunopera; saizvozvowo mupfumi achasvava panzira dzake." 
James1:12 Akaropafadzwa munhu uyo anotsunga mwoyo pakuedzwa; nokuti kana atendwa, achapiwa korona youpenyu yakapikirwa avo vanomuda." 
James1:13 Kana munhu achiedzwa, ngaarege kuti ndinoedzwa naMwari; nokuti Mwari haangaedzwi nezvakaipa, naiye amene haangaedzi munhu." 
James1:14 Asi munhu mumwe nomumwe anoedzwa kana achikwewa nokuchiva kwake achinyengerwa. 
James1:15 Zvino kuchiva, kana kwarema, kunozvara zvivi; nezvivi, kana zvakura, zvinobereka rufu." 
James1:16 Musanyengerwa, hama dzangu dzinodikanwa." 
James1:17 Zvipo zvose zvakanaka nezvipiwa zvose zvakakwana zvinobva kumusoro, zvichiburuka kuna Baba vezviedza, uyo asina kupinduka kana mumvuri wokushanduka." 
James1:18 Nokuda kwake akatibereka neshoko rechokwadi, kuti isu tiite sechibereko chokutanga chezvisikwa zvake." 
James1:19 Munozviziva henyu izvozvi, hama dzangu dzinodikanwa. Asi munhu mumwe nomumwe ngaakurumidze kunzwa, anonoke kutaura, anonoke kutsamwa;" 
James1:20 nokuti kutsamwa kwomunhu hakuiti kururama kwaMwari. 
James1:21 Saka bvisai tsvina yose nokuipa kwakawanda, mugamuchire nomwoyo munyoro shoko rakasimwa mukati menyu, rinogona kuponesa mweya yenyu." 
James1:22 Asi ivai vaiti veshoko, musava vanzwi voga, muchizvinyengera." 
James1:23 Nokuti kana munhu ari munzwi weshoko, asati ari muiti waro, akafanana nomunhu anoona chiso chake, chaakaberekwa nacho, muchionioni." 
James1:24 Nokuti anozviona, ndokuenda, ndokukanganwa pakarepo kuti akadini iye." 
James1:25 Asi munhu anocherechedza murairo wakakwana, iwo murairo wokusunungurwa, akaramba achidaro, asati ari munzwi, anokanganwa, asi muiti webasa, iye acharopafadzwa pane zvaanoita." 
James1:26 Kana munhu achiti ndinonamata Mwari, asingadzori rurimi rwake, asi achinyengera mwoyo wake, kutenda kwaiyeyo munhu hakuna maturo." 
James1:27 Kunamata, kwakarurama, kusina mhosva pamberi paMwari wedu naBaba, ndiko kufambira nherera nechirikadzi mukutambudzika kwavo, nokuzvichengeta, kuti arege kusvibiswa nenyika." 
James2:1 Hama dzangu, kutenda kwenyu kuna Ishe wedu Jesu Kristu, iye wokubwinya, ngakurege kuva nokutenda zvinoonekwa zvomunhu." 
James2:2 Nokuti kana musinagoge renyu mukapinda munhu ane mhete yendarama, akapfeka nguo dzakanaka, mukapindawo murombo, akapfeka nguo dzakaipa;" 
James2:3 mukatarira uyo akapfeka nguo dzakanaka, mukati, “Gara pano pakanaka;” mukati kumurombo, “Mira papo, kana, gara pasi, pechitsiko chetsoka dzangu;”" 
James2:4 ko hamuna kutsaura mumwoyo yenyu, mukava vatongi vane mifungo yakaipa here?" 
James2:5 Inzwai, hama dzangu dzinodikanwa: Ko Mwari haana kutsanangura varombo venyika here kuti vave vapfumi pakutenda, navadyi venhaka youshe hwaakapikira vanomuda?" 
James2:6 Asi imi makazvidza murombo. Ko havazi vapfumi vanokuremedzai, naivo vanokukwirirai kuzvigaro zvokutonga here?" 
James2:7 Ko havazi ivo vanomhura zita rakanaka ramunotumidzwa naro here? 
James2:8 Asi zvino kana muchizadzisa murairo woushe, sezvazvakanyorwa, zvichinzi, “Ida wokwako sezvaunozvida iwe,” munoita zvakanaka." 
James2:9 Asi kana muchitenda zvinoonekwa zvomunhu, munoita zvivi, munopiwa mhosva nomurairo, muchinzi vadariki." 
James2:10 Nokuti munhu unochengeta murairo wose, akagumburwa kune chinhu chimwechete, wava nemhosva." 
James2:11 Nokuti iye, akati, “Usaita upombwe, ndiyewo,” akati, “Usauraya.” Zvino, kana asingaiti upombwe, asi achiuraya, wava mudariki womurairo." 
James2:12 Taurai, uye itai savanhu vanozotongwa nomurairo wokusunungurwa." 
James2:13 Nokuti kutonga hakungavi nengoni kuno asina kuitira vamwe ngoni; ngoni dzinozvirumbidza dzichikunda kutonga. 
James2:14 Zvinobatsirei hama dzangu, kana munhu achiti, ndinokutenda, asi asina mabasa? Ko kutenda uko kungamuponesa here?" 
James2:15 Kana kune hama, murume kana mukadzi, asina zvokufuka, anoshayiwa zvokudya zuva rimwe nerimwe," 
James2:16 mumwe wenyu akati kwavari, “Endai henyu nomufaro, mudziyirwe, mugute,” musingavapi izvo zvinodikanwa nomuviri, zvinogobatsirei?" 
James2:17 Saizvozvowo, nokutenda kana kusina mabasa, kwakafa hako." 
James2:18 Asi mumwe angati, “Iwe unokutenda, neni ndina mabasa; ndiratidze kutenda kwako kusina mabasa, neni ndigokuratidza namabasa angu kutenda kwangu.”" 
James2:19 Iwe unotenda kuti Mwari ndiye mumwechete; unoita zvakanaka; mweya yakaipa inotendawo izvozvo, ichidedera." 
James2:20 Zvino iwe munhu woupenzi, unoda kuziva here kuti kutenda kusina mabasa kwakafa?" 
James2:21 Ko Abhurahamu, baba vedu, haana kururamiswa namabasa here, nguva yaakabayira mwanakomana wake Isaka paatari?" 
James2:22 Unoona kuti kutenda kwake kwakabata pamwechete namabasa ake, uye kuti kutenda kwake kwakakwaniswa namabasa;" 
James2:23 rugwaro rukaitika, runoti, “Abhurahamu akatenda Mwari, kukanzi kwaari ndiko kururama; akanzi hama yaMwari.”" 
James2:24 Munoona kuti munhu anoruramiswa namabasa, haaruramiswi nokutenda bedzi." 
James2:25 Saizvozvowo, Rakabhi, chipfeve, haana kururamiswa here namabasa, nguva yaakachingamidza nhume, nokuvaendesa neimwe nzira?" 
James2:26 Nokuti somuviri usina mweya wakafa, saizvozvo kutenda kusina mabasa kwakafawo." 
James3:1 Hama dzangu, musava vadzidzisi vazhinji, zvamunoziva kuti tichatongwa nokupfuurisa." 
James3:2 Nokuti tinogumburwa tose muzvinhu zvizhinji. Kana munhu asingagumburwi mukutaura, iye munhu akakwana, anogona kudzora muviri wosewo." 
James3:3 Zvino kana tichiisa matare amabhiza mumiromo yawo, kuti atiteerere, tinodzorawo muviri wawo wose." 
James3:4 Tarirai magwa makuru, kunyangwe ari makuru akadai, achidzingwa nemhepo dzine simba guru, anodzorwa nechidzoreso chidukuduku kwose–kwose nokuda kwomwoyo womufambisi wawo." 
James3:5 Saizvozvowo rurimi mutezo muduku, runozvirumbidza zvikuru. Tarirai, moto muduku unotungidza huni zhinji sei!" 
James3:6 Rurimi moto, rwakaita senyika izere nezvisakarurama; ndizvo zvakaita rurimi pakati pemitezo yedu, runosvibisa muviri wose, runotungidza nzira yose youpenyu, runotungidza irwo neGehena." 
James3:7 Nokuti marudzi ose emhuka, neeshiri, neezvinokambaira, neezviri mugungwa angapingudzwa, uye ukambopingudzwa navanhu;" 
James3:8 asi hakuna munhu angapingudza rurimi; ndicho chinhu chakaipa chinoshanduka–shanduka, chizere nomuti unouraya." 
James3:9 Narwo tinorumbidza Ishe Baba; narwo tinotuka vanhu, vakaitwa nomufananidzo waMwari;" 
James3:10 mumuromo mumwe munobva kurumbidza nokutuka. Hama dzangu, hatifaniri kudaro." 
James3:11 Tsime rinobudisa pachitubhu chimwe mvura inonaka neinovava here? 
James3:12 Hama dzangu, muonde ungabereka maorivhi, kana muzambiringa maonde here? Kunyangwe nemvura inovava haingabudisi inonaka." 
James3:13 Ndiani pakati penyu akachenjera, akangwara? Ngaaratidze nomufambiro wake wakanaka mabasa ake nounyoro hwouchenjeri." 
James3:14 Asi kana mune godo rinovava norukave mumwoyo menyu, musazvirumbidza nokurevera zvokwadi nhema." 
James3:15 Kuchenjera uku hakuburuki kuchibva kumusoro, asi ndokwenyika, kwatakamuka nako, kwomweya wakaipa." 
James3:16 Nokuti pane godo norukave, ndipo pane nyonganiso namabasa ose akaipa." 
James3:17 Asi kuchenjera, kunobva kumusoro, zvikuru kwakachena, uye kuno rugare, kunyoro, kunoteerera, kuzere nengoni nezvibereko zvakanaka, kusingatsauri kusinganyengeri." 
James3:18 Chibereko chokururama chinodyarwa parugare navanoita rugare. 
James4:1 Kurwa nokukakavara pakati penyu zvinobvepiko? Hazvibvi pakuchiva kwenyu, kunorwa pamitezo yenyu here?" 
James4:2 Munochiva, asi hamuna chinhu; munouraya, munogodorana, musingagoni kuwana chinhu; munokakavara, muchirwa; hamuna chinhu, nokuti hamukumbiri." 
James4:3 Munokumbira, musingapiwi; nokuti munokumbira zvakaipa, kuti muzviparadze pakuchiva kwenyu." 
James4:4 Imi voutere, hamuzivi here kuti ushamwari hwenyika hunovengana naMwari? Naizvozvo mumwe nomumwe, anoda kuva shamwari yenyika, anozviita muvengi waMwari." 
James4:5 Munofunga kuti Rugwaro runotaura pasina here, ruchiti, “Mweya, waakagarisa mukati medu anotishuva negodo?”" 
James4:6 Asi anopa nyasha dzakapfuura. Saka Rugwaro runoti, “Mwari anodzivisa vanozvikudza, asi anopa nyasha vanozvininipisa.”" 
James4:7 Naizvozvo muzviise pasi paMwari; dzivisai Dhiabhori, agokutizai." 
James4:8 Swederai kuna Mwari, iye agoswedera kwamuri. Shambai maoko enyu, imi vatadzi; natsai mwoyo yenyu, imi mune mwoyo miviri." 
James4:9 Shuwai mucheme, murire; kuseka kwenyu ngakushandurwe kuve kuchema, nokufara kwenyu dzive shungu." 
James4:10 Muzvininipise pamberi paIshe, agokukudzai." 
James4:11 Hama dzangu, musareverana zvakaipa. Unorevera hama yake zvakaipa, kana kutonga hama yake, unorevera murairo zvakaipa nokutonga murairo; zvino kana uchitonga murairo, hauzi muiti womurairo, asi mutongi." 
James4:12 Mumwe chete ndiye mutemi womurairo nomutongi, iye anogona kuponesa nokuparadza; asi iwe ndiwe aniko unotonga wokwako?" 
James4:13 Nhai imi, munoti “Nhasi, kana mangwana tichaenda kuguta rokuti, tigogarako gore, tichishambadzira, tifume" 
James4:14 imi musingazivi zvamangwana. Upenyu hwenyu Chiiko? Nokuti muri mhute, inoonekwa nguva duku, ndokunyangarika.”" 
James4:15 Mungadai muchiti, “Kana Ishe achida, tichararama tiite zvokuti nezvokuti.”" 
James4:16 Asi zvino munozvirumbidza pakuzvikudza kwenyu; kuzvirumbidza kwose kwakadai kwakaipa. 
James4:17 Naizvozvo uyo, anoziva kuita zvakanaka, akasazviita, iye ane zvivi." 
James5:1 Nhai, imi vapfumi, chemai muridze mhere nokuda kwamatambudziko achakuwirai." 
James5:2 Pfuma yenyu yakaora, nguo dzenyu dzapera nezviundudzi." 
James5:3 Ndarama yenyu nesirivha yenyu zvine ngura; ngura yazvo ichakupupurirai zvakaipa, ichapedza nyama yenyu somoto. Makazvichengetera pfuma pamazuva okupedzisira." 
James5:4 Tarirai, mubairo wavaranda venyu vakacheka minda yenyu, wamakaramba nawo nokunyengera, unodanidzira; nokudana kwavacheki kwakasvika kunzeve dzaIshe wehondo." 
James5:5 Makagara zvinonaka panyika muchikarira zvinofadza; makakodza mwoyo yenyu nezuva rokubaya. 
James5:6 Makatongera wakarurama, mukamuuraya; haakudzivisiyi." 
James5:7 Naizvozvo hama dzangu, tsungirirai kusvikira pakuuya kwaIshe. Tarirai, murimi anomirira chibereko chenyika chinokosha, achitsungirira pamusoro pazvo kusvikira zvapiwa mvura yokutanga neyokuguma." 
James5:8 Nemiwo tsungirirai; simbisai mwoyo yenyu, nokuti kuuya kwaIshe kwava pedyo." 
James5:9 Hama dzangu, musanyunyutirana kuti murege kutongwa; tarirai, mutongi amire pamusuwo." 
James5:10 Hama dzangu mukutambudzika nokutsungirira teverai makwara avaporofita vakataura nezita raIshe. 
James5:11 Tarirai, vakatsunga mwoyo tinoti vakaropafadzwa; makanzwa zvokutsungirira kwaJobho, akaona Ishe zvaakavavarira naye, kuti Ishe ano mwoyo munyoro kwazvo, ane tsitsi." 
James5:12 Asi, hama dzangu, kupfuura zvinhu zvose, musapika, kunyangwe nedenga, kana nenyika, kana nokupika kumwe kwose; asi hongu yenyu ngaive hongu, kwete yenyu ngaive kwete; kuti murege kutongwa." 
James5:13 Kuno mumwe anotambudzika pakati penyu here? Ngaanyengetere. Kuno mumwe anofara here? Ngaaimbe nziyo. 
James5:14 Kuno mumwe anorwara pakati penyu here? Ngaadane vakuru vechechi; ngavamunyengeterere, vamuzodze namafuta nezita raIshe." 
James5:15 Kunyengetera kwokutenda kuchaponesa anorwara, Ishe achamumutsa; kana akaita zvivi achazviregererwa." 
James5:16 Naizvozvo reururanai zvivi zvenyu, munyengetererane kuti muporeswe. Kukumbira kwomunhu akarurama kune simba guru pakubata kwako." 
James5:17 Eriya akanga ari munhu akaita sesu, akanyengetera nomunyengetero kuti mvura irege kunaya; ikasanaya panyika makore matatu nemwedzi mitanhatu." 
James5:18 Akanyengeterazve; denga rikanaisa mvura, nyika ikabereka zvibereko zvayo." 
James5:19 Hama dzangu, kana kuno munhu pakati penyu akatsauka pazvokwadi, mumwe akamudzora," 
James5:20 ngaazive kuti anodzora mutadzi panzira yokutsauka kwake, uchaponesa mweya parufu nokufukidza zvivi zvizhinji." 
1Peter1:1 Petirosi, mupostori waJesu Kristu, kuna vakasanangurwa vari vaeni, vakapararira muPondusi, neGaratia, neKapadhosia, neEzhia, neBhitinia," 
1Peter1:2 vakasanangurwa nokuziva zviri mberi kwaMwari Baba, muutsvene hwoMweya, kuti vateerere, vasaswe neropa raJesu Kristu: Nyasha norugare ngazviwanzwe kwamuri." 
1Peter1:3 Mwari, Baba vaIshe wedu, Jesu Kristu, ngaatendwe, akatiberekazve nengoni dzake huru, kuti tive netariro mhenyu, inouya nokumuka kwaJesu Kristu kuvakafa," 
1Peter1:4 kuti tive nenhaka isingaori, isina mhosva, isingasvavi, yamakachengetererwa kudenga," 
1Peter1:5 imi munorindwa nesimba raMwari nokutenda, kuti mupiwe ruponeso, rwakagara rwagadzirwa, kuti ruratidzwe nenguva yokupedzisira." 
1Peter1:6 Iyo yamunofarira zvikuru, kunyangwe zvino, kana zvichifanira, muchichemedzwa nguva duku nemiedzo mizhinji;" 
1Peter1:7 kuti kuedzwa kwokutenda kwenyu kunokosha zvikuru kupfuura ndarama inopera hayo, kunyangwe inoedzwa nomoto, kuwanikwe kuchibereka kurumbidzwa, nokubwinya, nokukudzwa pakuonekwa kwaJesu Kristu;" 
1Peter1:8 iye wamunoda, kunyangwe musina kumuona; iye wamunotenda kwaari, kunyangwe musingamuoni zvino, muchifara zvikuru nomufaro usingagoni kutaurwa, uzere nokubwinya," 
1Peter1:9 muchipiwa chinovavarirwa nokutenda kwenyu, ndirwo ruponeso rwemweya yenyu." 
1Peter1:10 Ruponeso urwu rwakabvunzisiswa nokunzverwa kwazvo navaporofita, vakaporofita zvenyasha dzamaizoitirwa imi," 
1Peter1:11 vachinzvera kuti nguva ndeipi, kana yakadini, yakataurwa noMweya waKristu, wakanga uri mukati mavo, nguva yaakapupura kare zvokutambudzika kwaKristu, nokubwinya kunozotevera izvozvo." 
1Peter1:12 Avo, vakaratidzwa kuti vakanga vasingazvibatiri ivo, asi imi, pazvinhu izvo zvamakataurirwa zvino naivo vakakuparidzirai Vhangeri noMweya Mutsvene akatumwa achibva kudenga; zvinhu izvo vatumwa vanoda kuzvichirekedza." 
1Peter1:13 Saka zvisungei zviuno zvendangariro dzenyu, musvinure, mutarire nomwoyo wose kunyasha dzamuchazopiwa pakuonekwa kwaJesu Kristu;" 
1Peter1:14 muve savana vanoteerera, musingaenzanisi mufambiro wenyu nokuchiva kwakare pakusaziva kwenyu;" 
1Peter1:15 asi saiye mutsvene akakudanai, nemiwo mumene muve vatsvene pamufambiro wenyu wose;" 
1Peter1:16 nokuti kwakanyorwa, kuchinzi, “Ivai vatsvene, nokuti ini ndiri mutsvene.”" 
1Peter1:17 Zvino kana muchimuti Baba, iye anotonga achitarira zvakaitwa nomumwe asingatariri zvinoonekwa zvomunhu, garai panguva youtorwa hwenyu muchitya;" 
1Peter1:18 muchiziva kuti hamuna kudzikinurwa nezvinoora, sesirivha kana ndarama, pamufambiro wenyu usina maturo, wamakasiyirwa namadzibaba enyu;" 
1Peter1:19 asi neropa raKristu, seregwayana risina charingapomerwa, risina ruvara;" 
1Peter1:20 iye wakazikanwa kare, nyika isati yavambwa, asi akaratidzwa pakuguma kwenguva nokuda kwenyu," 
1Peter1:21 imi, munotenda naye kuna Mwari, wakamumutsa kuvakafa, akamupa kubwinya; kuti kutenda kwenyu netariro yenyu zvive kuna Mwari." 
1Peter1:22 Zvamakanatsa mweya yenyu muchiteerera chokwadi, kuti mude hama nokusanyengera, munofanira kudana zvikuru nomwoyo wose;" 
1Peter1:23 nokuti makaberekwa kutsva, zvisingabvi pambeu inoora, asi pane isingaori, neshoko raMwari benyu rinogara nokusingaperi." 
1Peter1:24 Nokuti, “Nyama yose yakaita souswa, Nokunaka kwose seruva rouswa. Uswa hunosvava, neruva rinowira pasi;" 
1Peter1:25 Asi shoko raIshe rinogara nokusingaperi.” Ndirori shoko romufaro ramakaparidzirwa. 
1Peter2:1 Naizvozvo rasai zvakaipa zvose, nokunyengera kwose, namano–mano, negodo, nokuchera kwose," 
1Peter2:2 savacheche vachangoberekwa, pangai mukaka womweya, usina kushatiswa; kuti mukure nawo, mugoponeswa;" 
1Peter2:3 kana makaravira kuti Ishe ano mwoyo munyoro. 
1Peter2:4 Uyai kwaari, iye ibwe benyu, rakaraswa navanhu, asi rakasanangurwa naMwari, rinokosha." 
1Peter2:5 Nemiwo, samabwe mapenyu, muvakwe muve imba yoMweya, muve upristi utsvene, kuti mubayire zvibairo zvoMweya, zvinofadza Mwari nokuda kwaJesu Kristu." 
1Peter2:6 Nokuti muRugwaro zvirimo, zvinoti, “Tarira, ndinoisa muZioni ibwe rekona, rakasanangurwa, rinokosha; Neanotenda kwaari haanganyadziswi.”" 
1Peter2:7 Naizvozvo imi, munotenda, munako kukudzwa; asi kuna vasingatendi, “Ibwe rakaraswa navavaki, Ndiro rakaitwa musoro wekona;”" 
1Peter2:8 uye, “Ibwe rokugumbusa, Nedombo rokupinganidza.” Ndivo avo vanogumburwa neshoko, nokuti havariteereri; ndizvo zvavakaisirwawo." 
1Peter2:9 Asi imi muri rudzi rwakasanangurwa, upristi hwamambo, rudzi rutsvene, vanhu vaakazviwanira, kuti muparidze kunaka kwaiye akakudanai, kuti mubve parima muuye kuchiedza chake chinoshamisa." 
1Peter2:10 Imi kare makanga musi vanhu; asi zvino muri vanhu vaMwari; makanga musinganzwirwi ngoni, asi zvino manzwirwa ngoni." 
1Peter2:11 Vadikanwi, ndinokumbira zvikuru kwamuri, zvamuri vatorwa navaeni, kuti muzvidzore pakuchiva kwenyama kunorwa nomweya;" 
1Peter2:12 mufambiro wenyu uve wakanaka pakati pavahedheni; kuti pavanokupomerai vachiti munoita zvakaipa, varumbidze Mwari nezuva rokushanyira kana vachiona mabasa enyu akanaka." 
1Peter2:13 Muzviise pasi pechirevo chimwe nechimwe chavanhu nokuda kwaIshe: kana ari mambo, nokuti ndiye mukuru;" 
1Peter2:14 kana vari vabati, nokuti vakatumwa naye kuti vatsive vanoita zvakaipa, uye varumbidze vanoita zvakanaka." 
1Peter2:15 Nokuti ndiko kuda kwaMwari, kuti nokuita kwenyu zvakanaka munyaradze kusaziva kwamapenzi;" 
1Peter2:16 savanhu vakasununguka, musingaiti kusununguka kwenyu kuti chive chifukidzo chezvakaipa, asi muve varanda vaMwari." 
1Peter2:17 Kudzai vanhu vose. Idai hama dzose. Ityai Mwari. Kudzai mambo. 
1Peter2:18 Varanda, teererai vatenzi venyu nokutya kwose, musingazviiti kuna vakanaka navanyoro bedzi, asi kuna vasakaruramawo." 
1Peter2:19 Nokuti ndidzo nyasha kana munhu achitsungirira mukutambudzika nokuda kwehana kuna Mwari, achitambudzika asina mhosva." 
1Peter2:20 Nokuti kune rumbidzo yeiko, kana muchitsungirira matadza, mukarohwa? Asi kana mukatsungirira kana muchiita zvakanaka mukatambudzika, izvozvo inyasha kuna Mwari." 
1Peter2:21 Nokuti makadanirwa izvozvo, Kristu zvaakakutambudzikiraiwo, akakusiyirai mufananidzo, kuti mutevere makwara ake;" 
1Peter2:22 iye asina kuita zvivi, nokunyengera hakuna kuonekwa mumuromo make;" 
1Peter2:23 iye akati achitukwa, haana kutukazve; akati achitambudzika, haana kutyisidzira; asi akaisa mhaka yake kuna iye anotonga zvakarurama;" 
1Peter2:24 iye akatakura amene zvivi zvedu mumuviri wake pamuti, kuti isu, kana tafa kuzvivi, tiraramire zvakarurama; iye wamakaporeswa namavanga ake." 
1Peter2:25 Nokuti makanga makatsauka samakwai; asi zvino madzokera kumufudzi nomutariri wemweya yenyu. 
1Peter3:1 Saizvozvo, imi vakadzi, ivai pasi pavarume venyu; kuti kunyangwe kana vamwe vasingateereri shoko, vadzorwe nomufambiro wavakadzi vavo pasina shoko rinorehwa," 
1Peter3:2 kana vachiona mufambiro wenyu, wakachena pamwechete nokutya Mwari." 
1Peter3:3 Kushonga kwenyu ngakurege kuva kwokunze, kwokuruka vhudzi, nokushonga ndarama, kana kupfeka nguo;" 
1Peter3:4 asi ngakuve munhu akavanzikawo mwoyo, akashonga zvisingaori zvomweya munyoro wakanyarara, unokosha, zvikuru pamberi paMwari." 
1Peter3:5 Nokuti saizvozvowo kare vakadzi vatsvene, vaitarira kuna Mwari, vakazvishongedza, vachizviisa pasi pavarume vavo," 
1Peter3:6 saSara waiteerera Abhurahamu, achimuti, “Ishe,” mava vana vake zvino, kana muchiita zvakanaka, musingatyiswi nechinhu chipi nechipi chinovhundusa." 
1Peter3:7 Saizvozvo imi varume, garai navakadzi venyu nokuziva, muchikudza mukadzi muchiti ndiye mudziyo une simba duku kwamuri, zvavari vadyi venhaka dzenyasha dzoupenyu pamwechete nemi; kuti minyengetero yenyu irege kudziviswa." 
1Peter3:8 Pakupedzisira, muve nomwoyo mumwe mose, munzwirane ngoni, mude hama, muve nomwoyo munyoro, muzvininipise;" 
1Peter3:9 musingatsivi zvakaipa nezvakaipa, kana kutuka nokutuka; asi muropafadze, nokuti ndizvo zvamakadanirwa, kuti mugare nhaka yokuropafadzwa." 
1Peter3:10 Nokuti, “Uyo, anoda upenyu, Nokuona mazuva akanaka, Ngaadzore rurimi rwake pane zvakaipa, Nemiromo yake, kuti irege kutaura zvinonyengera." 
1Peter3:11 Ngaanzvenge zvakaipa, aite zvakanaka; Ngaatsvake rugare, arutevere." 
1Peter3:12 Nokuti meso aIshe ari pamusoro pavakarurama, Nenzeve dzake pakukumbira kwavo. Asi chiso chaIshe chiri pamusoro pavanoita zvakaipa.”" 
1Peter3:13 Ndianiko achakuitirai zvakaipa, kana muchishingairira zvakanaka?" 
1Peter3:14 Asi kana muchitambudzika nokuda kwokururama, makaropafadzwa; musatya kutyisa kwavo, uye musakanganiswa." 
1Peter3:15 Asi itai Kristu mutsvene mumwoyo menyu ave Ishe; mugare makazvigadzira kupindura mumwe nomumwe anokubvunzai pamusoro petariro iri mukati menyu, asi muchiita nounyoro nokutya;" 
1Peter3:16 ivai nehana yakanaka, kuti pavanokucherai, ivo vanomhura mufambiro wenyu wakanaka muna Kristu, vanyadziswe." 
1Peter3:17 Nokuti zviri nani, kana kuri kuda kwaMwari, kuti mutambudzike kana muchiita zvakanaka, pakuti kana muchiita zvakaipa." 
1Peter3:18 Nokuti naKristu akatambudzikawo kamwechete pamusoro pezvivi, iye akarurama nokuda kwavasakarurama, kuti atiise kuna Mwari; akaurayiwa hake panyama, asi akararamiswa mumweya;" 
1Peter3:19 mauri akandoparidzirawo mweya iri mukusungwa," 
1Peter3:20 yakanga isina kuteerera kare, panguva iya mwoyo murefu waMwari uchimirira kugadzirwa kweareka pamazuva aNowa; mukati mayo vashoma, ivo vanhu vasere, vakaponeswa nemvura." 
1Peter3:21 Naiwo mufananidzo worubhabhatidzo, runokuponesai zvino, rusingarevi kubviswa kwetsvina yenyama, asi kutsvaka hana yakanaka kuna Mwari nokumuka kwaJesu Kristu;" 
1Peter3:22 iye ari kurudyi rwaMwari; akapinda kudenga, vatumwa namadzishe namasimba zvikaiswa pasi pake." 
1Peter4:1 Naizvozvo, Kristu zvaakatambudzika panyama, nemiwo mushonge murangariro iwoyo; nokuti munhu akatambudzika panyama arega zvivi;" 
1Peter4:2 kuti panguva yakasara panyama arege kurarama nokuchiva kwavanhu, asi nokuda kwaMwari." 
1Peter4:3 Nokuti nguva yakapfuura yakaringana kuita kuda kwavahedheni, nokufamba noutere, nokuchiva, nokunwa waini, nokutamba kwakaipa, namabira, nokunamata zvifananidzo zvisakafanira;" 
1Peter4:4 vanoshamiswa nechinhu ichi, kuti hamufambidzani navo pakusazvidzora kwavo uku kwakawanda, vachikureverai zvakaipa." 
1Peter4:5 Ivo vachazvidavirira kuna iye akazvigadzira kutonga vapenyu navakafa. 
1Peter4:6 Nokuti nokuda kwaizvozvi Vhangeri yakaparidzirwa vakafa, kuti vatongwe havo panyama nomutowo wavanhu, asi vararame nomutowo waMwari pamweya." 
1Peter4:7 Zvino kuguma kwezvinhu zvose kwava pedyo; naizvozvo ivai vakachenjera, musvinure kuti munyengetere." 
1Peter4:8 Zvikuru kune zvose danai norudo rukuru, nokuti rudo runofukidzira zvivi zvizhinji." 
1Peter4:9 Itiranai rudo pakati penyu kana muri vaeni, musinganyunyuti." 
1Peter4:10 Mumwe nomumwe sezvaakapiwa chipo chenyasha, shumiranai nacho savatariri vakanaka venyasha zhinji dzaMwari." 
1Peter4:11 Kana munhu achitaura, ngaataure saanenge ari mashoko aMwari; kana munhu achishumira, ngazviitwe nesimba raanopiwa naMwari; kuti Mwari akudzwe pazvose naJesu Kristu, iye ano kubwinya nesimba nokusingaperi–peri. Ameni." 
1Peter4:12 Vadikanwi, musashamiswa nokunyanyisa kwokuedzwa pakati penyu, kwakauya kukuedzai, muchiti mawirwa nechisingazikanwi;" 
1Peter4:13 asi farai zvamunogovana naKristu mukutambudzika kwake, kuti pakuonekwa kwokubwinya kwake mufarewo nomufaro mukuru." 
1Peter4:14 Kana muchizvidzwa nokuda kwezita raKristu, makaropafadzwa, nokuti Mweya wokubwinya waMwari ugere pamusoro penyu;" 
1Peter4:15 nokuti kurege kuva nomumwe wenyu achatambudzika nemhaka yokuti muurayi, kana mbavha, kana anoita zvakaipa, kana asingaregi zvavamwe;"
