1Peter4:16 asi kana munhu achitambudzika nokuda kwokuti mukristu, ngaarege kunyadziswa; asi ngaakudze Mwari nezita iri." 
1Peter4:17 Nokuti nguva yasvika yokuti kutonga kutange muimba yaMwari; zvino kana kukatanga kwatiri, kuguma kwavasingateereri Vhangeri yaMwari kuchagoveiko?" 
1Peter4:18 Uye kana zvichiremera akarurama kuti aponeswe, ko uyo, asingadi Mwari, nomutadzi, vachagoonekwepi?" 
1Peter4:19 Naizvozvo naivo, vanotambudzika nokuda kwaMwari, ngavaise mweya yavo kuMusiki akatendeka vachiita zvakanaka." 
1Peter5:1 Naizvozvo ndinorayira vakuru pakati penyu, ini mukuru pamwechete navo nechapupu chamatambudziko aKristu, nomugovani nawo wokubwinya kuchazoratidzwa, ndichiti:" 
1Peter5:2 Fudzai boka raMwari riri pakati penyu, musingazviiti nokurovererwa, asi nomwoyo unoda nokuda kwaMwari, musingazviiti nokuda kwokukarira pfuma yakaipa;" 
1Peter5:3 musingaiti nesimba nezvamakagoverwa, asi muve vatungamiriri veboka." 
1Peter5:4 Kana Mufudzi mukuru achizoonekwa, muchawana korona yokubwinya isingasvavi." 
1Peter5:5 Saizvozvo imi vaduku, muzviise pasi pavakuru, nemi mose pfekai kuzvininipisa mumwe kune mumwe, nokuti Mwari anodzivisa vanozvikudza, asi anopa nyasha vanozvininipisa." 
1Peter5:6 Naizvozvo zvininipisei pasi poruoko rune simba rwaMwari, kuti akukudzei nenguva yakafanira;" 
1Peter5:7 kandirai pamusoro pake kufunganya kwenyu kwose, nokuti iye anokuchengetai." 
1Peter5:8 Svinurai, murinde; muvengi wenyu Dhiabhori, anofamba–famba seshumba inorira, ichitsvaka waingaparadza." 
1Peter5:9 Mumudzivise, makamira nesimba pakutenda, muchiziva kuti kutambudzika ikoko kunoitirwa hama dzose dziri panyika." 
1Peter5:10 Zvino Mwari wenyasha dzose, iye akakudanirai kukubwinya kwake kusingaperi muna Kristu, kana mambotambudzika kanguva kaduku, achakukwanisai, nokukumisai, nokukusimbisai, nokukuteyai." 
1Peter5:11 Ngaave nesimba nokusingaperi–peri. Ameni. 
1Peter5:12 Ndakakunyorerai mashoko mashomanene naSirivhano, hama yakatendeka pakufunga kwangu, ndichirayira, nokupupura kuti idzi ndidzo nyasha dzechokwadi dzaMwari; mirai madziri." 
1Peter5:13 Chechi iri muBhabhironi, yakasanangurwa pamwechete nemi, naMako, mwanakomana wangu, vanokukwazisai." 
1Peter5:14 Kwazisanai nokutsvoda kworudo. Rugare ngaruve nemi mose muri muna Kristu. 
2Peter1:1 Simioni Petirosi, muranda nomupostori waJesu Kristu, kuna vakagoverwa kutenda kumwe nokwedu, kunokosha, nokururama kwaMwari wedu noMuponesi Jesu Kristu;" 
2Peter1:2 nyasha ngadzive nemi norugare ngaruwanzwe mukuziva Mwari naJesu, Ishe wedu;" 
2Peter1:3 nokuti nesimba rouMwari hwake takapiwa zvose zvinodikanwa muupenyu nomukunamata Mwari, nenzira yokumuziva iye akatidana nokubwinya kwake nokunaka;" 
2Peter1:4 akatipa nazvo zvipikirwa zvinokosha zvakakura kwazvo; kuti nazvo muve vanhu vakagoverwa umwari, matiza kuora kuri panyika nokuchiva." 
2Peter1:5 Zvino nemhaka iyi muchishingaira kwazvo wedzerai kunaka pakutenda kwenyu, napakunaka wedzerai kuziva;" 
2Peter1:6 napakuziva, kuzvidzora; napakuzvidzora, kutsungirira; napakutsungirira, kunamata Mwari;" 
2Peter1:7 napakunamata Mwari, kuda vatendi, napakuda vatendi, rudo." 
2Peter1:8 Nokuti kana mune zvinhu izvi, zvichiramba zvichiwanzwa, zvichakuitai vanhu vasina usimbe navasingashayiwi zvibereko mukuziva Ishe wedu, Jesu Kristu." 
2Peter1:9 Nokuti munhu, asina izvozvi ibofu, anoona zviri pedyo bedzi, akanganwa kusukwa kwezvivi zvake zvakare." 
2Peter1:10 Saka, hama dzangu, shingairai kwazvo kuti musimbise kudanwa nokusanangurwa kwenyu; nokuti kana muchiita izvozvi hamungatongogumburwi;" 
2Peter1:11 nokuti muchizviita muchazarurirwa zvakanaka kuti mupinde muushe husingaperi hwaIshe wedu, noMuponesi Jesu Kristu." 
2Peter1:12 Saka handingaregi kukuyeuchidzai zvinhu izvi nguva dzose, kunyangwe muchizviziva henyu, uye makasimba muchokwadi chamunacho." 
2Peter1:13 Ndinoti zvakanaka, kuti ndichiri mutabhenakeri ino ndikumutsei nokukuyeudzai;" 
2Peter1:14 ndichiziva kuti kubviswa kwetabhenakeri yangu kwava pedyo, sezvandakaratidzwa naIshe wedu Jesu Kristu." 
2Peter1:15 Zvino ndichashingaira, kuti mugogona kurangarira zvinhu izvi nguva dzose kana ndaenda." 
2Peter1:16 Nokuti hatina kutevera ngano dzakarukwa nouchenjeri, nguva yatakakuzivisai simba nokuuya kwaIshe wedu Jesu Kristu, asi takanga tiri vanhu vakaona umambo hwake." 
2Peter1:17 Nokuti iye akapiwa kukudzwa nokubwinya naMwari, Baba, panguva iya, yakauya izwi rakadai kwaari, richibva kukubwinya kukuru–kuru, richiti, “Uyu ndiye Mwanakomana wangu anodikanwa, wandinofarira.”" 
2Peter1:18 Izwi iri takarinzwa isu, richibva kudenga, nguva yatakanga tinaye mugomo dzvene." 
2Peter1:19 Uye tine shoko rouporofita rakasimba kwazvo, ramunoita zvakanaka kana muchiriteerera, rakaita somwenje unovhenekera mune rima, kusvikira utonga huchitsvuka, nenyamasase ichibudira mwoyo yenyu;" 
2Peter1:20 muchiziva pakutanga, kuti hakuna uporofita hworugwaro hunongodudzirwa nomunhu;" 
2Peter1:21 nokuti hakuna uporofita hwakatongouya nokuda kwomunhu, asi vanhu vaMwari vakataura, vachimutswa naMweya Mutsvene." 
2Peter2:1 Asi kwakanga kuna vaporofita venhema pakati pavanhu, sezvavachavapo pakati penyuwo vadzidzisi venhema, vachapinza pakavanda dzidziso dzakatsauka dzinoparadza, vachiramba naiye Tenzi akavatenga, vachizviwisira kuparadzwa kunokurumidza." 
2Peter2:2 Vazhinji vachatevera utere hwavo; nokuda kwavo nzira yezvokwadi ichazvidzwa. 
2Peter2:3 Pakukarira kwavo mari vachakunyengerai namashoko amano–mano; kutongwa kwavo, kwakatarwa kare, hakunonoki, nokuparadzwa kwavo hakukotsiri." 
2Peter2:4 Nokuti kana Mwari asina kurega vatumwa pavakatadza, asi akavakandira mugomba romoto akavasunga nengetani mumakomba erima ekutambudzika." 
2Peter2:5 akasaregawo nyika yekare asi akaponesa Nowa muparidzi wokururama pamwechete navamwe vanomwe, nguva yaakauyisa mvura zhinji panyika yavanhu vakanga vasingadi Mwari;" 
2Peter2:6 akashandura maguta eSodhoma neGomora akaaita madota, akaatongera kuti aparadzwe, akaaita chive chiratidzo kuna ivo vachagara vasingadi Mwari;" 
2Peter2:7 akasunungura Roti, akanga akarurama, akanga afa neshungu nokuda kwomufambiro woutere wavakashata," 
2Peter2:8 (nokuti munhu uyu akarurama, agere pakati pavo achiona nokunzwa, wakarwadzisa mweya wake wakarurama zuva rimwe nerimwe namabasa avo akanga asina kururama)." 
2Peter2:9 Ishe anoziva kusunungura pamiedzo vanonamata Mwari, nokuchengeta vasakarurama vave mukurohwa kusvikira pazuva rokutongwa;" 
2Peter2:10 zvikuru ivo vanofamba nomutoo wenyama pakuchiva kunosvibisa nokuzvidza ukuru; vanotsunga, vachiita nokuda kwavo, vasingatyi kutuka avo vane kubwinya." 
2Peter2:11 Vatumwa, kunyangwe vanovapfuura nesimba noukuru, havauyi pamberi paIshe nemhosva yokuvapomera nayo." 
2Peter2:12 Asi ava zvavanotuka zvavasingazivi, vakaita semhuka dzisina murangariro, dzakaberekwa kuti dzibatwe, dziparadzwe, naivo vachaparadzwa pakuora kwavo," 
2Peter2:13 vachiitirwa zvisakarurama, uri mubairo wokusarurama kwavo; vanhu vanoti, kutamba masikati ndizvo zvinofadza, ivo makwapa namavara, vanofara nokunyengera kwavo kana vachidya nemi;" 
2Peter2:14 vana meso azere noupombwe, asingaregi kutadza; vanonyengera vanhu vasina simba; vano mwoyo wakadzidziswa kuchiva; ivo vana vokutukwa;" 
2Peter2:15 vakasiya nzira yakarurama, vakatsauka, vakatevera nzira yaBharami, mwanakomana waBheori, akada mubairo wokusarurama;" 
2Peter2:16 asi akarairwa pamusoro pokudarika kwake, nokuti mbongoro, isingagoni kutaura, yakataura nezwi romunhu, ikadzivisa kupenga kwomuporofita." 
2Peter2:17 Ivava matsime asina mvura, mhute rinodzingwa nemhepo; ivo vakachengeterwa kusviba kwerima." 
2Peter2:18 Nokuti nokutaura kwavo mashoko mazhinji okuzvikudza asina maturo, vanonyengera pakuchiva kwenyama noutere, avo vachangotiza vachibva kuna vanogara pakutsauka;" 
2Peter2:19 vachivapikira kusunungurwa, nyamba ivo vamene vari varanda vakuora; nokuti waakundwa naye, munhu anoitwa muranda wake." 
2Peter2:20 Nokuti ivo, kana nenzira yokuziva Ishe, Muponesi Jesu Kristu, vambotiza havo zvinosvibisa zvenyika, kana vakabatwa nokukundwazve nazvo, kuguma kwavo kwaipa kupfuura kutanga kwavo." 
2Peter2:21 Nokuti zvaiva nani kwavari kana vasaiziva nzira yokururama, pakuti vadzoke pamurairo mutsvene wavakapiwa, wavakanga vambouziva havo." 
2Peter2:22 Zvinorehwa netsumo yechokwadi ndizvo zvakaitwa kwavari, zvinoti, “Imbwa yakadzokera kumarutsi ayo,” “Nenguruve yakanga yashambidzwa, kuumburuka mumatope.”" 
2Peter3:1 Vadikanwi, iyi ndiyo tsamba yechipiri yandinokunyorerai zvino; pane idzodzi dzose mbiri ndinomutsa ndangariro dzenyu ndichikuyeudzirai;" 
2Peter3:2 kuti mugorangarira mashoko akataurwa kare navaporofita vatsvene, nomurairo waIshe, Muponesi, wamakapiwa navapostori venyu;" 
2Peter3:3 pakutanga muzive henyu chinhu ichi, kuti pamazuva okupedzisira vaseki vachauya vachiseka, vachifamba nokuchiva kwavo," 
2Peter3:4 vachiti, “Chipikirwa chokuuya kwake chiripiko zvino? Nokuti kubva pakuparara kwamadzibaba, zvinhu zvose zvinongoramba zvakaita sezvazvakanga zvakaita kubva pakutanga kwokusikwa.”" 
2Peter3:5 Nokuti vanokanganwa nohwoni chinhu ichi, kuti kare denga raivapo, nenyika yakabudiswa mumvura, yakaitwa nemvura neshoko raMwari;" 
2Peter3:6 nazvo nyika, yaivapo nguva iyo, yakafukidzwa nemvura ikaparadzwa;" 
2Peter3:7 asi denga, riripo zvino, nenyika, zvakavigirwa moto neshoko irori, zvinochengetererwa zuva rokutonga, nerokuparadzwa kwavanhu vasingadi Mwari." 
2Peter3:8 Asi vadikanwi, musakanganwa chinhu chimwe ichi, kuti kuna Ishe zuva rimwe rakaita samakore ane chiuru, namakore ane chiuru sezuva rimwe." 
2Peter3:9 Ishe haanonoki kuita sezvaakapikira, sezvinoreva vamwe vachiti, “Anonoka, asi ano mwoyo murefu kwamuri, nokuti haadi kuti vamwe varashike, asi kuti vose vatendeuke.”" 
2Peter3:10 Asi zuva raIshe richauya sembavha; naro denga richapfuura nokutinhira kukuru, nezvedenga zvichaparadzwa zvichipiswa, nenyika namabasa ari mairi achapiswa." 
2Peter3:11 Izvi zvose zvazvichaparadzwa saizvozvo, imi munofanira kuva vanhu vakadiniko pamufambiro wenyu mutsvene nokunamata Mwari," 
2Peter3:12 imi munotarira nokushuvawo kwazvo kuuya kwezuva raMwari; naro denga richaparadzwa nokutsva, nezvedenga zvichanyauka zvichipiswa." 
2Peter3:13 Asi sezvaakapikira, tinotarira denga idzva nenyika itsva, munogara kururama mazviri." 
2Peter3:14 Saka vadikanwi, zvamunotarira zvinhu izvi, shingairai kuti muwanikwe naye muno rugare, musina ruvara, musina mhosva;" 
2Peter3:15 muchiti, mwoyo murefu waIshe wedu ruponeso; saPauro, hama yedu inodikanwa, akakunyoreraiwo nokuchenjera kwaakapiwa;" 
2Peter3:16 sezvaanotaura mumatsamba ake ose pamusoro pezvinhu izvi; madziri mune zvimwe zvikukutu kunzwisiswa; zvinominamiswa, samamwe magwarowo, navasingazivi navasina simba, kusvikira vaparadzwa." 
2Peter3:17 Naizvozvo imi vadikanwi, zvamunoziva zvinhu izvi zvisati zvaitwa, chenjerai kuti murege kurashwa nokutsauka kwavakashata, muve pakusimba kwenyu." 
2Peter3:18 Asi kurai munyasha napakuziva Ishe wedu, Muponesi Jesu Kristu. Ngaave nokubwinya zvino, nokusingaperi. Ameni."

Jude1:4 Nokuti kuna vamwe varume vakapinda pakavanda, vakagara vaisirwa kare kutongwa uku, vanhu vasingadi Mwari, vanoshandura nyasha dzaMwari wedu vachidziita utere, vachiramba Tenzi uyu mumwechete, Ishe wedu Jesu Kristu."

Jude1:10 Asi vanhu ava vanotuka zvavasingazivi; napazvinhu izvo, zvavanonzwisisa kubva pakuberekwa kwavo, semhuka dzisingazivi, vanoparadzwa pazviri."

Jude1:13 mafungu egungwa anopenga, anopupuma nyadzi dzawo; nyenyedzi dzinofamba–famba, vakachengetererwa kusviba kwerima nokusingaperi."

Jude1:16 Ivo vanyunyuti vasingatendi nezvavanazvo, vanofamba nokuchiva kwavo; (miromo yavo inotaura mashoko okuzvikudza), vachikudza vanhu nokuda kwokufumiswa."

Revelation2:1 “Nyorera mutumwa wechechi iri paEfeso uti, ‘Zvanzi naiye akabata nyenyedzi nomwe muruoko rwake rworudyi, anofamba pakati pezvigadziko zvemwenje zvinomwe zvendarama." 
Revelation2:2 Ndinoziva mabasa ako, nokutambudzika kwako, nokutsungirira kwako, uye kuti haudi kuonana navanhu vakaipa; wakavaedza ivo vanoti, tiri vapostori, vasi ivo chaivo, ukavawana vari venhema;" 
Revelation2:3 ukatsungirira nokuva nomwoyo murefu nokuda kwezita rangu, ukasaneta." 
Revelation2:4 Asi handifari nechinhu ichi kwauri, kuti wakasiya rudo rwako rwokutanga." 
Revelation2:5 Naizvozvo rangarira pawakawa, utendeuke, ugoita mabasa ako okutanga; kana usingaiti saizvozvo, ndichauya kwauri; ndikabvisa chigadziko chako chomwenje panzvimbo yacho, kana usingatendeuki." 
Revelation2:6 Asi chinhu ichi unacho, kuti unovenga mabasa avaNikoraiti, andinovenga neniwo." 
Revelation2:7 Ane nzeve, ngaanzwe zvinoreva Mweya kuchechi; anokunda, ndichamutendera kuti adye muti woupenyu, uri muParadhiso yaMwari.’" 
Revelation2:8 “Nyorera mutumwa wechechi iri paSimena, uti: ‘Zvanzi naiye wokutanga nowokupedzisira, akanga afa, akararamazve.’" 
Revelation2:9 “Ndinoziva kutambudzika kwako nourombo hwako, (asi uri mupfumi), nokutuka kwaivo vanoti, tiri vaJudha, vasi ivo chaivo, asi isinagoge raSatani," 
Revelation2:10 usatya izvo zvauchatambudzika nazvo. Tarira, Dhiabhori woda kuisa vamwe venyu mutorongo, kuti muedzwe; muchatambudzika mazuva ane gumi. Uve wakatendeka kusvikira parufu, ndigokupa korona youpenyu." 
Revelation2:11 “Ane nzveve, ngaanzwe zvinoreva Mweya kuchechi; anokunda, haangakuvadzwi norufu rwechipiri." 
Revelation2:12 “Nyorera mutumwa wechechi iri paPegamamu uti: ‘Zvanzi naiye ano munondo, unopinza, unocheka kwose.’" 
Revelation2:13 Ndinoziva paunogara, ndipo pane chigaro choushe chaSatani; wakabatisisa zita rangu, ukasaramba kutenda kwangu, kunyangwe napamazuva aAndipasi, chapupu changu, munhu wangu akatendeka, akaurayiwa pakati penyu, apo panogara Satani." 
Revelation2:14 Asi handifari nezvimwe zvinhu zvishoma kwauri, nokuti una vamwepo vanobatisisa dzidziso yaBharami, akadzidzisa Bharaki kuisa chigumbuso pamberi pavana VaIsiraeri, nokuti vadye zvakabayirwa zvifananidzo, nokuita upombwe." 
Revelation2:15 Nokudaro una vamwewo vanobatisisa saizvozvo dzidziso yavaNikoraiti. 
Revelation2:16 Naizvozvo tendeuka; kana usingaiti saizvozvo, ndichakurumidza kuuya kwauri, ndigorwa navo nomunondo womuromo wangu." 
Revelation2:17 “Ane nzeve, ngaanzwe zvinoreva Mweya kuchechi. Anokunda, ndichamupa mana yakavanzika, uye ndichamupa ibwe jena, napabwe iro zita idzva rakanyorwapo, risingazikanwi nomunhu, asi naiye anoripiwa." 
Revelation2:18 “Nyorera mutumwa wechechi iri paTiatira uti, ‘Zvanzi noMwanakomana waMwari, ana meso akafanana nomurazvo womoto, netsoka dzake dzakaita sesafuri inopenya.’" 
Revelation2:19 Ndinoziva mabasa ako, norudo, nokutenda, nokushumira, nokutsungirira kwako, uye kuti mabasa ako okupedzisira anopfuura okutanga." 
Revelation2:20 “Asi handifari nechinhu ichi kwauri, kuti unotendera uya mukadzi Jezebheri, anozviidza muporofitakadzi, uye anodzidzisa nokutsausa varanda vangu, kuti vaite upombwe, nokudya zvakabayirwa zvifananidzo." 
Revelation2:21 Ndakamupa nguva kuti atendeuke; akaramba kutendeuka pakufeva kwake. 
Revelation2:22 Tarira, ndoda kumukandira panhoo; navanoita upombwe naye panhamo huru, kana vasingatendeuki pamabasa avo." 
Revelation2:23 Navana vake ndichavauraya norufu; nechechi dzose dzichaziva kuti ndini ndinonzvera itsvo nemwoyo, ndichapa mumwe nomumwe wenyu paakabata napo." 
Revelation2:24 Asi kwamuri, imi makasara paTiatira, vose vasina dzidziso iyi, vasingazivi izvo zvavanoti, ‘Zvakadzika zvaSatani,’ ndinoti kwamuri: Handingakutakudziyi mumwe mutoro." 
Revelation2:25 Asi batisai izvo zvamunazvo kusvikira ndichiuya. 
Revelation2:26 “Anokunda achichengeta mabasa angu kusvikira pakupedzisira, ndichamupa simba pamusoro pamarudzi;" 
Revelation2:27 achaafudza netsvimbo yedare, sehari dzomuumbi dzinoputsanyiwawo; sezvandakapiwawo naBaba vangu." 
Revelation2:28 Uye ndichamupa nyamatsatsi. 
Revelation2:29 Ane nzeve, ngaanzwe zvinoreva Mweya kuchechi." 
Revelation3:1 “Nyorera mutumwa wechechi iri paSadhisi uti: ‘Zvanzi naiye ane mweya minomwe yaMwari, nenyenyedzi nomwe.’ Ndinoziva mabasa ako, kuti unonzi uri mupenyu asi wakafa." 
Revelation3:2 Pepuka, usimbise izvo zvakasara, zvakanga zvoda kufa; nokuti handina kuwana mabasa ako ari akakwana pamberi paMwari wangu." 
Revelation3:3 “Naizvozvo rangarira kuti wakagamuchira nokunzwa sei; uzvichengete, utendeuke. Naizvozvo kana usingapepuki, ndichauya sembavha, haungazivi nguva yandichakuwira nayo." 
Revelation3:4 Asi unamazita mashoma paSadhisi avanhu vasina kusvibisa nguo dzavo; vachafamba neni vane nguo chena, nokuti vakafanirwa nazvo." 
Revelation3:5 Anokunda, achapfekedzwa saizvozvo nguo chena; handingatongodzimi zita rake pabhuku roupenyu, ndichapupura zita rake pamberi paBaba vangu, napamberi pavatumwa vake." 
Revelation3:6 “Ane nzeve, ngaanzwe zvinoreva Mweya kuchechi." 
Revelation3:7 “Nyorera mutumwa wechechi iri paFiradherifia, uti: ‘Zvanzi naiye mutsvene, iye wechokwadi, iye ane kiyi yaDhavhidhi, iye anoti kana achizarura, hakuna anopfiga, kana achipfiga hakuna anozarura:" 
Revelation3:8 Ndinoziva mabasa ako, (tarira, ndakaisa pamberi pako musuwo wakazaruka, hakuna angagona kuupfiga), ndinoziva kuti une simba shoma hako; wakachengeta shoko rangu, ukasaramba zita rangu." 
Revelation3:9 Tarira ndinokupa vamwe vari vesinagoge raSatani, vanoti, tiri vaJudha, vasi ivo chaivo, asi vanoreva nhema; tarira, ndichavauyisa kuti vanamate pamberi petsoka dzako, uye vazive kuti ndakakuda." 
Revelation3:10 Zvawakachengeta shoko rokutsungirira kwangu, ndichakuchengetawo panguva yokuedzwa yoda kuuya panyika yose, kuedza vanogara panyika." 
Revelation3:11 Ndinokurumidza kuuya; batisisa icho chaunacho, kuti urege kutorerwa korona yako." 
Revelation3:12 Anokunda ndichamuita mbiru mutemberi yaMwari wangu, haangazobudimozve; ndichanyora pamusoro pake zita raMwari wangu, nezita reguta raMwari wangu, Jerusaremu idzva rinoburuka kudenga kuna Mwari wangu, nezita rangu idzva.’" 
Revelation3:13 “Ane nzeve, ngaanzwe zvinoreva Mweya kuchechi." 
Revelation3:14 “Nyorera mutumwa wechechi iri paRaodhikia uti: “Zvanzi naAmeni, chapupu chakatendeka, chechokwadi, kutanga kwezvisikwa zvaMwari." 
Revelation3:15 Ndinoziva mabasa ako, kuti hautonhori kana kupisa. Dai uchitonhora kana kupisa." 
Revelation3:16 Zvino zvaunodziya, usingatonhori kana kupisa, ndichakusvisvina mumuromo mangu." 
Revelation3:17 “Nokuti unoti, ‘Ndakapfuma, ndakapfumiswa; handishayiwi chinhu;’ usingazivi, kuti ndiwe uno urombo nenhamo, uri murombo nebofu usina chokufuka." 
Revelation3:18 “Ndinokupa zano kuti utenge kwandiri ndarama yakaedzwa mumoto, kuti uve nepfuma, nenguo chena, kuti ufukidze; nyadzi dzokusafuka kwako dzirege kuonekwa; nechizoro chameso, kuti uzore meso ako, uone." 
Revelation3:19 Vose vandinoda ndinovaranga nokuvarova; naizvozvo shingaira utendeuke. 
Revelation3:20 Tarira, ndimire pasuwo, ndichigogodza; kana munhu akanzwa izwi rangu, akazarura musuwo, ndichapinda kwaari, ndicharayira naye, naiye neni." 
Revelation3:21 Anokunda ndichamupa chinhu ichi, kuti agare neni pachigaro changu choushe, seniwo ndakakunda, ndikagara pamwechete naBaba vangu pachigaro chavo choushe." 
Revelation3:22 “Ane nzeve, ngaanzwe zvinoreva Mweya kuchechi.”" 
Revelation4:1 Shure kwaizvozvi, ndakatarira ndikaona musuwo wakazaruka kudenga; nezwi rokutanga randakanzwa rakaita sehwamanda richitaura neni, richiti, “Kwira pano, ndigokuratidza zvinofanira kuitwa shure kwaizvozvi.”" 
Revelation4:2 Pakarepo ndakava muMweya; tarira chigaro choushe chakagadzwa kudenga, nomumwe agere pachigaro." 
Revelation4:3 Iye akanga agerepo akanga akafanana nebwe rejasipisi neresaridhio; kwakanga kuno muraraungu wakakomberedza chigaro choushe, wakafanana nebwe resimaragidhino." 
Revelation4:4 Kwakanga kune zvigaro zvoushe zvina makumi maviri namana zvakanga zvakakomberedza chigaro choushe; napazvigaro pakanga pagere vakuru vana makumi maviri navana, vakapfeka nguo chena; vakanga vane korona dzendarama pamisoro yavo." 
Revelation4:5 Napachigaro choushe pakanga pachibuda mheni, namazwi, nokutinhira; nemwenje minomwe yakanga ichipfuta pamberi pechigaro choushe, iri Mweya minomwe yaMwari." 
Revelation4:6 Pamberi pechigaro choushe pakanga pane gungwa rakaonekera, rakafanana nekristaro; napakati pechigaro choushe, napamativi ose echigaro choushe, pakanga pane zvisikwa zvina zvipenyu, zvizere nameso mberi neshure kwazvo." 
Revelation4:7 Chisikwa chipenyu chokutanga chakanga chakafanana neshumba, chisikwa chipenyu chechipiri chakanga chakafanana nemhuru, chisikwa chipenyu chechitatu chakanga chine chiso chakaita sechomunhu, nechisikwa chipenyu chechina chakanga chakafanana negondo rinobhururuka." 
Revelation4:8 Nezvisikwa zvipenyu izvi zvina zvakanga zvina mapapiro matanhatu, chimwe nechimwe; zvakanga zvizere nameso kunhivi dzose nomukati; hazvizorori masikati nousiku, zvichiti, “Mutsvene, mutsvene, mutsvene, iye Ishe Mwari, waMasimbaose, iye akanga aripo, aripo, noachazouya.”" 
Revelation4:9 Zvino kana zvisikwa zvipenyu izvi zvovigira iye anogara pachigaro choushe, iye ari mupenyu nokusingaperi–peri, kubwinya, nokukudzwa, nokuvonga." 
Revelation4:10 Vakuru vana makumi maviri navana vowira pasi pamberi paiye agere pachigaro choushe, vachinamata iye, ari mupenyu nokusingaperi–peri, vachikandira korona dzavo pamberi pechigaro choushe, vachiti," 
Revelation4:11 “Imi Ishe, Mwari wedu, makafanira kuti muvigirwe kubwinya, nokukudzwa, nesimba, nokuti ndimi makasika zvinhu zvose, zvakavapo, zvikasikwa nokuda kwenyu.”" 
Revelation5:1 Zvino ndakaona muruoko rworudyi rwaiye akanga agere pachigaro choushe bhuku rakanyorwa mukati nokunze kwaro, rakanamatidzwa nezvisimbiso zvinomwe." 
Revelation5:2 Ipapo ndakaona mutumwa, ane simba, achidanidzira nezwi guru, achiti, “Ndianiko akafanira kuti azarure bhuku iri, nokusunungura zvisimbiso zvaro?”" 
Revelation5:3 Asi kwakanga kusina munhu kudenga napanyika, kana napasi nepanyika, akagona kuzarura bhuku iro, kana kutarira mariri." 
Revelation5:4 Ipapo ndakachema zvikuru, zvakusina kuwanikwa munhu, akafanira kuti azarure bhuku, kana kutarira mariri." 
Revelation5:5 Zvino mumwe waVakuru akati kwandiri; “Usachema hako, tarira, Shumba yorudzi rwaJudha, Mudzi waDhavhidhi, yakakunda kuti izarure bhuku nezvisimbiso zvayo zvinomwe.”" 
Revelation5:6 Zvino ndakaona pakati pechigaro choushe nezvisikwa zvipenyu zvina, napakati paVakuru, Gwayana rimire, rakaita serakabayiwa, rine nyanga nomwe nameso manomwe, iri Mweya minomwe yaMwari, yakatumwa kunyika yose." 
Revelation5:7 Iro rikauya, rikatora bhuku muruoko rworudyi rwaiye akanga agere pachigaro choushe." 
Revelation5:8 Zvino rakati ratora bhuku, zvisikwa zvipenyu zvina naVakuru vana makumi maviri navana vakawira pasi pamberi peGwayana, mumwe nomumwe anorudimbwa, nendiro dzendarama, dzakanga dzizere nezvinonhuwira, iri minyengetero yavatsvene." 
Revelation5:9 Vakaimba rwiyo rutsva, vachiti, “Ndimi makafanira kuti mutore bhuku nokuzarura zvisimbiso zvayo; nokuti makabayiwa, makatengera Mwari neropa renyu vanhu vanobva kumarudzi ose, nendimi dzose, navanhu vose, nendudzi dzose;" 
Revelation5:10 mukavaitira Mwari wedu, kuti vave ushe navapristi, vabate ushe panyika.”" 
Revelation5:11 Zvino ndakaona, ndikanzwa izwi ravatumwa vazhinji vakanga vakakomberedza chigaro choushe nezvisikwa zvipenyu, naVakuru. Kuwanda kwavo kwakanga kuri zviuru zvezviuru nezviuru zvamazana" 
Revelation5:12 vachiti nezwi guru, “Gwayana rakabayiwa rakafanira kuti rivigirwe ushe, nepfuma, nokuchenjera, nesimba, nokukudzwa, nokubwinya, nokurumbidzwa.”" 
Revelation5:13 Ndikanzwa zvisikwa zvipenyu zvose zviri kudenga, napanyika, nezviri pasi penyika, napagungwa, nezvose zviri mukati mazvo, zvichiti, “Kurumbidzwa, nokukudzwa, nokubwinya, nesimba ngazvive kuna iye agere pamusoro pechigaro choushe, nokuGwayana nokusingaperi–peri.”" 
Revelation5:14 Ipapo zvisikwa zvipenyu zvina zvakati, “Ameni.” Vakuru vana makumi maviri navanavo vakawira pasi, vakanamata." 
Revelation6:1 Zvino ndakaona Gwayana richizarura chimwe chezvisimbiso zvinomwe, ndikanzwa chimwe chezvisikwa zvipenyu zvina chichiti nezwi romutinhiro, “Uya!”" 
Revelation6:2 Ndikatarira, ndikaona bhiza jena, naiye akanga akaritasva, akanga anohuta; akapiwa korona, akabuda achikunda, uye kuti akunde." 
Revelation6:3 Akati azarura chisimbiso chechipiri, ndikanzwa chisikwa chipenyu chechipiri chichiti, “Uya!”" 
Revelation6:4 Ipapo rimwe bhiza rakabuda riri dzvuku; akanga akaritasva akapiwa simba kuti abvise rugare panyika, kuti vaurayane; akapiwa munondo mukuru." 
Revelation6:5 Akati azarura chisimbiso chechitatu, ndikanzwa chisikwa chipenyu chechitatu chichiti, “Uya!” Ndikatarira, ndikaona bhiza dema; akanga akaritasva akanga ane chiyereso muruoko rwake." 
Revelation6:6 Ndikanzwa izwi pakati pezvisikwa zvipenyu zvina, richiti, “Chiyero chezviyo chichatengwa nedhinari, nezviyero zvitatu zvebhari nedhinari; usatadzira mafuta newaini.”" 
Revelation6:7 Akati azarura chisimbiso chechina, ndikanzwa izwi rechisikwa chipenyu chechina richiti, “Uya!”" 
Revelation6:8 Ndikatarira, ndikaona bhiza rakachenuruka; akanga akaritasva, zita rake Rufu; uye Hadhesi rakamutevera. Ivo vakapiwa simba pamusoro pechechina chenyika, kuti vauraye nomunondo, nenzara, norufu, nezvikara zvenyika." 
Revelation6:9 Akati azarura chisimbiso chechishanu, ndikaona panyasi peatari mweya yavanhu vakanga vaurayiwa nokuda kweshoko raMwari, nokupupura kwavo kwavakapupura;" 
Revelation6:10 vakadana nezwi guru vachiti, “Tenzi mutsvene wechokwadi, mucharega kutonga vanogara panyika nokutsiva ropa redu kusvikira rinhiko?”" 
Revelation6:11 Ipapo mumwe nomumwe wavo akapiwa nguo chena; vakaudzwa kuti vambozorora chinguva chiduku, kusvikira vamwe varanda pamwechete navo nehama dzavo, dzaifanira kuurayiwa saivo, varinganiswa vose." 
Revelation6:12 Zvino ndakaona pakazarura kwake chisimbiso chechitanhatu, kwakanga kunokudengenyika kwenyika kukuru, zuva rakasviba segudza remvere, mwedzi wose ukaita seropa;" 
Revelation6:13 nenyenyedzi dzedenga dzikawira pasi, somuonde unozuza maganga awo, kana uchizununguswa nomututu mukuru." 
Revelation6:14 Denga rikabva sebhuku, kana richipetwa; namakomo ose nezviwi zvose zvakabviswa panzvimbo dzazvo." 
Revelation6:15 Namadzimambo enyika, navakuru, navatungamiriri vehondo, navapfumi, navane simba, navaranda vose, navakasununguka vose, vakandovanda mumapako nomumabwe amakomo;" 
Revelation6:16 vakati kumakomo nokumabwe, “Tiwirei, mutivige pameso aiye anogara pachigaro choushe, napakutsamwa kweGwayana;" 
Revelation6:17 nokuti zuva guru rokutsamwa kwavo rakasvika; ndianiko anogona kumira?” 
Revelation7:1 Shure kwaizvozvi ndakaona vatumwa vana, vamire kumativi mana enyika, vakabata mhepo ina dzenyika, kuti mhepo irege kurira panyika, kana pagungwa, kana pamiti yose." 
Revelation7:2 Ipapo ndakaona mumwe mutumwa achikwira achibva kumabvazuva, ane chisimbiso chaMwari mupenyu; akadana nezwi guru kuvatumwa vana, vaya vakanga vapiwa simba kuti vatadzire nyika negungwa," 
Revelation7:3 achiti, “Musatadzira nyika, kana gungwa, kana miti, kusvikira taisa chisimbiso pahuma dzavaranda vaMwari.”" 
Revelation7:4 Ndikanzwa kuwanda kwavakaiswa chisimbiso; vane zviuru zvine zana namakumi mana nezvina, vakaiswa chisimbiso vachibva kumarudzi ose avana VaIsiraeri." 
Revelation7:5 Kurudzi rwaJudha vakaiswa chisimbiso vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviri; Kurudzi rwaRubheni vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri; Kurudzi rwaGadhi vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri; 
Revelation7:6 Kurudzi rwaAseri vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri; Kurudzi rwaNefitarimi vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri; Kurudzi rwaManase vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri; 
Revelation7:7 Kurudzi rwaSimioni vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviri; Kurudzi rwaRevhi vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri; Kurudzi rwaIsakari vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviri; 
Revelation7:8 Kurudzi rwaZabhuroni vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri; Kurudzi rwaJosefa vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri; Kurudzi rwaBhenjamini vakaiswa chisimbiso vane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri. 
Revelation7:9 Shure kwaizvozvo ndakatarira, ndikaona vazhinjizhinji vasingagoni kuverengwa nomunhu, vakabva kundudzi dzose, namarudzi, navanhu, nendimi, vamire pamberi pechigaro choushe, napamberi peGwayana, vakapfeka nguo chena, vakabata muchindwe mumaoko avo;" 
Revelation7:10 vakadanidzira nezwi guru, vachiti, “Ruponeso ngaruve kuna Mwari anogara pachigaro choushe, nokuGwayana.”" 
Revelation7:11 Ipapo vatumwa vose vakamira, vakakomba chigaro choushe, naVakuru, nezvisikwa zvipenyu zvina, vakawira pasi nechiso pamberi pechigaro choushe, vakanamata Mwari," 
Revelation7:12 vachiti, “Ameni: Kurumbidzwa, nokubwinya, nokuchenjera, nokuvonga, nokukudzwa, noushe, nesimba, ngazvive kuna Mwari nokusingaperi–peri. Ameni!”" 
Revelation7:13 Ipapo mumwe waVakuru akapindura, akati kwandiri, “Ava vakapfeka nguo chena ndivanaaniko? Vanobvepiko?”" 
Revelation7:14 Ndikati kwaari, “Ndivo vanobva mukutambudzika kukuru, vakasuka nguo dzavo vakadzichenesa muropa reGwayana.”" 
Revelation7:15 Naizvozvo vari pamberi pechigaro choushe chaMwari, vanomushumira masikati nousiku mutemberi yake; iye, anogara pachigaro choushe, achavadzitira netabhenakeri." 
Revelation7:16 Havachazoziyi nenzara, havachazofi nenyota; havangapiswi nezuva kana nokumwe kupisa;" 
Revelation7:17 nokuti Gwayana riri pakati pechigaro choushe richavafudza, richavatungamirira kumatsime emvura youpenyu; Mwari achapukuta misodzi yose kumeso avo." 
Revelation8:1 Wakati azarura chisimbiso chechinomwe, kunyarara kukavapo kudenga kunenge sehafu yenguva." 
Revelation8:2 Ipapo ndakaona vatumwa vanomwe vamire pamberi paMwari; vakapiwa hwamanda nomwe. 
Revelation8:3 Zvino mumwe mutumwa akauya, akamira paatari, anomudziyo wendarama wezvinonhuwira; akapiwa zvinonhuwira zvizhinji kuti azviise pamwechete neminyengetero yavatsvene vose pamusoro peatari yendarama, yakanga iri pamberi pechigaro choushe." 
Revelation8:4 Utsi hwezvinonhuwira hukakwira pamberi paMwari huchibva muruoko rwomutumwa pamwechete neminyengetero yavatsvene. 
Revelation8:5 Mutumwa akatora mudziyo wezvinonhuwira, akauzadza nomoto weatari, akaukandira panyika; ipapo kwakauya kutinhira, namazwi, nemheni, nokudengenyeka kwenyika." 
Revelation8:6 Ipapo vatumwa vanomwe vakanga vane hwamanda nomwe, vakazvigadzira kuti varidze." 
Revelation8:7 Wokutanga akaridza, kukauya chimvuramabwe nomoto zvakavhenganiswa neropa, zvikakandirwa panyika; ipapo chetatu chenyika chikatsva, nechetatu chemiti chikatsva, nouswa hutema hwose hwakatsva." 
Revelation8:8 Zvino mutumwa wechipiri akaridza, chimwe chakaita segomo guru rinopfuta moto chikakandwa mugungwa; ipapo chetatu chegungwa chikashanduka ropa;" 
Revelation8:9 chetatu chezvisikwa zvakanga zviri mugungwa zvikafa, izvo, zvakanga zvino upenyu; nechetatu chezvikepe chikaparadzwa." 
Revelation8:10 Zvino mutumwa wechitatu akaridza, nyenyedzi huru, yakapfuta sezhenje, ikawa kudenga, ikawira pamusoro pechetatu chenzizi napamatsime emvura;" 
Revelation8:11 zita renyenyedzi rakanga richinzi, “Chinovava;” ipapo chetatu chemvura chikavaviswa, vanhu vazhinji vakafa nemvura, nokuti yakanga yavaviswa." 
Revelation8:12 Zvino mutumwa wechina akaridza, chetatu chezuva chikarohwa, nechetatu chomwedzi, nechetatu chenyenyedzi, kuti chetatu chazvo chisvibiswe, uye kuti chetatu chamasikati chirege kuvhenekera, nousiku saizvozvo." 
Revelation8:13 Ipapo ndakatarira, ndikanzwa gondo rimwe richibhururuka pakati pedenga, richiti nezwi guru, “Nhamo, nhamo, nhamo, kuna vanogara panyika, nokuda kwamazwi mamwe ehwamanda avatumwa vatatu vachazoridza.”" 
Revelation9:1 Zvino mutumwa wechishanu akaridza, ndikaona nyenyedzi, yakabva kudenga, yawira pasi; ikapiwa kiyi yegomba rakadzika–dzika." 
Revelation9:2 Ikazarura gomba rakadzika–dzika, hutsi hukakwira huchibva mugomba, sohutsi hwevira guru; zuva nedenga zvikasvibiswa nohutsi hwegomba." 
Revelation9:3 Muhutsi makabuda mhashu dzikauya panyika, dzikapiwa simba sesimba rezvinyavada zvenyika." 
Revelation9:4 Dzikaudzwa kuti dzirege kutadzira uswa hwenyika, nechinhu chinyoro, kana miti yose, asi vanhu bedzi vasina chisimbiso chaMwari pahuma dzavo." 
Revelation9:5 Hadzina kupiwa basa rokuvauraya, asi kuti varwadziswe mwedzi mishanu; kurwadzisa kwadzo kwakanga kwakaita sokurwadzisa kwechinyavada, kana chichiruma munhu." 
Revelation9:6 Namazuva iwayo vanhu vachatsvaka rufu, asi havangatongoruwani, vachavinga kufa, asi rufu ruchavatiza." 
Revelation9:7 Pakuonekwa kwadzo mhashu dzakanga dzakaita samabhiza akagadzirirwa kurwa; pamisoro yadzo pakanga panezvimwe zvakaita sekorona dzakafanana nendarama; zviso zvadzo zvakanga zvakaita sezviso zvavanhu. 
Revelation9:8 Dzakanga dzine vhudzi rakaita sevhudzi ravakadzi, nameso adzo akanga akaita seeshumba." 
Revelation9:9 Dzakanga dzine zvidzitiro zvechipfuva zvakaita sezvamatare; nokutinhira kwamapapiro adzo kwakaita sokutinhira kwengoro dzamabhiza mazhinji anomhanyira kurwa. 
Revelation9:10 Dzakanga dzine miswe, yakaita seyezvinyavada, noumborera; pamiswe yadzo pakanga pane simba rokukuvadza vanhu mwedzi mishanu." 
Revelation9:11 Dzakanga dzina mambo wadzo, ari mutumwa wegomba rakadzika–dzika, zita rake neChiHebheru ndiAbhadhoni, neChiGiriki zita rake ndiAporioni." 
Revelation9:12 Nhamo imwe yapfuura; tarira, nhamo dzimwe mbiri dzinotevera shure kwaizvozvi." 
Revelation9:13 Zvino mutumwa wechitanhatu akaridza, ndikanzwa izwi richibva panyanga ina dzeatari yendarama yakanga iri pamberi paMwari," 
Revelation9:14 richiti kumutumwa wechitanhatu akanga ane hwamanda, “Sunungura vatumwa vana vakasungwa parwizi rukuru runonzi Yufuretesi.”" 
Revelation9:15 Ipapo vatumwa vana vakasunungurwa, vakanga vakagadzirirwa nguva, nezuva, nomwedzi, negore, kuti vauraye chetatu chavanhu." 
Revelation9:16 Kuwanda kwehondo dzavatasvi vamabhiza kwakanga kuri zviuru zvezviuru zvamazana maviri; ndikanzwa kuverengwa kwavo. 
Revelation9:17 Saizvozvowo ndakaona mabhiza pakuratidzwa kwangu, navakanga vakaatasva, vane zvidzitiro zvechifuva zvakaita sezvomoto, nezvehiasindo, nezvesuriferi; nemisoro yamabhiza yakanga yakaita semisoro yeshumba; nomumiromo yawo makabuda moto, nohutsi nesuriferi." 
Revelation9:18 Chetatu chavanhu chakaurayiwa namatambudziko awa matatu, anoti, moto nohutsi nesuriferi, zvakabuda mumiromo yawo." 
Revelation9:19 Nokuti simba ramabhiza riri mumiromo yawo, nomumiswe yavo; nokuti miswe yawo yakaita senyoka, ine misoro; anokuvadza nayo." 
Revelation9:20 Vamwe vanhu vasina kuurayiwa namatambudziko awa, havana kutendeuka pamabasa amaoko avo, kuti varege kunamata mweya yakaipa, nezvifananidzo zvendarama, nezvisirivha, nezvendarira, nezvamabwe, nezvemiti, zvisingagoni kuona, kana kunzwa, kana kufamba;" 
Revelation9:21 havana kutendeukawo pakuuraya kwavo, kana pakurowa kwavo, kana paupombwe hwavo, kana pakuba kwavo." 
Revelation10:1 Zvino ndakaona mumwe mutumwa ane simba achiburuka kudenga, akapfeka gore; muraraungu wakanga uri pamusoro wake, chiso chake chakanga chakaita sezuva, netsoka dzake sembiru dzomoto." 
Revelation10:2 Akanga akabata bhuku duku rakazaruka muruoko rwake, akaisa rutsoka rwake rworudyi pamusoro pegungwa, norworuboshwe pamusoro penyika;" 
Revelation10:3 akadanidzira nezwi guru seshumba inorira; iye akati adanidzira, kutinhira kunomwe kukabudisa mazwi ako." 
Revelation10:4 Zvino kutinhira kunomwe kwakati kwareva, ndakanga ndonyora, ndikanzwa izwi richibva kudenga, richiti, “Zarira zvarehwa nokutinhira kunomwe, usazvinyora.”" 
Revelation10:5 Ipapo mutumwa uya wandakaona amire pamusoro pegungwa napamusoro penyika, akasimudzira ruoko rwake rworudyi kudenga," 
Revelation10:6 akapika naiye ari mupenyu nokusingaperi–peri, akasika denga nezvirimo, nenyika nezvirimo, negungwa nezvirimo, kuti nguva haingazovipo." 
Revelation10:7 Asi namazuva ezwi romutumwa wechinomwe, kana vodakuridza, zvakavanzika zvaMwari zvichapedziswa, sezvaakaparidzira varanda vake, ivo vaporofita." 
Revelation10:8 Ipapo izwi riya randakanzwa richibva kudenga, rakataurazve kwandiri, richiti, “Enda utore bhuku rakazaruka riri muruoko rwomutumwa, amire pamusoro pegungwa napamusoro penyika.”" 
Revelation10:9 Ndikaenda kumutumwa, ndikati kwaari, “Ndipei bhuku duku.” Iye akati kwandiri, “Tora, uridye, richavavisa mudumbu mako, asi mumuromo mako richanaka souchi.”" 
Revelation10:10 Ipapo ndakatora bhuku duku muruoko rwomutumwa, ndikaridya; rikanaka mumuromo mangu souchi; asi ndakati ndaridya, mudumbu mangu mukavaviswa." 
Revelation10:11 Vakati kwandiri, “Unofanira kuporofitazve pamusoro pavanhu vazhinji, nendudzi, nendimi, namadzimambo.”" 
Revelation11:1 Zvino ndakapiwa rutsanga rwakaita somudonzvo; zvikanzi, “Simuka, uere temberi yaMwari, neatari, navanonamata mairi." 
Revelation11:2 Asi siya ruvazhe ruri kunze kwetemberi, usaruera; nokuti rwakapiwa vahedheni; vachatsika guta dzvene mwedzi ina makumi mana nemiviri." 
Revelation11:3 Ndicharaira zvapupu zvangu zviviri kuti zviporofite, zvakapfeka masaga, mazuva ane chiuru china mazana maviri namakumi matanhatu.”" 
Revelation11:4 Ava ndiyo miorivhi miviri nezvigadziko zvemwenje zviviri zvimire pamberi paIshe wenyika. 
Revelation11:5 Kana kuno munhu anoda kuvakuvadza, moto uchabuda mumiromo yavo uchiparadza vavengi vavo; kana kuno munhu anoda kuvakuvadza, anofanira kuurayiwa saizvozvo." 
Revelation11:6 Vane simba rokuzarira denga, kuti mvura irege kunaya namazuva okuporofita kwavo; vane simba pamusoro pemvura kuti vaishandure ive ropa, nokurova nyika namatambudziko ose nenguva dzose dzavanoda." 
Revelation11:7 Kana vapedza kupupura kwavo, chikara chinokwira chichibva mugomba rakadzika–dzika chicharwa navo, chichivakunda nokuvauraya." 
Revelation11:8 Mitumbi yavo icharaswa panzira dzomuguta guru, rinonzi, nezita rokufananidzira, Sodhoma neIjipiti, pakaroverwawo Ishe wavo pamuchinjikwa." 
Revelation11:9 Vanobva kuvanhu, namarudzi, nendimi, nendudzi, vachaona mitumbi yavo mazuva matatu nehafu, vasingatenderi kuti ivigwe muhwiro." 
Revelation11:10 Navanogara panyika vachafara nokupembera pamusoro pavo, vachitumirana zvipo, nokuti vaporofita ava vaviri vakatambudza avo vanogara panyika." 
Revelation11:11 Zvino mazuva matatu nehafu akati apfuura, mweya woupenyu, wakabva kuna Mwari, ukapinda mukati mavo, vakamira netsoka dzavo, kutya kukuru kukawira vose vakavaona." 
Revelation11:12 Ipapo vakanzwa izwi guru, rinobva kudenga, richiti kwavari, “Kwirai pano.” Vakakwira kudenga negore, vavengi vavo vakavaona." 
Revelation11:13 Zvino nenguva iyo kudengenyeka kwenyika kwakavapo, chegumi cheguta chikaputsikira pasi, navanhu vane zviuru zvinomwe vakaurayiwa nokudengenyeka; vakasara vakatya, vakarumbidza Mwari wokudenga." 
Revelation11:14 Nhamo yechipiri yapfuura; tarira, nhamo yechitatu inokurumidza kusvika." 
Revelation11:15 Zvino mutumwa wechinomwe akaridza; mazwi makuru akavapo kudenga, achiti, “Ushe hwenyika hwava hwaIshe wedu, naKristu wake; uchahubata nokusingaperi–peri.”" 
Revelation11:16 Ipapo Vakuru vana makumi maviri navana vanogara pazvigaro zvavo zvoushe pamberi paMwari, vakawira pasi nezviso zvavo, vakanamata Mwari," 
Revelation11:17 vachiti, “Tinokuvongai imi, Ishe Mwari waMasimbaose, muripo, makanga muripo; nokuti makatora simba renyu guru, makabata ushe." 
Revelation11:18 Marudzi akatsamwa, nokutsamwa kwenyu kwakasvika, nenguva yavakafa, kuti vatongwe, uye kuti mupe varanda venyu mubairo, ivo vaporofita, navatsvene, navanotya zita renyu, vaduku navakuru; uye kuti muparadze avo vanoparadza nyika.”" 
Revelation11:19 Ipapo temberi yaMwari iri kudenga yakazarurwa; areka yesungano ikaonekwa mutemberi yake; ipapo kwakavapo mheni, namazwi, nokutinhira, nokudengenyeka kwenyika, nechimvuramabwe chikuru." 
Revelation12:1 Zvino kudenga kwakaonekwa chiratidzo chikuru ichi: Mukadzi, akanga akapfeka zuva, mwedzi uri pasi petsoka dzake, napamusoro wake korona ine nyenyedzi dzine gumi nembiri;" 
Revelation12:2 iye akanga ane mimba, akadanidzira pakupona kwake, achitambudzika pakuzvara." 
Revelation12:3 Ipapo kudenga kwakaonekwa chimwe chiratidzo ichi: Tarira, shato huru tsvuku, ine misoro minomwe, nenyanga dzine gumi, napamisoro wayo korona nomwe." 
Revelation12:4 Muswe wayo ukakweva chetatu chenyenyedzi dzokudenga, ndokudzikandira pasi panyika; shato iyo ikamira pamberi pomukadzi akanga ozvara, kuti iparadze mwana wake kana azvara." 
Revelation12:5 Akazvara mwana womukomana, anozofudza marudzi ose netsvimbo yedare; mwana wake ndokutorwa kuna Mwari, nokuchigaro chake choushe." 
Revelation12:6 Mukadzi akatizira kurenje, paakagadzirirwa nzvimbo naMwari, kuti vamuchengetepo mazuva ane chiuru china mazana maviri namakumi matanhatu." 
Revelation12:7 Zvino kurwa kwakavapo kudenga; Mikaeri navatumwa vake vakarwa neshato, shato ikarwa inavatumwa vayo;" 
Revelation12:8 vakasakunda, nenzvimbo yavo haina kuzowanikwa kudenga." 
Revelation12:9 Zvino shato huru yakakandirwa pasi, iyo nyoka yekare, inonzi Dhiabhori, naSatani, munyengeri wenyika yose; yakakandirwa panyika, navatumwa vayo vakakandirwa pasi pamwechete nayo." 
Revelation12:10 Ndikanzwa izwi guru kudenga, richiti, “Zvino ruponeso rwasvika, nesimba, noushe hwaMwari wedu, noumambo hwaKristu wake; nokuti mupomeri wehama dzedu wakakandirwa pasi, wakavapomera pamberi paMwari wedu masikati nousiku." 
Revelation12:11 Ivo vakamukunda neropa reGwayana, uye neshoko rokupupura kwavo; havana kuda upenyu hwavo kusvikira parufu." 
Revelation12:12 Saka farai kudenga nemi munogarako. Mune nhamo imi nyika negungwa, nokuti mweya wakaipa wakaburukira kwamuri, akatsamwa kwazvo, nokuti anoziva kuti achine nguva duku.”" 
Revelation12:13 Shato yakati yaona kuti yakandirwa pasi panyika ikatambudza mukadzi akazvara mwana womukomana. 
Revelation12:14 Ipapo mukadzi akapiwa mapapiro maviri egondo guru, kuti abhururukire kurenje kunzvimbo yake, kwaanochengeterwa nguva nedzimwe nguva nehafu yenguva, kwaasingaonekwi nenyoka." 
Revelation12:15 Ipapo nyoka yakabudisa mvura mumuromo mayo, yakaita sorwizi shure kwomukadzi, kuti akukurwe norwizi." 
Revelation12:16 Ipapo nyika yakabatsira mukadzi, nyika ikashamisa muromo wayo, ikamedza rwizi neshato mumuromo mayo." 
Revelation12:17 Zvino shato yakatsamwira mukadzi ikaenda kundorwa navamwe vana vake, vanochengeta mirairo yaMwari, navanobata kupupura kwaJesu." 
Revelation12:18 Ikamira pajecha regungwa. 
Revelation13:1 Zvino ndakaona chikara chichikwira chichibva mugungwa, chine nyanga dzine gumi nemisoro minomwe; napamusoro penyanga dzacho pakanga pane korona dzine gumi, napamusoro pemisoro yacho mazita okumhura Mwari." 
Revelation13:2 Chikara ichi chandakaona, chakanga chakaita sengwe; netsoka dzacho sedzebere, nomuromo wacho somuromo weshumba; shato ikachipa simba rayo, nechigaro chayo chohushe, namasimba makuru." 
Revelation13:3 Mumwe musoro wacho wakanga wakaita sowakakuvadzwa kusvikira parufu; asi vanga, raifanira kuuraya, rakanga rapora; nyika yose ikashamiswa ikatevera chikara." 
Revelation13:4 Vakanamata shato, nokuti yakapa chikara masimba; vakanamata chikara, vachiti, “Ndianiko akafanana nechikara? Ndianiko anogona kurwa nacho?”" 
Revelation13:5 Ipapo chakapiwa muromo unotaura mashoko makuru nezvokumhura; chikapiwa simba kuti chizviite mwedzi ina makumi mana nemiviri. 
Revelation13:6 Chikashamisa muromo wacho kuti chimhure Mwari, nokumhura zita rake netabhenakeri yake naivo vanogara kudenga." 
Revelation13:7 Chikapiwa masimbawo kuti chirwe navatsvene, nokuvakunda; chikapiwa masimbawo pamusoro pamarudzi ose, navanhu vose, nendimi dzose, nendudzi dzose." 
Revelation13:8 Vose vanogara panyika vachachinamata, ivo vasina kunyorerwa zita ravo mubhuku yeGwayana rakabayiwa, kubva pakusikwa kwenyika." 
Revelation13:9 Ane nzeve, ngaanzwe." 
Revelation13:10 Kana munhu achitapa, achatapwa; kana munhu achiuraya nomunondo anofanira kuurayiwa nomunondo. Ndipo panokutsungirira nokutenda kwavatsvene." 
Revelation13:11 Zvino ndakaona chimwe chikara chichikwira, chichibva panyika; chakanga chine nyanga mbiri segwayana, chikataura seshato." 
Revelation13:12 Chinobata namasimba ose echikara chokutanga pamberi pacho. Chinomanikidza nyika navagere mukati mayo kuti vanamate chikara chokutanga, chiya chakapora vanga rokuuraya racho." 
Revelation13:13 Chinoita zviratidzo zvikuru, zvokuti chinoburusira moto unobva kudenga panyika pamberi pavanhu;" 
Revelation13:14 chinonyengera vanogara panyika nezviratidzo zvachapiwa kuti chizviite pamberi pechikara; chichiti kuna vanogara panyika kuti vaitire chikara mufananidzo, chiya chakanga chine vanga romunondo chakararama." 
Revelation13:15 Chikapiwa masimba okupa mufananidzo wechikara mweya, kuti mufananidzo wechikara utaure, chiraire kuti vose vasinganamati mufananidzo wechikara vaurawe." 
Revelation13:16 Chinomanikidza vose, vaduku navakuru, vafumi navarombo, vakasununguka navaranda, kuti vapiwe chiratidzo muruoko rwavo rworudyi, kana pahuma yavo;" 
Revelation13:17 kuti munhu arege kuvapo anogona kutenga nokutengesa, asi iye ane chiratidzo, iro zita rechikara kana chiverengo chezita racho." 
Revelation13:18 Ndipo panokuchenjera. Anoziva, ngaaverenge chiverengo chechikara; nokuti chiverengo ndechomunhu; chiverengo chacho ndimazana matanhatu namakumi matanhatu nenhanhatu." 
Revelation14:1 Zvino ndakatarira, ndikaona Gwayana rimire pagomo reZioni, rina vamwe vane zviuru zvine zana namakumi mana navana, vane zita raro, nezita raBaba varo, rakanyorwa pahuma dzavo." 
Revelation14:2 Ipapo ndakanzwa izwi richibva kudenga, sezwi remvura zhinji, uye sezwi rokutinhira kukuru; nezwi randakanzwa rakanga rakaita seravaridzi vorudimbwa vachiridza madimbwa avo." 
Revelation14:3 Vakaimba rwiyo rutsva pamberi pechigaro choushe, napamberi pezvisikwa zvipenyu zvina, naVakuru; hakuna munhu akagona kudzidza rwiyo urwu, asi vaya vane zviuru zvine zana namakumi mana navana, vakadzikinurwa vachibva panyika." 
Revelation14:4 Ndivo vasina kusvibiswa navakadzi; nokuti vakanaka semhandara. Ndivo vanotevera Gwayana kwose kwarinoenda. Ndivo vakadzikinurwa pakati pavanhu, kuti vave zvibereko zvokutanga kuna Mwari nokuGwayana." 
Revelation14:5 Mumuromo mavo hamuna kuonekwa nhema, havana chavangapomerwa." 
Revelation14:6 Zvino ndakaona mumwe mutumwa achibhururuka pakati pedenga, ane Vhangeri isingaperi, kuti aiparidzire vanogara panyika, namarudzi ose, nendudzi dzose nendimi dzose, navanhu vose." 
Revelation14:7 Akati nezwi guru, “Ityai Mwari, mumurumbidze; nokuti nguva yake yokutonga yasvika; namatai iye, akasika denga, nenyika, negungwa, namatsime emvura.”" 
Revelation14:8 Ipapo mumwe mutumwa akatevera, achiti, “Rawa, Rawa, Bhabhironi, guta guru, rakanwisa marudzi ose waini yokutsamwa kwoupombwe hwaro.”" 
Revelation14:9 Ipapo mumwe mutumwa wechitatu akatevera, akati nezwi guru, “Kana munhu akanamata chikara nomufananidzo wacho, nokugamuchira chiratidzo pahuma yake kana paruoko rwake," 
Revelation14:10 naiye achanwawo waini yokutsamwa kwaMwari, yakadirwa isina kuvhenganiswa mumukombe wehasha dzake; achatambudzwa mumoto nesuriferi pamberi pavatumwa vatsvene, napamberi peGwayana." 
Revelation14:11 Hutsi hokutambudzika hwavo hunokwira nokusingaperi–peri; havana zororo masikati nousiku, ivo vanonamata chikara nomufananidzo wacho, noanogamuchira chiratidzo chezita racho.”" 
Revelation14:12 Ndipo panokutsungirira kwavatsvene, vanochengeta mirairo yaMwari nokutenda kwaJesu." 
Revelation14:13 Ipapo ndakanzwa izwi richibva kudenga, richiti, “Nyora, uti: Vakafa, vanofira muna Ishe, vakaropafadzwa kubva zvino. Hongu, ndizvo zvinotaura Mweya, kuti vazorore pakubata kwavo kukuru, nokuti mabasa avo anovatevera.”" 
Revelation14:14 Ipapo ndakatarira, ndikaona gore jena, nomumwe wakaita soMwanakomana womunhu agere pamusoro paro, ane korona yendarama pamusoro wake, naparuoko rwake ane jeko rinopinza." 
Revelation14:15 Zvino mumwe mutumwa akabuda mutemberi, akadanidzira nezwi guru kuna iye akanga agere pamusoro pegore, achiti, “Tumai jeko renyu mucheke; nokuti nguva yokucheka yasvika, nokuti kucheka kwenyika kwaibva.”" 
Revelation14:16 Ipapo akanga agere pamusoro pegore akakandira jeko rake panyika, nyika ikachekwa." 
Revelation14:17 Zvino mumwe mutumwa akabuda mutemberi iri kudenga, naiyewo ane jeko rinopinza." 
Revelation14:18 Nomumwe mutumwa akanga ane simba pamusoro pomoto, akabuda paatari, akadanidzira nezwi guru kuna iye akanga ane jeko rinopinza, achiti, “Tumai jeko renyu rinopinza, mucheke masumbu omuzambiringa wenyika, nokuti mazambiringa ayo aibva.”" 
Revelation14:19 Ipapo mutumwa wakakandira jeko rake panyika, akacheka muzambiringa wenyika, akazvikandira muchisviniro chikuru chokutsamwa kwaMwari." 
Revelation14:20 Chisviniro chikatsikwa kunze kweguta, ropa rikabuda muchisviniro rikasvika pamatomo amabhiza, rikaenda masitadhia ane chiuru china mazana matanhatu." 
Revelation15:1 Zvino ndakaona chimwe chiratidzo kudenga, chikuru chinoshamisa, ichi: Vatumwa vanomwe vanamatambudziko manomwe okupedzisira, nokuti kutsamwa kwaMwari kwakapera nawo." 
Revelation15:2 Ndikaona chakaita segungwa rinoonekera rakavhenganiswa nomoto, naivo vakauya vakunda chikara nomufananidzo wacho, nechiverengo chezita racho, vamire pamusoro pegungwa rinoonekera, vanohudimbwa hwaMwari." 
Revelation15:3 Vakanga vachiimba rwiyo rwaMosesi, muranda waMwari, norwiyo rweGwayana, vachiti, “Ishe, Mwari waMasimbaose, mabasa enyu akakura, anoshamisa; Mambo wamarudzi, nzira dzenyu dzakarurama, ndedzazvokwadi." 
Revelation15:4 “Ndianiko angarega kutya nokukudza zita renyu, Ishe? Nokuti imi moga muri mutsvene; nokuti marudzi ose achauya, achinamata pamberi penyu; nokuti kururama kwenyu kwakaratidzwa.”" 
Revelation15:5 Shure kwaizvozvo ndakaona temberi yetabhenakeri yohuchapupu yokudenga yakazarurwa; 
Revelation15:6 mutemberi mukabuda vatumwa vanomwe vanamatambudziko manomwe, vakafuka mucheka wakachena unopenya, vakasungwa pazvipfuva zvavo namabhandi endarama." 
Revelation15:7 Ipapo chimwe chezvisikwa zvipenyu zvina chakapa vatumwa vanomwe ndiro nomwe dzendarama, dzizere nokutsamwa kwaMwari, iye mupenyu nokusingaperi–peri." 
Revelation15:8 Temberi ikazara nohutsi hunobva pakubwinya kwaMwari napasimba rake; kukasava nomunhu akagona kupinda patemberi, kusvikira matambudziko manomwe avatumwa vanomwe apera." 
Revelation16:1 Zvino ndakanzwa izwi guru richibva mutemberi, richiti kuvatumwa vanomwe, “Endai, mundodurura panyika ndiro nomwe dzokutsamwa dzaMwari.”" 
Revelation16:2 Wokutanga akaenda, akadurura ndiro yake panyika; ronda rakaipa rinorwadza rikavapo pavanhu vakanga vane chiratidzo chechikara, vakanamata mufananidzo wacho." 
Revelation16:3 Wechipiri akadurura ndiro yake pagungwa; rikashanduka ropa seromunhu akafa; nezvipenyu zvose zvakanga zviri mugungwa zvikafa. 
Revelation16:4 Wechitatu akadurura ndiro yake panzizi nomumatsime emvura, ikashanduka ropa." 
Revelation16:5 Ndikanzwa mutumwa wemvura achiti, “Imi, Makarurama, muripo, namakanga miripo, Mutsvene, nokuti makatonga saizvozvo." 
Revelation16:6 Nokuti vakadurura ropa ravatsvene neravaporofita, mukavapa ropa, kuti vanwe; vakafanirwa naizvozvo.”" 
Revelation16:7 Ndikanzwa atari ichiti, “Hongu, Ishe, Mwari wamasimba ose, kutonga kwenyu ndokwechokwadi kwakarurama.”" 
Revelation16:8 Zvino wechina akadurura ndiro yake pamusoro pezuva, rikapiwa simba kuti ripise vanhu nomoto." 
Revelation16:9 Vanhu vakapiswa nokupisa kukuru, vakamhura zita raMwari, ane simba pamusoro pamatambudziko aya; havana kutendeuka, kuti vamukudze." 
Revelation16:10 Wechishanu akadurura ndiro yake pamusoro pechigaro choushe chechikara; ushe hwacho hukasvibiswa, vakatsenga marimi avo nokurwadzwa;" 
Revelation16:11 vakamhura Mwari wokudenga pamusoro pokurwadzwa kwavo namaronda avo; asi havana kutendeuka pamabasa avo. 
Revelation16:12 Zvino wechitanhatu akadurura ndiro yake pamusoro porwizi rukuru, runonzi Yufuretesi; mvura yarwo ikapwa, kuti nzira dzamadzimambo anobva kumabvazuva dzigadzirwe." 
Revelation16:13 Ipapo ndakaona mweya yetsvina mitatu yakaita samatafi ichibva mumuromo weshato nomumuromo wechikara, nomumuromo womuporofita wenhema;" 
Revelation16:14 nokuti ndiyo mweya yakaipa inoita zviratidzo; inoenda kumadzimambo enyika yose, kuvakokera kukurwa pazuva iro guru raMwari waMasimbaose." 
Revelation16:15 Tarira, ndinouya sembavha. Akaropafadzwa anorinda, anochengeta nguo dzake, kuti arege kufamba asina kupfeka, vaone nyadzi dzake." 
Revelation16:16 Akavaunganidzira panzvimbo inonzi Harimagedhoni neChiHebheru. 
Revelation16:17 Zvino wechinomwe akadurura ndiro yake mudenga, izwi guru rikabuda muchigaro choushe, richiti, “Zvapera!”" 
Revelation16:18 Ipapo mheni yakavapo, namazwi nokutinhira; nokudengenyeka kwenyika kukuru kwakavapo; kudengenyeka kwenyika kwakakura–kura kukadai hakuna kumbovapo kubva pakusikwa kwavanhu panyika." 
Revelation16:19 Guta guru rikakamurwa rikaita zvikamu zvitatu, maguta amarudzi akaputsika; Bhabhironi guta guru rikarangarirwa pamberi paMwari, kuti ripiwe mukombe wewaini yokutsamwa kwehasha dzake." 
Revelation16:20 Zviwi zvose zvikatiza, namakomo haana kuwanikwa." 
Revelation16:21 Chimvuramabwe chikuru, chinobva kudenga, chikawira pamusoro pavanhu, kurema kwebwe rimwe nerimwe kukaita setarenda; vanhu vakamhura Mwari nokuda kwedambudziko rechimvuramambwe, nokuti dambudziko racho raiva guru kwazvo." 
Revelation17:1 Zvino mumwe wavatumwa vanomwe, vakanga vane ndiro nomwe, akauya akataura neni, achiti, “Uya pano, ndichakuratidza kutongwa kwemhombwe huru, inogara pamusoro pemvura zhinji;" 
Revelation17:2 madzimambo enyika akaita upombwe nayo, navanogara panyika vakabatwa newaini youpombwe hwayo.”" 
Revelation17:3 Ipapo akandiisa kurenje mumweya, ndikaona mukadzi akatasva chikara chitsvuku, chizere namazita okumhura Mwari, chine misoro minomwe nenyanga gumi." 
Revelation17:4 Mukadzi akanga akapfeka nguo tsvuku neshava, akashonga ndarama namabwe anokosha, namapera, nomuruoko rwake makanga munomudziyo wendarama uzere nezvinonyangadza netsvina youpombwe hwake." 
Revelation17:5 Pahuma yake pakanga pakanyorwa zita rakavanzika iri: “BHABHIRONI, GUTA GURU, MAI VEMHOMBWE NAVEZVINONYANGADZA ZVENYIKA.”" 
Revelation17:6 Ipapo ndakaona mukadzi akabatwa neropa ravatsvene, uye neropa rezvapupu zvaJesu; ndikati ndichimuona ndikashamiswa nokushamiswa kukuru." 
Revelation17:7 Ipapo mutumwa akati kwandiri, “Washamiswa neiko? Ndichakuudza zvakavanzika zvomukadzi, nezvechikara chinomutakura chine misoro minomwe nenyanga dzine gumi." 
Revelation17:8 Chikara chawaona, chaivapo, hachichipo; choda kukwira chichibva mugomba rakadzika–dzika kundoparadzwa; vanogara panyika vasina kunyorwa mazita avo mubhuku youpenyu kubva pakusikwa kwenyika, vachashamiswa kana vachiona chikara, kuti chaivapo, hachichipo, uye chichazovapo." 
Revelation17:9 “Ndipo panokufunga kune njere. Misoro minomwe ndiwo makomo manomwe, anogarwa nomukadzi." 
Revelation17:10 Ndiwo madzimambo manomwe; vashanu vawa, mumwe aripo, mumwe agere kusvika; kana achisvika, anofanira kugara chinguva chiduku." 
Revelation17:11 Chikara chaivapo, chisisipo, ndiye worusere, mumwe wavanomwe, anondoparadzwa." 
Revelation17:12 “Nyanga dzine gumi dzawaona, ndiwo madzimambo ane gumi, achigere kupiwa ushe, asi vachapiwa simba samadzimambo pamwechete nechikara nguva imwe." 
Revelation17:13 “Ivo vane ndangariro imwe, vanopa chikara simba ravo noushe hwavo." 
Revelation17:14 Ava vacharwa neGwayana, Gwayana richavakunda; nokuti iro ndiIshe wamadzishe, namambo wamamdzimambo; naivo vanaro ndivanhu vakadanwa, vatsvene, vakatendeka.”" 
Revelation17:15 Zvino akati kwandiri, “Mvura yawaona, inogarwa nemhombwe, ndivo vanhu, navazhinji, namarudzi, nendimi." 
Revelation17:16 Nyanga dzine gumi dzawaona, nechikara, ndivo vachavenga mhombwe, vachaiparadza, nokuitorera nguo; vachadya nyama yayo, nokuipisa nomoto." 
Revelation17:17 Nokuti Mwari akaisa mumwoyo yavo kuti vaite kurangarira kwake, vave nokurangarira kumwe, vape chikara ushe hwavo, kusvikira mashoko aMwari aitika." 
Revelation17:18 “Mukadzi wawaona ndiro guta guru, rinobata ushe hwamadzimambo enyika.”" 
Revelation18:1 Shure kwaizvozvi ndakaona mumwe mutumwa achiburuka kudenga, ane simba guru; nyika ikavhenekerewa nokubwinya kwake." 
Revelation18:2 Akadanidzira nezwi guru, achiti, “Rawa, Rawa, Bhabhironi, guta guru, yava nzvimbo munogara mweya yakaipa, nenhare yemweya yose yetsvina, nenhare yeshiri dzose dzine tsvina, dzinovengwa." 
Revelation18:3 Nokuti marudzi ose akawa newaini yokutsamwa kwoupombwe hwaro, namadzimambo enyika akaita upombwe naro, navatengesi venyika vakapfuma nesimba rokuzvirasa kwaro.”" 
Revelation18:4 Zvino ndakanzwa rimwe izwi rinobva kudenga, richiti, “Budai mariri, vanhu vangu, kuti murege kuwadzana naro pazvivi zvaro, mugorega kupiwa matambudziko aro." 
Revelation18:5 Nokuti zvivi zvaro zvasvika kudenga, Mwari arangarira zvisakarurama zvaro." 
Revelation18:6 Muritsive parakakutsivai napo, muchiriitira kaviri parakabata napo; mumudziyo iwoyo marakadira iro, muridirire kaviri." 
Revelation18:7 “Parakazvikudza nokuzvifadza napo, murirwadzise nokurichemedza; nokuti rinoti mumwoyo maro, ‘Ndinogara pachigaro choushe ndiri vahosi, handizi chirikadzi, handingatongooni kuchema.’" 
Revelation18:8 “Saka matambudziko aro achasvika nezuva rimwe, rufu, nokuchema, nenzara; richapiswa kwazvo nomoto, nokuti Ishe Mwari anoritonga, ane simba.”" 
Revelation18:9 Madzimambo enyika, akaita upombwe nokuzvifadza naro, achiona hutsi hokupiswa kwaro;" 
Revelation18:10 ivo vamire kure nokutya kurwadzwa kwaro, vachiti, “Nhamo, nhamo, newe, guta guru, iwe Bhabhironi, guta rakasimba! Nokuti kutongwa kwako kwakasvika nenguva imwe.”" 
Revelation18:11 Vatengesi venyika vacharira nokuchema pamusoro paro, nokuti hakuchina munhu anotenga nhumbi dzavo;" 
Revelation18:12 nhumbi dzendarama, nesirivha, nedzamambwe anokosha, nedzamapera nedzomucheka wakanaka, nedzemicheka mitsvuku, nedzesiriki, nedzemicheka mishava, namarudzi ose emiti inonhuwira, namarudzi ose emidziyo yenyanga dzenzou, namarudzi ose emidziyo yamatanda anokosha, nedzesafuri, nedzedare, nedzamabwe machena;" 
Revelation18:13 nesinamoni, nomuamumoni, nezvinonhuwira, namafuta okuzora, namafuta omuribhanoni, newaini, namafuta omuorivhi, nohupfu hwakatsetseka, nezviyo, nemombe, namakwai, nenhumbi dzamabhiza, nedzengoro, nedzavatapwa, nedzemweya yavanhu." 
Revelation18:14 Michero yaidikanwa nomwoyo wako, yakabva kwauri, nezvinhu zvose zvakanaka nezvinopenya, zvakabva kwauri, vanhu havangatongozozviwanizve." 
Revelation18:15 Vatengesi vezvinhu izvi, vakanga vafumiswa naro, vachamira kure nokutya kurwadzwa kwaro, vachirira nokuchema," 
Revelation18:16 vachiti, “Nhamo, nhamo, guta guru rakanga rakapfeka mucheka wakanaka, mutsvuku nomushava, rakanga rakashonga ndarama, namabwe anokosha, namapera!" 
Revelation18:17 Nokuti nenguva imwe pfuma huru yakadai yaparadzwa.” Zvino vafambisi vose vezvikepe, navose vanofamba nezvikepe papi napapi, navafambi navabati pagungwa, vakamira kure," 
Revelation18:18 vakadanidzira vachiona hutsi hwokutsva kwaro, vachiti, “Guta rakafanana neguta iri guru nderipiko?”" 
Revelation18:19 Ipapo vakakandira guruva pamisoro yavo, vakadanidzira vachirira nokuchema, vachiti, “Nhamo, nhamo, guta guru, kwaifumiswa nezvinokosha zvaro vose vaiva nezvikepe zvavo pagungwa; nokuti rakaparadzwa nenguva imwe.”" 
Revelation18:20 Farai pamusoro paro iwe denga, nemi vatsvene navapostori, navaporofita, nokuti Mwari akaritongera kutongwa kwenyu." 
Revelation18:21 Zvino mumwe mutumwa ane simba akasimudza ibwe rakaita seguyo guru, akarikandira mugungwa, achiti, “Saizvozvo guta guru, Bhabhironi, richaputsirwa pasi nesimba, rikatongowanikwazve." 
Revelation18:22 Nezwi ravanoridza madimbwa, neravanoimba, neravanoridza nyere, neravanoridza hwamanda, harichatongonzwiki mauri, nemhizha yebasa ripi neripi haichatongowanikwi mauri, nezwi reguyo harichatongonzwiki mauri;" 
Revelation18:23 chiedza chomwenje hachichatongovhenekeri mauri, nezwi rechikomba kana romwenga harichatongonzwiki mauri; nokuti vatengesi vako vaiva vakuru venyika; nokuti nouroyi hwako marudzi ose akanyengerwa.”" 
Revelation18:24 Mukati maro mukawanikwa ropa ravaporofita neravatsvene, neravose vakaurayiwa panyika." 
Revelation19:1 Shure kwaizvozvo ndakanzwa izwi guru seravazhinji zhinji kudenga, richiti, “Hareruya! Ruponeso, nokubwinya, nesimba ndezvaMwari wedu;" 
Revelation19:2 nokuti kutonga kwake ndokwechokwadi kwakarurama; nokuti akatonga mhombwe huru yakaodza nyika noupombwe hwayo, akatsiva ropa ravaranda vake paruoko rwayo.”" 
Revelation19:3 Ipapo vakapamhidza, vachiti, “Hareruya! Hutsi hwayo hunokwira nokusingaperi–peri.”" 
Revelation19:4 Zvino Vakuru vana makumi maviri navana nezvisikwa zvipenyu zvina vakawira pasi vakanamata Mwari akanga agere pachigaro choushe, vakati, “Ameni, Hareruya!”" 
Revelation19:5 Izwi rikabva pachigaro choushe, richiti, “Rumbidzai Mwari, imi mose varanda vake, imi munomutya, vaduku navakuru.”" 
Revelation19:6 Ipapo ndakanzwa sezwi ravazhinji zhinji, sezwi remvura zhinji, sezwi rokutinhira kukuru, richiti, “Hareruya! Nokuti Ishe Mwari wedu waMasimbaose anobata ushe." 
Revelation19:7 Ngatifarei, tifarisise, timukudze; nokuti mutambo wokuwana weGwayana wasvika, mukadzi waro wazvigadzirira." 
Revelation19:8 “Akapiwa simba kuti apfeke mucheka wakanaka, unopenya, asina tsvina; nokuti mucheka wakanaka ndizvo zvakarurama zvavatsvene.”" 
Revelation19:9 Zvino akati kwandiri, “Nyora, uti: Vakaropafadzwa vakakokerwa kuchirayiro chokuwana cheGwayana.” Akati kwandiri, “Mashoko awa ndeechokwadi aMwari.”" 
Revelation19:10 Ipapo ndakawira pasi pamberi petsoka dzake, kuti ndimunamate. Akati kwandiri, “Rega kudaro, nokuti ndiri muranda pamwechete newe nehama dzako dzinobata kupupura kwaJesu; namata Mwari,” nokuti kupupura kwaJesu ndiwo mweya wokuporofita." 
Revelation19:11 Ipapo ndakaona kudenga kwakazarurwa, ndikaona bhiza jena; naiye akanga agere pamusoro paro akanzi: Akatendeka noWechokwadi; anotonga nokurwa zvakarurama." 
Revelation19:12 Meso ake akanga akaita somurazvo womoto; pamusoro wake pakanga pane korona zhinji; wakanga ane zita rakanyorwa, risina kuzikanwa nomunhu, asi naiye bedzi." 
Revelation19:13 Akanga akapfeka nguo yakanyikwa muropa; zita rake rinonzi, “Shoko raMwari.”" 
Revelation19:14 Hondo dzokudenga dzakamutevera, dzakatasva mabhiza machena, dzakafuka mucheka wakanaka muchena, usina tsvina." 
Revelation19:15 Mumuromo make makabuda munondo unopinza, kuti arove marudzi nawo; achaafudza netsvimbo yedare; anotsika chisviniro chehasha dzokutsamwa kwaMwari waMasimbaose." 
Revelation19:16 Panguo yake napachidya chake pakanga pakanyorwa zita rinoti, “MAMBO WAMADZIMAMBO NAISHE WAMADZISHE.”" 
Revelation19:17 Zvino ndakaona mutumwa amire muzuva; akadanidzira nezwi guru, achiti kushiri dzose dzinobhururuka pakati pedenga, “Uyai muungane pachirariro chikuru chaMwari," 
Revelation19:18 kuti mudye nyama yamadzimambo, nenyama yavakuru vezviuru zvamazana, nenyama yavane simba, nenyama yamabhiza, neyavatasvi vawo, nenyama yavanhu vose vakasununguka navakasungwa, vaduku navakuru.”" 
Revelation19:19 Zvino ndakaona chikara chiya namadzimambo enyika nehondo dzavo, vakaungana kuti varwe naiye akanga akatasva bhiza, nehondo dzake." 
Revelation19:20 Ipapo chikara chakabatwa pamwechete nomuporofita wenhema, akaita zviratidzo pamberi pacho, zvaakanyengera nazvo vaya vakapiwa chiratidzo chechikara, navainamata mufananidzo wacho. Ava vaviri vakakandirwa vari vapenyu mugomba romoto unopfuta nesuriferi." 
Revelation19:21 Vakasara vakaurayiwa nomunondo waiye akanga akatasva bhiza, akabuda mumuromo make; shiri dzose dzikaguta nyama yavo." 
Revelation20:1 Zvino ndakaona mutumwa achiburuka kudenga, ane kiyi yegomba rakadzika–dzika, nengetani huru muruoko rwake." 
Revelation20:2 Akabata shato, nyoka yakare, ndiye Dhiabhori naSatani, akamusunga makore ane gumi ramazana," 
Revelation20:3 akamukandira mugomba rakadzika–dzika akamupfigiramo, akaisa chisimbiso pamusoro pake, kuti arege kuzonyengera marudzi kusvikira makore ane gumi ramazana apera; shure kwaizvozvo anofanira kusunungurwa chinguva chiduku." 
Revelation20:4 Ipapo ndakaona zvigaro zvoushe; vakagara pamusoro pazvo, vakapiwa simba rokutonga; ndikaona mweya yavakanga vagurwa misoro nokuda kwokupupura kwaJesu, nokweshoko raMwari, navose vasina kunamata chikara kana mufananidzo wacho, vasina kupiwa chiratidzo pahuma dzavo naparuoko rwavo; vakararama vakabata ushe pamwechete naKristu makore ane gumi ramazana." 
Revelation20:5 Vamwe vakafa havana kurarama kusvikira makore ane gumi ramazana apera. Ndiko kumuka kwokutanga. 
Revelation20:6 Munhu anomugove pakumuka kwokutanga akaropafadzwa, mutsvene; rufu rwechipiri harune simba pamusoro paivava; asi vachava vapristi vaMwari navaKristu, vachabata ushe pamwechete naye makore ane gumi ramazana." 
Revelation20:7 Zvino kana makore ane gumi ramazana apera, Satani achasunungurwa mutorongo yake," 
Revelation20:8 achabuda kundonyengera marudzi ose ari kumativi mana enyika, ivo Gogi naMagogi, avaunganidzire kundorwa; kuwanda kwavo kwakaita sejecha regungwa." 
Revelation20:9 Vakakwira pakufara kwenyika, vakakomba misasa yavatsvene neguta rinodikanwa; ipapo moto wakaburuka uchibva kudenga; ukavaparadza." 
Revelation20:10 Zvino Dhiabhori, akavanyengera, akakandwa mudziva romoto nesuriferi, pane chikara nomuporofita wenhema, kuti varwadzwe masikati nousiku nokusingaperi–peri." 
Revelation20:11 Zvino ndakaona chigaro choushe chikuru chichena, naiye akanga agere pamusoro pacho, nyika nedenga zvakatiza pamberi pake, zvikasawanirwa nzvimbo." 
Revelation20:12 Ipapo ndakaona vakafa, vaduku navakuru, vamire pamberi pechigaro choushe; bhuku dzikazarurwa, neimwe bhuku youpenyu ikazarurwa; vakafa vakatongwa nezvakanga zvakanyorwa mubhuku, sezvavakabata." 
Revelation20:13 Gungwa rikabudisa vakafa vakanga vari mariri; norufu neHadhesi zvikabudisa vakafa vakanga vari mazviri; mumwe nomumwe akatongwa sezvaakabata. 
Revelation20:14 Ipapo rufu neHadhesi zvakakandirwa mudziva romoto. Ndirwo rufu rwechipiri, ndiro dziva romoto." 
Revelation20:15 Zvino kana munhu akawanikwa asina kunyorwa mubhuku youpenyu, akakandirwa mudziva romoto." 
Revelation21:1 Zvino ndakaona denga idzva nenyika itsva, nokuti denga rokutanga nenyika yokutanga zvakanga zvapfuura; negungwa rakanga risisipo." 
Revelation21:2 Ndikaona guta dzvene, Jerusaremu idzva, richiburuka kudenga richibva kuna Mwari, rakagadzirwa somwenga akashongerwa murume wake." 
Revelation21:3 Ndikanzwa izwi richibva kudenga, richiti, “Tarirai, tabhenakeri yaMwari iri pakati pavanhu, iye achagara navo, ivo vachava vanhu vake; Mwari amene achava navo, ave Mwari wavo." 
Revelation21:4 Achapukuta misodzi yose pameso avo; rufu haruchavipo, kana kuchema, kana kurira, kana kutambudzika hazvingavipo; nokuti zvokutanga zvapfuwura.”" 
Revelation21:5 Akanga agere pachigaro choushe akati, “Tarirai, ndinovandudza zvose.” Akati, “Nyora, nokuti mashoko aya angatendwe, ndeechokwadi.”" 
Revelation21:6 Akati kwandiri, “Zvaitwa. Ndini Arifa neOmega, kutanga nokuguma. Ini ndichapa ane nyota zvinobva patsime remvura youpenyu asingatengi." 
Revelation21:7 Anokunda achagara nhaka yezvinhu izvi; ndichava Mwari wake, iye achava mwanakomana wangu." 
Revelation21:8 “Asi kana vari vanotya, navasingatendi navanyangadzi, navaurayi, nemhombwe, navaroyi, navanonamata zvifananidzo, navose vanoreva nhema, mugove wavo uri mudziva rinopfuta nomoto nesuriferi; ndirwo rufu rwechipiri.”" 
Revelation21:9 Zvino mumwe wavatumwa vanomwe, vakanga vane ndiro nomwe dzizere namatambudziko manomwe okupedzisira, akasvika, akataura neni, achiti, “Uya pano, ndigokuratidza mwenga, mukadzi weGwayana.”" 
Revelation21:10 Ipapo wakandiisa muMweya kugomo guru refu, akandiratidza guta dzvene, Jerusaremu, richiburuka kudenga, richibva kuna Mwari," 
Revelation21:11 rinokubwinya kwaMwari; chiedza charo chakanga chakaita sebwe rinokosha kwazvo, sebwe rejasipisi, rinowonekera sekirisitaro;" 
Revelation21:12 rakanga rinorusvingo rukuru, rurefu, rakanga rina masuwo ane gumi namaviri; navatumwa vane gumi navaviri pamasuwo, namazita akanyorwa pamusoro pawo, ari mazita amarudzi ane gumi namaviri avana VaIsiraeri." 
Revelation21:13 Kumabvazuva kwakanga kuna masuwo matatu; kumusoro masuwo matatu, zasi masuwo matatu; nokumavirira masuwo matatu;" 
Revelation21:14 rusvingo rweguta rwakanga rune nheyo dzine gumi nembiri; napamusoro padzo mazita avapostori vane gumi navaviri veGwayana. 
Revelation21:15 Uyo, akataura neni, akanga anorutsanga rwendarama rwokuera guta narwo, namasuwo aro norusvingo rwaro." 
Revelation21:16 Guta rakanga rakavakwa namatavi mana akaenzana, kureba kwaro kwakaenzana nokufara kwaro; akayera guta norutsanga, zvikasvika pamasitadhia ane zviuru zvine gumi nezviviri kureba nokufara nokukwirira kwaro zvakanga zvakaenzana." 
Revelation21:17 Akaera rusvingo rwaro, makubhiti ane zana namakumi mana namana, nechiyero chomunhu, chiri chiyero chomutumwa." 
Revelation21:18 Rusvingo rwaro rwakanga rwakavakwa nejasipisi, uye guta rakanga riri rendarama yakaisvonaka, yakaonekera kwazvo." 
Revelation21:19 Nheyo dzorusvingo rweguta dzakanga dzakashongedzwa namambwe amarudzi ose anokosha. Nheyo yokutanga yakanga iri yejasipisi; yechipiri yesafiri; yechitatu yekarisidhoni; yechina yesimaragidhino; 
Revelation21:20 yechishanu yesaridhonikisi; yechitanhatu yesaridhio; yechinomwe yekirisoriti; yorusere yebheriri; yepfumbamwe yetopasi; yegumi yekirisopirasi; yegumi neimwe yehiakinti; yegumi nembiri yeametesti. 
Revelation21:21 Masuwo ane gumi namaviri akanga ari amapera ane gumi namaviri; suwo rimwe nerimwe rakanga riri reparera rimwe; nzira yomuguta yakanga iri yendarama yakaisvonaka, inoita seinoonekera." 
Revelation21:22 Handina kuona temberi mukati maro, nokuti Ishe Mwari waMasimbaose neGwayana itemberi yaro." 
Revelation21:23 Guta haritsvaki zuva kana mwedzi, kuti rivhenekerwe nazvo; nokuti kubwinya kwaMwari ndiko kwairivhenekera, nomwenje waro ndiro Gwayana." 
Revelation21:24 Ndudzi dzinofamba nechiedza charo; madzimambo enyika anouyisa kubwinya kwawo mukati maro. 
Revelation21:25 Masuwo aro haangatongozarirwi masikati, nokuti usiku hahuchazovipo." 
Revelation21:26 Vachauyisa mukati maro kubwinya nokukudzwa kwendudzi. 
Revelation21:27 Mukati maro hamungatongopindi chinhu chinosvibisa, kana chinonyangadza, kana chine nhema; asi avo bedzi vakanyorwa mubhuku youpenyu yeGwayana." 
Revelation22:1 Zvino akandiratidza rwizi rwemvura youpenyu, yakapenya sekirisitaro, inobuda pachigaro choushe chaMwari necheGwayana," 
Revelation22:2 pakati penzira yaro. Kumativi maviri orwizi kwakanga kunomuti woupenyu, unobereka michero yamarudzi ane gumi namaviri, uchiita michero yaro mwedzi mumwe nomumwe; namashizha omuti aiva mushonga wokuporesa ndudzi." 
Revelation22:3 Hakuchavi nechinhu chakatukwa; chigaro choushe chaMwari necheGwayana chichava mukati maro; varanda vake vachamushumira; vachaona chiso chake; 
Revelation22:4 uye zita rake richava pahuma dzavo. 
Revelation22:5 Usiku hahuchazovepo; havatsvaki chiedza chomwenje, kana chiedza chezuva; nokuti Ishe Mwari achavavhenekera; vachabata ushe nokusingaperi–peri." 
Revelation22:6 Zvino akati kwandiri, “Mashoko awa angatendwe, ndeechokwadi; Ishe, Mwari wemweya yavaporofita wakatuma mutumwa wake kuti aratidze varanda vake zvinhu zvoda kuitwa.”" 
Revelation22:7 Tarirai, ndokurumidza kuuya; anochengeta mashoko okuporofita kwebhuku iri akaropafadzwa." 
Revelation22:8 Ini Johani, ndini ndakanzwa, ndikaona izvozvi. Zvino ndakati ndichinzwa, nokuona, ndikawira pasi kuti ndinamate pamberi petsoka dzomutumwa akandiratidza izvozvi." 
Revelation22:9 Akati kwandiri, “Rega kudaro; ndiri muranda pamwechete newe, nehama dzako, vaporofita, navanochengeta mashoko ebhuku iyi; namata Mwari.”" 
Revelation22:10 Ipapo akati kwandiri, “Usazarira mashoko okuporofita kwebhuku iri, nokuti nguva yava pedyo." 
Revelation22:11 Asina kururama ngaarambe achiita zvisakarurama; mutsvene ngaarambe achiitwa mutsvene.” 
Revelation22:12 “Tarirai, ndinokurumidza kuuya; mubairo wangu ndinawo, kuti ndipe mumwe nomumwe sezvaakabata." 
Revelation22:13 Ndini Arifa neOmega, wokutanga nowokupedzisira, kutanga nokuguma.”" 
Revelation22:14 Vanosuka nguo dzavo vakaropafadzwa, kuti vave nesimba rokuuya kumuti woupenyu, vapinde napamasuwo eguta." 
Revelation22:15 Kunze ndiko kune imbwa, navaroyi, nemhombwe, navaurayi, navanonamata zvifananidzo, navose vanoda nhema vachidziita." 
Revelation22:16 “Ini Jesu, ndakatuma mutumwa wangu, kuti akupupurirei izvozvi pachechi. Ndini mudzi worudzi rwaDhavhidhi, nyamatsatse inopenya.”" 
Revelation22:17 Mweya nomwenga vanoti, “Uya!” Naiye anonzwa ngaati, “Uya!” Ane nyota ngaauye. Anoda ngaatore mvura youpenyu asingatengwi." 
Revelation22:18 Ndinopupurira mumwe nomumwe anonzwa mashoko okuporofita kwebhuku iri, ndichiti: Kana munhu akawedzera pazvinhu izvi, Mwari achawedzera kwaari matambudziko akanyorwa mubhuku iri;" 
Revelation22:19 kana munhu akabvisa mashoko ebhuku yokuporofita uku, Mwari uchabvisa mugove wake pamuti woupenyu, nomuguta dzvene, napazvinhu zvakanyorwa mubhuku iri." 
Revelation22:20 Iye anopupura izvozvi anoti, “Hongu, ndinokurumidza kuuya.” Ameni, uyai, Ishe Jesu."
